jaina - vividha sāhitya-śāstramālā ( 6 )
śrīlakṣmaṇagaṇiviracitaṁ
supāsanāhacariyaṁ ।
( dvitīyō bhāgaḥ )
gurjaradēśāntargatarājadhanya puravāstavyēna śrēṣṭhitrikamacandratanūjēna kalikātā viśvavidyālayē
saṁskr̥ta-prākr̥tādhyāpaka-parīkṣakēṇa nyāya - vyākaraṇatīrthapadavīkēna paṇḍita -
haragōvindadāsēna
saṁśōdhitaṁ saṁskr̥tacchāyayā vibhūṣitaṁ ca ।

vīrasaṁvat 2444 |

nibhicca saccāī hōi avāī ya nēhalōēvi । jaha kamalō niravāō jāō jasavihavaābhōgī || 2 ||
tathāhi ; -
||8||
puramatthi bharahakhētē vijayapuraṁ nāma tijayavikkhāyaṁ । savilāsavilāsiṇiāṇaṇaṁva pavarālayasusōhaṁ ||3||
tattha jasajala hirāyā narayaṇanā hōvi su-ra-yaṇā hivaī । tassatthi piyā ghariṇī hariṇīnayaṇā vasumaitti ॥4॥
tatyatthi paramō dhammaviyaḍḍhō aīva kamalaḍḍhō । kamalōtti suppasiddhō kamalasirī bhāriyā tassa ॥5॥
tāṇaṁ ca suō vimalō nāmēṇaṁ, ciṭṭiēṇa puṇa samalō | dōsāyarō kalāṇa ya kulabhavaṇaṁ tahavi hu na sōmō ॥
vāraṁtassava piṇō caliō dēsatarammi vaṇijatthaṁ । thalamaggēṇaṁ aha sō bahuvaladdīu ladēu ||7||
tasōciyapaṇiyaṁ ghittūṇaṁ bahuyavaṇiyapariyariō । pattō malayapurammi sōpārayadēsa sīmāē || 8 ||
tattha ya niyayaṁ paṇiyaṁ vikkēūṇaṁ kayāgaṇaṁ annaṁ । gahiraṁ caliō niyadēsasamuhō jāva tā sahasā ||9||
vuṭṭō akālamēhō akaliyasalilēṇa pūriyā maggā । tō tatthavi chāē sō thakkō kaivaya diṇāṇi ॥ 10 ॥
aha sāgarābhihāṇō uttariu sāgarāu tannayarē । saṁpattō vimalēṇaṁ diṭṭō niyanayavāṇiyaō ॥11॥
uciyapaḍivattipuvaṁ saṁbhāsēūṇa tēṇa tō bhaṇiō । jaha ēsa tumaṁ samagaṁpi jēṇa jāmō niyaṁ dēsaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
tō sāyarēṇa tōsāyarēṇa sō sāyarēṇa paḍibhaṇiō । baṁdhava ! paḍikkha pakkhaṁ, tuma saha jēṇa gōṭṭhīē ॥ 13 ॥
āgacchāmi sadēsaṁviviṇiuṁ kiṁpi kiṁpi kiṇiūṇaṁ । ghaḍiyacciya maha saṭṭī iha vaṇiēhiṁ samaṁ jēṇa ॥ 14॥
kanyāgōbhūmā'līkasthāpanīyāpahārakūṭasākṣīyam । varjayēd gr̥hī alīkaṁ pīnamidaṁ dūṣakaṁ dharmē ॥ 1 ॥
nirbhr̥tyasatyavādī bhavatyapāyī ca nēhalōkē'pi । yathā kamalō nirapāyō jātō yaśōvibhavābhōgī ॥2॥
puramasti bharatakṣētrē vijayapuraṁ nāma trijagadvikhyātam । savilāsāvilāsinyānanamiva pravarālaya (ka) suśōbham ॥3॥
tatra yaśōjaladhirājō nara jananāthō'pi surajanā (ratnā) dhipatiḥ । tasyāsti priyā gr̥hiṇī hariṇīnayanā vasumatīti ॥
tatrāsti paramaśrāddhō dharmavidagdhō'tīva kamalāḍhyaḥ । kamala iti suprasiddhaḥ kamalaśrīrbhāryā tasya ॥5॥
tayōśca sutō vimalō nāmnā, cēṣṭitēna punaḥ samalaḥ । dōṣākaraḥ kalānāṁ ca kulabhavanaṁ tathāpi khalu na sōmaḥ || 6 ||
vārayatyapi pitari calitō dēśāntarē vāṇijyārtham । sthalamārgēṇātha sa bahubalīvardān bhārayitvā ||7||
taddēśōcitapaṇyaṁ gr̥hītvā bahuvaṇikparikaritaḥ । prāptō malayapurē sōpārakadēśasīni ॥ 8 ॥
tatra ca nijaṁ paṇyaṁ vikrīya krayāṇakamanyat । gr̥hītvā calitō nijadēśasaṁmukhō yāvattāvat sahasā ॥9॥
vr̥ṣṭśē'kālamēvō'kalyasalilēna pūritā mārgāḥ । tatastatrāpi cchādayitvā sa sthitaḥ katipayadināni ॥ 10 ॥
atha sāgarābhidhāna uttīrya sāgarāt tannagarē | saṁprāptō vimalēna dr̥ṣṭō nijanagaravāṇijaḥ ॥ 11 ॥
ucitapratipattipūrvaṁ saṁbhāṣya tēna tatō bhaṇitaḥ । yathaihi tvaṁ samakamapi yēna yāvō nijaṁ dēśam ॥ 12॥
tataḥ sāgarēṇa tōṣākarēṇa sa sādarēṇa pratibhaṇitaḥ । bāndhava ! pratīkṣasva pakṣaṁ, tvayā saha yēna gōṣṭhyā || 13 |
1 kha. ga. ālāvaṁ kāuṁ tē ।

supāsanāha cariammi-
tō paḍivannaṁ tēṇaṁ tavtrayaṇaṁ tassa satyamajjhammi | āvāsiō ya vimalō bhuṁjai tēṇēva saha tattha ॥ 15॥
lahumavi vikkaṇa bahu kayāṇagaṁ tassa, sāgarasamēō । gacchai vaṇiāṇa gihē girahai annaṁpi bahupaṇiyaṁ ।।
ditōya hatthasanna tērsi sō givhaē ya bahulābhaṁ । avalavai vikiṇitō kiṁcivi majjhāu paṇiyassa || 17॥
tā jāva dasa sahastā gahiyā kaṇayassa vaṁciūṇa tayaṁ । appāṇaṁ vimalēṇaṁ citaṁtēṇaṁ aiviyaḍūḍhaṁ || 18 ||
suddhasahāvēṇa taō sāgaravaṇiēṇa saha samāraddhā । pīī anannasarisā, saṁcaliyā dōvi niyadē ||19||
avarayapayāmi gacchati garuyanēhēṇa । pavaraturayāhirūḍhā javalīē jāva tō kamasō ||20||
vimalaviyā pacōṇi samāgaō niyayaputtanēhēṇa | 'tērhipi savahumāṇaṁ namiō, āliṁgiyā tē ||21||
tō tēhiṁ samaṁ paṁthē vaccai kamalōvi niyapurābhinu । tō sāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mitta ! adipi diva || 22||
sāhēmi avita tuha nisuṇasu, gaḍḍī iō purō jāi । bhariyā aṁbāṇaṁ, taṁ ca khēḍaē māhaṇō kuṭṭī ||23||
dāhimya jāi tattha juttōṁ phuḍaṁ galī kujjō । vāmēvi vāmacaraṇammi khaṁjaō gōṇaō vahai ॥ 24 ॥
khēḍa vēlapharaka māyaṁgō pālaō akāsaṁtō । sṭṭhā kastavi pacchā samāgayā puttaganbhavaī ||25||
kakuṁkumaṁgarāyā raiyāmēlā ya baulamālāē । savvaṇadēhā rattuttarīyayā sigghapasavā ya ||26||
villayaphirakkacaḍiyā itthī, taṁ nisuṇiuṁ bhaṇai vimalō । varanāṇī piva jaṁpasi bhada ! tumaṁ, taṁ na tuha juttaṁ ॥
muhamatthitti vattavyaṁ, jaṁ ca taṁ cāpi vālisā | jaṁpati, na jiappāṇō visēsēṇa bhavārisā ||28||
āgacchāmi svadēśaṁ vikrīya kimapi kimapi krītvā । ghaṭita ēva mama vinimaya iha vaṇigbhiḥ samaṁ yēna ॥ 14 ॥
tataḥ pratipannaṁ tēna tadvacanaṁ tasya sārthamadhyē | āvāsitaśca vimalō bhuṅktē tēnaiva saha taṁtra ॥ 15 ॥
ladhvapi vikrīyatē bahu krayāṇakaṁ tasya, sāgarasamētaḥ । gacchati vaṇijāṁ gr̥hē gr̥hṇātyanyadapi bahupaṇyam ॥16॥
dadaca hastasaṁjñāṁ tēbhyaḥ sa gr̥hṇāti ca bahulābham । apalapati vikrīṇan kiñcidapi madhyāt paṇyasya ॥ 17 ॥
tāvad yāvaddaśa sahasrāṇi gr̥hītāni kanakasya vañcayitvaitam । ātmānaṁ vimalēna cintayatā'tividagdham ॥
śuddhasvabhāvēna tataḥ sāgaravaṇijā saha samārabdhā । prītirananyasadr̥śī, saṁcalitau dvāvapi nijadēśē ॥ 19॥
anavarata prayāṇairmārgē gacchatō gurusnēhēna । pravaraturagādhirūḍhau javēna yāvat tataḥ kramaśaḥ ॥20॥
।
vimalapitā saṁmukhaṁ samāgatō nijaputrasnēhēna । tābhyāmapi sabahumānaṁ nataḥ, āliṅgitau tēna ॥ 21 ॥
tatastābhyāṁ samaṁ pathi vrajati kamalō'pi nijapurābhimukham । tataḥ sāgarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ mitra ! adr̥ṣṭamapi dr̥ṣṭamiva ॥
kathayāmyavitathaṁ tava śr̥ṇu, gantrītaḥ purō yāti । bhr̥tā''traiḥ, tāṁ ca vāhayati brāhmaṇaḥ kuṣṭhī ||23||
dakṣiṇapakṣē ca yāti tatra yuktaḥ sphuṭaṁ galiḥ kubjaḥ । vāmē'pi vāmacaraṇē khañjakō gaurvahati ॥ 24 ॥
khēṭati vēṣṭakaprālambaṁ mātaṅgaḥ pālakōsspr̥śan । ruṣṭā kasyāpi paścāt samāgatā putragarbhavatī ॥25॥
kr̥takuṅkumāṅgarāgā racitāpīḍā ca bakulamālayā । satraṇadēhā raktōttarīyakā śīghraprasavā ca ॥ 26 ॥
vēṣṭakaprālambacaṭitā strī, tat śrutvā bhaṇati vimulaḥ । varajñānīva jalpasi bhadra ! tvaṁ tanna tava yuktam ॥27॥
1 ga. dōhiṁ । 2 sa. ga. vēlli । 3 kha phirikkaṁ ।

kamalasiṭṭikahā ।
277
sāgarō jaṁpara bhāya ! nāsaṁbaddhaṁ payaṁpiyē । vālaggatilatusēṇāvi ēyaṁ bhavai nannā ॥ 29 ॥
hatthamma kaṁkaṇē pattē kajjaṁ kiṁ dappaṇēṇa vā ? | paccāsannēva sā gaṁtī gacchaē bhada ! nicchiyaṁ ॥ 30 ॥
vimalō vēi kiṁ ēvaṁ avalaṁvēsi viṭṭimaṁ । dhidvēṇa saha japatō dhiṭṭhō cēva ahaṁ phuḍaṁ ||31||
japiē sāgarēṇēvaṁ vimalō paricitaē । ginhā mimassa savvassaṁ samaō ēsa vaṭṭaē ||32||
tō para imaṁ sacca jai savrvvapi tō niaṁ । savvaṁ kayāṇagaṁ dēmi, lēmi tē savyamannahā ||33||
ēvaṁ ca dūmiō tēṇaṁ tālaṁ tālāē mēliḍaṁ | sāgarō kamalaṁ sēṭṭhi 'tuma sakkhi' tti bhāsa ||34||
ive kamalō sēṭṭī jai ēsa ajāṇaō । tō ki tumapi, tō bēi vimalō tāya ! saṁpayaṁ ||35||
kiṁ tumha jujjaē ēvaṁ lāghavaṁ maha āṇiuṁ ? । divvanāṇīva jaṁpēra ēsō ēvaṁ palāvirō || 36 ||
sāgarōvi paryaṁpēi kamalaṁ taṇaō tuha । jai pāēsu laggēi, tō haiṁ chōḍēmi hōḍḍuō ||37||
vimalō bhai pāēsa tujjha lagaṁtu kukkurā । niccaṁ bhikkhaṁ bhavaṁtassa savvassē gahiē maē ||38||
sōuṁ ca kamalō ēvaṁ tattō mōṇēṇa saṁṭhiō । ittō a tēhi dōhipi samaṁ caiva turaṁgamā ||39||
vāhiā gaḍḍipiṭṭhīē pattā gaḍḍīvi tēhi sā । gaēhi jōaṇaṁ ēkaṁ itthī tattha na dīsai ॥ 40 ॥
tō tuṭṭō vimalō ēvaṁ savvassaṁ lēmi ciṁtai । sō puṭṭhō. sārahī tēṇa sā itthī kiṁ na dīsa ? ||41 ||
bhaṇiaṁ tēṇa sā bhava ! gubviṇī sūlapīḍiā । pasavatthaṁ gayā ittha vaṇamajjhammi ciṭṭhāī ॥42॥
I
mukhamastīti vaktavyaṁ, yacca taccāpi bāliśāḥ । jalpanti, na jitātmānō viśēṣēṇa bhavādr̥śāḥ ॥ 28 ॥
sāgarau jalpati bhrātaḥ ! nāsaṁbaddhaṁ prajalpitam । vālāgratilatuṣēṇāpyētad bhavati nānyathā ||29||
hastē kaṅkaṇē prāptē kāryaṁ kiṁ darpaṇēna vā ? | pratyāsannaiva sā gantrī gacchati bhadra ! niścitam ||30||
vimalō bravīti kimēvamabalamba sē vr̥ṣṭimānam ? | dhr̥ṣṭēna saha jalpan ghr̥ṣṭa ēvāhaṁ sphuṭam ॥31॥
jalpitē sāgarēṇaivaṁ vimalaḥ paricintayati । gr̥hṇāmyasya sarvasva samaya ēṣa vartatē ॥ 32॥
tatō jalpatīdaṁ satyaṁ yadi sarvamapi tatō nijam । sarva r̥yāṇakaṁ dadyāṁ lāyāṁ tē sarvamanyathā ||33||
ēvaṁ ca dāvitastēna tālāṁ tālayā mēlayitvā । sāgaraḥ kamalaṁ śrēṣṭhinaṁ 'tvaṁ sākṣī' iti bhāṣatē ||34||
jalpati kamalaḥ śrēṣṭhī yadyēṣō'jñāyakaḥ । tataḥ kiṁ tvamapi tatō bravīti vimalastāta ! sāṁpratam ॥35॥
kiṁ tava yujyata ēvaṁ lāghavaṁ mamānētum ? | divyajñānīva jalpatyēṣa ēvaṁ pralapitā ||36||
sāgarō'pi prajalpati kamalaṁ tanayastava । yadi pādayōlagēta, tatō'haṁ muñcāmi paṇataḥ ||37||
vimalō bhaṇati pādayōstava lagantu kukkurāḥ । nityaṁ bhikṣāṁ bhramataḥ sarvasvē gr̥hītē mayā ॥ 38 ॥
śrutvā ca kamala ētat tatō maunēna saṁsthitaḥ । itaśca tābhyāṁ dvābhyāmapi samamēva turaṅgamau ॥39॥
vāhitau mantrīpr̥ṣṭhē prāptā gantryapi tābhyāṁ sā । gatābhyāṁ yōjanamēkaṁ strī tatra na dr̥śyatē ||40||
tatastuṣṭō vimala ētatsarvasvaṁ lāyāṁ cintayati । sa pr̥ṣṭaḥ sārathistēna sā strī kiṁ na dr̥śyatē ? || 41 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ tēna sā bhadra ! gurviṇī śūlapīḍitā । prasavārthaṁ gatā'tra vanamadhyē tiṣṭhati ॥42॥

supāsanāha variammi-
ef paṭṭaṇē saṁti māyāvittāṇi saṁpayaṁ । māyaṁgō pēsiō tattha tāṇa vattānivēaō ||43||
ahaṁ tu bhaṇō bhada ! ēā vaṇimahēliā । maggammi miliā majjha ruṭṭhā bhattāratāḍiā ||44॥
sāma ēkkagāmammi sātri majjha saijjhiā । ēēṇa kāraṇēṇaṁ taṁ muttaṇaṁ jāmi nō ahaṁ ॥ 45||
ittō a khanamittaṇaṁ māyaṁgō lahu āgaō । sāhai, ēi ēīē māyā mujjhēva piō ||46 ||
suhāsaṇasamārūḍhā sāvi pacchā samāgayā । daṁsaē sōvitaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ jattha vālā vilaṁba ||47 ||
pattāi tīi tō tattha sāvi puttaṁ payāyaī । suhāsaṇammi kāūṇa vaṁbhaṇassa nivēḍaṁ ||48 ||
puttajammaṁ, taō jāi paṭṭaṇamma niē gihē । vinnāyaṁ vimalēṇāvi saccē sāgarabhāsiaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
kamalēṇāvi taṁ diṭṭhaṁ pāsaṭṭēṇa jahadviaṁ । nagaraṁ tu samāsannaṁ kāuṁ tē tattha patthi ||50||
arrafai as ca ēē turaṁgamā । kayāṇagaṁpi gēhāō pēsia gihē maha ॥ 51 ॥
vimalō bēi bhō ! tujha uvahāsavayaṁ vayaṁ । jāyā caiva tō bhaṇasu jaṁ kiṁpi paḍihāsa || 52 ||
sāgarō citaē ēsa fast ghiḍō a mannaē । khēḍaṁ hōpi duttuṁḍō, kiṁtu ēassa uttaraṁ ॥ 53 ॥
nadāum̐ para jutta, taō kāūṇa gaṁgēli । sagihē sāgarō pattō piaputā niē gihē ॥ 54 ॥
pacchā kayāṇagaṁ savvaṁ saṁpattaṁ puravāhirē । vimalassa gihē jāva jāi nō tassa saṁtiaṁ ॥ 55 ॥
tāvataṁ āgayaṁ nāuṁ sāgarō sammūhō gaō । paḍhamaṁ ciya gahēūṇa pakkhittaṁ vāḍaē balā || 56 ॥
।
ētasyāḥ pattanē tō mātāpitarau sāṁpratam । mātaṅgaḥ prēṣitastatra tayōrvārtānivēdakaḥ ॥43॥
ahaṁ tu brāhmaṇō bhadra ! ēṣā vaṇigmahēlā । mārgē militā mama ruṣṭā bhartr̥tāḍitā ||44 ||
basāva ēkagrāmē sāpi mama prātivēśmikī । ētēna kāraṇēna tāṁ muktvā yāmi nō aham ||46 ॥
itaśca kṣaṇamātrēṇa mātaṅgō ladhvāgataḥ । kathayati, ētyētasyā mātā mamaiva pr̥ṣṭhataḥ ॥ 46 ॥
sukhāsanasamārūḍhā sāpi paścāt samāgatā । darśayati sō'pi tatsthānaṁ yatra bālā vilambatē ||47 ||
prāptāyāṁ tasyāṁ tatastatra sāpi putraṁ prajāyatē । sukhāsanē kr̥tvā brāhmaṇāya nivēdya ||48 ||
putrajanma, tatō yāti pattanē nijē gr̥hē । vijñātaṁ vimalēnāpi satyaṁ sāgarabhāṣitam ॥49॥
kamalēnāpi tad
dr̥ṣṭaṁ pārśvasthēna yathāsthitam । nagaraṁ tu samāsannaṁ kr̥tvā tau tatra prasthitau ॥50॥
sāgarō vimalaṁ brūtē dvāvapyētau turaṅgamau । krayāṇakamapi gēhāt prēṣayitatryaṁ gr̥hē mama ॥51॥

na dātuṁ paruṣaṁ yuktaṁ, tataḥ kr̥tvōpēkṣām (!) | svagr̥hē sāgaraḥ prāptaḥ pitāputrau nijē gr̥hē ॥ 54 ॥

tasmāttvayā mama sākṣyamājñayā mama tēna saha paṇaḥ । vihitaḥ, atra na bhrāntiḥ tava dhanaṁ sarvamapi tasya ॥ 66 ॥
tēna yathāyad bhaṇitaṁ yasmātsarvaṁ tathaiva nirvartitam । ēkamapi tasya vacanaṁ nānyathā jāta ! saṁjātam ||67 ||

iti śikṣitō vimalō'nala ivānilapūritō jvalitaḥ । trivalītaraṅgabhaṅgurabhālaṁ bhaṇituṁ samārabdhaḥ ॥72॥
adyāpi bhaṇitaṁ na smarasi, āstāṁ bahudivasabhāṣitaṁ tu mayā । garalamiva mukhē madhuraḥ pariṇāmē tvamapi tatsadr̥śaḥ ॥

tataḥ pr̥ṣṭō narapatinā kuśalaṁ tava vimala ! ētāvān kālaḥ । kiṁ lagnastatra gatēnārjitaṁ kiyad dravyam ? ॥76॥

ramaṇī vipayatī nadīsai dhōriyātri asamatthā । tattō sāmatthāō vēllayagatī maē nāyā || 98 ||
jaṁpai rāyā sāgara ! itthatthē atthi kōvi sakkhīvi ? | sō bhaṇai savvabhēyaṁ jāṇai sāmī ! kamala siṭṭī ॥ 99 ॥
bhaṇai nariṁdō 'pucchaha kamala' ti taē purāvi bhaṇiyamiṇaṁ । kiṁtu sa vimalassa piyā tō daviṇaṁ jāi tassamiṇaṁ ।।
tō bhai sāgarō dēva ! ēvamēyaṁ, paraṁ sa savrvvapi । jāṇai ēyaṁ kila dhammiō ya tā sōcciya pamāṇaṁ ॥ 101 ॥
vimalō citai tamahaṁ jai appamāṇaṁ bhaṇēmi tō hōmi । iṇhipi hīṇavāī mōṇēṇaṁ cēva tō ṭhāī ॥ 102 ॥

tara ciṭṭhai vivāō ēsō tō sōma ! tulasamō hōuṁ । niddhārēsu vivāyaṁ puttapasūṇaṁpi samacittō ॥ 104 ॥

muṇiṇō samatiṇamaṇiṇō, tō jai ahamavitahaṁ na jaṁpēmi । tō tēvi maē pāgayajarṇāmma kijjati sakalaṁkā ।।

niyakulaṁ sakalaṁka kuṇai narō kōvi atthalavaluddhō । naranāha ! asaccēṇaṁ visēsaō muṇiyajiṇadhammō ॥

nahi parakajjē kavi hu pāyaṁ jaṁgi sayannaō aliyaṁ । rāgō vā dōsō vā tattha visēsēṇa jaṁ hēū ॥ 109 ॥

ramaṇyā api pādapaṅktirna dr̥śyatē dhuryāvapyasamarthau । tataḥ sāmarthyād vēṣṭaka [ : ] gantrī mayā jñātā ॥98 ॥

tatō bhaṇati sāgarō dēva ! ēvamētat paraṁ sa sarvamapi । jānātyētat kila dhārmikaśca tasmāt sa ēva pramāṇam ॥

tvayi tiṣṭhatē vivāda ēṣa tataḥ sōma ! tulāsamō bhūtvā । nirdhāraya vivādaṁ putra - paśvōrapi samacittaḥ ॥ 104 ॥
tataḥ kamalēna bhaṇitaṁ śr̥ṇōtu dēvaḥ, surēndrakr̥ta sēvaḥ । dēvō mama sarvajñō guravastrailōkyaśirōmaṇayaḥ || 105 ||
munayaḥ samatr̥ṇamaṇayaḥ, tatō yadyahamavitathaṁ na jalpēyam । tatastē'pi mayā prākr̥tajanē kriyēran sakalaṅkāḥ ॥ 106 ॥
nijakulaṁ sakalaṅka karōti naraḥ kō'pyarthalavalubdhaḥ । naranātha ! asatyēna viśēṣatō jñātajinadharmaḥ ॥ 107 ॥
atha putramittrakāryē bhaṇantyalīkamapi tadapi na khalu yuktam । yēna sphuṭaṁ satyasuvarṇasyaiṣa ēva kaṣapaṭṭaḥ ॥ 108॥
nahi parakāryē kō'pi khalu prāyō jalpati sakarṇakō'līkam । rāgō vā dvēṣō vā tatra viśēṣēṇa yad hētuḥ ॥ 109 ॥
sarvē jātā jātāḥ sarvē mitrāṇi cātra saṁsārē । kastēṣu pratibandhaḥ sujñātajinadharmasārāṇām ॥ 110 ॥

ahava jahadviyabhaṇaṇē rūsai puttō viraccaī sayaṇō । ēvaṁpi hōu tahavi hu asacauccāraṇamajuttaṁ ॥ 111 ॥
yataḥ:-
rūsa vā parō mā vā visaṁ vā pariyattau । bhāsiya sayā sacca savvēsiṁ hiyakāraṇaṁ ॥ 112||
hamahurāī pariṇaivirasāī na sajjaṇā payapaṁti । kiṁtu pariṇaisuhāī muhakaḍuyāīpi vayaṇāī | | 113 ||
kēśca ।
yamēva muṇa dēvō jō jārisaō tahāvi mēṁ ēyaṁ । pucchara jahaṭṭhiyaṁ, tā sāgarabhaṇiya iha pamāṇaṁ ॥ 114॥
ya bhaṇiē tō rannā harisabharugbhinnavahalapulaēṇaṁ । niyakaṁṭakaṁdalāō takkaṁṭhē ṭhāviō hārō ॥ 115 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ puṇō puṇō taha ahō ahō purisavaggasirarayaṇaṁ । dhaṇataṇayahāṇimagaṇiya jēṇēvaṁ avitahaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
ajjavi rayaṇādhārā dharaṇī ajjavi na ēi kalikālō । dīsaṁti jēṇa ēvaṁvihāī varapurisarayaṇāī ।। 117 ॥
kālē varisaṁti ghaṇā kusumati vaṇassaīu jaṁ kālē । huti tiṇāivi duddhaṁ taṁ savvaṁ saccamāhappaṁ ॥ 118 ॥
jaṁ gacakaṁpi nahē rahēi jamilā na jāi pāyālaṁ । tamahaṁ mannē savvaṁ māhappaṁ saccasaṁghāṇaṁ ॥ 119 ॥
tā savvahāva ēsō kamalō siṭṭhī visiṭṭajaṇa jihō । iya bhaṇiuṁ kaṇayamayaṁ siripa ṭhāvaē bhālē ॥ 120 ॥
bhaṇiō vimalō majjhavi puraō tuha aliyavayaṇapauṇassa । juttō jīhāchēō lajjijjara kiṁtu sēṭṭhissa ।।
sāgara gahiyassa kayāṇagassa nāmapi puṇa na vittavyaṁ । sirikamala siṭṭicariēṇa raṁjiō sōvi pabhaṇēi ॥
savvapi samapissaṁ tamahaṁ naranāha ! kamalasiṭṭhissa । kiṁ ūṇaṁ maha tai sāmiyammi pūrissara jamimō ||
rāyā sāgaramavihavaraṁjiō sayalamaṁtivaggassa । ṭhāvēi taṁ pahuttē viviha kāūṇa sammāṇaṁ ॥ 124 ॥
athavā yathāsthitabhaṇanē ruṣyati putrō virajyatē svajanaḥ । ēvamapi bhavatu tathāpyasatyōccāraṇamayuktam ॥ 111 ॥
ruṣyatu vā parō mā vā viṣaṁ vā parivartatām । bhāṣitavyaṁ sadā satyaṁ sarvēṣāṁ hitakāraṇam ॥ 112 ॥
mukhamadhurāṇi pariṇativirasāni na sajjanāḥ prajalpanti । kintu pariṇati sukhāni mukhakaṭukānyapi vacanāni ॥
svayamēva jānāti dēvō yō yādr̥śastathāpi māmētam । pr̥cchati yathāsthitaṁ, tataḥ sāgarabhaṇitamiha pramāṇam ॥
iti bhaṇitē tatō rājñā harṣabharōnnivahalapulakēna । nijakaṇṭhakandalāt tatkaṇḍē sthāpitō hāraḥ ॥ 115 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ punaḥ punastathā ahō ahō puruṣavargaśirōratnam । dhanatanaya hānimagaṇayitvā yēnaivamavitathaṁ bhaṇitam ।।
adyāpi ratnādhārā dharaṇiradyāpi naiti kalikālaḥ । dr̥śyantē yēnaivaṁvidhāni varapuruṣaratnāni ॥ 117 ॥
kālē varṣanti ghanāḥ kusumayanti vanaspatayō yatkālē । bhavanti tr̥ṇānyapi dugdhaṁ tatsarvaṁ satyamāhātmyam ॥ 118 ॥
yad grahacakramapi nabhasi tiṣṭhati yadilā na yāti pātālam । tadahaṁ manyē sarva māhātmyaṁ satyasaṁdhānām ॥ 119॥
tasmāt sarvathāpyēṣa kamalaḥ śrēṣṭhī viśiṣṭajanajyēṣṭhaḥ । iti bhaṇitvā kanakamayaṁ śrīpaṭṭē sthāpayati bhālē ॥120॥
bhaṇilō vimalō mamāpi puratastavālīkavacanapraguṇasya । yuktō jihvācchēdō lajjyatē kintu śrēṣṭhinaḥ ॥121॥
sāgaragr̥hītasya krayāṇakasya nāmāpi punarna grahītavyam । śrīkamala śrēṣṭhicaritēna rañjitaḥ sō'pi prabhaṇati ॥ 122॥
sarvamapi samarpayiṣyāmi tadahaṁ naranātha ! kamalaśrēṣṭhinē । kimūnaṁ mama tvāyē svāmini pūrayiṣyati yadayam ॥ 123 ॥

abhakkhāṇaṁ sahasā hāsēṇavi jō parassa uvaṇēi । bhavaṇavaḍāyā iva parabhavammi sō lahai taṁ caiva ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi ; -
asthi kaṁcaṇapurī jā sōmā jaccakacaṇamaēhiṁ । jiṇabhavaṇēhi laṁkāpuraṁpi savibhīsaṇaṁ hasai ||2||

taṁ dadrūṇaṁ dēvī paḍibuddhā sāhaē nariṁdassa । sōvi duhiyāē jammaṁ kahēi sumiṇāṇusārēṇa ||7||
tō saṁbhū gabhē dēvīē para maharisasaṁjaṇaē । ganbhāṇubhāvaucciya jāō ii dōhalō samaē ॥ 8 ॥
jaha ja aṇāhadīgaṁdhakiviṇakaṣpaḍiyavahirapabhiīṇa । ditī pauraṁ dāṇaṁ vaccāmi jidigēhē ||9||

abhyākhyānaṁ sahasā hāsyēnāpi yaḥ parasyōpanayati । bhavanapatākēva parabhavē sa labhatē tadēva ॥1॥
ihāsti kāñcanapurī yā sōmā jātyakāñcanamayaiḥ । jinabhavanairlaṅkāpuramapi savibhīṣaṇaṁ hasati ॥2॥
tatrāsti siddharājō rājā ripucakramākramya । gr̥hītā yēna saha śrīyaśōbhyāṁ samarēṣu jayalakṣmīḥ ॥ 3 ॥

tāṁ dr̥ṣṭvā dēvī pratibuddhā kathayati narēndrāya । sōpi duhiturjanma kathayati svapnānusārēṇa ||7||

yathā yatyanāthadīnāndhakr̥paṇakāpaṭikabadhiraprabhr̥tibhyaḥ । dadatī pracuraṁ dānaṁ vrajāmi jinēndra gēhēṣu ॥9॥
jinabimbānāṁ pūjāṁ karōmyatyantaparamabhaktyā । sādhubhyō bhaktapānaṁ dadāmi varaṁ prāsukaiṣaṇīyam ॥10॥
dōhadamimaṁ dēvī nivēdayati naravarāya, rājāpi । parituṣṭamanāḥ śīghramapi sādhayati tattathā sarvam ॥ 11 ॥

tyāhārihiṁ pavarihiṁ gurugaurakhu karai, sō avasi suralōyaha sāmittaṇu dharai ||21||
sīlālaṁkiyasāviyahaṁ varapaḍivatti karēi ju ihabhavi ।

atha paripūrṇadinēṣu praśastatithir̥kṣakaraṇayōgē । supraśastē muhūrtē sukhēna sā prasūtā duhitaram ||26||
udyōtayantīṁ kāntyā sūtibhavanaṁ nabhaḥ pradēśamiva । navaśaśikalāmiva saṁjanitasakalajananayanānandām ॥ 27॥

ittō ya rayaṇamālāē āgaō jaṇayabhavaṇaō cēḍō । vayaṇakusalutti jāō kīlaṭhāṇaṁ naravaissa ||34||

sīmāgāmē luṁṭa, siddhanariṁdōvi taṁ samatthōtri । navi viggahai na saṁdha, tō sō citai na laṭṭhamimaṁ ॥ 36 ॥
tō jaggavēmi ēyaṁti citiūṇaṁ vasaṁtariusamaē । sahasā tassāgamasāvaṇēṇa sē saṁbhamanimittaṁ ||37||
āgaṁtu naranāhaṁ vinnavai sasaṁbhramaṁ jahujjāṇē । cauraṁgavalasamēō vasaṁtarāō samaṇupattō ॥ 38 ॥
taṁ sahasā sōūṇaṁ jaṁvara rē pēkkharēha varaturaē । gum̐ḍaha gaīdē pauṇīkarēha rahacakkapāikkē ||39||
tattō sēṇāvaṇā sasaṁbhramaṁ karituraṁgarahamāī । vihiyaṁ āhavasajjaṁ bhērī tāḍāviyā turiyaṁ ॥ 40 ॥
tassadasavaṇaucchaliyavahalapulayāṇa sinnasuhaḍāṇa | pattaparamūsavāṇava vivihā vahati vāvarā ॥41॥
vagaṁtiya kudaṁtiya naccaṁti karaṁti taha karapphōḍaṁ । paccāraṁti parōpparamudadhurakhaṁdhā paribhamaṁti ||42 ||
aha tēhi bhaḍēhiṁ samaṁ caliō rāyā kamēṇa pattō ya । ujjāṇē tattha ya sattusinnamaniyaṁtaō bhai ||
ujjāṇa pālayaṁ bhō ! kattha gayaṁ taṁ vasaṁtariusinnaṁ ? । sō bhaṇai dēva ! puraō ṭhiyapi taṁ kiṁ na picchēsi ||
tō puṇaravi harisavisāyasaṁkulēṇaṁ nitrēṇa sō puṭṭō । sāhai vasaṁtariuṇō cauraṁgavalaṁ imō ēvaṁ ॥ 45 ॥
aisaralamaṁjarītikkhabhallinimma hiyavira hijaṇahiyayā । sahayārā varajōhā dalavaya sannāhaduddharisa।।। 46 ।।
duddharaturaṁgathaṭṭā iō taō bhamiraparahuya nikāyā । kalakūiya hēsārakhamuhariyanīsēsadisikkā ||47 ||
vyākaraṇacchandō 'laṅkāratarka siddhānta jyautiṣādīni । catuḥṣaṣṭivijñānāni śikṣatē stōkadivasaiḥ ॥ 33॥
itaśca ratnamālāyā āgatō janakabhavanataścēṭaḥ । vacanakuśala iti jātaḥ krīḍāsthānaṁ narapatēḥ || 34॥
udyānapālakatvē sa ca niyuktō vasundharāpatinā । tasya ca rājñaḥ śatrurvasantarājō'tipracaṇḍaḥ ||35||
sīmagrāmôlluṇṭatē, siddhanarēndrō'pi taṁ samarthō'pi । nāpi vigr̥hṇītē na saṁdadhāti, tataḥ sa cintayati na ramyamidam।।
tatō jāgarayāmyētamiti cintayitvā vasantartusamayē । sahasā tasyāgamaśrāvaṇēna tasya saṁbhramanimittam ||37||
āgatya naranāthaṁ vijñapayati sasaṁbhramaṁ yathōdyānē । caturaṅgabalasamētō vasantarājaḥ samanuprāptaḥ ॥ 38 ॥
tat sahasā śrutvā jalpati sē saṁnāhayata varaturagān । guḍata gajēndrān praguṇīkuruta rathacakrapadātīn ||39||
tataḥ sēnāpatinā sasaṁbhramaṁ karituraṅgarathādi । vihitamāhavasajjaṁ bhērī tāḍitā tvaritam ॥40॥
tacchabdaśravaṇācchalitabahalapulakānāṁ sainyasubhaṭānām । prāptaparamōtsavānāmiva vividhā vartantē vyāpāraḥ ॥ 41 ॥
valganti ca kūrdantē ca nr̥tyanti kurvanti tathā karāsphōṭam । upālabhantē parasparamuddharaskandhāḥ paribhramanti ॥
atha tairbhaṭaiḥ samaṁ calitō rājā kramēṇa prāptaśca । udyānē tatra ca śatrusainyamapaśyan bhaṇati ||43||
udyānapālakaṁ bhōḥ kva gataṁ tadvasantaripusainyam ? । sa bhaṇati dēva ! purataḥ sthitamapi tatkiṁ na paśyasi ॥44॥
tataḥ punarapi harṣaviṣādasaṁkulēna nr̥pēṇa sa pr̥ṣṭaḥ । kathayati vasantataścaturaṅgabalamidamēvam ॥45॥
atisaralamañjarītīkṣṇabhallinirmathitavirahi janahr̥dayāḥ । sahakārā varayōdhā dalanajasaṁnāhadurdharṣāḥ || 46 ॥
1 ga. parikarēhi । 2 ma. suhaga ।

gayavaśvāmāṇa araikāriṇō malayamāruyā kariṇō । caṁdaṇaṁgaṁdhasugaṁdhiyavēlāsīyaramayasaṇāhā ||48 ॥
pahiyahiyayāṇa ditā dukkhāī dōlayā rahappavarā । dōlaṁdōlirasussararamaṇīyaṇasārahisaṇāhā ||49||
aha tavvayaṇaparisadakkhatta akhōhabhattisattīhi । raṁjiyahiyaō sammāṇiūṇa sēṇāvaittammi ॥50॥
taṁ ṭhāviūṇa pēsai cauraṁgavalēṇa parigayaṁ rāyā । rāyaṁ vasaṁtarāyaṁ viggahiuṁ viggahasamatthaṁ ||21||
mahulacchīvicchaḍuṁ picchai aha naravaīvi ujjāṇē । saṁtēurō sanayarō samaṁḍaliō samatiyaṇō ॥ 52 ॥
bhavaṇapaḍāyāvi tahā rāyādēsēṇa tattha saṁpattā । niyasahiyaṇapariyariyā ujjāṇē jaṇamaṇāṇaṁdē ॥53॥
jariyaṁva jaraṁ maccuṁ mayaṁva vāhīu bāhiyāunna । mannatō nicitō vilasai ēvaṁ tahiṁ lōō || 54 ||
gāyati kēi naccati kē kīlati kēi taruṇīhi । mahilāō cacarīō sunaccirīō payati ॥55॥
iṁdōvva parigaō accharāhi aurīhi saha rāyā । vimhāviṁtō jaṇamāṇasāīṁ kīlai aṇēgavihaṁ ॥ 56 ॥
bhramai ramaī jahicchē picchaṁtī vacchalacchivicchaṅkaṁ । bhavaṇapaḍāyā kumarīvi cēḍiyāvēḍhiyā tattha ||57॥
surasariyāpulisa ya parisappaṁtīē tīē payapaṁtī । saccaviyā cakkissava cakkakusakamalalaṁkariyā ॥ 58 ॥
taṁ aggaō samaggē maggē maggaṁtiyā vayai jāva । parivārē vārēuṁ tā rairamaṇēṇa sāricchaṁ || 59 ||
picchā purisaṁ ēkkaṁ avahiyahiyayā ya tēṇa taṁ bhaṇai । bhayavaṁ ! mayaṇa ! namō tē pūēmi tumati bhaṇiūṇa ||
niyakaṁṭhakaṁdalāō uttārēṇa tassa kaṁṭhammi । muttāhāraṁ nikkhivai jāva tā pabhaṇaē sōvi ॥ 61 ॥
dudhaturaṅgaghaṭā itastatō bhramitr̥parabhr̥tanikāyāḥ । kalakūjitahēṣārava mukharitaniḥ śēṣadikcakrāḥ ॥47॥
gatapativāmānāmaratikāriṇō malayamārutāḥ kariṇaḥ । candanagandhasugandhitavēlāsī karamadasanāthāḥ ||18||
pathikahr̥dayānāṁ dadatō duḥkhāni dōlā rathapravarāḥ । dōlāndōlitr̥susvararamaṇījanasārathisanāthāḥ ॥ 49 ॥
atha tadvacanaprakarṣadakṣatvākṣōbhabhaktiśaktibhiḥ । rañjitahr̥dayaḥ sammānya sēnāpatitvē ॥50॥
taṁ sthāpayitvā prēpayati caturaṅgabalēna parigataṁ rājā । rājānaṁ vasantarājaṁ vigrahītuṁ vigrahasamartham ॥51॥
madhulakṣmīvistāraṁ paśyatyatha narapatirapyudyānē । sāntaḥpuraḥ sanagarō samaṇḍalikaḥ samantrijanaḥ ॥52॥
bhavanapatākāpi tathā rājādēśēna tatra saṁprāptā । nijasakhījanaparikaritōdyānē janamanaānandē ॥ 53 ॥
jvaritāmiva jarāṁ mr̥tyuṁ mr̥tamiva vyādhīn bādhitāniva । manyamānō niścintō vilasatyēvaṁ tatra lōkaḥ ॥ 54 ॥
gāyanti kēcinnr̥tyanti kē citkrīḍanti kēcittaruṇībhiḥ । mahilāścarcarī ḥ sunartanyaḥ pravartayanti ॥55॥
indra iva parigatō'psarōbhirāntaḥ purībhiḥ saha rājā । vismāyayañjanamānasāni krīḍatyanēkavidham ॥56॥
bhramati ramatē yathēcchaṁ paśyantī vr̥kṣalakṣmīvistāram । bhavanapatākā kumāryapi cēṭikāvēṣṭitā tatra ॥57॥
surasaritpulinēṣu ca parisarpantyā tayā pādapaṅkiḥ । dr̥ṣṭā cakriṇa iva cakrāṅkuśakamalālaṁkr̥tā ॥58॥
tamagrataḥ samagrē mārgē mārgayantī vrajati yāvat । parivāraṁ vārayitvā tāvad ratiramaṇēna sadr̥kṣam ॥59॥
paśyati puruṣamēkamavahita hr̥dayā ca tēna taṁ bhaṇati । bhagavan ! madana ! namastē pūjayāmi tvāmiti bhaṇitvā ॥ 60 ॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
nāhaṁ mayaṇō muddhē ! sā bhaṇai majjha mayaṇajaṇaṁō taṁ । tā kiṁ bahuṇā, hārō tuha varamālāē mai khittō ||
kiṁpuṇa thōvadihi hōhī vīṇāsayaṁvarō majjha । niyadaṁsaṇāmaēṇaṁ tatthāgaṁtuṁ tara suhaya ! ||63 ||
nivvaviyavtrāī maha lōyaṇāī niyavirahajalaṇataviyāī । hiyaē taē saṇā hē īsāē vinaḍiyāīva || 64 ||
iccāi jāva jaṁpai tēṇa samaṁ tāva kamalanāmāē । niyadāsīē nivapēsiyāē hakkāriyā valiyā ||65||
pattā ya nivasayāsē taccaraṇē paṇamiūṇa uvaviṭṭhā | puṭṭhā piuṇā vacchē ! kattha ṭhiyā ēttiyaṁ vāraṁ ? ॥ 66 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ tīē vaṇarāirēhiraṁ varabhaḍaṁva ujjāṇaṁ । avalōyaṁtī taha cēva, aha nivō bhaṇai tayabhimuhaṁ ॥ 67॥
vacchē ! kamaladalacchē ! pēcchāṇīyāṇi rāyakumarāṇa । ruvāī paṭṭiyāsuṁ cittayarēhiṁ 'vilihiūṇa ||68॥
jassa ya kassavirūvaṁ paḍihāsai tujjha taṁ maha kahēhi । aṁgīkarēmi taṁ caiva jēṇa jāmāuyattēṇa ॥ 69॥
cittakalā niuṇāē tō tīi nirikkhiūṇa ruvāī | jō jassa guṇō dōsō sō kahiō tāṇa paccakrasaṁ ॥ 70 ॥
jō ēttha paṭṭiyāē lihiō kumarō sa rōsadōsillō । diṭṭhīē mē nāō, annēsiṁpi hu guṇē dōsē ||71 |
jā ēvaṁ sā paḍai tō rāyavāriyā tahiṁ sacvē । guṇadōsavibhāgannū savvēsi tēsiṁ kumarāṇa || 72॥
nihuyaṁ bhāṁti annōnnamaisaō kōī rāyaputtīē । kōsallaṁpi kalāsuṁ, kahannahā jāṇaē ēvaṁ 1 || 73 ||
kumarīvi tahā kahiuṁ vinnavai narēsaraṁ jahā tāya ! | lēhayavēgunnāō cittāī huṁti cittāī ||74 ||
majjhavi atthi pannā vīṇāē raṁjihī maṇa jō mē । sō pariṇēhī, tamhā divasē nirr̥kiyammi taō ।।75।
nijakaṇṭhakandalāduttārya tasya kaṇṭhē | muktāhāraṁ nikṣipati yāvattāvat prabhaṇati sō'pi ॥ 61 ॥
nāhaṁ madanō mugdhē ! sā bhaṇati mama madanajanakastvam । tasmātkiṁ bahunā, hārastava varamālāyāṁ mayā kṣiptaḥ ॥
kintu stōkadinairbhaviṣyati vīṇāsvayaṁvarō mama । nijadarśanāmr̥tēna tatrāgatya tvayā subhaga ! ॥ 63 ॥
nirvāpayitavyē mama lōcanē nijavirahajvalanataptē | hr̥dayē tvayā sanāthē īrṣyayā vinaṭi iva ॥ 64 ॥
ityādi yāvajjalpati tēna samaṁ tāvatkamalānāmnyā । nijadāsyā nr̥paprēṣitayā hakkāritā valitā ॥ 65 ॥
prāptā ca nr̥pasakāśē taccaraṇau praṇamyōpaviṣṭā । pr̥ṣṭā pitrā vatsē ! kva sthita tāvantaṁ vāram ? || 66 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ tathā vana (vraṇa) rājirājamānaṁ varabhaṭamivōdyānam । avalōkamānā tathaiva, atha nr̥pō bhaṇati tadabhimukham ।
vatsē ! kamaladalākṣi ! paśyānītāni rājakumārāṇām । rūpāṇi paṭṭikāsu citrakarairvilikhya ॥ 68 ॥
yasya ca kasyāpi rūpaṁ pratibhāsatēṁ tava tanmama kathaya । aṅgīkarōmi tamēva yēna jāmātr̥tvēna ॥69॥
citrakalānipuṇayā tatastayā nirīkṣya rūpāṇi । yō yasya guṇō dōṣaḥ sa kathitastēṣāṁ pratyakṣam ॥70॥
yō'tra paṭṭikāyāṁ likhitaḥ kumāraḥ sa rōṣadōṣitaḥ । dr̥ṣṭyā mayā jñātō, anyēṣāmapi khalu guṇān dōṣān ॥ 71 ॥
yāvadēvaṁ sā prakaṭayati tatō rājadauvārikāstatra sarvē । guṇadōṣavibhāgajñāḥ sarvēṣāṁ tēṣāṁ kumārāṇām ॥ 72 ॥
nibhr̥taṁ bhaṇantyanyōnyamatiśayaḥ kō'pi rājaputryāḥ । kauśalamapi kalāsu, kathamanyathā jānātyēvam ? ॥73 ||
kumāryapi tathā kathayitvā vijñapayati narēśvaraṁ yathā tāta ! । lēkhaka vaiguṇyāccitrāṇi bhavanti citrāṇi ॥74॥

ēē anēvi ya iṁti khattiyā jaha tahā kuṇau tāō । tō māsadugassaṁtō vīṇāē sayaṁvaraṁ kahium̐ || 76 ॥
tē cittayarā rannā visajjiyā jāva tāva halavōlō । nisuō rannā, tajjāṇaṇatthamāisai paḍihāraṁ ||77 ||
sō turiyaṁ gaṁtūṇaṁ samāgaō kahai dēva ! aimattō । raṇarāyakarī ummūliūṇa ālāṇagurukhaṁbhaṁ ||78 ||
bhajatō gurubhavaṇāvaṇāī didaimattha paōlidārāī | cūraṁtō tūṁraṁtō rahaturayakharāiyaṁ ēi ॥ 79 ॥
pahu ! karipasu saṁkalāṇa vittharō kuṁḍalīkaō sahai । naṁ tabbhārakkatō tassavi saraṇāgaō sēsō ॥ 80 ॥
ēvaṁ jāva kaī paḍihārō karivarassarūvaṁ tu । tātra sahasā tarhi sō pattō ujjāṇabhavaṇam ||81||
taṁ daṇaṁ rāyā sasaṁbhramubhaṁtamāṇasō turiyaṁ । maṁtimahāyaṇajuttō caḍiō dhavalaharauvarimpi ||82 ॥
bhagāō caccarīō naṭṭō lōōvi kōvi katthavi ya । tumulakhaṁ sōūṇaṁ sōvi kumārō tarhi pattō ॥ 83॥
kumarī puṇa kumarēṇaṁ hayahiyayā tammi nisiyaniyadiṭṭhī । tatthēva ṭhiyā tattō pattā mattēṇa sā kariṇā ॥ 84 ॥
aha kumarēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ dē saṁtariēṇa hakkiō hatthī । haṇiō ya muṭṭiṇā niṭṭurēṇa tō vāliyaṁ mōtu ॥85॥
tassābhimuṁha caliō uḍḍhakarō gaḍabaḍaṁ pakuvvatō । kumarapahāravihurō surakariṇaṁ sadayaṁtōvva ॥ 86 ॥
tō kumarēṇa valiūṇa dāhiṇāvattaṇēṇa bhamiūṇa | ujjāṇabhavaṇadārammi nīṇiō sō mahāhatthī ॥ 87॥
aha jāvakarī kumaraṁ karēṇa kira gihihī samāsanaṁ । tāva kumarēṇa khittā tappuraō vatthaviṁṭaliyā ॥ 88॥
tāhē guru amarisajāyarattanittēṇa tēṇa varakariṇā । tīē viṭaliyāē dinō vēhō sarōsēṇa ॥ 89 ॥
mamāpyasti pratijñā vīṇayā rakṣyatē manō yō mē । sa pariṇēṣyati, tasmāddivasē niṣṭaṅkitē tataḥ ॥75॥
ētē'nyē'pi cāyanti kṣatriyā yathā tathā karōtu tātaḥ । tatō māsadvikasyāntō vīṇāyāḥ svayaṁvaraṁ kathayitvā ॥
tē citrakarā rājñā visarjitā yāvattāvat kalakalaḥ । śrutō rājñā, tajjñānārthamādiśati pratihāram ||77 ||
sa tvaritaṁ gatvā samāgataḥ kathayati dēva ! atimattaḥ । raṇarājakarī unmūlyālāna gurustambham ॥ 78 ॥
bhañjan gurubhavanāpaṇāni dr̥ḍhamatra pratōlidvārāṇi । cūrayaṁstvarayan rathaturagakharādikamēti ॥ 79 ॥
prabhō ! karipādēṣu śr̥ṅkhalānāṁ vistaraḥ kuṇḍalīkr̥tō rājatē । nanu tadbhārākrāntastasyaiva śaraṇāgataḥ śēṣaḥ ॥ 80 ॥
ēvaṁ yāvatkathayati pratihāraḥ karivarasvarūpaṁ tu । tāvat sahasā tatra sa prāpta udyānabhavanē ॥ 81 ॥
taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā rājā sasaṁbhramadrāntamānasastvaritam । mantrimahājana yuktaśvaṭitō dhavalagr̥hōpari ॥82॥
bhagnāścaryō naṣṭō lōkō'pi kō'pi kvāpi ca । tumularavaṁ śrutvā sō'pi kumārastatra prāptaḥ ||83 ॥
kumārī punaḥ kumārēṇa hr̥tahr̥dayā tasmin nyastanijadr̥ṣṭiḥ । tathaiva sthitā tataḥ prāptā mattēna sā kariṇā ॥ 84 ॥
atha kumārēṇa tēna dēśāntaritēna niṣiddhō hastī । hataśca muṣṭinā niṣṭhurēṇa tatō bālikāṁ muktvā ॥ 85॥
tasyābhimukhaṁ calita ūrdhvakarō gaḍagaḍaṁ prakurvan । kumāraprahāravidhuraḥ surakariṇaṁ śabdayanniva ॥ 86 ॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa valitvā dakṣiṇāvartanēna bhramayitvā । udyānabhavanadvārē nītaḥ sa mahāhastī || 87॥
atha yāvatkarī kumāraṁ karēṇa kila grahīṣyati samāsannam । tāvatkumārēṇa kṣiptaṁ tatpuratō vastraṁ vartulīkr̥tam ॥ 88 ॥

rakkhaha rakkhaha ēvaṁ nararayaṇaṁ naravarē iyaṁ bhaṇaṁtē । jīviyaniravikkhā jhati dhāiyā sañcaō suhaḍā ||90 ॥
tāhē bhavaṇapāyā ciṁtā hā hā ! sa ēsa subhagavaśē । majjha kaē saṁjāō guruvaibhāyaṇaṁ ēvaṁ ॥91॥
ittō ya jhatti kumarō tassa gaiṁdassa daṁtamusalēsu | ṭhaviḍaṁ niyacaraṇajuyaṁ ārūḍhō saṁghasamma ||12||
tēṇa ya mahāvalēṇaṁ ūrūhi bhīḍiō karī kaṁṭhē । taha jaha khuḍaṁti nayaṇāī tassa, tō sō karī bhīō ॥ 93॥
saṁjāō tassa basē, tō kumarī citaē arē hiyaya ! । naccasu maṇōrahāṇaṁ agōyaraṁ varamimaṁ laddhaṁ ॥ 94 ॥
rūvēṇa dujjaē raivaisma sōṁḍīrimāē kaṇhassa । ēyammi varē mannasu bhuvaṇammi kayatthamappāṇaṁ ॥ 95||
ēkkasaraṁ ca pukkārapuvvayaṁ bhaṇai savvalōōvi । purisarayaṇēṇa imiṇā rayaṇāhārā phuḍaṁ dharaṇī ॥ 96 ॥
rāyā ya paṁcavallahasāhaṇiyaṁ bhaṇai bhaṇaha maha vayaṇā । suhaḍamimaṁ ālāṇakkhaṁbhē jaha nēi gayamēyaṁ ॥97॥
uttariyaṁ ca gayāō ēyaṁ ārōviḍaṁ varaturaṁgē | āṇēha majjha pāsē tō sō gaṁtuṁ bhaṇai kumaraṁ ॥ 98 ॥
aha sō kumarō hatthiṁ khaṁbhē aggaliya jhatti uttariḍaṁ । muhaguliyāparivattiyarūvō tattō avakkatō ॥ 99 ॥
sāhaṇiō tamadarddha tatyannatthaṁ gavēsiḍaṁ suciraṁ । vinnavai jahāvittaṁ naravaiṇō, sō ya ciṁtēi ॥ 100 ॥
kiṁ ēsa kō aṁjaṇasiddhō vijjāharōvva uvayāraṁ । iya kāmavakkatō suyaṇō saccavai vayaṇamiṇaṁ || 10 ||
suyaṇaha suyaṇihi uvayariṅa, jittiu sāyaranīru । paḍiuvayāraha namaṇa gaya laṁghitra paratīru ॥ 102 ॥
kannā puṇa niyacittē sudiṭṭhā jaṁpēi tāya ! tē kumarā । hakkārijaṁtu lahu vīṇāsālā ya sajjiyau || 103 ॥
I
tadā gurvamarṣajātaraktanētrēṇa tēna varakariṇā । tasmin vartulavastrē dattō vēdhaḥ sarōṣēṇa ॥ 89 ॥
rakṣata rakṣataitad nararatnaṁ naravara iti bhaṇati । jīvitanirapēkṣā jhaṭiti dhāvitāḥ sarvataḥ subhaṭāḥ ॥90॥
tadā bhavanapatākā cintayati hā hā ! sa ēva subhagavaraḥ । mama kr̥tē saṁjātō gurvādbhājanamēvam ॥91॥
itaśca jhaṭiti kumārastasya gajēndrasya dantamuśalayōḥ । sthāpayitvā nijacaraṇayugamārūḍhaḥ skandhadēśē ॥ 92 ॥
tēna ca mahābalēnōrubhyāṁ pīḍitaḥ karī kaṇṭhē । tathā yathā tuḍatō nayanē tasya, tataḥ sa karī bhītaḥ ॥ 93 ॥
saṁjātastasya vaśē, tataḥ kumārī cintayatyarē hr̥daya ! | nr̥tya manōrathānāmagōcaraṁ varamimaṁ vā ॥94॥
rūpēṇa durjayē ratipatēḥ śaiauṇḍīrimṇā kr̥ṣṇasya । ētasmin barē manyasva bhuvanē kr̥tārthamātmānam ॥95॥
ēkasvaraṁ ca pūtkārapūrvakaṁ bhaṇati sarvalōkō'pi । puruṣaratnēnānēna ratnādhārā sphuṭaṁ dharaṇī ॥ 96 ॥
rājā ca pañcavallabhasādhanikaṁ bhaṇati bhaṇata mama vacanāt । subhaṭamimamālānastambhē yathā nayati gajamētam । 97 ।
uttīrṇa ca gajādanamārōpya varatura । ānayata mama pārśvē tataḥ sa gatvā bhaṇati kumāram ॥98॥
atha sa kumārō hastinaṁ stambhē'rgalayitvā jhaṭityuttīrya । mukhaguṭikāparivartitarūpastatō'pakrāntaḥ ॥ 99 ॥
sādhanikastamadr̥ṣṭvā tatrānyatra gavēṣayitvā suciram । vijñapayati yathāvr̥ttaṁ narapatayē, sa ca cintayati ॥ 100 ॥
kimēṣa kō'pyañjanasiddhō vidyāharō vōpakāram । iti kr̥tvāpakrāntaḥ, sujana : satyāpayati vacanamidam ॥ 101 ॥
- sujanasya sujanairupakr̥taṁ yāvat sāgaranīram । pratyupakārē naṣṭamanasō gatā laṅghitvā paratīram ॥ 102 ॥
kanyā punarnijacittē sudr̥ḍhā jalpati tāta ! tē kumārāḥ । hakkāryantāṁ laghu vīṇāśālā ca sajjyatām ॥ 103 ॥

bhavaṇapaḍāyākahā ।
૨૩
rāyā pabhaṇai ēvaṁ kijjau, kijjau kimannamiha bacchē || navaraṁ uciō tuha pāṇadāyagō sōciya na annō ॥
bhavapāyā paḍū mā khēyaṁ kuṇaha tāya ! iha visaē । bhaviyanvayāvasāō vihaḍaṁti ghaḍaṁti kajjāī ||
aha annadiṇē yāmaṁtiyapattēhiṁ rāyaputtēhiṁ । vīṇāsālāi gaō rāyā- aṁḍarasamēō || 106 ॥
tō savvē nivakumarā jahārihaṁ āsaṇēsu uvaviṭṭā | niyaniyaparivārajyā, miliō annōvi tattha jaṇō ||
rūvaṁtaraṁ karē sō kumarō tattha raṁgabhūmīē | vāyaṁtō varamurayaṁ kaṁṭhanihittaṇa hārēṇa ॥ 108 ॥
jā citā diṭṭhā āgacchaṁtī sahīyaṇasamēyā । bhavaṇavaḍāyā dāsīhiṁ parigayā baṁdhuragaīē || 109 ॥
katham ।
sarayachaṇacaṁda araviṁdaruṁdāṇaṇā, kamaladalasaralasusalūṇavaralōyaṇā ।
aharadalavijiyaaisarasarvivīphalā, dasaṇakaraniyarasaṁphusiyadisimuhamalā ||110 ॥
laḍahala yaṇṇajalajala hilaharīgamā, mayaṇakōyaṁḍa aikuḍilabhūcaṁgimā ।
bhaggasagaṁgaṇā aṁgasōhaggiyā, taruṇajaṇajaṇiyaduvvisahamayaṇaggiyā ॥ 111 ॥
aha kumarī dhāī sahāgayā aṁjali sirē kāuṁ । iya vinnavara kumārē, mahāpasāyaṁ karēūṇa ॥ 112 ॥
vīṇāē viṇōēṇa aṇurahaṁ kuṇaha rāyaputtīē । vīṇaṁ vittr̥ṇa imaṁ jahōvavēsakamēṇēva ॥ 113 ॥
iya bhaṇiūṇa samappara ḍāhālanarēsarassa sā vīṇaṁ । nēunēṇaṁ kumarīē suttiyaṁ rayaṇacicaiyaṁ ॥ 114 ॥
aha vāiya khaṇamēgaṁ ēvaṁ anēvi naravarakumārā । niyasattīē tavvāyaṇammi payati vinnāṇaṁ || 195॥
1
rājā praṇatyēvaṁ kriyatām, kriyatāṁ kimanyadiha vatsē ! | navaramucitastava prāṇadāyakaḥ sa ēva nānyaḥ ॥ 104॥
bhavanapatākā jalpati mā khēdaṁ kuruta tāta ! iha viṣayē । bhavitavyatāvaśād vighaṭantē ghaṭatē kāryāṇi ॥ 105 ॥
athānyadinē dūtāmantritaprāpta rājaputraiḥ । vīṇāśālāyāṁ gatō rājā'ntaḥpurasamētaḥ ॥ 106 ॥
tataḥ sarvē nr̥pakumārā yathāīmāsanēṣūpaviṣṭāḥ । nijanijaparivārayutāḥ, militō'nyō'pi tatra janaḥ ॥ 107॥
rūpāntaraṁ kr̥tvā sa kumārastatra raṅgabhūmau । vādayan varamurajaṁ kaṇṭhanihitēna hārēṇa || 108॥
yāvattiṣṭhati tāvad dr̥ṣṭā'gacchantī sakhījanasamētā । bhavanapatākā dāsībhiḥ parigatā bandhuragatyā ॥ 109 ॥
śāradakṣaṇacandrāravindavipulānanā, kamaladalasarala susalāvaṇyavaralōcanā |
adharadalavijitātisarasabimbīphalā, daśanakaranikara saṁmr̥ṣṭa digmukhamalā ॥ 110 ॥
ramyalāvaṇyajalajaladhilaharīgamā, madanakōdaṇḍātikuṭila caṅgimā ।
bhagnasvargāṅganā'ṅgasaubhāgitā, taruṇajanajanitadurviṣahamadanāgnikā ॥ 111 ॥
atha kumāryā dhātrī sabhāgatā'ñjaliṁ śirasi kr̥tvā । iti vijñapayati kumārān mahāprasādaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 112 ॥
vīṇāyā vinōdēnānugrahaṁ kuruta rājaputryāḥ । vīṇāṁ gr̥hītvēmāṁ yathōpavēśakramēṇaiva ॥113॥
iti bhaṇitvā samarpayati dābhālanarēśvarasya sā vīṇām । naipuṇyēna kumāryā sūtritāṁ ratnamaṇḍitām ॥ 114 ॥
1 ga. pacchannasvadhārī sō ।

ક
supāsanāha cariammi
dhāī karē caḍiyaṁ tattō vīṇaṁ palōiuṁ bhaṇai । sō maddaliyakumārō annōvi hu kōvi kiṁ lahai ॥ 116 ॥
vīmimaṁ vāēuṁ, tō kumarī tassa kaṁṭhadēsammi । picchara taṁ niyahāraṁ tō jāṇai ēsa sō suhaō ।। 117॥
kēṇāvi paōgēṇa rūvaṁ parivattiūṇa sāhaṇiyaṁ । bhōlaviu tammi diṇē jahā gaō saṁpayapi tahā ॥ 118 ॥
manē samāgaō iha, hāraṁ jaṁ tassa bhuvaṇavīrassa । ghittuṁ sakai sakōvinēya, tō sōcciya imōti ॥ 119 ॥
ēvaṁ ca viyakatīē tīē dhāīē appiyaṁ vīṇaṁ । vāyaṁtō saccaviō sō vimhayarasavasā tattō ||120||
paricita kō ēsō saggāu tuṁburō samōinō ? | ahavā hatthiviṇōē jaṁ kōsallaṁ maē tassa || 121 ||
dihaṁ, tēṇaṇumijjai savvāsu kalāsu tassa kōsalaṁ । tō sō ēsōtti viṇicchiyammi rōmaṁcakaṁcuiyā ।
jā ci tā aimahurimāē vīṇājhuṇissa kumarīē । hayahiyayāē niddā samāgayā takkhaṇammi daḍhaṁ ||
anōvi tattha jō rāyarāyaputtāiō jaṇō asthi । sōvi hu niddā muddāmuddiyanayaṇō daḍhaṁ jāō || 124 ॥
aha kahavi payattēṇaṁ mahayā cēyāviūṇa sō kumariṁ । vīṇaṁ vāyatōcciya tīsēbhimuhaṁ bhaṇai ēvaṁ || 125॥
ēyāṇa nivakumārāṇa bhālaphalaēsa aggahatthēṇa | ghaṇasāramīsacaṁdaṇarasēṇa gāhaṁ lihasu ēvaṁ || 126 ||
taha caiva kaē tīē bhai puṇō kuṁḍalaṁpi ēkikaṁ । giṇhasu kannērhitō kuṇasu ya pēcchati jaha na imē ॥
aha taha kampri vīṇā saṁhariyā tēṇa, tēvi paḍibuddhā । picchaṁti ya avarupparamii gāhaṁ bhālaphalaēsu ।।
sirimūrasēṇataṇaō dēsadidicchāē niggaō ēsō । kittijalahīkumārō vāyai vīṇaṁ viṇōraṇa || 129|
atha vādayitvā kṣaṇamēkamēvamanyē'pi naravarakumārāḥ । nijaśaktyā tadvādanē prakaṭayanti vijñānam ॥ 115 ॥
bhājyāḥ karē caṭitāṁ tatō vīṇāṁ pralōkya bhaṇati । sa mārdalikakumārō'nyō'pi khalu kō'pi kiṁ labhatē ||
vīṇāmiyāṁ vādayitum, tataḥ kumārī tasya kaṇṭhadēśē । paśyati taṁ nijahāraṁ tatō jānātyēṣa sa subhagaḥ ॥
kēnāpi prayōgēṇa rūpaṁ parivartya sādhanikam । vañcayitvā tasmin dinē yathā gataḥ sāṁpratamapi tathā ॥ 118 ॥
manyē samāgata iha, hāraṁ yattasya bhuvanavīrasya । grahītuṁ śaknōti śakrō'pi naiva tataḥ sa ēvāyamiti ॥
ēvaṁ ca vitarkayantyāṁ tasyāṁ dhātryā'rpitāṁ vīṇām । vādayan dr̥ṣṭaḥ sa vismayarasavaśāt tataḥ ॥ 120॥
paricintayati ka ēṣa svargāt tumburuḥ samavatīrṇaḥ ? | athavā hastivinōdē yatkauśalaṁ mayā tasya ॥ 121 ॥
dr̥ṣṭaṁ tēnānumīyatē sarvāsu kalāsu tasya kauśalam । tataḥ sa ēṣa iti viniśvitē rōmāñcakañcukitā ॥ 122 ॥
yāvattiṣṭhati tāvadatimadhurimṇā vīṇādhvanēḥ kumāryāḥ । hr̥tahr̥dayāyā nidrā samāgatā tatkṣaṇē dr̥ḍham ॥ 123 ॥
anyō'pi tatra yō rājarājaputrādikō janō'sti । sō'pi khalu nidrāmudrā mudritanayanō dr̥ḍhaṁ jātaḥ ॥ 124 ॥
abha kathamapi prayatnēna mahatā cētayitvā sa kumārīm । vīṇāṁ vādayannēva tasyā abhimukhaṁ bhaṇatyēvam ॥125॥
ētēṣāṁ nr̥pakumārāṇāṁ bhālaphala kēṣvagrahastēna । ghanasāramiśracandanarasēna gāthāṁ likhaivam ॥ 126 ॥
tathaiva kr̥tē tayā bhaṇati punaḥ kuṇḍalamapyēkaikam । gr̥hāṇa karṇēbhyaḥ kuru ca paśyanti yathā nēmē ॥127॥
atha tathā kr̥tē vīṇā saṁhr̥tā tēna, tē'pi pratibuddhāḥ । paśyanti ca parasparamiti gāyāṁ bhālaphalakēṣu ॥ 128 ॥
śrīśūrasēnatanayō dēśadidr̥kṣayā nirgata ēṣaḥ । kīrttijaladhikumārō vādayati vīṇāṁ vinōdēna ॥ 129 ॥

sapaḍāyākahā ।
265
bhālaphalaēsu jēsiṁ lihiyā gāhulliyā ya tē savvē | saṁbaṁdhēṇaṁ kēṇāvi kēvi sē baṁdhuṇō huti ॥ 130 ॥
raanakuṁḍalamaha taṁpi parōpparaṁ na picchaṁti । tō tē vimhiyavayaṇā maṁtaṁti imaṁ ta savvē ॥ 131 ॥
saṁvaya guṇēhiṁ imō na uṇō taguṇatti bhāvamāṇēsu । pakkhivai rāyaputtī varamālaṁ kumarakaṁṭammi || 132 ||
aha khuhiyakhīrajalanihisararuṁdī tūrapūraṁgurusadō। dhavalakhō ucchaliō bahūṇa kalayaṁṭikaṁṭhāṇa || 133||
tō tassa baṁdhuṇō tē bhaṇati taṁ kattha suṁdarataṁ tē 1 । tō sō payaḍai laḍahaṁ niyarūvaṁ guliyamavaṇēuṁ ॥ 134 ॥
āliṁgaṁti saharisaṁ bahukumarā kittijalahivarakumaraṁ । sōbi tāja jahārihāvitti kuṇai sappaṇayaṁ ||
bhaṇaiya kumariṁ adhpasu kuṁḍēlarayaṇāī rāyaputtāṇa । īsi hasatī sāvi hu tāī tāṇaṁ samappē ॥ 136 ॥
tē kumarakusala saṁgamasayaṁtraśēdaṁtapayaḍaṇanimittaṁ । dhāvaṇayaṁ takkhaṇamēva kumarajaṇayāṇa pēsaṁti ॥137॥
rāyāvi siddharāō uvaladdhapaṇamaṇinihāṇōcca । harisavasapulaiyaṁgō vivāhasāmaggiyaṁ kuṇai ॥ 138 ॥
aha sōhammadivasē paramapamōēṇa kumarakumarīṇa । pāṇiggahaṇamahasavamaṇōra hō pūriō raṇṇā ॥ 139 ॥
tō kittijala hikumarō bhavana paḍāyāē parigaō pavarē | paṁcappayārabhōē aṇurbhujai jaha surō saggē ॥ 140 ॥
aha rahavīrapurāō piṇō sirisūrasēṇarāyassa । bahuparivārō pattō rāyaduvārī tarhi varuṇō ॥ 141 ॥
paḍihārasaiō sō pavisai sirikittijalahiatthāṇē । uciyapaḍivattipuvvaṁ kumaraṁ vinnavai sō ēvaṁ | 142 ।
jaha sūrasēṇaranō rōgā aidāruṇā samubbhūyā । tō lahu āgatūṇaṁ piumuhakamalaṁ palōēsu ॥ 143 ॥
iya sōuṁ taṁ kumarō sahappaṇā nēi rāyapāsammi । kumarā ēsēṇa sō taṁ ciya vinnavai naravaṇō || 144 ॥
bhālaphalakēṣu yēṣāṁ likhitā gāthā ca tē sarvē । saṁbandhēna kēnāpi kē'pi tasya bandhavō bhavanti ॥ 130 ॥
ēkaikakarṇa kuṇḍalamatha tadapi parasparaṁ na paśyanti । tatastē vismitavadanā mantrayantīdaṁ tataḥ sarvē ॥ 131 ॥
saṁvadati guṇairayaṁ na punastanvēti bhāvayatsu । prakṣipati rājaputrī varamālāṁ kumārakaṇṭhē ॥ 132 ॥
atha kṣubdhakṣīra jalanidhisvaravipulastūrapūraguruśabdaḥ । dhavalarava ucchalitō vadhūnāṁ kalakaṇṭhīkaṇṭhānām ॥ 133 ॥
tatastasya bandhavastē bhaṇanti tat kva sundaratvaṁ tē ? । tataḥ sa prakaṭayati ramyaṁ nijarūpaṁ guṭikāmapanīya ॥ 134 ॥
āliṅganti saharṣaṁ bahukumārāḥ kīrttijaladhivarakumāram । sō'pi tēṣāṁ yathārhapratipattiṁ karōti sapraṇayam ॥
bhaṇati ca kumārīmarpaya kuṇḍalaratnāni rājaputrēbhyaḥ । īṣad hasantī sāpi khalu tāni tēbhyaḥ samarpayati ॥ 136 ॥
tēṁ kumāra kuśalasaṁgama svayaṁvarōdantaprakaṭanānimittam । dhāvanaṁ tatkṣaṇamēva kumārajanakayōḥ prēṣayanti ॥ 137॥
rājāpi siddharāja upalabdhapranaṣṭamaṇinidhāna iva । harṣavaśapulakitāṅgō vivāhasāmagrī karōti ॥ 138 ॥
atha śōbhanē divasē paramapramōdēna kumārakumāryōḥ । pāṇigrahaṇamahōtsavamanōrathaḥ pūritō sajñā ॥ 139॥
tataḥ kīrttijaladhikumārō bhavanapatākayā parigataḥ pravarān । pañcaprakārabhōgānanubhuṅktē yathā suraḥ svargē ॥140॥
atha rathavīrapurāta pituḥ śrīśūrasēnarājasya । bahuparivāraḥ prāptō rājadvārī tatra varuṇaḥ ॥ 141 ॥
pratihārasūcitaḥ sa praviśati śrīkīrttijaladhyāsthānē । ucitapratipattipūrvaṁ kumāraṁ vijñapayati sa ēvam ॥ 142 ॥
yathā śūrasēnarājasya rōgā atidāruṇāḥ samudbhūtāḥ । tatō ladhvāgatya pitr̥mukhakamalaṁ pralōkasva ॥ 143 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi
tō kariharirahapākka cakkarayaṇāiyaṁ bahuṁ dāum̐ । bhaṇaḍāyāē samaṁ rāyā kumaraṁ visajjēi || 145||
uciyapaḍivattiputraṁ visajjiō kumarabaṁdhuvaggōvi । akhaṁḍapāṇēhiṁ rahavīrapurē gaō kumarō || 146 |
sirisūrasēṇarāyā ārōvēūṇa tammi rajjabharaṁ । vihiṇā kālaṁ kārḍa sakkasamāṇō surō jāō || 147॥
sirikittijalahirāyā rāyā iva suyaṇamaṇacaōrāṇa । jiṇamayamucchaṣpaṁtō aṇupālai rajjamaṇavajjē । 148
।
aha desenagāō sudādavijjāharēṇa vijhammi । gacchaṁtēṇaṁ kajjaṁtarēṇa gimhami bhavaṇuvariṁ ||149 |
diṭṭā bhavaṇavaḍāyā suttā sirikittijalahinivāsē । tadēhaluddhacittēṇa avahaḍā naravarē sutē ॥ 150 ॥
aha paccūsē rāyā suttaviddhō palōyaē jāva । tāva na picchai taṁ pāṇavalaṁ paṇaiṇi pāsē ।। 151 ।।
āsannapariyaṇāō sanvattha gavēsiyāvi sā tattha । nō uvaladdhā tattō citai ēyaṁ mahacchariyaṁ ॥ 152॥
jāmilamahalayasaṁkulammi maṇuyāṇa tāva na pavēsō । vīsabhavaṇammi, navaraṁ surakhayarāṇaṁ imaṁ kammaṁ ।। 153 |
tā kiṁ iha kāyavvaṁ ahavā kāyavyamitya na hu asthi । divvēṇa jrēṇa ghaḍiūṇa vihaḍiyā tassa isa ciṁtā ।
yata uktam;
-
ampatthiyaī iṁti jaha dukkhaī, sahasā pariṇamaṁti taha sukkhaī ।
pubvajjiyaī dharivi kō sakkara, sappurisahaṁ ciṁttuvi na camakai || 155 ॥
ēvaṁ samāhiyamaṇō dr̥mijjatōvi tīē virahēṇa । uvaviṭṭhō atthāṇē saṁṭhaviḍaṁ pariyaṇaṁ tīē ॥ 156 ॥
iti śrutvā taṁ kumāraḥ sahātmanā nayati rājapārśvē । kumārādēśēna sa tadēva vijñapayati narapatayē || 144 ॥
tataḥ kariharirathapadāticakraratnādikaṁ bahu dattvā । bhavanapatākayā samaṁ rājā kumāraṁ visr̥jati ॥ 145 ॥
ucitapratipattipūrva visr̥ṣṭaḥ kumārabandhuvargē'pi । akhaṇḍaprayāṇai rathavīrapurē gataḥ kumāraḥ ॥ 146 ॥
śrī śūrasēnarāja ārōpya tasmin rājyabharam । vidhinā kālaṁ kr̥tvā śakrasamānaḥ surō jātaḥ ॥ 147 ॥
śrī kī tijaladhirājō rājēva sujanamanaścakōrāṇām | jinamatamutsarpayannanupālayati rājyamanavadyam ॥ 148॥
atha vaitāḍhyanagāt sudaṁṣṭravidyādharēṇa vindhyē । gacchatā kāryāntarēṇa grīṣmē bhavanasyōpari ॥ 149 ॥
dr̥ṣṭa। bhavanapatākā supta। śrīkīrttijaladhinr̥papārśvē । taddēhalubdhacittēnāpahr̥tā naravarē suptē ॥ 150 ॥
atha pratyūṣē rājā suptavibuddhaḥ pralōkatē yāvat । tāvat na paśyati tāṁ prāṇavallabhāṁ praṇayinīṁ pārśvē ॥ 151 ॥
āsannaparijanāt sarvatra gavēṣitāpi sā tatra । nō upalabvā tataścintayatyētad mahāścaryam ॥ 152 ॥
yāmikanivahasaṁkulē manujānāṁ tāvanna pravēśaḥ । vāsabhavanē, navaraṁ surakhacarayōridaṁ karma ॥153॥
tasmātkimiha kartavyamathavā kartavyamatra na khalvasti । daivēna yēna ghaṭitvā vighaṭitā tasyēyaṁ cintā ॥ 154॥
aprārthitānyāyanti yathā duḥkhāni, sahasā pariṇamanti tathā saukhyāni ।
pūrvārjitāni dhartuṁ kaḥ śaknōti, satpuruṣāṇāṁ cittamapi na camatkarōti ॥ 155॥
ēvaṁ samāhitamanā dūyamānō'pi tasyā virahēṇa । upaviṣṭa āsthānē saṁsthāpya parijanaṁ tasyāḥ ॥156॥
1 ka. bhajjha gēhammi nakha, majma gimmi na° । 2 ka. ga. vinnuvi ।

૨૨૭
āgaṁtūṇaṁ aha vāyasēṇa paḍhamammi divasajāmammi । vāyavvāē disāē phaliē sahakāra rukkhammi ॥ 157 ॥
laviya maṁjulakalayaṁṭhikaṁṭhamahurēṇa saravisēsēṇa । taṁ sōuṁ sauṇavika naranāhaṁ vinavē imaṁ ॥ 158 ॥
dēvīsamāgamēṇaṁ baddhāvara dēva ! vāyasō ēsa | sauṇagaṁthē bhaṇiyaṁ jēṇa imaṁ nāha ! nisuṇēsu || 159॥
siddhibhayaṁ caravattābhōgaṇavuṭṭitthinathīlābhē । kahai lavaṁtō kāō puvbāisu paḍhamajāmapi ।। 160 ।।
vēsāgamathīlābhaṁ vuṭṭhī battā arīṇa nāsaṁ ca । thī lābhamacchabhakkhaṇaaggī pūvvāi viyajāmē ॥ 169 ॥
bhayakalahabuddhikārī aṁriniddhagurūṇa āgamō vattā । puvvāi taiyapaharē vaṁbhammi ya kajjasaṁsiddhī || 162 ||
bhayasuyavattāatihī ḍamaraṁ thīvaṁchanitragurūprayā । baṁbhē lēhāgavaṇaṁ puvvāisu turiyapaharammi || 163 ||
gōhatthīṇaṁ piṭṭhē kāō jai lavai dēva ! thīlābhaṁ । krūvataḍē piyadasaṇa naītaḍē nivabhayaṁ kahaī || 164 ||
ēvaṁ sāuṇiēṇaṁ saṇasarūyē kahijjamāṇammi । sahasā pārasiyasuō samāgaō rāyapayalē || 165 ||
namiuṁ bhaṇai narēsara ! tuha payaparamāṇa vinavaṇahē । bhavaṇapaḍāyādēvīsayāsaō ahamiha pattō ॥ 166 ॥
tannāmasavaṇa saṁjāyaharisapulaēṇa rāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ । bhō kīra ! khīrasakaradakhābhakkhaṁ karahi tāva ।। 167॥
tō jhatti taṁ tava ya karāviya pucchiō puṇō kīrō । hē kahasu kattha diṭṭhā maha ā kēna cānīyā ? ||
tō sō kai nimusu naravara ! dēvīē mūlaō suddhiṁ । suravijjāharakīlāvaṁjhō viṁjhō girī asthi ॥ 169 ॥
jō bhamiratiyasavilayācalayāvaliraṇiranēuraravēhiṁ । hakāraivva varataruṇataruṇijuyalāī kīlatthaṁ || 170 ||
āgatyātha vāyasēna prathamē divasayāmē । vāyavyāṁ diśi phalitē sahakāravr̥kṣē ॥ 157 ॥
lapitaṁ majjulakalakaṇṭhīkaṇṭhamadhurēṇa svaraviśēṣēṇa । tat śrutvā śakunavid naranārtha vijñapayatīdam ॥ 158 ॥
dēvīsamāgamēna vardhayati dēva ! vāyasa ēṣaḥ । śakunagranthē bhaṇitaṁ yēnēdaṁ nātha ! śr̥ṇu ॥ 159 ॥
siddhibhayacaravārtābhōjanavr̥ṣṭistrīnaṣṭastrīlābhān । kathayati lapan kākaḥ pūrvādiṣu prathamayāmē ॥ 160 ॥
vēśyāgamastrīlābhau vr̥ṣṭiṁ vārtāmarīṇāṁ nāśaṁ ca । strīlābhamatsyabhakṣaṇāgnīn pūrvādau dvitīyayā ॥ 161॥
bhavakalaha vr̥ṣṭikāryarisnigdhagurūṇāmāgamaṁ vārtām । pūrvādau tr̥tīyapraharē brahmaṇi ca kāryasaṁsiddhim ॥ 162 ॥
bhayasutavārtā'tithīn ḍamaraṁ strīvāñchānu gurupūjāḥ । brahmaṇi lēkhāgamanaṁ pūrvādiṣu turyapraharē ॥ 163 ॥
gōhastinōḥ pr̥ṣṭhē kākō yadi lapati dēva ! strīlābham । kūpataḍē priyadarśanaṁ nadītaṭē nr̥pabhayaṁ kathayati ॥ 164 ॥
ēvaṁ śākunikēna śakunasvarūpē kathyamānē । sahasā pārasīkaśukaḥ samāgatō rājapādamūlē ॥ 165॥
natvā bhaṇati narēśvara ! tava pādapadmayōrvijñapanahētōḥ । bhavanapatākādēvī sakāśatō'hamiha prāptaḥ ॥ 166॥
tannāmaśravaṇasaṁjātaharṣapulakēna rājñā bhaṇitam । bhōḥ kīra ! kṣīraśarkarādrākṣābhakṣaṇaṁ kuru tāvat ॥ 167॥
tatō jhaṭiti tattathaiva ca kārayitvā pr̥ṣṭaḥ punaḥ kīraḥ । hē kathaya kva dr̥ṣṭā mamēṣṭā kēna cānītā ? ॥ 169 ॥
tataḥ sa kathayati śr̥ṇu naravara ! dēvyā mūlataḥ śuddhim । suravidyādharakrīḍā'vandhyō vindhyō girirasti ॥ 168॥
yō bhramitr̥tridaśavanitāvalayāvaliraṇitr̥nūpuraravaiḥ । hakkārayatīva varataruṇataruṇī yugalāni krīḍārtham ॥170॥
1 ka. siddhi bhayaṁ ca । 2 kha aini । 3 ka. kha. naima ।

tami ma sā dēvī dakkhāyaṇamaṁḍavassa majjhammi । diṭṭhā nidāmuddādadamuddiyanayaṇapuḍajuyalā ||171 ॥
maharihasijāē gayā, ēgō vijjāharō ya tīē purō । japatōṇēgāī vayaṇāī sihasā rāī || 172 ||
tadyathā ;-
pasīya pasayaccha! chaṁṭasu niyadiṭṭicchōha amavadhārāhi । mayaṇaggisaṁpalittaṁ hayahiyayaṁ majjha karabhōru ! |
paḍibujjha piē! daiē, ēvaṁ suṇiuṁ jhaḍatti paḍibuddhā । tumhapaḍirūvadhāri pāsai vijjāharasudā || 174||
tō kasiṇīkayavayaṇā bāhulliyalōyaṇā maē bhaṇiyā । kiṁ tumamēyāvatthaṁ pattā niyapiyayamaṁ daṭhṭhē ? ।। 175 ।
tattō dēvī jaṁpara na hōi maha piyayamō imō kīra ! । kittimasiṇēhamēsō payāsaē jamiya jaṁpatō ॥ 176 ।
pāsāōvi na dīsai na caiva maha pariyaṇōvi pāsammi । tō nicchaēṇa imiṇā avahari ahamihāṇīyā ।
mahai maha sīlarsa ēsō vahutarammitā bhulō । jai sīlaṁpi na hōjā nārīṇaṁ tō varaṁ maraṇaṁ ॥ 178 ॥
varamammi pavēsō varaṁ vaṇē hariguhāē saṁvāsō | mā sīlassa ubhaṁsō havijja sukula pasūyāṇaṁ ॥ 179 ॥
sīlaṁ paramanihāṇaṁ sīlaṁ mahilāṇa bhūsaṇamaṇajyaṁ । taha sugaihēū sīlaṁ sivasuhataruniruvahayavīyaṁ ॥ 180 ॥
tā vijayasārabhūyaṁ sīlaṁ pāṇacaēvi na caissaṁ । kō vā jīvaṁtīē maha sakai khaṁḍijaṁ sīlaṁ ? ॥ 189 ॥
ēvaṁ maha kahiūṇaṁ mōṇēṇaṁ jāva saṁṭhiyā dēvī । vijjāhararāyasuō tō sō bhaṇiō maē ēvaṁ ।। 182 ॥
rasaṇaṁ asiuṁ dasa marai sīlassa khaṁḍaṇē ēsā । taha ya na vaṁchiyasiddhī ihalōē tumha picchāmi ॥
paralōē puṇa sīlassa khaṁḍaṇē kayamaṇassa jaṁ pāvē । narayāisu dukkhaparaṁparāē taṁ kāraṇaṁ paramaṁ ॥ 184 ॥

tasmin mayā sā dēvī drākṣāghanamaṇḍapasya madhyē । dr̥ṣṭā nidrāmudrādr̥ḍhamudritanayanapuṭayugalā ॥ 171 ॥
mahārhaśayyāyāṁ gatā, ēkō vidyādharaśca tasyāḥ puraḥ । jalpannanēkāni vacanāni snēhasārāṇi ॥ 172 ॥
prasīda mr̥gākṣi ! ukṣa nijadr̥ṣṭikṣēpa | mr̥tadhārābhiḥ । madanāgnisaṁpradīptaṁ hr̥tahr̥dayaṁ mama karabhōru ! ॥ 173 ॥
pratibudhyasva priyē ! dayitē ! ētat śrutvā jhaṭiti pratibuddhā । yuṣmatpratirūpadhāriṇaṁ paśyati vidyādharasudaṣṭam ॥
tataḥ kr̥ṣṇīkr̥tavadanā bāṣpavallōcanā mayā bhaṇitā । kiṁ tvamētadavasthāṁ prāptā nijapriyatamaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā ॥ 175॥

prāsādō'pi na dr̥śyatē naiva mama parijanō'pi pārśvē । tatō niścayēnānēnāpahr̥tyāhamihānītā ॥ 177॥
kāṅkṣati mama śīlabhraṁśamēṣa mahāntarē tāvad bhraṣṭaḥ । yadi śīlamapi na bhavēd nārīṇāṁ tatō varaṁ maraṇam ॥ 178

ēvaṁ māṁ kathayitvā maunēna yāvat saṁsthitā dēvī । vidyāhararājasutastataḥ sa bhaṇitō mayaivam ॥182॥
rasanāmaśilā daśanaimriyatē śīlasya khaṇḍana ēṣā । tathā ca na vāñchitārthasiddhirihalō kē yuṣmākaṁ paśyāmi ।
paralōkē punaḥ śīlasya khaṇḍanē kr̥tamanasō yatpāpam । narakādiṣu duḥkhaparamparāyāstata kāraṇaṁ paramam ॥ 184 |

jaṁ puṇa maraṇassa mahāsaīē īi kāraṇaṁ tumhē । saṁjāyaha, ēyassa u pāvassa aīvaghōrassa ॥ 185 ॥
pāvāṇubaṁdhiṇō bahupuggalapariyaṭṭakōḍikōḍīhiṁ । nitthārō jai bhaviyavvayāē vasaō kahavi hōhī ।। 186 ॥
tā tuha vijjāhararāyavaṁsapa bhavassa pavarajāissa | vijjāsayanilayassavi hōi avijjā imaṁ cōjjaṁ ॥ 187॥
tā tiriyassavi vayaṇēṇa majjha muccara asaggahō ēsō । khaṁḍasarāvaṭhiyapi hu pīyaṁ amayaṁ ruyaṁ haṇai ॥ 188 ॥
tō maṁ pucchara vihiyahiyaō vijjāharō imaṁ kīra ! | kaha tuha iya dakkhattaṁ ēvaṁvivayaṇavinā sē || 189 ॥
rōrō jaha rayaṇavaī jāya rayaṇāyaraṁ nisēbaṁtō । taha suyanihimaṇisēvāē majjha iya vayaṇavinnāṇaṁ ॥ 190 ॥
tō jōḍiyakarakamalō nivaḍiya calaṇēsu bhaṇai maṁ khayarō | dhammagurū maha tumhē ēsāvi hu sīlarayaṇanihī ||
maha bhaiṇī, tā ēyaṁ ṇēmi ahaṁ tammi caiva nayarammi । saha tumaē tattha gaō ṭhāma ahaṁ nagaravāhimmi ||
tumamēyaṁ
naravaṇō sāhasa jāsu majjha abhayaṁ ca । taṁ ca tahacciya jāyaṁ, saṁpai dēvō pamāṇaṁti ॥ 193॥
tō rāyā kīravaraṁ taṁ ārōviya niyammi ucchaṁgē । niyakaṁṭhāō rayaṇāvaliṁ ca khiviūṇa takkaṁṭhē ॥ 194 ॥
utō bhai suyaṁ sahalīkuṇa lōyaṇāī, daṁsēuṁ । taṁ nararayaṇaṁ, tārisaitthīrayaṇē vasagayammi || 195॥
jassāsattamaṇassavi tuha pannavaṇēṇa ērisā buddhī । jāyā, taha abhayaṁ ciya dinnaṁ mē savvahā tassa ॥ 196॥
aha pāṇiṭhāviyasuō rāyā tasiēṇa maggēṇa । aṇugammatō bahupariyaṇēṇa ṭhāṇaṁ tamaṇupattō ॥ 197॥
tō tāīvi naranāhaṁ iṁtaṁ daṭṭhūṇa dūraō cētra । saṁmuhamurviti, uciyaṁ paḍivatti tō karēūṇa ॥ 198 ॥
nayarammi payaṭṭamahasamma pattō nivō samaṁ tēṇa । khayaraṁ kīraṁ ca tahi sammāṇē visajjēi ॥ 199 ॥
yat punarbharaṇasya mahāsatyā ētasyāḥ kāraṇaṁ yūyam । saṁjāyadhvē, ētasya tu pāpasyātīvaghōrasya ॥ 185 ॥
pāpānubandhinō bahupudgalaparāvartakōṭikōṭibhiḥ । nistārō yadi bhavitavyatāyā vaśataḥ kathamapi bhaviṣyati ॥ 186॥
tasmāttava vidyādhararājavaṁśaprabhavasya pravarajātēḥ । vidyāśatanilayasyāpi bhavatyavidyēdamāścaryam ॥ 187॥
tasmāttiraśvō'pi vacanēna mama mucyatāmasagraha ēṣaḥ । khaṇḍaśarāvasthitamapi khalu pītamamr̥taṁ rujaṁ hanti ॥ 188 ॥
tatō māṁ pr̥cchati vismitahr̥dayō vidyāvara idaṁ kīra ! । kathaṁ tavēti dakṣatvamēvaṁvidhavacanavinyāsē ? ॥ 189 ॥
rōrō yathā ratnapatirjāyatē ratnākaraṁ niṣēvamāṇaḥ । tathā śrutanidhimunisēvayā mamēti vacanavijñānam ॥ 190॥
tatō yōjita karakamalō nipatya caraṇayōrbhaṇati māṁ khacaraḥ । dharmaguravō mama yūyamēṣāpi khalu śīlaratnanidhiḥ ॥
mama bhaginī, tasmādētāṁ nayāmyahaṁ tasminnēva nagarē । saha yuṣmābhistatra gatastiṣṭhāmyahaṁ nagara bahiḥ ॥192॥
yūyamētad narapatayē kathaya yācasva mamābhayaṁ ca । tacca tathaiva jātaṁ, saṁprati dēvaḥ pramāṇamiti ॥ 193॥
tatō rājā karivaraṁ tamārōpya nija utsaṅgē । nijakaṇṭhād ratnāvaliṁ ca kṣiptvā tatkaṇṭhē ॥ 194 ॥
uttiṣṭhan bhaṇati śukaṁ saphalīkuru lōcanē, darśayitvā । tannararatnaṁ, tādr̥śastrīratnē vaśagatē ॥ 199॥
yasyāsaktamanasō'pi tava prajñāpanēnēdr̥śī buddhiḥ । jātā, tathā'bhayamēva dattaṁ mayā sarvathā tasyaṁ ॥ 196॥
atha pāṇisthāpitaśukō rājā taddarśitēna mārgēṇa । anugamyamānō bahuparijanēna sthānaṁ tadanuprāptaḥ ॥ 197 ॥
tatastāvapi naranāthamāyāntaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā dūrata ēva । saṁmukhamupētaḥ, ucitāṁ pratipattiṁ tataḥ kr̥tvā ॥ 198 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
pāunbhūō gabbhō dēvīē tammi caiva samayasmi । tō bhaṇai jaṇō ganbhō nivasaṁbhōyāu jai hum̐tō || 200
tāpuvvaṁ ēyāē annāē ahava rāyadēvīē । kiṁ nō pāu bhūō ēttiyavarisēhi, taṁ nr̥ṇaṁ ॥ 209 ॥
tattha gayā paribhuttā ēsā vijjāharēṇa pacchā ō | gurujaṇabhaṇiēṇa imaṁ chaumaṁ raiūṇa āṇīyā ॥ 202 ॥
lōyavayuṇijjamēyaṁ rāyā āyanniūṇa ciṁtēi । saccō ēsa pavāō lōō aliō ya baliō ya || 203 |
lōēṇa ghaḍiyajattī visaē ēyammi majjhavi maṇammi । uppāyai sabbhāvaṁ saṁbhāvijjai na purṇa ēyaṁ ॥ 204 ॥
ahavā savvamasaccaṁ hōi kammōdayāu ēīē । tahavi hu iya jaṇavāō na suṁdarō kulappasūyāṇa || 205 ॥
tā pēsijja ēsā jaṇaya gihē virai imaṁ chaumaṁ । jaha jaṇaō apaḍataṇū tēvi maha pēsiō lēhō || 206 ।
jaṁ lēhadaṁsaṇāō bhavaṇāyā jhaḍati maha pāsē । pēsaiyavvā tumaē iya kahiuṁ tīi tō rannā ॥207॥
āṇatō sēṇāṇī ēvaṁ mōttūṇa jaṇayagēhammi । taṁ āgacchatu sigghaṁ imīē jaṇayassa parikahiuṁ ॥ 208 ॥
jaha bhaṇiyamimaṁ rannā kāraṇavasau imāē iha pasavō । uciutti pēsiō haṁ ēvaṁ vittr̥̄ṇa iha jhatti || 209 |
tēṇavi tahēva vihiyaṁ, sāvi gayā tattha pāsiuṁ jaṇayaṁ । nīrōgaṁ paricita majjha vilīyaṁ naravaissa ॥210॥
parivasa kiṁpi cittē, chaumaṁ kāūṇa tēṇa tēṇēha । pēsaviyā piugēhē, tamahaṁ thēvaṁpi na sarēmi || 211 |
vijjāhara avaharaṇē kiṁcivi lōyāu puṇa alīyapi । nisuṇēūṇa vilīyaṁ anivēēūṇa mē puraō ॥ 212
mannē paricattā hūṁ, taṁ maha kammāṇa vilasiyamasēsaṁ । iya aparikkhiyakārī kaha nahā ajjauttōvi ? || 213
nagarē pravr̥ttamahōtsavē prāptō nr̥paḥ samaṁ tēna । khacaraṁ kīraṁ ca tatra sammānya visr̥jati ॥ 199 ॥
prādurbhūtō garbhō dēvyāstasminnēva samayē । tatō bhaṇati janō garbhō nr̥pasaṁbhāgād yadyabhaviṣyat ॥200॥
tadā pūrvamētasyā anyasyā athavā rājadēvyāḥ । kiṁ nō prādurbhūta ētāvadvarṣaiḥ, tannūnam ॥201॥
tatra gatā paribhuktaiṣā vidyādharaṇa paścāttu । gurujanabhāṇatēnēdaṁ chadma racayitvā''nītā ॥ 202 ॥
lōkavacanīyamētad rājā''karṇya cintayati । satya ēṣa pravādō lōkō'līkaśca paniśca ॥ 203 ॥
lōkēna ghaṭitayuktirviṣaya ētasminmamāpi manasi । utpādayati sadbhāvaṁ, saṁbhāvyatē na punarētat ॥ 204 ॥
athavā sarvamasatyaṁ bhavati karmōdayādētasyāḥ । tathāpi khalviti janavādō na sundaraḥ kulaprasūtānām ॥205॥
tasmāt prēṣyatāmēṣā janakagr̥hē viracayyēdaṁ chadma । yathā janakōspaṭutanustēnāpi mama prēṣitō lēkhaḥ ॥206॥
yalēkhadarśanād bhavanapatākā jhaṭiti mama pārśvē । prēṣayitavyā yuṣmābhiriti kathayitvā tasyai tatō rājñā ॥ 207॥
ājñaptaḥ sēnānaritāṁ muktvā janakagēhē । tvamāgaccha śīghramasyā janakasya parikathya || 208 ॥
yathā bhaṇitamidaṁ rājñā kāraṇavaśatō'syā iha prasavaḥ । ucita iti prēṣitō'hamēnāṁ gr̥hītvēha jhaṭiti ॥ 209 ॥
tēnāpi tathaiva vihitaṁ, sāpi gatā tatra dr̥ṣṭvā janakam । nīrōgaṁ paricintayati mama vyalīkaṁ narapatēḥ ॥210 ॥
parivasati kimapi cittē, chadma kr̥tvā tēna tēnēha । prēṣitā pitr̥gēhē, tadahaṁ stōkamapi na smarāmi || 211 ॥
vidyādharāpaharaṇē kiñcidapi lōkāt punaralīkamapi । śrutvā vyalīkamanivēdya mē purataḥ ॥ 212 ॥
manyē parityaktā'hama, tanmama karmaṇāṁ vilasitamaśēṣam । ityaparīkṣitakārī kathamanyathā''rya putrō'pi ॥ 213

haṭṭagāvitti sahasā bhaṇiyā ēsā, imaṁ ca paumēṇa । nisuyaṁ tahēva taṁ pariṇayaṁ ca tō vāsabhavaṇammi 228
dinō na sē pavēsō tō sā gaṁtūṇa kahai paumāē । sāvi hu pucchara paramaṁ tumhavaraddhaṁ kimēyāē ? |229।
sō bhai haṭṭagāī bhaṇiyā ēsā taē, taō paumā । 'khiḍḍēṇa maē bhaṇiyaṁ ēvaṁ' iccāi bhaṇiū || 23 ||
pattijjāvara paumaṁ, tō sō puvva vaṭṭaī tīē । paumā ya dēsavirayā kiṁtu aṇābhōgaō ēvaṁ ||23||
.nō paricitai ēsā bīyammi vayammi majjha aiyārō । sahasā abbhakkhāṇaṁ, ājammaṁ pāliuṁ sammaṁ । 232 |
sētu savira, aṁtimasamayammi imamaīyā rē । appaḍikkamiūṇa mayā pattā sōhammakappammi || 233 ||
tattō ya cuyā jāyā kamēṇa tuha bhāriyā imā inhi । tantrayaṇaphalaṁ pattā vayaṇijjamimaṁ susīlāvi |
taṁ sōuṁ puralōō bhai muṇidaṁ bahu visūraṁtō । dēvīē vayaṇijjaṁ ēyaṁ suvisuddhasīlāē ||235||
ārōviyamamhēhi, tā pahū ! ēyassa pāvakammassa । jaha muccāmō amhē karuṇaṁ. kāuṁ tahā kuṇaha ॥ 236॥
pāvāvagamōvāē kahiyammi savitrē muṇidēṇa । kēhipi savvaviraī gahiyā dēsēṇa annahi || 237॥
sammattamittamannēhi, naravarō puṇa namittu muṇināhaṁ । vinnavai puṇō ēvaṁ jaha mai karuṇaṁ karēūṇa || 238 ||
ṭhāyavvamittha kavayadiṇāṇi kajjaṁ jamittha taṁ pahuṇō । jāṇati puṇa sayaṁ ciya iya bhaṇiuṁ uṭṭhiō tattō ॥
niyarajjakajjasikkhaṁ dāumamañcassa pavarasuhaḍēhiṁ । saha varaturayārūḍhērhi jāi kaṁcaṇapuriṁ nayariṁ ॥ 240 ॥
saṁpannaputtarayaṇaṁ bhavaṇapaḍāyaṁ taō khamāvēi । lōyavayaṇēṇa ēyaṁ kayaṁ maē maṁda hēṇa || 241॥
pariṇāyitaḥ sa mahilāmanyāma, duhitaramiva manyatē tāṁ sā । athānyadā pravr̥ttē kathāprabandhē padmayā ॥227॥
haṭṭagavīti sahasā bhaṇitaiṣā, idaṁ ca padmana । śrutaṁ tathaiva tat pariṇataṁ ca tatō vāsabhavanē ॥ 228 ॥
dattō na tasyāḥ pravēśastataḥ sā gatvā kathayati padmām । sāpi khalu pr̥cchati padmaṁ tavāparāddhaṁ kimētayā ? ||
sa bhaṇati haṭṭagavī bhaṇitaiṣā tvayā, tataḥ padmā । ' krīḍayā mayā bhaṇitamētat' ityādi bhaṇitvā ॥ 230॥
pratyāyayati padmaṁ, tataḥ sa pūrvamiva vartatē tasyām । padmā ca dēśaviratā kintvanābhōgata ēvam ॥231॥
nō paricintayatyēṣā dvitīyatratē mamāticāraḥ । sahasā'bhyākhyānaṁ, ājanma pālayitvā samyak ॥ 232॥
śēṣaṁ tu dēśaviratim, antimasamayē imamatīcāram । apratikramya mr̥tā prāptā saudharmakalpē ॥ 233 ॥
tataśca cyutā jātā kramēṇa tava bhāryēyamidānīm । tadvacanaphalaṁ prāptā vacanīyamidaṁ suśīlāpi ॥ 234॥
tat śrutvā puralōkō bhaṇati munīndraṁ bahu khidyamānaḥ । dēvyā vacanīyamētat suviśuddhaśīlāyāḥ ॥ 235॥
ārōpitamasmābhiḥ, tasmātprabhō ! ētasmātpāpakarmaṇaḥ । yathā mucyāmahē vayaṁ karuṇāṁ kr̥tvā tathā kuruta ॥ 236 ॥
pāpāpagamōpāyē kathitē savistarē munīndrēṇa । kairapi sarvaviratigr̥hītā dēśēnā'nyaiḥ ॥ 237॥
samyaktvamātramanyaiḥ, naravara : punarnatvā muninātham । vijñapayati punarēvaṁ yathā māya karuṇāṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 238॥
sthātavyamatra katipayadināni kāryaṁ yadatra tat prabhavaḥ । jānanti punaḥ svayamēvēti bhaṇitvōtthitastataḥ ॥239॥

asthi iha bharavāsē vāsava aṁgaṁva su-ra-yaṇakayagyaṁ । vīrauraṁ nāma puraṁ rāyā raṇavīranāmōti ||2||

tathā harihī cittaṁ raṇavīrarāyataṇaō jō । ēīē varō sō, iya sōuṁ iha pēsiyā kumarī || 15 |
praṇava laggamavi ajja caitra, tā dōṇhamēsiṁ rayaṇāṇaṁ । nimmavaṇē āyāsō hōu kayatthō payāvaiṇō ||
ittā ya savalamūlē ṭhāūṇaṁ bhaṇai naravaraṁ dharaṇō । jaha kumarassavi sammayamēyaṁ tā kuṇau lahu dēvō || 17 ||
tō paḍivannamma tahā nivēṇa vittē vivāhapavvammi | sammāṇiūṇa khayarō visajjiō jāi sahāṇaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
aha annayā kumārō atthāṇasahāē jaṇayapāsammi । jā ciṭṭhai tā pattō paḍihāranirūviyasarūvō ॥19॥
ujjāṇavalapurisō vinnavai narēsaraṁ paṇamiūṇa । jaha amaracaṁdasūrī thuvvatō amaraviṁdēṇaṁ ||20||
naṁdaṇava ujjāṇē samōsaḍhō ajja, iya nisāmēuṁ । amayasittōnva kumarō vinnavai kayaṁjalī jaṇaya || 21 ॥
jaha jaṁgamatitthāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ tāyassa daṁsaṇaṁ juttaṁ । tō tavvaṁdaṇahēu jāi nariṁdō saparivārō ||22||
tattha gaō taṁ daddhaṁ gaīdakhaṁdhāu uttarēūṇa । saha kumarēṇaṁ vihiṇā vaṁdai rōmaṁcakaṁcuiō ||23||
tō duhigahirōddāmaruṁdasadēṇa dhammalābhēṇa । ādium̐ nariṁdaṁ tayaṇu imaṁ dēsaṇaṁ kuṇai ||24||
tathāhi :-
jaṁ jaṁ iha saṁpajjai maṇōramaṁ ruvariddhimāīyaṁ । taṁ taṁ dhammassa phalaṁ vivarīyaṁ puṇa ahammassa ||25||
dhammābhāsēhi samāulammi bhuvaṇē jahadviyaṁ dhammaṁ । āsannabhāvibhaddā viralacciya kēi jāṇaṁti ॥ 26 ॥
viralāṇavi tē viralā dhammavisēsaṁ viyāṇiuṁ sammaṁ । jaṁ jaha bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ taha kuṇaṁti niyadēhaniravikkhā ||
jatthaya visayavirāō kasāyacāō guṇēsu aṇurāō । karuṇāē apamāō sō dhammō sivasuhōvāō। 28॥
ucitaṁ varamalabhamānasya tasyā naimittikēna mē kathitam । vīrapurōdyānavarē manōramē prēṣayata kumārīm ||14||
tatra sthitāyā hariṣyati cittaṁ raṇavīrarājatanayō yaḥ । ētasyā varaḥ saḥ, iti śrutvēha prēṣitā kumārī ॥15॥
pariṇayanalagnamapyadyaiva tasmād dvayōranayō ratnayōḥ । nirmāpaṇa āyāsō bhavatu kr̥tārthaḥ prajāpatēḥ ॥16॥
itaśca śravaṇamūlē sthitvā bhaṇati naravaraṁ dharaṇaḥ । yathā kumārasyāpi saṁmatamētat tasmātkarōtu laghu dēvaḥ ॥17॥
tataḥ pratipannē tathā nr̥pēṇa vr̥ttē vivāhaparvaṇi । sammānya khacarō visr̥ṣṭō yāti svasthānam ॥ 18 ॥
athānyadā kumāra āsthānasabhāyāṁ janakapārśvē । yāvattiṣṭhati tāvatprāptaḥ pratīhāranirūpitasvarūpaḥ ॥ 19॥
udyānapālapuruṣō vijñapayati narēśvaraṁ praṇamya । yathā'maracandrasūriḥ stūyamānō'maravr̥ndēna ॥20॥
nandanavanōdyānē samavasr̥tō'ya, iti niśamya । amr̥tasikta iva kumārō vijñapayati kr̥tāñjalirjanakam॥21॥
yathā jaṅgamatīrthānāṁ tēṣāṁ tātasya darśanaṁ yuktam । tatastadvandana hē bōryāti narēndraḥ saparivāraḥ ||22||
tatra gatastaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā gajēndraskandhāduttīrya । saha kumārēṇa vidhinā vandatē rōmāñcakañcukitaḥ ॥23॥
tatō dundubhigabhīrōddāmavipulaśabdēna dharmalābhēna । ānandya narēndraṁ tadanvimāṁ dēśanāṁ karōti ॥ 24 ॥
yadyadiha saṁpadyatē manōramaṁ rūpadikam । tattad dharmasya phalaṁ viparītaṁ punaradharmasya ॥ 25 ॥

dharmābhāsaḥ samākulē bhuvanē yathāsthitaṁ dharmam । āsannabhāvibhadrā viralā ēva kēcijjānanti ॥ 26 ॥
viralānāmapi tē viralā dharmaviśēṣaṁ vijñāya samyak । yadyathā bhaṇitaṁ tattathā kurvanti nija dēha nirapēkṣam ||27||

sō puṇa jiṇabhaṇiucciya suhatthiṇā tēṇa tattha jaiyantraṁ । annaha aṁbayasaddha|ē sēyaṇaṁ akkarukkhā || 2'
tatthavi jaimmōcci kāyavvō hōi asthi jai sattī । sa samaggasaṁgavigamā paramaṁga jēṇa mōkkhassa ||30|
apaviriyāṇa tajjōgayāē rahiyāṇagāridhammōvi । kālakamēṇa bhavabhayadukkhāṇa jalaṁjali dēi ||31||
iccāidēsaṇaṁ nisuṇiūṇa raṇavīrarāiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ । bhayavaṁ ! jai uciō hūṁ jaidhammaṁ dēsu tā majjha ||32
tō bhaṇiō sō guruṇā nivvigghaṁ hōu tujjha ēsatthō । aha rāyā niyakumaraṁ guṇajalahiṁ ṭhāviḍaṁ rajjē || 3
giuts sayaṁ dikkha guṇajala hinivōvi dharaṇamittajuō । dēsaviraī pavajjiya namiuṁ ca guruṁ vayai gēhē
mōyāvara guttīō kārai aṭṭhāhiyā jiṇagihēsu | sāhammiyavacchallaṁ dīṇajaṇuddharaṇamannaṁ ca ||35||
pavvajjaṁ giṇhaṁtō jaṁ rāyā bhaṇai kuṇai taṁ savvaṁ । ṭhavai dharaṇaṁ amacaṁ sayaṁ tu ujjamai dhammammi || 36 |
aha annayā nariṁdō rayaṇīē addharattasamayammi । picchara kamaladalacchi ēvaṁ navajōvvaṇaṁ ramaṇi ॥ 37
taṇukaṁtipayatimiraṁ ḍamaruyahatthaṁ suvannadaṁḍakaraṁ । vararayaṇāvalikaṁṭhaṁ siyavatthaṁ pāuyārūḍhaṁ ||38||
tō taṁ pucchai rāyā kā si tumaṁ kēṇa kāraṇēṇēha । chaṇasasisamāṇavayaṇē ! saṁpattā, kahai sāvi taō ।। 3
īsiviya saṁtatrayaṇā pabhaṇai pañcaṁgirā ahaṁ vijjā । ēttō bhavāu taiē bhavammi vihiyāu majjha taē ||4
puvyuttarasēvāō vihipuvvaṁ bhattinibbharamaṇēṇaṁ । jā kira sijjhissamahaṁ tā taṁ paṁcattamaṇupattō ॥ 41 ॥
puṇyabhavavioiyabhattīē cēva ahamāsi tujjha aṇukūlā | saṁpai puṇa jiṇadhammē rayassa taha dēsavirayassa ।
yatra ca viṣayavirāgaḥ kaṣāyatyāgaśca guṇēṣvanurāgaḥ । karuṇāyāmapramādaḥ sa dharmaḥ śivasukhōpāyaḥ ॥ 28 ॥
sa punarjinabhaṇita ēva sukhārthinā tēna tatra yatitavyam । anyathā''mra śraddhayā sēcanamarkavr̥kṣāṇām ||29||
tatrāpi dharma ēva kartavyō bhavatyasti yadi śaktiḥ । sa samagrasaṅgavigamātparamāṅgaṁ yēna mōkṣasya || 30
alpavīryāṇāṁ tadyōgyatayā rahitānāmagāridharmō'pi । kālakramēṇa bhavabhayaduḥkhānāṁ jalāñjaliṁ dadāti ॥31॥
ityādidēśanāṁ śrutvā raṇavīrarājēna bhaṇitam । bhagavan ! yadyucitō'haṁ yatidharmaṁ dēhi tadā mē ||32||
tatō bhaṇitaḥ sa guruṇā nirvighnaṁ bhavatu tavaiṣō'rthaḥ । atha rājā nijakumāraṁ guṇajaladhiṁ sthāpayitvā rājyē ॥ 3
gr̥hṇāti svayaṁ dīkṣāṁ guṇajaladhinr̥pō'pi dharaṇamityutaḥ । dēśaviratiṁ prapadya natvā ca guruṁ vrajati gēhē ||34|
mōcayati guptīḥ kārayatyaṣṭāhikā jinagr̥hēṣu । sādharmika vātsalyaṁ dīnajanōddharaṇamanyacca ॥ 35 ॥
pravrajyāṁ gr̥hṇan yad rājā bhaṇati karōti tatsarvam । sthāpayati dharaṇamamātyaṁ svayaṁ tadyacchati dharmē ॥ 36 ॥
athānyadā narēndrō rajanyāmardharātrasamayē । paśyati kamaladalākṣīmēkāṁ navayauvanāṁ ramaṇīm ||37||
tanukāntiprahatatimirāṁ ḍamarukahastāṁ suvarṇadaṇḍakam । vararatnāvalīkaṇṭhāṁ sitavastrāṁ pādukārūḍhām ||38||
tatastāṁ pr̥cchati rājā kā'si tvaṁ kēna kāraṇēnēha | kṣaṇaśaśisamānavadanē ! saṁprāptā, kathayati sāpi tataḥ ॥ 39
īṣadvikasadvadanā prabhaṇati pratyaṅginyahaṁ vidyā । itō bhavāt tr̥tīyē bhavē vihitā mama tvayā ॥ 40 ॥

rajjaṁ kulakamā yariṇamitra tuha dhanna ! mannamāgassa । kiṁkarabhāvaṁ pattā kajjavisēsēsu sariyanvā ||43||
tō udvivirannā dinamāsaṇaṁ tīi taha imaṁ bhaṇiyā । aṇavbhuvāṇāviṇaō khamiyanvō majjha dēvī || 44 ॥
tumhē guṇāhiyā majjha aviṇaō avirayāē kō tumha ? | iya bhaṇiuṁ kaṁṭāō niyāō rayaṇāvalī tīē ।
khittā nivasa kaṁṭhē kahiyaṁ ēvaṁ ca tīi māhaṣpaṁ । jaha kaṁṭhagayāē imāē jati ariṇōvi bhicattaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
ya bhaṇiuṁ sārannāṇunnāyā vaccaē niyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ । rāyāvi syaṇisēsaṁ dhammajjhāṇēṇa nigamaī ||47 ||
divasanā kāūṇāvassayāikiriyāō । atthāṇē svaviṭṭō kaṁṭhē rayaṇāvali kāuṁ ||48 ||
tī pahāvēṇa taō nivastra acētapacaṇīyāvi । naravaiṇō valaguruṇō sirēṇa āṇaṁ paḍicchaṁti ।। 49 ।
gōṭhaviḍaṁ rajjadhuraṁ dharaṇāmaccami niñcalō niccaṁ । jiṇadhammakammaniraō gamēi kālaṁ bhavigō ॥50॥
sāgara siṭṭi suvāvivāhē pavaṭṭamāṇampri । rajjaṁtarāgaēṇaṁ varapiuṇā mahaṇadēvēṇa || 51||
bhavadaviē jāē kōlāhalē sayaṇavaggō । ālōccaṁtō diṭṭhō dharaṇēṇaṁ ṭāgaṭhāṇēsu ॥ 52 ॥
jō
bhai tumha maṁtō ēsa maē avagaōmha mammāī । niyarannō sāhissaha, taṁ sōuṁ mahaṇadēvasuō || 53 ॥
duttuṁḍō tayabhimuhaṁ bhaṇai jahā lūḍiyaṁ imaṁ rahaṁ । taha amhēvi hu icchasi lūḍēḍaṁ, taṁ ca suṇiūṇa ॥ 54 ॥
kuviō gharāviṇaṁ baṁdhāvara tē taō ya tajjaṇaō । tapaḍivakkhē caḍiō jaṁpaō sōvi taha caiva ॥ 55 ॥
mēliyapuralōō dharaṇaṁ vinnava sāyarō siṭṭī | akayavarāhāṇēvaṁ kiṁ juttaṁ vaṁdhaṇamimēsi 1 ॥ 56 ॥
aṇa dharaṇō amaccō rāyaviruddhā maṁtayatāvi । akayavarāhā ēē tumaṁpi, iya vayaṇapaḍivaṇē ॥57॥
rājyaṁ kulakramāgatarṇamiva tava dhanya ! manyamānasya । kiṁkarabhāva prāptā kāryaviśēṣēṣu smartavyā ॥ 43 ॥
ta utthāya rājñā dattamāsanaṁ tasyāstathēdaṁ bhaṇitā । anabhyutthā nāvinayaḥ kṣantavyō mama dēvyā ||44 ॥
yūyaṁ guṇādhikā mamāniyō'viratāyāḥ kō yuṣmākam । iti bhaṇitvā kaṇṭhād nijād ratnāvalī tathā ॥ 45 ॥
kṣiptā nr̥pasya kaṇṭhē kathitamēvaṁ ca tasyā māhātmyam । yathā kuṇṭhagatāyāmasyāṁ yāntyarayō'pi bhr̥tyatvam || 46 ॥
ti bhaṇitvā sā rājñā'nujñātā vrajati nijaṁ sthānam । rājāpi rajaniśēṣaṁ dharmadhyānēna nirgamayati ॥ 47 ॥
uditē divasanāyē kr̥tvā''vaśyakādikriyāḥ । āsthāna upaviṣṭaḥ kaṇṭhē ratnāvalīṁ kr̥tvā ॥48॥
tasyāḥ prabhāvēṇa tatō nr̥pasyātyantapratyanīkā api । narapatayō balaguravaḥ śirasā''jñāṁ pratīcchanti ॥ 49 ॥
tataḥ sthāpayitvā rājyadhurāṁ gharaṇāmātyē niścalō nityam | jinadharmakarmaniratō gamayati kālaṁ bhavōdvignaḥ ॥50॥
atha sāgaraśrēṣṭhigr̥hē sutāvivāhē pravartamānē । rājyāntarāgatēna varapitrā mahanadēvēna ॥ 51 ॥
ābhāvyadravyaviṣayē jātē kōlāhalē svajanavargaḥ । ālōcyamānō dr̥ṣṭō varaṇēna sthānasthānēṣu ||12||
tatō bhaṇati yuṣmākaṁ mantra ēṣa mayāvagatō'smākaṁ marmāṇi । nijarājāya kathayiṣyatha, tat śrutvā mahanadēvasutaḥ ॥
dustuṇḍastadabhimukhaṁ bhaṇati yathā luṇṭitamidaṁ rāṣṭram । tathā'smānapi khalvicchasi luṇṭituṁ tacca śrutvā ॥
kupitō dhārayitvā bandhayati taṁ tataśca tajjanakaḥ । tatpratipakṣē caṭitō jalpan sō'pi tathaiva ॥ 55॥
tō mēlitapuralōkō dharaṇaṁ vijñapayati sāgaraḥ śrēṣṭhī । akr̥tāparāvayōrēvaṁ kiṁ yuktaṁ bandhanamanayōḥ 4 ॥ 56 ॥

varaṁ kuviō sāgarammi dharaṇō gharāviḍaṁ tassa । savrvvapi hu gharasāraṁ lhasāviya vivai bhaṁḍārē || 58
agannara savvēvi hu purapahāṇēvi tēhiṁ tō gaṁtuṁ । vinnattō naranāhō sacivaṁ hakāriu bhai ||29||
ēē bhaṇati jaṁ taṁ kiṁ saccaṁ, sō bhaṇēi kimasaccaṁ । tuha bhaṁḍāraṁ bharimō jē tē amhēcciya na saccā !
agai nivō ki imiṇā, avarāhō jō imēsi taṁ kahaha । rāyaviruddhāī imē maṁtati imaṁ kahai dharaṇō ॥ 66
tō rāyā tē pucchara uttarapaccattarēhiṁ tō tēhiṁ । vihiō niruttarō sō rāyaṁ para jaṁpaē ēvaṁ ||62 ||
pāgayajaṇēṇa saddhi uttarapaccuttarāī kārēsi । jō ahamannāyaparō tuha paḍihāmi cittami ||63 ||
tā kōvinayaparō jō tassa samappēha appaṇō muhaṁ । iya bhaṇiuṁ hatthāō uttārivikhivai taṁ dūrē ||6|
tō rāyā bhaṇai imaṁ kiṁ mudaṁ muyaha, kuṇasu nīīē । paripālaṇaṁ payāṇaṁ bhaṁḍāraṁ bharasu nāṇaṁ ||65 ||
yataḥ,

annapi tujjha ēsō bīyammi vayammi bīya aiyārō । tā ālōyasa ēvaṁ gaṁtūṇa guruṇa payamūlē ||66 |
sō sō aṇakkhabhariō uṭṭiya gēhammi jāi tō ṭhavai । rāyā annamamaccaṁ appāvara vaṇiyagharasāraṁ ॥ 6
tēṇa ya annāēṇaṁ davvaṁ lōmaō appaṇā gahiyaṁ । ladbhāvasarō lōō dhariūṇaṁ lēi taṁ tattō ॥ 68॥

lahiūṇa chalaṁ churiyāē āhaō taha jahā gaō nihaṇaṁ । rudrajjhāṇōvagaō pattō taccāē puḍhavīē ॥ 7

bhaṇati dharaṇō'mātyō rājaviruddhāni mantrayantō'pi । akr̥tāparādhā ētē tvamapi iti vacanaprativacanē ॥
vartamānē kupitaḥ sāgarē dharaṇō vārayitvā tasya । sarvamapi khalu gr̥hasāraṁ suṁsitvā kṣipati bhāṇḍāgārē ||"

bhagati nr̥paḥ kimanēna, aparādhō ya ēṣāṁ taṁ kathayata । rājaviruddhānīmē mantrayantīdaṁ kathayati dharaṇaḥ ||6|
tatō rājā tān pr̥cchatyuttara pratyuttaraistatastaiḥ । vihitō niruttaraḥ sa rājānaṁ pratijalpatyēvam ॥ 62 ॥
prākr̥tajanēna sārdhamuttarapratyuttarāṇi kārayasi । yadyahamanyāyaparastava pratibhāsē cittē ॥ 63 ॥
tā kō'pi nayaparō yastasmai samarpayatātmanō mudrām । iti bhaṇitvā hastāduttārya kṣipati tāṁ dūrē ||64|
tatō rājā bhaṇatīmaṁ kiṁ mudrāṁ muñcasi, kuruṣva nītyā । paripālanaṁ prajānāṁ bhāṇḍāgāraṁ bhara nyāyēna ॥
anyadapi tavaiṣa dvitīyē tratē dvitīyāticāraḥ । tasmādālōcayaitad gatvā gurūṇāṁ pādamūlē ||66 ||
tataḥ sa rōṣabhr̥ta utthāya gr̥hē yāti tataḥ sthāpayati । rājā'nyamamātyamarpayati vaṇigr̥hasāram ||67||
tēna cānyāyēna dravyaṁ lōkādātmanā gr̥hītam । labdhāvasarō lōkō dhr̥tvā lāti tat tataḥ ॥ 68 ॥
atha kuṇṭhēnaikēna lañcādravyaṁ mārgayamāṇēna । dhr̥taṁ taṁ kuṭṭayati bhr̥tyaistathā tēna ||69 ||
lañdhvā chalaṁ kṣurikayā''hatastathā yathā gatō nivanam । raudradhyānōpagataḥ prāptastr̥tīyāṁ pr̥thivīm ॥70॥

tattō bhamiūṇa bhavē kayāi pāvihai mōkkhasōkkhapi । guṇa jalaniravaīvi hu nimpala gihidhammasaṁjuttō ॥
jiṇasāsaṇammi sayayaṁ rahajattāpamuhavividhaūhiṁ । ucchapaṇā pavatta kārāvai garuyajiṇabhavaṇē || 72 ॥
jinnuddhārapurassaramamāriyōsapi savyavitayampi | sāhammiyavacchallāī kuṇaī saddhammakicāī ॥ 73 ॥
pajjatē pavvajjaṁ pavajjiūṇaṁ samāhimaraṇēṇa । sōhammē uvavannō taiyabhavē sivasuhaṁ lahihī ॥74॥
iya bhamiō saṁsārē dharaṇō vīyavvayassa bīēṇa । aiyārēṇa tamhā vajjaha ēyapi jattēṇa ॥ 75 ॥
॥ iti mr̥ṣāvādavatē dvitīyāticāravipākē dharaṇākhyānakaṁ samāptam ॥
tatō bhrāntvā bhavē kadācitprāpsyasi mōkṣasaukhyamapi । guṇajaladhinarapatirapi hi nirmalagr̥hidharmasaṁyuktaḥ ॥ 71 ॥
jinaśāsanē satataṁ rathayātrāpramukha vividhahētubhiḥ । utsarpaṇāḥ pravartayati kārayati gurujinabhavanāni ॥ 72॥
jīrṇōddhārapurassara mamārighōṣamapi sarvaviṣayē । sādharmika vātsalyāni karōti saddharmakr̥tyāni ॥73॥
paryantē pratrajyāṁ prapadya samādhimaraṇēna । saudharmē upapannastr̥tīyabhavē śivasukhaṁ lapsyatē ॥74॥
iti bhrāntaḥ saṁsārē dharaṇō dvitīyatratasya dvitīyēna । aticārēṇa tasmād varjayatatamapi yatnēna ॥ 75 ॥

gayasaṁkhalacchikaliyaṁ viṇhutaṇuṁ pitra sudaṁsaṇāhāraṁ । suvirāiyaṁ varēhiṁ rayaṇēhiṁ rayaṇapuranagaraṁ ||2||

iti bhaṇitvā vanditaḥ saḥ, dhyānaṁ saṁhr̥tya dharmalābhēna । abhinanditāvanēna, dvijēnaikēna tatō bhaṇitam ॥8॥
kiṁ bhōḥ ! māṁ muktvaiṣa śūdrō'bhivādita ēvam । prāptē mānasasara sē kaḥ pibati khātikānīram ॥9॥

saṁgaṇakahā ।

taya ucivā muṇiṇā pāraddhā dhammadēsaṇā jāva । tā baṁbhaṇēṇa puṭṭhō samasārō muṇivarō ēvaṁ ||15||
tuha ataṇū taṇulacchī sāhai vararāyalacchivicchaḍuṁ । chaḍḍiya vayaṁ pavannaṁ tumaē, tā kahasu vēraggē ॥ 16॥
kō ū, āha muṇī bhavammi vēraggahēuṇō sulahā । tahavi visēsēṇa idaṁ hēū maha paṇaiṇī jāyā || 17॥
tō tēṇa puṇō bhaṇiyaṁ vr̥ttaṁtamiṇa savittharaṁ kahaha । jai puṇa taṁ sōūṇaṁ vēragaṁ hōi amhapi || 18 ||
tō jaṁpa muṇicadō iṁdōvi hu niyayacariyakahaṇēṇa । lajjai, tahavi kahijjai tumhaṁ uvayāra hē utti ।। 19 ।।
tathāhi ;-
āsī rahavīrapuraṁ samarakariṁdō nivōvi guṇanilaō | bhajjā viṇayasusajjā mayaṇa sirīnāmiyā tassa ||
visayahanahavatāṇa tāṇa supasatyalakkhaṇōvēō । jāō suō suruvō nāmēṇaṁ mēghakumarōti ॥ 21 ॥
aha annayā nidāhē dāhajjarapīḍiē nariṁdampi | mayaṇasirī varavijjōvadaṁsiē ōsa hē kuṇai ||22|
kaḍhai jalaṁ ḍaivauttā karēi savvaṁpi tassa sayamēva । niyachāyavva sathāvi hu tappāsaṁ muyai na kayāvi ||23||
satta diṇāṇi ya laṁghai samaṁ naridēṇa piyai kaḍhiyajalaṁ । ōyāiyaṁ ca icchai tahērisaṁ khittadēvīē ॥ 24॥
sillēhi viddhāhi bāhāhiṁ jōḍiyāhi dōrhipi । niyaliyapayāē bhuvaṇē kāyavvā hamaē jaccā || 25 |
bhavivyāvasēṇa saṁjāō naravarō pauṇadēhō । tīē bhaṇiyavihīē dēvīē lahu kayā jattā ॥ 26 ॥
tō naranāhō ēvaṁ citaṛa dēvīē majjha uvarimmi । appuvva paḍibaṁdhō jīviyamavi cayai maha kajjē ॥ 27 ॥
iti vacanāmr̥tōpaśāntāmitājñānarōgasaṁtāpaḥ । vanditvā dvijaḥ sādhuṁ savinayamavanāvupaviṣṭaḥ ॥ 14 ॥
tasya cōcitā muninā prārabdhā dharmadēśanā yāvat । tāvad brāhmaṇēna pr̥ṣṭaḥ śamasārō munivara ēvam ॥ 19 ॥
tavātanustanulakṣmīḥ kathayati vararājalakṣmīvistāram । muktvā vrataṁ prapannaṁ tvayā, tasmātkathaya vairāgyē ॥ 16 ॥
kō hētu:, āha munirbhavē vairāgyahētavaḥ sulabhāḥ । tathāpi viśēṣēṇēha hēturmama praṇayinī jātā ॥ 17 ॥
tatastēna punarbhaṇitaṁ vr̥ttāntamimaṁ savistaraṁ kathaya । yadi punastaṁ śrutvā vairāgyaṁ bhavatyasmākamapi ॥18॥
tatō jalpati municandra indrō'pi khalu nijacaritakathanē । lajjatē, tathāpi kathyatē yuṣmākamupakārahēturiti ॥19॥
āsīd rathavīrapuraṁ samarakarīndrō nr̥pō'pi guṇanilayaḥ । bhāryā vinayasusajjā madanaśrīnāmikā tasya ॥ 20 ॥
viṣayasukhamanubhavatōstayōḥ supraśastalakṣaṇōpētaḥ । jātaḥ sutaḥ surūpō nāmnā mēghakumāra iti ॥ 21 ॥
athānyadā nidāghē dāhajvarapīḍitē narēndrē । madanaśrīrvara vaidyōpadarśitānyaiauṣadhāni karōti ॥ 22 ॥
।
kvathati jalamupayuktā karōti sarvamapi tasya svayamēva । nijacchāyēva sadāpi hi tatpārśva muñcati na kadāpi ॥ 23 ॥
sapta dināni ca laṅghatē samaṁ narēndrēṇa pibati kvathitajalam । upayācitaṁ cēcchati tathēdr̥śaṁ kṣētradēvyāḥ ॥ 24 ॥
kuntairvidvābhyāṁ bāhubhyāṁ yōjitābhyāṁ dvābhyāmapi । nigaḍitapādadyā bhuvanē kartavyā tava mayā yātrā || 25॥
bhavitavyatāvaśēna saṁjātō naravaraḥ praguṇadēhaḥ । tayā bhaṇitavidhinā dēvyā laghu kr̥tā yātrā || 26॥
tatō naranātha ēvaṁ cintayati dēvyā mamōpari । apūrvaḥ pratibandhō jīvitamapi tyajati mama kāryē ||27||
1. bhagada muṇivariṁdō । 2 ga. patthapi huka ।

supāsanāha cariśrammi-
0
tō tīē aṇurattō avahīrai sayalamannamavarōhaṁ । aha annayā nisāē tīicciya vāsabhavaṇammi ||28||
jā ci naranāhō iya bhaṇiyaṁ tāva tattha kēṇāvi । ōsuyai suhī lōō ajjavi, tattō imaṁ vayaṇaṁ ॥ 29 ॥
- sāṁhikvēvaṁ sōuṁ sāmarisaṁ bhaṇai naravarō ēvaṁ | kassēsō bhō ! sō pāhariyā ! kahaha muṇiūṇa || 3
tō saṁbhatā tēvi hujā kiṁcivi jaṁpihaṁti tā dēvī । pabhaṇai kā pahu ! saṁkā jāmillasyāulē bhavaṇē || 3
kōsī pavisa kō khivai karaṁ jalaṁtajalaṇammi | kaṁḍuyai kō'hituṁḍaṁ kō piyai payaṁ ca pullīē ?
jattha pavaṇōvi na visai dinakarakiraṇāvi jattha na caraṁti । kaha tattha gihē tuha visau kōvi, tānāha ! ēmē
nisuō sadō ēsō mā bhaṁti kuṇaha paranarapavēsē । tō rāyā tavvayaṇaṁ parvacapauraṁ nisuṇiūṇa ||34||
saṁkiyahiyaōvi hu nivvuucca kavaḍēṇa jāva niddāi । tā sā saṇiyaṁ saṇiyaṁ uṭṭhiya ughāḍiya kavā
āsannē ciya bhaṁḍāramaṁdirē pavisiūṇa ālavai । dāsīvēsa purisaṁ sō ya na sē dēi paḍivayaṇaṁ || 36
pāēsaṁ nivaḍiuṁ sā pabhaṇai apiyaṁgasaṁgadavadahaṁ । nivvavasu maha sarīraṁ piya ! niyasaṁgāmayarasēṇa || 3 |
tahavihu avahīraṁtaṁ taṁ sā baṁdhēttu bāhupāsēṇa । sihiṇatūlīē ṭhaviu vimāṇaē mukkasikkāraṁ ||38|
aha tammaggē laggōṁ samāgaō naravarō tamuddēsaṁ । paccakkhaṁ ciya pāsai suṇai ya tavvavasiya savvaṁ ॥ 39
tō kōvāō tāī jā kila dō khaṁḍihī ya khaggēṇa । tā takkhaṇēṇavi cittammi ṭhāi iya puhavināhasa
arikarikuṁbha phālaṇamuttā daṁtura karālakaravālē । kaha galiyasīlajīyāṇa vahau iya mōhasuttāṇa ? ॥41
iya saṁvariṁu kharaṁga kōvēṇa samaṁ puṇōvi vāsaharē । gaṁtr̥ṇaṁ pallēkē ōllariō pasamakayacittō ॥ 42 ॥
tatastasyāmanuraktō'vadhīrayati sakalamanyamavarōdham । athānyadā niśi tasyā ēva vāsabhavanē ||28||
yāvattiṣṭhati naranātha iti bhaṇitaṁ tāvattatra kēnāpi । avasvapiti sukhī lōkō'dyāpi tata idaṁ vacanam ॥29
sāvikṣēpaṁ śrutvā sāmarṣa bhaṇati naravara ēvam । kasyaiṣa bhōḥ ! śabdaḥ prāharikāḥ ! kathayata jñātvā ॥ 30 ॥
tataḥ saṁbhrāntāstē'pi hi yāvatkiñcidapi jalpiṣyanti tāvadēvī । prabhaṇati kā prabhō ! śaṅkā yāmikaśatākulē bhavanē
kaḥ siṁhaguhāṁ praviśati kaḥ kṣipati karaṁ jvalajjvalanē । kaṇḍūyati kō'hituṇḍaṁ kaḥ pibati payaśca vyāghrayāḥ
yatra pavanō'pi na viśati dinakarakiraṇā api yatra na canti । kathaṁ tatra gr̥hē tava viśatu kōpi tasmānnātha ! ēvamēva
śrutaḥ śabda ēṣa mā bhrānti kuruta paranarapravēśē । tatō rājā tadvacanaṁ prapañcapracuraṁ śrutvā ॥ 34 ॥
śaṅkitahr̥dayō'pi khalu nirvr̥ta iva kapaṭēna yāvannidrāti । tāvatsā śanaiḥ śanairutthāyōnāṭya kapāṭān ॥35
āsanna ēva bhāṇḍāgāramandirē praviśyālapati । dāsīvēṣaṁ puruṣaṁ sa ca na tasyai dadāti prativacanam ॥ 36 ॥
pādayōrnipatya sā prabhaṇatyapriyāṅgasaṅgadavadagdham । nirvāpaya mama śarīraṁ priya ! nijasaṁgamāmr̥tarasēna ॥ 37॥
tathāpi khalvavadhīrayantaṁ taṁ sā badūvā bāhupāśēna । stanatūlyāṁ sthāpayitvā vimānayati muktasītkāram ॥30
atha tanmārgē lagnaḥ samāgatō naravarastamuddēśam । pratyakṣamēva paśyati śr̥ṇōti ca tadvyavasitaṁ sarvam ॥39॥
tataḥ kōpāttau yāvatkila dvidhā khaṇḍayiṣyati ca khaṅgēna । tāvattatkṣaṇēnāpi cittē tiṣṭhatīti pr̥thivīnāthasya
arikari kumbhāsphālana muktādanturakarālakaravālaḥ । kathaṁ galitaśīlajīvitau hantviti mōhaptau ? ॥ 41 ॥

mayaṇakahā ।
313
bhāvēi bhavasarūvaṁ tanuṁ ca nārīṇa paṇayabhāvaṁ ca । ahaha ! bhavē jaṁpi suhaṁ taṁpi hu paramatthaō dukkhaṁ ||43||
uktaṁ ca-
"duḥkhacchēdē sukhabhrāntirbhrātaḥ ! yēyaṁ vibhāti tē । tāṁ vibhāvaya kiṁ saukhyaṁ kiṁ dr̥ḥ khāduḥkhavismr̥tiḥ ? ||”
ramaṇīṇa ramaṇīyaṁ kimatthi dēhē amijjhabhariyammi ? | bahuchiddajharaṁtā suirasammi taha asuiummi ? || 44॥
savvāuvi ramaṇīō ramaṇīyāō havaṁti tā jāva । ākibhūyavivēyā picchaṁti na tattabuddhīē ॥ 45 ॥
ēyāsu aipasattā purisā pārvati vividukkhāī । avamāṇaṇāiyāī nirayānalativvatābāī || 46 ॥
jō
puṇa bhaṇē 'ēsā sasahā paṇaiṇī maiṇurattā' । nissiṁgō sō gōṇō vivēyaparivajjiyattāō ||47||
kāraṇavamēṇa phēṇai jaṇāṇuvittīē atthalōbhēṇa । payaḍaṁti kahavi nēhaṁ thēvō puṇa tāsu sambhāvō ||48 ॥
iya citatō rāyā jā ciṭṭhā tāva caramarāīē । saṇiyaṁ saṇiyaṁ parisakkiūṇa tō tassa sijjā ।। 49 ॥
āgaṁtūṇa pattā gāḍhaṁ āliṁgiūṇa tadēhaṁ । nidāvasaucca nivō pavīhiō mahuravāṇīē || 50||
takkālōciyavihiṇā rannā saṁbhāsiuṁ imaṁ bhaṇiyā । ajjavi na muyai nidā maha pāsaṁ paṇaiṇi! tumaṁtra || 51 ॥
atrāntarē paṭhitaṁ kālanivēdakēna;-
gamiūṇaṁ gayaṇasirī savvaṁ dōsāyarēṇa saha syaṇi । payaḍaṁtī aṇurāyaṁ saṁpai diṇanāhamaṇusaraha ॥52॥
iya tavvayaṇaṁ sōuṁ rāyā utti gōsakiccāī | kāṁūṇaṁ atthāṇē uvavisara harivva suramajjhē || 53 ||
saṁbhāsēuṁ lōyaṁ savrvvapi jahōciyaṁ uciyasamaē । varakarikhaṁdhārūḍhō gaō varhi rāyavāḍī ||54 ||
sahayāratarussa talē uvasamapuṁja muṇivaraṁ dayuṁ । uttariḍaṁ gayakhaṁdhāu vaṁdaē paramabhattīē ॥ 55 ॥
iti saṁvr̥tya khaṅgaṁ kōpēna samaṁ punarapi vāsagr̥hē । gatvā palyaṅkē suptaḥ praśamakr̥tacittaḥ ||42 ||
bhāvayati bhavasvarūpaṁ tanūṁ ca nārīṇāṁ praṇayabhāvaṁ ca । ahaha ! bhavē yadapi sukhaṁ tadapi khalu paramārthatō duḥkham ॥43॥
ramaṇīnāṁ ramaṇīyaṁ kimasti dēhē'mēdhyabhr̥tē । bahucchidrakṣaradaśucirasē tathā'śucihētauṁ ? ॥ 44 ॥
sarvā api ramaṇyō ramaṇīyā bhavanti tāvad yāvat । āvirbhūtavivēkāḥ paśyanti na tattvabuddhayā ॥ 45 ॥
ētāsvatiprasaktāḥ puruṣāḥ prāpnuvanti vividhaduḥkhāni । avamānanādikāni nirayānalatīvratāpāni ॥ 46 ॥
yaḥ punarbhaṇati 'ēṣā sasnēhā praṇayinī mayyanuraktā' । niḥśr̥ṅgaḥ sa gaurvivēkaparivarjitatvāt ॥47॥
kāraṇavaśēna kēnacijjanānuvr̥ttyā'rthalōbhēna । prakaṭayanti kathamapi snēhaṁ stōkaḥ punastāsu sadbhāvaḥ || 48 ॥
iti cintayan rājā yāvattiṣṭhati tāvaccaramarātrau । śanaiḥ śanaiḥ pariṣvaṣkya tatastasya śayyāyām ||49 ॥
āgatya prasuptā gāḍhamāliṅgya taddēham । nidrāvaśaga iva nr̥paḥ prabōdhitō madhuravāṇyā ॥50॥
tatkālōcitavidhinā rājñā saṁbhāṣyēdaṁ bhaṇitā । adyāpi na muñcati nidrā mama pārśva praṇayini ! tvamiva ॥51॥
gamayitvā gaganaśrīḥ sarvā dōṣākarēṇa saha rajanim । prakaṭayantyanurāgaṁ saṁprati dinanāthamanusarati ॥52॥
iti tadvacanaṁ śrutvā rājōtthāya prātaḥ kr̥tyādi । kr̥tvā''sthānē upaviśati haririva suramadhyē ||13||
saṁbhāṣya lōkaṁ sarvamapi yathōcitamucitasamayē । varakariskandhārūḍhō gatō bahī rājavāṭyām ||14||
