dāūṇa dhammalābhaṁ muṇiṇā bhaṇiō narēsarō ēvaṁ । ajjavi i vilasijjai muṇiēvi nisāē vr̥ttaṁtē

tō muṇiṇāṁ saṁlattaṁ kiṁ ciṁtāē imāē naranāha ! | taṁ 'ciṁtasu jēṇa viḍavaṇāō nō huṁti puṇa ēvaṁ ||5

sō dhammō hōi duhā jaigihibhēēṇa tattha jaidhammō । pavara mahavvayaṁmūlō iyarō ya aṇuvvayāīō ॥ 61 ॥

saha sampattēṇa taō paḍhamaṁ bīyaṁ caṇuvvayaṁ tēhi । pariyāṇiūṇa sammaṁ paḍivannaṁ bhāvasuddhī || 6.3 ||

sahakāratarōstalē upaśamapuñjamiva munivara dr̥ṣṭvā । uttīrya gajaskandhād vandatē paramabhaktyā ||15||
dattvā dharmalābhaṁ muninā bhaṇitō narēśvara ēvam | adyāpīti vilasyatē jñātē'pi niśō vr̥ttāntē ॥ 56॥
tatō rājñā tōṣavaśātsaviśēṣaṁ pr̥ṣṭō muniravam । bhagavan ! jñānadivākara ! katidivasastayōḥ saṁbandhaḥ ? ||17|

tataḥ prabhaṇati naranāthaḥ kathaya mē nātha ! śuddhanijadharmam । tataḥ kathitō munidharmaḥ savistarastēnāpi prapannaḥ
sa cāhama, iti kathita viśēṣanirvēda kāraṇaṁ nijam । idānīṁ śr̥ṇuta dharmaṁ samyak śivamārgagamanaratham ॥ 60 ॥
sa dharmō bhavati dvidhā yatigr̥hibhēdēna tatra yatidharmaḥ । pravaramahātratamūla itaraścāṇutratādikaḥ ॥ 61 ॥
prathamaṁ prathamaḥ kathitaḥ savistarastēṣāṁ tadasamarthānām । samyaktvādirdvitīyō'pi kathitaḥ saprapañcō'pi ॥ 62
saha samyaktvēna tataḥ prathamaṁ dvitīyaṁ cāṇutrataṁ taiḥ । parijñāya samyak pratipannaṁ bhāvaśuddhayā ॥ 63 ॥
vanditvā munivr̥ṣabhaṁ nijanijasthānēṣu tē gatāstataḥ । sādhurapi vihārēṇānyatra gataḥ, tatastē'pi ॥ 64 ॥
munikathitēna vidhinā pālayanti prayatnatō gr̥hītāniyamān । samyaktvē dr̥ḍhacittāḥ parasparaṁ paramaprītyā || 65|
kintu prakr̥tyā madana uttānaḥ parāpavādabhāsī ca । kēlikilatvakalitaḥ kalipriyō duṣpriyabhāsī ॥ 66 ॥

★ kahavi tēṇa kahiyaṁ rahassamēyaṁ tahāvi taṁ tumha । nō payaḍēḍaṁ juttaṁ jamhā mammaṁ parassa imaṁ ॥70॥
r̥ha kō jāṇai saccaṁ aliyaṁ va imaṁti aliyaviraīē । ēsa kalaṁkō jāyai, mittarahappayaḍaṇaṁ ca imaṁ ॥ 71 ॥
kalattamaṁtaō uvalakkhaṇamēva maṁtabhēyāṇaṁ । sēsāṇaṁ, sō tamhā vajjēyavvō payattēṇa ॥ 72 ॥
vaṁ dhanasārēṇaṁ puṇō puṇō sikkhavijjamāṇōvi । ēvaṁvivayaṇāī jaṁpatō viramaē nēya ||73 ||
savi ghariṇī paḍamā dhammaparā viṇayakhaṁtisaṁpannā | saṁ punnasasaharamuhī susīlakaliyā kulapasūyā ||74 ||
maha annayā ya mayaṇaṁ mōēḍaṁ sā niyammi gāmammi । nīyā niyajaṇaēṇaṁ mahūsavaṁ kaṁpi āsajja || 75 ||
tōya samāṇīyā cirēṇa campaṭṭhimittaṭhiyadēhā । puṭṭhā rahammi mayaṇēṇa kiṁ gayā tumamimamavatthaṁ ? ॥76॥
vāhāvilanapaṇā pāsuṁ nivaḍiuṁ bhaṇai sāvi । mā puccha vaiyaramimaṁ uppannaṁ maha apunēhiṁ ॥ 77 ||
sō jaṁpara ki majjhavi avalavaṇijjaṁti sā taō bhaṇai । jīviyanāha ! na ēvaṁ, kiṁtu pamāyāō jai tumha ॥
kavi hu kōviviyāṇa tō haṁ pāṇē paricayāmi dhuvaṁ । tō sō bhaṇai na ēvaṁ hōi jugaṁtēvi, kahasu tumaṁ ॥ 79 ॥
vō lajjāvasagaggayagirāē tīēvi sāhiyaṁ ēvaṁ । maha asthi lahū bhāyā aviṇayakulamaṁdiraṁ paramaṁ ॥ 80 ॥
dāraraō paramammabhāsaō paravavāyabhāsī ya । vēsājūyapasattō nittisō ahannayā kahavi ॥ 81 ॥
saṁghiyakulamajjāō majjaṁ pāūṇa āgaō gēhē । ittō ya tassa bhajjā kajjēṇa gayā jaṇayagēhaṁ ॥ 82 ॥ |
sīē ya ahaṁ bhaṇiyā jā baṁdhū ēi tujjha tā tumaē । iha amhavāsabhavaṇē ṭhāyavvaṁ, tō ahaṁ tattha ॥83॥
madanēna kathitaṁ puratō ghanasārasujana śirōmaṇēḥ । tatastēna sa bhaṇitō na yuktamiti prakaṭayituṁ tava ॥ 69 ॥
pradi kathamapi tēna kathitaṁ rahasyamētattathāpi tattava । nō prakaṭayituṁ yuktaṁ yasmānmarma parasyēdam ॥ 70 ॥
tathā kō jānāti satyamalīkaṁ vēdamityalīkaviratēḥ । ēṣa kalaṅkō jāyatē, mittrarahaḥ prakaṭanaṁ cēdam ॥ 71 ॥
svakalatramantrabhēda upalakṣaṇamēva mantrabhēdānām । śēṣāṇāṁ sa tasmād varjayitavyaḥ prayatnēna ||72 ||
ēvaṁ dhanasārēṇa punaḥ punaḥ śikṣyamāṇō'pi । ēvaṁvidhavacanāni jalpan viramati naiva ॥ 73 ॥

athānyadā ca madanaṁ muktvā sā nijē grāmē । nītā nijajanakēna mahōtsavaṁ kamapyāsādya ॥ 75 ॥
tataśca samānītā cirēṇa carmāsthimātrasthitadēhā । pr̥ṣṭā rahāsē madanēna kiṁ gatā tvāmimāmavasthām ? || 76 ॥

jā ciṭṭhāmi pattā tō tēṇa ahaṁ niyāē bhajjāē। bhaṁtīē akkaṁtā mayabhibhalamāṇasēṇa dadaṁ ॥ 84
tō bhaṇiyaṁ tuha bhajjā nāhaṁ baṁdhava ! havēmi tuha bhaiṇī । iya sōuṁ sōvi galiyamaya marō lajjiō nahō ||
tattō haṁ vigaliyasīlajīviyaṁ appayaṁ vicitaṁtī । kayamaraṇajjhavasāyā ārūḍhā jāva māluvariṁ ॥ 86
dāu jhapaṁ tattō cāraṇasamaṇō nahēṇa gacchaṁtō । diṭṭhō sōvi hu maṁ pāsiūṇa bhavaṇammi avayariō ॥
paṇayaṁ sē payakamalaṁ bhaṇiō tēṇāvi dhammalāhōti । puṭṭhā haṁ ki bhaddē ! dīsasi ēvaṁ vivannamuhī ? |
tō pāē - paḍiḍaṁ puṇōvi bhaṇiyaṁ maē jahā tumha । sugurūṇaṁ kahiyavtraṁ duccariyaṁ suddhirati ॥ 89 ॥
tō sabbō vr̥ttaṁtō tassa maē sāhiō, taō tēṇa । bhaṇiyaṁ bhaddē ! tuha ittha natthi paramatthaō dōsō ।
ēsō puṇa taha dōsō jiṇatrayaṇēṇaṁ maṇē saṇāhēvi । jaṁ iya mariuṁ vaṁchasi tattō bhaṇiyaṁ maē ēvaṁ ॥
hutaṁ ciya iya ēvaṁ jai tumha na daṁsaṇaṁ suguru ! hutaṁ । maraṇajjhavasāyavisōhaṇatthamaha tattha varaguruṇā ।।
dinaṁ mē cchittē tavaṁ bahuṁ taṁ ca mē caraṁtīē । jāyaṁ kisa sarīraṁ ēyaṁ sōuṁ taō mayaṇō ॥ 93 ॥
sīlēṇa sahāvēṇa ya saṁjāō tīē gāḍhayahiyaō । taha jaha aṇavarayaṁ ciya taṁ lālatō gamai kālaṁ ।। 9
aha annayā sa miliō mittāṇa samāṇasīlakaliyāṇaṁ । tē niyaniyavr̥ttaṁtē sāhati parōparaṁ savvē ॥
annajaṇassavi cariyaṁ payaḍaṁti hasati taha vikatthaṁti । ēvaṁ kahāpabaṁdhē rahē payaṭṭammi tucchattā ॥ 96 ॥
sāhai butaṁtaṁ taṁ maṇō mittāṇa tēvi taṁ sōuṁ । sicchāē vikatthaṁtā hasaṁti, aha mayaṇabhajjāē ॥ 9
tayā cāhaṁ bhaṇitā yāvad bandhurēti tava tāvattvayā । ihāsmadvāsabhavanē sthātavyaṁ, tatō'haṁ tatra ॥ 83॥
yāvattiṣṭhāmi prasuptā tatastēnāhaṁ nijāyāṁ bhāryāyāḥ । bhrāntyā ākrāntā sadamugdhamānasēna dr̥ḍham ॥84॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ tava bhāryā nāhaṁ bāndhava ! bhavāmi tava bhaginī । iti śrutvā sō'pi galitamadaprasarō lajjitō naṣṭaḥ ॥ 8
tatō'haṁ vigalitaśīlajīvitamātmānaṁ vicintayantī । kr̥tamaraṇādhyavasāyā''rūḍhā yāvanmālāyā upari ॥ 8
dātuṁ jhampāṁ, tataścāraṇaśramaṇō nabhasā gacchan । dr̥ṣṭaḥ, sō'pi khalu māṁ dr̥ṣṭrā bhavanē'vatīrṇaḥ ॥ 87 ॥
praṇataṁ tasya pādakamalaṁ bhaṇitastēnāpi dharmalābha iti । pr̥ṣṭā'haṁ kiṁ bhadrē ! dr̥śyasa ēvaṁ vivarṇamukhī ॥ 8
tataḥ pādayōḥ patitvā punarapi bhaṇitaṁ mayā yathā yuṣmākam । sugurūṇāṁ kathayitavyaṁ duścaritaṁ śuddhihēturiti
tataḥ sarvō vr̥ttāntastasmai mayā kathitaḥ, tatastēna । bhaṇitaṁ bhadrē ! tavātra nāsti paramārthatō dōṣaḥ ॥ 90 ॥
ēva punastava dōṣō jinavacanēna manasi sanāthē'pi । yaditi martuṁ vāñchasi tatō bhaṇitaṁ mayaivam ॥ 91 ॥
abhaviṣyadēvētyēvaṁ yadi tava na darśanaṁ sugurō ! abhaviṣyat । maraṇādhyavasāyaviśōdhanārthamatha tatra varaguruṇā
dattaṁ mē prāyaśvitē tapō bahu taca mē carantyāḥ । jātaṁ kr̥śaṁ śarīramētat śrutvā tatō madanaḥ ॥93॥
śīlēna svabhāvēna ca saṁjātastasyāṁ gāḍhahr̥tahr̥dayaḥ । tathā yathā'navaratamēva tāṁ lālayan gamayati kālam ||9
athānyadā sa militō mittrāṇāṁ samānaśīlakalitānām । tē nijanijavr̥ttāntān kathayanti parasparaṁ sarvē ||9
anyajanasyāpi caritaṁ prakaṭayanti hasanti tathā vikatthantē । ēvaṁ kathāprabandhē rahasi pravr̥ttē tucchatvāt ॥9
kathayati vr̥ttāntaṁ taṁ madanō mitrēbhyastē'pi tat śrutvā । svēcchayā vikatthamānā hasanti, aśrō madanabhāryaya

vihu gacchaṁtīē jiṇabhavaṇē tē tarhi ṭhiē dahum̐ । pacchannāē ṭhiyāē nisuyaṁ savvaṁ kahijjataṁ ॥ 98 ॥

'namukkāraparā jāyā dēvī suhammakaṣpammi । mayaṇōvi bhōyaṇaṭṭā haṭṭāu gimmi saṁpattō ॥ 102 ॥
pēcchai sakalattaṁ pucchara jaṇaṇi kahi bahū tujjha ? | sā pabhaṇai jiṇabhavaṇē gayā ya na puṇō niyattā sā ॥
tavyāharaṇatthaṁ kampayarō pēsiō lahuṁ tattha । mayaṇēṇaṁ, sōvigaō taṁ pāsai nēya, aha tassa ॥ 104 ॥
hēya kēvi malaē iha pavisaṁtī maē ya sā diṭṭhā । tatthamaō taṁ pāsai jhullaṁti rukkhasāhāē।। 105 ।।
hā ahō akajjaṁ jamimā pattā imaṁ duhāvatthaṁ । suhasīlasāliṇī, tō jhaḍatti chidēvi galapāsaṁ ॥ 106 ॥
hā taruchāyāē jalēṇa sittā na cēyaē tahavi । tō dhāhaṁ millatō saṁpattō mayaṇagēhammi || 107 ||

mukapu runaṁ taha kahavi jēṇa nayarajaṇō । rōyāviō samaggō tīē guṇē saṁbharaṇaṁ ॥ 109 ॥
īē riddhīē taṇusakāraṁ karitu sō tīē । aṭṭavasaṭṭō ciṁtā maraṇē ēīī kō hēū ? ॥110॥
kēvi sē kahiyē tuha bhajjā ajja tujjha haṭṭassa । bhittariyā diṭṭhā nisuṇaṁtī kiṁpi mayaṇa ! taē |

yamapi khalu gacchantyā jinabhavanē tāṁstatra sthitān dr̥ṣṭrā । pracchannayā sthitayā śrutaṁ sarva kathyamānam ॥ 98 ॥

rusamīpaṁ tatō gatvā jinabhavanamalayamadhyē । siddhasamakṣaṁ śuddhiṁ trōccaraṇādiṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 100 ॥
jōttarīyēṇaiva pāśaṁ kr̥tvā vr̥kṣaśākhāyām । valmīkamāruhyātmā muktō nirālambaḥ ॥ 101 ॥
janamaskāraparā jātā dēvī saudharmakalpē । madanō'pi bhōjanārthaṁ haṭṭād gr̥hē saṁprāptaḥ ॥ 102 ॥
ca paśyati svakalatraṁ pr̥cchati jananīṁ kva vadhūstava । sā prabhaṇati jinabhavanē gatā ca na punarnivr̥ttā sā ॥

thitaṁ kēnāpi malaya iha praviśantī mayā ca sā dr̥ṣṭā । tatra gatastāṁ paśyatyandōlayantīṁ vr̥kṣaśākhāyām ॥ 105 ॥
hā ahō ! akāryaṁ yadiyaṁ prāptēmāṁ duḥkhāvasthām | śubhaśīlaśālinī, tatō jhaṭiti cchittvā galapāśam ||
ktā tarucchāyāyāṁ jalēna siktā na cētati tathāpi । tata ārāṭiṁ muñcan saṁprāptō madanagēhē ||107 ||
tō madanēna pr̥ṣṭaḥ karmakarō rē ! kimēvamāraṭāṁsa ? । tataḥ sarvō vr̥ttāntaḥ kathitō madanāya tēna tataḥ ॥ 108 ॥
'danēna muktapūtkāraṁ ruditaṁ tathā kathamapi yēna nagarajanaḥ । rōditaḥ samagrastasyā guṇān smaratā ॥ 109 ॥
hatyā r̥ddhayā tanusaṁskāraṁ kr̥tvā sa tasyāḥ । ārtavaśārtaścintayati maraṇē ētasyāḥ kō hētuḥ 1 ॥ 110 ॥
taḥ kēnāpi tasmai kathitaṁ tava bhāryā'dya tava haṭṭasya । bhittyantaritā dr̥ṣṭā śr̥ṇvatī kimapi madana ! tvayā ॥ 111 ॥

sais vilavamāṇō na suyai bhuṁjēi nēya dhammaṁpi । sō kuṇa jhuṇa jhāya ṁ taṁ ciya duccariyamaṇavarayaṁ ॥

muddhō musōvaēsa dāu aīyara jō vayaṁ bīyaṁ । ihaparalōyaduhāī sō pāvara paumavaṇiucca || 1 ||
tathāhi-
supaōharapavarasaraṁ savaṇamaṇōhāri dīharacchaṁ ca । vararamaṇisarīraṁ piva malayapuraṁ nāma iha nayaraṁ ||2||
akhaliyāṇappasarō unnayavaṁsō palaṁbakararuirō | vararayaṇarēhirō surakarivva vīrō tarhi siddhō || 3 ||
supaōharā suhārā guṇapōggarasaṁgayā sirinivāsā । khaggalayā iva saralā vīramaī piyayamā tassa ||4||
tāṇa suō saṁjāō paramō nāmēṇa paumasamavayaṇō । bāhattarikalakusalō pattō ya kamēṇa tārunnaṁ ॥5॥
aha suyasāgara sāhū tēsimagārammi jāṇasālāē । tēsimaṇunnāē ṭhiō tō taṁ tē pajjuvāsaṁti ॥6॥
aha muṇivaṁdaṇa tāṇuvavidvāṇa vaṁtarō ēgō । ubaviṭṭhō sō bhaṇiō muṇiṇā kajja viṇā ēvaṁ ||7|
dukva uppāyaṁtō jaṇassa, ajjēsi dāruṇaṁ pāvaṁ । sō pabhaṇai kēlīē hōi kuṇaṁtassa kaha pāvaṁ ? ॥8॥
bhai muṇī kiṁ kēlīē kavaliyaṁ haṇai nēya tālaurḍa ? । tamhā jaha taha pīṛā parassa nō bhada ! kāyanvā ।।
kiṁca viṇā kajjēṇa jō parapīḍaṁ karēi sē pāvaṁ । ahiyayaraṁ saṁpajjai aṇatthadaṁḍō jaō ēsa ॥ 10॥
uktaṁ ca-
aṭṭhāya taṁ na baṁdhai jamaṇaṭṭāē ya baṁdhaē jīvō । aṭṭhē kālāīyā niyāmayā na u aṇaṭṭhāē ||11||
tō bhai vīrasiṭṭhī mahāṇubhāvēṇa munivara ! imēṇaṁ । ki vihiyaṁ jaṁ ēvaṁ sāsijjai, tō muṇī bhaṇai ॥
bhō bhō tara ! kiṁ tuha payaḍijjau vaiyarō imō ēsi ? | sō bhaṇai kiṁ ajuttaṁ, patthaṇamēsiṁ kuṇaha sahalaṁ ||
mugdhō mr̥ṣōpadēśaṁ dattvāticarati yō vrataṁ dvitīyam । ihaparalōkaduḥkhāni sa prāpnōti padmavaṇigiva ॥ 1 ॥
supayōbha (gha)rapravarasaraskaṁ (mālaṁ) śravaṇamanōhāri dīrgharathyaṁ (rghākṣaṁ) ca । vararamaṇīśarīramiva malayapuraṁ nāmēha nagaram ॥
askhalitadānaprasara unnatavaṁśaḥ pralambakararuciraḥ । vararatnarājamānaḥ surakarīva vīrastatra śrēṣṭhī ॥3॥
supayōbha (gha ) rā suhā (ghā)rā guṇapudgalasaṁgatā śrīnivāsā । khaḍgalatēva saralā vīramatī priyatamā tasya || 4 ||
tayōḥ sutaḥ saṁjātaḥ padma nāmnā padmasamavadanaḥ । dvāsaptatikalākuśalaḥ prāptaśca kramēṇa tāruṇyam ॥ 7॥"
atha śrutasāgarasādhustēṣāmagārē yānaśālāyām । tēṣāmanujñayā sthitastatastaṁ tē paryupāsatē ॥ 6 ॥
atha munivandana hē tō stēṣāmupaviṣṭānāṁ vyantara ēkaḥ । upaviṣṭaḥ sa bhaṇitō muninā kārya vinaivam ॥7॥
duḥkhamutpādayañjanasya, arjayāsi dāruṇaṁ pāpam । sa prabhaṇati kēlyā bhavati kurvataḥ kathaṁ pāpam ? ॥ 8 ॥
bhaṇati muniḥ kiṁ kēlyā kavalitaṁ hanti naiva tālapuṭam ? । tasmādyathā tathā pīḍā parasya nō bhadra ! kartavyā ॥
kiñca vinā kāryēṇa yaḥ parapīḍāṁ karōti tasya pāpam । adhikataraṁ saṁpadyatē'narthadaṇḍō yata ēṣaḥ ॥ 10 ॥
arthāya tanna badhnāti yadanarthāya ca badhnāti jīvaḥ । arthē kālādikā niyāmakā na tvanarthē ॥11॥
tatō bhaṇati vīraśrēṣṭhī mahānubhāvēna munivara ! anēna । kiṁ vihitaṁ yadēvaṁ śiṣyatē, tatō munirbhaṇati ॥12॥
bhō bhō vyantara ! kiṁ tava prakaṭayatāṁ vyatikarō'yamēṣām । sa bhaṇati kimayuktaṁ, prārthanāmēṣāṁ kuruta saphalām ||
1 kha bhāṇa° ।

supāsanāha- variśrammi --
aha caunāṇī bhayavaṁ sāhai kēlīkilassa taṁ cariyaṁ । jaha bharahē kaṇayapurē yā riumaddaṇō nāma || 14
buddhisamuddō maṁtī tassa suō vissuō vijayasīhō । aha annayā nariṁdō savvāvasarasmi uvavihō । 15
kārāvara picchaṇayaṁ tā paḍihārēṇa sūiē purisō | ahaṁganimittadharō saṁpattō rāyapāsamma ॥ 16 ॥
uciyapaḍivattipuvvaṁ puṭṭhō puhaīsarēṇa sō ēyaṁ । jaha maha sahāē kiṁcivi kahaha bhavissaṁ suhaṁ asuhaṁ ॥ 17
nāūṇa nimittēṇaṁ tēṇavi niyamatthara karē kāuṁ । nīsasiūṇa ya dīhaṁ puṇō puṇō matthayaṁ dhuṇiyaṁ ॥ 18
tō bhūvaiṇā bhaṇiya abhayaṁ tuha kahasu niyanimittaṇa । jassa suhaṁ asuhaṁ vā jaṁ dihaṁ natthi tuha dōsō
tō mattī paṇa sattadiṇaṁtē imassamacassa । sakuṭuṁbassa viṇāsō saṁbhāvijjai imaṁ sōuṁ ||20|:
bhai nariṁdō kō ēttha pañcaō, kahai sōvi jaha hatthī । bhaggālāṇakkhaṁbhō jai ēhī tā imaṁ sacca ॥ 21
taṁ ca tava ya jāyē tō saṁbhataṁ narēsaraṁ bhaṇai । buddhisamuddō maṁtī mā aikhēyaṁ kuṇau dēvō ||22||
sōvakkamaniruvakkamabhāvēṇaṁ āvayāu huṁti duhā । nēmittiraṇa saha maha vattanvaṁ asthi iha atthē ||23|
iccāisujutīhiṁ nivassa khēyaṁ nivāriṁu pacchā । jōisiēṇa samēō maṁtī niyamaṁdiraṁ pattō ||24||
pucchai bhuṁjāvēḍaṁ vatthāharaṇēhiṁ pūiṁu ca imaṁ । kō. hēū maha maraṇē, tēṇa vicitiya taō kahiyaṁ ||25||
tuha taṇaō jō jiṭṭhō tassavarahāu naravarō hēū । iya tāva maē nāyaṁ nicchayaō muṇai savvannū || 26
sōūṇa imaṁ maṁtī visajjaē pūiūṇa taṁ tattō । hakāriya jihasuyaṁ vaiyaramēyaṁ kahai savvaṁ ||27||
sō bhai tāya ! huṁtē mai, avarāhēṇa majjha, iya hōi । ahamēva tā marissaṁ savvāṇatthāṇa patthārī ॥ 28
atha catunō bhagavān kathayati kēlī kilasya taccaritam । yathā bharatē kanakapurē rājā ripumardanō nāma ॥ 16
buddhisamudrō mantrī tasya sutō viśrutō vijayasiṁhaḥ । athānyadā narēndraḥ sarvāvasara upaviṣṭaḥ ॥ 15 ॥
kārayati prēkṣaṇakaṁ tāvatpratihārēṇa sūcitē puruṣaḥ । aṣṭāṅganimittadharaḥ saṁprāptō rājapārśvē ॥ 16॥
ucitapratipattipūrva pr̥ṣṭaḥ pr̥thivīśvarēṇa sa ētat । yathā mama sabhāyāḥ kiñcidapi kathaya bhaviṣyacchubhamaśubham ॥ 1
jñātvā nimittēna tēnāpi nijamastakē karau kr̥tvā । niḥśvasya ca dīrgha punaḥ punarmastakaṁ dhūtam ॥ 18॥
tatō bhūpatinā bhaṇitamabhayaṁ tava kathaya nijanimittēna । yasya śubhamaśubhaṁ vā yad dr̥ṣṭaṁ, nāsti tava dōṣaḥ ॥ 19
tatō naimittikaḥ prabhaṇati saptadināntē'syāmātyasya । sakuṭumbasya vināśaḥ saṁbhāvyata idaṁ śrutvā ॥20॥
bhaṇati narēndraḥ kō'tra pratyayaḥ, kathayati sō'pi yathā hastī । bhagnālānastambhō yadyēṣyati tadēdaṁ satyam ॥2
tacca tathaiva ca jātaṁ tataḥ saṁbhrāntaṁ narēśvaraṁ bhaṇati । buddhisamudrō mantrī mā'tikhēdaṁ karōtu dēvaḥ ||22||
sōpakramanirupakramabhāvēnāpadō bhavanti dvidhā । naimittikēna saha mama vaktavyamastīhārthē ||23||
ityādisuyuktibhirnr̥pasya khēdaṁ nivārya paścāt । jyōtiṣikēṇa samētō mantrī nijamandiraṁ prāptaḥ ||24||
pr̥cchati bhōjayitvā vastrābharaṇaiḥ pūjayitvā cēmam । kō hēturmama maraṇē, tēna vicintya tataḥ kathitam ॥21
tava tanayō yō jyēṣṭhastasyāparādhānnaravarō hētuḥ । iti tāvanmayā jñātaṁ niścayatō jānāti sarvajñaḥ ॥ 26 ॥
śrutvēda mantrī visr̥jati pūjayitvā taṁ tataḥ । hakkārayitvā jyēṣṭhasutaṁ vyatikaramētaṁ kathayati sarvam ||27||

ēvaṁ ṭimmi sutthaṁ sakuṭuṁbassavi ya havai tuha tāya ! । tō bhaṇiyaṁ sacivēṇaṁ tuha maraṇē vaccha ! kiṁ sutthaṁ ॥
na hu havai ēsa maṁtō, jamahaṁ maṁtēmi taṁ taē vaccha ! । kāyavvaṁ sō pabhaṇai āisaha jamittha kāyavvaṁ ॥ 30 ॥
bhaṇiō sacivēṇaṁ sō maṁjūsabbhaṁtarammi patrisēḍaṁ । gamaha diṇāī sattavi phalajalabhariyammi dhammaparō ||31||
sō jaṁpa āēsō pamāṇamiha kiṁtu kuṇaha mā karuṇaṁ । jalamavi na piēma ahaṁ kiṁ phalamāīhiṁ kila kajjaṁ ||
tattō maṁjūsāē rahammi puttaṁ pavēsiḍaṁ sōvi । gaḍḍīē ārōviya mukkā naranāhabhavaṇammi ||33||
vinnattō naranāhō maha dēva ! ihatthi savvagharasārō । taha pēhu ! avvayabhaṁḍārabīyayāī ca savvāī ||34||
sō dēvō niyacāruyaōyaraē vāsarāī sattēva । muddāya muddiyamimaṁ rakkhāvaḍa aṁgarakkhēhiṁ ||35||
taha cētra kuṇai rāyā pucchai ya jahā imassa vasaṇassa । paḍiyārammi uvāō ki laddhō, tō bhaṇai sacivō ॥
lō dēva! uvāō vinaviyanvō sa kiṁtu dēvassa । āvaikālammi gaē, diṇāṇi taha satta ēāṇi ॥
arrai dhammaparāyaṇēṇa niyagiṭiēṇa caitra maē । bhaṇai nivō taha kijjau jaha hōi na āvayā tujjha ॥ 38 ॥
niyagihagaēṇa tattō bhaṇiō hakāriḍaṁ samaggōvi । nibbhiccabhiccavaggō jaha maha gēhammi satta diṇē ॥ 39 ॥
āhavasāmaggīsaṁgaēhiṁ ṭhāyavyamappamattēhi । tēhivi vihiya taha cētra maṁtisukayaṁ saraṁtēhi ||40||
dhanivaṇajalatīraṇasaṁgahamaha kuṇai sattadiṇajōggaṁ । sajjāvara pāyāraṁ hissa, aha sattamē divasē ॥ 41 ॥
naravaravallahadhūyaṁ kila jiṭṭō naṁdaṇō amaccassa । sijjatē ubaviḍō patthaē, kuviā ya sāvi taō ॥ 42 ॥
sa bhaṇati tāta ! sati māya, aparādhēna mama, iti bhavēt । ahamēva tasmānmariṣyāmi sarvānarthānāṁ prastaraḥ ||28||
ēvaṁ sthitē sausthyaṁ sakuṭumbasyāpi ca bhavēttava tāta ! । tatō bhaṇitaṁ sacivēna tava maraṇē vatsa ! kiṁ sausthyam ? ||
na khalu bhavatyēṣa mantraḥ, yadahaṁ mantrayāmi tattvayā vatsa ! | kartavyaṁ sa prabhaṇatyādiśata yadatra kartavyam || 30 ॥
bhaṇitaḥ sacivēna sa mañjūṣābhyantarē praviśya । gamaya dināni saptāpi phalajalabhr̥tē dharmaparaḥ ||31||
sa jalpatyādēśaḥ pramāṇamiha kintu kuruta mā karuṇām । jalamapi na pibāmyahaṁ kiṁ phalādibhiḥ kila kāryamḥ ॥
tatō mañjūṣāyāṁ rahāsa putraṁ pravēśya sō'pi । gantryāmārōpya muktā naranāthabhavanē ॥ 33 ॥
vijñatō naranāthō mama dēva ! ihāsti sarvagr̥hasāraḥ । tathā prabhō ! avyayabhāṇḍāgārabījakāni ca sarvāṇi ॥ 34 ॥
tatō dēvō nijacārukāpabarakē vāsarāṇi saptaiva । mudrayā mudritāmimāṁ rakṣayatvaṅgarakṣaiḥ ॥35॥
tathaiva karōti rājā pr̥cchati ca yathā'sya vyasanasya । pratikāra upāyaḥ kiṁ labdhaḥ, tatō bhagati sacivaḥ ॥ 36॥
labdhō dēva ! upāyō vijñapayitavyaḥ sa kintu dēvāya । āpatkālē gatē, dināni tathā saptaitāni ॥ 37॥
sthātatryaṁ dharmaparāyaṇēna nijagr̥hasthitēnaiva mayā । bhaṇati nr̥pastathā kriyatāṁ yathā bhavati nāpat tava ॥ 38 ॥
nijagr̥hagatēna tatō bhaṇitō hakkārayitvā samagrō'pi । nibhr̥tyabhr̥tyavargō yathā mama gēhē sapta dinān ||39||
āhahvasāmagrīsaṁgataiḥ sthātavyamapramattaiḥ । tairapi vihitaṁ tathaiva mantrisukr̥taṁ smaradbhiḥ ॥40॥
dhānyēndhanajalatīraṇasaṁgrahamatha karōti saptadinayōgyam । sajjayati prākāraṁ gr̥hasya, atha saptamē divasē ॥41॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
vāharai jāmaillē tēvi ya dhāvaṁti sō taō tīē । pikkhaṁtāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ chiṁdiya vēṇi karē kārḍa ||43||,
dhavalaharāō jhaṁpa dāu nāsēī tēvi paṭṭīē । dhāvaṁti tassa, sōvi hu pavisai gēhammi maṁtissa || 44 ||
tatō tē valiūṇaṁ kati rāyassa sōvi kōvēṇa । aṁtariō sēṇāvaimāṇavara jahā lahuṁ duhuṁ ||45 ||
sacivāhamamāṇāvasu baṁdhāvēḍaṁ samaṁ kuṭuṁbēṇa । sōvi taō āsanna sinnaṁ vittūṇa tattha gaō ॥ 46 ॥
maṁtigihappāyārārūḍhēhiṁ dhaṇuddharēhiṁ tasminnaṁ । āsannaṁ daṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ rē rē ! iō puraō || 47||
jai āgacchaha tō natthi jīviyaṁ tumha, taṁ ca suṇiūṇa । sēṇāṇī savvaṁpi hu paḍikhaliya balaṁ taō purisaṁ
saṁpēsiuṁ kahāvai maṁtissa jahā narēsarō ruṭṭhō । suyavaiyarēṇa tumhēṁ tā taṁ appasu naridassa || 49 ॥
|
taṁ sōūṇa maṁtī savyavibhāgē gihassa niyayassa । tassa purisassa daṁsiya bhaṇai imaṁ majjha vayaṇēṇa ॥ 50
sēṇāvaṇō sāhasa jahaṭṭhiyaṁ taha ya majjha patthaṇayā । bhaṇaha imaṁ, tumhēvi hu jāṇaha jaha rāya atthāṇē ||5
maha vasaṇamimaṁ nēmittiēṇa kahiyaṁ nivassa paccakkhaṁ । tō iya sāmaggīē ciṭṭhāmi ahaṁ ṭhiō gēhē ॥5
na ya maha puttō ēvaṁ vavasara annōvi kōvi hu sayannō । kiṁ kōvi jīviyatthī kaṁḍuyai ahissa tuṁḍīē
sakuṭuṁbassavi pāṇā majjha naridassa saṁtiyā cēva । lēu jahā paḍihāsai, kiṁtu maē asthi maṁjūsā ||5
naravarabhavaṇē mukkā avyayabhaṁḍārabīyayāī tarhi । saṁti maccitra tāī kahiyāī citha muṇijjaṁti ॥ 55 ॥
jāṇāvēmi tayatthaṁ naranāhaṁ, taha ṭhiō ya tatthēva । appēmi suyaṁ jihaṁ pacchā icchā naridassa ||56 |

iha pūrvabhavakr̥tēbhyō mucyasē pāpēbhyō yēna, tathā bhavati । sulabhō dharmē bōdhiḥ, tatpratipadya gataḥ sō'pi ॥
atha śrēṣṭhī padmayutaḥ samyaktvāṇutratādigr̥hidharmam । pratipadya yāti gr̥haṁ, viharatyanyatra sādhurapi ॥ 70 ॥
atha kō'pi tatra dhūrtaḥ samāgataḥ sō'pi bahuprabandhaiḥ । vismāyayati mugdhajanaṁ, kadāpi hi tasya pārśvē ॥
padmō'pi gataḥ kutūhalairvihitō'nēna hr̥tahr̥dayaḥ । īśvaraputra iti pradarśitaṁ ca tasmai kalpaṭippanakam ॥72॥
tatra ca rasēndrakalpastathaiva bhr̥ṅgarajavittakalpaśca । aśvagandhabrāhmītulasīśuṇṭhīpāṭhādikalpāśca ॥73॥
ētēṣu ca samarthaḥ kathitō dāridryakhaṇḍanē kōpi । bahuvyādhijarāvidravaṇapratyalaḥ kō'pi tathā kō'pi ॥ 7
vandhyāyāḥ sutajanakaḥ kō'pi ca saubhāgyakārakō'nyaḥ । kō'pi tathā'dr̥śyatvaprasādhaka iti prapañcya ||7
upajīvya ca tataḥ subahu draviṇaṁ gataḥ sō'nyatra । tatkathitavidhānēna padmaḥ satyāpayati tānkalpān ॥ 76
naca kimapi taiḥ sidhyati bhavati draviṇakṣayaḥ klēśaśca । tathāpi karōti saṁvaraṇaṁ prakaṭayati na yathāsthitaṁ lō
anyacca tasya mitraṁ dhūrtēna tēna dhūrtitamēvam । tat taṁ pr̥cchati tava sphurati kimapi kiṁ kalpaviṣayē ? || 78
sa bhaṇati sphuratyāma kathamanyathā mama bhōgavistāra: ? । tata itarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ bāndhava ! na khalu kimapi mē sphura
yadi punardhūrtēnāhaṁ vipratāritaḥ, bhaṇati tata idaṁ padmaḥ । kiṁ kalpairbahubhirvandhyākalpaṁ svamēkam ||80||
śikṣasva yēna janatō dravyaṁ prāpsyāsa, tēnēti śrutvā । bhaṇitaṁ taṁ mama prasadya kathaya, padmēna tataḥ kathitaḥ ॥
alīkō vandhyākalpaḥ sō'pi khalu vandhyābhya auṣadhāni dadāti । atha dattamanyadā naravarasya bhāryāyai vandhyā
garbhārthamauṣadhaṁ, tēna tasyāḥ śūlaṁ tathā samutpannam । yathā prāṇāḥ saṁdēhē caṭitāḥ, sa nr̥patinā tataḥ ॥ 83॥

bhai muṇī rahamaṇapurapahulīlāvilāsanaravaiṇō । līlāvaidēvīē pattō nāmēṇa guṇasēṇō || 13 ||
yō likhati kūṭalēkhamalīkavacanē gr̥hītaniyamō'pi । ihalōkē paralōkē sa bandhudatta iva labhatē duḥkham ॥ 1 ॥
suratnaśōbhaṁ surakaritanuriva tridivamiva sukavikāvyamiva । rōhaṇagiririva gajapuramihāsti rājā ca kumāragiriḥ ॥
ripukarikumbhanirbhēdabhinnamuktālikalitakhaṅgalatā । sitasitakusumā rājatē jayaśrīvēṇīva yasya karē || 3॥
vibhrama-ra-hitāpi vilāsasaṁgatā raṇamānahaṁsakasanāthā । tasyāsti priyā nalinīva guṇavarā kamalinī nāma ॥ 4 ॥
tasyāpi ca bandhudattō mantrī, athānyadā cāparādham । dr̥ṣṭvā sa mudrāṁ rājñā mōcitaḥ sahasā ||5||
sthāpitaśca viśvadattō mantrī suramantrisadr̥śamativibhavaḥ । samyaktvaprāptarēkhaḥ prakr̥tinirīhaḥ svavaśa jihnaḥ ॥ 6 ॥
krūraśca bandhudattaḥ prakr̥tyā punarapi mudrāgrahaṇārtham । pada bhraṣṭō'pi hi pārśva kṣaṇamapi na muñcati narēndrasya ॥7॥
athānyadā narēndraḥ prāptō dr̥rē vāhyālyā । sacivēna bandhudattēna saṁyutō vāhayati turagān ||8||
viparītaśikṣākśatō mantrinr̥payōsturaṅgamau tvaritam । vrajantau saṁprāptau vanagahanē, tābhyāmatha tatra ॥9॥
dr̥ṣṭaṁ munyōryugalamaśōkavarapādapasyādhaḥ । turagāvapi pariśrāntau sthitau tasmin pradēśē ॥10॥
tata uttīrya tau dvāvapi praṇamya muniyugaṁ samupaviṣṭau । atha dr̥ṣṭvā kaniṣṭhamuniṁ jyēṣṭhamuniṁ bhaṇatīti rājā ॥ 11 ॥
yathā'vamanyatē madanamayaṁ munistanuśriyā tathaiṣā । kathayati vararājaśriyamasya tasmātkathaṁ nu tattyāgaḥ 1 ॥ 12 ॥
bhaṇati munī rathamardanapurapramulīlā vilāsanarapatēḥ । līlāvatīdēvyāḥ putrō nāmnā guṇasēnaḥ ॥ 12 ॥
,
1 nagarapakṣē suratnaśōbham, surakaritanupakṣē suratnaśōbhaṁ surajanaśōbhaṁ vā, tridivapakṣē murajanaśōbhama, sukavikāvyapakṣē suracanāśōbham,
rōṇagiripakṣē suratnaśōbhamiti । 2 ga. parimuhaṁva ।

aivallahō piūṇaṁ kīlai dullaliyabālakīlāē । givhai kalākalāvaṁ piūṇa guruṇōvarōhēṇa || 14 ||
ummukavābhāvō mahānaridāṇa pavaradhūyāō । pariṇāviō vilāsē karē dugudugōvva surō ||15||
aha annā vasaṁtē ujjāṇē bhāriyāhi pariyariō । kīlai jalakīlāē kīlāvāvī, taha tattha ॥ 16
maṇirayaṇasiṁgiyāē ghusiṇā gurusumiganāhisalilēṇa । chaṁṭai niyamajjāō chaṁṭijjai sōvi tāhipi ॥ 17
aha ēkāē pahaō paōharēṇa paōharēṇēva । dhūlakaḍhiṇēṇa tattō valiō sō tīi lahu samuha ॥ 18 ॥
sā nahā vēgēṇaṁ sōvi hu paṭṭīē dhāviō gahīu । bhariyajalaṁ gurusiṁgiṁ tā jāva asōyavaṇamajjhē || 19
miliō tīē, sāvi hu ussaggaṭhiyassa sāhuṇō saraṇaṁ । paḍivannā, tō thaṁbhai jalaṁ muyaṁtarasa sē bāhu ।
muṇibhattadēvayā, tō sō uvaviṭṭhō vilakkhaō hōuṁ । muṇiṇāḍhattā aṁtaramalakhālaṇavayaṇajalakīlā ||21
tadyathā; -
jō
saṁsārō duhahēū hēū kammāṇa tassa puṇa udaō । sō tēsiṁ baddhāṇaṁ, baṁdhō kammāṇa puṇa duvihō || 22 ||
atthē aṇatthēṇaṁ, tatthatthēṇaṁ viṇā imaṁ jēṇaṁ । nivvahai nō sarīraṁ kīrai sō tassa atthammi || 23॥
puṇa ummāyāō kajjēṇa viṇāvi kōvi vāvārō । tattō jō baṁdhō sō aṇatyahē utti nāyavvō । 24
ēkamma udgavidummi jē jīvā jiṇavarēhiṁ pannattā । tē pārēvayamittā jaṁbūdīvē ṇa mājjā || 25 ||
jalaghaḍasyāṇa jīvē tumhē ēvaṁ muhā virāhaṁtā । jaṁ baṁdhaha kammabharaṁ nittharihaha taṁ kahaṁ bhadda | 1 || 26॥
uvalakkhaṇaṁ ca ēvaṁ anēvi hu thāvarē tasē taha ya । ghāyaha tubbhē jīvē tattō pāvaṁ taō naraō ||27||
ativallabhaḥ pitrōḥ krīḍati durlalitabālakrīḍayā । gr̥hṇāti kalākalāpaṁ pitrōrguruṇōparōdhēna ॥ 14 ॥
unmuktabālabhāvō mahānarēdrāṇāṁ pravaraduhitaḥ । pariṇāyitō vilāsān karōti daugunduka iva suraḥ ॥ 15 ॥
athānyadā vasanta udyānē bhāryābhiḥ parikaritaḥ । krīḍati jalakrīḍayā krīḍāvāpīṣu, tathā tatra ॥ 16 ॥
maṇiratnaśr̥ṅgikayā ghusr̥ṇāgurusumr̥ganābhisalilēna । ukṣati nijabhāryā ukṣyatē sō'pi tābhirapi ॥ 17 ॥
athaikayā prahataḥ payōbharēṇa payōdharēṇēva । sthūlakāṭhanēna tatō valitaḥ sa tasyā laghu saṁmukhaḥ ॥ 18 ॥
sā naṣṭā vēgēna sō'pi hi pr̥ṣṭhē dhāvitō gr̥hītvā । bhr̥tajalāṁ guruśr̥ṅgī tāvadyāvadaśōkavanamadhyē ||19||
militastayā, sāpi khalūtsargasthitasya sādhōḥ śaraṇam । pratipannā, tataḥ stabhnāti jalaṁ muñcatastasya bāhum ॥
munibhaktadēvatā, tataḥ sa upaviṣṭō vilakṣō bhūtvā । muninārabdhā''ntaramalakṣālanavacanajalakrīḍā ॥21॥
saṁsārō duḥkhahēturhētuḥ karmaṇāṁ tasya punarudayaḥ । sa tēṣāṁ baddhānāṁ, bandhaḥ karmaṇāṁ punardvividhaḥ ॥22॥
arthēnā'narthēna, tatrārthēna vinēdaṁ yēna । nirvahati nō śarīraṁ kriyatē sa tasyārthē ॥ 23॥
yaḥ punarunmādāt kāryēṇa vināpi kō'pi vyāpāraḥ । tatō yō bandhaḥ sō'narthahēturiti jñātavyaḥ ||24||
ēkasminnudakavindau yē jīvā jinavaraiḥ prajñaptāḥ । tē pārāpatamātrā jambūdvīpē na māyēran ॥25॥
jalaghaṭaśatānāṁ jīvān yūyamēvaṁ mudhā virādhayantaḥ । yaṁ badhnītha karmabhara nistariṣyatha taṁ kathaṁ bhadra ? ॥ 26॥
upalakṣaṇaṁ caitadanyānapi hi sthāvarāṁstrāṁstathā ca । ghātayatha yūyaṁ jīvāṁstataḥ pāpaṁ tatō narakaḥ॥ 27 ॥

acchinimīlaṇamittaṁ natthi suhaṁ dukkhamēva aṇupaddhaṁ । naraē nēraiyāṇaṁ ahōnisiṁ pañcamāṇā ||28||
tarāyaṇapariyaṇā jaṁ pāvaṁ taṁpi rāgavasapattā | annāṇaṁdhā jīvā kuṇaṁti tattaṁ ayāṇatā ||29||
annaha imēṇa taṇuṇā kāyantraṁ kiṁpi hōi ta, jēṇa । bhavanucchēō niruvamaanaṁtasivasōkkhasaṁpattī ॥30॥

-
“mahatā puṇyapaṇyēna krītayaṁ kāyanaustvayā । pāraṁ duḥkhōdadhērgantuṁ tvara yāvanna bhidyatē ॥”
iya ēvamāi suṇiuṁ muṇivayaṇaṁ nāyadhaspaparamatthō । patthara jā jaidhammaṁ tā pattō pariyaṇō tattha ॥ 32 ॥
daddaṇaṁ muṇipuraō gharōvaviddhaṁ sabhajjayaṁ kumaraṁ । mittā ya kalattāṇi ya bhāṁti kiṁ aśuciyaṁ ēvaṁ ||33||
iha uvā cihna, uṭṭhēha puracacarīō ēyāō । saphalaparissamāō karēha niyadiṭṭidāṇa ||34||
bhaṇai kumārō kiṁ caccarīhiṁ uvavisiya muṇisayāsammi । suvvara dhammō, kijjau ēsa kayatthō maṇuyajammō ॥
tō tēhi sō bhaṇiō kō'vasarō ēsa dhammasavaṇassa । ēvaṁ payaṭṭamāṇē mahasavē pauralōyassa ? ॥36॥
uha muṇipāsāō, bhaṇiō sāhūvi tēhiṁ 'muṁca imaṁ' । tō muṇiṇā saṁlattaṁ ahaṁ na ēvaṁ paḍikhalēmi|37|
tō kumarēṇaṁ kahiyaṁ tāṇaṁ mā kōvi kiṁpi maṁ bhaṇau । majjha pannā ēsā bhōtanvaṁ gahiyadivakhēṇa ॥ 38 ॥
tō tassavarōhēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mā nāha ! ērisaṁ kuṇasu । āgaccha tāyapāsē pacchā sicchā tuha ihatthē ||39॥
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ puṇaruttēṇa, niyaniyapiūṇaṁ । gacchaha bhavaṇē tumhē pavvajjaṁ vātri hi ॥ 40 ॥
akṣinimīlanamātraṁ nāsti sukhaṁ duḥkhamēvānubaddham । narakē nairayikāṇāmahōniśa pacyamānānām ||28||
tanusvajanaparijanārthaṁ yatpāpaṁ tadapi rāgavaśaprāptāḥ । ajñānāndhā jīvāḥ kurvantiṁ tattvamajānantaḥ ||29||
anyathā'nayā tanvā kartavyaṁ kimapi bhavati tat, yēna । bhavanyucchēdō nirupamānantaśivasaukhyasaṁprāptiḥ ॥30॥
tasmād bahupuṇyōpalabdhē'tra śarīrē pōtakalpē । pañca mahāvratasitapaṭamārōpya tarata bhavajaladhim ॥31॥
ityēvamādi śrutvā munivacanaṁ jñātadharmaparamārthaḥ । prārthayatē yāvadyatidharmaṁ tāvatprāptaḥ parijanastatra ||32||
dr̥ṣṭvā munipuratō gharōpaviṣṭaṁ sabhāryakaṁ kumāram । mitrāṇi ca kalatrāṇi ca bhaṇanti kimanucitamēvam ||33||
ihōpaviṣṭāstiṣṭhatha, uttiṣṭhata puracarcarīrētāḥ । saphalapariśramāḥ kuruta nijadr̥ṣṭidānēna ||34||
bhaṇati kumāraḥ kiṁ carcarībhirupaviśya munisakāśē । śrūyatāṁ dharmaḥ kriyatāmētat kr̥tārthaṁ manujajanma ||35||
tatastaḥ : sa bhaṇitaḥ kō'vasara ēṣa dharmaśravaṇasya । ēvaṁ pravartamānē mahōtsavē pauralōkasya ? || 36 ||
uttiṣṭhata munipārśvāt, bhaṇitaḥ sādhurapi tai: 'muñcēm' । tatō muninā saṁlapitamahaṁ nainaṁ pratiskhalayāmi ||37||
tataḥ kumārēṇa kathitaṁ tēbhyō mā kō'pi kimapi māṁ bhaṇatu । mama pratijñēṣā bhōktavyaṁ gr̥hītadīkṣēṇa ॥ 38 ॥
tatastasyāvarōdhēna bhaṇitaṁ mā nātha ! īdr̥śaṁ kuru । āgaccha tātapārśvē paścātsvēcchā tavēhārthē ॥ 39 ॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ kiṁ punaruktēna, nijanijapitr̥̄ṇām । gacchata bhavanē yūyaṁ pravrajyāṁ vāpi gr̥hṇīta ॥ 40 ॥

tō tassa nicchayaṁ jāṇiūṇa mittēṇa rāyapāsammi । gaṁtūṇa kumaravilasiyamēgatē sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ ॥ 41 ॥
tō takkhaṇēṇa rāyā dēvīē samanniō kumarapāsaṁ । saṁpattō kumarēṇavi nami abbhuṭṭiuṁ bhaṇiō || 42॥
paṇamaha ēvaṁ sāhuṁ tassuvarōhēṇa namiya bhaṇiō sō । mā majjha puttamēyaṁ vuggāharu payaisaralaṁpi ||43||
ēyāṇa bāliyāṇaṁ tārunnabharammi vaṭṭamāṇāṇaṁ । mā ginhasu taṁ va visaṛakaṁdōhanamā ||44 ||
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ mā tāya ! bhaṇēsu pāgayanarōvva । jō daṁsēi sumagaṁ bhullāṇaṁ bhāvibhadāṇaṁ ॥ 45 ॥
kiṁ sō va pāḍa, pāḍai sō taṁ sumaggapaḍikūlō । jō visaē hi nimaṁtara hiō hamēyassiya maīē || 46 ॥
jara tuha tāyaṇukaṁpā mai, taha jaṛa vallabhō havāē । tā niggacchataṁ bhavadavāōṁ tatthēva mā chuhaha ॥ 47 ॥

---
bhavahimajjhammi pamāyajalaṇajaliyammi mōhaniddāē । jō jaggavaḥ sa mitta, vāraṁtō sō puṇa amittaṁ ॥
iccāisaṇāē piyarē paḍivōhiūṇa pavvajjā । gahiyā imēṇa cihiṇā pacchā gacchē bahūhnipi ॥ 49 ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ bhūvaiṇā bhayavaṁ ! ēvārisa purisarayaṇaṁ । viralā jaṇēi jaṇaṇī jaṇiyācchariyaṁ tihuyaṇassa ||
amhārisāṇavi imō juttō maggō imēṇa jō vihiō । kiṁpuṇa asamatthō haiṁ, daṁsaha māṁtaraṁ amha || 51 ॥
tō muṇiṇā gidhammō kahiō aṁgīkaō ya sō tēhiṁ । tammi khaṇē tassinaṁ samāgayaṁ namivi muṇijuyalaṁ ।।
saṁpattā niyanayaraṁ dhammaṁ pāliti dōvi jahagahiyē । kiṁpuṇa sacivō maggai ahiṇavasacivassa chidāī ॥
naya pāva, tō kūrḍa lēhaṁ lihiūṇa annayā channaṁ । nigbhiccabhiccapāsamma apiuṁ dēi sō sikkhaṁ ॥ 54॥
tatastasya niścayaṁ jñātvā mittrēṇa rājapārśvē । gatvā kumāravilasitamēkāntē kathitaṁ sarvam ॥ 41 ॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna rājā dēyā samanvitaḥ kumārapārśvam । saṁprāptaḥ kumārēṇāpi natvā'bhyutthāya bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 42 ॥
praṇamataitaṁ sādhuṁ tasyōparōdhēna natvā bhaṇitaḥ saḥ । mā mama putramētaṁ vyudgrāhaya prakr̥tisaralamapi ॥43॥
ētāsāṁ bālikānāṁ tāruṇya bharē vartamānānām । mā gr̥hāṇa tvaṁ panthānaṁ vikasitōtpala nayanānām ॥44॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ mā tāta ! bhaṇa prākr̥tanara iva । yō darśayati sumārga bhraṣṭānāṁ bhāvibhadrāṇām ॥45॥
kiṁ sa panthānaṁ pātayati, pātayati sa taṁ sumārgapratikūlaḥ । yō vipayān hi nimantrayati hitō'hamētasyēti matyā ॥
yadi tava tātānukampā mayi, tathā yadi vallabhō'hamambāyāḥ । tadā nirgacchantaṁ bhavadavāt tatraiva mā kṣipata ॥
bhavagr̥hamadhyē pramādajvalanajvalitē mōhanidrāyāḥ । yō jāgarayati sa mittraṁ, vārayansa punaramittram ॥ 48 ॥
ityādidēśanayā pitarau pratibōdhya pravrajyā । gr̥hītā'nēna vidhinā paścād gacchē bahubhirapi ॥ 49||
tatō bhaṇitaṁ bhūpatinā bhagavan ! ētādr̥śaṁ puruṣaratnam । viralā janayati jananī janitāścaryaṁ tribhuvanasya ॥50॥
asmādr̥śāmapyayaṁ yuktō mārgō'nēna yō vihitaḥ । kintvasamarthō'haṁ darśayata mārgāntaramasmākam ॥51॥
tatō muninā gr̥hidharmaḥ kathitō'ṅgīkr̥taśca sa tābhyām । tasmin kṣaṇē tatsainyaṁ samāgataṁ, natvā muniyugalam ॥
saṁprāptau nijanagaraṁ dharma pālayatō dvāvapi yathāgr̥hītam । kintu sacivō mr̥gayatē'bhinavasacivasya cchidrāṇi ॥13॥
na ca prāpnōti, tataḥ kūṭaṁ lēkhaṁ likhikhā'nyadā cchannam । nirbhr̥tyabhr̥tyapārśvē'rpayitvā dadāti sa śikṣām ॥ 54 ॥

badhudattakahā ।
331
tō uddhūliyajadhō sōvi vahiṁ vāhiyālisammi । kaḍivaṭṭīē khiviṁḍaṁ lēhaṁ suttō kilaṁtuvva ॥ 55॥
rāyāvi rāyavāḍīē nimgaō tēṇa cētra maggēṇa । tattha pattō diṭṭhō sō jaggaviō bhaḍēhiṁ taō ॥ 56 ॥
saṁbhataṁ apāṇa daṁsaṁtassuṭṭiyassa tassa tahiṁ । kaḍavaṭṭīō paḍiō lēhō gahiō nivabhaḍēhi ||57 ||
kassa tumaṁtiya puṭṭhō khuddhavva na jāva jāē kiṁpi । tō daṁsiō nivaiṇō sōvi hu taṁ vāyaē lēha ||
sirivaddhamāṇanayarā rāyā riumahaṇō kusalapuvaṁ । sirivissadattamaṁti sasaṇēhaṁ sāraṁ bhai ॥ 59 ॥
saṁpattō tuha lēhō maē ya avahāriō ya tassatthō । taha caiva nivvilaṁvaṁ tayaṇuṭṭhāṇē jaissāmi || 60 ॥
jēsiṁ maṁḍaliyāṇaṁ jattiyamappāviyaṁ taē kaṇayaṁ । tēttiyamittaṁ tērsi pēsiyamaṁgīkayaṁ tēhiṁ ॥ 61॥
tujjha nimittaṁ tu maē lakkhaṁ kaṇayassa dhavalavaṇihatthē | saṁpēsiyaṁ sa ēhī thēvēhiṁ diṇēhiṁ tuha pāsē || 62 ||
pramāitthaṁ lēhassa viyāṇiuṁ naravariṁdō । taṁ lēhavāganaraṁ samappaē aṁgarakkhāṇa || 63 ||
lēhaṁ ca vissadattassa daṁsaē, sōvi vāiuṁ bhaṇai । pahu ! vinnāṇaṁ ēyaṁ kassavi maha asahamāṇassa ॥ 64॥
tō lēhavāgaṁ taṁ rāyā caḍḍāvaē tahā jaha sō | maraivva kila tahāvi hu na appara kahavi sanbhāvaṁ || 65 ॥
tō bhai vissadattō tassēsō kūḍalēhakārissa । nibbhiccō, tā suddhī maha kīrau kāliyā kuṁḍē ॥ 66 ॥
ēvaṁ hōutti narēsarēṇa bhaṇiyammi sattamīdivasē । kayavavāsō baṁbhavvayadhārī bhūmisaya ṇijjō ||67 ||
paṁcanamōkkāraparō gamiuṁ rayaṇi pabhāyasamayasmi । kālībhavaṇammi gaō rannō taha pavaralōyassa || 68 ||
pacakkhaṁ hōuṁ kāliyāē aggammi bhaṇai sō ēvaṁ । iha magaragāhatimisuṁsumārakaliē agāhammi ॥ 69 ॥
tata uddhūlitajaṅghaḥ sō'pi bahirvāhyālīdēśē । kaṭīpaṭyāṁ kṣiptvā lēkhaṁ suptaḥ klānta iva ॥ 99 ॥
rājāpi rājavāṭyāṁ nirgatastēnaiva mārgēṇa । tatra prasuptō dr̥ṣṭaḥ sa jāgaritō bhaṭaistataḥ ॥ 56 ॥
saṁbhrāntamātmānaṁ darśayata utthitasya tasya tatra । kaṭīpaṭītaḥ patitō lēkhō gr̥hītō nr̥pabhaṭaiḥ ॥ 57 ॥
kasya tvamiti ca pr̥ṣṭaḥ kṣubdha iva na yāvajjalpati kimapi । tatō darśitō nr̥patayē sō'pi hi taṁ vācayati lēkham ॥
śrīvardhamānanagarād rājā ripumardanaḥ kuśalapūrvam । śrīviśvadattamantriṇaṁ sasnēhaṁ sādaraṁ bhaṇati ||19||
saṁprāptastava lēkhō mayā cāvadhāritaśca tasyārthaḥ । tathaiva nirvilambē tadanuṣṭhānē yatiṣyē ॥ 60 ॥
yēbhyō maṇḍalikēbhyō yāvadarpitaṁ tvayā kanakam । tāvanmātraṁ tēbhyaḥ prēṣitamaṅgīkr̥taṁ taiḥ ॥69॥
tava nimittaṁ tu mayā lakṣaṁ kanakasya dhavalavaṇigvastē | saṁprēṣitaṁ sa ēṣyati stōkairdinaistava pārśvē ॥62॥
ityēvamādyarthaṁ lēkhasya vijñāya naravarēndraḥ । taṁ lēkhavāhakanaraṁ samarpayatyaṅgarakṣāṇām ॥ 63 ॥
lēkhaṁ ca viśvadattasya darśayati, sō'pi vācayitvā bhaṇati । prabhō ! vijñānamētatkasyāpi māmasahamānasya ॥ 64 ॥
tatō lēkhavāhakaṁ taṁ rājā mardayati tathā yathā saḥ । mriyata iva kila tathāpi hi nārpayati kathamapi sadbhāvam ॥
tatō bhaṇati viśvadattastasyaiṣa kūṭalēkhakāriṇaḥ । nirbhr̥tyaḥ, tasmācchuddhirmama kriyatāṁ kālikākuṇḍē ॥66॥
ēvaṁ bhavatviti narēśvarēṇa bhaṇitē saptamīdivasē । kr̥tōpavāsō brahmavratadhārī bhūmiśayanīyaḥ ॥ 67 ॥

pañcamaskāraparō gamayitvā rajaniṁ prabhātasamayē । kālībhavanē gatō rājñastathā pravaralōkasya ||68 ||

kuṁḍē jamataṁḍē iva majjha paviṭussa hōu niggamaṇaṁ । nivvigdhaṁ ciya jai ittha kumara giripuhaināhammi || 70 ॥
vāyākāra karaṇēṇaṁ karāvaṇēṇa aṇumaiṇā । hiyamēva savvakālaṁ aṇuḍiyaṁ, jai puṇa kayāvi ॥71॥
ahiē atha pavittī tā maha kuṁḍammi iha paviṭṭhassa । mā hōu nivittī, iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ jāi kuṁḍataḍē ।।72 ॥
kāūṇaṁ sāgāraṁ paccakkhāṇaṁ maṇē phuraṁtēsu । paṁcasu paramiṭṭisu jhatti dēi jhaṁpaṁ tarhi kuṁḍē ||73 ||
tō vimaladīhadalakōmalammi kamalammi sō samārūḍhō । kamalāsaṇōcca rēhai sajjaṇavayaṇē viyāsatō ॥ 74 ॥
bhamai jalamajjhayārē cuṁṭatō kamalakuvalayāīṇi । tattō suddhō muddhōtti jaṇaravō jhatti ucchaliō ||75 ||
tālāravasaṁmissō, ugghuddhaṁ taha ya baṁdivasahēṇa । taccariyacamakkiyamāṇasēṇa bhinnapuṇa || 76 ॥
tadyathā;-
jaya jiṇēsarasāsaṇu jahiṁ suparidviyahaṁ duttara āvayasarasī gōpayahaṁ ।
jiṇavaravayaṇu samaggu ju millai puṇa purisu, tasu duriyāvalī miliyaha jāyai diṇu vari ||7||
aha narapatraru papaī taṁ para himaṇu, tuha savvaha thalu jalanihi kuṁḍaha puṇu kavaṇu ? |
jali ramaṁtu dīsaṁtu jiṁva tōsahi nayaṇa, tiṁtra niyataṇuuccāiṇi maha bhuya kari pauṇa || 78 ||
iya rannā āhūō samāgaō kuṁḍatīradēsammi । dāūṇa sayaṁ bāhuṁ tattō uttāriō jhatti ॥ 79 ॥
ārōviō jayakuṁjarammi saha appaṇā nariṁdēṇa । garuyapyabhāvaṇāē pavēsiō niyayabhavaṇammi ||80||
sō lēhavāhaō abhayadānapucvaṁ puṇōvi naravaṇā । puṭṭhō ciṁtai saṁpai jai nō ēyaḍēmi sambhāvaṁ ॥ 81 ॥
,
pratyakṣaṁ bhūtvā kālyā agrē bhaṇati sa ēvam । iha makasya hatimisuṁsumārakalitē'gādhē ||39||
kuṇḍē yamatuṇḍa iva mama praviṣṭasya bhavatu nirgamanam । nirvighnamēva yadyatra kumāra giripr̥thivīnāthē ||70||
manōvākkāyaiḥ karaṇēna kāraṇēnānumatyā । hitamēva sarvakālamanuṣṭhitaṁ yadi punaḥ kadāpi ॥ 71 ॥
ahitē'sti pravr̥ttistadā mama kuṇḍa iha praviṣṭasya । mā bhavatu nivr̥ttiḥ, iti bhaṇitvā yāti kuṇḍataṭē ॥ 72 ॥
kr̥tvā sākāraṁ pratyākhyānaṁ manasi sphurattu । pañcasu paramēṣṭhiṣu jhaṭiti dadāti jhampāṁ tatra kuṇḍē ||73 ||
tatō vimaladīrghadalakōmalē kamalē sa samārūḍhaḥ । kamalāsana iva rājatē sajjanavadanāni vikāsayan ॥74॥
bhramati jalamadhyē cinvan kamalakuvalayādīni । tataḥ śuddhaḥ śuddha iti janavō jhaṭityucchatiḥ ॥75॥
tālāravasaṁmiśraḥ, udduṣṭaṁ tathā ca bandivr̥ṣabhēṇa । taccaritacamatkr̥tamānasēnōdbhinnapulakēna ॥76॥
jayati jinēśvaraśāsanaṁ yatra supratiṣṭhitasya, dustarā''patsarasī gōṣpadaḥ ।
jinavaravacanē samagraṁ yō muñcati punaḥ puruṣaḥ, tasya duritālīmilitasya jāyatē dinaṁ varṣam ॥ 77 ||
atha narapravaraḥ prajalpati taṁ prati hr̥ṣṭamanāḥ, tava sarvathā sthalaṁ jalanidhiḥ kuṇḍaḥ punaḥ kiyān ? |
jalē ramamāṇō dr̥śyamānō yathā tōṣayasi nayanē, tathā nijatanuparirambhēṇa mama bhujaṁ kuru praguṇam ॥78॥
iti rājñā''hūtaḥ samāgataḥ kuṇḍatīradēśē । dattvā svayaṁ bāhuṁ tata uttāritō jhaṭiti ॥ 79 ॥
ārōpitō jayakuñjarē sahātmanā narēndrēṇa । guruprabhāvanayā pravēśitō nijagavanē ॥ 80 ॥

dēvajasakahā |

isa asamaṁjasabhāsī tassa parōkkhē, gaō ya sē pāsē । tacchidē maggēuṁ kuṇai aṇēgāī cāḍūṇi || 15||
sō puṇa sanbhāvēṇa pāsa pīīē baṁdhubuddhīē । saṁbhāsa saṁmāṇai tahavi na sō cayai niyapagaī || 16 ||
yataḥ
“khalaḥ satkriyamāṇō'pi dadāti kalahaṁ satām । dugdhaidhatō'pi kiṁ yāti vāyasaḥ kalahaṁsatām ? || "
aha annayā ya tēṇaṁ dēvajasō dēvavaṁdaṇanimittaṁ । ujjāṇē jiṇabhavaṇē jaṁtō avalōiḍaṁ bhaṇiō ||17||
ahamavi samāgamissaṁ tubhēhiṁ samaṁ jiṇidabhavaṇasmi । tā itthēva vilaṁbaha jā parihiyaē mi suivatthē ॥ 18 ॥
tattha ṭiō dēvajasō rannāvaliēṇa vāhiyālīō । diṭṭhō puṭṭō ki iha, sō pabhaṇai paṇamiuṁ rāyaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
gacchassaṁ jiṇabhavaṇē iya saṁbhāsiya gayammi naranāhē । paricitai dēvajasō ajjavi nō ēi dhaṇadēvō ॥ 20 ॥
jai ēhī tō milihī jiṇabhavaṇē iya vicitiḍaṁ caliō । piccha nivaṁgulīyaṁ thōvarayacchāiyaṁ sahasā ||
dēvajasēṇaṁ tattō cattō maggōvi ahibhaēva । puṭṭhiṭhiō dhaṇadēvō 'kimēsa valiō ?' vicitēi ||22|
kiṁ maggē iha sappō cihna jaṁ ēsa ēyaṭhāṇāō । valiō jhaḍatti, tō taṁ ṭhāṇaṁ sō niyai savisēsaṁ ॥ 23 ॥
sacchabhapaḍalapihiyaṁ taraṇiva phuraṁtakiraṇaniuraṁvaṁ । tō rayakaṇasaṁchannaṁ pāsa taṁ muddiyārayaṇaṁ || 24॥
avalōsi disāō gahiraṁ taṁ yattiūṇa uṭṭīē । tappaṭṭamaggalaggō pattō jiṇamaṁdirassaṁtō ॥ 25 ॥
dēvajasēṇaṁ samagaṁ pūyāsakāravaṁdaṇē kāuṁ । jiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ tattō viṇiyattō taggihē gaṁtuṁ ॥ 26 ॥
dēvajasēṇaṁ saddhi bhuttō suttō ya rayaṇisamayammi | citēi ēsa samaō ēyastucchēyaṇē majjha ||27||
,
gamitāśca bahavō'smābhirīdr̥śā iha purē । yātāṁ dhūlirna khalu dr̥ṣṭā sphāracaritānām ॥14॥
ityasamañjasabhāṣī tasya parōkṣē, gataśca tasya pārśvē । tacchidrāṇi mārgayituṁ karōtyanēkāni cāṭūni ॥15॥
sa punaḥ sadbhāvēna paśyati prītyā bandhubuddhayā । saṁbhāṣatē sammānayati tathāpi na sa tyajati nijaprakr̥tim ॥16॥
athānyadā ca tēna dēvayaśā dēvavandananimittam । udyānē jinabhavanē yān avalōkya bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 17॥
ahamapi samāgamiṣyāmi yuṣmābhiḥ samaṁ jinēndrabhavanē । tasmādatraiva vilambadhvaṁ yāvatparidadhāmi śucivastrāṇi ॥
tatra sthitō dēvayaśā rājñā valitēna vāhyālītaḥ । dr̥ṣṭaḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ kimiha sa prabhaṇati praṇamya rājānam ॥19॥
gamiṣyāmi jinabhavana iti saṁbhāṣya gatē naranāthē । paricintayati dēvayaśā adyāpi naiti dhanadēvaḥ ॥20॥
yadyēṣyati tatō miliṣyati jinabhavana iti vicintya calitaḥ । paśyati nr̥pāṅgalīyaṁ stōkarajaśyāditaṁ sahasā ||
dēvayaśasā tatastyaktō mārgō'pyahibhayēnēva । pr̥ṣṭhasthitō dhanadēvaḥ ' kimēṣa valitaḥ ?' vicintayati ॥22॥
kiṁ mārgē iha sarpastiṣṭhati yadēṣa ētatsthānāt । valitō jhaṭiti, tatastatsthānaṁ sa paśyati saviśēṣam ||23||
svacchābhrapaṭalapihitaṁ taraṇimiva sphuratkiraṇanikurambam । tatō rajaḥkaṇasaṁchannaṁ paśyati tanmudrikāratnam ||
avalōkya diśō gr̥hītvā tad gōpayitvā vastrāṁśē । tatpr̥ṣṭhamārgalagnaḥ prāptō jinamandirasyāntaḥ ॥25॥
dēvayaśasā samaṁ pūjāsatkāravandanāni kr̥tvā । jinapratimānāṁ tatō vinivr̥ttō tadgr̥hē gatvā ॥26॥
dēvayaśasā sārdhaṁ bhuktaḥ sutaśva rajanisamayē । cintayatyēṣa samaya ētasyōcchēdanē mama ||27||

supāsanāha variśrammi-
tattō muddārayaṇaṁ khivēi tappēḍamajjhabhāgapi । ukkhuḍiya cammasaṁdhī jaha na ya taṁ kavi picchēi ||28|
ittō ya naravariṁdō uttārai jāva savvamāharaṇaṁ । tō aṁgulīyarayaṇaṁ nō pēcchara muṇai paḍiyamiṇaṁ ||29
ārakyissa tō kahai sōvi āgaṁtugaṁ purajaṇaṁ ca । sōhai vivihōvāēhi vāhiyālīē taha maggē || 3 |
dhūlīdhōēhiṁtō rēṇuṁ sōhāvaē asēsaṁpi । nō lahai, kahai tattō imaṁ sakhvaṁ nariṁdassa ||31||
tēṇāvi tatya nagarē davāviō paḍahaō samaggammi । jēṇaṁ kēṇavi pattaṁ muddārayaṇaṁ samappēu || 32 ॥
abhayaṁ tassa payacchāmi, paṁcadivasāṇa jai paraṁ kahavi । puttēṇavi taṁ gahiyaṁ jāṇissaṁ, sōvi maha vajjhō
tattō taṁ dēvajasō sōuṁ hakāriūṇa dhaṇadēvaṁ । bhāi jahā baccha । taē tajhyā taṁ dimaṁguliyē ? ||34|
tajhyā kaiyā, iccāi bhaṇiē tēṇa bhaṇai dēvajasō । jaiyā maha piṭṭīē gaō si ujjāṇajiṇabhavaṇē
taṁ dihaṁ āsi jayā mavi, tā jai imaṁ taē gahiyaṁ । tō apasu naravaṇō hōhī pacchā u tamapatyaṁ
taha takaradhikārō vaccha ! atucchō imassa vaṁsassa । tō tēṇaṁ paḍibhaṇiyaṁ na hu tē saṁgāō phalamanna
cōraṁkārakalaṁkaṁpi majjha taṁ dēsi natthi tuha sarisō । annō visisuyaṇō, alāhi tā tujjha saṁgēṇa
iya bhaṇiḍaṁ niyabhavaṇē pattō sō niyamaṇammi saṁtuṭṭō । aha rannō paḍihārō ēgatē tēṇa vinnattō ॥ 39॥
naravaiṇōcipa kajjaṁ vinaviyanvaṁ nivassa atthi maē । acaṁtaṁ ētaṁ tō mēṁ daṁsēhi naravaiṇō ||40||
taha tēṇa kaē sōvi hu rāyaṁ vinnavai dēva ! dēvajasō । dhammichalēṇa jēṇaṁ musiōvi na cēyaē lōō ॥
sō caliō jiṇabhavaṇē jammi dinē paḍiyamaṁgulīyaṁ tē । tapiṭṭhīē gaō haiṁ tēṇaṁ ugguḍiya dharaṇīō ||
tatō mudrāratnaṁ kṣipati tatpēāmadhyabhāgē । tuḍitvā carmasaṁdhī yathā na ca tatkō'pi paśyati ॥28॥
itaśca naravarēndra uttārayati yāvat sarvamābharaṇam । tatō'ṅgulīyaratnaṁ nō paśyati jānāti patitamidam ॥29॥
ārakṣikasya tataḥ kathayati sō'pyāgantukaṁ purajanaṁ ca । śōdhayati vividhōpāyairvāhyālyāstathā mārgān ॥30॥
dhūlīdhōtr̥bhyō rēṇu śōdhayatyaśēṣamapi । nō labhatē, kathayati tata idaṁ svarūpaṁ narēndrasya ||31||
tēnāpi tatra nagarē dāpitaḥ paṭahaḥ samagrē । yēna kēnāpi prāptaṁ mudrāratnaṁ samarpayatu ॥32॥
abhayaṁ tasya prayacchāmi, pañcadivasthā yadi paraṁ kathamapi । putrēṇāpi tad gr̥hītaṁ jñāsyāmi, sō'pi mama vadhyaḥ
tatastad dēvayaśāḥ śrutvā hakkārayitvā dhanadēvam । bhaṇati yathā vatsa ! tvayā tadā tad dr̥ṣṭamaṅgulīyam ||34
tadā kadā, ityādau prabhaṇitē tēna bhaṇati dēvayaśāḥ । yadā mama pr̥ṣṭhē gatō'syudyānajinabhavanē || 36 |
tad dr̥ṣṭamāsīdyadā mayāpi, tatō yadīdaṁ tvayā gr̥hītam । tatō'rpaya narapatayē bhaviṣyati paścāttu tadaprārthyam ॥36
tathā taskaradhikārō vatsa ! atucchō'sya vaṁśasya । tatastēna pratibhaṇitaṁ na khalu tē saṅgātphalamanyat ॥37॥
caurya kārakalaṅkamapi mama tvaṁ dadāsi nāsti tava sadr̥śaḥ । anyō viśiṣṭasujanaḥ, alaṁ tasmāttava saṅgēna || 38
iti bhaṇitvā nijabhavanaṁ prāptaḥ sa nijamanasi saṁtuṣṭaḥ । atha rājñaḥ pratīhāra ēkāntē tēna vijñaptaḥ ||39||
narapatērēva kārya vijñapayitavyaṁ nr̥pāyāsti mayā । atyantamēkāntē tatō māṁ darśaya narapatayē ॥40॥
tathā tēna kr̥tē sō'pi khalu rājānaṁ vijñapayati dēva ! dēvayaśāḥ । dharmicchalēna yēna muṣitō'pi na cētati lōka :

gahiyaṁ kipi vikēmi jāva tā tēṇa muddiyārayaṇaṁ । gōvijaṁtaṁ dihaṁ samaṇīya gēhammi pēḍāē ||43||
pahukajjaṁ bhaṇiūṇaṁ sāhijjai tujjha, annahā niyayaṁ । kō niyaudaraṁ dārai, jamhā sō hōi maha baṁdhū || 44 ||
tō rāyā paricita saṁbhavai imapi tammi samayasmi । jaṁ diṭṭō dēvajasō matimmi ppaēsamma ||45||
iya citi bhaṇai tayaṁ, uciyaṁ bhattīē tuha karissāmi । kiṁtu jahi paḍihārō ṭhāvai tatthēva ṭhāha khaṇaṁ ॥
tō paḍihārassa tayaṁ samapi talavarassa pāsāō । hakkārāvara kajjaṁtaramudisiūṇa dēvajasaṁ || 47॥
tō ētē rāyā taṁ paṇai aṁgulīyarayaṇaṁ mē । tammi samayasmi tumaē laddhaṁ jiṇabhavaṇamaggami ||48 ॥
iya sunvai, tā sacaṁ jaṛa ēvaṁ tā samapyasu taminhiṁ । ajjavi tuha abhayaṁ ciya, nāhaṁ kāhaṁ tuha virūvaṁ ॥
rajaīivi ēppabhāvaō amha gijjaē vaisē tō pabhaṇai dēvajasō na bhaē laddhaṁ imaṁ dēva ! ॥ 50 ॥
abhaē u na saṁdēhō dēvē saccappainna sirarayaṇē । papaiēcciya aṇujīvivacchalē kiṁtu iha lōē ॥ 51 ॥
paralōē puṇa taiyavtrayabhaṁgasamubbhavassa pāvarasa | narayāisu dukkhanibaṁdhaṇassa mōkkhō kaō hōi ? ||52 ||
pāṇacaēvi tamhā ēvaṁ vavasēmi nāha ! nēya ahaṁ । bhagai niyō ēvamiṇaṁ, kiṁpuṇa niyayampi vāsagihē ॥53॥
khaṭṭāsamīpēḍāē gōviyaṁ kahai sō, taō pēḍaṁ । taṁ tumbhē ēttha diyā appāvaha majjha purisāṇa ||54॥
tō tattha asaṁtē muddārayaṇammi taṁ ahaṁ pisuṇaṁ । kārissaṁ bhūyabali, taha cēva karēi dēvajasō ॥55॥
tō tīē pēḍāē tō rāyā pariggahapamāṇaṁ । pāsai kapi katthai navakāraphalaṁ ca ṭippaṇaē || 56॥
1
।
sa calitō jinabhavanē yasmin dinē patitamaṅgalīyaṁ tē । tatpr̥ṣṭhē gatō'haṁ tēna namrībhūya dharaṇītaḥ ॥ 42 ॥
gr̥hītaṁ kimapi vitarkayāmi yāvattāvattēna mudrikāratnam । gōpyamānaṁ dr̥ṣṭaṁ śayanīyagēhē pēṭāyām ||43 ॥
prabhukāryaṁ bhaṇivā kathyatē tava, anyathā niyatam । kō nijōdaraṁ dārayēt yasmāt sa bhavati mama bandhuḥ || 44 ॥
tatō rājā paricintayati saṁbhavatīdamapi tasmin samayē । yad dr̥ṣṭō dēvayaśā mayāpi tasminpradēśē ॥ 45 ॥
iti cintayitvā bhaṇati taṁ, ucitaṁ bhaktēstava kariṣyāmi । kintu yatra pratīhāraḥ sthāpayati tatraiva tiṣṭha kṣaṇam ॥
tataḥ pratihārasya taṁ samarthya purarakṣakasya pārśvāt । hakkārayati kāryāntaramuddiśya dēvayaśasam ॥47॥
tat ēkāntē rājā taṁ prabhaṇatyaṅgulīyaratnaṁ mē । tasmin samayē tvayā labdhaṁ jinabhavanamārgē ॥48॥
iti śrūyatē, tasmātsatyaṁ yadyētat tataḥ samarpaya tadidānīm । adyāpi tavābhayamēva nāhaṁ kariṣyē tava virūpam ॥
rājyasthitirapyētatprabhāvatō'smākaṁ gīyatē vaṁśē । tataḥ prabhaṇati dēvayaśā na mayā labdhamidaṁ dēva ! ॥ 50 ॥
abhayē tu na saṁdēhō dēvē satyapratijñaśirōratnē । prakr̥tyaivānujīvivatsalē kintviha lōkē ॥ 51 ॥
paralōkē punastr̥tīyatratabhaṅgasamudbhavasya pāpasya । narakādiṣu duḥkhanibandhanasya mōkṣaḥ kutō bhavati ? ॥ 52 ॥
prāṇatyāgē'pi tasmādēvaṁ vyavasyāmi nātha ! naivāham । bhaṇati nr̥pa ēvamidaṁ, kintu nijē vāsagr̥hē ॥53॥

tatastatrādr̥śyamānē mudrāratnē, tamahaṁ piśunam । kariṣyāmi bhūtabaliṁ tathaiva karōti dēvayaśāḥ ||15||
tatastasyāḥ pēṭāyā antā rājā parigrahapramāṇam । paśyati kathamapi kvacinnamaskāraphalaṁ ca ṭippanakē ॥56॥

supāsanāha cariasmi ---
1
tammiya vāijaṁtē tassa pariggahapamāṇaṭippaṇaē । paricitai naranāhō imassa jassērisā niyamā || 57
sō kahamēvaṁ vavasara, tattō paḍihāramāisai ēvaṁ । taṁ āṇāvasu sigdhaṁ jēṇa imaṁ majjha parikahiyaṁ ॥ 58 ॥
āhūō dhaṇadēvō, bhaṇiyaṁ tuha vayaṇamannahā jāyaṁ । tō sō pēḍaṁ pakkhōḍiūṇa pāḍēi taṁ muī || 59 ||
tō pāhiyalōō jaṁpara amayaṁpi kuṇai visakajjaṁ । naranāhōvi hu ruṭṭhō dēvajasaṁ tajjaē ēvaṁ ॥ 60 ॥
rēdhi krūḍadhammiya ! kimimaṁ, sō bhaṇai vilasiyē vihiṇō । bhaṇai nivō saccamiṇaṁ iya buddhī tēṇa tuha dina-
tō rannā sō vajjhō āṇattō bahuviḍaṁbanāpuvvaṁ । ārakkhiēṇa tattō kharammi ārōviō vr̥ḍē ||62 ||
gēruyaka yaṁgarāō surattakaṇavīra raiyagalamālō । ḍamaḍa miyaḍiṁḍimaggō pahēsu bhāmijjai purassa || 63 ||
guruvaṁsaggavilagga muddārayaṇaṁ bhamēi narahatthē । pukkariumanāyaṁ purasiriē naṁ ubhiō hatthō || 64 ||
sayaṇēṇa parajaṇēṇa ya runnaṁ taṁ picchiūṇaṁ taha kahavi । rōyāviyā pasūvihu sudukkhiyā pakkhiṇōvi tahā
ucchaliō lōyaravō ahō ajuttaṁ kathaṁ imaṁ rannā । ēyassavi jaṁ vihiō daṁḍō sārīriō ēvaṁ ॥ 66 ॥
avarāhōvi hu ēsō saṁbhāvijjai imassa na hu, kiṁtu । dhaṇadēvassēva kapi vilasiyaṁ pāvacariyassa ||67
tō dēsassa purassavi rajjassa ya rāiṇō ya dēhassa । hōyavyamaṇiṇaṁ mā bhaṁti kōvi iha kuṇau || 68
।
dhaṇadēvōvi hudahuṁ dēvajasaṁ bhaṇai taha naḍijjaṁtaṁ । jō maṁgulaṁ vicitara parassa taṁ paḍai tassēva || 69 ||
rāyapurisēhi ruddhaṁ dadrūṇaṁ niyagharaṁ tahā sōuṁ । niyapaiṇō tamavatthaṁ tabbhajjā mucchiyā jhatti ॥ 70 ॥
pariyaṇakaōvayārā pacāgayacēyaṇā aiduhaṭṭā | tō palaviḍaṁ pauttā hā hā hā divtra pāviṭṭa ! || 71 ॥
tasmiṁśca vācyamānē tasya parigrahapramāṇaṭippana kē । paricintayati naranāthō'sya yasyēdr̥śā niyamāḥ ||17||
sa kathamēva vyavasyēt, tataḥ pratihāramādiśatyēvam । tamānāyaya śīghraṁ yēnēdaṁ mama parikathitam ॥ 58 ॥
āhūtō dhanadēvaḥ, bhaṇitaṁ tava vacanamanyathā jātam । tataḥ sa pēṭāṁ vikāśya pātayati tāṁ mudrām ||59 ॥
tataḥ pārśvasthitalōkō jalpatyamr̥tamapi karōti viṣakāryam । naranāthō'pi hi ruṣṭō dēvayaśasaṁ tarjayatyēvam ॥ 60|
rē dhr̥ṣṭa kūṭadhārmika ! kimidaṁ sa bhaṇati vilasitaṁ vidhēḥ । bhaṇati nr̥paḥ satyamidamiti buddhistēna tava dattā ||6 1 |
tatō rājñā sa vadhya ājñatō bahuviḍambanāpūrvam । ārakṣikēṇa tataḥ kharē ārōpitaḥ pr̥ṣṭhē (4) ॥62॥
gērukakr̥tāṅgarāgaḥ suraktakaṇavīraracitagalamālaḥ । udghaṣṭaḍiṇḍimāgraḥ pathiṣu bhrāmyatē purasya ॥ 63॥
guruvaṁśāgracilagnaṁ mudrāratnaṁ bhramati narahastē । pūtkartumanyāyaṁ puraśriyā nūrcchitō hastaḥ ||64 ||
svajanēna parajanēna ca ruditaṁ tad dr̥ṣṭrā tathā kathamapi । rōditāḥ paśavō'pi hi suduḥkhitāḥ pakṣiṇō'pi tathā
ucchalitō lōkaravō'hō ayuktaṁ kr̥tamidaṁ rājñā । ētasyāpi yad vihitō daṇḍaḥ śārīrika ēvam || 66 ॥
aparādhō'pi khalvēṣa saṁbhāvyatē'sya na khalu kintu । dhanadēvasyaiva kathamapi vikasitaṁ pāpacaritasya ॥ 67 ॥
tatō dēśasyāpi purasyāpi rājyasya ca rājñaśca dēhasya । bhavitavyamaniṣṭēna mā bhrānti kō'pīha karōtu ॥ 68 ।
dhanadēvō'pi khalu dr̥ṣṭvā dēvayaśasaṁ bhaṇati tathā naṭyamānam । yō'niṣṭaṁ vicintayati parasya tatpatati tasyaiva ।
rājapuruṣai ruddhaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā nijagr̥haṁ tathā śrōtum । nijapatēstāmavasthāṁ tadbhāryā mūrcchitā jhaṭiti ॥70॥

taṁ kaha paharasi ēvaṁ ēvaṁvipurisarayaṇadēhammi । viyaliyakalaṁka kāṇa dēsi garuyaṁ kalaṁkaṁpi ॥ 72 ॥
ahavā kiṁ khēēṇaṁ, karēmi jaṁ ittha hōi kāyavvaṁ । iya vavasiūṇa pavisai pōsahasālāē suibhūyā ॥73॥
kuṇai ya kāussaggaṁ sāsaṇadēvi maṇē karēūṇa । nāsamganisiyadiṭṭhī saramāṇā paṁcaparamiṭṭhē ||74 ||
tō takkhaṇāgayāē dēvīē pabhaṇiyā jahā vacchē ! । mā kuṇasu khēyamēvaṁ savvaṁ bhavvaṁ karissāmi ॥75॥
aha sahasacciya nivamaṁdirammi jalapanna annapūṁgāī । avahariyāṁ dēvīē maṁtipamuhāṇavi gihēsu ॥ 76 ॥
aha rāyā jā nīraṁ pāuṁ maggēi tāva jalabhariō । gaggarikaragāīsuṁ na niyai biṁdupi salilassa ||77||
tō bhīō sō rannō vinnavai jahā jalassa bhariēsu । nicchiḍḍēmuvi dīsai na nīrabiṁdūvi ṭhāṇēsu ॥78॥
thaiyaggāhī bhaṇiō bīḍagamappēsu tāva tumamēgaṁ । sō thaiyāē hatthaṁ khivēi jā sāvitā rittā ॥ 79 ॥
ēvaṁ jaṁ jaṁ pucchai taṁ taṁ natthitti nisuṇiuṁ rāyā | hakkārāviyaṁ maṁti kahai sarūvaṁ imaṁ tassa ||80||
sō bhai gihē majjhavi vr̥ttaṁtō ēsa taha ya annēsiṁ । tumhapayasēvayāṇaṁ gihē vaṭṭa asēsāṇa ॥ 81 ॥
bhai nivō paribhāvaha kiṁ kāraṇamittha, bhaṇai tō maṁtī । nidōsō dēvajasō saṁbhāvijjai jaō jēṇaṁ ॥
ghaṇadēvēṇaṁ dōsō imammi ārōviō sa duṭṭappā | tassēva kiṁpi vilasiyamēyaṁ, na hu dēva ! dēvajasō ॥
pāṇañcaēva ēvaṁ karē, tattō ya camaradhārīē । avayariḍaṁ sāsaṇadēvayāē bhaṇiyaṁ jahā maiḍha ! || 84 ॥
maṁtī tumapi vaccasi jō samuvakkhēsi niyayasāmipi । ēvamakajjapayahaṁ, aha bhaṇasi na majjha kahiyamiṇaṁ ||
hu
parijanakr̥tōpacārā pratyāgatacētanā'tiduḥkhārtā । tataḥ pralapituṁ pravr̥ttā hā hā hā daiva pāpiṣṭha ! ॥71॥
tvaṁ kathaṁ praharasyēvamēvaṁvidhapuruṣaratnadēhē । vigalitakalaṅkāśaṅkānāṁ dadāsi guruṁ kalaṅkamapi ॥ 72 ॥
athavā kiṁ khēdēna, karōmi yadatra bhavati kartavyam । iti vyavasāya praviśati pauṣadhaśālāyāṁ śucibhūtā ॥73॥
karōti ca kāyōtsarga śāsanadēvīṁ manasi kr̥tvā । nāsāgranyastadr̥ṣṭiḥ smarantī pañca paramēṣṭhinaḥ ॥74॥
tatastatkṣaṇāgatayā dēvyā prabhaṇitā yathā vatsē ! । mā kuruṣva khēdamēva sarvaṁ bhavyaṁ kariṣyāmi || 75 ॥
atha sahasaiva nr̥pamandirājjalaparṇānnapūgādayaḥ । apahr̥tā dēvyā mantripramukhāṇāmapi gr̥hēbhyaḥ ॥ 76 ॥
atha rājā yāvannīraṁ pātuṁ mārgayati tāvajjalabhr̥tyaḥ । gargarīkarakādiṣu na paśyati bindumapi salilasya ॥77॥
tatō bhītaḥ sa rājñē vijñapayati yathā jalasya bhr̥tēṣu । niśchidrēṣvapi dr̥śyatē na nīrabindurapi sthānēṣu ||78॥
sthagikāgrāhī bhaṇitō bīṭakamarpaya tāvat tvamēkam । sa sthagikāyāṁ hastaṁ kṣipati yāvatsāpi tāvadviktā ॥79॥
ēvaṁ yadyat pr̥cchati tattad nāstīti śrutvā rājā । hakkārayitvā mantriṇaṁ kathayati svarūpamidaṁ tasya ॥80॥
sa bhaṇati gr̥hē mamāpi vr̥ttānta ēṣa tathā cānyēṣām । yuṣmatpādasēvakānāṁ gr̥hēṣu vartatē'śēṣāṇām ॥ 81 ॥
bhaṇati nr̥paḥ paribhāvaya kiṁ kāraṇamatra, bhaṇati tatō mantrī । nirdōṣō dēvayaśāḥ saṁbhāvyatē yatō yēna ॥ 82 ॥
dhanadēvēna dōṣō'sminnārōpitaḥ sa duṣṭātmā । tasyaiva kimapi vilasitamētat, na khalu dēva ! dēvayaśāḥ ॥ 83॥
prāṇatyāgē'pyēvaṁ karōti, tataśca cāmaradhāriṇyām । avatīrya śāsanadēvatayā bhaṇitaṁ yathā mūḍha ! ॥ 84 ॥
1. ghuggāī, ga. puragāī । 2 ka. ga. °yāī dē° । 3 ka. mūḍhā ।

supāsanāha cariśrammi-
ramā sayamēva kaō ēsa viyārō, imapi nō juttaṁ । jaṁ tuha taṁ vīsariyaṁ jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ nīisatyammi ||86
" durvr̥ttēṣvapyapatyēṣu yathā mātā hitaiṣiṇī । durvr̥ttē'pi tathā rājñi nōpēkṣāṁ sacivō'rhati ॥”
dhaṇadēvēṇaṁ ēsā muddā nihiyā chalēṇa pēḍāē । dēvajasamaccharēṇaṁ kayaṁ ca pāvēṇa sayalamiṇaṁ || 87 ||
ēvaṁ ca taṁ bhaṇati sōuṁ nāūṇa dēvayā itthaṁ । avayariyā kāvi taō namaṁti naranāhasacivāī ||88 ||
vihiyavivihōvayārā khāmaṁti ya jāva tāva dhaṇadēvō । ṭhiyapacchāmuhavayaṇō kuṭṭijjatōvya lauḍēhiṁ ॥ 89
aivirasamāra saṁtō samāgaō bhaṇai maccharēṇa maē । pāvēṇa vilasiyamimaṁ dēvajasē phalihavimalammi ||90
dēvajasōviya dīsara āgāsagayaṁ vimāṇamārūḍhō । thuvvaṁtō suyaṇēhiṁ harisaṁsukilinnanayaṇēhiṁ ॥91॥
suvvaṁti ya ārakkhiyabhicāṇaṁ tavviḍaṁgaṇakarāṇaṁ । dīṇāṇaṁ dhāhāō ubhiyabāhāṇa virasāō ॥92
dhavalaharē pattāō taō vimāṇāō uttaraṁ tammi । dēvajasē abbhui sā cāmaradhāriṇī jhati ॥93॥
rāyāiṇōvi ēvaṁ, uttaramāṇassa tō vimāṇāō । sā dēi sayaṁ bāhaṁ, uttinnaṁ puṇa nimaṁtē ॥ 94 ॥
sīhāsaṇēṇa rāyā uvavisai āsaṇammi annamma । bhaṇai ya sāsaṇadēvī dēvajasaṁ tumha ēēhiṁ ॥95॥
jiṇavayaṇarayassa dayāluyassa paḍivannasugihidhammassa । niddōsassavi jēhiṁ viḍaṁtraṇā viraiyā ēvaṁ ॥ 96
tē nigami savvē jiṇasāsaṇakikarī ahaṁ jēṇa । tujjha ghariṇīē kāuṁ kāussagaṁ ihāhūyā ॥97॥
sō jaṁpara dēvajasō kammēhi viḍaṁbanā kayā majjha । dēvi ! imā, tā tāṇummūlaṇapaṇō ahaṁ vihiō। 98.
pāṇē rakkhatīē ayasakalaṁkaṁ tahā phusaṁtīē । dēvīicciya, savvaṁ ēyaṁ tu jaṇaṁ kuṇau dēvī ॥ 99 ॥
mantrī tvamapyucyasē yaḥ samupēkṣasē nijasvāminamapi । ēvamakāryapravr̥ttaṁ, atha bhaṇasi na mama kathitamidam ||85||
rājñā svayamēva kr̥ta ēṣa vicāraḥ, idamapi nō yuktam । yattava tad vismr̥taṁ yad bhaṇitaṁ nītiśāstrē ॥ 86 ॥
dhanadēvēnaiṣā mudrā nihitā chalēna pēṭāyām । dēvayaśōmātsaryēṇa kr̥taṁ ca pāpēna sakalamidam ||87 ||
ēvaṁ ca tāṁ bhaṇantīṁ śrutvā jñātvā dēvatātra | avatīrṇā kāpi tatō namanti naranāthasacivādayaḥ ॥ 88 ॥
vihitavividhōpacārāḥ kṣamayanti ca yāvattāvad dhanadēvaḥ । sthitapaścānmukhavadanaḥ kuṭyamāna iva laguḍaiḥ ||89||
ativirasamārasan samāgatō bhaṇati mātsaryēṇa mayā । pāpēna vilasitamidaṁ dēvayaśasi sphaṭika vimalē ॥90॥
dēvayaśā api ca dr̥śyatē ākāśagataṁ vimānamārūḍhaḥ । stūyamānaḥ sujanairharṣāśruklinnanayanaiḥ ॥ 91 ॥
śrūyantē cārakṣikabhr̥tyānāṁ tadviḍambanakarāṇām । dīnānāṁ rājya ūdhvitabāhūnāṁ virasāḥ ॥92॥
dhavalagr̥hē prāptāt tatō vimānāduttarati । dēvayaśasyabhyuttiṣṭhati sā cāmaradhāriṇī jhaṭiti ॥ 93 ॥
rājādayō'pyēvam, uttaratastatō vimānāt । sā dadāti svayaṁ bāhum, uttīrṇa punarnimantrayati ॥94॥
siṁhāsanēna rājōpaviśatyāsanē'nyasmin । bhaṇati ca śāsanadēvī dēvayaśasaṁ tavaitaiḥ ॥95॥
jinavacanaratasya dayālōḥ pratipannasugr̥hidharmasya । nirdōṣasyāpi yairviḍambanā viracitaivam ॥96॥
tān nigr̥hṇāmi sarvāñjinaśāsanakiṁkarī ahaṁ yēna । tava gr̥hiṇyā kr̥tvā kāyōtsargamihāhūtā ॥ 97 ॥
tatō jalpati dēvayaśāḥ karmabhirviḍambanā kr̥tā mama । dēvi ! iyaṁ tasmāttēṣāmunmūlanapraguṇō'haṁ vihitaḥ ॥ 98॥

sōvara hiyaṁ mai vacchalaṁ kathaṁ havai ēvaṁ । tō tabbhaṇiyaṁ kāuṁ aṇujāṇāviya gayā dēvī ॥ 100 ॥
dhaṇadēva āṇatō ramnā vajjhō viḍaṁbanāpuvvaṁ । karuṇāē dēvajasēṇa mōiō naravaraṁ bhaṇiuṁ ॥ 101 ॥
aha paṭṭamahādēvi pēsiya rāyā suhāsanārūḍhaṁ । āṇāvara dēvajasassa gēhiṇi ruppiṇi tattha ॥ 102 ॥
pattā yadiṭṭigōyaramabhuṭṭiya paḍai tīi pāēsu । sā bhaṇai sayalakallāṇabhāyaṇa hōsu narapavara ! ।। 103 ॥
bhāsaṇē nivēaiya kāuṁ karasaṁpuḍhaṁ ṇiḍālammi । savvasabhāpaccavakhaṁ kayannusira sēharō rāyā ॥ 104 ॥
bhai i aparikkhiyakāri ēvaṁvihāō pāvāō । mēṁ mōyaṁtīē tara subahiṇi ! taṁ kiṁpi uvayariyaṁ ।।
jassa na nikkayamahamēmi raṭṭharajjēṇa ahava dēhēṇaṁ । tō vāvārasu ēyāī jattha paḍihāra tuha tēttha ||106 ॥
dēvajasassa ya puttō sayaṇēhiṁ dhannakhēḍauvanayarē । ṭhaviō āsi duvārē samāgaō naravarridassa ॥ 107 ॥
kahiō paḍihārēṇa rannā mōyāviō, taō jhatti । rāyaṁ jaṇayaṁ jaṇaṇi paṇamai tō naravarēṇēsō || 108 ||
āliṁgiya ucchaṁgē nivēsiō, tō bhaṇai dēvajasō । dēvēṇaṁ āyattaṁ savvaṁpi hu ruppiṇī kayaṁ ॥ 109 ॥
sā puṇa maha āyattā tā saṁpai bhōyaṇaṁ karēūṇaṁ । jēsiṁ ahamāyattō tē vaṁdijjaṁtu suhaguruṇō ॥ 110 ॥

puṇa ajjēva ihaṁ samōsaḍhā naṁdaṇammi ujjāṇē । diṭṭhā iha iṁtēṇaṁ vimāṇacaḍiēṇa paṇayā ya ॥ 111 ॥
tāṇaṁ āēsō kāya rupiṇīē saha inhi । tubbhēhivi sattīē, tattō bhuttarē rāyā ॥ 112 ॥
mahayā vicchaḍḍēṇaṁ saha dēvajasēṇa ruppiṇīē ya । tāṇa suraṇaṁ saddhiṁ pattō sūrīṇa payamūlē ॥ 113 ॥
prāṇān rakṣantyā'yaśaḥ kalaṅkaṁ tathā mr̥jatyā । dēvyaiva, sarvamētaṁ tu janaṁ karōtu dēvī ॥99॥
sarvōpadravarahitaṁ mayi vātsalyaṁ kr̥taṁ bhavatyēvam । tatastadbhaṇitaṁ kr̥tvā'nujñāpya gatā dēvī ॥ 100 ॥
dhanadēva ājñaptō rājñā vadhyō viḍambanāpūrvam । karuṇayā dēvayaśasā mōcitō naravaraṁ bhaṇitvā ॥ 101 ॥
atha paṭṭamahādēvīṁ prēṣya rājā sukhāsanārūḍhām । ānāyayati dēvayaśasō gēhinīṁ rukmiṇīṁ tatra ॥ 102 ॥
prāptā ca dr̥ṣṭigōcaramabhyutthāya patati tasyāḥ pādayōḥ । sā bhaṇati sakalakalyāṇabhājanaṁ bhava narapravara ! ॥
bhadrāsanē nivēśya kr̥tvā karasaṁpuṭaṁ lalāṭē । sarvasabhāpratyakṣaṁ kr̥tajñaśiraḥ śēkharō rājā ॥ 104 ॥
bhaṇatīmamaparīkṣitakāriṇamēvaṁvidhāt pāpāt । māṁ mōcayantyā vayā subhagini ! tatkimapyupakr̥tam ॥105॥
yasya na niṣkrayamahamēōmi rāṣṭrarājyēnāthavā dēhēna । tatō vyāpārayaitāni yatra pratibhāti tava tatra ॥ 106 ॥
dēvayaśasaśca putraḥ svajanairdhānyakhēṭōpanagarē । sthāpita āsīd dvārē samāgatō naravarēndrasya ॥ 107॥
kathitaḥ pratīhārēṇa rājñā mōcitaḥ, tatō jhaṭiti । rājānaṁ janakaṁ jananīṁ praṇamati tatō naravarēṇaiṣaḥ ॥ 108 ॥
āliṅgyōtsaṅgē nivēśitaḥ, tatō bhaṇati dēvayaśāḥ । dēvēnāyattaṁ sarvamapi hi rukmiṇyāḥ kr̥tam ॥109॥
sā punarmamāyattā tasmāt saṁprati bhōjanaṁ kr̥tvā । yēṣāmahamāyattastē vandyantāṁ śubhaguravaḥ ॥ 110 ॥
tē punaravēha samavasr̥tā nandana udyānē । dr̥ṣṭā ihā''yatā vimānacaṭitēna praṇatāśca ॥ 111 ॥
tatastēṣāmādēśaḥ kartavyō rukmiṇyā sahēdānīm । yuṣmābhirapi śaktyā, tatō muktōttarē rājā ॥ 112 ॥

supāsanāha variammi-
sūrīhi jammē gihidhammēvi ya savittharē kahiē । rannā ya parinnāē, dēvajasō rupiṇīē samaṁ ।। 114
aṇujāṇāvara rāyaṁ vittuṁ dikkhaṁ taō ya sō bhaṇai । kāyavvaṁ ciya ēvaṁ kiṁpuṇa dasadivasapajjētē ।। 115
tēhivi taha paḍivanē puṇōvi vaṁdiya vihīē gurucaraṇē । dēvajasāīhiṁ samaṁ rāyā niyamaṁdiraṁ pattō ॥ 11 ॥
tērsi pāsē āṇi gōttiṁ mēlāvaē samagaṁpi । taha savvattha amāriṁ ugghōsāvai purē tattha | | 117॥
taha niyabhaṁḍārāō dē hicchāē cēiyaharēsu । dāvai daviṇaṁ subahu pūyai ya caunvihaṁ saṁgha ॥ 118 ॥
taha dīṇāṇāhāṇaṁ dāva dāṇaṁ taō sabahumāṇaṁ । siṭṭiē tapputtaṁ ṭhāvai dāuṁ subahudaviṇaṁ ॥ 219 ॥
tō vihiputraṁ tēsiṁ dāi dikkhaṁ sayaṁ ca gihidhammaṁ । paḍivajjiya ucchappara savvattō jiṇamayaṁ tattō ॥
sāhū dēvajasō ruppiṇī ya paripāliḍaṁ vayaṁ sammaṁ । lahiuṁ kēvalanāṇaṁ tēṇēva bhavēṇa siddhāī ॥ 121 ॥
॥ iti tr̥tīyāsuvratē dēvayaśaḥ kathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
mahatā vistārēṇa saha dēvayaśasā rukmiṇyā ca । tayōḥ sutēna sārdhaṁ prāptaḥ sūrīṇāṁ pādamūlē ॥113॥
sūribhiryatidharmē gr̥hidharmē'pi ca savistarē kathitē । rājñā ca parijñātē, dēvayaśā rukmiṇyā samam ॥ 114 ॥
anujñāpayati rājānaṁ grahītuṁ dīkṣāṁ tataśca sa bhaṇati । kartavyamēvaivaṁ kintu daśadivasaparyantē ॥115॥
tābhyāmapi tathā pratipannē punarapi vanditvā vidhinā gurucaraṇān । dēvayaśaādibhiḥ samaṁ rājā nijamandiraṁ prāptaḥ ॥
tēṣāṁ pārśvē ānīya gōtriṇaṁ mēlayati samagramapi । tathā sarvatrāmārimudghōṣayati purē tatra ॥ 117 ॥
tathā nijabhāṇḍāgārāddadāti yadr̥cchayā caityagr̥hēṣu । dāpayati draviṇaṁ subahu pūjayati ca caturvidhaṁ saṁgham ॥ 118
tathā dīnānāthēbhyō dāpayati dānaṁ tataḥ sabahumānam । śrēṣṭhipadē tatputraṁ sthāpayati dattvā subahu draviṇam ||119|
tatō vidhipūrvaṁ tayōrdāpayati dīkṣāṁ svayaṁ ca gr̥hidharmam । pratipadyatē utsarpati sarvatō jinamataṁ tataḥ ॥ 120 ॥
sādhurdēvayaśā rukmiṇī ca paripālya vrataṁ samyak । labdhvā kēvalajñānaṁ tēnaiva bhavēna siddhau ॥ 121 ॥

āsi. jaladivva vimamaṇōharaṁ viulalacchikulabhavaṇaṁ । bhadilapuraṁ pasiddhaṁ siṭṭhī tatthathi thiradēvā || 2 ||
bhajjā tassa susīlā kamalasirī tāṇa nāhaḍō puttō । sō ya payaīē buddhō haṭṭē vavaharai bhayarahiō || 3 ||
aha annayā sa kēvi mittēṇa palōbhiō jahā bāhiṁ । vaṇijārayāṇa satthō bahubhaṁḍō āgaō atthi ।।
tō sō tēṇa samaṁ ciya tahi gaō paṇiyasahikaraṇatyaṁ । pabhaṇai mittaṁ vāṇijjakāra tē payaṁsēhi ||5||
tō ujjāṇē sūri sō daṁsaha sāhuparivuḍaṁ tassa । sō jaṁpai niggaṁthā ēē, iyarō bhaṇē tahavi || 6 ||
bahumulabhaṁḍakaliyā ditiya niyabhaṁḍayaṁ aimahagghaṁ । tallābhēṇa salōbhō nāsai dālidavēyālō ||7||
tō namiūṇaṁ sūriṁ bhaṇiyaṁ mittēṇa ēsa vaṇiputtō । vaṇijatthaṁ iha pattō tā daṁsaha kiṁpi niyabhaṁḍa ||8||
niyayiyagaṭhiṭhaviyaṁ bahumulaṁ rayaṇamuttiyāīyaṁ । tō tēhiṁ sō bhaṇiō gāhagabuddhī jai imassa ||9||
tā daṁsimō samaggaṁ annaha ki āluyārabhaṇiēhiṁ । āyāsijjai appā tadaṁsaṇasaṭṭisannāhiṁ 1 ॥ 10 ॥
tō nāhaḍēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ chōḍaha gaṁṭhī payaṁsaha maṇīō । na hi thaviyamōttiyāṁṇaṁ naṇu agghō tīraē kāuṁ ॥ 11 ॥
tō savaṇāmaya suharaṇa gahirasadēṇa muṇivarō bhaṇai । sammattamahārayaṇaṁ jai tuha paḍihāi tō givha ॥12॥
jiṇasāsaṇa suddhāgarasaṁbhūyaṁ bhūriguṇagaṇagghaviyaṁ । ciṁtāmaṇivva maṇavaṁchiyattha saṁpāyaṇapavīṇaṁ ॥ 13॥
taha vimalaṁ sacchāyaṁ duiyaṁ muttābhirāmayaṁ hāraṁ । pāṇivahaviraināmaṁ tivihaṁ tivihēṇa navasariyaṁ ॥ 14॥
stēnaiḥ samānītaṁ gr̥hṇāti kāṇakrayēṇa yō vaṇik । sa nāhaṭa iva vadhabandhabhājanaṁ bhavatīhāpi ॥ 1 ॥
āsījjaladhivad vidrumamanōharaṁ vipulalakṣmīkulabhavanam । bhaddilapuraṁ prasiddhaṁ śrēṣṭhī tatrāsti sthiradēvaḥ ॥2॥
bhāryā tasya suśīlā kamalaśrīstayōrnāhaṭaḥ putraḥ । sa ca prakr̥tyā lubdhō haṭṭē vyavaharati bhayarahitaḥ ॥3॥
athānyadā sa kēnāpi mittrēṇa pralōbhitō yathā bahiḥ । vāṇijyakārakāṇāṁ sārthō bahubhāṇḍa āgatō'sti ॥ 4 ॥
॥
tataḥ sa tēna samamēva tatra gataḥ paṇyavinimayakaraṇārtham । prabhaṇati mittraṁ vāṇijyakārakāṁstān pradarśaya ||5||
tata udyānē sūriṁ sa darśayati sādhuparivr̥taṁ tasya । sa jalpati nirgranthā ētē, itarō bhaṇati tathāpi ॥6॥
bahumūlyabhāṇḍakalitā dadati ca nijabhāṇḍamatimahārtham । tallābhēna salōbhō naśyati dāridrayavētālaḥ ||7||
tatō natvā sūriṁ bhaṇitaṁ mittrēṇaiṣa vaṇikputraḥ । vāṇijyārthamiha prāptastasmād darśaya kimapi nijabhāṇḍam ||8||
nijahr̥dayagranthisthāpitaṁ bahumūlyaṁ ratnamauktikādikam । tatastaiḥ sa bhaṇitō grāhakabuddhiryadyasya ||9||
tadā darśayāmaḥ samagramanyathā kiṁ nirarthakabhaṇitaiḥ । āyasyata ātmā taddarśanavinimaya saṁjñābhiḥ ? ॥ 10 ॥
tatō nāhaṭēna bhaṇitaṁ chōṭayata granthīn pradarśayata maṇīn । nahi stutamauktikānāṁ nanvarṣaḥ śakyatē kartum ॥ 11॥
tataḥ śravaṇāmr̥tasukhadēna gabhīraśabdēna munivarō bhaṇati । samyaktvamahāratnaṁ yadi tava pratibhāti tatō gr̥hāṇa ॥ 12 ॥
jinaśāsanaśuddhākarasaṁbhūtaṁ bhūriguṇagaṇapūrṇam । cintāmaṇivad manōvāñchitārthasaṁpādanapravaṇim ॥13॥

iccāsādhammō gihidhammōvi hu pavaṁcaō kahiō । kammakhaōvasamāō paḍivannō tēhiṁ samagaṁpi ॥ 15 ॥
namiūṇa muṇi dunniva saṁpattā niyagihēsu kuvvaṁti । jahagihiyaṁ gihidhammaṁ ahannayā nāhaḍō haṭṭē || 16 ||
hara jāva tattō cōrā gahiūṇa kaṇayamāīyaṁ । āṇaṁti tassa haṭṭaṁ pacchannaṁ girahaē sōvi || 17||
kāṇakyaṁ kutō kayāi diṭṭhō sa tēṇa mittēṇa । bhaṇiō na juttamēyaṁ taiyavayaṁ tujjha sakalaṁkaṁ ॥ 18 ॥
ēvaṁ hōiti, taō paryapaē nāhaḍō jahā mitta ! | adinnādāṇaṁ ciya paccakkhāyaṁ maē na imaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
iyarō bhāi gurūhi tayammi vayammi ēsa aiyārō । tēnāiḍakayarūvō kahiō tamhā cayasu ēyaṁ ||20|
iya bhaṇiya gaō mittō, ṭhāvai puṇa nāhaḍō maṇē ēvaṁ । jaidhammōvi huṁ kahiō gurūhi kiṁ taṁpi pālēmi ? |
aha ēkkatakkarēṇaṁ pavarā rayaṇāṁvalī samāṇīyā । taha caiva nāhaḍēṇaṁ gahiyā sā thēvamullēṇa ॥ 22 ॥
vavahara tassa haṭṭē nivassa bhaṁḍāriō vimalanāmā । tavvēlāē sōvi hu saṁpattō tassa pāsamma ||23||
pabhaṇai paḍipaṭṭaulayakappaḍakōḍīsayaṁ payaṁsēsu । giṇhāmō abhiruiyaṁ jēṇaṁ tō sō samuṭṭhē ||24||
sayamēva ya. puṭṭaliyaṁ gahiraṁ bāhiṁ samāgaō jāba । tāva ya kaḍivaḍīō paḍiyā rayaṇāvalī jhatti ||25||
taṁ gahiūṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ bhūvaibhaṁḍāriēṇa bhō siddhi ! । kiṁ ēyaṁti taō sō khuhiō jaṁpēṛa na hu kiṁpi ॥ 26
tā gahiūṇaṁ hatthē bhaṇiō annapi kuṁḍalāīyaṁ । samagaṁ gayamēīē tā kiṁ taṁpi hu tuha sayāsē ? ||27||
taṁ sōuṁsō jaṁpa, ēsā dēsāgayāṇa vaṇiyāṇa | hatthāō maē gahiyā lakkhēṇaṁ, bhāi tō iyarō ||28||
1
tathā vimalaṁ sacchāyaṁ dvitīyaṁ muktābhirāmaṁ hāram । prāṇivadhaviratināmānaṁ trividhaṁ trividhēna navamālam ॥ 14 ॥
ityādisādhudharmō gr̥hidharmō'pi khalu prapañcataḥ kathitaḥ । karmakṣayōpaśamāt pratipannastābhyāṁ samamapi ॥ 15 ॥
natvā muniṁ dvāvapi saṁprāptau nijagr̥hayōḥ kurutaḥ । yathāgr̥hītaṁ gr̥hidharmamathānyadā nāhaṭō haṭṭē ॥ 16 ॥
vyavaharati yāvat tataścaurā gr̥hītvā kanakādikam । ānayanti tasya haṭṭaṁ pracchannaṁ gr̥hṇāti sō'pi ॥ 17॥
kāṇakrayaṁ kurvan kadācid dr̥ṣṭaḥ sa tēna mittrēṇa । bhaṇitō na yuktamētat tr̥tīyatrataṁ tava sakalaṅkam ॥ 18 ॥
ēvaṁ bhavatīti, tataḥ prajalpati nāṭō yathā mitra ! | adattādānamēva pratyākhyātaṁ mayā nēdam ||19||
itarō bhaṇati gurubhistr̥tīyē vrata ēṣō'ticāraḥ । stēnāhr̥takr̥tarūpaḥ kathitastasmāt tyajaitam ||20||
iti bhaṇitvā gataṁ mittraṁ, sthāpayati punarnāhaṭō manasyēvam । yatidharmō'pi hi kathitō gurubhiḥ kiṁ tamapi pālayāmi ?|
athaikataskarēṇa pravarā ratnāvalī samānītā । tathaiva nāhaṭēna gr̥hītā sā stōkamūlyēna ॥22॥
vyavaharati tasya haṭṭē nr̥pasya bhāṇḍāgārikō vimalanāmā । tadvēlāyāṁ sō'pi hi saṁprāptastasya pārśvē ॥23॥
prabhaṇati paṭīpaṭakulakakarpaṭakōṭiśataṁ pradarśaya । gr̥hṇīmō'bhirucitaṁ yēna tataḥ sa samutthāya ||24||
svayamēva ca pōṭalikāṁ gr̥hītvā bahiḥ samāgatō yāvat । tāvacca kaṭīpaṭītaḥ patitā ratnāvalī jhaṭiti ||25||
tāṁ gr̥hītvā bhaṇitaṁ bhūpatibhāṇḍāgārikēṇa bhōḥ śrēṣṭhin ! । kimētaditi tataḥ sa kṣubhitō jalpati nahi kimapi ॥
tatō gr̥hītvā hastē maṇitō'nyadapi kuṇḍalādikam । samaṁ gatamētayā tasmātkiṁ tadapi hi tava sakāśē ? ॥27॥
tat śrutvā sa alpati, ēṣā dēśāgatānāṁ vaṇijām । hastād mayā gr̥hītā lakṣaṇa, bhaṇati tata itaraḥ ॥ 28 ॥

nāhaḍa kahā ।
345.
mā jaṁpa asaṁbaddhaṁ jaṁ ēsā nitraiṇō hiyayaharaṇā । varapaṇaiṇivva saguṇā tā sayamappasu naravaissa ||29|
annaha niṣēṇa nāē dhaṇēṇa dēhēṇa chuṭṭasi na vaccha ! | iya tattha bhaṇatāṇaṁ pattō ārakkhiō sahasā ॥ 30 ॥
haṇa haṇa haṇatti bhaṇirēṇa tēṇamabhihaṇiya khaggajavaēhiṁ । vaddhō tēṇa raḍatō sō varaō nāhaḍō vaṇiō ॥ 31 ॥
bhaṁḍāriēṇa puḍhaṁ kimimaṁ ārakkhiō bhaṇai ēttha । ēkkō pattō cōrō sēhijjētēṇa tēṇēsō ||32||
kahiō mōṭṭhāṇa rāyabharaṇāiyāṇa savvāṇa । aha rayaṇāvalisahiō nīō sō tēṇa nivapāsē ||33||
taha vittaṁ nō takkaracakkassa dēva ! vaṇiōvi । hārāvaiuṁ ēsō mōsaṁ ginhai samagaṁpi ||34|
tōranō maṁtimuhamma nivaḍiyā kōvataraliyā diṭṭhī । tēṇavi vaṇiō bhaṇiō nivaāharaṇaṁ samaggaṁpi ॥
appasu jaṁ gahiyaṁ taha annajaṇassāvi saṁtiyaṁ tujjha । jaṁ mōsamatthi pāsē taṁ, annahā nittulaṁ marasi ॥ 36 ॥
tō tēṇaṁ paḍibhaṇiyaṁ savvaṁ adhpēmi jaṁ mayā kīyaṁ । mōtuṁ hāraṁ ēkkaṁ gaō sa jamhā avagaīē ||37||
tailōkkasārahāraṁ hā rē ! jai taṁpi nō samappēsi । tō natthi tujjha jīyaṁ iya bhaṇijaṁ mōrabaṁdhērhi ||38||
baṁdhāviya tāḍāvara kasāya ghāēhiṁ ghōrataraēhiṁ । tahavi na mannai hāraṁ samappiraṁ maṁtiṇā tattō ||39||
hakkāriya tajjaṇaō bhaṇiō pucchēhiṁ niyasuyaṁ ēyaṁ । tēṇavi rahammi bhaṇiō rē rē kulapaṁsaṇa ! suṇēhi ||
maha vāraṁtassa tara tayā samaṁ caraḍacōramāīhiṁ । pāraddhō vavahārō tassa phalaṁ ērisa jāyaṁ ॥ 41 ॥
ailōhaggahagahiō rāyaviruddhapi kuṇasi vavahāraṁ । kāuvva niyasi piṁḍaṁ na piṭṭhaō lauḍayapahāraṁ ॥ 42॥
।
mā jalpāsaṁbaddhaṁ yadēṣā nr̥patērhr̥dayaharaṇī । varapraṇayinīva saguṇā tasmātsvayamarpaya narapatayē ॥29॥
anyathā nr̥pēṇa jñātē dhanēna dēhēna chuṭyasē na vatsa ! । iti tatra bhaṇatōḥ prāpta ārakṣikaḥ sahasā ||30 ॥
hata hata hatēti bhaṇitrā tēnābhihatya khaḍgajavaiḥ । baddhastēna raṭansa varākō nāiṭō vaṇik ॥ 31 ॥
bhāṇḍāgārikēṇa pr̥ṣṭaṁ kimidam ārakṣikō bhaṇatyatra । ēkaḥ prāptaścaurō naśyatā tēnaiṣaḥ ||32||
"
kathitō mōṣasthānaṁ rājābharaṇādikānāṁ sarvēṣām । atha ratnāvalīsahitō nītaḥ sa tēna nr̥papārśvē ॥ 33॥
tathā vijñaptaṁ rājñē taskaracakrēṇa dēva ! vaṇigapi । hārayitvaiṣa mōṣaṁ gr̥hṇāti samagramapi ॥ 34 ॥
।
tatō rājñō mantrimukhē nipatitā kōpataralitā dr̥ṣṭiḥ । tēnāpi vaṇig bhaṇitō nr̥pābharaṇaṁ samagramapi ॥35॥
arpaya yad gr̥hītaṁ, tathānyajanasyāpi saṁbandhī tava । yō mōṣō'sti pārśvē tam, anyathā nistulaṁ mriyasē ॥36॥
tatastēna pratibhaṇitaṁ sarvamarpayāmi yad mayā krītam । muktvā hāramēkaṁ gataḥ sa yasmādapagatyā ॥ 37॥
trailōkyasārahāraṁ hā rē ! yadi tamapi nō samarpayasi । tatō nāsti tava jīvitamiti bhaṇitvā mōrabandhaiḥ ॥ 38॥
bandhayitvā tāḍayati kaśāyā ghātaighōrataraiḥ । tathāpi na manyatē hāraṁ samarpayituṁ, mantriṇā tataḥ ॥ 39 ॥
hakkārayitvā tajjanakō bhaṇitaḥ pr̥ccha nijasutamētat । tēnāpi rahasi bhaṇitō rē rē kulapāṁsana ! śr̥ṇu ॥ 40 ॥
mama vārayatastvayā tadā samaṁ caraṭacaurādibhiḥ । prārabdhō vyavahārastasya phalamīdr̥śaṁ jātam ॥ 41 ॥
atilōbhagrahagr̥hītō rājaviruddhamapi karōṣi vyavahāram । kāka iva paśyasi piṇḍaṁ na pr̥ṣṭhatō laguḍaprahāram ||

supāsanāha-caritryami--
avyavahāravidattō atthō'ṇatthassa kāraṇa hōi । iha paralōē ya tahā dēi agāī dukhāī ||43||
vīsasiyaghāyaṇēṇaṁ tahēva muddhāṇa vaṁcaṇēṇaṁ vā । parapīḍājaṇaēṇaṁ annaṇa ya taha uvāraṇa || 44 ||
jō dhippa parakīō atthō niru nigviṣēṇa cittēṇa । sō kuṇai bhayaṁ ghōraṁ khayaṁ ca puvvilla atthassa || 45॥
tā tumbha ihaṁ hōhī maraṇaṁ, rakkhēmi jai puṇa kahēsi । hārō jattha taē sō mukkō dina va kassā ||46
tō tēṇa piyā bhaṇiō nahu nahu hārassa tāya ! vattāvi । kāyavvā jēṇaṁ sō dinō mittassa amussa || 47 |
mā tassa hōu nāsō sadavbasakuṭuṁbassa rāyāō । maha hōu imaṁ savvaṁ dunnayakā rissa pāvassa ||48 ||
iya nicchayaṁ niēḍaṁ puttassa maṇammi raṁjiō siṭṭhī । ēyaṁpi supurisattaṁ imassa jaṁ rakkhaē mittaṁ ।। 49
tō tapāsa mōtuṁ siṭṭhī nivaaṁtiyammi saṁpattī | vinnavai dēva ! kī majjha pasāō niyavaṇissa || 50
hāravivajjaṁ savvaṁ sarūō caiva apihī ēsa | majjha ya atthanihāṇē paṇa kōḍīō suvannassa || 51 ॥
tamajjhāō giṇha dēvō hārassa mullamahiyaṁpi । taha ēyassavi daṁḍē lēu suvannati iya sōuṁ ॥ 52 ॥
bhai nivō uppajjai visamamayāō tamittha acchariyaṁ । thiradēvasarīrāō jaṁ uppannō imō puttō ॥ 53
ēyārisamma samaē payaḍēpi hu gōvaē dhaṇaṁ annō । ēsa nihāṇagayaṁpi hu payaḍai iya riumaittāē || 54॥
।
tō nāhaḍamāṇāviya appara siṭṭhista bhai tuha mukō। ēsō, āharaṇaṁ puṇa appāvasu iya nisāmēuṁ ॥
bhaṇiuṁ mahāpasāyaṁ paṇamiya taha naravaraṁ siṁhaṁ pattō । saha putrēṇa siṭṭhī rāyāiṭuṁ aṇuṭṭhēi ||56 ||
avyavahārārjitō'rthō'narthasya kāraṇaṁ bhavati । iha paralōkē ca tathā dadātyanēkāni duḥkhāni ||43||
viśvastaghātanēna tathaiva mugdhānāṁ vañcanēna vā । parapīḍājanakēnā'nyēna ca tathōpāyēna ॥ 44 ॥
1
yō gr̥hyatē parakīyō'tha niścitaṁ nirghr̥ṇēna cittēna । sa karōti bhayaṁ ghōraṁ kṣayaṁ ca pūrvīyārthasya ॥ 45 ॥
tasmāt tavēha bhaviṣyati maraṇaṁ, rakṣāmi yadi punaḥ kathayasi । hārō yatra tvayā sa muktō dattō vā kasyāpi
tatastēna pitā bhaṇitō nahi nahi hārasya tāta ! vārtāpi । kartavyā yēna sa dattō mitrāyāmukāya ||47||
mā tasya bhavatu nāśaḥ saṅgvyasakuṭumbakasya rājñaḥ । mama bhavatvidaṁ sarvaṁ durnayakāriṇaḥ pāpasya ॥48॥
iti niścayaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā putrasya manasi rañjitaḥ śrēṣṭhī । ētadapi supuruṣatvamasya yad rakṣati mitram ||49॥
tatastatpārśva muktvā śrēṣṭhī nr̥pāntikē saṁprāptaḥ । vijñapayati dēva ! kriyatāṁ mama prasādō nijavaṇijē ||10||
hāravivarjaṁ sarvaṁ svarūpata ēvārpayiṣyatyēṣaḥ । mama cārthanidhānē pañca kōṭyaḥ suvarṇasya ॥ 51 ॥
I
tanmadhyād gr̥hṇātu dēvō hārasya mūlyamadhikamapi । tathaitasyāpi daṇḍē lātu suvarṇamiti śrutvā ॥52॥
bhaṇati nr̥pa utpadyatē viṣamamr̥tāttadatrāścaryam । sthiradēvaśarīrād yadutpannō'yaṁ putraḥ ॥ 53॥
ētādr̥śē samayē prakaṭamapi hi gōpāyati vanamanyaḥ । ēṣa nidhānagatamapi hi prakaṭayatīti r̥jumatitvāt॥54
tatō nāhaṭamānāyyā'rpayati śrēṣṭhinē bhaṇati tava muktaḥ । ēṣaḥ, ābharaṇaṁ punararpayēti niśamya ॥55 ॥
bhaṇitvā mahāprasādaṁ praṇamya tathā naravaraṁ gr̥haṁ prāptaḥ । saha putrēṇa śrēṣṭhī rājādiṣṭamanutiṣṭhati ॥ 56 ॥
1 ka. sudvāṇa baṁdhavāṇaṁ vā !

nāhaḍakahā ।
sō ya taō ṭhāṇāō appaḍikaṁtō maō gaō narayaṁ । iya nāuṁ aīyāraṁ vajjaha ēvaṁ rōga
॥ iti tr̥tīyānuvatē prathamāticāradr̥ṣṭāntē nāhaṭakathā samāptā ॥
sa ca tataḥ sthānādayatikrāntō mr̥tō gatō narakam । iti jñātvā'tīcāraṁ varjayēnaṁ prayatnēna ॥ 57 ॥

jō vittuṁ taiyavvayamucchāhara takarē jaṇē musiuṁ । ihalōē paralōē dukkhaṁ sō lahai mahaṇōvva || 1 ||
tathāhi ;-
sappāyāraṁ bahusauṇasēviyaṁ paurasāvayāinnaṁ । asthi nayaraṁ pasiddhaṁ mahāaraṇṇava kusumapuraṁ || 2 ||
uvūḍhakhamābhārō nivvūḍhadaō parūḍhaguruvaṁsō । varapavvantra suthirō rāyā vairōyaṇō tattha || 3 ||
mahumahataṇuvva lacchīē parigayā varavilāsakayasōhā । laliyā tassatthi piyā sāraṁgasudaṁsaṇasaṇāha || 4
tāṇaṁ dulaharāō puttō asurōvva surasamūhassa । gurudukkhalakkhakhāṇī mahaṇō nāmēṇa sē mitō ||5||
kavi harē davvaṁ kavi mahilē balāvi girahē । ummiṭṭakariva iva ummūlai nayasamūhaṁ sō || 6 |
tō paurajaṇa rāvaṁ karēi rāyassa aggaō ēvaṁ | dēva ! anāhavva purī kumarēṇa viluṁṭiyā ahiyaṁ ||7||
tō naranāhō kumaraṁ ruṭṭhō tajjēi rē durāyāra ! । maha sīmaṁ muttūṇaṁ gacchasu sicchāē nicchayaō || 8 ||
na hu hōsi tumaṁ puttō jō maha puvvillapurisapaṁtīē । jattēṇa pāliyāō payāu lūḍēsi līlāē ॥ 9
pasuputtapavittiya tullayaṁ khu rajjavvayaṁ vayaṁti bahā । taṁ vivarīyaṁ jāyai tuha dōsē maha sahatassa ॥ 10 ॥
ēsō ya lakkhahōmō ēvaṁ saravadēvagihakaraṇaṁ । nīīē pālijjai jaṁ niyarajjē jō sabbō ॥11॥ .
uktaṁ ca;
“
duṣṭasya daṇḍa: sujanasya pūjā nyāyēna kōśasya ca saṁpravr̥ddhiḥ ।
apakṣapātō ripurāṣṭrarakṣā pañcaiva yajñāḥ kathitā nr̥pāṇām ॥
kiṁ dēvakāryēṇa narādhipānāṁ kr̥tvā hi manyuṁ viṣamasthitānām ? |
yō gr̥hītvā tr̥tīyatratamutsāhayati taskarāñjanān mōṣitum । ihalōkē paralōkē duḥkhaṁ sa labhatē mahana iva ॥ 1
saprākā (padhā ) raṁ bahusaguṇa (śakuna ) sēvitaṁ pracuraśrāvakā ( śvāpadā) kīrṇam ।
asti nagaraṁ prasiddhaṁ mahāraṇyamiva kusumapuram ||2||
uddvyūḍhakṣamābhārō nirvyūḍhadayaḥ (dakaḥ) prarūḍhaguruvaṁśaḥ । paraparvata iva susthirō rājā vairōcanastatra ॥3॥
madhumathatanuriva lakṣmyā parigatā varavilāsakr̥taśōbhā । lalitā tasyāsti priyā sā ( sa ) raṅgasudarśana sanāthā ॥ 4
tayōrdurlabharājaḥ putrō'sura iva surasamūhasya । guruduḥ khalakṣakhānirmahanō nāmnā tasya mitram ॥5॥
kasyāpi harati dravyaṁ kasyāpi mahilāṁ balādapi gr̥hṇāti । unmuktakarivara ivōnmūlayati naya ( naga ) samūhaṁ saḥ
tataḥ paurajanō rāvaṁ karōti rājñō'grata ēvam | dēva ! anāthēva purī kumārēṇa viluṇṭitā'dhikam ॥7॥
tatō naranāthaḥ kumāraṁ ruṣṭastarjayati rē durācāra ! । mama sīmānaṁ muktvā gaccha svēcchayā niścayataḥ ॥8॥
na khalu bhavasi tvaṁ putrō yō mama pūrvīyapuruṣapaṅkayā । yatnēna pālitāḥ prajā luṇṭasi līlayā ||9||
paśuputrapravr̥ttau tulyaṁ khalu rājyatrataṁ vadanti budhāḥ । tad viparītaṁ jāyatē tava dōṣān mama sahamānasya ॥ 10॥
ēṣa ca lakṣahōma ētat saraḥ kūpadēvagr̥hakaraṇam । nītyā pālyatē yad nijarājyē janaḥ sarvaḥ ॥ 11 ॥

sīyaṁ khuhaṁ pivāsaṁ sahēmi jēsi kaē sayāvi ahaṁ । tēsiṁ taṁ gharasāraṁ dārē ya haḍhēṇa avaharasi || 12 ||
tāna taē maha kajja sajjō rajjaṁ caēsu mahataṇayaṁ । vara sunnacciya sālā mā bhariyā cōracaraḍaṇaṁ ॥ 13 ॥
tō rāyavayaṇavaṇadava guruyarajālāvalīpalittaṁgō । kumarō mahaṇasamēō caliō nayaraṁ vimuttūrṇa ॥14॥
tājā kammivinayarē talāyapālīē muṇivarō tēṇa । diṭṭō siddhasuraṇaṁ saṁvāhijjatapayakamalō || 15॥
taṁ vaṁdiūṇa sōvi hu uvaviṭṭhō tattha ciṭṭhaē jāva । tā tannayarapahāṇaṁ vilāsiṇīnaṁdamaṇupattaṁ ॥ 16 ॥
ēkāē tō bhaṇiya halā halā ! piccha piccha acchariyaṁ । nayaṇamahūsava bhūyaṁ rūvaṁ ēyassa bhikkhussa | 17|
niyarūtragavviyāē tā bhaṇiyā thukkiūṇa annāē । cuchiyagallaṁ ēyaṁ mā bhattāraṁ halā ! kuṇasu || 18॥
taṁ suṇiya siddhaputtō kuviō guruparibhavōtti kaliūṇa । vijjāvalēṇa taṁ lahu kuṇai muṇiṁ paṛa sakāmamaṇaṁ ।।
aha sā picchaṁtīṇa annāṇaṁ bhaṇai muṇivaraṁ suhaya! | rahiyāē tara pāyā vahaṁti nō maha iō gaṁtuṁ ॥ 20 ॥
iyarāja bhaṇati halā ! daṭṭumimaṁ thukkiyassa tuha tassa । iya nivvāṇaṁ jāyaṁ tō sā dīṇāṇaṇā bhaṇai ||
mā maha khayammi khāraṁ khivēha sahapaṁsukīliyā hōuṁ । mannāvaha kiṁtu imaṁ jalaṁjali dēha vā majjha ||22||
aha niviḍapīḍiyā sāpaḍiyā bhūmīē vilavaē subahuṁ । tō vijjaṁ saṁhariḍaṁ sā bhaṇiyā siddhaputtrēṇa ॥ 23॥
ramaṇīu ēsa mannai māyaṁgīuvva jō achippāō । tā tuha ittha kilēsō hōhī viphalō virama taṁmhā || 24 ॥
kiñca ।
śītaṁ kṣudhaṁ pipāsāṁ sahē yēṣāṁ kr̥tē sadāpyaham । tēṣāṁ tvaṁ gr̥hasāraṁ dārāṁśca haṭhēnāpaharasi ॥ 12 ॥
tasmānna tava mama kāryaṁ sadyō rājyaṁ tyaza madīyam । varaṁ śūnyaiva śālā mā bhr̥tā cauracaraṭaiḥ ||13||
tatō rājavacanavanadavagurutarajvālāvalīpradīptāṅgaḥ । kumārō mahanasamētaścalitō nagaraṁ vimucya ॥ 14 ॥
tāvadyāvatkasminnapi nagarē taḍākapālyāṁ munivarastēna । dr̥ṣṭaḥ siddhasutēna saṁvāhyamānapadakamalaḥ ॥ 15 ॥
taṁ vanditvā sō'pi khalūpaviṣṭastatra tiṣṭhati yāvat । tāvattannagarapradhānaṁ vilāsinīvr̥ndamanuprāptam || 16॥
ēkayā tatō bhaṇitaṁ halāhalā ! paśya paśyāścaryam | nayanamahōtsavabhūtaṁ rūpamētasya bhikṣōḥ ॥ 17॥
nijarūpagarvitayā tadā bhaṇitā thūtkr̥tyānyayā । pariśōṣitagallamētaṁ mā bhartāraṁ halā ! kuruṣva ॥ 18 ॥
tatśrutvā siddhaputraḥ kupitō guruparibhava iti kalayitvā । vidyābalēna tāṁ laghu karōti muniṁ prati sakāmamanasama ||
atha sā paśyatīṣvanyāsu bhaṇati munivaraṁ subhaga ! | rahitayā tvayā pādau vahatō nō mamētō gantum ||20|
itarā bhaṇanti halā ! dr̥ṣṭē maṁ thūtkr̥tasya tava tasya । idaṁ nirvāṇaṁ jātaṁ tataḥ sā dīnānanā bhaṇati ॥21॥.
mā mama kṣatē kṣāraṁ kṣipata sahapāṁśukrīḍitā bhūtvā । mānayata kintvimaṁ jalāñjaliṁ datta vā mama ॥ 22॥
atha nibiḍapīḍitā sā patitā bhūmau vilapati subahu । tatō vidyāṁ saṁhatya sā bhaṇitā siddhaputrēṇa ||23||
ramaṇīrēṣa manyatē mātaṅgīriva yōsspr̥śyāḥ । tasmāttavātra klēśō bhaviṣyati viphalō virama tasmāt ||24||
।

tattha saṁkalatamitō jā jiṇabhavaṇammi vaṁdaē dēvē । tā tappurāhigārī samāgaō tattha tammi khaṇē ॥36

tatō bhaṇati muniṁ vēśyā yatkartavyaṁ mayā tadādiśata । tataḥ kathayitvā saṁsāraṁ duḥkhānāṁ khaniṁ munistāsām

muktārambhāṇāṁ saḥ, viṣayaviraktānāṁ sā punaravasthā | ityādi prapañcya mahāvratāṇuvratāni kathayati ॥ 28 ॥

sōvitavyutta jahaṭṭiya sāhaē ahahigārī । jōḍiyahatyā kumaraṁ patthiya niyamaṁdiraṁ nēi ||39||
sammā sakāra, ittō ya jamālipallināhēṇa । suyaaliyana rēsara vissasēṇapaṁcattavattēṇa ॥ 40 ॥
āgaṁtūṇaṁ ruddhaṁ taṁ puramittō jalaṁ na tammajjhē । bāhirajalaṁ niruddhaṁ paracakēṇaṁ taō lōō ||41||
accatamālattaṁ pattō ahiġāriṇaṁ bhaṇai ēvaṁ । pugbhēyassa samappaha kāūṇa dayaṁ ubari amha ||42||
kiṁkāvyavimūḍhō ahigārī jāna ciṭṭhaē tāva | tō kumarēṇaṁ maṇiyaṁ ēgaṁtē, bhaṇaha lōyamiṇaṁ ||43||
jaha ja juttaṁ hōhī taṁ kāmahaṁ pabhāyasamayampi । tō tēṇa tahēva kayaṁ pacchā kumaraṁ bhaṇai sōvi ||44 ||
kiṁ kāvyāṇi kumarō taṁ bhaṇai jamiha kāyantraṁ । pabhāēcciya kahiyavaṁ saṁpayaṁ nēya || 45॥
tō rayaṇīē hamasē pāyāraṁ laṁghiūṇa kiraṇēṇa । vijyukttēṇa gaō āvāsē pallināhassa ॥46॥
tassa ya sayaṇahāṇaṁ saṁcārinakamēḍayastuvariṁ । taḍiō ta suttaṁ dhariya vāhāē ||47॥
bhai ahaṁ ittha purē jakkhō āravakhagō ya ēkssa । tā jai ittha pabhāē ciṭṭhasi tō marasi nibrbhataṁ ।।
iya bhaṇi nākamudārapaṇaṁ ca tassa hatthā ō । dhittuṁ tahēva kiraṇaṁ dāūṇaṁ jāi sahāṇaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
pallivaīvi bhīō takkhaṇamēva ya payāṇayaṁ dēi । kahiuṁ jahadviyaṁ pariyaṇassa āsannavattissa ॥50॥
aha ahiṁgāricarāvi hu picchatā taṁ tahēva suṇiūṇaṁ । sāhaṁti tassa sōvi hu hiṭṭhō kumarassa taṁ kaiha || 51||
paṇa kumarō punnōdaēṇa tuha jāyasēyamaha sōvi । kumaraṁgulīē pāsai muddārayaṇaṁ sudippataṁ || 52 ||
kōūhalē hatthā tassa gahiūṇa taṁ palōyaṁtō । pallīvaissa nāmaṁ daṭhṭhē raṁjiyamaṇī bhaṇai ||53 ||
