sō'pi hi tadavr̥ttāntaṁ yathāsthitaṁ kathayatyathādhikārī । yōjitahastaḥ kumāraṁ prārthya nijamandiraṁ nayati ॥39॥
sammānayati satkārayātē, itaśca jamālipallīnāthēna । śrutālīkanarēśvaraviśvasēnapañcatvavārtēna ॥ 40 ॥
āgatya ruddhaṁ tatpuramitō jalaṁ na tanmadhyē । bāhyajalaṁ niruddhaṁ paracakrēṇa tatō lōkaḥ ॥41॥
atyantamākulatva prāptō'dhikāriṇaṁ bhaṇatyēvam । puramētasmai samarpayata kr̥tvā dayāmupasmākam ॥42॥
kiṁkartavyavimūḍhō'dhikārī yāvattiṣṭhati tāvat । tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitamēkāntē, bhaṇata lōkamimam ॥ 43 ॥
yathā yad yuktaṁ bhaviṣyatiṁ tatkariṣyē'haṁ prabhātasamayē । tatastēna tathaiva kr̥taṁ paścātkumāraṁ bhaṇati sō'pi ॥ 44 ॥
kiṁkartavyamidānīṁ kumārastaṁ bhaṇati yadiha kartavyam । tad yuṣmākaṁ prabhāta ēva kathayitavyaṁ sāṁprataṁ naiva ॥ 45 ॥
tatō rajanyāṁ kumāraḥ prākāraṁ laṅghitvā kiraṇēna । vidyatkṣiptēna gata āvāsē pallīnāthasya ॥ 46 ॥
tasya ca śayanasthānaṁ saṁcārimakāṣṭhamālāyā upari । tathaiva tatra caṭitastaṁ suptaṁ śrutvā bāhunā ॥ 47 ॥
bhaṇatyahamatra purē yakṣa ārakṣakañcatasya । tasmād yadyatra prabhātē tiṣṭhasi tatō mriyasē nirbhrāntam ||48||
iti bhaṇitvā nāmāṅkitamudrāratnaṁ ca tasya hastāt । gr̥hītvā tathaiva kiraṇaṁ dattvā yāti svasthānam ॥ 49 ॥
pallīpatirapi khalu bhītastatkṣaṇamēva ca prayāṇakaṁ dadāti । kathayitvā yathāsthitaṁ parijanasyāsannavartinaḥ ||50 ॥
athādhikāricarā api hi paśyantastattathaiva śrutvā । kathayanti tasya sō'pi hi hr̥ṣṭaḥ kumārasya tatkathayati ॥ 51 ॥

supāsanāha-cariammi-
tuha purisarayaṇa ! ēsō vavasāō sāhasikkarasiyassa । sō bhaṇai saccamēyaṁ kiṁpuṇa taiyavvayaṁ bhaggaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
sō āha ēvamēyaṁ kiṁpuṇa sāhammiyammi vacchallaṁ । mai tumbhēhiṁ vihiyaṁ taṁ puṇa uvayāri saṁjāyaṁ ॥ 55॥
saṁghassa paramabhaṭṭārayassa jiṇanāhacēiyāṇaṁ ca । tahavi iha saṁti guruṇō, ālōijjau imaṁ tēsiṁ ॥ 56 ॥
kumarēṇa tō tahēva ya vihiyaṁ, ittō ya vissasēṇōvi । naranāhō nīrōgō jāōtti samāgayā vattā ॥57॥
puvyuttavaiyarēṇaṁ purassa abhayaṁti saha kumārēṇa । nivavissasēṇamaṁgalakaraṇatthaṁ jāi ahigārī ||58 ||
kahai kumarassarūvaṁ taṁ sōuṁ naravarō viciṁtēi । puttara hiyassa puttō ēsōciya hōu maha inhiṁ ॥ 59 ॥
dhūlāṇavarāhāṇaṁ jaṁtūṇa vahammi ēsa jaṁ viraō । tō vissāsagayassavi maha atthi bhayaṁ na ēyāō || 60||
iya taṁ juvarāyapaē ṭhaviya nikkhivai taimmi rajjabharaṁ । ucchappara tassaṁgāḍu jiṇamayaṁ laddhasammattō ॥ 61 ॥
puvyutthāiyanaravaradē sē daṁḍāhinaṁ ṭhavai mahaṇaṁ । taddēsaṭṭhiyacaraḍā rajjaṁtara niyaḍadēsa ṭiyaṁ ॥ 62 ॥
luṁṭaṁti jaṇaṁ āṇaṁti taddhaṇaṁ māṇusaṁ ca mahaṇō ya । ucchāhai tē, tēvi ya diti payatthāṇa chanbhāgē ॥ 63 ॥
sō lōhaggahaghatthō na gaṇai taiyavvayassa mālinnaṁ । sīmāladēsarāōvi jāṇiuṁ ciṁtai, na dēsa ॥ 64॥
lūḍāvatō ṭhāhī ēsō tō ghāyagāō sō mahaṇaṁ । vaivarōyāvai, sōvi hu vihiūṇaṁ taiyavayabhaṁgaṁ ||65 ||
saṁciyapavarapatthēsu mucchiō ghāyagammi aikuddhō । rudajjhāṇōvagaō pattō taccāē puḍhavīē ॥ 66 ॥
bhamihī bhavammi suciraṁ tamhā taiyavvayammi aiyāraṁ । takkarapaōgarūvaṁ. vajjaha jai mahaha sivasōkkhaṁ ॥ 67
kutūhalēna hastāttasya gr̥hītvā tatpralōkamānaḥ । pallīpatērnāma dr̥ṣṭrā rañjitamanā bhaṇati ॥53॥
tava puruṣaratna ! ēṣa vyavasāyaḥ sāhasaikarasikasya । sa bhaṇati satyamētat kintu tr̥tīyatatraṁ bhagnam ॥54॥
sa āhaivamētat kintu sādharmikē'pi vātsalyam । mayi yuṣmābhirvihitaṁ tatpunarupakāri saṁjātam ||55॥
saṁghasya paramabhaṭṭārakasya jinanāthacaityānāṁ ca । tathāpīha santi guravaḥ, ālōcyatāmidaṁ tēbhyaḥ ॥ 56 ॥
kumārēṇa tatastathaiva ca vihitam, itaśca viśvasēnō'pi । naranāthō nīrōgō jāta iti samāgatā vārtā ॥ 57 ॥
pūrvōktavyatikarēṇa purasyābhayamiti saha kumārēṇa । nr̥paviśvasēnamaṅgalakaraṇārthaṁ yātyadhikārī ||18||
kathayati kumārasvarūpaṁ tat śrutvā naravarō vicintayati । putrarahitasya putra ēṣa ēva bhavatu mamēdānīm ॥ 59॥
sthūlānaparādhānāṁ jantūnāṁ vadha ēṣa yad virataḥ । tatō viśvāsagatasyāpi mamāsti bhayaṁ naitasmāt ||60 ||
iti taṁ yuvarājapadē sthāpayitvā nikṣipati tasminrājyabharam । utsarpayati tatsaṅgājjinamataṁ labdhasamyakr̥tvaḥ ॥ 61 ॥
pūrvōtthāpitanaravaradēśē daṇḍādhipaṁ sthāpayati mahanam । taddēśasthitacaraṭā rājyāntara nikaṭadēśasthitam ॥ 62॥
luṇṭhanti janamānayanti taddhanaṁ mānuṣaṁ ca, mahanaśca । utsāhayati tān, tē'pi ca dadati padārthānāṁ ṣaṣṭhabhāgān ॥
sa lōbhagrahagrastō na gaṇayati tr̥tīyatratasya mālinyam । sīmasthadēśarājō'pi jñātvā cintayati, na dēśam ॥ 64|
luṇṭayan sthāsyatyēṣa tatō ghātakātsa mahanam । vyaparōpayati, sō'pi khalu vidhāya tr̥tīyatratabhaṅgam || 65॥
saṁcitapravarapadārthēṣu mūcchitō ghātakē'tikruddhaḥ । raudradhyānōpagataḥ prāptastr̥tīyāyāṁ pr̥thivyām ||66 ॥

niyanivaviruddharajjē vāṇijjaṁ udayaṇōvva jō kuṇai । taiyatrayamaiyaraṁtō sō lahai ghaṇataṇuviṇāsaṁ ca ॥ 1॥
tathāhi;
-
bahumupasupattiṁ sattarisinisēviyaṁ nahaṁ hasai । jaṁ bahubuhamēgavuhaṁ taṁ naraṁ asthi vibhadaṁ ||2|
bahukaṇaō surayaṇasēviō ya sannaṁdaṇī suragirivva । tatthathi thirapagaī siṭṭī rayaṇāyarō nāma || 3 ॥
tassatthi vaha surasuṁdarivva thirajuvvaṇā kaṇayakaṁtī | aṇamisanayaṇā bahuvibuhasaṁmayā suṁdarī nāma ||4||
tāṇa taṇaō viṇīō viṇayātaṇaucca sauṇakaya sēvō । nāmēṇa rāyapālō savvāsu kalāsu aikusalō || 5 |
kagayaddhaya siṭṭisuō tammittaṁ udayaṇōtti vikkhāō । tēṇa samaṁ sō kīlai sarisara ārāmamāīsu || 6 ||
aha diṭṭhā varavālā kītēhi naīē annadiṇē । jaladēvayanva divvaṁga saṁgayā sāralaṁkārā ||7||
kaṭṭhavilaggaṁ majjaṇanimmajjaṇēhiṁ mayaṁva appāṇaṁ । mannatī dūrāō daṭṭṇaṁ tē imaṁ bhaṇai ||8||
maraṇabhayabhīruyāē saraṇavihūṇāē dīṇavayaṇāē । dēha maha pāṇabhikkhaṁ mōvēkkhaha, tō khaṇadvēṇa ॥9॥
uttāriūna tēhi naiṣpavāhāō pucchiyāṁ ēvaṁ | kā si tumaṁ kō hēū ihāgamē, kahai sā ēvaṁ ॥ 10॥
1
asthi nayaraṁ pasiddhaṁ siddhē saranāmayaṁ dhaṇasamiddhō । tattha vaṇī guṇasēṇō tanbhajjā jayasirī nāma |
sattasuyāṇaṁ ubariṁ jāyā uvajāiēhiṁ tēsimahaṁ । aivalahatti kāuṁ dullahadēvī kayaṁ nāma || 12 ||
aha juvvaṇapattāē vaṇiputtā iṁti majjha varaṇatthaṁ । nāhaṁ mannēmi taē bhaṇiyāvi hu ammāī || 13 |
sāvayakulē pasūyā aṇavarayaṁ sāhusaṁgamarayā ya । lahukammayāvasēṇaṁ nāhaṁ maṇasāvi gihivāsa || 14 ||
nijanr̥paviruddha rājyē vāṇijyamudayana iva yaḥ karōti । tr̥tīyatratamaticaran sa labhatē dhanatanuvināśaṁ ca ॥1॥
bahumunipadapavitraṁ saptarṣiniṣēvitaṁ nabhō hasati । yad bahubudhamēkabudhaṁ tannagaramasti śivabhadram ॥2॥
bahukanakaḥ suratna [ jana ] sēvitaśca sannandanaḥ suragirivat । tatrāsti sthira prakr̥tiḥ śrēṣṭhī ratnākarō nāma ||3|
tasyāsti vadhūḥ surasundarība sthirayauvanā kanakakāntiḥ । animiṣanayanā bahuvibudhasaṁmatā sundarī nāma ||4॥
tayōstanayō vinītō vinatātanaya iva saguṇa [ kuna ]kr̥ta sēvaḥ । nāmnā rājapālaḥ sarvāsu kalāsvatikuśalaḥ ॥5॥
kanakadhvajaśrēṣṭhisutastanmittramudayana iti vikhyātaḥ । tēna samaṁ sa krīḍati saritsara ārāmādiṣu ॥ 6 ॥
atha dr̥ṣṭā gharabālā krīḍadbhyāṁ nadyāmanyadinē । jaladēvatēva divyāṅgasaṁgatā sārālaṅkārā ॥7॥
kāṣṭhavilagnaṁ majjananimajjanairmr̥tamivātmānam । manyamānā dūrād dr̥ṣṭvā tāvidaṁ bhaṇati ॥8॥
maraṇabhayabhīrōḥ śaraṇavihīnāyā dīnavadanāyāḥ । dattaṁ mama prāṇabhikṣāṁ mōpēkṣāthāṁ, tataḥ kṣaṇārdhēna ॥ 9 ॥
uttārya tābhyāṁ nadīpravāhāt pr̥ṣṭavam । kā'si tvaṁ kō hēturihāgamē, kathayati saivam ॥ 10 ॥
asti nagaraṁ prasiddhaṁ siddhēśvaranāmakaṁ, dhanasamr̥ddhaḥ । tatra vaṇig guṇasē nastadbhāryā jayaśrīrnāma ॥11॥
saptasutānāmupari jātōpayācitaistayōraham । ativallabhēti kr̥tvā durlabhadēvī kr̥taṁ nāma ॥12॥
atha yauvanaprāptāyā vaṇikputrā āyanti mama varaṇārtham । nāhaṁ manyē tān bhaṇitāpi khambādibhiḥ ॥13॥
śrāvakakulē prasūtā'navarataṁ sādhusaṁgamaratā ca । laghukarmatāvaśēna nāhaṁ manasāpi gr̥hivāsam ॥14॥

patthēmi saṁjamaṁ ciya paraṁ piṁyā nēhēparavasō majjha । na visajjai tō ya ahaṁ sāvayadhammaṁpi pālēmi ॥ 15 ॥
suhāliyā piūhiṁ ciṭṭhēmi gimmi, annayā caliyā । jiṇabhavaṇē tā diṭṭhā ṭhakkuraputtāṇa juyalēṇa ||
ēkkēṇa taō bhaṇiyā mayacchi ! pasiūṇa mēṁ palōēsa । tuhadiṭṭiśramayavuṭṭīē chaṁṭiō nivvuō hōmi ।।
bīēṇa puṇō bhaṇiyā jai sacca sāviyā dayapahāṇā । tā maṁ mōtuṁ annō maṇasāvi na patthaṇijjō tē । । 18 ॥
annaha kaē ya niyamā mama pāṇā pavisihaṁti paralōē । isa asamaṁjasavayaṇē sōūṇaṁ tāṇa vēgēṇa ॥ 19 ॥
jiṇabhavaṇaṁ tō pattā pūēvi vihīē vaṁdiuṁ dēvē । caliyā jāva siṁhaṁ paṛa tā magaṁ baṁdhiuṁ dōvi || 20 ||
tē yadarddha naṭṭhā ummaggaō gayā dūraṁ । piṭṭhīē tēvi diṭṭhā āgacchaṁtā turiyaturiyaṁ ॥ 21 ॥
tō haṁ saṁkaragēhē pavisēuṁ baṁdhiūṇa tadāraṁ । jāna ṭhiyā tā tēvi hu parōpparaṁ jujjhiuṁ laggā ||22||
tres ēgō maha bhāriyā imā bīyaō bhaṇai majjha । tō paḍhamēṇaṁ khaggēṇa āhaō sōvi bīēṇa ॥23॥
iya asamaṁjasamēyaṁ nāuṁ ugghāḍiūṇa tadāraṁ । avalōiyā maē tē dunnividiṭṭhā gayappāṇā || 24||
tō ciṁtiyaṁ ahaṁ ciya hī maraṇassa kāraṇamimēsiṁ । saṁjāyā ahavā mōhavilasiyaṁ majjha kō dōsō ? |
suīrasa nijjharaṇē haḍḍukkaraḍampi cammanasanaddhē । kō nāma kimi mōtuṁ ramēi dēhammi ramaṇīṇaṁ ? ॥ 26 ॥
kāmiṇiniyaṁvarvivaṁ kaṁdaṣpavilā sarāyahāṇitti । na muṇai amējjhapōṭṭaṁ ahaha ahō ! mōhamāhaṇaṁ ||27|
tivalītaraṁgasaṁgayanāhiṁ ramaṇīṇa amayakuṁḍaṁti । mannaṁti na uṇa nīsaṁkhadukkhalakkhakkhaṇi mūḍhā ॥ 28 ॥
prārthayē saṁyamamēva paraṁ pitā snēhaparavaśō mama । na visr̥jati tataścāhaṁ śrāvakadharmamapi pālayāmi ॥15॥
sukhalālitā pitr̥bhyāṁ tiṣṭhāmi gr̥hē, anyadā calitā । jinabhavanē tadā dr̥ṣṭā ṭhakkuraputrayōryugalēna ॥ 16 ॥
ēkēna tatō bhaṇitā mr̥gākṣi ! prasadya māṁ pralōkaya । tvadr̥ṣṭamr̥tavr̥ṣṭayōkṣitā nirvr̥tō bhavāmi ॥17॥
dvitīyēna punarbhaṇitā yadi satyaṁ śrāvikā dayāpradhānā । tadā māṁ muktvā'nyō manasāpi na prārthanīyastē ॥ 18 ॥
anyathā kr̥tē ca niyamānmama prāṇāḥ pravēkṣyanti paralōkē । ityasamañjasavacanāni śrutvā tayōrvēgēna ॥ 19 ॥
jinabhavanaṁ tataḥ prāptā pūjayitvā vidhinā vanditvā dēvān । calitā yāvad gr̥haṁ prati tāvanmārga baddhā dvāvapi ॥ 20॥
sthitau ca tau ca dr̥ṣṭrā naṣṭōnmārgatō gatā dūram । pr̥ṣṭhē tāvapi dr̥ṣṭāvāgacchantau tvaritatvaritam ॥21॥
ca,
tatō'haṁ śaṅkaragēhē praviśya baddhvā tadddvāram । yāvatsthitā tāvattāvapi hi parasparaṁ yōddhuṁ lagnaiau ॥22॥
pratyēkō mama bhāryēyaṁ dvitīyō bhaṇati mama । tataḥ prathamēna khaṅgēna hataḥ sō'pi dvitīyēna ॥23॥
ityasamañjasamētajjñātvōdghāṭya taddvāram । avalōkitau mayā tau dvāvapi dr̥ṣṭau gataprāṇau ॥ 24 ॥

aśucirasanirjharaṇē'sthiviṣṭhārāśau carmanasanaddhē । kō nāma kr̥miṁ muktvā ramatē dēhē ramaṇīnām ! ||26||

ēvaṁpi imē daṭhṭhē maṁ mūḍhā jaha mayā tahanēvi । mā mujjhaṁtu maraṁtu ya ciṁtiya paḍiyā naīē ahaṁ ||29||
pacchā puṇō vicitiyamahaha ! mahāpātramēyamāyariyaṁ । appāṇammi parammi ya vahō nisiddhō jiṇidē hiṁ
iya maraṇabhīruyā haṁ tumhāṁ dihigōyaraṁ pattā । nikkāraṇakaruṇārasaparēhiṁ jīvāviyā ēvaṁ ||31||
tō tēhiṁsā bhaṇiyā bhaiṇī amhāṇa taṁ mahābhāgē ! । āgaccha gihē pacchā piūṇa pāsē naissāmō ॥ 3ḥ
tō tēhiṁ samaṁ rayaṇāyarassa siṭṭissa sā gihaṁ pattā । kahiyā ya tassa vattā tēṇa kayā uciya1ḍivattī ॥3
bhaṇiō tattō tīē siṭṭī rayaṇāyarō maha piūṇaṁ । hōi athiī, tēsiṁ tā jāṇāvaha maha saruvaṁ ||34|
tēṇāvi tahēva kayaṁ sāvi puṇō tammi cēva samayammi । na gayā 'imāī dhammē ṭhāvēmī' isa vicitē ॥ 3
giridhammaṁ tō tīē sammaṁ jāṇāviyāī savvāī । tēhivi sō sattīē paḍivannō sugurumūlammi || 36॥
tajjayāī tatyāgayāiṁ thēvēhiṁ caiva diyahēhiṁ । gauraviyāī rayaṇāyarēṇa kahiyē ca tēsimimaṁ ||37|
tumha viōē tumhēṁ suyāē amhāṇa saphaliō jammō । jiṇadhammapayāṇēṇaṁ, imaṁ ca saccaṁ kathaṁ vayaṇaṁ ॥ 3
“yadyapi vipadi vinaśyati paramupakurutē tathāpi khalu sujanaḥ । svayamagururdānna[ ? ]pi samīpalōkaṁ tu surabhayati
tō tīsē piyarāī ciṁtaṁti jahā imīē visaēsuṁ । giddhiṁ jaṇaislāmō āsāmittaṁ imaṁ amha || 39॥
jā iya annapi jaṇaṁ visaēsa viraṁjaī ṭhavara dhammē । tīsē sayaṁmāsattī visaēsa kaō iha bhavammi ? ॥4
ittō ya sā paryapara calaṇēsuṁ paṇamiūṇa piyarāṇa । kijjau mē anukaṁpā dikkhā dāvijjaḍa ihēva ||4
jaṁ maha ēyāvatthā maraṇassa nibaṁdhaṇaṁ varāyāṇaṁ । saṁjāyā tēsimahaṁ vivēyaviyalattaṇēṇaṁ ca ॥42॥
ēvamapamau dr̥ṣṭvā māṁ mūḍhau yathā mr̥tau tathānyē'pi । mā muhyantu mriyantāṁ ca cintayitvā patitā nadyāmahara
paścāt punarvicintitamahaha 1 mahāpāpamētadācaritam । ātmanaḥ parasya ca vadhō niṣiddhō jinēndraiḥ ||30||
iti maraṇabhīrurahaṁ yuvayōrhaṣṭigōcaraṁ prāptā । niṣkāraṇa karuṇārasaparābhyāṁ jīvitaivam ॥31॥
tatastābhyāṁ sī bhaṇitā bhāginyāvayōstvaṁ mahābhāgē ! । āgaccha gr̥hē paścāt pitrōḥ pārśvē nēṣyāvaḥ ॥ 32
tatastābhyāṁ samaṁ ratnākarasya śrēṣṭhinaḥ sā gr̥haṁ prāptā । kathitā ca tasya vārtā tēna kr̥tōcitapratipattiḥ ॥3
bhaṇitastatastayā śrēṣṭhī ratnākarō mama pitrōḥ । bhavatyadhr̥tiḥ, tau tasmājjñāpaya mama svarūpam ॥ 34 ॥

tajjananījanakō tatrāgatau stōkairēva divasaiḥ । gauravitau ratnākarēṇa kathitaṁ ca tayōridam ||37||

tatastasyāḥ pitarau cintayatō yathā'syā viṣayēṣu । gr̥ddhiṁ janayiṣyāma āśāmātramidamasmākam ॥ 39॥
yētyanyamapi janaṁ viṣayēṣu virañjayati sthāpayati dharmē । tasyāḥ svayamāsaktirviṣayēṣu kuta iha bhavē ? ||40|

“śabdādyāḥ sumanōramāḥ priyajanō ramyaḥ prabhutvōjjvalā lakṣmī rityanubhāvayankila hitō'smyasyēti buddhacā janaḥ |

tuha asamasīlasuvivēyavayaṇaviṇaēhiṁ raṁjiyamaṇassa । sahasā adaṁsaṇēṇaṁ araisamudē nimaggassa || 47||
hōi taraṁḍaṁ tuha caiva daṁsaṇaṁ, tā tarhi lahu ēhi । kāhamahaṁ gayamittō sahalaṁ tuha vaṁchiṁya vacchē ! ॥ 48 ॥

atha ratnākara śrēṣṭhinaṁ nagarē siddhēśvarē gamanārtham । āpr̥cchatē guṇasēnaḥ śrēṣṭhī tataḥ sa bhaṇatyēvam ॥ 49 ॥

tassaṁsaggāō udayaṇōvi ujjamai dhammakajjēsu । vavahāraṁpi hu pāyam̐ kuṇaṁti tē dōvi samamēva ॥ 55 ॥
aha annayā payaṭṭē pōyaṇapurarāyasayala sammi | dubbhikkhē aghōrē, sivabhadapurē sadēsē u ॥ 56 ॥
savvattha subhikkhēcciya taddēsanarāhivēṇa savvōvi । lōō bhaṇāviō jaha māṇayamikkaṁpi dhannassa ॥ 57
pōyaṇapurasammī jō pēsissai vaṇī ahaṁ tassa । kāhāmi mahādaṁḍē tahēva savvassaavaharaṇaṁ ॥ 58 ॥
iya jāṇiuṁpi dhannaṁ pacchannaṁ udayaṇō tarhi dētē । pēsai vaṇiuttēhiṁ taṁ nāyaṁ rāyapālēṇa ॥ 59 ॥
tō bhai udayaṇaṁ sō tujjha na juttaṁ viruddharajjammi । vabahariḍaṁ tā saṁhara jai sumarasi nivaiṇō āṇaṁ ।। 60
kiñca ।
jamhā taiyavayammī ēvaṁ aiyāramāyaraṁtassa । hōhī dhammaviruddhaṁ kōvāō taha nariṁdassa ॥ 61 ॥
attha sō māṇasa khaṁḍaṇaṁ jīviyassa saṁdēhō । ahamajaṇāṇaṁ kīlā pīlā taha sayaṇavaggassa || 62 ||
sr vāriōvi viramai jāva na sō naravarēṇa tō nāō । avahariṁḍaṁ savvassaṁ nijjaṁtō vajjhaṭhāṇammi || 63
kicchrēṇa rāyapālēṇa mōiō naravarāō karuṇāē । tō mariumapaḍikkaṁtō bhamihī bhavasāya suciraṁ ॥ 66
gihidhammaṁ paripālaya rayaṇāyarasāvayassavi kuṭuṁbaṁ । laddhasudēvattasumāṇusattamacirā sivaṁ pattaṁ ॥ 65 ॥
॥ iti tr̥tīyāvatē viruddharājyātikramāticārē udayanakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
1
itaśca śrēṣṭhī ratnākarō'pyaṅgīkr̥tē gr̥hidharmē । udyacchati kuṭumbayutastasya sutō rājapālō'pi ॥ 54 ॥
tatsaṁsargādudayanō'pyudyacchati dharmakāryēṣu । vyavahāramapi hi prāyaḥ kurutastau dvāvapi samamēva ||15||
athānyadā pravr̥ttē pōtanapurarājasakaladēśē । durbhikṣē'tighōrē śivabhadrapurē svadēśē tu ॥ 56 ॥
sarvatra subhikṣa ēva taddēśanarādhipēna sarvō'pi । lōkō bhāṇitō yathā māṇakamēkamapi dhānyasya ॥57॥
pōtanapuradēśē yaḥ prēṣayiṣyati vaṇigahaṁ tasya । kariṣyāmi mahādaṇḍaṁ tathaiva sarvasvāpaharaṇam ||18||
iti jñātvāpi dhānyaṁ pracchannamudayanastatra dēśē । prēṣayati vaṇikputraistajjñātaṁ rājapālēna ||19||
tatō bhaṇatyudayanaṁ sa tava na yuktaṁ viruddharājyē । vyavahartuṁ tasmātsaṁhara yadi smarasi nr̥patērājñām ||60 ॥
yasmāt tr̥tīyatrata ēvamaticāramācarataḥ । bhaviṣyati dharmaviruddhaṁ kōpāt tathā narēndrasya ||31||
arthabhraṁśō mānasya khaṇḍanaṁ jīvitasya saṁdēhaḥ । adhamajanānāṁ krīḍā pīḍā tathā svajanavargasya ॥ 62 ॥
iti vāritō'pi viramatiyāvanna sa naravarēṇa tatō jñātaḥ । apahr̥tya sarvasvaṁ nīyamānō vadhyasthānē ||63||
kr̥cchrēṇa rājapālēna mōcitō naravarāt karuṇayā । tatō mr̥tvā'pratikrāntō bhramiṣyati bhavasāgarē suciram ||
gr̥hidharma paripālya ratnākara śrāvakasyāpi kuṭumbam । labdhasudēvatvasumānuṣatvamacirācchivaṁ prāptam ॥ 65 ॥

varuṇakahā |
356
jō tayavvadhārī kuḍatalāīhiṁ kuṇai vavahāraṁ । iha parabhavē ya dukkhaṁ varuṇōvva sa pāva avassaṁ ||1||
tathāhi ;
mahumahadēva suvanasaṁgayaṁ taha ya pavaragayaṭhāṇaṁ । iha bharahammi pasiddhaṁ nagaraṁ nāmēṇa maṇikhēḍaṁ ||2||
harivikamābhihāṇō taṁ pālai naravarō gayaṁduvva । aṇavarayadāṇapasarō tabbhajjā caṁdalēhatti ||3||
tammi purē purajiṭṭō siṭṭī nāmēṇa dēvasēṇōti । bhajjā vijayabhihāṇā varuṇō nāmēṇa tāṇa suā || 4॥
sō ya kalākulabhavaṇaṁpi bhavaṇaō piivaṇē hōvavaṇē । paribhama mittakaliō viraialīlō aṇatthēsu ॥
aha jaṇadayāē rannā paṭṭiyaṁ haṭṭamajjhayārammi । siribhara cakavaṭṭissa nāḍayaṁ taṁ ca varuṇōvi ॥ 6 ॥
jā picchiuṁ payatō likhayaputtēṇa tā tarhi samaē । āyaṁsagihapavēsō bharahanadista saccaviō ||7॥
tattha alaṁkāravibhūsiṁyaṁ niyatanuṁ palōyamāṇō a । galiyammi aṁgulīē gayasōhaṁ aṁguliṁ darda ||8||
jaha mukālaṁkārō vigalipasōhaṁ niyaṁ tanuṁ darddha । saṁsārē vatthūṇaṁ mannatō kittimaṁ sōhaṁ ॥9॥
vēragamagapattō khaṇēṇa upapannakēvalannāṇō । dēvayaapiyaliṁgō namasiō jaha suriṁdēṇa ॥ 10 ॥
niggamamāṇō u jahā bhavaṇāō aṇugaō naravarāṇaṁ । paṁcahiṁ saēhiṁ saddhiṁ taha daṭhṭhē abhiṇajjaṁtaṁ ॥
sōuṁ ca savēraggē vaya saṁvēgaraṁgasālāē । pavisai vivēyavasaō tō pucchai suttahāraṁ sō ॥ 12 ॥
ēēhi mahāsattērhi aṇugaō bharahasāmiṇō maggō । nissattāṇaṁ amhārisāṇa kiṁ asthi kāvi gaī ? || 13||
atthitti bhaṇiya tēṇa sammattāī duvālasavihōvi । kahiō giridhammō ahigaō ya varuṇēṇa saha piuṇā ॥
yastr̥tīyatratadhārī kūṭatulādibhiḥ karōti vyavahāram । iha parabhavē ca duḥkhaṁ varuṇa iva sa prāpnōtyavaśyam ॥ 1 ॥
madhumathadēhamiva suvarṇasaṁgataṁ tathā ca pravaragaja [ gadā] sthānam । iha bharatē prasiddhaṁ nagaraṁ nāmnā maṇikhēṭam ॥2॥
hariravikramābhidhānastatpālayati naravarō gajēndra iva । anavaratadānaprasarastadbhāryā candralēkhēti ॥ 3 ॥
tasminpurē purajyēṣṭhaḥ śrēṣṭhī nāmnā dēvasēna iti । bhāryā vijayābhidhānā varuṇō nāmnā tayōḥ sutaḥ ॥ 4 ॥
sa ca kalākulabhavanamapi bhavanataḥ pitr̥vanē tathōpavanē । paribhramati mitrakalitō viracitalīlō'narthēṣu ||5||
atha janadayayā rājñā pravartitaṁ haṭṭamadhyē | śrībharatacakravartinō nāṭakaṁ taca varuṇō'pi ॥6॥
yāvad draṣṭuṁ pravr̥ttō liṅkhakaputrēṇa tāvattatra samayē । ādarśagr̥hapravēśō bharatanarēndrasya satyāpitaḥ ||7||
tatrālaṁkāravibhūṣitāṁ nijatanūṁ pralōkamānaśca । galitē'ṅgulīyē gataśōbhāmaṅguliṁ dr̥ṣṭā ॥ 8॥
yathā muktālaṅkārō vigalitaśōbhāṁ nijāṁ tanuṁ dr̥ṣṭā । saṁsārē vastūnāṁ manyamānaḥ kr̥trimāṁ śōbhām ॥9॥
vairāgyamārgaprāptaḥ kṣaṇēnēōtpannakēvalajñānaḥ । dēvatā'rpitaliṅgō namasthitō yathā surēndrēṇa ॥10॥
nirgacchaṁstu yathā bhavanādanugatō naravarāṇām । pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ sārdhaṁ tathā dr̥ṣṭrā'bhinīyamānam ॥11॥
śrutvā ca savairāgyāṇi vacanāni saṁvēgaraṅgaśālāyām । praviśati vivēkavaśatastataḥ pr̥cchati sūtradhāraṁ saḥ ॥ 12 ॥
ētairmahāsattvairanugatō bharatasvāminō mārgaḥ । niḥsattvānāmasmādr̥śāṁ kimasti kāpi gatiḥ 1 ॥ 13 ॥
1 ka ta ya vaṇē | 2 kha siyaṁgamappaṁ 1° ।

supāsanāha variśrasmi-
aha vuḍḍhatē piuṇō vavaharai sayaṁpabhō sa haṭṭammi । viśvai ya tattiyaṁ jattiēṇa nivvaha sakuḍuṁba ॥ 15 ॥
kiṁpuṇa iḍḍhīpattē annē daṭuṁ jaṇampi gauraviē । daviṇapivāsānaḍiō parivaḍiō suddhabhāvāō || 16 ॥
garuyāē lēi lahuyāē dēi tōlēvi tulāē dharimāi । kaṇanēhamappaēhivi taha kāuṁ vavaharai varuṇō || 17 ||
jaṇa vāriōvi hunō viramai kahai sōvi diṛaṁta । jaha baccha ! sāligāmē nivasai vaṇiō ghaṇō nāma।।
paīvi sō saccō vavaharaē taha ya appalābhēṇa । jāyā iyappasiddhī haṭṭē mōtūṇa tō annē ॥ 19 ॥
hara tassa haṭṭē lōō bhupi sō ya kaṭṭhēṇa । lahai jaṇāō tō bhaṇai majjha haṭṭaṁ na iha ēkaṁ ॥ 20 ॥
tā cayaha majjha puṭṭhi pajjattaṁ majjha ahiyalābhēṇa । paramannabhōyaṇapi hu aimattaṁ jaṇa uvvēyaṁ ||21||
ēvaṁ jaṁpatassavi viramai lōō na tassa haṭṭāō । bahuyayarō āgaccha mōtuṁ sāṇi haṭṭāṇi ||22||
taṁ sōuṁ saṁnihiyā vaṇiṇō jaṁpati jaha ahō lōyā ! । iya tajjiyāvi na muyaha kiṁ duttuṁḍasa taṁ havaṁ ? |
ēsōvi tāva vaṇijjaṁ karēi lāṁhatthamēva nahu iharā । na viṇā kayāṇagēṇa mullaṁ amhēvi ghicchāmō ||24||
tō paḍiṇiyaṁ kēhivi tōlatamatirahiṁ tubhēhiṁ । cōrēhiṁ jaṇō musiō sabbō vaṇivēdhārī hi ||25|
saccēṇa vavaharaṁtō ēsa duttuṁḍōvi valahō aha । uvajī vijjai kaṭuyapi ōsahaṁ samai jaṁ rōgaṁ ||26||
taṁ sōuṁ savisēsaṁ dhaṇammi tē maccharaṁ parivahaṁtā । chiḍḍuṁ savvattha gavēsayaṁti na lahaṁti thēvapi ||27||
aha tammajjhē kēṇavi diṭṭhē ahiṇavamayaṁ lahuṁ ḍiṁbhaṁ । tō tēsiṁ annēhiṁ saha maṁtivi kāvi āhīrī ॥ 28 ॥
astīti bhaṇitvā tēna samyaktvādirdvādaśavidhō'pi । kathitō gr̥hidharmō'dhigataśca varuṇēna saha pitrā || 14 ||
atha vr̥ddhatvē piturvyavaharati svayaṁprabhaḥ sa haṭṭē | arjayati ca tāvad yāvatā nirvahati sakuṭumbaḥ ॥ 15 ॥
kintu r̥ddhiprāptānanyān dr̥ṣṭrā janē gauravitān । draviṇapipāsānaṭitaḥ paripatitaḥ śuddhabhāvāt ॥ 16 ॥
gurdhyā lāti layā dadāti tōlayitvā tulayā gharimādi । kaṇasnēhamā pakairapi tathā kr̥tvā vyavaharati varuṇaḥ ।
janakēna vāritō'pi khalu nō viramati kathayati sō'pi dr̥ṣṭāntam । yathā vatsa ! śāligrāmē nivasati vaṇigdhanō nāma |
prakr̥tyā'pi sa satyō vyavaharatē tathā cālpalābhēna । jātēti prasiddhirhadvān muktvā tatō'nyān ॥19॥
vyavaharati tasya haṭṭē lōkō bhōktumapi sa ca kaṣṭēna । labhatē janāt, tatō bhaṇati mama haṭṭaṁ nēhaikam ॥20॥
tasmāttyajata mama pr̥ṣṭhaṁ paryāptaṁ mamācikalāmēna । paramānnabhōjanamapi khalvatimātraṁ janayatyudvēgam ॥ 21 ॥
ēvaṁ jalpatō'pi viramati lōkō na tasya haṭṭāt । bahutara āgacchati muktvā śēṣān dr̥ṭṭān ॥ 22 ॥
tatśrutvā saṁnihitā vaṇijō jalpanti yathā'hō lōkāḥ ! । iti tarjitā api na muñcata kiṁ dvituṇḍasya taṁ haṭṭam ॥
ēṣō'pi tāvadvāṇijyaṁ karōti lābhārthamēva na khalvitarathā । na vinā r̥yāṇakēna mūlyaṁ vayamapi jighr̥kṣāmaḥ || 24|
tataḥ pratibhaṇita kairapi tōlayantamabruvadbhiryuṣmābhiḥ । caiaurairjanō muṣitaḥ sarvō vaṇigvēṣadhāribhiḥ ||25||
satyēna vyavaharannēṣa dvituṇḍō'pi vallabhō'smākam । upajīvyatē kaṭukamapyauṣadhaṁ śamayati yad rōgam ॥ 26 ॥
tat śrutvā saviśēṣaṁ dhanē tē matsaraṁ parivahantaḥ । chidraṁ sarvatra gavēṣayanti na labhantē stōkamapi ॥27॥

lōbhaviuṁ ārōviya kaḍīē taṁ cīravēdiyaṁ ḍibhaṁ । paṭṭaviyā dhaṇahaṭṭē maggai suttaṇa sā tillaṁ ||29||
annēhiṁ hārēhiṁ vāvaḍaṁ vaṇiyaputtasahiyaṁ taṁ । sā bhaṇai kirāḍa ! na uttaraṁpi taṁ dēkhi amhāṇaṁ ॥ 30॥
tō kuviēṇaṁ tēṇa thōvaṁ sā pilliyā mayagaḍiṁbhaṁ । pāḍēuṁ dharaṇīē muṭṭhā muṭṭhatti pōkaraṛa ||31||
tō dhāviyā tārā dhaṇamāhīriṁ mayaṁ ca taṁ ḍiṁbhaṁ । vittūṇa gāmapahuṇō appaṁti kahati vr̥taṁta ||32||
mittassava pucassava jaṇayassava tassa āvaī nāuṁ । savvōvi gāmalōō bhōiyagēhammi saṁpattī ||33||
savrvvapi imamalīyaṁ ahaṁ samatthēmi iya vicitē । yuṁ paṭṭailēṇaṁ bhaṇiyāhīrī jahā raṁḍē ! ||34||
mayagaṁ vālē ghittuṁ kaḍīē bhaṇiēṇa āgayā jassa । taṁ kahasu annahā tuha chiṁdissa kannanāsāō ||35||
tō khuddhā sā jaṁpa saṁtariyā ahaṁ aṇāhā ya । vacchavva, vaṇiyasaṁpēsiyā ēvaṁ maē vihiyē || 36॥
tō mēlā majjhē samāgaē daṁsaē ya tē vaṇiē । gāmapahūvi samatthai tavvayaṇaṁ iya vicitatō ||37||
jaha saccō nillōbhōti sammaō bahujaṇassa siṭṭitraṇō । māyāviṇō ya sēsā ii vihiyē tēhi maccharaō ।।
tā ēēsi nivaḍa kūḍa bahuuttarē karaṁtāṇaṁ । āhīrīē gahiyē daviṇaṁ āṇāviḍaṁ sōvi ||39||
kāuṁ nirutarē tē savvassaṁ tērsi lūḍiuṁ lēi । taha appara guttīē dhaṁṇa tu sammāṇiraṁ muai ||40 ॥
savvōvi gāmalōō dhaṇassa baddhāvaō gharē jāi । bhaṇai ya visaṭṭaharisō 'sacca jaya'tti saccamiṇaṁ । । 41 ।।
dhaṇamaṇiṇaṁ gāmēṇa mōiyā tēvi aṁgamittaṇa । tā vaccha ! cayasu kūḍaṁ vavahāraṁ kuṇasu maha vayaṇaṁ ॥ 42 ॥
atha tanmadhyē kēnāpi dr̥ṣṭō'bhinavamr̥tō laghurḍimbhaḥ । tatastēṣāmanyaiḥ saha mantrayitvā kāpyābhīrī ॥ 28 ॥
lōbhayitvā''rōpya kaṭyāṁ taṁ cīravēṣṭitaṁ ḍimbham । prasthāpitā dhanahaṭṭhē mr̥gayatē sūtrēṇa sā tailam ॥ 29 ॥
anyairhr̥ṭṭabhārairvyaṣṭataṁ vaṇikputrasahitaṁ tam । sā bhaṇati kirāta ! nōttaramapi tvaṁ dadāsyasmākam ? ॥30॥
tataḥ kupitēna tēna stōkaṁ sā prēritā mr̥takaḍimbham । pātayitvā dharaṇyāṁ muṣṭā muṣṭēti pr̥tkarōti ||31||
tatō dhāvitāḥ purārakṣakā dhanamābhīrīṁ mr̥taṁ ca taṁ ḍimbham । gr̥hītvā grāmaprabhōrarpayanti kathayanti vr̥ttāntam ॥
mittrasyēva putrasyēva janakasyēva tasyāpada jñātvā । sarvō'pi grāmalōkō grāmaprabhugēhē saṁprāptaḥ ॥ 33॥
sarvamapīdamalīkamahaṁ samarthaya iti vicintya । duṣṭhu padrēśēna bhaṇitā''mīrī yathā raṇḍē ! ||34||
mr̥takaṁ bālaṁ gr̥hītvā kaṭyō bhaṇitēnā''gatā yasya । taṁ kathayānyathā tava chētsyāmi karṇanāsāḥ ॥35॥
tataḥ kṣubdhā sā jalpati dēśāntaritā'hamanāthā ca । vatsēva, vaṇiksaṁprēṣitayaivaṁ mayā vihitam ॥ 36 ॥
tatō mēlakamadhyē samāgatān darśayati ca tān vaṇijaḥ । grāmaprabhurapi samarthayati tadvacanamiti vicintayan ॥
yathā satyō nirlōbha iti sammatō bahujanasya śrēṣṭhivanaḥ । māyāvinaśca śēṣā iti vihitaṁ tairmatsarataḥ ॥38॥
tasmādētēṣu nipatatu kūṭaṁ bahūttarāṇi kurvatsu । ābhīryā gr̥hītaṁ draviṇamānāyya sō'pi ॥39॥
,
kr̥tvā niruttarāṁstān sarvasvaṁ tēṣāṁ luṇṭitvā lāti । tathā'rpayati guptau dhanaṁ tu sammānya muñcati ||40|
sarvō'pi grāmalōkō 'vanasya vardhakō gr̥hē yāti । bhaṇati ca vikasitaharṣaḥ 'satyaṁ jayati' iti satyamidam ॥

supāsanāha-caritryammi-
iya vāriōvi varuṇō tahēva vavaharai sēṭṭiṇā tattō । sayaṇasamakkhaṁ bhāgaṁ dāūṇaṁ sō puḍhō vihiō ||43|
aha kēṇai kharaḍēṇaṁ kiṇiuṁ haṭṭammi varuṇavaṇiyassa । guḍajīragāi mittēṇa tassa puṇa annaṭṭammi ||44|
taṁ ciya kiṇiyaṁ di iyarēṇaṁ, taṁ samēvi mōlammi । paḍihāsiyamahiyaṁ sē tō sō ēgammi haṭṭamma ।। 45 ।
niyakīyaṁ tōlāviya mavāvaē jāva taṁ tibhāgr̥ṇaṁ । saṁjāyaṁ tō kahiyaṁ gaṁtūṇaṁ tēṇamañcassa || 46 ॥
tēṇa ya saha varuṇēṇaṁ āṇēviya tassa haṭṭamappāṇi । saṁkhāviyāṇi ūṇāhiāṇi savvāṇi jāyāī ॥। 47 |
bahudhēhi sudiḍhaṁ maṁtī baṁdhāvara taō varuṇaṁ । tō dēvasēṇasēhī jāi amañcassa pāsamma ||48 ||
- vinnavai amacaṁ jāva tātra tēṇāvi sō uvāladdhō । tujjhavi puttō hōuṁ ēvaṁ vavaharai ēsa kahaṁ ? ॥49॥
bhai amacaṁ siṭṭī jāyamimaṁ tāva saṁpayamimasta । kiṁ kāyavvaṁ tubbhēhi, bhaṇai ēvaṁ taō maṁtī ॥ 50 ॥
hatthacchēō nayaṇāṇa kaḍhaṇaṁ savvadaviṇa avaharaṇaṁ । juttaṁ iha avarāhē jāṇēsi tumaṁpi iya tāva ॥51॥
tahavi hu gharasārakhaṁ dēhō ya imassa tumaṁ maē mukkī । taṁ paḍivajjai sēṭṭhī kuṇai amaccō tahēva taō || 52 ॥
baṁdhēhi mōḍiyaṁgō sō pattō maṁdirammi niyayammi । upapannativvaviyaṇō mukkī pāṇēhiṁ taiyadi ॥ 53॥
ajjhāō tattō sō sūyarō samunnō । bhamiūṇa bhavamaṇataṁ aṇatamavi pāvahī ṭhāṇaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
siṭṭhī sāvayadhammaṁ sammaṁ paripāliūṇa pajjaṁtē । aṇasaṇavihiṇā mariḍaṁ sōhammē suravarō jāō ॥55॥
॥ iti tr̥tīyāṇuvratē caturthāticāravipākē varuṇakathā samāptā ॥
dhanabhaṇitēna grāmēṇa mōcitāstē'pyaṅgamātrēṇa । tasmād vatsa ! tyaja kūṭaṁ vyavahāraṁ kuru mama vacanam ॥ 42 ॥
iti vāritō'pi varuṇastathaiva vyavaharati śrēṣṭhinā tataḥ । svajanasamakṣaṁ bhāgaṁ dattvā sa pr̥thag vihitaḥ || 43 ||
atha kēnacit kharēṇa krītvā haṭṭē varuṇavaṇijaḥ । guḍajīrakādi mittrēṇa tasya punaranyahaṭṭē ||44 ||
tadēva krītaṁ dr̥ṣṭamitarēṇa, tat samē'pi mūlyē । pratibhāsitamadhikaṁ tasya tataḥ sa ēkasmin haṭṭē ॥ 45 ॥
nijīyaṁ tōlayitvā māpayati yāvattat tribhāgōnam । saṁjāta tajñaḥ kathitaṁ gatvā tēnāmātyasya ॥ 46 ॥
tēna ca saha varuṇēnānāyya tasya haṭṭamānāni । saṁkhyāpitānyūnādhikāni sarvāṇi jātāni ॥ 47 ॥
bahubandhaiḥ sudr̥ḍhaṁ mantrī bandhayati tatō varuṇam । tatō dēvasēnaśrēṣṭhī yātyamātyasya pārśvē ॥ 48 ॥
vijñapayatyamātyaṁ yāvattāvat tēnāpi sa upālabdhaḥ । tavāpi putrō bhūtvaivaṁ vyavaharatyēṣa katham ? ॥ 49 ॥
bhaṇatyamātyaṁ śrēṣṭhī jātamidaṁ tāvat sāṁpratamasya । kiṁ kartavyaṁ yuṣmābhiḥ, bhaṇatyēvaṁ tatō mantrī ||50॥
hastacchēdō nayanayōḥ karṣaṇaṁ sarvadraviṇāpaharaṇam । yuktamihāparādhē jānāsi tvamapīdaṁ tāvat ॥ 51 ॥
tathāpi hi gr̥hasārārdhaṁ dēhaścāsya tava mayā muktaḥ । tat pratipadyatē śrēṣṭhī karōtyamartyastathaiva tataḥ ॥ 52॥
bandhairmōṭitāṅgaḥ sa prāptō mandirē nijē । unnatīvra vēdanō muktaḥ prāṇaistr̥tīya dinē ॥ 53 ॥
ārtadhyānōpagatastataḥ sa śūkaraḥ samutpannaḥ । bhrāntvā bhavamanantamanantamapi prāpsyasi sthānam ॥54॥
śrēṣṭhī śrāvakradharmaṁ samyak paripālya paryantē । anaśana vidhinā mr̥tvā saudharmē suravarō jātaḥ ॥ 55 ॥

tappaḍirūvaṁ davtraṁ khiviḍaṁ jō bhavvadavvamajjhami । vikkiṇai kiṇai dukkhaṁ sāgaracaṁdōvva sō ihaī || 1॥
tathāhi ;
1
visabhāsiya sanaṁdi naṁdiuraṁ nāma puravaraṁ asthi । kēlāsasēlasiharaṁva sahai ra bhūidhavalaharaṁ || 2 ||
samara gaīdō rāyā caṁdō iva suyaṇakumuyasaṁḍassa । taṁ pālai, tarasa piyā suviṇīyā kumuiṇī nāma || 3 ||
tatthathi thirapaī siṭṭhī sumaī, piyā ya sē sulasā । tāṇaṁ ca suyā dōnni ya sāgaracaṁdō ya guṇacaṁdō ॥
dōna kalāsu kusalā dōnivi annōnnanēhapaviddhā । viyaraṁti saicchāē vavahāravihārakajjēsu ||5||
kajjavasēṇaṁ gāmaṁtarammi samagaṁpi dōhivi payaṭṭā । kōsadurgaṁ ca gaēhiṁ tā diṭṭhō muṇiva ēgō || 6 |
tō bhaṇiyaṁ jiṇaṁ mā gammau vaccha ! ēsa avasauṇō । lāhassa vigghakārī jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ sauṇasatsu ॥7॥
malamailavatthadēhō muṁḍiyasiratuṁḍaō asuivayaṇō | mukkavibhūsō maggē diṭṭhō kajjaṁ na sāhēī ॥8॥
guṇacaṁ dēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ mā baṁdhava ! bhaṇasu ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ । jai ēsōvi na sauṇō tō sauṇō natthi bhuvaṇēvi ॥ 9 ॥
jō diṭṭhōvi hu pāvaṁ paṇāsaē vaṁdiō ya paṇayāṇa । kallāṇāī paṇāmai avasauṇō kaha ṇu sō hōi 1 ॥ 10 ॥
tō sāgarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ saṁsagī sāvaēhi saha tujjha । tēṇēha pakkhavāō pāvaphalaṁ aṇuhavaṁtami || 11 ||
tō iyarēṇa bhaṇiaṁ jaṁ tuha ēyaṁmmi muṇivarē cittaṁ । tēṇa gayassa ṭhiyassavi baṁdhava ! naṇu dullahaṁ kusalaṁ ॥
javi imē bhayavaṁtō maṁgalabhūyā sahāvaō huṁti । tahavi hu niṁdijjaṁtā diti amaṁgalaphalaṁ viḍalaṁ ||13||
iha lōē tā ēvaṁ paralōē duggaī abōhiṁ ca । dukkhāī aṇatāī tā dudvaṁ citithaṁ tumaē || 14 ||
tatpratirūpaṁ dravyaṁ kṣiptvā yō bhavyadravyamadhyē | vikrīṇāti krīṇāti duḥkhaṁ sāgaracandra iva sa iha ॥1॥
vr̥ṣabhāsitaṁ sanandi nandipuraṁ nāma puravaramasti । kailāsaśailaśikharamiva rājatē varabhūtidhavalagr̥ha (hara) m ॥2॥
samaragajēndrō rājā candra iva sujanakumudaṣaṇḍasya । tatpālayati, tasya priyā suvinītā kumudinī nāma || 3 ||
tatrāsti sthiraprakr̥tiḥ śrēṣṭhī sumatiḥ, priyā ca tasya sulasā । tayōśca sutau dvau ca sāgaracandraśca guṇacandraḥ ॥4॥
dvāvapi kalāsu kuśalau dvāvapyanyōnyasnēha pratibaddhau । vicarataḥ svēcchayā vyavahāravihārakāryēṣu ||5||
kāryavaśēna grāmāntarē samakamapi dvāvapi pravr̥ttau । krōśadvikaṁ ca gatābhyāṁ tāvad dr̥ṣṭō munivara ēkaḥ ॥ 6 ॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ jyēṣṭhēna mā gamyatāṁ vatsa ! ēṣō'paśakunaḥ । lābhasya vighnakārī yad bhaṇitaṁ śakunaśāstrēṣu ॥7॥
malamalinavastradēhō muṇḍitaśirastuṇḍa kō'śucivadanaḥ । muktavibhūṣō mārgē dr̥ṣṭaḥ kāryaṁ na sādhayati ॥8॥
guṇacandrēṇa bhaṇitaṁ mā bāndhava ! bhaṇēdr̥śaṁ vacanam । yadyēṣō'pi na śakunastataḥ śakunō nāsti bhuvanē'pi ||9||
yō dr̥ṣṭō'pi khalu pāpaṁ praṇāśayati vanditaśca praṇatānām । kalyāṇāni praṇamayatyapaśakunaḥ kathaṁ nu sa bhavaṁti ? ॥
tataḥ sāgarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ saṁsargaḥ śrāvakaiḥ saha tava । tēnēha pakṣapātaḥ pāpaphalamanubhavati ॥11॥
1
tata itarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ yattvaitasmin munivarē cittam । tēna gatasya sthitasyāpi bāndhava ! nanu durlabhaṁ kuśalam ॥
yadyapī mē bhagavantō maṅgalabhūtāḥ svabhāvatō bhavanti । tathāpi hi nindyamānā dadatya maṅgalaphalaṁ vipulam ||13||
iha lōkē tāvadēvaṁ paralōkē durgatimabōdhiṁ ca । duḥkhānyanantāni tasmād duṣṭaṁ cintitaṁ yuṣmābhiḥ ॥ 14 ॥

damma bahumāṇaṁ maha puṇa kallāṇakulaharē ittha । hōhī gayassa nūṇaṁ kallāṇaparaṁparā garuī || 15 ||
tā ajjavi taṁ baṁdhana ! phuraṁtatavajāyatēyaduddharisaṁ । ēyaṁ khamāviūṇaṁ turiyaṁ kuṇa appaṇō saṁti ॥ 16 ॥
tattō jaṁpara jiṭṭō ēēṇa khamāviēṇa jā saṁtī । tīē maha natthi kajjaṁ jaṁ jāsi tumaṁ tu tattha ahaṁ ।। 17
diē jjhatēvi hu karēmi kiṁ jaṁ tumaṁ aiviyadaṁ । appāṇaṁ mannatō maṁ gaṇasi na gōṇatulaṁpi ।। 18 ।
iya bhaṇiya valai jiṭṭō iyarō uṇa jāi paṇamiūṇa muṇi । vahiūṇa diṇaṁ suttō rayaṇīē purassa ēkassa
bāhiṁ haridēva lē jā cihna addharattasamayammi । tō nisuṇai iya sadaṁ sāmiya ! guṇacaṁda ! uṭṭhēhi ॥ 20
āruhaha rahē sig pattā sā sāmiṇī rahārūḍhā । tō sō ciṁtai ēyaṁ tammuṇidaṁsaṇaphalaṁ kiṁpi ॥ 21 ॥
annaha kahamaṇukūlō iya saddō savaṇagōyaraṁ ēi ? । tō sahakāriṇīē karammi laggō gaō tattha || 22 ॥
gahiūṇa karēṇa karaṁ rahammi ārōviō - rahaṭiyāē । bhariyaṁ phalōhalīē kaccōlayamapiyaṁ hatthē ||23||
kaṇayakaragēṇa nīraṁ pāiya taṁbōlamappiyaṁ taha ya | ghaṇasāramīsiēṇa littō caṁdaṇarasēṇa sayaṁ ||24||
vēgēṇa rahō jaṁtō jā pattō ajōyaṇaṁ bhūmiṁ । tō aruṇōdayasamaē diṭṭhō kumarīē guṇacaṁdō ॥ 25 ॥
kayasaṁkēyā narāu suṁdarō paḍhamajōvvaṇatthō ya । tō bhaṇiō sō tīē pariṇēsu mamaṁ ihajjēva ||26||
vihiṇā tumaṁ viinnō maha bhattā annahā kahaṁ ēvaṁ । anēṇa samaṁ ghaḍiē saṁghaḍiō subhagarayaṇa ! tumaṁ ? ||27|
tā hu jō vasō vā tumaṁ gaī majjha kōḍimullāī । āharaṇāī imāī vāvārasu niyayaicchāē ||28||
dr̥ṣṭē subahumānō mama punaḥ kalyāṇa kulagr̥hē'tra । bhaviṣyati gatasya nūnaṁ kalyāṇaparamparā gurvīṁ ॥15॥
tasmādadyāpi tvaṁbāndhava ! sphurattapōjātatējōdurdharṣam । ēnaṁ kṣamayitvā tvaritaṁ kurvātmanaḥ śāntim ||16||
tatō jalpati jyēṣṭha ētēna kṣamitēna yā śāntiḥ । tayā mama nāsti kāryaṁ yad yāsi tvaṁ tu tatrāham ॥ 17॥
hr̥dayē dahyamānē'pi hi karōmi kiṁ yattvamatividagdham । ātmānaṁ manyamānō māṁ gaṇayasi na gōtulyamapi ॥ 18
iti bhaṇitvā valatē jyēṣṭha itaraḥ punaryātiṁ praṇamya munim । ūḍhā dinaṁ suptō rajanyāṁ purasyaikasya ॥19॥
bahirharidēvakulē yāvattiṣṭhatyardharātrasamayē । tataḥ śr̥ṇōtīti śabdaṁ svāmin ! guṇacandra ! uttiṣṭha ||20||
ārōha rathē śīghraṁ prāptā sā svāminī rathārūḍhā । tataḥ sa cintayatyētattanmunidarśanaphalaṁ kimapi ॥21॥
anyathā kathamanukūla iti śabdaḥ śravaṇagōcaramēti ? । tataḥ śabdakāriṇyāḥ karē lagnō gatastatra ॥22॥
gr̥hītvā karēṇa karaṁ rathē ārōpitō rathasthitayā । mr̥taṁ phalaughēna pātramarpitaṁ hastē ||23||
kanakakarakēṇa nīraṁ pāyayitvā tāmbūlamarpitaṁ tathā ca । ghanasāramiśritēna liptaścandanarasēna svayam ॥24॥
vēgēna rathō yān yāvatprāptō'ṣṭayōjanāṁ bhūmim । tatō'ruṇōdayasamayē dr̥ṣṭaḥ kumāryā guṇacandraḥ || 25 ||
kr̥tasaṁkētād narāt sundaraḥ prathamayauvanasthaśca । tatō bhaṇitaḥ sa tayā pariṇaya māmihādyaiva ॥ 26 ॥
vidhinā tvaṁ vitarṇō mama bharttā'nyathā kathamēvam । anyēna samaṁ ghaṭitē saṁghaṭitaḥ subhagaratna! tvam? ||27||
tasmād bhavatu yō vāsa vāṁ tvaṁ gatirmama kōṭimūlyāni । ābharaṇānīmāni vyāpāraya nijēcchayā ॥28॥
1. ga. saṁpattā sāmi ।

sāgaracaṁda kahā ।
I
365
naṁdiurarāyataṇayā vasaṁtasēṇā ahaṁ niyayapiuṇā । dinnā sīmālanarāhivassa vuḍḍhassa iya nisu || 29 ॥
tō dukkhapīḍiyāē ghaḍiō guṇacaṁdanāmadhēēṇa । saha pavarakhattiēṇaṁ dēvaulē ittha saṁkēō ||30||
dāsīsaddēṇa tumaṁ āgaṁtuṁ maha rahē samārūḍhō । tāyabhaēṇaṁ sō puṇa mannē nō āgaō ittha ||31||
tō bhaṇiyā sā tēṇaṁ jai ēvaṁ tā api naṁdiurē । vatthavvō vāṇiyagō tō ghaḍiya duggharḍa vihiṇā ||32||
iya vieir majjha piyā sakuḍuṁba garuyamāvaī sahihī । tō bhai rāyataṇayā mā hu bhayaṁ kuṇasu jēṇa ahaṁ ॥
aivallahā piūṇa majjha suhēṇaṁ suhaṁ khu tēsipi । tēṇavi sauṇavalēṇaṁ pariṇīyā jhatti sā kumarī ॥ 34 ॥
tō paḍihārō paṭṭīē āgaō sāhaṇēṇa pariyariō । jā pēcchai taṁ bālaṁ pariṇiyacitraṁ sabhattāraṁ ॥ 35 ॥
namiūṇaṁ tō tēṇaṁ sadhavā viniyattiyā nivaṁgaruhā । pattā piupayamūlē paṇamai taṁ niyapaisamēyā ॥ 36 ॥
feat farmarsō dēsō kōsō ya taha hayagayāī । vīryādiṇē jaṇayagihē sakalattō jāi guṇacaṁdō ॥ 37॥
pavisatō aggajaṇō paripuṭṭō siṭṭiṇā kahai tassaṁ । jaha ēsō tuha gēhē nivassa jāmāuō ēi || 38 ॥
tō siṭṭī paricita kiṁ iha āgamaṇakāraṇamimassa | ahavā ki ēēṇaṁ, pasāiyanvō imō tāva ॥ 39 ॥
tō jāi abhimūhō jā tō sō kariṇīē avayarēūṇa । pāēsa paḍai piuṇō samaṁ piyāē, taō siṭṭhī ।।
pucchara vaccha ! kahaṁ taṁ riddhiṁ pattō si sōvi sē kahiuṁ । muṇidaṁsaṇāi savvaṁ taṁ pucchara majjha gurubaṁdhū ॥
kiṁ nō dī sai gēhē, piuṇāvi nivēiyaṁ jahā baccha ! । taiyā taē samaṁ ciya iō gaō ēttiyaṁ nāyaṁ ॥ 42 ॥
cāuddisiṁpi tēṇa caḍāviya sāhaṇaṁ taō sōvi । pattō sāhaṇiēṇaṁ āṇīō tassa pāsammi ||43||
nandipurarājatanayā vasantasēnā'haṁ nijapitrā । dattā sīmasthanarādhipāya vr̥ddhāyēti śrutam ||29||
tatō duḥkhapīḍitayā ghaṭitō guṇacandranāmadhēyēna । saha pravarakṣattriyēṇa dēvakulē'tra saṁkētaḥ ॥ 30 ॥
dāsīśabdēna tvamāgatya mama rathē samārūḍhaḥ । tātabhayēna sa punarmanyē nō āgatō'tra ॥ 31 ॥
tatō bhaṇitā sā tēna yadyēvaṁ tadā'hamapi nandipurē । vāstavyō vaṇik, tatō ghaṭitaṁ durghaṭaṁ vidhinā ॥ 32 ॥
iti vihitē mama pitā sakuṭumbō gurumāpadaṁ lapsyatē । tatō bhaṇati rājatanayā mā khalu bhayaṁ kuru yēnāham ॥
ativallabhā pitrōrmama sukhēna sukhaṁ khalu tayōrapi । tēnāpi śakunabalēna pariṇītā jhaṭiti sā kumārī ॥ 34 ॥
tataḥ pratīhāraḥ pr̥ṣṭha āgataḥ sādhanēna parikaritaḥ । yāvatpaśyati tāṁ bālāṁ pariṇītacihnāṁ sabhartr̥kām ||35|
natvā tatastēna sadhavā vinivartitā nr̥pāṅgaruhā । prāptā pitr̥padamūlē praṇamati taṁ nijapatisamētā ॥ 36॥
dattō vipulāvāsō dēśaḥ kōśaśva tathā hayagajādiḥ । dvitīyadinē janakagr̥hē sakalatrō yāti guṇacandraḥ ||37||
praviśannagrajanaḥ paripr̥ṣṭaḥ śrēṣṭhinā kathayati tasya । yathaiṣa tava gēhē nr̥pasya jāmātaiti ॥ 38 ॥
,
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī paricintayati kimihāgamanakāraṇamasya । athavā kimētēna prasādayitavyō'yaṁ tāvat ॥ 39॥
tatō yātyabhimukhō yāvat tataḥ sa kariṇyā avatīrya । pādayōḥ patati pituḥ samaṁ priyayā, tataḥ śrēṣṭhī ॥ 40 ॥
pr̥cchati vatsa ! kathaṁ tvamr̥ddhiṁ prāptō'si sō'pi tasya kathayitvā । munidarśanādi sarvaṁ taṁ pr̥cchati mama gurubandhuḥ ॥
kiṁ nō dr̥śyatē gēhē, pitrāpi nivēditaṁ yathā vatsa ! । tadā tvayā samamēvētō gata ētāvajjñātam ॥ 42 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi---
tēvi puṭṭhō bhāyā muṇipāsāō niyattamāṇēhiṁ । tumhēhi kimaṇubhūyaṁ, sāgaracaṁdō taō kahara ||44||
avasaṇāō valiō purahuttaṁ jāva tāva cōrēhiṁ । āhaṇiūṇaṁ lauḍēhiṁ pāḍiō dharaṇivaṭummi ||45 ॥
tthāī ghittr̥ṇaṁ vivi vayaṇammi ḍējjayaṁ ahayaṁ । baddhō rukkhassa thuḍē gaēsu cōrēsu pahiē || 46 ||
tatthāgaraṇa diṭṭhō karuṇāē chōḍiūṇa maha dinō । sālikaraṁbō niyasaṁvalāō taha pāiō salilaṁ ||47|
tō ciṁtiya maē iya sacca guṇacaṁdabhāsiyē jāyaṁ । sauṇōvi asauṇōcciya muṇī mahappā maē gaṇiō ।
phaliō maha maṇabhāvō tā ajjavi taṁ muṇīsaraṁ gaṁtuṁ । khāmēmi tattha punnōdaēṇa jai kahavi pāvē ||49 |
iya citiūṇa caliō diṭṭhō ya muṇī taō paṇamiṇaṁ । niyadōsaṁ payaḍēūṇa khāmiō bhaṇiyamaha muṇiṇā
dhammāhammāṇa phalaṁ sayayaṁ payaḍamiha vēyamāṇōvi । bhāvibhadō viyāṇai iyarō ya na yāṇaē kahavi || 21|
ēgō saṁsārē saraṇaṁ jīvāṇa niyamaō dhammō । annaṁ puṇa savvaṁpi hu dukkhāṇa nibaṁdhaṇaṁ caiva ॥ 52 ॥
annādhī jīvō kasāyavasagō ya visayagiddhō ya । diṭṭhē kahiyapi phuḍaṁ paḍivajjai nēya saddhammaṁ ॥ 53॥
vivēga puṇadhammaṁ kāraṇa viśuddhamaggasaṁpannō । taṁ natthi jaṁ na pāvai kallāṇaparaṁparaṁ paramaṁ ||14||
iya guṇinā bittharaō jaigihibhēēṇa sāhiē dhammē । gihidhammō paḍivanō jaidhammassāsamatyēṇa || 55
puvyāvarāhamalakhālaṇikkapacchittajalapavāhēṇa । nīō appā suddhiṁ ṭhiēṇa muṇipāyamūlammi ॥ 56 ॥
tō tattha ahaṁ diṭṭhō tuha sāhaṇiēṇa, bhaṇai tō iyarō | aṇurbhujasu rajjasiriṁ muṇidaṁsaṇaō maē pattaṁ ।
caturdikṣvapi tēna prēṣitaṁ sādhanaṁ tataḥ sō'pi । prāptaḥ sādhanikēnānītastasya pārśvē ॥ 43 ॥
tēnāpi pr̥ṣṭō bhrātā munipārśvād nivartamānaiḥ । yuṣmābhiḥ kimanubhūtaṁ, sāgaracandrastataḥ kathayati ॥ 44 ॥
apaśakunād valitaḥ purābhimukhaṁ yāvattāvaccauraiḥ । āhatya laguḍaḥ pātitō dharaṇipr̥ṣṭhē ||45॥
vastrādīn gr̥hītvā kṣiptvā vadanē vastramaham । baddhō vr̥kṣasya mūlē gatēṣu caurēṣu pathikēna ॥46॥ .
tatrāgatēna dr̥ṣṭaḥ karuṇayā chōṭayitvā mē dattaḥ । śālikarambō nijaśambalāttathā pāyitaḥ salilam ||47 ॥
tataścintitaṁ mayēti satyaṁ guṇacandrabhāṣitaṁ jātam । śakunō'pyaśakuna ēva munirmahātmā mayā gaṇitaḥ || 48 |
phalitō mama manōbhāvastasmādadyāpi taṁ munīśvaraṁ gatvā । kṣamayāmi tatra puṇyōdayēna yadi kathamapi prāpnuyām |
iti cintayitvā calitō dr̥ṣṭaśca munistataḥ praṇamya । nijadōṣaṁ prakaṭayya kṣamitō bhaṇitamatha muninā ||10||
dharmādharmayōḥ phalaṁ satataṁ prakaṭamiha vēdayannapi । bhāvibhadrō vijānātītaraśca na jānāti kathamapi ॥51॥
ēka ēva saṁsārē śaraṇaṁ jīvānāṁ niyamatō dharmaḥ । anyat punaḥ sarvamapi khalu duḥkhānāṁ nibandhanamēva ॥ 52 ॥
ajñānāndhō jīvaḥ kaṣāyavaśagaśca viṣayagr̥ddhaśca । dr̥ṣṭaṁ kathitamapi sphuṭaṁ pratipadyatē naiva saddharmam ॥53॥
savivēkaḥ punadharma kr̥tvā viśuddhamārgasaṁpannaḥ । tad nāsti yanna prāpnōti kalyāṇaparamparāṁ paramām ॥54॥
iti muninā vistaratō yatigr̥hibhēdēna kathitē dharmai । gr̥hidharmaḥ pratipannō yatidharmasyā sāmarthyēna ॥55॥
pūrvāparādhama lakṣālanē kaprāyaścittajalapravāhēṇa । nīta ātmā śuddhiṁ sthitēna munipādamūlē ॥ 56 ॥
1 kha vuja । 2 kha. ga. adayaṁ ।

sāgaracaṁdakahā ।

tō sāga pāi muṇipāyapasāyaō maē pattō । jiṇadhammō, kiṁ imiṇā rajjēṇaṁ pāvakajjēṇaṁ 1 || 58 ||
tō jaṇayaṁ guṇacaṁdō niyayāvāsammi nēi sagihē u । sāmaracaṁdō cihna kahai naridassa guṇacaṁdō ॥ 59 ॥
muṇidaṁsaṇavattataṁ pucchara taha jāmi vēdiuṁ tamahaṁ । bhai nariṁdō ēmō amhēvi, taō naravariṁdō ॥ 60॥
guṇacaṁdō sakalattō sāgaracaṁdōvi sumaijaṇayajuō | vaṁdēti muṇi gaṁtuṁ suṇati dhammaṁ, taō rāyā ॥ 61 ॥
sampattaṁ paḍivajjai guṇacaṁdō'ṇubvayāī anē u । sammattamittamavarē jahasattīē, nivaipamuhā ||62 ||
vaṁdēṇaṁ sāhu pattā niyaniyagihēsu, guṇacaṁdō । chaṇacaṁdō iva gayaṇaṁ pabhāvaē patrayaṇaṁ payaō || 63 ||
sāgaracaṁda ha hara vaḍhavaē ya tammittaṁ । jittiyamittēṇa kuṭuṁbauyaraparipūraṇaṁ hōī || 64 ||
guṇacaṁdēṇa savihavē aṇisaṁ ditēvi vivibhaṁgīhiṁ । micchābhimāṇanaḍiō aṇuṇijjaṁtōvi nō lēi || 65 ॥
kiṁca guṇacaṁda riddhiṁ ḍajjhai daṭṭṇa sōvi īsāē । daviṇapivāsāē tahā pīḍijjai aidaṁ tattō ॥ 66॥
āsōiyāimīsaṁ cōlaṁ ghusiṇaṁ kusuṁbhasaṁmīsaṁ । katthūriṁ karaṇīē taha kappūrāidavvāī ||67||
vittr̥ṇa micchabhūmīē jāi aha tēṇa kōvi kampayarō | avamāṇiō sarūvaṁ taṁ payaḍai micchanāhassa |
sō tabbhaṁḍaṁ savvaṁ uddāliya lēi khivai guttīē । tattha ya chuhākilaṁtō sō mariu vaṁtarī jāō || 69 ॥
tattō aiyāraphalaṁ sumaraṁtō maṇuyajammaaṇubhūyaṁ । paccakkhamaṇuhavatō taṁ ca kudēvattamaṇupattaṁ ॥ 70 ॥
pacchāyāvapavattō jahasattīē jiṇidabhavaṇēsu । saṁghappaōyaṇēsu ya ujjamiṁu pattamaṇuyattō ॥ 71 ॥
|
tatastatrāhaṁ dr̥ṣṭastava sādhanikēna, bhaṇati tata itaraḥ । anubhuṅkṣva rājyaśriyaṁ munidarśanatō mayā prāptām ॥57॥
tataḥ sāgaraḥ prajalpati munipādaprasādatō mayā prāptaḥ । jinadharmaḥ, kimanēna rājyēna pāpakāryēṇa 1 ॥ 58 ॥
tatō janakaṁ guṇacandrō nijāvāsē nayati svagr̥hē tu । sāgaracandrastiṣṭhati kathayati narēndrasya guṇacandraḥ ॥59॥
munidarśanavr̥ttāntaṁ pr̥cchati tathā yāmi vandituṁ tamaham । bhaṇati narēndra ēmō vayamapi, tatō naravarēndraḥ ||60 ॥
guṇacandraḥ sakalatraḥ sāgaracandrō'pi sumatijanaka yutaḥ । vandantē muniṁ gatvā śr̥ṇvanti dharma, tatō rājā ॥ 61 ॥
samyaktvaṁ pratipadyatē guṇacandrō'ṇutratānyanyē tu । samyaktvamātramaparē yathāśakti, nr̥patipramukhāḥ ॥62॥
banditvā sādhuṁ prāptā nijanijagr̥hēṣu, guṇacandraḥ । kṣaṇacandra iva gaganaṁ prabhāvayati pravacanaṁ prayataḥ ||63 ||
sāgaracandrō haṭṭē vyavaharatyarjayati ca tanmātram । yāvanmātrēṇa kuṭumbōdaraparipūraṇaṁ bhavati ॥64॥
guṇacandrēṇa svavibhavē'niśaṁ dadatyapi vividhabhaṅgibhiḥ । mithyābhimānanaṭitō'nunīyamānō'pi nō lāti ॥ 65 ॥
kiñca guṇacandrārddha dahyatē dr̥ṣṭvā sō'payiyā । draviṇapipāsayā tathā pīḍyatē'tidr̥ḍhaṁ tataḥ ॥66॥
āsōtikādimiśraṁ cōlaṁ ghusr̥ṇaṁ kusumbhasaṁmiśram | kastūrī karaṇyā tathā karpūrādidravyāṇi ॥ 67 ॥
gr̥hītvā mlēcchabhūmau yātyatha tēna kō'pi karmakaraḥ । apamānitaḥ svarūpaṁ tatprakaṭayati mlēcchanāthasya॥68॥
sa tadbhāṇḍaṁ sarvamuddālya lāti kṣipati guptau । tatra ca kṣutklāntaḥ sa mr̥tvā vyantarō jātaḥ ॥ 69 ॥
tatō'ticāraphalaṁ smaran manujajanmānubhūtam । pratyakṣamanubhavaṁstacca kudēvatvamanuprāptam ॥70॥

tabbhavakrayasukayavasā paḍhamavaē caiva pāviḍaṁ dikkhaṁ । paripāliūṇa sammaṁ vihuṇiyakammō gaō mōkkhaṁ ॥
guṇacaṁdōvihu suciraṁ gihidhammaṁ pāliuṁ gahiya dikkhō । saha bhajjāē kāuṁ kammakhayaṁ mōkkhamaṇupattō ।। 73 ।
paradavvaharaṇavirayā nirayāiduhāṇa tē khaluvvariyā । sōhaggasaṁgacaṁgā saggasirī tēhiṁ niru variyā || 74|
adattadāṇavirayā vissāsapayaṁ havaṁti savvēsiṁ । kitti suhaṁ ca viulē pārvati ihēva jammammi || 75 ||
paralō dhaṇahāṇī na hōi sijjhai samīhiyaṁ savvaṁ । ciṁtāiōvi dhuvaṁ jāyā suhasaṁpayālābhō ॥ 76 ॥
iya aiyāravisuddhaṁ tajhyavayaṁ jēhiṁ duddharaṁ dhariyaṁ । babhaṁḍamaṁḍavōvari kittilayā tāṇa vitthariyā ||77 ||
॥ iti tr̥tīyāṇuvratē pañcamāticāravipākē sāgaracandrakathā samāptā ॥
॥ tr̥tīyamaṇuvrataṁ samāptam ॥
paścāttāpapravr̥ttō yathāśakti jinēndrabhavanēṣu । saṁghaprayōjanēṣu cōdyamya prāptamanujatvaḥ ॥71॥
tadbhavakr̥tasukr̥tavaśāt prathamavayasyēva prāpya dīkṣām । paripālya samyagvidhūtakarmā gatō mōkṣam ॥72॥
guṇacandrō'pi khalu suciraṁ gr̥hidharma pālayitvā gr̥hītadīkṣaḥ । saha bhāryayā kr̥tvā karmakṣayaṁ mōkṣamanuprāptaḥ ॥ 73 ॥
paradravyaharaṇaviratā nirayā diduḥ khēbhyastē khalavr̥ttāḥ । saubhāgyasaṅgacaṅgā svargaśrīstairniścitaṁ vr̥tā ॥ 74 ॥
adattādānaviratā viśvāsapadaṁ bhavanti sarvēṣām । kīrtiṁ sukhaṁ ca vipulaṁ prāpnuvantīhaiva janmani ॥ 75 ॥
paralōkē dhanahānirna bhavati sidhyati samīhitaṁ sarvam । cintāditō'pi dhruvaṁ jāyatē sukhasaṁpalābhaḥ ॥ 76 ॥
ityaticāraviśuddhaṁ tr̥tīyatrataṁ yairdugharaṁ dhr̥tam । brahmāṇḍamaṇḍapōpari kīrtilatā tēṣāṁ vistr̥tā ॥77॥ -

jō vajjai paradāraṁ sō sēvai nō kayāi paradāraṁ । sakalatē saṁtuṭṭhō sakalattō sō narō hōi ॥ 1 ॥
ullasai jasō kittī viyaṁbhaē vittharaṁti purisatthā । paradāravajjiṇō iha bhavēvi jaha vīrakumarassa ||2||
tathāhi ;-
purimuttamakayarayaṇaṁ surayaṇamahiya supōyakulabhavaṇaṁ । asthi puraṁ supasiddhaṁ jala hissa jalaṁva sirinilayaṁ ॥
nilaō kalāṇa kallāṇasaṁgaō gayaghaḍāhi saṁghaḍiō | ghaḍiyavihattasakajjō rāyā riumaddaṇō nāma ॥ 4 ॥
tassatthi piyā rairaṁbhavibhamā vigbhamāṇa kulabhavaṇaṁ । bhuvaṇasarakamaliṇī iva kamalasirī nāma siribhavaṇaṁ ।।
visayasuhapasattāṇaṁ tāṇa taṇaō ahannayā jāō । nāmēṇa vīrakumarō saṇakumārōcva rūvēṇa ||6||
sūrō dhīrō cāī kayannasirasēharō viṇayakaliō । atrikalakalālaōvi hu sasivtra gayalaṁchaṇō tahavi ॥ 7 ॥
aha sō aviḍā āhēḍayakīlaṇatthamaḍavīē । pattō na picchaē tattha ēkamavi sasayamigamāī ||8||
tō vimyiyiō jāva iō taō bhamai pariyaṇasamēō । tā niustrībhūē picchai ēgattha dēsammi || 9 ||
sasyamaya mahisagayatrayapasava harivacittayāīē । bhayaparicatē mittavva vairiṇō jēvi annōnnaṁ ॥ 10 ॥
taha sajalajalaharudāmasamāyannaē muṇivarasta । savaṇāmayavuddhisamaṁ saṁjhāyaṁtassa avarayaṁ ॥ 11 ॥
ēttō ya paharaṇāī sarasilāīṇi jhatti khittāī । kumaravarapariyaṇēṇaṁ laggāī na tiriyadēhēsu || 12 |
tō tiriyavairasamaṇaṁ paharaṇavihalattaṇaṁ ca mannaṁtō । kumarō muṇippabhāvaṁ paṇamiya muṇiṇō caraṇakamalaṁ ॥ 13 ॥
uvavisai dharaṇivīḍhē taṁ daddhuṁ pariyaṇōvi taha kuṇai । sāhūvi dhammalābhaṁ dāūṇaṁ kahai dhammaka || 14॥
yō varjayati paradārānsa sēvatē nō kadācitparadvāram । svakalatrē saṁtuṣṭaḥ sakalatraḥ sa narō bhavati ॥ 1 ॥
ullasati yaśaḥ kīrttirvijr̥mbhatē vistr̥ṇanti puruṣārthāḥ । paradāravarjina iha bhavē'pi yathā vīrakumārasya ||2||
puruṣōttamakr̥tasada (śaya) naṁ suratnamahitaṁ supōtakulabhavanam । asti puraṁ suprasiddhaṁ jaladhērjalamiva śrīnilayam ॥3॥
nilayaḥ kalānāṁ kalyāṇasaṁgatō gajaghaṭābhiḥ saṁghaṭitaḥ । ghaṭitavibhaktasvakāryō rājā ripumardanō nāma || 4 ||
tasyāsti priyā ratirambhāvibhramā vibhramāṇāṁ kulabhavanam । bhuvanasaraḥ kamalinīva kamalaśrīrnāma śrībhavanam ॥5 ॥
viṣayasukhaprasaktayōstayōstanayō'thānyadā jātaḥ । nāmnā vīrakumāraḥ sanatkumāra iva rūpēṇa || 6 ||
śūrō dhīrastyāgī kr̥tajñaśiraḥ śēkharō vinayakalitaḥ । avikala kalālayō'pi hi śaśīva gatalāñchanastathāpi ॥7॥
atha sō'tivikaṭāyāmākhēṭaka krīḍanārthamaṭavyām । prāptō na paśyati tatraikamapi śaśaka mr̥gādim ॥ 8 ॥

tatō vismitahr̥dayō yāvaditastatō bhramati parijanasamētaḥ । tāvannikurambībhūtān paśyatyēkatra dēśē ॥9॥
śaśaka mr̥gamahiṣagaja gavayahariṇaharivyāghracitrakādīn । bhayaparityaktānmittrāṇi vairiṇō yē'pyanyōnyam ॥ 10 ॥
tathā sajalajaladharōddāmaśabdamākarṇayati munivarasya । śravaṇāmr̥tavr̥ṣṭisamaṁ saṁdhyāyatō'navaratam ॥11॥
itaśca praharaṇāni śaraprāsādīni jhaṭiti kṣiptāni । kumāravaraparijanēna lagnāni na tiryagdēhēṣu ||12||
tatastiryagvairaśamanaṁ praharaṇaviphalatvaṁ ca manyamānaḥ । kumārō muniprabhāvaṁ praṇamya munēścaraṇakamalam ॥13॥

kō nāma purisayārō jīvē taṇajīviṇō haṇatassa । kō lahai sāhuvāyaṁ ghāyaṁtō thērapaṁgula || 15||
ēgassa pāṇanāsō kīrai annō phuraṁtapariōsō । saccamiṇaṁ jaṁ mārai gāmillō gōdahillāē ||16||
satahamuhaṁ kilēsa masamaṁ sarhati mōhaṁdhā । itthēva bhavē pāvā kupparajāṇuṭṭhiyakiṇōhā ||17||
savvāṇavi pāvāṇaṁ pāvamiṇaṁ narayakāraṇaṁ paramaṁ । pāṇivahō taha sōvāgajīviyā maṁsaparibhōgō ॥ 18 ॥
savvēsi jīvāṇaṁ nipajīyaṁ vallahaṁ sayākālaṁ । maraṇaṁ puṇō aṇi pasiddhamēya jaō bhaṇiyai ॥ 19 ॥
"amēdhyamadhyē kīṭasya surēndrasya surālayē । samānā jīvitākāṅkṣā samaṁ mr̥tyubhayaṁ dvayōḥ ॥ "
duvvayaṇagālighāyā parābhavō vaṁcaṇaṁ tahā maraṇaṁ । jaha apaṇō aṇi muṇa annēsipi taha cēva || 20 |
jaṁ jassa hōi iṭuṁ dijjau taṁ tassa parabhavē patthaṁ । jārisamiharaṁ dijjai lagbhai annattha tārisayaṁ ||21|
ēgattha hōi jīyaṁ ēgacchattaṁ ca rajjamēgattha । annayaranāsakālē jīyaṁ jīyāṇa iyaraṁ ॥ 22 ॥
kiśca ।
dhaṇabaṁdhavasayaṇēsuṁ puttakalattēsu caiva savrvvasu । niyajīyaṁ iṭṭhayaraṁ aṇubhavasiddhaṁ imaṁ lōē ||23||
jai māṇusāvi maṁsaṁ asaṁti ruhiraṁ piyaṁti pāṇīṇaṁ । tō naṇu kīḍayasāṇāiēhi saha kō visēsō siṁ? ॥
jaṁ jīvaṁta sattaṁ hariūṇamasaraṇayaṁ niravarāhaṁ । bhakkhijjai sē maṁsaṁ pijjai ruhiraṁ ca tuṭṭhēhi ||25||
mōttūṇa narayapaḍaṇaṁ kiṁ annaṁ maṁsabhakkhaṇassa phalaṁ ? | saṁtēvi pavarabhakkhē jamakkhamalakkhaṇā khaṁti ||26||
hōu ajaṇaṇī tēsi dubbharaṇī paḍau tadudarassāvi । jē bhakkhaṁti nisugā nikkaruṇā maṁsamasuisamaṁ ॥। 27
upaviśati dharaṇīpīṭhē taṁ dr̥ṣṭrā parijanō'pi tathā karōti । sādhurapi dharmalābhaṁ dattvā kathayati dharmakathām ॥
kō nāma puruṣakārō jīvāṁstr̥ṇajīvinō ghnataḥ । kō labhatē sādhuvādaṁ ghātayan sthavirapaṅgulān ||15||
ēkasya prāṇanāśaḥ kriyatē'nyaḥ sphuratparitōṣaḥ । satyamētad yanmārayati gāṁ daridrō gōdadhyartham ॥ 16 ॥
śītōṣṇatr̥ṣṇāpramukhaṁ klēśamasamaṁ sahantē mōhāndhāḥ । atraiva bhavē pāpāḥ kūrparajānusthita kiṇaughāḥ || 17||
sarvēṣāmapi pāpānāṁ pāpamētannarakakāraṇaṁ paramam । prāṇivadhastathā śvapākajīvikā māṁsaparibhōgaḥ || 18 ||
sarvēṣāṁ jīvānāṁ nijajīvitaṁ vallabhaṁ sadākālam । maraṇaṁ punaraniṣṭaṁ prasiddhamētad yatō bhaṇitam ॥ 19 ॥
durvacanagālighātāḥ parābhavō vañcanaṁ tathā maraṇam । yathā''tmanō'niṣṭaṁ jānīhyanyēṣāmapi tathaiva ॥ 20 ॥
yad yasya bhavatīṣṭaṁ dīyatāṁ tattasya parabhavē prārthyam । yādr̥śamiha dīyatē labhyatē'nyatra tādr̥śam ॥21॥
ēkatra bhavati jīvitamēkacchatraṁ ca rājyamēkatra । anyataranāśakālē jīvitaṁ jīvānāmiṣṭataram ||22||
dhanabāndhavasvajanēṣu putrakalatrēṣvēva sarvēṣu । nijajīvitamiṣṭataramanubhavasiddhamidaṁ lōkē ॥ 23 ॥
yadi mānuṣā api māṁsamaśnanti rudhiraṁ pibanti prāṇinām । tatō nanu kīṭaśvānādikaiḥ saha kō viśēṣa ēṣām
yajjīvantaṁ sattvaṁ hatvā'śaraṇakaṁ niraparādham । bhakṣyatē tasya māṁsaṁ pīyatē rudhiraṁ ca tuṣṭaiḥ ॥25॥
.
muktvā narakapatanaṁ kimanyad māṁsabhakṣaṇasya phalam ? । satyapi pravarabhakṣyē yadakṣamalakṣaṇāḥ khādanti ॥ 26 ॥

vīrakumārakahā ।
371
iccāidēṇāra kumarō saṁpattaparamasammattō । niyamai saṁkappēṇaṁ thūlāṇavarāhapāṇiva ||28||
paradārasēvaṇaṁ maṁsabhakkhaṇaṁ taha ya pariyaṇō tassa । niyamēi kōvi kiṁpi hu, namiya muṇi jaṁti sahāṇē ॥ 29 ॥
ai annayā kumārā rannā puṭṭhā maīparikkhaṭṭhā | jaha paṁcālēsu maē ṭaviō jō cihna niōgī ||30||
sō ainiuṇō ya avaṁcagōvi payaīē tattha dasa lakkhē | kaṇayassuppajjaṁtē sāhai ēgammi varisammi|| 31 ॥
annō bhai panarasa lakkhē kaṇayassa ahamihajjēmi । puvvaniōgissa imaṁ kahiyē amhēhi tahāvi imō ॥ 32 ॥
bhagai ma vittaṁ jattiyamittaṁ taō ahaṁ ahiyaṁ । uppāiumasamatthō jaṁ jujjara kuṇau taṁ dēvō ॥33॥
tā iha kiṁ kāyavvaṁ, vīrakumāraṁ vivajji annē । savvē bhaṇati kumarā jō uppāyara bahuṁ kaṇayaṁ ॥ 34॥
sō ṭhāvijña dēsē, vīrakumāraṁ taō bhai rāyā । kiṁ kiṁpi tumaṁ na bhaṇasi, sō bhaṇai na majjha mayamēyaṁ ॥
jaṁtāṇaṁ kahiō puvvaniōgī avacagō niuṇō । sōcciya tāyassa hiō pīḍēuṁ mahai na payāō ॥ 36॥
tāṇa ya apīḍiyāṇaṁ hōi samiddhī taō payati । vavasāyā tē jēsiṁ karēṇa nīīē naravaṇō ||37||
upajjai bahudaviṇa viṇa! anīī taō ya paivarisaṁ । ahiyayaraṁ ahiyayaraṁ vaḍūḍhēi daviṇaṁ ca dhammō ya॥ 38 ॥
uktaṁ ca;
"arthāt trivarganiṣpattiryāṁyōpājitavardhanāt । atharmānarthaśōkānāṁ viparītāt samudbhavaḥ ॥”
tā paḍhamōciya jōggō ahigārī jō napuṇa lēi dhaṇaṁ । iyarō uṇa anaēṇaṁ panarasa lakkhē samajjiṇihī |
tumha niōī hōuṁ jaṁ annāyaṁ imō samāyarihī । taṁ tubbhaṁpi ahammaṁ ajasappaharaṁ ca uvaṇēhī ||40||
bhavatvajananistēṣāṁ durbharaṇiḥ patatu tadudarasyāpi । yē bhakṣayanti niḥśūkā niṣkaruṇā māṁsamaśucisamam ॥ 27 ॥
ityādidēśanayā kumāraḥ saṁprāptaparamasamyaktvaḥ । niyamayati saṁkalpēna sthūlānaparādhaprāṇivadham ||28||
paradārasēvanaṁ māṁsabhakṣaṇaṁ tathāca parijanastasya । niyamayati kō'pi kimapi khalu, natvā muniṁ yānti svasthānē ॥
athānyadā kumārā rājñā pr̥ṣṭā matiparīkṣārtham । yathā pāñcālēṣu mayā sthāpitō yastiṣṭhatiṁ niyōgī ॥30॥
sō'tinipuṇaścāvañcakō'pi prakr̥tyā tatra daśa lakṣān । kanakasyōtpadyamānān kathayatyēkasmin varṣē ॥31॥
anyō bhaṇati pañcadaśa lakṣānkanakasyāhamihārjayāmi । pūrvaniyōgina idaṁ kathitamasmābhistathāpyayam॥ 32 ॥
bhaṇati mayā vijñataṁ yāvanmātraṁ tatō'hamadhikam । utpādayitumasamarthō yad yujyatē karōtu tad dēvaḥ ॥ 33॥
tasmādiha kiṁ kartavyaṁ, vīrakumāraṁ vivarjyānyē । sarvē bhaṇanti kumārā ya utpādayati bahu kanakam ||34||
sasthāpyatāṁ dēśē, vīrakumāraṁ tatō bhaṇati rājā । kiṁ kimapi tvaṁ na bhaṇasi, sa bhaṇati na mama matamētat ॥
yattātēna kathitaḥ pūrvaniyōgī avañcakō nipuṇaḥ । sa ēva tātasya hitaḥ pīḍayituṁ na kāṅkṣati prajāḥ ॥36॥
tāsāṁ cāpīḍitānāṁ bhavati samr̥ddhistataḥ pravartantē । vyavasāyāstē yēṣāṁ karēṇa nītyā narapatēḥ ॥37॥
utpadyatē bahudraviṇaṁ vinā'nīti tataśca prativarṣam । adhikatara madhikataraṁ vardhatē draviṇaṁ ca dharmaśca ॥ 38 ॥
1
I
tasmāt prathama ēva yōgyō'dhikārī yō nayēna lāti dhanam । itaraḥ punaranayēna pañcadaśa lakṣānsamarjayiṣyati ॥
tava niyōgī bhūtvā yamanyāyamayaṁ samācariṣyati । sa yuṣmākamapyadharmamayaśaḥ prahāraṁ cōpanēṣyati ॥40॥

kiñca ।
supāsanāha-caritryammi -
।
panarasa lakkhē ēgammi vaccharē jai paraṁ uvajjēhī । viyammi tacca utthaṁ tattaiyaṁ vā uvajjijjā ॥41॥
tayammi vaccharammī ajuttadāṇō tarhi jaṇō hōhī । tā lakkhaṁpi na hōhī hōhī saccē imaṁ vayaṇaṁ ||42|
" atyupādānamarthasya prajābhyaḥ pr̥thivībhujām । dugdhamādāya dhēnūnāṁ māṁsāya stanakartanam || "
tō naranāhō ciṁtai lahuōvi imō vaēṇa savvēsiṁ । aigaruō buddhīē, tā rajjadhuraṁ imō dharihī ||43||
tājaivi ahaṁ maccharijaṇāu ēyassa kahavi hu avāyaṁ । rakkhaṁtō payaḍissaṁ na rajjapayajōggayamimassa || 44 |
tahavi huē saṁgaṭṭiē guṇē taha jaṇāṇurāyaṁ ca । pacchāi na sakkā iya ciṁtiya bhāi tō ēvaṁ ॥ 45 ॥
vaccha ! imē savvēvi hukubuddhiṇō buddhimaṁ tumaṁ caiva । jaṁ savvasammayāō vivarīyaṁ bhaṇasi iya ēvaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
tā annavidvattā tujjha na sōhai sirīi paribhōgō । niyabuddhīē avannā hōi kayā jaṁ taē ēvaṁ || 47|
tā maṁca vivamēyaṁ dēsa ca imaṁ jamittha dēsammi । tuha buddhīē pabhāvō saṁtōvi na hōi aipayaḍō ||48 |
tō naravarassa pāē namiūṇaṁ niggaō taō kumarō । maisāgaramaṁtisuraṇa vimalanāmēṇa sasahāō ||49 |
pacchannanivanirūviyadēsaṁtarapahiyavēsa suhaḍēhiṁ । aṇugammatō sayayaṁ saṁpattī kōsalapuram ||50 ॥
puraparisarasaratīrē vissamiō jāva ciṭṭhai kumārō | tāva halabōlamuhalō ucchaliō tūranigghōsō || 51|
tō puṭṭhō kavi narōtthavō vimalamaṁtiṇā kiṁ bhō ।। kōvi hu mahūsakō iha jaṁ suvbai tūranigghōsō ? |
tō sō kai raṇadhavalarāiṇō atthi kurumaīnāmā । niyāṇāṇavi ahiyā duhiā naravēsiṇī kannā ।
tō tapaṇā ārāhiyāē kuladēvayāē iya kahiyaṁ । jassajja paṭṭahatthī kaṁṭhē khivihī kusumamālaṁ ||24|
pañcadaśa lakṣānēkasminvatsarē yadi paramupārjayiṣyati । dvitīyē taccaturthaṁ tattr̥tīyaṁ vōpārjayēt ॥41॥
tr̥tīyē vatsarē'yuktadānastatra janō bhaviṣyati । tatō lakṣamapi na bhaviṣyati bhaviṣyati satyamidaṁ vacanam ॥
tatō naranāthaścintayati laghurapyayaṁ vayasā sarvēṣām । atigurubuddhayā, tasmādrājyadhurāmayaṁ dhariṣyati ॥ 43 ॥
tasmādyadyapyahaṁ matsarijanādētasya kathamapi pāyam । rakṣan prakaṭayiṣyāmi na rājyapadayōgyatāmasya || 44 ॥
tathāpi hyētasyāṅgasthitānguṇāṁstathā janānurāgaṁ ca । pracchādayituṁ na śakyā iti cintayitvā bhaṇati tata ēvam ॥
vatsa ! imē sarvē'pi khalu kubuddhayō buddhimāṁstvamēva । yatsarvasammatād viparītaṁ bhaṇasītyēvam ॥46॥
tasmādanyārjitāyāstava na śōbhatē śriyāḥ paribhōgaḥ । nijabuddhēravajñā bhavati kr̥tā yattvayaivam ॥47॥
tasmānmuñca vibhavamētaṁ dēśa cēmaṁ yadatra dēśē । taba buddhēḥ prabhāvaḥ sannapi na bhavatyatiprakaṭaḥ ॥ 48 ॥
tatō naravarasya pādau natvā nirgatastataḥ kumāraḥ । matisāgaramantrisutēna vimalanāmnā sasahāyaḥ ॥ 49 ॥
pracchannanr̥panirūpitadēśāntarapathikavēṣasubhaṭaiḥ । anugamyamānaḥ satataṁ saṁprāptaḥ kōśalapurē ॥50॥
puraparisarasarastīrē viśrāntō yāvattiṣṭhati kumāraḥ । tāvatkalakala mukhara ucchalitastūryanirghōṣaḥ ||11||
tataḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ kō'pi narō vāstavyō vimalamantriṇā kiṁ bhōḥ ! । kō'pi hi mahōtsava iha yat śrūyatē tūryanirghōṣaḥ ॥
tataḥ sa kathayati raṇavavalarājasyāsti kurumatīnāmā। nijaprāṇēbhyō'pyadhikā duhitā naradvēṣiṇī kanyā ॥ 53 ॥

1
sō kumarīē bhattā aṇurattā tammi nicchiyaṁ hōhī । tō pūivi paṭṭakariṁ kumari ārōviḍaṁ uvari || 55 ॥
mukō niraṁkusō sō puraō vajjaṁtatūraniyarēṇa । tēṇavi māliyapaṭṭē gaṁtūṇa karē kayā mālā ॥ 56 ॥
naravaisēṇāhiba maṁḍalīya sāmaṁtamaṁtiparikaliō । sō inhi puramajjhē kayakaramālō paribhamai ||27||
iya kahiūṇaṁ viraē tammi narē jāva ciṭṭhaē vimalō । tō takkhaṇēṇa pattō paṭṭakarī tassa dipihaṁ ॥ 58 ॥
vigalaṁtavimalamayajalaparimalavasamiliyamahalabhamaraḍalaṁ । taṁ picchiūṇa iṁtaṁ vimalō paḍibōhara kumaraṁ ॥ 59 ॥
jātā khaṇēṇa pattō hatthī kumarassa saṁnihāṇampi । karakaliyakusumamālaṁ khiviya kumārassa kaṁṭammi ॥ 60॥
niyakhaṁdhē ārōvara vīrakumāraṁ karē karēūṇa । rāyāvi hu parituṭṭhō taṁ daddhaṁ mayaṇasamarūvaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
kumārī sō dō anannalāyannalahariparikaliō । amayajalahivva sahasā taraṁgiō punnimanisāē ||
aha rāyā karidasagaṁ suvannalakkhaṁ turaṁgamasahassaṁ । kumarassa dhūlijhāḍāvaṇīē dāūṇa vihipuvvaṁ || 63 ||
chāyālaggaṁ ciya kurumaīē kumarīē saha kumārēṇa । kārai pāṇiggahaṇaṁ saṁtōsiyasayalajaṇahiyayaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
gāmasahassē pāṇissa mōyaṇē dēi appaṇō varaṁ । pāsāyaṁ naranāhō, vilasai tatthaḍiō kumarō || 65॥
jaō kumarassa sayaṁ pēsiyapacchannapurisavayaṇāō । sōuṁ vr̥ttaṁtamimaṁ ainivyamāṇasō jāō || 66 ||
pāṇiggahadivasēsu ya naranāhēṇaṁ niyammi bhavaṇammi | paribhuṁjatō maṁsāivajjiyaṁ pucchi kumarō ||67||
jaha kiṁ ēyaṁ tattō kumarēṇa jāva kahiumādattaṁ । tō rāyā bhaṇai aṇāulēṇa sōyavvamaha kumarō ॥ 68 ॥
tatastātpatrā''rādhitayā kuladēvatayēti kathitam । yasyādya paṭṭahastī kaṇṭhē kṣēpsyati kusumamālām ॥14॥
sa kumāryā bhartā'nuraktā tasminniścitaṁ bhaviṣyati । tataḥ pūjayitvā paṭṭakariṇaṁ kumārīmārōpyōpari ||15||
muktō niraṅkuśaḥ sa puratō vādyamānatūryanikarēṇa । tēnāpi mālikapaṭṭē gatvā karē kr̥tā mālā ||16||
narapatisēnādhipamaṇḍalikasāmantamantriparikalitaḥ । sa idānīṁ puramadhyē kr̥takaramālaḥ paribhramati || 57 ॥
iti kathayitvā viratē tasmin narē yāvattiṣṭhati vimalaḥ । tatastatkṣaṇēna prāptaḥ paṭṭakarī tasya dr̥ṣṭipatham ॥ 58 ॥
vigaladvimalamadajalaparimalavaśamilitamukharabhramarakulam । taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā''yantaṁ vimala: pratibōdhayati kumāram ||19||
yāvattāvatkṣaṇēna prāptō hastī kumārasya saṁnidhānē । karakalitakusumamālāṁ kṣiptvā kumārasya kaṇṭhē ॥ 60 ॥
nijaskandha ārōpayati vīrakumāraṁ karē kr̥tvā । rājāpi khalu parituṣṭastaṁ dr̥ṣṭvā madanasamarūpam ॥ 61 ॥
kumāryāpi sa dr̥ṣṭō'nanyalāvaṇyalahariparikalitaḥ । amr̥tajaladhivatsahasā taraṅgitaḥ pūrṇimāniśayā ॥ 62 ॥
atha rājā karidaśakaṁ suvarṇalakṣaṁ turaṅgamasahasram | kumārasya dhūlicchōṭanāvanyāṁ dattvā vidhipūrvam ॥ 63 ॥
chāyālagnēnaiva kurumatyāḥ kumāryāḥ saha kumārēṇa । kārayati pāṇigrahaṇaṁ saṁtōṣitasakalajanahr̥dayam ॥ 64 ॥
grāmasahasraṁ pāṇērmōcanē dadātyātmanaḥ pravaram । prāsādaṁ naranāthō, vilasati tatra sthitaḥ kumāraḥ ॥ 65॥
janakaḥ kumārasya svayaṁ prēṣitapracchannapuruṣavacanāt । śrutvā vr̥ttāntamimamatinivr̥tamānasō jātaḥ ॥ 66 ॥
pāṇigrahadivasēṣu ca naranāthēna nijē bhavanē । paribhuñjānō māṁsādivarjitaṁ pr̥ṣṭaḥ kumāraḥ ||67 ||
yathā kimētat, tataḥ kumārēṇa yāvatkathayitumārabdham । tatō rājā bhaṇatyanākulēna śrōtavyamatha kumāraḥ ॥ 68 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi -
.
vinnavai jahā ēvaṁ hōu paraṁ iha vivāhamajjhammi । vārijjau pāgō rasavaīē maṁsassa, tō rannā ||69 ॥
taṁ caiva kayaṁ tattō vittammi vivāhapakkamē bhaṇiō । kumarēṇa nivō suvvara maṁsassa abhakkhaṇē hēū ||70 |
paṁciṁdiyavavajjaṁ hōi na maṁsaṁ, vahō ya ēēsi । narayassa paramahēū vannijjai dhammasatthē ॥ 71 ॥
iccā dēṇāra parikahiyā maṁsabhakkhaṇē dōsā । kahiyaṁ ca pasaṁgēṇaṁ jaigihidhammāṇa tattapi ॥ 72 ॥
taha attaṇō aṇuvvayapariggahō maṁsapabhiiparihārō । taṁ sōuṁ naravaṇō visēsaō tammi bahumāṇō ||73।
vissāsōviya paramō saṁjāō taha ya tēṇa paḍivannaṁ । maṁsaparibhōgaparivajjaṇēṇa saha dēvagurutattaṁ ॥ 74॥
aha adi paḍihāra sūiyā itthiyā samaṇupattā । saṁjhāsamaē ēvaṁ vibhattō tīi kumaravarō || 75 ||
jaha kumara ! ittha nayarē caurō nivasaṁti paramakhvadharā । nivamaṁtisidvipaḍihārabhāriyā tāhiṁ taṁ diṭṭhō ।
mayaṇavihurāhiṁ caurhivi tuha pāsē pēsiyamhi pattēyaṁ । na muṇaṁti vaiyaramimaṁ parōpparaṁ tā kamēṇa jahā ।। 77 ।
tuha saṁgamamēyāō lahaṁti karuṇaṁ tahā kuṇasu nāha ! । tattō jaṁ kāyavvaṁ taṁ nicchai bhai kumarō || 78 |
bhāvinisi paḍhamapaharē paḍihārī ēu siṭṭiṇī bīē । taiyampi sacivabhajjā carimē puṇa ēu nivapattī ।
niyamaṇakāmiya saṁpattipayaḍasaṁghaḍiyavahalapulayā sā । taṁ pattēyaṁ tāsiṁ jāṇāvara kumara paḍivanaṁ ||80||
tō bīyadiṇē kumarō bhaṇai naridaṁ jahā ahaṁ tumha । daṁsēmi kiṁpi, kiṁpuṇa jai tamadiṭuṁba mannēsi ॥ 81 ॥
bhai nivō puttasamō taṁ vavahārēṇa amha sappurisa ! । nicchayaō puṇa saddhammadāṇaō maṇuyajammamimaṁ ।
saphalatō jaṇaōcciya, tā kiṁ iha vaccha ! iya vikappēṇaṁ । vāvārasu jaṇamēyaṁ jattha va tattha va niyaruīē ।
vijñapayati yathaivaṁ bhavatu paramiha vivāhamadhyē | vāryatāṁ pākō rasavatyāṁ māṁsasya, tatō rājñā ॥ 69 ॥
tadēva kr̥taṁ tatō vr̥ttē vivāhaprakramē bhāṇataḥ । kumārēṇa nr̥paḥ śrūyatāṁ māṁsasyābhakṣaṇē hētuḥ ॥ 70 ॥
pañcēndriyavadhavarja bhavati na māṁsaṁ vadhaścaitēṣām । narakasya paramahēturvarṇyatē dharmaśāstrēṣu ॥ 71 ॥
ityādidēśanayā parikathitā māṁsabhakṣaṇē dōṣāḥ । kathitaṁ ca prasaṅgēna yatigr̥hidharmayōstattvamapi ॥ 72॥
tathātmanō'ṇutrataparigrahō māṁsaprabhr̥tiparihāraḥ । tat śrutvā narapatērviśēṣatastasmin bahumānaḥ ॥73॥
viśvāsō'pi ca paramaḥ saṁjātastathā ca tēna pratipannam । māṁsaparibhōgaparivarjanēna saha dēvagurutattvam ॥74
athānyadinē pratihārasūcitā strī samanuprāptā । saṁdhyāsamaya ēvaṁ vijñaptastayā kumāravaraḥ ॥75॥
yathā kumāra ! atra nagarē catasrō nivasanti paramarūpadharāḥ । nr̥pamantri śrēṣṭhipratihāra bhāryāstābhistvaṁ dr̥ṣṭaḥ ॥ 76 ॥
madanavidhurābhiścatasr̥bhirapi tava pārśvē prēṣitāsmi pratyēkam । na jānanti vyatikaramimaṁ parasparaṁ tasmā kramēṇa yathā ॥
tava saṁgamamētā labhantē karuṇāṁ tathā kuruṣva nātha ! । tatō yatkartavyaṁ tanniścitya bhaṇati kumāraḥ ॥ 78 ॥
bhāviniśi prathamapraharē pratīhāryētu śrēṣṭhinī dvitīyē । tr̥tīyē sacivabhāryā caramē punarētu nr̥papatnī ॥ 79 ॥
nijamanaḥkāmitasaṁprāptiprakaṭasaṁghaṭita bahalapulakā sā । tat pratyēkaṁ tābhyō jñāpayati kumārapratipannam ||80||
tatō dvitīyadanē kumārō bhaṇati narēndraṁ yathā'haṁ tvām । darśayāmi kimapi, kintu yadi tadadr̥ṣṭamiva manyasē ॥
bhaṇati nr̥paḥ putrasamastvaṁ vyavahārēṇa mama satpuruṣa ! | niścayataḥ punaḥ saddharmadānatō manujajanmēdam ॥ 82॥

vīrakumārakahā ।
૨૬
tō bhai nivaṁ kumarō sajhāē ajja majjha āvāsē । pacchannā ēha, taō bhaṇai nivō kijjaē ēvaṁ ॥ 84॥
taha caiva kathaṁ rannā, kumarēṇaṁ apaṇō samāsanē । pacchannē pakampi ṭāviō naravarō pavarē ॥85॥
aha kē gavi chaumēṇa niragaṁtuṁ niyagharāō paḍihārī । saṁpattā ubaviṭṭhā kumarēṇa bhaṇiumādattā ||86 |
tathāhi ;-
iha lōē duhahēū paralōē narayakāraṇaṁ visayā । taṁ saccamiṇaṁ jāyaṁ vāyasamaṁsaṁpi ucchiṣṭaṁ ॥87॥
sēvēsu nāma visara duggaihēūvi hōi jai tittī | bhakkhijjau ucchiṣṭaṁ jaī miṭṭha hōi bhujaṁta ||88 ||
bhuttēhivi visarahina hōi tittī imassa jīvassa । paralōē narayagaī dō daṁḍā kaha sahijaṁti ? ॥ 89 ॥
jīvēhi ciraṁ bhuttā visayā tiyasattaṇammi saggēsu । tahavi na tittī jāyā bahusāyarasaṁkhakālēna ॥ 90॥
tō kaha tittī hōi imēhiṁ tucchēhi visayasōkkhēhiṁ । taha thēvakāliēhi māṇusammammi bhuttē hi ? || 91 ॥
jaivi jaṇaṁtukarisa āvāyamaṇōramā imē visayā । tahavi pariṇāmavirasā kiṁpāgaphalōvamā pāvā || 92 ॥
tamhā visaē parivajjiūṇa iṁdiyamaṇāī damiūṇa । nāūṇa mōkkhamaggaṁ tammi sayā ujjamaṁ kuṇasu || 93॥
mōkkhassa puṇō maggō sammaṁ sammattanāṇacaraṇāī | tāī ca sabhēyāī kahiyāī tappurō tattō ||94 ||
paḍibuddhā paḍihārī, bīē paharammi siṭṭiṇī pattā | javaṇiyamajjhē paḍhamaṁ khiviraṁ paḍibōhaē bīyaṁ ॥ 95 ॥
sāvi tahā paḍibuddhā, saṁpattā sacivabhāriyā tattō । rayaṇīē taiyajāmē sāvi sumammi saṁṭhaviyā ॥ 96 ॥
niyapipicchaō ṭāviūṇa tāōvi javaṇiyaṁtariyā । dhariyā kumarēṇa, taō saṁpattā rāyapattīvi ॥ 97॥
saphalayañjanaka ēva tasmātkimiha vatsa ! iti vikalpēna । vyāpāraya janamētaṁ yatra vā tatra vā nijarucyā ॥ 83 ॥
tatō bhaṇati nr̥paṁ kumāraḥ saṁdhyāyāmadya mamāvāsē । pracchannā ēta, tatō bhaṇati nr̥paḥ kriyata ēvam ॥ 84 ॥
tathaiva kr̥taṁ rājñā, kumārēṇātmanaḥ samāsanē । pracchannē palyaṅkē sthāpitō naravaraḥ pravarē ॥85॥
atha kēnāpi cchadmanā nirgatya nijagr̥hāt pratihārī । saṁprāptōpaviṣṭā kumārēṇa bhaṇitumārabdhā ॥ 86 ॥
iha lōkē duḥkhahētuḥ paralōkē narakakāraṇaṁ viṣayāḥ । tatsatyamētajjātaṁ vāyasamāṁsamapyucchiṣṭam ॥87॥
sēvasva nāma viṣayān durgatihētūnapi bhavati yadi tr̥ptiḥ । bhakṣyatāmucchiṣṭaṁ yadi miṣṭaṁ bhavati bhujyamānam ॥
bhuktairapi viṣayairna bhavati tr̥ptirasya jīvasya । paralōkē narakagatidvau daṇḍau kathaṁ sahyētē ? ॥89॥
jīvaiściraṁ bhuktā viṣayāstridaśatvē svargēṣu । tathāpi na tr̥ptirjātā bahusāgarasaṁkhyakālēna ॥90॥
tataḥ kathaṁ tr̥ptirbhavatyēbhistucchairviṣayasaukhyaiḥ । tathā stōkakālikairmānuṣajanmani bhuktaiḥ ॥91॥
yadyapi janayantūtkarṣamāpātamanōramā imē viṣayāḥ । tathāpi pariṇāmavirasāḥ kimpākaphalōpamāḥ pāpāḥ ॥92॥
tasmād
viṣayān parivarjyēndriyamanāṁsi damitvā । jñālā mōkṣamārga tasminsadōdyamaṁ kuruṣva ॥ 93 ॥
mōkṣasya punarmārgaḥ samyaksamyaktvajñānacaraṇāni । tāni ca sabhēdāni kathitāni tatpurastataḥ ॥ 94 ॥
pratibuddhā pratihārī, dvitīyē praharē śrēṣṭhinī prāptā । yavanikāmadhyē prathamāṁ kṣiptvā pratibōdhayati dvitīyām ॥95॥
sāpi tathā pratibuddhā, saṁprāptā sacivabhāryā tataḥ । rajanyāstr̥tīyayā mē sāpi sumārgē saṁsthāpitā ॥ 96 ॥

supāsanāhacariśrammi-
mōsūṇa taō sijjaṁ kumarēṇanmuṭṭhiūṇa paṇayā sā । tō jaṁpai sā jīviyanāha ! kimēyaṁ samāraddhaṁ ? ॥98॥
raria imō kōvasarō kō va bahupaṇāmassa ? । niyaaṁgasaṁgamāmayarasēṇa nivvavasu maha aṁgaṁ ॥ 99||
niyavirahaggipalittaṁ kharṇapi mā sāmi ! maṁ uvēhēsu । iharā picchihisi phuḍaṁ hiyayaṁ phuḍiḍaṁ mayaṁ caiva ।
iya bhaṇirī tī kumarō'bhimurhapi nō palōēi । jaṁ sā mayaṇummattā ajjavi arihai na uvaēsa || 101 ॥
tō avahīrijjatī kumarēṇaṁ bhaṇai sā imaṁ vayaṇaṁ । huti hu saccaparannā sappurisā kira tuha saricchā ।
uktaṁ ca ;---
“ sakr̥dapi yatpratipannaṁ tatkathamapi na tyajanti satpuruṣāḥ । nēndustyajati kalaṅkaṁ nōjjhati vaḍavānalaṁ sindhuḥ ||"
saṁjayamimamasacaṁ maha visaē sāmi ! maṁdabhagāē । annaha mēṁ vāharivaṁ parammuhattaṁ kahaṁ bhayasi ? || 103 ।
tō bhai imaṁ kumarō tuha dūīē pavajjiḍaṁ vayaṇaṁ । vāhariyā si tumaṁ iha kira tuha kahiūṇa jiṇadhammaṁ ॥ 104 ॥
duccariyā imāō iha paralōē duraṁtadukkhāō । cittaṁ niyattiūṇaṁ ṭhāvissaṁ suddhadhammammi ॥ 105 ॥
sā bhai karijjasu taṁpi nivvuī suhaya ! maha jaṇēūṇa । niyaaṁgasaṁgamaiṇaṁ tō kumarō bhaṇai jā tujjha ।। 106 ।
ā pāṇiggahaṇāō naravaiṇō'ṇaṁgatullarūvassa । paidivasasaṁgamēṇaṁ jai tittī nēya saṁjāyā || 107॥
sā cōriyaramiyāō maha aṁgā hōhihitti dubbuddhī । tā muṁca asaggāhaṁ sēvasu maggaṁ nirābāī || 108 |
iya ēvamuvakkamiḍaṁ puvvattapattigabbhiṇaṁ subahuṁ । kumarēṇa bhaṇiyāvi hu bhaṇēi sā tujjha savvaṁpi । । 109 ।
kāhāmi ahaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁpuṇa saccavasu tāva taṁ vayaṇaṁ । maha dūīē puraō jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ, annaha asaccē ॥ 110 ॥
nijaṣpr̥ṣṭhapaścāt sthāpayitvā tē api yavanikāntaritē । dhr̥tē kumārēṇa, tataḥ saṁprāptā rājapatnyapi ॥97॥
muktvā tataḥ śayyāṁ kumārēṇābhyutthāya praṇatā sā । tatō jalpati sā jīvitanātha ! kimētatsamārabdham ॥
abhyutthānasyāyaṁ kō'vasaraḥ kō vā bahupraṇāmasya ? | nijāṅgasaṁgamāmr̥tarasēna nirvāpaya mamāṅgam ॥99॥
nijavirahāgnipradīptaṁ kṣaṇamapi mā svāmin! māmupēkṣasva । itarathā drakṣyasi sphuṭaṁ hr̥dayaṁ sphuṭitvā mr̥tāmēva ।
iti bhaṇitryāstasyāḥ kumārō'bhimukhamapi na pralōkatē । yatsā madōnmattā'dyāpyarhati nōpadēśam ॥ 101 ॥
tatō'vadhīyamāṇā kumārēṇa bhagati sēdaṁ vacanam । bhavanti khalu satyapratijñāḥ satpuruṣāḥ kila taba sadr̥kṣāḥ ॥
saṁjātamidamasatyaṁ mama viṣayē svāmin! mandabhāgyāyāḥ । anyathā mā vyāhr̥tya parāṅmukhatvaṁ kathaṁ bhajasi ? |
tatō bhaṇatīdaṁ kumārastava dūtyāḥ prapadya vacanam । āhūtāsi tvamiha kila tava kathayitvā jinadharmam ॥ 104॥
duścaritādasmādiha paralōkē durantaduḥkhāt । cittaṁ nivartya sthāpayiṣyāmi śuddhadharmē ॥ 105 ॥
sā bhaṇati kriyatāṁ tadapi nirvr̥tiṁ subhaga ! mama janayitvā । nijāṅgasaṁgamēna tataḥ kumārō bhaṇati yā tava । 106 ।
ā pāṇigrahaṇād narapatēranaṅgatulyarūpasya । pratidivasasaṁgamēna yadi tr̥ptirnaiva saṁjātā ॥ 107 ॥
sā cauryaramitād mamāṅgād bhaviṣyatīti durbuddhiḥ । tasmānmuñcāsagrāhaṁ sēvasva mārga nirābādham ॥ 108 ॥
ityēvamupakramya pūrvōktapravr̥ttigarbhaṁ subahu । kumārēṇa bhaṇitāpi hi bhagati sā tava sarvamapi ॥109॥
kariṣyāmyahaṁ bhaṇitaṁ kintu satyāpaya tāvattad vacanam । mama dr̥tyāḥ puratō yad bhaṇitam, anyathā'satyē ||

jāē ēyammi na majjha pacaō asthi tujjha vayaṇēsu । bhaṇai kumarō na vaṁchiyamēyaṁ tuha hōi iha jammē ॥ 111 ॥
iya kumarassa asarisaṁ sattaṁ vayaṇāī supahanayaṇāīṁ । taṁ taha duraśvasiyaṁ ca appaṇō sā vibhāvatī ॥ 112 ॥
taha vēraggaṁ pattā bhai jahā paṇamiṁu kumaracaraṇē । baṁdhava ! nillajjāē majjāyāvajjiyāē maē ॥113॥
baṁdhūvi kaṇitamō māimamāṇāē pāvabhaiṇīē । sattikkanihī āyāsiō si jaṁ tassa pāvarasa || 194 ||
kaha chuṭṭīhāmi ahaṁ vacchō jāṇai na vaiyaraṁ ēyaṁ । tuha piuṇō haṁ dhūyā savakkijaṇaṇīē saṁbhūyā ।। 115 ।।
mūlē naktamma piuṇōpāyammi pēsiyā tattō । dhāīhiṁ pariggahiyā māulanivapavarasēṇassa ॥ 116 ॥
baṁgāladēsavaiṇō tēṇaṁ tuha sasurayassa dinnā hai। ēyāō vaiyarāō gaēsu paurēsu varisēsu ॥ 117 ॥
niyakula nahayalasaṁ punna amayakiraṇō tumaṁ samuppannō | paranārīu tumaṁ jō mannasi savvāu bhaiṇīō ॥ 118 ॥
tō iya kalaṁkamaliṇē pāṇē kēṇavi ahaṁ paōgēṇa । vaccāmi pariccaiuṁ jīvasu maha jīviēṇa tumaṁ ॥ 119॥
tō kumarō bhai imaṁ iya paricattērhi tujjha pāṇēhiṁ । vālamaraṇaṁti kāuṁ parivaḍḍhai dukkharichōlī || 120 ||
tō sāṇē gaṁtuṁ nisisēsaṁ gamaha, tumha tamuvāyaṁ । daṁsissamahaṁ jēṇaṁ jalaṁjali dēsi pāvāṇaṁ ।। 121||
savahō ya ittha visaē tuha mahataṇaō bhaṇai tō sāvi । maha tuha āṇā saraṇaṁ anivvuī tā na kāyavvā ।।
tō kumarāṇunāē jāi taō udvijaṁ niyayaṭhāṇē | iyarāu puṇō tinnivi niyamiyaparapurisasaṁbhōgā || 123 ||
uvagayasampattaguṇā sammaṁ namiūṇa kumarapayajuyalaṁ । vittuṁ puṇōvi sikkhaṁ kumarāō jati sahāṇē ॥ 124 ॥
bhāi nariṁdō kumaraṁ kaō taē ēsaṇuggahō majjha । aṇurāyaviḍēvaṇānāḍayassa iya daṁsaṇēṇa taō ।। 125 ।।
jāta ētasminna mama pratyayō'sti tava vacanēṣu । bhaṇati kumārō na vāñchitamētattava bhavatīha janmani ॥ 111 ॥
iti kumārasyāsadr̥śaṁ sattvaṁ vacanāni supathanayanāni । tattathā duradhyavasitaṁ cātmanaḥ sā vibhāvayantī ॥ 112 ॥
tathā vairāgyaṁ prāptā bhaṇati yathā praṇamya kumāracaraṇau । bāndhava ! nirlajjayā maryādāvarjitayā mayā ॥113॥
bandhurapi kaniṣṭhatamō mātr̥samānayā pāpabhaginyā । saccaikanidhirāyāsitō'si yattasmāt pāpāt ॥ 114॥
kathaṁ chuṭiṣyāmyahaṁ vatsō jānāti na vyatikaramētam । tava piturahaṁ duhitā sapatnījananyāṁ saṁbhūtā ।। 115 ।।
mūlē nakṣatrē patrōtpādē prēṣitā tataḥ । dhātrībhiḥ parigr̥hītā mātulanr̥papravarasēnasya ॥ 116 ॥
baṅgāladēśapatēstēna tava śvaśurasya dattā'ham । ētasmādvyatikarād gatēṣu pracurēṣu varṣēṣu ॥ 117 ॥
nijakulanabhastalasapūrṇāmr̥ta kiraṇastvaṁ samutpannaḥ । paranārīstvaṁ yō manyasē sarvā bhaginīḥ ॥ 118 ॥
tata iti kalaṅkamalinān prāṇān kēnāpyahaṁ prayōgēṇa । vrajāmi parityaktuṁ jīva mama jīvitēna tvam ॥ 119 ॥
tataḥ kumārō bhaṇatīmāmiti parityaktaistava prāṇaiḥ । bālamaraṇamiti kr̥tvā parivardhatē duḥkhapaṅgiḥ ॥120॥
tataḥ svasthānē gatvā niśāśēṣaṁ gamaya, tava tamupāyam । darśayiṣyāmyahaṁ yēna jalāñjaliṁ dadāsi pāpānām ॥
śapathaścātra viṣayē tava madīyō bhaṇati tataḥ sāpi । mama tava ājñā śaraṇamanirvr̥tistasmānna kartavyā ॥ 122 ॥
tataḥ kumārānujñayā yāti tata utthāya nijasthānē । itarāḥ punastisrō'pi niyamitaparapuruṣa saṁbhōgāḥ ॥ 123॥
. upagata samyaktvaguṇāḥ samyag natvā kumārapādayugalam । gr̥hītvā punarapi śikṣāṁ kumārādyānti svasthānē ॥ 124॥

supāsanāha cariśrasmi-
tā aṇujāṇa jāmō, kumarō caliō samaṁ naridēṇa । mukkō thakkō namiḍaṁ pattō rāyāvi dhavalaharē ।। 126 ।
sō vigōsakicca āhūya samāgaēṇa kumarēṇa । saha kira jā jaṁpissai tā puvyuttara disābhāgē ।। 127|
aiaccanyuyatēya pasaraṁ daṭṭūṇa bhaṇai paḍihāraṁ । kiṁ ēyaṁti taō sō khaṇēṇa nāūṇa vinnavai || 128||
jaha iha kavi muṇidō kēvalanāṇī samōsaḍhō tassa | baṁdaṇahē dēvā urviti tērsi imā dittī || 129 ।
tō kumarēṇa samaṁ ciya rāyā kajjaṁtarāī mōttaṇaṁ । savvāē iḍḍhīē pattō tavvaṁdanimittaṁ ॥ 130 ॥
uvavi vaṁdittā vihīē saha pariyaṇēṇa tō kumarō | dhammassa dāyagaṁ jāṇiūṇa taṁ appaṇō bhagai || 131 |
bhūnihiyajāṇujuyalō bhālayalakayaṁjalī pulaiyaṁgōṁ । jaha vīyarāyapayavi pattēṇavi sāmiṇā majjha ॥ 132॥
garuō kaō pasa.ō jaṁ daṁsiyamappaṇō caraṇakamalaṁ । aha rāyā bhaṇai ahaṁ kumāra ! ēvaṁ puṇō mannē ॥
kāuṁ aṇurahaṁ maha maṇīgukūlēṇa dikkhadāṇēṇa । iya āgamō pahūṇaṁ, bhaṇai muṇidō phuḍaṁ ēyaṁ ।। 134 |
tō parisaṁ uddhati vāriya saha pariyaṇēṇa pavarēṇa । kumaraṁ karēṇa vittuṁ gaṁtu muṇiuggahāu barhi || 135 ॥
mauḍāialaṁkārē appara kumarassa, pariyaṇaṁ bhaṇai । ēsō tumhēṁ rāyā, tassahiō paṇamitaṁ kumaraṁ ।। 136 ।
kēvaliṇī mūlē gives divakhaṁ nivassa bhajjāvi । pucchiya navaṁ nariṁdaṁ niyaduccariyassa suddhikaē ।
paḍivajjai pavvajjaṁ annāuvi kaīvi rāyapattīō । rāyā kēvaliṇaṁ dikkhiē yadi u || 138
muṇināhōvi hu naranāhapajjuvāsijjamāṇakamakamalō । kavi divasāī ṭhāuṁ viharas vivi dēsēsu ।
bhaṇati narēndraḥ kumāraṁ kr̥tasttrayaiṣō'nugrahō mama । anurāgaviḍambanānāṭakasyēti darśanēna tataḥ ॥ 125 ॥
tasmādanujānīhi yāmaḥ, kumāraścalitaḥ samaṁ narēndrēṇa । muktaḥ sthitō natvā prāptō rājāpi dhavalagr̥hē ॥ 126॥
sa vihitaprabhātakr̥tya āhūtasamāgatēna kumārēṇa । saha kila yāvajjalpiṣyati tāvatpūrvōttaradigbhāgē ॥ 127॥
atyatyadbhutatējaḥ prasaraṁ dr̥ṣṭrā bhaṇati pratihāram । kimētaditi tataḥ sa kṣaṇēna jñātvā vijñasyati ॥ 128॥
yathēha kō'pi munīndraḥ kēvalajñānī samavasr̥tastasya । vandanahētōrdēvā upayanti tēṣāmiyaṁ dīptiḥ ॥ 129॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa samamēva rājā kāryāntarāṇi muktatvā । sarvayā r̥ddhayā prāptastadvandananimittam ॥130॥
upaviṣṭō vanditvā vidhinā saha parijanēna tataḥ kumāraḥ । dharmasya dāyakaṁ jñātvā tamātmanō bhaṇati ॥ 131 ॥
bhūnihitajānuyugalō bhālatalakr̥tāñjaliḥ pulakitāṅgaḥ । yathā vītarāgapadavīṁ prāptēnāpi svāminā mama ॥ 132 ॥
guruḥ kr̥taḥ praptādō yad darśitamātmanaścaraṇakamalam । atha rājā bhaṇatyahaṁ kumāra ! ēvaṁ punarmanyē ॥133॥
kartumanugrahaṁ mama manō'nukūlēna dīkṣādānēna । ityāgamaḥ prabhūṇāṁ, bhaṇati munīndraḥ sphuṭamētat ॥ 134 ॥
tataḥ pariṣadmuttiṣṭhantīṁ vārāyatvā saha parijanēna pravarēṇa । kumāraṁ karēṇa gr̥hītvā gatvā munyavagrahād bahiḥ ।। 135॥
mukuṭādyalaṁkārārnapayati kumārāya parijanaṁ bhaṇati । ēṣa yuṣmākaṁ rājā, tatsahitaḥ praṇamya kumāram ॥136॥
kēvalinaḥ padamūlē gr̥hṇāti dīkṣāṁ nr̥pasya bhāryāpi । pr̥ṣṭrā navaṁ narēndraṁ nijaduścaritasya śuddhikr̥tē ॥ 137॥
pratipadyantē pratrajyāmanyā api katyapi rājapatnyaḥ । rājā kēvalinaṁ dīkṣitāṁśca vanditvōttiṣṭhati ॥138॥
munināthō'pi hi naranātha paryupāsyamānakramakamalaḥ । katyapi divasāni sthitvā viharati vividhēṣu dēśēṣu ॥

rāyā ya pālai payaṁ nīīē jiṇamayaṁ prabhāvitō । savvattha kayapamāṇaṁ maṁtisurya kuṇai appamaṁ ॥ 140 ॥
riumaddaṇanaravara pēsiēṇa lēhēṇa jāi sirinilaē । sāraparivārasahiō vimalammi nihittarajjabharō ||
vināyadhammatattō riumadaṇanarakharōvi puttāō । tassappiyarajjabharō vihiṇā paḍivajjaē dikkhaṁ ॥ 142 ॥
rāyā vīrakumārō suciraṁ paripāliūṇa gihidhammaṁ । raṇadhavalarāyarisiṇā payamūlē gahiya pavvajjaṁ ॥
nāṇāvihadēsasarōvarēsu bhaviyāraviṁdavaṇanivahē । paḍivōhiūṇaṁ suciraṁ pattō sūravva nivvāṇaṁ ॥ 144 ॥
iya mayaṇamaḍa phahabhaṁjaṇēṇa saṁjaṇiyajaṇacamakkārō । vīrakumārō pattō kallāṇaparaṁparaṁ paramaṁ ॥ 145 ॥
iha lōēvi agammāgamaṇāinibaṁdhaṇaṁ na pāuṇai । savvajaṇagarahaṇīyattamiha visaē sōviditō ||
jaha imiṇā turiyavayaṁ taruṇēṇavi pāliyaṁ niraiyāraṁ । taha anēṇavi ēyaṁ pālēyavvaṁ payatē ॥ 147 ॥
॥ iti caturthatratē vīrakumāradr̥ṣṭāntaḥ samāptaḥ !!
rājā ca pālayati prajāṁ nītyā jinamataṁ prabhāvayan । sarvatra kr̥tapramāṇaṁ mantrisutaṁ karōtyātmasamam ॥ 140 ॥
ripumardananaravaraprēṣitēna lēkhēna yāti śrīnilayē । sāraparivārasahitō vimalē nihitarājyabharaḥ ॥ 141 ॥
vijñātadharmatattvō ripumardananaravarō'pi putrāt । tasmā arpitarājyabharō vidhinā pratipadyatē dīkṣām ॥142॥
rājā vīrakumāraḥ suciraṁ paripālya gr̥hidharmam । raṇadhavalarājarṣēḥ padamūlē gr̥hītvā pratrayām ॥143॥
nānāvidhadēśasarōvarēṣu bhavyāravindavananivahān । pratibōdhya suciraṁ prāptaḥ sūra iva nirvāṇam ॥144॥
iti madana garvabhañjanēna saṁjanitajana camatkāraḥ । vīrakumāraḥ prāptaḥ kalyāṇaparamparāṁ paramām ॥ 145 ॥
iha lōkē'pyagamyāgamanādinibandhanaṁ na prāpnōti । sarvajana garhaṇīyatvamiha viṣayē sō'pi dr̥ṣṭāntaḥ ॥ 146 ॥
yathānēna turyatrataṁ taruṇēnāpi pālitaṁ niraticāram । tathā'nyēnāpyētat pālayitavyaṁ prayatnēna ॥ 147॥

davvēṇa appakālē gahiyā vēsāvi hōi paradāraṁ । tassaṁgamāyaraṁtō vairō iva lahai dukhāī ॥ | 1 ||
tathāhi ;-
dharaṇīramaṇī tilayaṁ tilayapuraṁ nāma puramiha pasiddhaṁ । dariyāridappadalō rāyā sōmaō tattha || 2 ||
tassatthi piyā sujasā jasadhavalō nāma tattha purasiṭṭhī । tabbhajjā jayadēvī tāṇaṁ puttō vairanāmā ||3|
sō ya vilāsī dutaiṁdiō mittarvidapariyariō । surabhavaṇakāṇaṇāisu viyarai niyayāē icchā || 4 |
aha annayā kayāī paccūsē ṇammayānaītīrē । piuṇā saha saṁpattī baharō bhavivyāvasaō ||5||
kasōyasamāyārā jāva ṭhiyā tāva uttaradisāō । pajjaliyajalaṇajālōlibhāsurō ēi tattha surō || 6 |
taṁ taṁ daṇaṁ khuddhā tē dōtri, bhaṇai tō dēvō । mā bhāyaha bhō bhaddā ! tumha hi ahaṁ ēmi ||7||
tumhē puvvabhavē maha huṁtā iṭṭhā taō ihaṁ dayuṁ । appā payāsiō mē tā nisuṇaha puvvabhavacariyaṁ ||8||
ahamittha purē ubhāriyā āsi dēvaī nāma । tumhāvāsasamīvē amhāvāsōvi āsi tayā || 9 ||
sōmayanivasēvī mahabhattā, annayā ya patyāṇē । nammayanaīē tīrē ṭhiō nariṁdō saparivārō || 10 ||
majjha paī maē saha naīē tīrē vaḍassa hiṭṭammi | cihna dinnāvāsō annayaṇō kōvi katyavi ।। 11
tō haṁ naimōinnā jalāvagāhatyamāyavōvahayā । tō taṁtujaṁtuṇā mē baddhā caraṇā, ruyaṁtī ॥ 12 ॥
dhāhāviyaṁ maē tō uccuccayarēṇa karuṇasadēṇa । kōvi na caliō ṭhāṇā tahāvi mē pōkaraṁtīē ॥13॥
tō kēṇāvi hu bhaṇiyaṁ dhīrā hōtutti pavisiya naīē । jamajīhasacchahāē churiyāē jhaḍati sō chinnō |
,
dravyēṇāpakālaṁ gr̥hītā vēśyāpi bhavati paradārāḥ । tatsaṅgamācaran vajra iva labhatē duḥkhāni ॥ 1॥
dharaṇīramaṇītilakaṁ tilakapuraṁ nāma puramiha prasiddham । dr̥ptāridarpadalanō rājā sōmadhvajastatra || 2 ||
tasyāsti priyā suyaśā yaśōdhavalō nāma tatra puraśrēṣṭhī । tadbhāryā jayadēvī tayōḥ putrō vajranāmā ||3||
sa ca vilāsī durdāntēndriyō bhittravr̥ndaparikaritaḥ । surabhavanakānanādiṣu vicarati nijayēcchayā || 4 |
athānyadā kadācitpratyūṣē narmadānadītīrē । pitrā saha saṁprāptō vajrō bhavitavyatāvaśataḥ ||5||
kr̥taśaucasamācārau yāvatsthitau tāvaduttaradiśaḥ । prajvalitajvalanajvālālībhāsura ēti tatra suraḥ || 6 ||
tamāyantaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā kṣubdhau tau dvāvapi, bhaṇati tatō dēvaḥ । mā bhaiṣṭaṁ bhō bhadrau ! yuvayōrhitārthamahamēmi ॥ 7 ॥
yuvāṁ pūrvabhavē mamābhavatāmiṣṭō tata iha dr̥ṣṭā । ātmā prakāśitō mayā tasmāt śr̥ṇutaṁ pūrvabhavacaritam ॥8॥
ahamatra purē rāṣṭrakūṭabhāryā''saṁ dēvakī nāma । yuṣmadāvāsasamīpē'smadāvā sō'pyāsīt tadā ॥9॥
sōmadhvajanr̥pasēvī mama bhartā, anyadā ca prasthānē । narmadānadyāstīrē sthitō narēndraḥ saparivāraḥ ॥ 10 ॥
mama patirapi mayā saha nadyāstīrē vaṭasyādhaḥ । tiṣṭhati dattāvāsō'nyajanaḥ kō'pi kvāpi ca ॥11॥
tatō'haṁ nadīmavatīrṇā jalāvagāhārthamātapōpahatā । tatastantujantunā mē vaddhau caraṇau, rudatyā ॥ 12॥
āraṭitaṁ mayā tata uccōccatarēṇa karuṇaśabdēna । kō'pi na calitaḥ sthānāttathāpi mayi pr̥tkurvatyām ॥ 13॥
tataḥ kēnāpi hi bhaṇitaṁ vīrā bhavēti praviśya nadyām । yamajihvāsadr̥śyā kṣurikayā jhaṭiti sa chinnaḥ || 14 |
