chidaṁtassa ya taṁ tassa ūsuyattēṇa salilamajjhammi । uyarappavichuriyāē nīṇiō atapabbhārō || 15 |
tō maha bāhāē sō laggēuṁ niggaō maō jhatti । tō tassa baṁdhavērhi tatthēva ciyā lahu raiyā ||16||
ahama naīē gaṁtu majjaṇayaṁ kāumāgayā tattha । kira tacciyāē jhapaṁ dāhaṁ tō bhēttuṇā ghariyā || 17||
bāhāē ahaṁ tattō maē sa bhaṇiō jahā pavisiyavvaṁ । imiṇā samaṁ ciyāē nikāraṇabaṁdhuṇā nū ॥ 18 ॥
maha pukāraṁtīē ṭhāṇāōvi na caliō si taṁ taiyā । annaṇavi lōga uvēhiyāē sa puṇa turiyē ॥ 19 ॥
taha kariya sōuṁ jhatti paviṭṭhō jalassa majjhammi । mahapāṇarakkhaṇḍī taṇaṁva niyajīviyaṁ cattaṁ ॥ 20 ॥
tā iya ēyammi maē nāhaṁ jīvāmi ca bāhāō । sō bhai maē na suō varataṇu ! sadō tathā tujjha ||
annaha kahē vikkha pāṇasamāē karēmi tujjha ahaṁ । tō bhaṇiō ēsa maē ēvamimaṁ kiṁtu majjha kaē || 22||
pāṇā ēyassa gayā tō hamavassaṁ ciyāē ēyassa | pavisissaṁ tā muṁcasu khamasu ya jaṁ kiṁpi avaraṁ ||23||
jaivi na muṁcasi tahavi hu jaha taha pāṇē ahaṁ cahassāmi । tō mukkā tēṇa ahaṁ ciyaṁ paviṭṭā ya daḍḍhā ya ॥
avasāō sō imō tuha suō samuppannō । jāyā ya ahaṁ dēvō vaṁtarajāīṇa majjhami ||25||
isa paḍibaṁṇa maē tumhāṇaṁ dēsiyaṁ niyasarūvaṁ । ihiṁ vairābhimuhaṁ paḍiuvayārassa bhāvēṇa ||26||
pabhaṇēmi kiṁci jai majjha patthaṇaṁ niṣphalaṁ na ya karēsi । tō bhaṇiyaṁ vairēṇa bhaṇēhi taṁ jamihamaha uciyaṁ ॥
tā bhaṇiyaṁ dēvēṇa naīē parakūlalavalilayaharaē । cira muṇī mahatvā taṁ vaṁdaha dōvi bhattī ||28||
chindataśca taṁ tasyōtsukatvēna salilamadhyē | udarapraviṣṭakṣurikayā natō'ntraprāgbhāraḥ ॥ 15॥
tatō mama bāhau sa lagatvā nirgatō mr̥tō jhaṭiti । tatastasya bāndhavaistatraiva citā laghu racitā ॥ 16 ॥
ahamapi nadyāṁ gatvā majjanaṁ kr̥tvā''gatā tatra । kila taccitāyāṁ jhampāṁ dāsyē tatō bhatrī dhr̥tā ॥ 17 ॥
bāhunā'ham, tatō mayā sa bhaṇitō yathā pravēṣṭavyam । anēna samaṁ citāyāṁ niṣkāraṇabandhunā nūnam ॥18॥
mayi pūtkurvatyāṁ sthānādapi na calitō'si tvaṁ tadā । anyēnāpi lōkēnōpēkṣitāyāṁ sa punastvaritam ॥19॥
tathā pūtkr̥taṁ śrutvā jhaṭiti praviṣṭō jalasya madhyē | matprāṇarakṣaṇārthaṁ tr̥ṇamiva nijajīvitaṁ tyaktam ॥20॥
tasmādityētasminmr̥tē nāhaṁ jīvāmi muñca bāhutaḥ । sa bhaṇati mayā na śrutō varatanu ! śabdastadā tava ॥ 21 ॥
anyathā kathamupēkṣāṁ prāṇasamāyāḥ karōmi tavāham । tatō bhaṇita ēṣa mayaivamidaṁ kintu mama kr̥tē ॥22॥
prāṇā ētasya gatāstatō'hamavaśyaṁ citāyāmētasya । pravēkṣyāmi tasmānmuñca kṣamasva ca yatkimapyaparāddham ॥
yadyapi na muñcasi tathāpi hi yathā tathā prāṇānahaṁ tyakṣyāmi । tatō muktā tēnāhaṁ citāṁ praviṣṭā ca dagdhā ca ॥
adhyavasāyaviśēṣātsō'yaṁ tava sutaḥ samutpannaḥ । jātā cāhaṁ dēvō vyantarajātīnāṁ madhyē ||25||
iti pratibandhēna mayā yuvayōrdarśitaṁ nijasvarūpam । idānīṁ vajrābhimukhaṁ pratyupakārasya bhāvēna ||26||
pramaṇāmi kiñcidyadi mama prārthanāṁ niṣphalāṁ na ca karōṣi । tatō bhaṇitaṁ vajrēṇa bhaṇa tvaṁ yadiha mamōcitam ॥
tadā bhaṇitaṁ dēvēna nadyāḥ parakūlalavalīlatāgr̥hē । tiṣṭhati munirmahātmā taṁ vandēthāṁ dvāvapi bhaktyā ॥28॥

tēhivi taha caiva kayaṁ paḍivannāī aṇuvvayāī tahā । sampattabhūsiyāī dōhivi sāhussa payamūlē ||29||
tō tuṭṭhō sō dēvō pabhaṇai gurubaṁdhavā tumē majjha । jēṇa maēvi imāō muṇiṇō sammattamaṇupattaṁ ||30||
sāhammiyavacchallē ēsa maṇī ciṁtiyatthasaṁjaṇaṇō । tumhēṁ maē viinnō iya taṁ ayi gaō dēvō ॥ 31॥
tattō tē gihidhammaṁ kuṇati nisuṇaṁti sāhupāsamma । kiṁtu tahāvi na vairō vēsāgamaṇa paricaya ||32||
ēkāṇa dēi bhāḍi annāhiṁ samaṁ ramēi rayaṇīē । ēvaṁ ca aliyasiṁgāravinaḍiō gamēi rayaṇīō ||33||
citāmaṇiṣpabhāvā saṁpajjai tassa daviṇamaipauraṁ । taṁ vivvai jiṇabhavaṇē biṁbē saṁghammi sāsu || 34 ||
annāō gahiyabhāḍipi jāṇiuṁ nēya pariharai ēsō । tō pāyaṁ paidiyahaṁ saha lōēṇaṁ havai kalahō ||35||
taṁ sōuṁ tassa piyā vārai rē paravina bhāḍīsuṁ । vēsāsuṁ gacchaṁtō sutikkhadukkhāī pāvihisi ||36||
kiṁca |
aiyāramiṇaṁ turiyavvayassa mā kuṇasu sarasu muṇivayaṇaṁ । ihaparalōyaviruddhaṁ suyaṇanisiddhaṁ ca jēṇa imaṁ ।
savvāsuvi vēsā hōi pavittī aṇatthapatthārī । jāu paragahiyabhāḍīu tāu purṇa kālakūḍasamā ||38|
tō varēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ tahapi na sakkēmi tāya ! parihariṁ । ittariya saṁgamēyaṁ jaha taṁ vārēsi sayavāraṁ ॥ 39 ॥
tō jasadhavō siṭṭhī para jai tujjha nicchaō ēsa । paḍivajjissamahaṁ tā puttaya ! pavvajjamajjēva ||40|
jaō ।
bhuttā bhōgā suiraṁ jahicchiyaṁ vilāsiyā tahā lacchī । ānaṁdiyā ya suyaṇā mittā baṁdhū ya vihurā ya ।
tābhyāmapi tathaiva kr̥taṁ pratipannānyaṇutratāni tathā । samyaktvabhūṣitāni dvābhyāmapi sādhōḥ padamūlē ||29॥
tatastuṣṭaḥ sa dēvaḥ prabhaṇati gurubāndhavā yuvāṁ mama । yēna mayāpyasmānmunēḥ samyaktvamanuprāptam ||30||
sādharmikavātsalya ēṣa maṇiścintitārthasaṁjananaḥ । yuvābhyāṁ mayā vitīrṇa iti tamarpayitvā gatō dēvaḥ ॥ 31 ॥
tatastau gr̥hidharmaṁ kurutaḥ śr̥ṇutaḥ sādhupārśvē । kintu tathāpi na vajrō vēśyāgamanaṁ parityajati ||32||
ēkābhyō dadāti bhāṭimanyābhiḥ samaṁ ramatē rajanyām । ēvaṁ cālīkaśr̥ṅgāravinaṭitō gamayati rajanīḥ ||33||
cintāmaṇiprabhāvātsaṁpadyatē tasya draviṇamatipracuram । tad vyayatē jinabhavanē bimbē saṁtrē vēśyāsu || 34 ॥
anyasmād gr̥hītabhāṭimapi jñātvā naiva pariharatyēṣaḥ । tataḥ prāyaḥ pratidivasa saha lōkēna bhavati kalahaḥ ||
tat śrutvā tasya pitā vārayati rē paravitīrṇabhāṭiṣu । vēśyāsu gacchan sutīkṣṇaduḥkhāni prāpsyasi ||36|
aticāramimaṁ turyavratasya mā kuru smara munivacanam । ihaparalōkaviruddhaṁ sujana niṣiddhaṁ ca yēnēdam ||37||
sarvāsvapi vēśyāsu bhavati pravr̥ttiranarthaprastaraḥ । yā gr̥hītaparabhāṭyastāḥ punaḥ kālakūṭasamāḥ ॥38॥
tatō vajrēṇa bhaṇitaṁ tathāpi na śaknōmi tāta ! parihartum । itvarīsaṅgamētaṁ yadi tvaṁ vārayasi śatavāram ||

varakahā ।
pariṇayavaō ya saṁpai āsannō vaccha ! maraṇasamaōvi । kāuṁ paralōyahiyaṁ pattō tā avasarō majjha ॥
iya bhaṇiuṁ niyadavvaṁ dāuṁ ṭhāṇēsu bhāvaṇāpuvvaṁ । paḍivannō sō siṭṭhī vayaṁ vihāṇēṇa gurumūlē ||43||
nimmajjāō jāō jaṇayavimukō visēsaō vairō | aha annayā paviṭṭhō vasaṁtasēṇāē gēhammi ||44 ||
kumarakkhaṇiyāē vilāsiṇīē dāūṇa icchiyaṁ bhāḍiṁ । rayaṇīē paḍhamapaharē tappallukammi ubaviṭṭō ||45 ॥
jā ci tā diṭṭhō sahasā tatthāgaraṇa kumarēṇa । sō gahiō nāsatō tēṇaṁ sayamēva bāhāē || 46 ॥
baddhō thaṁbhēṇa samaṁ paccūsē kuṭṭiṇīē kumarāō । kicchēṇa mōiō tō saṁpattō niyayagēhami ||47 ||
sukumāradēhabhāvā bhariō sō lōhiyassa tō mariḍaṁ । aṭṭajjhāṇōvagaō saṁjāō gaḍaō || 48 ||
kaivayabhatragahaṇāī bhamiḍaṁ puṇaravi subōhijōgēṇa । lahihī siddhiṁ vairō siṭṭhī puṇa caiva tami bhavē ||
utthanvayaaīyāraṁ vēsāvasaṇaṁ caēha bhō bhavvā ! । jēma suhasiddhidvāṇaṁ lahēhamacirēṇa jiṇabhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 50 ॥
॥ iti caturthavrataprathamāticāravipākē vajrakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
pariṇatavayāśca saṁpratyāsannō vatsa ! maraṇasamayō'pi । kartuṁ paralōkahitaṁ prāptastasmādavasarō mama ॥42॥
iti bhaṇitvā nijadravyaṁ dattvā sthānēṣu bhāvanāpūrvam । pratipannaḥ sa śrēṣṭhī vrataṁ vidhānē gurumūlē ॥43॥
nirmaryādō jātō janakavimuktō viśēṣatō vajraḥ । athānyadā praviṣṭō vasantasēnāyā gēhē ॥ 44 ॥
kumārarakṣitāyai vilāsinyai dattvēpsitāṁ bhāṭim । rajanēḥ prathamapraharē tatpalyaṅka upaviṣṭaḥ ॥ 45 ॥
yāvattiṣṭhati tāvad dr̥ṣṭaḥ sahasā tatrāgatēna kumārēṇa । sa gr̥hītō naśyaṁstēna svayamēva bāhunā ॥ 46 ॥
baddhaḥ stambhēna samaṁ pratyūṣē kuṭṭinyā kumārāt । kr̥cchrēṇa mōcitastataḥ saṁprāptō nijagēhē ॥47॥
sukumāradēhabhāvād bhr̥taḥ sa lōhitēna tatō mr̥tvā । ārtadhyānōpagataḥ saṁjātō gartaśūkaraḥ ॥ 48 ॥
katipayabhavagrahaṇāni bhrāntvā punarapi suvōdhiyōgēna । lapsyatē siddhi vajraḥ śrēṣṭhī punarēva tasmin bhavē ॥49॥

kulaṭā'nāthavidhavāḥ paradārā naivēti vikalpya । tā yaḥ parimuṅktē durlabha iva sa duḥkhaṁ labhatē ॥ 1 ॥
puramasti vijayakhēṭaṁ kr̥tāvahēlaṁ purāṇāṁ pracurāṇām । tatrāsti prakr̥tibhadrō gaubhadrō nāma vaṇik ॥2॥
malayamatī tadbhāryā durlabhō nāmnā'sti tayōḥ sutaḥ । vaṇikkalānāṁ nidhānaṁ kulabhavanaṁ tathā'narthānām ॥3॥
athānyadā pravr̥ttau pitāputrau dvāvapi vāṇijyakāryēṇa । ujjayinīṁ prati gantuṁ grahītvōcitabhāṇḍāni ॥ 4 ॥
gacchadbhayāṁ dr̥ṣṭō'rdhapathē dhyānasaṁsthitaḥ sādhuḥ । taṁ vanditvōpaviṣṭau dhyānāntē sō'pi prabhaṇati ||5 ॥
kva gamiṣyathaḥ kāryēṇa kēna kutaḥ samāgatāvatra । tābhyāmapi sarvaṁ kathitaṁ yathādr̥ṣṭaṁ tatō munirbhaṇati ॥ 6 ॥
ardhavidagdhaṁ hiṇḍatē sarvō'pi janō dhanārthamudyuktaḥ । tatkāraṇadharma prati nirudyamaḥ sarvakālamapi ||7||
dharmēṇa vinā manōvāñchitāni yadi bhavēyuḥ kathamapyēvamēva । tadā tribhuvanē'pi sakalē na kō'pīha duḥkhitō bhavēt ।
sarvamapi ca saṁpadyatē manaīpsitaṁ niścitaṁ sapuṇyānām । yathā saṁprāptaṁ guṇasundaryā janakēna tyaktayā ॥9॥
bhaddilapuraprabhvarikēsariṇō dēvyāḥ kanakamālāyāḥ । pravarakalā kulabhavanaṁ tanayā guṇasundarī nāma ||10||

mama duṣpitustanayā vatsē ! guṇasundarīti nāma tvam । bhōjanakālē vatsā dr̥ṣṭāpi mayā na vijñātā ॥47॥

tathaiva kr̥tē tayā''hūtē tathā ca puṇyapālē । paripr̥ṣṭavibhavavārtō rājā guṇasundarīṁ bhaṇati ॥ 49 ॥
dr̥ṣṭāntēna vatsāyā ēva mama pariṇatamidaṁ tāvat । yathā vibhavō dharmaphalaṁ dharma punaḥ kathayatu mē vatsā ॥ 50 ॥
sā punaḥ kulakamēṇa jananyā śrāvikayā jinadharmē । bālatvē'pi ca nipuṇā''sītkr̥tā tathāpīti bhagati ॥51॥
ihāvāsāsannē'sti muniḥ sa viśēṣatō dharmam । jānāti parikathayati ca tatō rājā yāti tatraiva ॥ 52॥
saha puṇyapālaguṇasundarībhyāmākarṇya tatō dharmam । bhaṇati munīndraṁ rājā kr̥tvā rājyasthitiṁ susthām ||53॥
ahamanusarāmīdānīṁ tava caraṇau tatō bhaṇati munipravaraḥ । naranātha ! atrārthē nirudyamairna bhavitavyam ॥54॥
tatō rājā dhavalagr̥hē gatvā saha mantrayitā pradhānaiḥ । putrābhāvē sthāpayitvā tamēva jāmātaraṁ rājyē ॥55॥

tumha ||58 ॥
vihiṇā froes dikkha paripālai punnapālanaranāhō । nīīē ciraṁ rajjaṁ jiṇidadhammaṁ prabhāvitō ॥56॥

tō tē bhagati amhē asamatthā nāha ! sāhudhammassa | tō himacayaṁtāṇaṁ jō dhammō, kahaha taṁ amha || 59 ॥
tattō sammattāī gihidhammō tēṇa tāṇa vittharaō । kahiō tēhivi gahiō vārasabhēōvi sō vihiṇā ||

jaṇaō pālai sammaṁ dulahō puṇa dullahaṁpi taṁ ladhuṁ । aiyarai cautthavayaṁ ēvaṁ parikapaṇaṁ kāuṁ ॥ 62 ॥
paradārē maha niyamō na vajjiyavvā aṇāhakulaḍāō । vihavakulaḍaṁ ramatō aha diṭṭō sō talārēṇa ॥ 63॥
ḍaṁgāē jajjariu baddhō, millāviō ya dāūṇa । daṁḍaṁ piuṇā ēvaṁ baddhō mukkō ya sō bahuhā ॥ 64 ॥
tahavi na virama dulahō aṇāhakulaḍāē saṁgamē tattō । kālakkhariō piuṇā sakai na niyatti tahavi ।

guṇasundaryāstanayaṁ sulōcanaṁ sthāpayitvā rājyē । lāti saha tayā dīkṣāṁ kramēṇa prāpnōti tathā mōkṣam ||17|

yaṣṭyā jarjarayitvā baddhaḥ, mōcitaśca dattvā । daṇḍaṁ pitraivaṁ baddhō muktaśca sa bahudhā ॥ 64 ॥

aparigahiyāgamaṇa ēvaṁ dukkhāṇa kāraṇaṁ sammaṁ । cattaparadārasaṁgā parivajjaha bhō ! payatēṇa || 70 ||

gayarāyajaṇiyasōhaṁ sōhammana fagesakinna । vikramapuraṁ pasiddhaṁ taṁ pāla vikamanariṁdō ||2||

daṇaṁ taṁ vaṇiyā pucchati kuṭuṁbiyaṁ kimēsa muṇī । nāsagganisiyadiṭṭhī cikaṭuṁba niścihō ? || 7 ||
kōṇi bhaṇiyaṁ iha citassa māsamavi hōhī । na suyai ēsō na ya bhuṁjara ya ēmēva ciṭṭhē ॥8॥
tō tē tēṇa samēyā gaṁtūṇa muṇiṁ namitta pucchaṁti । kō hēū vayagahaṇē paḍhamava vaṭṭamāṇassa ? || 9 ||
tō bhai muṇī nisuṇaha saṁsārāō na annaō hēū । navaraṁ maha vayagahaṇē visēsaō kāraṇaṁ bhajjā ॥ 10 ॥

iha atthi suhāvāsaṁ nayaraṁ riumadaṇō tahi rāyā । maṁtī visālabuddhī bhajjā raīsuṁdarī tassa || 12॥

kīrīē tō bhaṇiō huṁ pajjattaṁ khu tujjha saṁgēṇa । gacchasu tīivi nīḍē mā niyaḍīhōsu maṁ rami || 16 |

I
annāsa pēmmaṁ pāvammi maī aṇujjamō dhammē । mā dijja divtra ! kahavi hu jai ruṭṭō hōsi sayavāraṁ ||17|
tō kīrēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ khamasu piē! majjha ēyamavarāhaṁ । tō kīrīē bhaṇiyaṁ mā mahamuhasamuha hō ||18 ॥
ēkaṁ tā ucchiṣṭaṁ vāyasaviṭṭhāliyaṁ ca sarvisa ca । kō bhuṁjēi sayannō annāsataṁ jahava annaṁ ? || 19॥
tō vāyāḍō pabhaṇai jai ēvaṁ maṁ caēsi tā puttaṁ । gahiūṇa gamissāmi sā pabhaṇai nēya appaimi ||20|
iya jāō saṁvāō tēsiṁ puttassa kāraṇē garuō । tō kīrēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ rāyasamīvē samāgaccha ||21||
jassappihī nariṁdō puttaṁ, tassēva hōhihī ittha । suīvi bhaṇai ēvaṁ gayāī dōnivi nivasayā ||22||
kahiō niyattatō tēhi, tō pabhaṇiyaṁ nariṁdēṇa । nīivayaṇaṁ vibhāvivi nisuha ēgaggacittāī || 23
putō tāyassa bhavē dhūyā jaṇaṇīē, ahava dhūyāvi । piuṇō bhavēi jamhā vīyaṁ vīyattissēva || 24||

ihāsti śubhāvāsaṁ nagaraṁ ripumardanastatra rājā । mantrī viśālabuddhirbhāryā ratisundarī tasya ॥ 12 ॥

jātaśca sutastaṁ ca pālayataḥ parasparaṁ, atha kadācit । parakīryāsaktō jātaḥ kīraḥ kathamapi jñātaḥ ||15|
karyā tatō bhaṇitō hūṁ paryāptaṁ khalu tava saṅgēna । gaccha tasyā ēva nīḍē mā nikaṭībhava māṁ ramayitum ॥ 16

iti jātaḥ saṁvādastayōḥ putrasya kāraṇē guruḥ । tataḥ kīrēṇa bhaṇitaṁ rājasamīpē samāgaccha ॥21॥

akṣarapaṅktiṁ dr̥ṣṭrā pūrvōktāṁ jātajātismaraṇā sā । jānāti kīrabhavaṁ taṁ savyatikaraṁ tata idaṁ jānāti ||
ētasya prabhāvēṇa jinasya jātāhaṁ sacivagēhē । tataḥ pratidinamapi pūjayati vandatē bhaktyā taṁ dēvam ॥ 36 ॥
sacivasya gr̥hē tiṣṭhati pradhānaturagō, nr̥pasya turagīṇām । tēna ca jātā bahavasturaṁgamā mantrigēhāt ॥37॥
ānāyayati tān rājā, bhuvanānandā na dadātyarpayitum । mattātakiśōrēṇa jātāḥ sarvē yata ētē ||38॥
tasmāttātasyēmē khalu bhavanti nō narapatēryēna purā । kīramithunasya jātē putravivādē iṁdaṁ likhitam || 39॥

supāsanāha-bariyammi-
tā taṁ tava daṭuṁ nāyā sā bālapaṁḍiyā rannā । sacivāu maggiūṇaṁ pariṇīyā tō imaṁ bhaṇiyā ||41 ||
apaṁḍiyā si vālē ! āgaṁtavvaṁ na tāva maha mēhē । jāva na jāō puttō savyuttamaguṇagaṇōvēō || 42 ॥
disa bhaṇiyaṁ piyayama ! puttē jāē avassa tuha gēhē । āgaṁtavvaṁ khu maē tahā painnaṁ imaṁ suṇasu || 43॥
jaṛa saccakōviā hūṁ tō tuha hatthāu sōyaissāmi । niacaraṇē, taha taṁ nipāṇahiyāuvi vāhissē ||
iya ētē bhaṇijaṁ gayā ya niyapi himmi sā bālā । piuṇō taṁ vr̥ttaṁtaṁ sāhai savvaṁpi gatē ||45॥
tō sacivō bhai kahaṁ vacchē ! aidugbaḍaṁ imaṁ ghaḍiyē ? | sā bhai tāya ! picchatru na dugdhaḍaṁ kiṁpi buddhīē ।
sacivēnōktam ;
visamā khalu kajjagaī naya sā dāṇēṇa nēya buddhīē । naya pōrisēṇa sijjhai ēkaṁ divvaṁ pamōttr̥̄ṇa ॥ 47
tō bhaṇiyaṁ bālāē ēvaṁ ciya ittha natthi saṁdēhō । buddhīvi kampravasāō jāyai jīvāṇa kila kajjē ॥
ki bahuṇā tāya ! tumaṁ nivassa gēhāu pacchimē bhāgē । siririsahasāmibhavaṇaṁ himagirisiharaṁ va nimmavasu ॥
tammivitikālapicchaṇaya ucchavō jaha havēi taha kuṇasu । majjhavi siṁha vihijjau vilāsiṇībhavaṇamajjhampi
kāōvi phārasiṁgārasāraaisarasagīya kusalāō । kāōvi bharahavarahāvabhāvaniraṇāu naṭṭammi ॥ 51 ॥
annāu vēṇuvīṇāmuiṁgapaḍupaḍa havāyaṇapavīṇā । kāyavvāō tāō bēsāucciya na uṇa purisā ॥ 52 ॥
tīē jaṁ jaha bhaṇiyaṁ taṁ taha sacivēṇa kāriyaṁ savvaṁ । yāvadiṇāṇaṁ majjhē sayamavi sā tattha nacēi || 53 |
aha annayā nariṁdō parigaliyanisāra nisuṇaē gīyaṁ । purisuttamāṇa tāṇaṁ jiṇāṇa siririmahamāīṇa ||
śrīkaraṇīyavahikāyāṁ 'bījaṁ vapturbhavati' iti । tatō vismitēna rājñā sā vahikā vācitā yāvat ॥40॥
tāvat tattathaiva dr̥ṣṭrā jñātā sā bālapaṇḍitā rājñā । sacivāda mārgayitvā pariṇītā tata idaṁ bhaṇitā ॥ 41 ॥
atiṇḍitā'si bālē ! āgantavyaṁ na tāvad mama gēhē । yāvatra jātaḥ putraḥ sarvōttamaguṇagaṇōpētaḥ ॥ 42 ॥
tathāpi bhaṇitaṁ priyatama ! putrē jātē'vaśyaṁ tava gēhē । āgantavyaṁ khalu mayā tathā pratijñāmimāṁ śr̥ṇu ॥ 43 ॥
yadi satyakōvidāhaṁ latastava hastācchōcayiṣyāmi । nijacaraṇau, tathā tvāṁ nijōpānahāvapi vāhayiṣyāmi ।।
ityēkāntē bhaṇitvā gatā ca nijapitr̥gr̥hē sā bālā । pitustaṁ vr̥ttāntaṁ kathayati sarvamapyēkāntē ॥45॥
tataḥ sacivō bhaṇati kathaṁ vatsē ! atidurghaṭamidaṁ ghaṭitam ? । sā bhaṇati tāta ! paśya na durghaṭaṁ kimapi buddhēḥ ।।
viṣamā khalu kāryagatirnaca sā dānēna naiva buddhayā । naca pauruṣēṇa sidhyatyēkaṁ daivaṁ pramucya ||47 ||
tatō bhaṇitaṁ bālayaivamēvātra nāsti saṁdēha: । buddhirapi karmavaśājjāyatē jīvānāṁ kila kāryē ॥ 48 ॥
kiṁ
bahunā tāta ! tvaṁ nr̥pasya gēhāt paścimē bhāgē । śrīr̥ṣabhasvābhibhavanaṁ himagiriśikharāmiva nirmāya ॥ 49
tasminnapi trikālaprēkṣaṇakōtsavō yathā bhavati tathā kuru । mamāpi gr̥haṁ vidhīyatāṁ vilāsinībhavanamadhyē ॥50॥
kā api sphāraśr̥ṅgārasārātisara saṁgīta kuśalāḥ । kā api bharatavarahāvabhāvanipuṇā nāṭyē ॥ 51 ॥
anyā vēṇuvīṇāmr̥daṅgapaṭupaṭahavādanapravīṇāḥ । kartavyāstā vēśyā ēva na punaḥ puruṣāḥ ॥ 52॥
tayā yadyathā bhaṇitaṁ tattathā sacivēna kāritaṁ sarvam । stōkadinānāṁ madhyē, svayamapi sā tatra nr̥tyati ॥53

tō pacchimadārēṇa viṇiggaō āgaō ya jiṇabhavaṇē । picchā acchīṇachaṇaṁ accharamaiyaṁva picchaṇayaṁ ॥
vādā sayamēva naccaē navanavēhiṁ pāḍhēhiṁ । akkhittō tō rāyā kayavaṁḍavisivattha ||26||
tō vittē picchaṇaē suhāsaṇēṇaṁ gayā sabhavaṇammi । rāyāvi tīē sarisō suttō rayaṇīē tatthēva ॥ 57 ॥
ēvaṁ paidiyahaṁ ci picchaṇayaṁ picchaē taha gimmi । tīi samaṁ saṁvasaī jaṁ jaṁpai sō tarhi taṁ sā ॥ 58 ॥
niyajaṇayassa kahāvai sōvi hu bahiyāē lihai taṁ savvaṁ । annadiṇē jaṁpāṇē pāṇahiē muttumārūḍhā ॥59॥
bhaṇiō rāyā tīē maha vāhaṇavāhiṇī ihaṁ natthi । tā taṁ ciya vahasu imē tahatti tēṇāvi niyasirasā ||
āṇīyāō tāō suttō tatthēva addharattammi । sā tayabhimuhaṁ para maha pāyā ajja ujjhati ॥ 61 ॥
tā uvēhi dāsi caraṇē talahaṭṭaē khaṇaṁ ēkaṁ । maha ēṛa jēṇa nidā tō sō talahaṭṭai sayapi ॥ 62||
tī nivāriōvi hu, aha suhasuttā pulōyaē sāvi । sumiṇammi punnacaṁdaṁ pavisaṁtaṁ niyayavayaṇammi ||
taṁ pāsi viddhā talahaṅkr̥taṁ niēvi taṁ caraṇē । tō sahasā uṭṭhēuṁ miralāviya kahai sē sumiṇaṁ ॥ 64 ॥
rannā bhaṇiyaṁ payacchi ! nicchiyaṁ tuha barō suō hōhī । jā tā vihāvarīviramasūyagō vajjiō saṁkhō ||
ittō uvi rāyā vaca gēhammi sāvi sajjhāyaṁ । kuṇamāṇī tātra ṭhiyā jā uiō diṇamaṇī tattō ॥
piugēhē saṁpattā dāraṁ pihiūṇa tassa gēhassa । pacchannaṭhiyā ciṭṭhai kahiḍaṁ piṇō syaṇicariyaṁ ||67 ||
tadivasabhavaṁ garbha paripāṭhai sā suhēṇa piugēhē । tō rāyā tīē gihē tahēva bīē diṇammi gaō ॥ 68 ॥
athānyadā narēndraḥ parigalitaniśāyāṁ śr̥ṇōti gītam । puruṣōttamānāṁ tēṣāṁ jinānāṁ śrī r̥ṣabhādīnām ॥ 54 ॥
tataḥ paścimadvārēṇa vinirgata āgataśca jinabhavanē । paśyatyakṣīṇakṣaṇamapsarōmayamiva prēkṣaṇakam ||15||
bhuvanānandā svayamēva nr̥tyati navanavaiḥ pāṭhaḥ । ākṣiptastatō rājā kr̥tagaṇḍaviśiṣṭa nēpathyaḥ ॥ 56 ॥
tatō vr̥ttē prēkṣaṇakē sukhāsanēna gatā svabhavanē । rājāpi tayā saha suptō rajanyāṁ tatraiva ॥57॥

ēvaṁ pratidivasamēva prēkṣaṇakaṁ paśyati tathā gr̥hē । tathā samaṁ saṁvasati yajjalpati sa tatra tatsā ||58 ||
nijajanakasya kathayati sō'pi khalu vahikāyāṁ likhati tatsarvam । anyadinē sōpānē upānahau muktatvā''rūḍhā ॥

ānītē tē, suptastatraivārdharātrē । sā tadabhimukhaṁ jalpati mama pādāvadya dahyētē ॥ 61॥

tathā nivāritō'pi khalu, atha sukhasuptā pralōkatē sāpi । svapnē pūrṇacandraṁ praviśantaṁ nijavadanē || 63 ॥
taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā vibuddhā siñcantaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā taṁ caraṇau । tataḥ sahasōtthāya mōcayitvā kathayati tasmai svapnam ||64 ||
rājñā bhaṇitaṁ mr̥gākṣi ! niścitaṁ tava varaḥ sutō bhaviṣyati । yāvattāvadvibhāvarīvirāmasūcakō vāditaḥ śaṅkhaḥ ॥
ita utthāya rājā vrajati gēhē sāpi svādhyāyam । kurvāṇā tāvatsthitā yāvaduditō dinamaṇistataḥ ॥66॥
pitr̥gēhē saṁpāptā dvāraṁ pidhāya tassa gēhamya । pracchannasthitā tiṣṭhati kathayitvā pitu rajanicaritam || 67॥

tā tattha na taṁ pāsa tō pucchara pāḍivēsiyaṁ tīsē । kattha gayā hē ! ēsā līlāvaināmiyā, sāha || 69 ॥

sō bhai dēva ! kairalē paccūsē sā balāvi gēhāō । nīsāriyā maēcciya jēṇa iyaṁ saṁpayē ruṭṭhā ॥ 72 ॥
kassavi ṭhakkaraputtassa vannaēṇaṁ na ēi jiṇabhavaṇē । naya paṁjalamōlaggai laggai rāḍīvi sikkhaviyā || 73 |
tō tahāṇē annā nivēsivvā maē ya mēhariyā । tō mōṇaṁ kāūṇaṁ ṭhiō nariṁdō, iō sāvi ||74|
pasava samayammi surya varalakkhaṇa saṁjayaṁ supacchannaṁ । vaḍūḍhai sacivassa gihē tā jāva kalāṇa pāragaō ।
tō annadiṇē maṁtī suvaṇānaṁda saputtayaṁ nēuṁ । daṁsai nivassa sōvi hu taṁ pucchara kā imā mahilā ? ||
tō maṁtī bhai imā nariṁda ! tuha paṇaiṇī maha suyā ya । ēsō ya tumha taṇaō maha puṇa dōhittaō nāha ||
tō vimiō rāyā jā kiṁpi hu jaṁpihī taō vahiyā । sacivēṇa tassa sahasā samappiyā sō uvāē ।
jaṁ kiṁci tīē saddhi rahammi parijaṁpiyaṁ taha karyapi । taṁ savvaṁ ciya pāsai lihiyaṁ vahiyāē saivvivaraṁ ।

bhaṇai ya bhuvaṇāṇaṁda araṁ jiō raṁjiō ahaṁ tumaē । niyayapainnānivvāhaṇēṇa taha tanayalaṁbhēṇa ॥ 81

pratipannatrataviśēṣa itarō'pi naitramācarati pāpam । kiṁ punaḥ kulōdgatastvaṁ jinadharmavid viśēṣēṇa 1 ॥ 93 ॥ ·
ēṣā'naṅgakrīḍā pīḍā turyatratasya śrāddhānām । ihaparalōka viruddhaṁ tasmāttyajēdaṁ tvaṁ bhrātaḥ ! ॥ 94 ॥
tatastēna sa maṇitō bhrātaḥ ! mā bhaṇa kimapi mama saṁmukham । na śaknōmyanaṅgakrīḍāṁ parihartuṁ ramaṇīlōlō'ham ॥
jātyandhēbhyō'pyadhikaṁ mōhāndhō bhavatīti vibhāvya । sa khalu dhanō ghanadēvēnōpēkṣitō bhramati svacchandam ॥96॥
1. sa. maē । 2 kē kula ।

yuddhō sarīraphāsē tīē pariraṁbha karēmāṇō । diṭṭhō tajjaṇaēṇaṁ nimūḍiḍaṁ kaṁvāē ||18||
baddhō cōru ta pakkhittō cārayammi ciṁtēi । haddhī maha vayabhaṁgā phaliō ihayapi pāvatarū || 99॥
jai kahavi ēkavāraṁ imāu dukkhāu naṇu vicchuṭṭissaṁ । tō na puṇōvi karissaṁ ēvamahaṁ kāmakīlati ॥
tō piuṇā bahudaviṇēṇa mōiō niyagimmi sō nīō | bīyadi mariūṇaṁ nāgakumārī samuppannō
tattō bhaūiṇa bhavē bhavakkhayaṁ pāvihī ya sō'vassaṁ । dhaṇadēvō uṇa taiē bhavammi sivasaṁpayaṁ lahihī ||
kīlāē kāmaṁ para pāvai ghaṇauvva ihabhavēvi duhaṁ । tamhā vivēṇā sā parihariyavvā payattēṇa ॥ 103 ॥
parihari aṇagakīla gharēi jō baṁbhacēravayamasamaṁ । sō pāvai nivvāṇaṁ aiśa kammakkhayaṁ kāuṁ ॥ 104 ॥

dōhammavasaō ramaṇī māṇasāvi taṁ na patthēi | nēhēṇavi ālaviyā akkōsē sē pacchē ||4॥

tataḥ pitrā bahudraviṇēna mōcitō nijagr̥hē sa nītaḥ । dvitīyadinē mr̥tvā nāgakumāraḥ samutpannaḥ ॥101॥

sō bhai asthi tipurāvijjā sajjōvi dēi sōhaggaṁ । jā sumaraṇamitṇavi vihiṇā saṁsāhiyā saṁtī ।।

tattō sō paricita nūṇaṁ sōhaggaguṇanihī ēsō । siddhatipurāivijjō kō vi mahaṇā mahāsiddhō ॥ 10 ॥

kāmaṁ kāmāsattō vijjāmaṁtēhi cunnajōgēhiṁ । ramaṇīu mōhiūṇaṁ jō bhuṁjai sō ya kālēṇa || 13 ||
na ya muṁbai paradāraṁ gammāgammaṁ ca na cayai kayāvi । iha jammammivi pāvara pāvō tō tikkhadukkhāī ||
ahiya taha dōhaggaṁ hōi aṇiṭṭhō ya savvalōyassa । dōhaggadukkhanaḍiō sō bhai bhīmabhavagaṇē || 15॥
nāyāgayāvi bhōgā bhayāvahā kammabaṁdhahēū ya। kiṁ puṇa ummamgagayā samaggalaṁ galiyaguṇagarimā ? ॥ 16 ॥
iyarō taṇuōvi guṇō mā hōu, havēu kēvalaṁ sīlaṁ । jō jīvāṇaṁ maṇavaṁchiyāī kajjāī pūrēi ||17||
jasavihavahāṇiparibhavakalaṁkaduhapamuhadōsadaṁdōlī । sīlaviyalāṇa purisāhamāṇa nūṇaṁ samāvaḍai || 18 ||
daurbhāgyatarjitēna pr̥ṣṭaḥ kāpālikastatastēna । tava kāpyasti vidyā saubhāgyakarī viśēṣēṇa ? ॥5॥
sa bhaṇatyasti tripurāvidyā sadyō'pi dadāti saubhāgyam । yā smaraṇamātrēṇāpi vidhinā saṁsādhitā satī ॥6॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ durgēṇa yadyēvaṁ tadā prayaccha mē vidyām । kr̥tvā guruprasādaṁ tēnāpi vidhinā vitīrṇā sā ॥ 7 ॥
kaṇavīrakusumalakṣaṁ saguggulu gr̥hītvā'nyadā durgaḥ । tripurāvidyādēvīprasādhanārthaṁ gatō malayē ॥8॥
tāvadyāvattatra nr̥pamandirasya dvārē kēvalī dr̥ṣṭaḥ । dēśayan sugatipathaṁ kinnara narasurasamūhasya ||9||
tataḥ sa paricintayati nūnaṁ saubhāgyaguṇanidhirēṣaḥ । siddha tripurādividyaḥ kō'pi mahātmā mahāsiddhaḥ ॥ 10 ॥
sātiśayaiva vidyētasya kāpālikāta, tasmādēnam । prārthayē kāmapi vidyāmiti hētōrvanditaḥ sādhuḥ ॥11॥
tēnāpi dharmalābhō dattaḥ saṁbhāṣitaścōpaviṣṭaḥ । munināpi samārabdhā dharmakathā tamapyuddiśya ॥ 12 ॥
kāmaṁ kāmāsaktō vidyāmantraiścūrṇayōgaiḥ । ramaṇīmahayitvā yō bhuṅga sa ca kālēna ॥ 13 ॥
na ca muñcati paradārān gamyāgamyāṁ ca na tyajati kadāpi । iha janmanyapi prāpnōti pāpastatastīkṣṇaduḥkhāni ॥
· adhikaṁ tathā daurbhāgyaṁ bhavatyaniṣṭaśca sarvalōkasya | daurbhāgyaduḥkhanaṭitaḥ sa bhramati bhīmabhavagahanē ॥ 15॥
nyāyāgatā api bhōgā bhayāvahāḥ karmabandhahētavaśca । kiṁ punarunmārgagatāḥ samargalaṁ galitaguṇagarimāṇaḥ 1 ॥

supāsanāda-variyami-
paṁca ēē mahāpāvā bhaṇiyā sanvannuṇā iha । jēsi pārvati dukkhāī pāvabuddhī narāhamā ||19||
bhūyahiṁsā musāvāō cōriyā mēhuṇaṁ tahā । pariggahō mahāraṁbhī mahāsahārihā imē ||20||
iccāidēsaṇaṁ nisuṇiūṇa saṁvēgamāgayā parisā । duggōvi bhaṇai bhayavaṁ ! paṁcamahāpātra parihārō ||21||
kāyanvō tā saṁpai niyamaṁ mē dēhi, nāṇiṇā dinnō । sampattapuvvagaṁ sō namiūṇa muṇi gaō gēhē ||22|
pālai sāvagadhammaṁ dhammabhāvēṇa vaḍḍhaē riddhī । dinnā sē niyadhūyā kēṇāvi mahiṭṭhiēṇa taō || 23 |
tīē samaṁ sō bhuṁjai visaē, jāyā yaṁ tassa dō puttā । aha annayā ya duggō jā vaccā haṭṭamaggami ||24|
tā tattha āgaēṇa diṭṭhō kāvāliēṇa tēṇēva । karakaliyakavālē dinnā tipurā purā jēṇa || 25॥
bhaṇiō ya imaṁ duggō majjha pasāēṇa ērisā riddhī । pattā savvāvi taē tō vayaṇaṁ suṇasu maha inhi ||
jēṇaṁ bhavaṁtarēvi hu dōhaggaṁ dugga ! tuha na hu bhavēi । bahuyāu kannayāu pariṇāvaha vaṁbhaṇāīṇaṁ ||27||
tō duggēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ tipurā nahu sāhiyā maē taiyā । na hu sāhiyā jaō iha lacchī uṇa dhammaprabhavā mē ॥
dhammō muṇipasāyā tumapi hēū ya tattha saṁjāō । jaṁ bhaṇasi kannayāṇaṁ pariṇāvaṇamiha na taṁ juttaṁ ||29|
bhavvayaaiyārō tēṇa karaṇaṁ havai mahāvastaṁ । lōyavyavahārēṇa niyataṇayāpi taṁ hōi ॥ 30॥
kāvāliēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ jai ēvaṁ tahātri mannaṇijjō haṁ । jaṁ hōhī iha pāvaṁ taṁ majjha havissai na tujjha ||31|
iya paidipi pabhaṇai sō taṁ tō tēṇa taduvarōhēṇa । bhaṇiō dasa kannāō vivāhaissaṁ ahaṁ tattō ||32|
yaśōvibhavahāniparibhavakalaṅkaduḥkhapramukha dōṣadvandvālī | śīlavikalānāṁ puruṣādhamānāṁ nūnaṁ samāpatati ॥ 18 ॥
pañcaitē mahāpāpā bhaṇitāḥ sarvajñēnēha । yēbhyaḥ prāpnuvanti duḥkhāni pāpabuddhayō narādhamāḥ ॥19॥
bhūtahiṁsā mr̥ṣāvādaścārikā maithunaṁ tathā । parigrahō mahārambhō mahāśabdāhī imē ॥20॥
ityādidēśanāṁ śrutvā saṁvēgamāgatā pariṣat | durgē'pi bhaṇati bhagavan ! pañcamahāpāpaparihāraḥ ॥ 21 ॥
kartavyastasmātsaṁprati niyamaṁ mē dēhi, jñāninā dattaḥ । samyaktvapūrvakaṁ sa natvā muniṁ gatō gēhē ॥22॥
pālayati śrāvakadharmaṁ dharmaprabhāvēṇa vartatē r̥ddhiḥ । dattā tasmai nijaduhitā kēnāpi maharddhikēna tataḥ ॥ 23॥
tayā samaṁ sa bhuṅktē viṣayān jātau ca tasya dvau putrau । athānyadā ca durgōṁ yāvad trajati haṭṭamārgē ॥24॥
tāvattatrāgatēna dr̥ṣṭaḥ kāpālikēna tēnaiva । karakalitakapālēna dattā tripurā purā yēna ||29||
'
bhaṇitaścēdaṁ durgē mama prasādanēdr̥śī r̥ddhiḥ । prāptā sarvāpi tvayā tatō vacanaṁ śr̥ṇu mamēdānīm || 26॥
yēna bhavāntarē'pi khalu daurbhāgyaṁ durga ! tava na hi bhavēt । bahūḥ kanyāḥ pariṇāyaya brāhmaṇādīnām ||27||
tatō durgēṇa bhaṇitaṁ tripurā nahi sādhitā mayā tadā । na khalu sā hitā yata iha lakṣmīḥ punardharmaprabhavā mē ।
dharmō muniprasādāt tvamapi hētuśca tatra saṁjātaḥ । yad bhaṇasi kanyānāṁ pariṇāyaṇamiha na tadyuktam ||29||
brahmatratā ticārastēna kr̥tēna bhavēd mamāvaśyam । lōkavyavahārēṇa nijatanayānāmapi tad bhavati ॥30॥
kāpālikēna bhaṇitaṁ yadyēvaṁ tathāpi mānanīyō'ham । yad bhatiṣyatīha pāpaṁ tanmama bhaviṣyati na tava ॥31॥

tathāhi ; -
caṁdaṇavaṇaṁva bahubhōgisaṁgayaṁ gayapuraṁ puraṁ asthi । atthiyaṇakappasāhī visāhanaṁdī tahiṁ rāyā || 2 ||
tattha ya nivasa siṭṭī piyavayaṇō tassa bhāriyā sulatā । sujasō tāṇaṁ taṇaō suryāviyalō jūyavasaṇī ya ।।
saṇiyaṁ saṇiyaṁ bālattaṇāō taṇuyāī taṭṭabaṭṭāī । avaharivi niyadharāō hārēi rahammi khilaṁtō ॥4॥
tō kasō vaḍhatē tē bahu hāriyaṁ ramaṁtēṇa । tāyavaṇaṁ tō tēṇaṁ bhaṇiyā bhajjā piē! putō ||5||
iti pratidinamapi prabhaṇati sa taṁ tatastēna taduparōdhēna । bhaṇitō daśa kanyā vivāhāyiṣyāmyahaṁ tataḥ ॥32॥
sa sarvatra gavēṣayitvā''nīya gr̥hē kanyāḥ । tāsāmucitāḥ kumārā api khalvāhūtā lagnadivasē ॥ 33॥
nijanijajanatayā yuktāḥ praviśantyahamahamikayā । maṇḍapadvārē yātāstatrāpi prathamapravēśārtham ॥ 34 ॥
yudhyantē parasparatō vācā tathā ca khaḍḍayātaiḥ । tāvadyāvanmahāyuddhaṁ janatānāṁ tadā jātam ||35||
tat śrutvā durgō vēgēna gatō nivāraṇārtham । tān vārayan viddhaḥ śarēṇa kēnāpi tatō naṣṭaḥ ॥36॥
prāptō gr̥hē ghātēna pīḍitaḥ pūtkarōti cintayati ca । turyatrataturyāticāravr̥kṣakusumōdgama ēṣaḥ ||37||
idānīmapi khalu saṁjātaḥ prāpsyāmi punaḥ phalaṁ tu prētyabhatrē । tasmātsarvathā hatō'haṁ yadaticaritaṁ caturthatratam ॥ 38 ॥
iti cintayan prāptaḥ pañcatvaṁ bhavanavāsimadhyē । upapannastatō'pi hi tr̥tīyabhavē śivasukhaṁ lapsyatē ॥ 39 ॥

yaḥ śabdādiṣu gr̥ddhō viddhō madanasya tīkṣṇabhallaiḥ । kāmē tītrābhilāṣī suyaśā iva sa duḥkhī bhavati ॥ 1 ॥
candanavanamiva bahubhōgisaṁgataṁ gajapuraṁ puramasti । arthijanakalpaśākhī viśākhanandī tatra rājā || 2 ||
tatra ca nivasati śrēṣṭhī priyavacanastasya bhāryā sulasā । suyaśāstayōstanayaḥ śrutavikalō dyūtavyasanī ca ॥3॥

tataḥ kramaśō vardhamānēna tēna bahu nāśitaṁ ramamāṇēna । tātaghanaṁ tatastēna bhaṇitā bhāryā priyē ! putraḥ ||5||

supāsanāha-cariammi
1
kālakkhariyai ēsō tō sā rōsēga bhaṇai tayabhimuhaṁ । mai jīvaṁtīē imaṁ na hōi tā jāu davvaṁpi ॥ 6 ॥
kiṁ kijjai lacchīē puttaviuttāṇa piyayama ! jayammi । cirapavasiyāvi lacchī āṇijjai puṇavi puttēhi ॥
tō annayā ya tēṇaṁ niyasīsaṁ hāriyē ramaṁtēṇaṁ । jūpāriēhiṁ nīō piuṇō pāsamma tēṇāvi ||8||
tajjaṇaṇīē pāsē pēsaviō tīi niyayaāharaṇaṁ । dāūṇa mōiō sō jyārīṇaṁ sayāsāō ||9 ॥
puṇaravi ramēi puṇaravi ya hāraē sīmahatyacaraṇāī । tō annayā sē nīō jaṇaya gihē baṁdhi tēhi ॥ 10॥
sirachēyaṁ kuṇamāṇā bhaṇiyā sujasēṇa uvavaṇassaṁtō । atthi mahatāyadavvaṁ āgacchaha jēṇa daṁsēmi ॥ 11 ॥
tō tattha gayāṇaṁ sō daṁsai ṭhāṇaṁpi kiṁpi kavaḍēṇa । takkhaṇaṇavāvaḍē tē nāuṁ dūrēga sō nahī || 12 ||
pattō ārāmajidimaṁdirē ajiyanāhasaraṇaṁ sō । puṭṭhīē tēvi pattā khaliyā kēṇāvi saṭṭēṇaṁ ॥ 13॥
ētyaṁtara mmi pattō sudādavijjāharō tahiṁ bhavaṇē । ukkhayakhaggā diṭṭā jūyārā tēvi duvārē ||14||
tō puṭṭhō sō saḍḍhō tēvi kahiyaṁ zahēsa jiṇasaraṇaṁ । paḍivannō, tā ēyaṁ nāhaṁ ēyāṇa appē || 15 ||
vijjāharēṇa tattō ārōvēūṇa sō vimāṇammi | naṁdīsarammi nīō vāvannajiṇālayaṁ dadr̥ḍhaṁ ||16||
sō kōvi samullasiō āṇaṁdō tammaṇammi bahupāvaṁ । jēṇa khaṇēṇa vilīṇaṁ tamaṁtra ravidaṁsaṇēṇa tahiṁ ॥ 17 ॥
tatthavi cāraṇasamaṇaṁ sujasō vaṁdēi suṇēi tassaṁtē । vijjāharēṇa sahiō sāvayadhammaṁpi bārasahā || 18 |
paḍivajjai ya pamōēṇa giṇhaē taha ya jūyaramaṇammi । niyamaṁ jāvajjīvaṁ tō sō vijjāharō tuṭṭō ||19|
kālakṣarīyatyēṣa tataḥ sā rōṣēṇa bhaṇati tadabhimukham । mayi jīvantyāmidaṁ na bhavati tasmādyātu dravyamapi ॥ 6 ॥
kiṁ kriyatē lakṣmyā putra viyuktayōḥ priyatama ! jagati । ciraprōṣitāpi lakṣmīrānīyatē punarapi putraiḥ ॥7॥
tatō'nyadā ca tēna nijaśīrṣa nāśitaṁ ramamāṇēna । dyūtakārakainatiḥ pituḥ pārśvē tēnāpi ॥ 8 ॥
tajjananyāḥ pārśvē prēṣitastayā nijābharaṇam । dattvā mōcitaḥ saghr̥takāriṇāṁ sakāśāt॥9॥
punarapi ramatē punarapi ca nāśayati śīrṣahastacaraṇādi । tatō'nyadā sa nītō janakagr̥hē baddhvā taiḥ ॥ 10 ॥
śiraśchēdaṁ kurvāṇā bhaṇitā suyaśasōpavanasyāntaḥ । asti mattātadravyamāgacchata yēna darśayāmi ॥ 11 ॥
tatastatra gatēbhyaḥ sa darśayati sthānamapi kimapi kapaṭēna । tatkhananavyā vr̥tāṁstān jñātvā dūrēṇa sa naṣṭaḥ ॥ 12॥
prāpta ārāmajinēndramandirē'jitanāthaśaraṇaṁ saḥ । pr̥ṣṭhē tē'pi prāptāḥ skhalitāḥ kēnāpi śrāddhēna ॥ 13॥
atrāntarē prāptaḥ sudaṁṣṭravidyādharastatra bhavanē । utkhātakhaḍā dr̥ṣṭā dyūtakārāstēnāpi dvārē ॥ 14 ॥
tataḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ sa śrāddhastēnāpi kathitaṁ yathaiṣa jinaśaraṇam । pratipannaḥ, tasmādētaṁ nāhamētēṣāmarpayāmi ||15||
vidyādharēṇa tata ārōpya sa vimānē । nandīśvarē nītō dvipañcāśajjinālayaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā ॥ 16 ॥

।
sa kō'pi samullasita ānandastanmanasi bahupa |pam । yēna kṣaṇēna vilīnaṁ tama iva ravidarśanēna tatra ॥ 17॥
tatrāpi cāraṇaśramaṇaṁ suyaśā vandatē śr̥ṇōti tasyāntē । vidyādharēṇa sahitaḥ śrāvakadharmamapi dvādaśadhā ॥ 18 ॥
pratipadyatē ca pramōdēna gr̥hṇāti tathā ca dyūtaramaṇē । niyamaṁ yāvajjīvaṁ tataḥ sa vidyādharastuṣṭaḥ ॥ 19 ॥

sujasassa dēi vijjaṁ mōrīnāmaṁ vihīē sō lēi । siddhā ē vijjāē tēṇa samaṁ jāi bēgaḍḍē ||20||
kaivayadiṇāī tatthavi vivihā vijjāō paḍhiyasiddhāō । vijjāharapāsāō gahium̐ sō gayapuraṁ pattō ॥ 21 ॥
gayapurapaipattīē sōhaggasirīē pasavasamayammiṁ । saṁpattō tappāsē pacchannō tīē mayaputtaṁ ||22||
avahariu kāūṇa ya maūrarūvaṁ sayaṁ ṭhiō tattha । tō sūikammaṁkusalā mahilā jaṁpēṛa sihī jāō || 23॥
ēyaṁ siddhaṁ rannō, tēvi nēmittiyāṇa taṁ kahiyaṁ । tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ narāhiva ! mahāaṇi imaṁ hōhī || 24 ॥
jai pariharāsa na dēvi mōrajuyaṁ, takkhaṇēṇa tō rannā । bhaṇiō niyasēṇāṇī dēvi mōrēṇa saha sahasā ||
phalajalabhōyaṇarahiē mahāarannammi nēvi pariharasu । tēṇavi tahēva vihiyaṁ tō dēvi karuṇa dēṇa ॥ 26 ॥
rōyatiṁ saṁṭhaviḍaṁ valiō sēṇāvaīvi, ittō ya । mōrōvi payaḍarūvō jāō purisō suravaruvva ||27||
paṇa mēuṁ taṁ dēvi saṁvara imēhiṁ mahurasadēhiṁ । mā māi ! ruyasu inhi picchasa niyaputtamāhappaṁ ||28||
tō takkhaṇēṇa vijjā taṁtrayaṇēṇaṁ puraṁ payaṭṭēi । sappāyāraṁ rannō rannava vicittabahubhavaṇaṁ ||29||
dhaṇadhannahirannasuvannavannavānnajiṇahara samiddhaṁ । bahudaviṇaṁ dāūṇaṁ lōō avayāriō tattha ||30||
mōruvariraiyamaṇimayavimāṇamāruhivi bhuvaṇamajjhammi | bahuvijjāhara sahiō gaurīputtōcca paribhamai ||31||
jē jattha vatthusatthaṁ supasatthaṁ picchaē purē gāmē । atthēṇa patthaṇāivi taṁ gihivi nēi mōraurē || 32 ॥
tapurasīmāē nivō saṁkhapurē saṁkhavaddhaṇō nāma । taduhiyā kamalasirī sayaṁvarā maṁḍavē tīsē ||33||
suyaśasē dadāti vidyāṁ mōrīnāmāṁ vidhinā sa lāti । siddhāyāṁ vidyāyāṁ tēna samaṁ yāti vaitāḍhyē ॥20॥
katipayadināni tatrāpi vividhā vidyāḥ paṭhitasiddhāḥ । vidyādharapārśvād gr̥hītvā sa rājapuraṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 29 ॥
gajapurapatipatnyāḥ saubhāgyaśriyaḥ prasavasamayē । saṁprāptastatpārśvē pracchannastasyā mr̥taputram ॥22॥
apahr̥tya kr̥tvā ca mayūrarūpaṁ svayaṁ sthitastatra । tataḥ sūtikarmakuśalā mahilā jalpati śikhī jātaḥ ॥23॥
ētat śiṣṭaṁ rājñē, tēnāpi naimittikēbhyastatkathitam । tairbhaṇitaṁ narādhipa ! mahā'niṣṭamidaṁ bhaviṣyati ॥ 24 ॥
yadi pariharasi na dēvīṁ mōrayutāṁ tatkṣaṇēna tatō rājñā । bhaṇitō nijasēnānīrdēvīṁ mōrēṇa saha sahasā ॥ 25 ॥
phalajalabhōjanarahitē mahāraṇyē nītvā parihara । tēnāpi tathaiva vihitaṁ tatō dēvīṁ karuṇaśabdēna ||26||
rudatīṁ saṁsthāpya valitaḥ sēnāpatirapi itaśca । mōrō'pi prakaṭarūpō jātaḥ puruṣaḥ suravaravat ॥27॥
praṇamya tāṁ dēvīṁ saṁsthāpayatyēbhirmadhuraśabdaiḥ । mā mātaḥ ! rōdīridānīṁ paśya nijaputramāhātmyam ||28||
tatastatkṣaṇēna vidyā tadvacanēna puraṁ pravartayati । saprākāraṁ rājña āraṇyamiva vicitrabahubhavanam ||29||
dhanadhānyahiraṇyasuvarṇavarṇadvipañcāśajjinagr̥hasamr̥ddham । bahudraviṇaṁ dattvā lōkō'vatāritastatra ॥ 30 ॥
mōrōpariracitamaṇimayavimānamāruhya bhuvanamadhyē | bahuvidyāvarasahitō gaurīputra iva paribhramati ॥31॥
yaṁ yatra vastusārtha supraśastaṁ paśyati purē grāmē । arthēna prārthanayāpi tad gr̥hītvā nayati mōrapurē || 32॥
tatpurasīmni nr̥paḥ śaṅkhapurē śaṅkhavardhanō nāma । taduhitā kamalaśrīḥ svayaṁvarāmaṇḍapē tasyāḥ ॥ 33 ॥

savvēvi nivakupārā pāṇiggaṇamitī saṁpattā । battīsakupara mahiō visāhanaṁdīvi lahū ēi ||34||
taṁ savvaṁ bhaṭṭāō suṇi vārijjadivasasamayammi । saṁkhaurē saṁpattō maūravēsēṇa sō sujasō || 35 ॥
tatō sayaṁtra maṁḍava bahunivakumararuirambhi | gaṁtūrṇa uvaviṭṭhō kaṁṭayalalulaṁtamaṇimālā ||36||
ittōsā kamalasirī karakaliyaviyāsikusumavaramālā | saṁpattā tattha taō paḍihārī daṁsaē kumarē || 37||
amuganivaṁgaruhō'yaṁ amugābhihāṇō niēhi pasaṁyacchi ! । iccāi tāva jātra ya gayapuranāhaṁpi daṁsē || 38||
nō ramai tīē diṭṭhī kathavi ya kumārarāyadēhēsu । viyasiyavimaladalēsu ya jahakakusumēsu bhamarī ||39||
tōshaṁ dasa taḍaviyasihaṁḍa maṁḍiyaṁ mōraṁ । paṇavanniyamaṇikiraṇōlibhāsuraṁ suravaidhaṇuvva ||40||
apayanisēēṇava tassa daṁsaṇē tīi nivvuyā diṭṭhī । tō sahasā pakkhittā varamālā tassa kaṁṭhammi ॥ 41 ॥
aha rōsaphuriyaaharā kumarā jaṁpati rē ! imaṁ mōraṁ । māraha sigmaṁ khaggēṇa, kōvi rōsēṇa tō kumarō ॥ 42 ॥
uḍēuṁ jā haṇihī taduttamaṁgaṁ mahīē tā paḍiyaṁ । tō saṁbhaṁtā kumarā samaṁ maūraṁ khamāvēuṁ || 43 ||
jaṁpati gurupāyaṁ kāuṁ paḍēsu attaṇō ruvaṁ । tēṇavi tavvayaṇēṇaṁ vijjāsāmatyaōṁ sahasā ||44||
sihiuvariviyipavaraṁ vimāṇamāruhivi daṁsiō appā | vijjāhararūtrēṇaṁ tō vimhaiyā nivā savvē ॥ 45 ॥
jayaṁti parōparaō imassahō ! rūvasaṁpayā paramā । iccāi jaṁpirēsuṁ payaṭṭaō usakō rannā ||46 ||
vittaṁ pāṇiggahaṇaṁ kamalasirīē samaṁ vibhūīē । aha sō visāhanaṁdipamukkhanivakumara parikaliō ||47||
pattō aḍavīnimmaviyaniyanayarammi tattha niyajaṇaṇi । paṇamai kamalasirīē samagaṁ taḥ nivakumārēhiṁ ॥ 48
sarvē'pi nr̥pakumārāḥ pāṇigrahaṇē tasyāḥ saṁprāptāḥ । dvātriṁśatkumārasahitō viśākhananyapi ladhvēti ॥34॥
tatsarvaṁ bhaṭṭāt śrutvā vivāhadivasasamayē । śaṅkhapurē saṁprāptō mayūravēṣēṇa sa suyaśāḥ ||35||
tataḥ svayaṁvarāmaṇḍapē bahunr̥pakumārarucirē । gatvōpaviṣṭaḥ kaṇḍatala luṭhanmaṇimālaḥ || 36 ||
itaḥ sā kamalaśrīḥ karakalita vikāsi kusumavaramālā । saṁprāptā tatra tataḥ pratihārī darśayati kumārān ||37||
amukanr̥pāṅgaruhō'yamamukābhidhānaḥ paśya mr̥gākṣi ! | ityādi tāvad yāvacca gajapuranāthamapi darśayati ||38|
nō ramatē tasyā dr̥ṣṭiḥ kutrāpi kumārarājadēhēṣu । vikasitavimaladalēṣu ca yathārkakusumēṣu bhramaryāḥ ॥ 39 ॥
tatō rōṣairdarśayati tataśikhaṇḍamaṇḍitaṁ mōram । pañcavarṇikamaṇikiraṇālīmāsuraṁ surapatidhanuriva ॥ 40 ॥
amr̥taniṣēkēṇaiva tasya darśanē tasyā nirvr̥tā dr̥ṣṭiḥ । tataḥ sahasā prakṣiptā varamālā tasya kaṇṭhē ॥ 41 ॥
atha rōṣasphuratādharāḥ kumārā jalpanti rē imaṁ mōram । māraya śīghraṁ khaṅgēna, kōpi rōṣēṇa tataḥ kumāraḥ ॥42
utthāya yāvaddhaniṣyati taduttamāṅgaṁ mahyāṁ tāvatpatitam । tataḥ saṁbhrāntāḥ kumārāḥ samaṁ mayūraṁ kṣamayitvā ॥ 43 ॥
jalpanti guruprasādaṁ kr̥tvā prakaṭayātmanō rūpam । tēnāpi tadvacanēna vidyāsāmarthyataḥ sahasā ||44॥
śikhyaparivihitapravaraṁ vimānamāruhya darśita ātmā । vidyādhararūpēṇa tatō vismitā nr̥pāḥ sarvē ॥ 45॥
jalpanti parasparatō'sya hō ! rūpasaṁpat paramā । ityādi jalpitr̥ṣu pravartita utsavō rājñā ॥ 46 ॥
vr̥ttaṁ pāṇigrahaṇaṁ kamalāśayāḥ samaṁ vibhūtyā | atha sa viśākhanādipramukha nr̥pa kumāraparikalitaḥ ॥47॥

aha sō visāhanaṁdī tajjagaṇi niyavi citaē kimiyaṁ । sā sōhaggasirī jā sihimmi jāē maē cattā 1 ॥
iya ciṁtaṁtassa imassa tīē sayamēva āsaṇaṁ dinaṁ । sōvi uvavisivi khāmai taṁ dēvi paṇayavayaṇēhiṁ ॥ 50॥
tathāhi ; .
khamasu piē! maha inhi jē tajhyā nigviṇaṁ kathaṁ kammaṁ । kunimittiō nimittaṁ jāō tumhāṇa cāyampi ॥
iccāi jāva jaṁpa taṁ paṛa tā pabhaṇaē imaṁ dēvī । kō tuha dōsō piyayama ! dōsō amhāṇa kammassa ॥52॥
jaō ।
jaṁ jēṇa pātriyavvaṁ suhamasuhaṁ vāvi jīvalōgammi । taṁ pāvijjai niyamā paḍiyārō natthi ēyassa ॥53॥
bhaṇiō ya niō putta vaccha ! imaṁ namaha tuha piyā ēsa । tēṇavi tahatti vihiyaṁ rāyā āliṁgiūṇa tayaṁ ॥
niyaaṁkē kāma kamēṇa pucchēi vaiyaraṁ savvaṁ । dēvīpasūyaṇāō pariṇayaṇataṁ kahai sōvi ॥ 55 ॥
tō bhaṇiyaṁ naravaṇā tumaṁ nariṁdō ihēva tatthēva । āgaccha maē saddhiṁ jēṇabhisiṁcāmi rajjammi || 56॥
saha sōhaggasirīē tō pattā gayapurammi tē dōvi । ahisittō niyarajjē rannā sujasō tarhi tēṇaṁ ॥57॥
puvvillā niyajaṇaṇī paṇayā gaṁtūṇa jaṇayupāyā ya | siṭṭivariṭṭhammi paē ṭhaviō jaṇaōvi, ittō ya ।।
rāyā visāhanaṁdī gioes dikkhaṁ navassa naravaiṇō । mōrajjhaō ya sujasō jāyāī duni nāmāī ॥ 59 ॥
kamalasirīpamuhāhiṁ dēvīhiṁ samaṁ lalēi sōvi taō । kāmē tivvahilāsō sē aisayadāruṇō jāō || 60 ॥
ramai ramaṇīhiṁ saddhiṁ aṇavarayaṁ ratharasammi āsattō । kamalasirīē bhaṇiō aha annayā viṇayapaṇayāē ||
prāptō'ṭavī nirmāpitānajanagarē tatra nijajananīm । praṇamati kamalaśriyā samaṁ tathā nr̥pakumāraiḥ ||18||
atha sa viśākhanandī tajjananīṁ dr̥ṣṭrā cintayati kimiyam । sā saubhāgyaśrīryā śikhini jātē mayā tyaktā ? ॥
iti cintayatō'sya tathā svayamēvāsanaṁ dattam । sō'pyupaviśya kṣamayati tāṁ dēvīṁ praṇayavacanaiḥ ॥50॥
kṣamasva priyē ! māmidānīṁ yattadā nirghr̥ṇaṁ kr̥taṁ karma । kunaimittikō nimittaṁ jātō yuvayōstyāgē ।।11।।
ityādi yāvajjalpati taṁ prati tāvatprabhaṇatī dēvī । kastava dōṣaḥ priyatama ! dōṣa āvayōḥ karmaṇaḥ ॥52॥
yataḥ ।
yadyēna prāptavyaṁ sukhamasukhaṁ vāpi jīvalōkē । tatprāpyatē niyamātpratikārō nāstyētasya ॥53॥
bhaṇitaśca nijaḥ putrō vatsa ! imaṁ nama, tava pitaiṣaḥ । tēnāpi tathēti vihitaṁ rājā''liṅgya tam ॥ 54 ॥
nijāṅkē saṁkramayati kramēṇa pr̥cchati vyatikaraṁ sarvam । dēvīprasavanāt pariṇayanāntaṁ kathayati sō'pi ॥55॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā tvaṁ narēndra ihāpi tatrāpi । āgaccha mayā sārdhaṁ yēnābhiṣiñcāmi rājyē ॥ 56 ॥
saha saubhāgyaśriyā tataḥ prāptau gajapurē tau dvāvapi । abhiṣiktō vijarājyē rājñā suyaśāstatra tēna ||17||
pūrvīyā nijajananī praṇatā gatvā janakapādāśca । śrēṣṭhivariṣṭhē padē sthāpitō janakō'pi, itaśca ॥98॥
rājā viśākhanandī gr̥hṇāti dakṣiāṁ navasya narapatēḥ । mōradhvajaśca suyaśā jātē dvē nāmanī ||19||
kamalaśrīpramukhābhirdēvībhiḥ samaṁ lalati sō'pi tataḥ । kāmē tīvrābhilāṣastasyātiśaya dāruṇō. jātaḥ ॥ 60 ॥

tumhārisāṇa nivapuṁgavāṇa suviiyavatthutattāṇa । satthapasatthamaīṇaṁ visayapasaṁgō hu nahu juttō ॥ 62 ॥
yataḥ,
.
kāmaḥ krōdhastathā harṣō māyā lōbhō madastathā । ṣaḍavargamutsr̥jēdēnaṁ tasmiṁstyaktē sukhī nr̥paḥ ॥”
chāvicchēyatthaṁ bhōgē bhuṁjaṁti bhōiṇō jē tē । siṁcaṁti pasamaṇaṭṭhā ghayāhuīē huyāsaṇayaṁ ॥ 63 ॥
chāvāhī asajhōna niyattai ōsahēhivi karahiṁ । tamhā tīutthāṇaṁ nirubhiyavaṁ hisīhi ||64॥
suviṇayapāviyapāṇiyapāṇēṇaṁ jaha paṇassai na taṇhā । visayapivāsāvi tahā na niyattai bhōyasēvā || 65 |
tā kāūna pasāyaṁ accāsattipi cayasu ramaṇīsu । paradāraviramaṇavayaṁ mailijjai jēṇa naranāha ! ||66॥
iya paṇī maṇi bhaṇēi juttaṁ taē imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ । ajjavi gurukammō haṁ na samatyō ērisa kārḍa ||37|
tō tīē appāṇaṁ mōyāvēūṇa sugurupāsamma | paḍivannā jiṇadikkhā mōkkhamuhaṁ vaḷamāṇīē || 68 ||
sujasōvivisayagiddha giddha iva āmisammi aṇavarayaṁ । na muyai tibvahilāsaṁ ramaṇīramaṇīyadēhēsu || 69|
thīsēvaappasaṁga jāō ghāukhaō ta tassa । taha saṁjāō khāsō kisō vivannō ya dēhēṇa || 70 ||
savvā viratāō cittēṇa tahāvi bajjhaciṭṭhāē । daṁsaṁti ya aṇurāyaṁ tappuraō paṇaiṇīu tahā ॥ 71 ॥
jaha jaha tāō piccha chaṇidukyaṇāu laḍahanayaṇāu । taha taha ahiyayaraṁ ciya visaēsa maṇaṁ paya || 72 |
ēgāṇa uvari caraṇē khivēi annāṇa bāhulaiyāō । saṁṭavara kāvi cihnarē saṁvāhai kāvi jaṁghāō ||73 ||
vāvārai savvāō kamēṇa kāmaggahābhibhūō sō । bhajjāō virattāō bhavāu tassaviya citi ॥ 74 ॥
ramatē ramaṇībhiḥ sārdhamanavarataṁ ratarasa āsaktaḥ । kamalaśriyā bhaṇitō'thānyadā vinayapraṇatayā ॥ 61 ॥
yuṣmādr̥śānāṁ nr̥papuṅgavānāṁ suviditavastutattvānām | śāstrapraśastamatīnāṁ viṣayaprasaṅgaḥ khalu ma yuktaḥ ||62
vāñchāvicchēdārtha bhōgān bhuñjatē bhōginō yē tē । siñcanti praśamanārthaṁ ghr̥tāhutyā hutāśanam ॥63॥
vāñchāvyādhirasādhyō na nivartata auṣatrairapi kr̥taiḥ । tasmāttasyā utthānaṁ nirōddhavyaṁ hitaiṣibhiḥ || 64 ॥
svapnaprāptapānīyapānēna yathā praṇaśyati na tr̥ṣṇā । viṣayapipāsāpi tathā na nivartatē bhōgasēvayā ||65॥
tasmātkr̥tvā prasādamatyāsaktimapi tyaja ramaṇīpu । paradārāṁvaramaṇatrataṁ malinīkriyatē yēna naranātha ! ॥ 66 ॥
iti praṇayinyā bhaṇitē bhaṇati yuktaṁ tvayēdaṁ bhaṇitam । adyāpi gurukarmāhaṁ na samartha īdr̥śaṁ kartum ॥ 67 ॥
tatastayā''tmānaṁ mōcayitvā sugurupārśvē । pratipannā jinadīkṣā mōkṣamukhaṁ vāñchantyā ॥ 38 ॥
suyaśā api viṣayagr̥ddhō gr̥ddha ivābhiṣa'navaratam । na muñcati tatrābhilāṣaṁ ramaṇīramaṇīyadēhēṣu ॥ 69 ॥
strīsēvātiprasaṅgājjātō ghātukṣayastatastasya । tathā saṁjātaḥ kāsaḥ vr̥śaḥ vivarṇaśva dēhēna ॥ 70 ॥
sarvāṁ viraktāścittēna tathāpi bāhyacēṣṭayā । daśayanti cānurāgaṁ tatpurataḥ praṇayinyastathā ॥ 71 ॥
yathā yathā tāḥ pr̥cchati kṣaṇēnduvadanā ramyanayanāḥ । tathā tathā'dhikataramēva viṣayēṣu manaḥ pravartatē ॥ 72 ॥
ēkāsāmupari caraṇau kṣipatyanyāsāṁ bāhulatē । saṁsthāpayati kā api cikurē saṁvāhayati kābhirapi jaṛē ||
vyāpārayati sarvāḥ kramēṇa kāmagrahābhibhūtaḥ saḥ । bhāryā viraktā bhavāt tasyāpi ca cintayanti ॥74॥

ahaha ahō ! māhappaṁ mōhassa sudāruṇaṁ maṇē phurai । ēyassa puhaivaiṇō jāmadisaṁ patthiyassāvi ||75 ||
aha paṇaiṇīhi bhaṇiō sāmiya ! dhammammi āyaraṁ kuṇasu । jō saha jāi hōhī bhavaṁtarē duhaparitāī ॥ 76 ॥
ēyāō paṇaīṇīō taha cauraṁga balaṁ ca riddhīō । na bhavaṁtaramaṇujāīṇi nāha ! dhammaṁ pamōttūṇa || 77 ||
tā muṁca mahāmōhaṁ amhāṇuvariṁpi, ciṁtasu sakajjaṁ । taṁ sōḍaṇaṁ kuviō bhaṇēi huṁ jāṇiyaṁ tumha ॥ 78 ॥

apariccaiḍaṁ visaē giddhō itthīsu sō marēūṇa । aṭṭajjhāṇōvagaō uvavanna tiriyajāīē ॥ 80 ॥
lahiūṇa puṇō bōrhi bhavammi sahiūṇa dukkhasaṁghāyaṁ । lahihī siddhisahaṁpi hu sujasō kampakkhayaṁ kāuṁ ॥

atha praṇayinībhirbhaṇitaḥ svāmin ! dharma ādaraṁ kuruṣva । yaḥ saha yāti bhaviṣyati bhavāntarē duḥkhaparitrāyī ॥
ētāḥ praṇayinyastathā caturaṅgaṁ balaṁ ca r̥ddhayaḥ । na bhavāntarānuyāyinyō nātha ! dharma pramucya ||77 ||
tasmānmuñca mahāmōhamasmākamuparyapi, cintaya svakāryam । tat śrutvā kupitō bhaṇati huṁ jñātaṁ yuṣmākam ॥
sarvamapi svarūpaṁ yadicchata mriyamāṇaṁ māmidānīm । tata ādhivyādhivēdanā viśēṣatastasya saṁjātāḥ ॥79॥
aparityajya viṣayān gr̥ddhaḥ strīṣu sa mr̥tvā । ārtadhyānōpagata upapannastiryagjātau ॥80॥
labdhvā punarbōdhaṁ bhavē sahitvā duḥkhasaṁghātam । lapsyatē siddhisukhamapi hi suyaśāḥ karmakṣayaṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 81 ॥
sarvāpi khalu sāmagrī prāptā suyaśasā nāśitā paścāt । kāmē tītrābhilāṣastasmāttyaktavyaḥ sukhaiṣibhiḥ ॥ 82 ॥
niścitaṁ niṣkalaṅkaliṁ līlayā dharanti yē mahāsattvāḥ । tē bhuvanavandanīyā bhūtvā sidhyanti vidhūtarajasaḥ ॥ 83 ॥

nibhacchiyāē tīē visajuttā mōyagā kayā ēē । tumhakaē, taha avisaṁ mōyagadugamattaṇō juggaṁ ॥ 15॥

aha bhāriyāē bhaṇiō sēṇō jaha niyagharaṁ sadavvaṁpiṁ । puttāṇa taē dinnaṁ tā taṁ kaha hō hisi iyāṇi ? ||

jñātajinavacanānāṁ bhāvitabhava bhūriduḥkhasvarūpāṇām । yajjāyata iha kalahō'haha ahō ! mōhamāhātmyam॥29॥
tatastē saṁvēgaparāḥ parasparaṁ kṣamayantyaparādham । mā khalu kaṣāyavaśānāṁ samyaktvaṁ galatvasmākam ||30||
atha bhāryayā bhaṇitaḥ sēnō yathā nijagr̥haṁ sadravyamapi । putrēbhyastvayā dattaṁ tatastvaṁ kathaṁ bhaviṣyasīdānīm ! ॥
tataḥ sēnēna bhaṇitaṁ yasya manasi jinamataṁ sadā vasati । tasyārthēna gr̥hēṇa vā cintāmaṇināpi kā gaṇanā ? ||
tatastayā sa bhaṇitō bhramaṁ bhikṣāṁ sāṁprataṁ vrataṁ gr̥hītvā । śmaśānē śūnyagr̥hē dēvakulē vāpi tvaṁ vasa ॥ 33॥
sa bhaṇati bhava dhīrā kramēṇaitadapyācariṣyāmi । aihalōkikamapi darśayāmi tāvattatva dharmamāhātmyam ॥ 34॥
iti bhaṇitvā gēhāt prāptō nijamittramantrigēhēṁ । kathayati kuṭumbavr̥ttaṁ tatpuratō mārgayati gr̥hamapi ॥ 35 ॥
bhaṇati sacivō'pi bāndhava ! nr̥pagr̥hamastīti mudgarapraviṣṭam । kintu sadōṣaṁ na hi vasati kō'pi kadāpi tasmin gr̥hē
yadi punarvarmaprabhāvātprabhaviṣyati vyantarō na tava kimapi । tatastēna śakunagranthirbaddhaḥ prāptaśca tasmin gr̥hē ॥ 37 ॥
naiṣēdhikīṁ kr̥tvā'nujñāpya gataḥ sa gr̥hamadhyē । īrṣyā pratikramya svādhyāyaṁ karōti sa ēvam ||38||
gajamētāryamahāmuniskandakaśiṣyādisādhucaritāni । smaran kathaṁ kupyasi ētāvanmātrē'pi rē jīva ! ||39||
paśya prāṇavināśē'pi na paridviṣanti yē mahāsattvāḥ । tava punahīnasattvasya vacanamātrē'pyēṣā kṣamā ॥ 40 ॥
rē jīva ! sukhaduḥkhēṣu nimittamātraṁ parō jīvānāmiti । svakr̥taphalaṁ bhuñjānaḥ kasmānmudhā kupyasi parasmai ! ||
11

mōhavimūḍhā jīvā atthē ya gharē ya mucchiyā dhaṇiyaṁ । jiṇavayaṇamayāṇaṁtā bhayaṁti saṁsārakaṁtārē || 42 ॥
śrī ahō aṇajjō mōhō jamimēṇa mōhiyā jīvā । na gaṇaṁti puttamittē paharaṁtā nikvinisaṁsā ॥43॥
iya sō jā paharadugaṁ rayaṇīē kuṇai pavarasajjhāyaṁ । tō vāṇamaṁtarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ suṇiūṇa dvēiṇaṁ ॥ 44 ॥
muṭu ta haṁ dhariō nivaḍatō viyaḍabhavamahāayaḍē । sō haṁ surō sarōsō ēyaṁ ubvāsiyaṁ jēṇa || 45 ||
tappuṭṭēṇaṁ kahiyē ēyassāmī purā ahaṁ āsi । maha dō puttā lahuō aiiḍō tassa gharasāraṁ ॥ 46 ॥
dāu jō vibhinnaharē tassa kiṁpi dāūṇa | tō kuddhēṇaṁ tēṇaṁ ahayaṁ mārāviō, pacchā ॥47॥
lahuō dharāviṇa rāyaulē appaṇā siṁhaṁ gahiyē । sōvi maō guttīē ahaṁ tu iha vaṁtaśē jāō ॥ 48 ॥
nāūṇa vibhagēṇaṁ niyajisuyassa vilasiyaṁ tō sō । sakuṭuṁba udaviō annōvi hu vasaī jō kōi ॥ 49 ॥
sōvi marai nita ii jāyē uccasaṁ imaṁ gēhaṁ । saṁpai taṁ dhammagurū tō tujjha imaṁ maē dinaṁ ॥ 50 ॥
sanihāṇaṁpi lahuṁpi hu ukkhaṇiūṇaṁ samappara tassa । dasa lakkhā saṁjāyā tampi taō pabhaṇaē sēṇō ॥
igalakkhō mōkkalaō sēsā nava lakkhagāu dhammammi । dāhissaṁ, tuha punnaṁ, sō pabhaṇai tujjhavi tayaddhaṁ ॥
annaṁpi kiṁpi pabhaṇasu jaṁ kāyavvaṁ maē mahābhāga ! | paccuvayārasamatthō na hōmi tuha jīviēṇāvi ॥53॥
tuha sajjhāyaṁ suṇiuṁ kiyā ki viyāṇi tattō । cattō vairapabaṁdhō, sēṇō tō bhai taṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 54 ॥
savvēhivi jīvēhi dvē paṁcidiyattaṇē pavarē । appahiyaṁ kāyavvaṁ parahiyakaraṇēṇa taṁ hōi || 55 ||
jaṁ parahiṁyaṁ vihijjaī jiṇidavayaṇānusāraō sammaṁ । pariṇamai appaṇō taṁ hiyabhāvēṇa na saṁdēhō ॥ 56 ॥
mōhavimūḍhā jīvā arthē ca gr̥hē ca mūrcchitā gāḍham । jinavacanamajānantō bhramanti saṁsārakāntārē ||42॥
vig dhigahōsnāryō mōhō yadanēna mōhitā jīvāḥ । na gaṇayanti putramittrāṇi praharantō niṣkr̥panr̥śaṁsāḥ ॥
iti sa yāvatpraharadvikaṁ rajanyāṁ karōti pravarasvādhyāyam । tatō vānavyantarēṇa bhaṇitaṁ śrutvā hr̥ṣṭēna || 44 ॥
suṣṭutvayā'haṁ ghr̥tō nipatan vikaṭabhava mahāvaṭē । sō'haṁ suraḥ sarōṣa ētadudvāsitaṁ yēna ॥45॥
tatpr̥ṣṭēna kathitamētatsvāmī purā'hamāsam । mama dvau putrau laghuratīṣṭastasmai gr̥hasāram ॥46॥
dattvā jyēṣṭhaḥ sthāpitō bhinnagr̥hē tasmai kimapi dattvā । tataḥ kruddhēna tēnāhaṁ māritaḥ, paścāt ॥47॥
laghu dhārayitvā rājakula ātmanā gr̥haṁ gr̥hītam । sō'pi mr̥tō guptāvahaṁ tviha vyantarō jātaḥ ॥ 48 ॥
jñātvā vibhaṅgēna nijajyēṣṭhasutasya vilasitaṁ tataḥ saḥ । sakuṭumba udbhāvitō'nyapi hi vasati yaḥ kō'pi ॥ 49 ॥
sō'pi mriyatē nirbhrāntamiti jātamudvasamidaṁ gēham । saṁprati tvaṁ dharmagurustatastubhyamidaṁ mayā dattam ||10|
svanidhānamapi laghvapi khalūtkhāya samarpayati tasmai । daśa lakṣāḥ saṁjātāstasmiṁstataḥ prabhaṇati sēnaḥ ॥51॥
ēka lakṣa ucitaḥ śēṣān nava lakṣāṁstu dharmē । dāsyē, tava puṇyaṁ, sa prabhaṇati tavāpi tadardham ॥12॥
anyadapi kimapi pramaṇa yatkartavyaṁ mayā mahābhāga ! । pratyupakārasamarthō na bhavāmi tava jīvitēnāpi ॥ 53 ॥
tava svādhyāyaṁ śrutvā kr̥tyākr̥tyaṁ vijñāya tataḥ । tyaktō vairaprabandhaḥ, sēnastatō bhaṇati tamēvam ॥54॥
sarvairapi jīvai pañcēndriyatvē pravarē । ātmahitaṁ kartavyaṁ parahitakaraṇēna tad bhavati ॥ 155 ॥

supāsanāha cariśrammi --
jē paramaṁgalakaraṇēṇa appaṇō maṁgalaṁ pakappaṁti । jiṇavayaṇabāhirā tē na muṇati hi tattaō sahiyaṁ ॥
tā apahiyē dhammaṁ mōtuṁ anna na vijjaē lōē । tā tattha taē suravara ! kāvvō ujjamō ni || 58
|
tō sō hatti bhaṇiuṁ gaō taō diyarammi uiyammi । tabbhajjā puramajjhē gavēmayaṁtī gihē tasmi ॥69 |
pattā piccha siddhiṁ visiddhaāharaṇarē hirasarīraṁ । pamaṇai ahaṁ nivvinnā gavēsayaṁtī tumaṁ suhaya ! ||60|
kēṇa imaṁ āharaṇaṁ kēṇa ya davvaṁ vinnayaṁ ēyaṁ ? । sō bhaṇai piē ! dhammēṇa caiva mā puccha tamannaṁ ॥ 61|
tō takkhaṇēṇa siṭṭī pattō jinamaṁdirapi jiṇapūyaṁ । kāuṁ savittharaṁ ciya kārāva pavarapicchaṇayaṁ ॥ 62 ॥
sammāṇēuṁ jāyagajapi namiūṇa gurujaṇaṁ payaō । pattō sō tammi gihē bhuṁjai sāhammiyasamēō || 63 |
rayaṇīya vaṁtarī sō rāyanihīō apatthiōvi lahū । ukkhaṇiuṁ kalasasayaṁ siddhigihē khivai nēhēṇa ॥
bhayamā nivaiyaṁ kāhisi sicchāē dēsu dāṇāī । vaiyammi imē davvē puṇaravi ya samappaissāmi |
jā kila kiṁciva maṇihī tāva gaō vaṁtarī niyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ । siṭṭī picchivi kalasē nivanāmaṁkiē sahasā ।
vittaṇaṁ paccūsē uvāyaṇaṁ suyaṇalōyapariyariō । nivadaṁsaṇa karēī kahai ya suravihiyavr̥ttaṁtaṁ ॥67॥
rāyāvi kalasamēgaṁ āṇāvara picchaē niyayanāmaṁ । tō tuṭṭō bhaṇai imaṁ mavi tuha caiva dinaṁti || 68|
tō saṁtōsaparēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ sēṇēṇa dēva ! dasa lakkhā । jē vaṁtarēṇa dinnā tāṇavi majjhāu igalakkhō || 69 ॥
maha sattāē sēsaṁ navalakkhapamāṇayaṁ tu jaṁ davvaṁ । taṁ dhammē dāhissaṁ vaṁtaravayaṇēṇa punnaṭṭhā ॥ 70 ॥
yat parahiṁta vidhīyatē jinēndravacanānusārataḥ samyak । pariṇamata ātmanastad hitabhāvēna na saṁdēhaḥ ||66 ॥
yē parāniṣṭakaraṇēnātmanō maṅgalaṁ prakalpayanti । jinavacanabāhyāstē na jānanti hi tattvataḥ svahitam ||57 ||
tasmādātmahitaṁ dharmaṁ muktvā'nyad na vidyatē lōkē । tasmāttatra tvayā suravara ! kartavya udyamō nityam ||18||
tataḥ sa tathēti bhaṇitvā gatastatō dinakara uditē । tadbhāryā puramadhyē gavēṣayantī gr̥hē tasmin ॥ 59 ॥
prāptā paśyati śrēṣṭhinaṁ viśiṣṭābharaṇarājitr̥śarīram । prabhaṇatyahaṁ nirviṇṇā gavēṣayantī tvāṁ subhaga ! ॥ 60॥
kēnēdamābharaṇaṁ kēna ca dravyaṁ vitīrṇamētat ? । sa bhaṇati priya ! dharmēṇaiva mā pr̥ccha tvamanyat ॥ 61 ॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna śrēṣṭhī prāptō jinamandirē jinapūjām । kr̥tvā savistaramēva kārayati pravaraprēkṣaṇakam ॥62॥
sammānya yācakajanamapi natvā gurujanaṁ prayataḥ । prāptaḥ sa tasmin gr̥hē bhutē sādharmikasamētaḥ ||63॥
rajanyāṁ vyantaraḥ sa rāja nidhitō'prārthitō'pi laghu । utkhāya kalaśaśataṁ śrēṣṭhigr̥hē kṣipati snēhēna ॥ 64 ॥
bhaṇati ca mā nr̥patibhayaṁ kārṣīḥ svēcchayā dēhi dānāni । vyayitē'smindravyē punarapi ca samarpayiṣyāmi ||
yāvatkila kiñcidapi bhaṇiṣyati tāvadbhutō vyantarō nijaṁ sthānam । śrēṣṭhī dr̥ṣṭrā kalaśānnr̥panāmāṅkitān sahasā ।
gr̥hītvā pratyūṣa upāyanaṁ sujanalōkaparikaritaḥ । nr̥padarśanaṁ karōti kathayati ca suravihitavr̥ttāntam ॥67॥
rājāpi kalaśamēkamānāyayati paśyati nijanāma । tatastuṣṭō bhaṇatīmaṁ mayāpi tubhyamēva dattamiti ॥ 68 ॥
tataḥ saṁtōṣaparēṇa maṇitaṁ sēnēna dēva ! daśa lakṣāḥ । yē vyantarēṇa dattāstēṣāmapi madhyādēkalakṣaḥ ॥ 69 ॥

hāīparimāṇaṁ kāuṁ jōēi pēlahiyāīyaṁ । ailōhaggahaghatthō sō pāvara navaghaṇō duhaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi ;-
asthi puramudayasēlava sūradiyarāyasaṁgamasaiṇhaṁ । udayapuraṁ nāmēṇaṁ udayāiccō ya tattha nivō ||2||
taha nivasa tattha vaṇī navaghaṇō navaghaṇōvva aṇavarayaṁ । dāṇasaililēṇa varisai samatthaatthiyaṇakhittēsu ॥
tassaviya piyā suhasīlasāliṇī saṁpayatti nāmēṇa । ainēhanivbharāī parōpparaṁ visayasattāī || 4 ||
ciṭṭhēti tāī, ēttō jiṇabhavaṇē ucchavammi pāraddhē । kōūhalakaliyāī pattāī tattha picchaṁti || 5 |
sūriṁ guṇarayaṇanihiṁ sāvayadhammaṁ kahaṁtayaṁ saṁtaṁ । bhavvāṇa taō tāīvi suṇaṁti namiūṇa taṁ cēka || 6 ||
tammi samayammi sūrī sāhai paṁcamamaṇuvvayaṁ tattō । sammattaṁ gahiūṇaṁ tēhivi taṁ caiva paḍivannaṁ ॥7॥
aṇusāsiyāī guruṇā pattāī himmatuṭṭhāī । apputtāī tattō pālaṁti vihīē jidhammaṁ ||8||
taha suvisuddha ēṇaṁ navaghaṇavaṇiō karēi vāṇijjaṁ । niyahaṭṭē uvaviṭṭhō visiṭṭhapaṇiēhiṁ niyaēhiṁ ॥ 9 ॥
aha kōvi ṭhakkurō kiṇai tassa haṭṭammi dasasahassāṇaṁ । bhaṁḍaṁ dāu dammē lēi puṇō taha puṇō dēi ॥ 10 ॥
aha annayā ya tēṇaṁ uddhārē vīsasahassadammāṇaṁ । gahiyā kappaḍamāī maggai tō navaghaṇō mulaṁ ॥ 11 ॥
thakō kuhaṇi dāu ruvagamittaṁpi dēi nō tassa । tō sō sāhai maṁtissa sōvi maggēi davvaddhaṁ ॥ 12॥
tatō aṁgarakvassa sāhaē sōvi maggaē addhaṁ । tō purasiṭṭhissa talārayassa taha tēvi maggati ॥ 13॥
tō pattō sa vilakkhō niyagēhaṁ bhāriyāē tō puṭṭhō । ubbiggō viya dīsasi kimakaṁḍē suhaya ! sāhēsu ||
gēhādiparimāṇaṁ kr̥tvā yōjayati parimitātītam । atilōbhagrahagrastaḥ sa prāpnōti navaghana iva duḥkham ॥ 1॥
asti puramudayaśaila iva śū (sū) radvijarāja saṁgamasatr̥ṣṇam । udayapuraṁ nāmnā udayādityaśca tatra nr̥paḥ ||2|
tathā nivasati tatra vaṇig navaghanō navaghanavadanavaratam । dānasalilēna varṣati samastārthijanakṣētrēṣu ॥ 3 ॥
tasyāpi ca priyā śubhaśīlaśālinī saṁpaditi nāmnā । atisnēhanirbharau parasparaṁ viṣayasaktau ॥4॥
tiṣṭhatastau itō jinabhavana utsavē prārabdhē । kutūhalakalitau prāptau tatra paśyataḥ ॥5॥
sūriṁ guṇaratnanidhiṁ śrāvakadharma kathayantaṁ santam । bhavyēbhyastatastāvapi śr̥ṇutō natvā tamēva ॥ 6 ॥
tasminsamayē sūriḥ kathayati pañcamamaṇutrataṁ tataḥ । samyaktvaṁ gr̥hītvā tābhyāmapi tadēva pratipannam ॥ 7॥
anuśāsitau guruṇā prāptau gr̥hē hr̥ṣṭatuṣṭau । aputrau tataḥ pālayatō vidhinā jinadharmam ॥8॥
tathā suviśuddha nayēna navadhanavaṇik karōti vāṇijyam । nijahaṭṭa upaviṣṭō viśiṣṭapaṇyairnijaiḥ ||9||
atha kō'pi ṭhakkuraḥ krīṇāti tasya haṭṭē daśasahasyāḥ । bhāṇḍaṁ dattvā drammāllāti punastathā punardadāti ॥ 10 ॥
athānyadā ca tēnōddhārē viṁśatisahasradrammāṇām । gr̥hītāḥ karpaṭādayō mārgayati tatō navaghanō mūlyam ॥ 11 ॥
sthitaḥ kūrparaṁ dattvā rūpyakamātramapi dadāti nō tasya । tataḥ sa kathayati mantriṇē sō'pi mārgayati dravyārdham॥
tatō'ṅgarakṣāya kathayati sō'pi mārgayatyardham । tataḥ puraśrēṣṭhinē purarakṣakāya tathā tāvapi mārgayataḥ ॥ 13॥
1 stra phala । 2 sva. rā. navaghaṇō sō pāvara dukkhaṁ । 3 ga, vārīhiṁ 1

tēvi kahiyaṁ savvaṁ savittharaṁ ṭhakkurāivavahāraṁ । tō sō tīē bhaṇiō ahaṁ bhalissāmi savvaṁpi ।। 15 ।।
taṁ tāmiva gāmē gacchacha ciṁtēmi jāva hamuvāyaṁ । mai saddiēṇa tumaē āgaṁtavvaṁ puṇō ēttha ॥ 16॥
ēvaṁti mantriṇaṁ navaghaṇavaṇiō gaō ya gāmammi । pattā sacivassa gihē sāvi piyā saṁpayā tassa || 17||
ubbhaḍakayasiṁgārā lāyannavilāsahāsakamaṇīyā । maṁtipuraō uvaviṭṭhā uvāyaṇaṁ kiṁpi kāūṇa || 18 |
rayaṇīya padamā visajjiyāsēsapariyaṇō maṁtī । tadaṁsaṇēṇa khuhiō paḍhai sakāmaṁ taō ēvaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
paraṁ juṇhā uṇhā garalasarisō caṁdanarasō, kharaṁ khārō hārō sisirapavaṇā dēhatavaṇā ।
muṇālī bāṇālī jalai va jaladā taṇugayā, niviṭṭhā jaṁ diṭṭhā kamalavayaṇā dīhanayaṇā ||20|
taṁ khuhiyaṁ nāūṇaṁ bhaṇē sā suṇasu majjha vinnattiṁ । tā ūsasiyamaṇō sō bhaṇēi āisa jaṁ kajjaṁ ॥ 21 ॥
tō vibhattō tī ṭhakkarasaṁbaṁdhivaiyarō saccō । tēṇavi sō paḍivannō bhaṇiyā ya tahā jahā suya ! || 22 ||
tumavi majjha kajjaṁ karaṇīyaṁ kiṁpi mayaṇavihurassa । tō tīē paḍibhaṇiyaṁ kimajuttaṁ kiṁtu kallammi ॥ 23 ॥
ajjāhaṁ baṁbharayā paccūsē paḍivayāē rayaṇīē । āgaṁtavvaṁ tumaē nivyaṁtaṁ padamajāmasmi || 24 ॥
iya vōtuṁ sā pattā nivaṁgarakkhassa gēhamaha sōvi । daṭṭhē ciṁtēṛa maṇē kā ēsā bāliyā ēi || 25 ||
pāyālā nāgagaṇā ṇu vijjāharī ṇu dēvī ṇu । asuraramaṇī ṇu siddhaṁgaṇā ṇu naralōyamōinnā || 26 ॥
kōsalliḍaṁ vihē ubaviṭṭhā āsaṇammi tō puṭṭhā | ṭhakkuravaiyaramakkhaṛa tō sō pabhaṇēi tōsēṇaṁ ||27||
tataḥ prāptaḥ sa vilakṣō nijagēhaṁ bhāryayā tataḥ pr̥ṣṭaḥ । udvigna iva dr̥śyasē kimakāṇḍē subhaga ! kathaya ॥ 14 ॥
tēnāpi kathitaḥ sarvaḥ savistaraṁ ṭhakkurādivyavahāraḥ । tataḥ sa tayā bhaṇitō'haṁ bhaliṣyē sarvamapi ॥ 15॥
tvaṁ tasmātkasminnapi grāmē gaccha cintayāmi yāvadahamupāyam । mayā śabditēna tvayā''gantavyaṁ punaratra ॥ 16 ॥
ēvamiti matvā navaghanavaṇig gataśca grāmē । prāptā sacivasya gr̥hē sāpi priyā saṁpat tasya ॥17॥
udbhaṭakr̥taśr̥ṅgārā lāvaṇyavilāsahāsakamanīyā | mantripurata upaviṣṭōpāyanaṁ kimapi kr̥tvā ॥ 18 ॥
rajanyāḥ prathamayāmē visarjitāśēṣaparijanō mantrī । taddarśanēna kṣubhitaḥ paṭhati sakāmaṁ tata ēvam ||19||
paraṁ jyōtsnōṣṇā garalasadr̥śaścandanarasaḥ, kharaṁ khārō hāraḥ śiśirapavanā dēhatapanāḥ ।
mr̥ṇālī bāṇālī jvalati ca jalārdrā tanugatā, niviṣṭā yad dr̥ṣṭā kamalavadanā dīrghanayanā ॥20॥
taṁ kṣubhitaṁ jñātvā bhaṇati sā śr̥ṇu mama vijñaptim । tata ucchasitamanāḥ sa bhaṇatyādiśa yatkāryam ॥21॥
tatō vijñaptastayā ṭhakkurasaṁbandhivyatikaraḥ sarvaḥ । tēnāpi sa pratipannō bhaṇitā ca tathā yathā sutanu ! ॥ 22 ॥
tvayāpi mama kāryaṁ karaṇīyaṁ kimapi madanavidhurasya । tatastayā pratibhaṇitaṁ kimayuktaṁ kintu kalyē ॥ 23 ॥
adyāhaṁ brahmaratā pratyūṣē pratipadōṁ rajanyāḥ । āgantavyaṁ tvayā nirbhrāntaṁ prathamayāmē ॥ 24 ॥
ityuktvā sā prāptā nr̥pāṅgarakṣasya gēhamatha sō'pi । dr̥ṣṭvā cintayati manasi kaiṣā bālikaiti ॥ 25 ॥
pātālād nāgāṅganā nu vidyādharī nu dēvī nu । asuraramaṇī nu siddhāṅganā nu naralōkamavatīrṇā ॥26॥
kauśalikāṁ vidhāyōpaviṣṭāṁsssanē tataḥ pr̥ṣṭā । ṭhakkuravyatikaramākhyāti tataḥ sa prabhaṇati tōṣēṇa ॥ 27 ॥

supāsanāha ammi-
ēyaṁ tuha kajjamahaṁ sāhissaṁ nicchaēṇa pasayacchi ! | amhāṇavi jaṁ kajjaṁ maṇubbhavaṁ taṁ taē kajjaṁ ॥ 28 ॥
tō tīē paḍibhaṇiyaṁ jaṁ saikkaṁ taṁ api kā hissaṁ । jalalavacaladēhassavi sāraṁ taṁ suyaṇakajjammi ||29||
jaṁ jāi uvaōgaṁ, iya suṇiuṁ sō bhaṇēi saṁtu hō । saṁpayamavi paḍaṇō haṁ sāvi hu paccuttaraṁ kāuṁ ||30||
taṁ bhai bīyapaharē paḍivayarayaṇīē haṁ sarēyavvā । iya bhaṇivi siṭṭitalavara gihē gayā tēhiṁ diṭṭhā ya ॥ 31 ॥
kahūṁ ।
pāusasirivva unnayapaōharā dhaṇulayantra guṇakaliyā । khaggalayavva suhārā sutucchamajjhā bhavasuhaṁva ॥ 32॥
tāvi puvvattavihī kahiō, tēhivi tahēva paḍibhaṇiyaṁ । taiyapaharammi siṭṭhī āhūō kōṭavālō u ||
carimē jāmē, ittō samāgayā sāvi niyayagēhammi । pabhaṇai ya duiyadivasē paōsasamaē niyaṁ dāsi || 34 ||
paṇaṁ karēhi maha majjaṇatthamuvagaraṇamuṇhasalilāī । aipauraṁ, tīi tahā vihiē tō paḍhamapaharammi ||35||
saṁpatō sō sacivō abhuṭṭhēūṇa gaṁdhatillēṇa । abhaṁgiyamuvvadr̥i sayaṁ taō bahalakhaliyāē ||36||
ussiṁca sirakamalaṁ jā sā sacivassa tā duvārammi | viyaḍakavāḍakaḍāṇaṁ khaḍakaō niṇiō tattō ॥
pēsēūṇaṁ dāsi jōyāvara jāva dāradēsaṁ sā । tō bhaṇai aṁgarakkhō ughāḍau kavāḍayaṁ jhatti ||38||
tassadaṁ suṇiūṇaṁ bhīō maṁtī - bhaṇēi katthavi ya | khivasu piē! maṁ khippaṁ jāvēsō bōlaī kahavi ॥ 39 ॥
tō ōyariyāmajjhē khittō maṁtī nirubhiyaṁ dāraṁ । dinnaṁ ca tālayaṁ tā bhayabhīō ciṭṭhaē tattha ॥40॥
ētattava kāryamahaṁ sādhayiṣyāmi niścayēna mr̥gākṣi ! | asmākamapi yatkārya manaudbhavaṁ tattayā kāryam ॥ 28॥
tatastayā pratibhaṇitaṁ yacchakyaṁ tadahamapi kariṣyē । jalalavacaladēhasyāpi sāraṁ tat sujanakāryē ॥ 29 ॥
yad yātyupayōgam, iti śrutvā sa bhaṇati saṁtuṣṭaḥ । sāṁpratamapi praguṇō'haṁ sāpi hi pratyuttaraṁ kr̥tvā ॥ 30 ॥
taṁ bhaṇati dvitīyapraharē pratipadrajanyāmahaṁ sartavyā । iti bhaṇitvā śrēṣṭhipurarakṣakagr̥hē gatā tābhyāṁ dr̥ṣṭā ca ॥
katham ।
prāvr̥ṭ śrīrivōnnatapayōdharā dhanurlatēva guṇakalitā । khagalatēva suhā ( dhā ) rā sutucchamadhyā bhavasukhamiva ॥ 32 ॥
tayōrapi pūrvōktavidhiḥ kathitaḥ, tābhyāmapi tathaiva pratibhaṇitam । tr̥tīyapraharē śrēṣṭhayāhūtō durgapālastu ||33||
caramē yāmē, itaḥ samāgatā sāpi nijagēhē । prabhaṇati ca dvitīyadivasē pradōṣasamayē nijāṁ dāsīm ||34||
praguṇaṁ kuru mama majjanārthamupakaraṇamuṣṇasalilādi । atipracuraṁ tayā tathā vihitē tataḥ prathamapraharē || 35 ||
saṁprāptaḥ sa sacivō'bhyutthāya gandhatailēna । abhyaṅgamuddhartayati svayaṁ tatō bahalakha liyā ||36||
utsiñcati śiraḥkamalaṁ yāvatsā sacivasya tāvad dvārē । vikaṭakapāṭaśr̥ṅkhalānāṁ khaṭatkāraḥ śrutastataḥ ॥ 37 ॥
prēṣya dāsīṁ darśayati yauvad dvāradēśaṁ sā । tatō bhaṇatyaṅgarakṣa udghāṭaya kapāṭaṁ jhaṭiti ॥ 38 ॥
,
tacchabdaṁ śrutvā bhītō maṁntrī bhaṇati kutrāpi ca । kṣipa priyē ! māṁ kṣipraṁ yāvadēṣa gacchati kathamapi ||39||
tatō'pavarikāmadhyē kṣiptō mantrī niruddhaṁ dvāram । dattaṁ ca tālakaṁ tatō bhayabhītastiṣṭhati tatra ॥ 40 ॥
? ka. sajyaṁ ।

navaghaṇakahā ।
415
tattō ya aṁgarakkhō samāgaō sōvi kharaḍivi khalīē । khittō ōyariyāē siṭṭimma samāgaē jhatti ॥
puvvakamēṇa siṭṭī khittō taiyāē ōyarīyāē । carimajāmammi sahasā saṁpattē kōṭavālammi ||42 ||
sōvi hu abhaṁgēuṁ kharaḍēvi khalīē ōariyāē । khittō saṁpattammī niyaē baṁdhummi sahasēva || 43 ॥
saṁvasā sōvi hu pukāratō gimmivi paviṭṭō । muṭṭhō muṭṭhatti payaṁpirō ya takaṁṭhamalaggō || 44 ॥
rōya navaghaṇaguṇavaṇēṇa tā saṁpayāci karuṇayaraṁ । dukkhattā iva rōyai tāṇaṁ paḍivōhaṇanimittaṁ ॥45॥
itthaṁtarammi sahasā vihāvarīviramasūyagō saṁkhō । pahaō gahīragururāvavahiriyā sēsadisivalaō || 46॥
tō miliō puralōō savvattō pasariyā imā vattā । jaha navaghaṇō vivanna, rāyā taṁ nisuṇiuṁ cittē ।
tamaputtaṁ kaliūṇaṁ maṁtigihē pēsiuṁ ca paḍihāraṁ । āṇāvā taṁ sigdhaṁ navaghaṇadavvassa gahaṇaṭṭhā ||48 ||
tō maṁtigihē gaṁtuṁ paḍihārō jā palōyaē maṁti । tāva na picchai tattō āgaṁtuṁ kahai naravaṇō || 49 ॥
tō aṁgarakkhatalavarasiṭṭīṇa gihēsu pēsiō rannā । sō vaccai navaghaṇavaiyarassa saṁsāhaṇanimittaṁ ॥ 50 ॥
tēvi sahēisu na niyai naya suddhiṁ kōvi jāṇaē tāṇa । tō puṇaravi paḍihārō rāyassa sa rūvaē ēyaṁ ।
tō vimhaiō rāyā sayaṁ gaō taggihammi uvaviṭṭhō । pabhaṇai muddhē ! mā ruyasu saṁpayaṁ mai gihaṁ pattē |
savvaṁpi niyayadavvaṁ vilasasu sicchāē dēsu dhammēṇa । khaṁḍakavaḍḍiyamittaṁpi gihimō nēya tuhataṇayaṁ ||
taṁ suṇijaṁ sā paṇa nāha ! na kajjaṁ imēṇa davvēṇa । gihissāmi vayaṁ ciya giṇhau dēvō imaṁ savvaṁ ॥
iya bhaṇiuṁ sā daṁsai ōyaraē sāhaē ya ēyāṇaṁ । majjhē navaghaṇataṇayaṁ cihna davvaṁti tō rāyā ॥ 55॥
tataścāṅgarakṣaḥ samāgataḥ sō'pi kharaṇṭayitvā khalyā । kṣiptō'pavarikāyāṁ śrēṣṭhini samāgatē jhaṭiti ॥ 41 ॥
pūrvakramēṇa śrēṣṭhī kṣiptastr̥tīyāyāmapavarikāyām । caramayā mē sahasā saṁprāptē durgapālē ||42 ॥
sō'pi khalvabhyaṅgaya kharaṇṭayitvā khalyā'pavarikāyām । kṣiptaḥ saṁprāptē nijē bandhau sahasaiva ॥ 43॥
saṁkētavaśāt sō'pi hi pūtkurvan gr̥hē'pi praviṣṭaḥ । muṣṭō muṣṭa iti prajalpitā ca tatkaṇṭhamanulagnaḥ ॥44॥
rōditi navaghanaguṇavarṇanēna tadā saṁpadapi karuṇataram | duḥkhārttēva rōditi tēṣāṁ pratibōdhananimittam ॥45॥
atrāntarē. sahasā vibhāvarīvirāmasūtrakaḥ śaṅkhaḥ । prahatō gabhīragururāvabadhiritāśēṣadigvalayaḥ || 46 ॥
tatō militaḥ puralōkaḥ sarvataḥ prasr̥tēyaṁ vārtā । yathā navavanō vipannō, rājā tat śrutvā cittē ||47 ||
tamaputraṁ kalayitvā mantrigr̥hē prēmya ca pratihāram । ānāyayati taṁ śīghraṁ navaghanadravyasya grahaṇārtham ||48 ॥
tatō mantrigr̥hē gatvā pratihārō yāvatpralōkatē mantriṇam । tāvanna paśyati tata āgatya kathayati narapatayē ||
tatō'ṅgarakṣapurarakṣaśrēṣṭhināṁ gr̥hēṣu prēṣitō rājñā । sa vrajati navaghanavyatikarasya saṁkathananimittam ॥ 50 ॥
tānapi svagr̥hēṣu na paśyati naca śuddhiṁ kō'pi jānāti tēṣām । tataḥ punarapi pratihārō rājñē sa rūpayatyēvam।।
tatō vismitō rājā svayaṁ gatastadgr̥ha upaviṣṭaḥ । prabhaṇati mugdhē ! mā rudihi sāṁprataṁ māya gr̥haṁ prāptē ||12||
sarvamapi nijadravyaṁ vilāsaya svēcchayā dēhi dharmē । khaṇḍakapardikāmātramapi gr̥hṇīmō naiva tvadīyam ||53॥
tat śrutvā sā prabhaṇati nātha ! na kāryamanēna dravyēṇa । grahīṣyāmi vratamēva gr̥hṇātu dēva idaṁ sarvam ||54॥

supāsaṁnāha cariammi-
ughāḍāvara dārāī tāṇaṁ kamasō, taō ya ēkkāē । khalilittaṁgō ciṭu maṁtī, sēsāvi sēsāsu ॥56॥
tō accabhūyaṁ tāṇa sarūvaṁ nirikkhiuṁ rāyā । pucchara sacivāīē tēvi na paccuttaraṁ diti ॥ 57 ॥
tō saṁpayāē bhaṇiyaṁ dēvāhamimāṇa sayalavuttaṁtaṁ । sāhissaṁ kiṁtu paraṁ abhaē ēyāṇa nimmi || 58 ||
tō bhūvaiṇā abhaē dinē tēsiṁ ca saṁpayāē taō । ṭhakkuravuttaṁtāō kahiyaṁ savvaṁ savittharaō ॥59॥
tō naravaiṇā bhaṇiyaṁ amaca ! sacaṁ imīē jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ? । ēvaṁti tō pamaṇiē tayabhimuhaṁ jaṁpaē rāyā ॥
bhō'macca ! suhumavāyaradūrēyaravatthujāṇaṇē niuṇaṁ । naravaiṇō paramatthēṇa maṁtiṇō huṁti nayaṇāī || 61 ||
na muti vivēyavilōyaṇāī. nayaṇāī vatthuparamatthaṁ । naravaiṇō mayaṇamahaṁdhayāravihurijjamāṇāī ॥ 62 ॥
tā ēyaṁ vivarīyaṁ jāyaṁ tuha saciva ! saṁpayaṁ cētra । tā saṁpayāē bhaṇiō khamiyavvaṁ dēva ! maha ēyaṁ ॥ 63॥
kō dōsō ēyāṇaṁ mayaṇamahācaraḍapīḍiyā purisā | kāumakiccaṁ lahuyā huṁti taṇāōvi jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ||
akayavahārēṇamaṇagaēṇa kusumāuhēṇavi khaṇēṇa । jē vippati hayāsā tē huṁti lahū taṇāōvi ॥ 65॥
na ravī na havvavāhō na nisānāhō na maṇisamūhōvi । vammahatamamāhappaṁ jayammi musumr̥rijaṁ tarai ||66 ||
jaṁ natthi taṁ palōyai jaṁ vijjai taṁ na picchai payatthaṁ । ahaha ahō ! appuvvaṁ timiraṁ mihiruggamē mayaṇō ॥ 67॥
ēyassa mayaṇatimirassa nāsaṇaṁ kiṁpi vijjaē na paraṁ । mōttūṇa maṇavivēyaṁ suhavatthupayāsaṇapavīṇaṁ ॥ 68॥
kiśca ।
'āsaṁsāraṁ visayāṇa sēvaṇā hōi savvajīvāṇa । paramajaṇa sēvaṇijjaṁ na uṇō maṇayaṁpiṁ saccaraṇaṁ ॥ 69 ॥
iti ṇitvā sā darśayatyapavarakānkathayati caitēṣām । madhyē navaghanasaṁbandhi tiṣṭhati dravyamiti tatō rājā ॥
udghāṭayati dvārāṇi tēṣāṁ kramaśaḥ, tataścaikasyām । khalīliptāṅgastiṣṭhati mantrī, śēṣā api śēṣēṣu ॥ 56 ॥
tatō'tyadbhutabhūtaṁ tēṣāṁ svarūpaṁ nirīkṣya rājā । pr̥cchati sacivādīṁstē'pi na pratyuttaraṁ dadati ॥57॥
tataḥ saṁpadā bhaṇitaṁ dēvāhamēṣāṁ sakalavr̥ttāntam । kathayiṣyāmi kintu paramabhayē ētēṣāṁ dattē || 18||
tatō bhūpatinā'bhayē. dattē tēṣāṁ ca saṁpadā tataḥ । ṭhakkaravr̥ttāntātkathitaṁ sarva savistaram ||19||
tatō narapatinā bhaṇitamamātya ! satyamanayā yadbhaṇitam ? । ēvamiti tataḥ prabhaṇitē tadabhimukhaṁ jalpati rājā ॥
bhō amātya ! sūkṣmabādaradūrētaravastujñānē nivr̥ṇam । narapatēḥ paramārthēna mantriṇō bhavanti nayanāni ॥ 61 ॥
na jānītō vivēkavilōcanē nayanē vastuparamārtham । narapatērmadanamahāndhakāravidhurāyamānē ॥ 62 ॥
tasmādētad viparītaṁ jātaṁ tava saciva ! sāṁpratamēva । tadā saṁpadā bhaṇitaḥ kṣantavyaṁ dēva ! mamaitat ॥ 63 ॥
kō dōṣa ētēṣāṁ madanamahācaraṭapīḍitāḥ puruṣāḥ । kr̥tvā'kr̥tyaṁ laghavō bhavanti tr̥ṇādapi yad bhaṇitam ॥ 64 ॥
akr̥taprahārēṇānaṅgēna kusumāyudhēnāpi kṣaṇēna । yē gr̥hyantē hatāśāstē bhavanti laghavastr̥ṇādapi ॥ 65॥
na ravirna havyavāhō na niśānāthō na maṇisamūhō'pi । manmathatamōmāhātmyaṁ jagati bhaṅktuṁ śaknōti ॥ 66 ॥
yō nāsti taṁ pralōkatē yō vidyatē taṁ na paśyati padārtham । ahaha ahō ! apūrva timiraṁ mihirōdgamē madanaḥ ॥
ētasya madanatimirasya nāśanaṁ kimapi vidyatē na param । muktvā manōvivēkaṁ śubhavastuprakāśanapravīṇam ॥ 68 ॥

saccaraṇaṁ ciya saṁsārasāya rē hōi tāraṇaṁ jēṇa । tō puṭṭhā naravaiṇā caraṇaṁ kiṁ bhannai mayacchi ! ॥ 70 ॥
aṭṭhaṣpavayaṇamāyāsarūvayaṁ sā kahēi vittharaō । taṁ suṇiuṁ paḍibuddhā bhaṇati sacivāiyā ēvaṁ ॥ 71 ॥
khamasuvarāhaṁ ahaṁ mōhamahaṇṇava nimaggasavvaṁgā । nitthāriyā taicciya paramēsari paramakāruṇiṇi ! ॥72॥
tā daṁsēhi kapi hu gurūṇa payapaṁkayaṁti, aha tattha । āgaṁtūṇaṁ ujjāṇapālagō bhai naranāhaṁ ॥ 73 ॥
vaddhāvijjai dēvō dēvāsuravaṁdaṇijjapayakamalō । sirisiricaṁda muṇidō samōsaḍhō malayasamma ||74 ||
dāvai niyaṁgalaggaṁ āharaṇaṁ tassa tōsavasaō sō। tō sacivāīhi nivō bhaṇiō jaha sūripāsammi॥75॥
giṇhāmō pavvajjaṁ visajja sē jai tumaṁti sō bhaṇai । juttamiṇaṁ savvēsiṁ tumhāṇaṁ sukulajāyāṇaṁ ॥ 76 ॥
tō saṁpayā savvē kāraviyā majjaṇaṁ lahuṁ tattō | caṁdaṇacacciyaaṁgā pavarālaṁkārakayasōhā ॥77॥
maṁgalāyāṇaputraṁ caurōvi hu karivarēsu ārūḍhā । saṁpattā sanariṁdā muṇidapāsamma vitthaō || 78 ॥
tēhivi dinnā dikkhā sacivāīṇaṁ kamēṇa ghuyakammā । tē siddhisuhaṁ pattā rannāvi gahittu gihidhammaṁ ॥ 79॥
sā saṁpayā pannā bhaiṇī taha tappaīvi gāmāō । āhūō siṭṭhipaē ṭhaviō puralōyapañcakkhaṁ ||80||
sō ṭhakkarōvi bhaṇidavvaṁ dāvāviō visēsēṇa । jiṇadhammaparā cihna saṁpayā navaghaṇasamēyā ||81 ॥
kālē taō naravaipasāyaō navaghaṇō aipamattō । cāsannagihāī kiṇiuṁ mēlēi sagihassa ||82 ॥
tō bhajjāē bhaṇiō tuha aiyārō havissaī ēvaṁ । ēkkagihaṁ mukkaliyaṁ taē kayaṁ paṁcamavayam ||83 ||
|
||
āsaṁsāraṁ viṣayāṇāṁ sēvanā bhavati sarvajīvānāṁm । paramajanasēvanīyaṁ na punarmanāgapi saccaraṇam ॥69॥
saccaraṇamēva saṁsārasāgarē bhavati tāraṇaṁ yēna । tataḥ pr̥ṣṭā narapatinā caraṇaṁ kiṁ bhaṇyatē mr̥gākṣi ! ॥ 70 ॥
aṣṭapravacanamātr̥svarūpaṁ sā kathayati vistarataḥ । tat śrutvā pratibuddhā bhaṇanti sacivādaya ēvam ॥ 71 ॥
kṣamasvāparādhamasmākaṁ mōha mahārṇavanimagnasarvāṅgāḥ । nistāritāstvayaiva paramēśvari paramakāruṇikē ! ॥ 72॥
tasmād darśaya kathamapi hi gurūṇāṁ padapaṅkajamiti, atha tatra । āgatyōdyānapālakō bhaṇati naranātham ॥ 73 ॥
vardhyatē dēvō dēvāsuravandanīyapadakamalaḥ । śrīśrīcandramunīndraḥ samavasr̥tō malayadēśē ॥ 74 ॥
dāpayati nijāṅgalagnamābharaṇaṁ tasya tōṣavaśataḥ saḥ । tataḥ sacivādibhirnr̥pō bhaṇitō yathā sūripārśvē ॥75॥
gr̥hṇāmaḥ pravrajyāṁ visr̥jasi yadi tvamiti sa bhaṇati । yuktamidaṁ sarvēṣāṁ yuṣmākaṁ sukulajātānām ॥76॥
tataḥ saṁpadā sarvē kāritā majjanaṁ laghu tataḥ । candanacarcitāṅgāḥ pravarālaṁkārakr̥taśōbhāḥ ॥77॥
maṅgalapradānapūrvaṁ catvārō'pi hi karivarēṣvārūḍhāḥ । saṁprāptāḥ sanarēndrā munīndrapārśvē vistarataḥ ॥ 78 ॥
tairapi dattā dīkṣā sacivādibhyaḥ kramēṇa dhūtakarmāṇaḥ । tē siddhisukhaṁ prāptā rājñāpi gr̥hītvā gr̥hidharmam ॥
sā saṁpat prapannā bhaginī tathā tatpatirapi grāmāt । āhūtaḥ śrōṣṭhapadē sthāpitaḥ puralōkapratyakṣam ॥ 80॥
ṭhakkurō'pi bhaṇitvā dravyaṁ dāpitō viśēṣēṇa | jinadharmaparā tiṣṭhati saṁpad navaghanasamētā ॥ 81 ॥
kālēna tatō narapatiprasādatō navaghanō'tipramattaḥ । pratyāsannagr̥hāṇi krītvā mēlayati svagr̥hē ॥ 82 ॥
tatō bhāryayā bhaṇitasvānivārō bhaviṣyatyēvam । ēkagr̥hamucitaṁ tvayā kr̥taṁ pañcagavatē ॥ 83 ॥

sō bhaī ki nahaṁ ēkahiṁ ciya imaṁ khu nō duiyaṁ । sā bhaṇai bahuṁ nadvaṁ tuhavayamālinnabhāvēṇa ॥ 84 ॥
aparaṁ ca -
jai ēvaṁ niravikkhō jaṁpasa kūttarāī maha puraō । tō gharasahiōvi tumaṁ cattō vayamārissama || 85 ||
iya bhaṇiuṁ tīē vayaṁ gahiṁūṇaṁ sāhiyaṁ sayaṁ kajjaṁ । navaghaṇasiṭṭīvi duhāvi saṁpayāē pariccattō ॥ 86 ॥
tō siḍhiliyadhammō sō gahiō gharavaṁtarēṇa kēṇāvi । ummattō puramajjhē bhamēi ḍiṁbhēhiṁ pariyariō ||87||
kō hu khivē dhūli pahaṇai liṭṭhēhiṁ kōvi hu hasēi । ēvaṁ sōvi bhamaṁtō mariḍaṁ asurēsu uvavannō ||88 ||
tā thēpi vayāṇa aiyāraṁ pariharēha bhō bhavvā ! । jai vaṁchaha sivasōkkhaṁ duhadaṁdōlīē niccinnā ||89 ||
॥ iti pañcamāṇuvrataprathamāticāravipākē navaghanadr̥ṣṭāntaḥ samāptaḥ ।।
sa bhaṇati kiṁ naṣṭamēkagr̥hamēvēdaṁ khalu nō dvitīyam । sā bhaṇati bahu naṣṭaṁ tvadvratamālinyabhāvēna ॥ 84 ॥
yadyēvaṁ nirapēkṣō jalpasi kūṭōttarāṇi mama purataḥ । tatō gr̥hasahitō'pi tvaṁ tyaktō vratamācariṣyāmyaham ॥
iti bhaṇitvā tayā vrataṁ gr̥hītvā sādhitaṁ svayaṁ kāryam । navaghanaśrēṣṭhyapi dvidhāpi saṁpadā parityaktaḥ ॥ 86॥
tataḥ śithilitadharmaḥ sa gr̥hītō gr̥havyantarēṇa kēnāpi । unmattaḥ puramadhyē bhramati ḍimbhaiḥ parikaritaḥ ॥87॥
kō'pi khalu kṣipati dhūli prahanti lēṣṭubhiḥ kō'pi hi hasati । ēvaṁ sō'pi bhramanmr̥tvā'surēṣūpapannaḥ ॥ 88 ॥
tasmātstōkamapi vratānāmaticāraṁ pariharata bhō bhavyāḥ ! | yadi vāñchata śivasaukhyaṁ duḥkhadvandvālyā nirviṇṇāḥ ॥

rāyāīṇa pasāyaṁ ladhuṁ davtraṁ suhīṇa appē | jō jāva niyamaavahiṁ bharahōvva sa khaṁḍaē viraī || 1 ||
tathāhi;
puramatthi māṇakhēḍaṁ māṇavarāō tarhi mahārāyā । tassa piyā paramasirī sirivva hariṇō maṇāṇaṁdā !
tatyatthi saṁkhasiṭṭī vikkhāō khēmiyā ya sē bhajjā । tāṇaṁ ca duvē puttā bharahō rahasō ya suviṇīyā ॥
kamalasirī paumasirī bhajjā tāṇaṁ kamēṇa kamaṇīyā । bhadagabhāvōvagayaṁ savvaṁpi kuṭuṁbagaṁ tēsiṁ ॥4॥
aha tāṇaṁ puravāhi ujjāṇē gaṇivarō vijayasūrī। saṁpattō saṁpattō saṁpatō pavaraca nāṇī ||5||
dō tatthavi kī lāgaēhiṁ sō bharaha - rahasarvadhūrhi । uvasappiūṇa tattō'bhivaṁdiō bhattijuttērhi ॥ 6 ॥
aha dhammalābhaputraṁ tēvi saṁbhāsiyā samuvaiṭṭā । jiṇapannattō dhammō kahiō ya kamēṇa duvihōvi ॥ 7 ॥ ॥
paḍhasamatthērhi taō gihidhammō daṁsaṇāiō gahiō । paṁcamavayaṁ visēsēṇa saṁkaḍaṁ tēhiṁ parigahiyaṁ ॥ 8 ॥
bhaṇiō ya muṇidēṇa bharahō jaha paṁcamē vara tujjha । hōhī duiyaaiyārō tā mā taṁ saṁkaḍaṁ ginha ||9||
tēvi bhaṇiyaṁ na ya saṁkaḍaṁ imaṁ gēhiyamappadēvasiyē । iya bhaṇiraṁ namiūṇa ya pattā tē niyagihē dōvi ॥
aha annadiṇē rayaṇīē picchaē lacchidēvayaṁ sahasā । vāsabhavaṇammi bharahō rahammi tīē imaṁ bhaṇiō ।।
vacchā haṁ tuha tuhā saṁtuṭṭō javi lacchivicchaḍḍē । tahavi payacchāmi ahaṁ maggasu jaṁ ruccaē davvaṁ ॥ 12 ॥
jamhā punvabhavammivi tuma ārāhiyā ahaṁ payaō । nāō ya tumaṁ saṁpai nicalacittō jiṇamayammi ||
bhaṇiyaṁ bharaṇaṁ na hu kajjaṁ kiṁpi majjha davvēṇa । igalakkhō maha gēhē ciṭṭhai sēsassa niyamō mē ॥ 14 ॥
rājādīnāṁ prasādaṁ labdhvā dravyaṁ suhr̥ddhayō'rpayati । yō yāvanniyamāvadhiṁ bharata iva sa khaṇḍayati viratim ॥1॥
puramasti mānakhēṭaṁ mānavarājastatra mahārājaḥ । tasya priyā paramaśrīḥ śrīriva harērmana ānandā ॥2॥
tatrāsti śaṅkhaśrēṣṭhī vikhyātaḥ kṣēmikā ca tasya bhāryā । tayōśca dvau putrau bharatō rabhasaśca suvinītau ॥3॥
kamalaśrīḥ padmaśrīrbhāryā tayōḥ kramēṇa kamanīyā । bhadrakabhāvōpagataṁ sarvamapi kuṭumbaṁ tēṣām ॥4॥
atha tēṣāṁ purād bahirudyānē gaṇivarō vijayasūriḥ । saṁpātraṁ prāptaḥ saṁprāptaḥ pravaracaturjñāna ḥ ||5||
dr̥ṣṭastatrāpi krīḍāgatābhyāṁ sa bharatarabhasabandhubhyām । upasr̥ṣya tatō'bhivanditō bhaktiyuktābhyām ॥ 6 ॥
atha dharmalābhapūrvaṁ tēnāpi saṁbhāṣitau samupaviṣṭau । jinaprajñaptō dharmaḥ kathitaśca kramēṇa dvividhō'pi ॥ 7 ॥
prathamāsamarthābhyāṁ tatō gr̥hidharmō darśanādikō gr̥hītaḥ । pañcamatrataṁ viśēṣēṇa saṁkaṭaṁ tāṁbhyāṁ parigr̥hītam ॥ 8॥
bhaṇitaśca munīndrēṇa bharatō yathā pañcamē vratē tava । bhaviṣyati dvitīyāticārastasmānmā tatsaṁkaṭaṁ gr̥hāṇa ||9||
tēnāpi bhaṇitaṁ na ca saṁkaṭamidaṁ gr̥hītamalpadaivasikam । iti bhaṇitvā natvā ca prāptau tau nijagr̥hē dvāvapi ॥
athānyadinē rajanyāṁ paśyati lakṣmīdēvatāṁ sahasā । vāsabhavanē bharatō rahasi tayēdaṁ bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 11 ॥
vatsāhaṁ tava tuṣṭā saṁtuṣṭō yadyapi lakṣmīvistāra । tathāpi prayacchāmyahaṁ mārgaya yad rōcatē dravyam ॥ 12॥

I
tō jaṁpara siridēvī dēvāṇaṁ vaccha ! daṁsaṇamamōhaṁ । āsi tumaṁ kōḍīsō puvvi tā hōsu iṇhipi ॥ 15 ॥
tō sō bhai bhayavai ! ēvaṁ ca kaē havēi vayabhaṁgō | tō dēvīē bhaṇiyaṁ dēsu jahicchāē sayaṇāṇa ॥ 16 ॥
tattō ya takkhaṇaṁ kaṁcanakōḍiṁ khivittu bharahassa | vāraṁtassavi gēhē sahāṇaṁ paḍigayā lacchī ||17||
niyaniyamabhaṁgabhīō tattō sō vibhajiūṇa kōḍipi । dēi sayaṇāṇa savvā uddhārē gayakalētarayā || 18 ||
dahūṇa kaṇiṭṭō baṁdhū vajjarai bhāga ! na hu juttaṁ । jaṁ kuṇasi sāiyāraṁ paṁcamatrayamāyara pavannaṁ ॥ 19 ॥
jamhā u lakkhamēgaṁ pariggahē tuha mamāvi sāhīṇaṁ । vilasasi kōḍīi puṇō nissaṁkō niyamavisayasmi ॥
kiṁ kajjaṁ vihavēṇaṁ samaggalēṇapi- pāvakajjēṇa । aha bhaṇasi dēsu dhammē dhammēṇavi tēṇa kiṁ kajjaṁ ? ||21||
vayamālinaṁ jāyai jēṇa karaṇaṁ na hōi sō dhammō । mahuraṁ bhaṇiūṇa visaṁ jai khajjai kiṁ na mārēi ? ||
tō taṁ niyasattāō daviṇaṁ pariharasu āsi jaṁ ahiyē । sayaṇāiyāṇa dinnaṁ anna bhinnō bhavissāmi ॥
tēvi yuddhēṇa taō bhaṇiyaṁ vaṇijēṇuvajjiyaṁ na maē । gahiyaṁ na cōriyāē na khattavāō maē vihiō ||
kiṁpuṇa vāraṁtassavi khittaṁ lacchīē maha gihē vaccha ! | taṁṣi maē sayaṇāṇaṁ samappiyaṁ jātra niyamō mē ॥
puṇa lakkhāō haṁ ahiṁ vivēmi dēmi taṁ dhammē । tō rahasēṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ baṁdhava ! suṇa ittha ditaṁ ॥
iha narē dhaṇasihī āsi purā paraṇasamiddhō sō । micchaṭṭiī bahuputtana ēhi gaō vuddhiṁ ||27||
aha annayā pattī picchai pasayacchiṁ lacchisāricchaṁ । siyavasagadhāriṇi hārahāriṇi pavararamaṇi sō ॥
jaṁ
tatō bhaṇitaṁ bharatēna na khalu kāryaṁ kimapi mama drayēṇa । ēkalakṣō mama gēhē tiṣṭhati śēṣasya niyamō mē ॥ 14 ॥
tatō jalpati śrīdēvī dēvānāṁ vatsa ! darśanamamōtram | āsīstvaṁ kōṭīśaḥ pūrvaṁ tasmādbhavēdānīmapi ॥ 15॥
tataḥ sa bhaṇati bhagavati ! ēvaṁ ca kr̥tē bhavati vratabhaṅgaḥ । tatō dēvyā bhaṇitaṁ dēhi yathēcchayā svajanēbhyaḥ ॥
tataśca tatkṣaṇēna kāñcanakōrṭi kṣiptvā bharatasya । vārayatō'pi gēhē svasthānaṁ pratigatā lakṣmīḥ ॥ 17॥
nijaniyamabhaṅgabhītastataḥ sa vibhajya kōṭimapi । dadāti svajanānāṁ sarvāmuddhārē gatakalāntaram ॥ 18 ॥
tad dr̥ṣṭvā kaniṣṭhō bandhuḥ kathayati bhrātaḥ ! na khalu yuktam । yatkarōṣi sāticāraṁ pañcamatratamādaraprapannam ॥19॥
yasmāttu lakṣamēkaṁ parigrahē tava mamāpi svādhīnam । vilasasi kōṭyā punarniḥśaṅkō niyamaviṣayē ||20||
kiṁ kāryaṁ vibhavēna samargalēnāpi pāpakāryēṇa । atha bhaṇasi dēhi dharmē dharmēṇāpi tēna kiṁ kāryam ॥21॥
vratamālinyaṁ jāyatē yēna kr̥tēna na bhavati sa dharmaḥ । madhuraṁ bhaṇivā viṣaṁ yadi khādyatē kiṁ na mārayati ? ||
tatastvaṁ nijasattātō draviṇaṁ pariharāsīd yadadhikam । svajanādibhyō dattamanyathā bhinnō bhaviṣyāmi ||23||
tēnāpi lubdhēna tatō bhaṇitaṁ vāṇijyēnōpārjitaṁ na mayā । gr̥hītaṁ na cōrikayā na kṣattravādō mayā vihitaḥ ॥ 24
kintu vārayatō'pi kṣiptaṁ lakṣmyā mama gr̥hē vatsa ! । tadapi mayā svajanēbhyaḥ samarpitaṁ yāvanniyamō mē ||25|
yatpunarlakṣādahamadhikamarjayāmi dadāmi tad dharmē । tatō rabhasēna bhaṇitaṁ bāndhava ! śr̥ṇvatra dr̥ṣṭāntam ॥26॥
iha nagarē dhanaśrēṣṭhī āsītpurā pracuradhanasamr̥ddhaḥ saḥ । mithyādr̥ṣṭirbahuputranaptr̥bhirgatō vr̥ddhim ॥27॥
athānyadā prasuptaḥ paśyati mr̥gākṣī lakṣmīsahakṣām । sitavasanadhāriṇīṁ hārahāriṇīṁ pravararamaṇa saḥ ||28||

bharahakahā ।

bhaṇiyaṁ tīē dhaṇasiddhi ! kiṁ tumaṁ maṁ viyāṇasē nō vā ? । sō bhai manāyā sāmanēṇaṁ tumaṁ ramaṇī ॥
tō tīē tastra kahiyaṁ lacchī haṁ tuha kulē vasiyapuvvā । ā sattamavaṁsāō, saṁpa annattha vaccisaṁ ॥ 30॥
nivvinnā haṁ jēṇaṁ ēttha nivāsaō ō tēṇa । bhaṇiyaṁ sigghaṁ vayasutti jaṁpaē tō imaṁ lacchī ॥ 31 ॥
asi taṁ siddhi ! jēṇa nahu ēttiyaṁpi tē bhaṇiyaṁ । kō hēū tuha gamaṇē tuha atyariyaṁ maē kiṁva ? |
kiñca ।
jaivi ahaṁ lacchīvi hu tumaē avaganniyā alacchīva । tujjha nirīhattaṇaō'ṇuraṁjiyā tahavi tuṭṭā hai ||
maggasu jaṁ tē ruccai, bhaṇiyaṁ tēṇāvi jai tuma tuṭṭā । tahavi taē na hu kajjaṁ, kajjaṁ puṇa ēttiēva ॥ 34 ॥
jaha maha kuṭuṁbavihaḍā na ghaḍai kaiyāvi daṁtakalahēṇa । taṁ taha karēsu jai taṁ suprasannā saccaō majjha || 35॥
annaha taē na kajjaṁ, tō hasiuṁ bhaṇai siṭṭhī ! dakkhō si । iya pabhaṇatēṇa taē nigaḍiyacaraṇā ahaṁ vihiyā ।।
jamhā vaccatīē paḍhamayarucciya imō maha uvāō | annunnamahaṁ paḍhamaṁ vihaḍaṁ pāḍēmi baṁdhūṇaṁ ||37||
tattō kuti kalahaṁ pacchā gacchēti rāyapāsammi । jaṁpati ya pēsunnaṁ daṁḍijaṁti ya tō rannā ||38||
ahavāvi parōparaō jujjhēvi maraṁti hum̐ti gayapunnā । tattō savvaṁ davvaṁ nariṁdabhavaṇaṁ samaliyai ||39||
micchadiṭṭhīvi vivēyatrajjiō jiṇamayammi aṇabhinnō । tassavi yaṁ iya aṇicchā lacchīvisaē visēsēṇa ॥
taṁ puṇa laddhavivēō gahiyavaō jiṇamayaṁ pavannōvi । bhaṁjasi niyaniyamadhuraṁ kruddhō nirddhadhasō dhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 41 ॥
kiñca ।
1
guruṇā nivāriēṇavi tumaē gahiyaṁ vayaṁ imaṁ mūḍha ! । tā virama virama ajjavi aiyārāō imāō tumaṁ ॥42॥
bhaṇitaṁ tayā dhanaśrēṣṭhin ! kiṁ tvaṁ māṁ vijānāsi nō vā । sa bhaṇati mayā jñātā sāmānyēna tvaṁ ramaṇī ||
tatastayā tasya kathitaṁ lakṣmīrahaṁ taba kula uṣitapūrvā । ā saptamavaṁśāta, saṁpratyanyatra vajiṣyāmi ॥30॥
nirviṇṇā'haṁ yēnaikatra nivāsatastatastēna । bhaṇitaṁ śīghraṁ vrajēti jalpati tata idaṁ lakṣmīḥ ॥ 31 ॥
ati niṣṭhurō'si tvaṁ śrēṣṭhin ! yēna na khalvētāvadapi tvayā bhaṇitam । kō hētustava gamanē tavāpakr̥taṁ mayā kiṁvā ? |
yadyapyahaṁ lakṣmīrapi hi tvayāvagaṇitā'lakṣmīriva । tava nirīhatvatō'nurañjitā tathāpi tuṣṭā'ham ||33||
mārgaya yattē rōcatē, bhaṇitaṁ tēnāpi yadi tvaṁ tuṣṭā । tathāpi tvayā na hi kārya, kārya punarētāvataiva ॥ 34 ॥
yathā mama kuṭumbavighaṭā na ghaṭatē kadāpi dantakalahēna । tattathā kuru yadi tvaṁ suprasannā satyatō mama ॥ 35॥
anyathā tvayā na kārya, tatō hasitvā bhaṇati śrēṣṭhin ! dakṣō'si । iti prabhaṇatā tvayā nigaḍitacaraṇāhaṁ vihitā ॥
yasmād vrajantyāḥ prathamatara ēvāyaṁ mamōpāyaḥ । anyōnyamahaṁ prathamaṁ vighaṭāṁ pātayāmi bandhūnām ॥37॥
tataḥ kurvanti kalahaṁ paścād gacchanti rājapārśvē | jalpanti ca paiśunyaṁ daṇḍyantē ca tatō rājñā ॥ 38 ॥
athavāpi parasparatō yuddhvā mriyantē bhavanti gatapuṇyāḥ । tataḥ sarva dravyaṁ narēndrabhavanaṁ samupasarpati ॥ 39 ॥
mithyādr̥ṣṭirapi vivēkavarjitō jinamata'nabhijñaḥ । tasyāpi cētyanicchā lakṣmīviṣayē viśēṣēṇa ॥40॥
tvaṁ punarlabdhavivēkō gr̥hītavratō jinamataṁ prapannō'pi । bhanakṣi nija niyamadhurāṁ lubdhō niṣṭhurō gāḍham ॥ 41 ॥
