tō bharaṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ kiṁ kiṁpi maē akajjamā yariyē । jaṁ taṁ sikkhavasi mamaṁpi dhammiō taṁ ciya na annō ||
rahasō bhai baṁdhava ! khamiyavvaṁ jaṁ maē tumaṁ bhaṇiō । niyabhāgaṁ gahiūṇaṁ jāō bhinnō taō sōvi ॥ 44 ॥
aarts for fastē dhammaṁ karēi niccapi । bharahō uṇa naranāhēṇa daṁḍiō kammivivarā ||45॥
jaha bhōyaṇamittaṁpi ha mahayā kaṭṭēṇa hōi tassēha । rahasō uṇa paidiyahaṁ pavaṭṭhaē vivakitīhi ॥46॥
jaha jaha asst vivō taha taha ahiyapi vica dhammē । tō kuṁṭhēṇaṁ kēṇavi kahiyaṁ rannō jahā ēsō || 47 ||
aviva tā dhippaḍa atthō ēyassa, tō nariṁdēṇa । hakkāriūṇa bhaṇiō rahammi rahasō jahā amha ॥ 48 ॥
tuṭṭōcciya bhaṁḍārō tā davvaṁ dēhi lakkhamāṇaṁ mē । tēṇavi bhaṇiyaṁ giṇhau dēvō jaṁ mē gihē asthi ||49॥
pāṇāvi dēvataṇayā ki atthē aṇatthabhūraṇa ? । tō taggihammi rannā atthatthaṁ pēsiō sacivō ॥50॥
tō sāsaṇadēvīē tasṇurāēṇa taggihē davvaṁ । pacchāiyaṁ samaggaṁ tattō lōhāulō sahasā ||51 ||
sacivōvi tattha pattō picchara maṁjūsapēḍiyāīyaṁ । rikkaṁ ciya nō ritthaṁ tā pucchara tassa māṇusē || 52॥
vi ya bhaṇati bhariyāī caiva pēḍāiyāī dihāī । ēttiyakāla saṁpai na yāṇimō kaha virikāī ॥ 53 ॥
tō vimhaō maṁtī pēsaī niyamāṇusaṁ naridassa । tēṇavi kahiyaṁ savvaṁ tō rāyā āgaō tattha ||54॥
sōvi hu tava piccha pucchara rahasē sahāgayaṁ kiṁ bhō ! । na ya pēḍāisu davvaṁ dīsaha annattha kiṁ khittaṁ ? ॥
sō bhai nāha ! nāhaṁ niuṇaṁ jāṇēmi kiṁtu ajjēva । haṭṭāō dasa sahassā khivium̐ iha tuha gihē pattō |
1
guruṇā nivāritēnāpi tvayā gr̥hītaṁ vratamidaṁ mūḍha ! । tasmādvirama viramādyāpyaticārādasmāttvam ॥42॥
tatō bharatēna bhaṇitaṁ kiṁ kimapi mayā'kāryamācaritam । yattvaṁ śikṣayasi māmapi dhārmikastvamēva nānyaḥ ॥43॥
rabhasō bhaṇati bāndhava ! kṣantavyaṁ yad mayā tvaṁ bhaṇitaḥ । nijabhāgaṁ gr̥hītvā jātō bhinnastataḥ sō'pi ॥ 44 ॥
vyavaharati nijahaṭṭē vidhinā dharma karōti nityamapi । bharataḥ punarnaranāthēna daṇḍitaḥ kasminnapyaparādhē ||45॥
yathā bhōjanamātramapi hi mahatā kaṣṭēna bhavati tasyēha । rabhasaḥ punaḥ pratidivasaṁ pravardhatē vibhavartibhyām ॥46॥
yathā yathā vardhatē vibhavastathā tathā'dhikamapi vyēti dharmē । tataḥ kuṇṭhēna kēnāpi kathitaṁ rājñē yathaiṣaḥ || 47 ||
ativibhavī tasmād gr̥hyatāmartha ētasya, tatō narēndrēṇa । hakkārayitvā bhaṇitō rahasi rabhasō yathā mama ॥ 48 ॥
truṭita ēva bhāṇḍāgārastasmād dravyaṁ dēhi lakṣamānaṁ mē । tēnāpi bhaṇitaṁ gr̥hṇātu dēvō yanmē gr̥hē'sti ॥ 49 ॥
prāṇā api dēvasaṁbandhinaḥ kimarthēnānarthabhūtēna ? । tatastadgr̥hē rājñā'rthārthaṁ prēṣitaḥ sacivaḥ ॥50॥
tataḥ śāsanadēvyā tasyānurāgēṇa tadgr̥hē dravyam । pracchāditaṁ samagraṁ tatō lōbhākulaḥ sahasā ||11||
sacivō'pi tatra prāptaḥ paśyati mañjūṣāpēṭāvikam | riktamēva nō riktthaṁ tataḥ pr̥cchati tasya mānuṣān ॥52॥
dspi ca bhaṇanti bhr̥tānyēva pēṭādikāni dr̥ṣṭāni । ētāvatkālaṁ saṁprati na jānīmaḥ kathaṁ viriktāni ॥ 53 ॥
tatō vismitō mantrī prēṣayati nijamānuṣaṁ narēndrāya । tēnāpi kathitaṁ sarvaṁ tatō rājā''gatastatra ॥ 54॥
sō'pi khalu
tathaiva paśyati pr̥cchati rabhasaṁ sahāgataṁ kiṁ bhōḥ ! । na ca pēṭādiṣu dravyaṁ dr̥śyatē'nyatra kiṁ kṣiptam ॥
sa bhaṇati nātha ! nāhaṁ nipuṇaṁ jānāmi kintvadyaiva । haṭṭād daśa sahasrān kṣiptvēha taba gr̥hē prāptaḥ ॥ 56 ॥

iya ēvaṁ varddhatē gayaṇē jaṁpēi dēvayā kāvi । bhō bhō bhūvai ! nisuṇasu maha vayaṇaṁ avahiō hōuṁ ॥ 57 ॥
ēyassa tara vaṇiṇō nirāvarāhassa dhammanirayassa । iṭṭhō atthō gahiraṁ tāṇatthō tujjha iha hōhī ॥ 58 ॥
mā bhaṇasu jaṁ na kahiyaṁ, cūrissamahaṁ sapariyaṇaṁ sapuraṁ । jai ēyassa tiṇassavi sammuhamavi taṁ palōēsi ।।
tattō bhīēṇa narāhivēṇa rahasō khamāvium̐ bhaṇiō । vilasasu davvaṁ niyayaṁ, tā sahasā payaḍiyaṁ davvaṁ ॥ 60 ॥
dēvīē vakamuha kārḍa mukkō taō ya sō kuṁḍhō । rāyāvi gaō gēhē rahasōvi visēsaō dāṇaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
dīṇāiyāṇa dāvai bharahō u kalaṁkiūṇa vayamēyaṁ । uvavannō nāgēsuṁ sattamammammi sijjhihihī || 62॥
rahasō uṇa pajjaṁ samāhimaraṇēṇa baṁbhalōyammi । uvavannō kayapunnō taiyabhavē sijjhihī ittha ॥ 63 ॥
iya nāūṇa bhaddā ! daḍhavvaēhiṁ sayāvi hōyavvaṁ । jammō maraṇavasāṇō vihavō ya calō jalalavun ||64॥
॥ iti parigrahaparimāṇavratē dvitīyāticāravipākē bharatakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
ityēvaṁ vartamānē gaganē jalpati dēvatā kāpi । bhō bhō bhūpatē ! śr̥ṇu mama vacanamavahitō bhūtvā ॥ 57 ॥
ētasya tvayā vaṇijō niraparādhasya dharmaniratasya । iṣṭō'rthō grahītuṁ tasmādanarthastavēha bhaviṣyati ॥ 58॥
mā bhaṇa yanna kathitam, cūrṇayiṣyāmyahaṁ saparijanaṁ sapuram । yadyētasya tr̥ṇasyāpi saṁmukhamapi tvaṁ pralōkasē ||19||
tatō bhītēna narādhipēna rabhasaḥ kṣamayitvā bhaṇitaḥ । vilāsaya dravyaṁ nijaṁ, tadā sahasī prakaṭitaṁ dravyam ॥ 60 ॥
dēvyā vakramukhaḥ kr̥tvā muktastataśca sa kuṇṭhaḥ । rājāpi gatō gēhē rabhasō'pi viśēṣatō dānam ॥ 61 ॥
dīnādibhyō dāpayati bharatastu kalaṅkayitvā vratamētat । upapannō nāgēṣu saptamajanmani sētsyati ॥ 62 ॥
rabhasaḥ punaḥ paryantē samādhimaraṇēna brahmalōkē । upapannaḥ kr̥tapuṇyastr̥tīyabhavē sētsyatyatra ॥ 63 ॥
iti jñātvā bhadrāḥ ! dr̥ḍhavrataiḥ sadāpi bhavitavyam । janma maraṇāvasānaṁ vibhavaśca calō jalalava iva ॥64॥

tathāhi; —-
asthi jaē supasiddhaṁ siddhapuraṁ dharaṇiramaṇitilayaṁva | supavittaṁ aviuttaṁ kalāṇaviyāsasōhāē || 2 ||
tyatthi dēvarāō supasiddhō suddhabuddhiladdhajasō । viṣayavasavihiyacōjjā bhajjā piyadasaṇā tassa ||3||
ēgūṇapaṇa sāīṁ maṁtīṇaṁ tassa saṁti pavarāī । tappūraṇatthamēgaṁ gavēsaē sō mahāmaṁti ||4||
ae are as fast vēsamaṇō amiyayaṇakaṇasamiddhō । caurō ya tassa puttā ghaṇaghaṇavaidhavalajasanāmā ॥
lēkkhāī kuṇai ēgō vīō dhannāṇa kuṇai puṇa vuddhiṁ । taiō caupayatattiṁ turiō bhaṁḍāriō tēsiṁ ॥6॥
aha annayā ya siṭṭī nāūṇaṁ attaṇō carimasamayaṁ । gharakōṇēsuṁ causuvi kalasē cattāri nikkhaṇai ||7||
tattō duiyadiṇammi hakārāvai samaggasyaṇajaṇaṁ । bhōyaṇavihiṇā sammāṇiūṇa taṁ bhai iya siddhī ||8||
niyabhuyadaṁḍē hi maē atthō uppāiō aṇappōvi । na niōiō suṭhāṇē kukuḍaṁbasiṇēhamūḍhēṇaṁ ॥ 9 ॥
saṁpai paralōya hē pāhēyaṁ pai bhaṇēmi niyasayaṇē । maha patthaṇāē lakkhō vivvēyacvō ya tumhēhiṁ ॥ 10 ॥
sattasu khittēsuṁ saṁpayaṁpi tā kuṇaha attaṇō pāsē । iya bhaṇiūṇa samappaṛa payaṇāṇaṁ tāṇa igalakkhē ॥11॥
as a deer ēē athanimittaṁpi kalahaissaṁti । maha pacchā iya muṇiuṁ suyaṇasamakkhaṁ bhaṇai taṇaē ।
jaṁ lōyaṇēhi vayaṇaṁ vayaṇēṇa ya lōyaṇāī sōrhati । cihurēhiṁ siraṁ rēhada cihurāvi siraṭṭiyā cēva || 13 ||
samacittā duvi sahā sagaḍaṁ kaṭṭhēti uvalabhariyaṁpi । avi vibhinnacittā phirakkajuttāvi tammaṁti ॥
virativirādhanābhītō dēśalaśrāddha iva yō'vikaṁ dhānyam । svajanādikēbhyō'rpayati sa virativirādhanāṁ karōti ॥
asti jagati suprasiddhaṁ siddhapuraṁ dharaṇīramaṇītilakamiva । supavitramaviyuktaṁ kalyāṇa vikāsaśōbhayā || 2 ||
tatrāsti dēvarājaḥ suprasiddhaḥ śuddhabuddhilabdhayaśāḥ । vinayavaśavihitāścaryā bhāryāṁ priyadarśanā tasya ॥3॥
ēkōnapañcaśatī mantriṇāṁ tasyāsti pravarā । tatpūraṇārthamēkaṁ gavēṣayati sa mahāmantriṇam ||4||
tathā tatra vasati śrēṣṭhī vaiśramaṇō'mitadhana kaṇasamr̥ddhaḥ । catvāraśca tasya putrā dhanadhanapatidhavalayaśōnāmānaḥ ||5||
lēkhyādi karōtyēkō dvitīyō dhānyānāṁ karōti punarvr̥ddhim । tr̥tīyaścatuṣpada cintāṁ turyō bhāṇḍārikastēṣām ॥6॥
athānyadā ca śrēṣṭhī jñātvā''tmanaścaramasamayam । gr̥hakōṇēṣu caturṣvapi kalaśāṁścaturō nidadhāti ॥7॥
tatō dvitīyadinē kārayati samagrasvajanajanam । bhōjanavidhinā sammānya taṁ bhaṇatīti śrēṣṭhī ॥8॥
nijabhujadaṇḍābhyāṁ mayā'rtha utpāditō'nalpō'pi । na niyōjitaḥ susthānē kukkuṭumbasnēhamūḍhēna ||9||
saṁprati paralōkapathē pāthēyaṁ prati bhaṇāmi nijasvajanān । mama prārthanayā lakṣōṁ vyētavyaśca yuṣmābhiḥ ॥ 10 ॥
saptasu kṣētrēṣu sāṁpratamapi tasmātkurutātmanaḥ pārśvē । iti bhaṇitvā samarpayati svajanānāṁ tēṣāmēkalakṣam ॥11॥
tathā mama tanayā ētē'rthaniṁmittamapi kalaha yiṣyanti । mama paścāditi jñātvā sujanasamakṣaṁ bhaṇati tanayān ||12||
yallōcanābhyāṁ vadanaṁ vadanēna ca lōcanē śōbhētē । cikuraiḥ śirō rājatē cikurā api śiraḥ sthitā ēva || 13||

tāpīīē vacchā! vaṭṭijjaha niścamēva annōnnaṁ । jai na kuṇaha puṇa ēvaṁ tō vayaṇaṁ suṇaha mahataṇayaṁ ॥ 15 ॥
jaha maha hissa majjhē kalasā cattāri causu kōṇēsu । saṁti maē viṇihittā tē tubbhēhi gahēyavvā ॥ 16 ॥
vāmē kōṇē kalasō jiṇaṁ dāhiṇammi bīēṇa । nēraiē taiēṇaṁ vāyavvē lahuyaputtēṇaṁ ॥ 17॥
jahajōgyā atthō kalasēsu āsi sō maē nihiō । lihiūṇa ya nāmāī tumhāṇaṁ tēsu khittāī ||
savi bhai siṭṭī jujjhati na davvakāraṇā kahavi । maha paralōyagayassavi taha jaiavvaṁ tu tumhēhi ||
jaṁ jasta maē dinnaṁ taṁ tassa, na annahā vihēyavvaṁ । iya bhaṇiuṁ tē sayaṇā visajjiyā khāmi namiḍaṁ. ।।
aha paralōē pattē piumma puttāvi niyaniē kalasē । giṇhati jiṭṭaputtā tinnivi tēsu iyaṁ niyaṁti ॥ 21 ॥
paḍhamē puḍhatriṁ vīyammi likkhayaṁ taiyammi aṭṭhīṇi । vararayaṇabhariyakalasō diṭṭō savvēhiṁ lahuyassa ||22||
tō tē bhāṁti hā tāya ! vaṁciyā dhammiēṇavi suyāvi । tā tumha sugaimaggō kaha hōhī vaṁcaṇaparassa ? ||23||
tō tēhi lahuyabhāyā bhaṇiō jaha vibhaiūṇa rayaṇāī । gihissāmō amhē, sō jaṁpa majjha tāṇa ॥ 24 ॥
sayaṇasamakkhaṁ dinnāī tumhakalasēsu maṭṭiyāīyaṁ । jāyaṁ apunnavasaō kō dōsō tattha tāyarasa ? || 25 ॥
tahavi na muṁcati taō tēvi sayaṇāṇa sāhiyaṁ savvaṁ । sayaṇēhiṁ vāriyāvi hu tē sirigaraṇammi saṁpattā ॥
sāhiti niyavivāyaṁ sacivassa, taō ya tēṇa bujjhaviyā । jāva na viramaṁti taō naravaṇō sāhiyaṁ paḍhamaṁ ॥
savvaṁ savittharaṁ carimabaṁdhuṇā sayaṇavaggajuttēṇa । tō bhaṇiyaṁ bhūvaiṇā na annahā kuṇai vēsamaṇō ||28||
jamhā sō jimmē suniccalō paccalō ya buddhīē । nō kavaḍakūḍakārī annassa kahavi, tā ēyaṁ ॥ 29 ॥
tasmātprītyā vatsāḥ ! vartadhvaṁ nityamēvānyōnyam । yadi na kuryāta punarēvaṁ tadā vacanaṁ śr̥ṇuta madīyam ॥ 15 ॥
yathā mama gr̥hasya madhyē kalaśāścatvāraścaturṣu kōṇēṣu । santi mayā vinihitāstē yuṣmābhirgrahītavyāḥ ॥ 16 ॥
vāmē kōṇēṁ kalaśō jyēṣṭhēna dakṣiṇē dvitīyēna । nairr̥tē tr̥tīyēna vāyavyē laghuputrēṇa ||17||
yathāyōgyatamarthaḥ kalaśēṣvāsīt sa mayā nihitaḥ । likhitvā ca nāmāni yuṣmākaṁ tēṣu kṣiptāni ॥ 18 ॥
svajanānapi bhaṇati śrēṣṭhī yudhyantē na dravyakāraṇātkathamapi । māya paralōkagatē'pi tathā yatitatryaṁ tu yuṣmābhiḥ ।।
yada yasmai mayā dattaṁ tattasmai, nānyathā vidhātavyam । iti bhaṇitvā tē svajanā visarjitā kṣamayitvā natvā ॥
atha paralōkē prāptē pitari putrā api nijanijānkalaśān । gr̥hṇanti jyēṣṭhaputrāstrayō'pi tēṣviti paśyanti ॥
prathamē pr̥thivīṁ dvitīyē lēkhyaṁ tr̥tīyē'sthīni । vararatnabhr̥takalaśō dr̥ṣṭaḥ sarvairlaghōḥ ||22||
yad
,
tatastē bhaṇantihā tāta ! vañcitā dhārmikēṇāpi sutā api । tasmāttava sugatimārgaḥ kathaṁ bhaviṣyati vañcanaparasyaḥ ॥
tatastairlaghubhrātā bhaṇitō yathā vibhajya ratnāni । grahīṣyāmō vayaṁ sa jalpati mama tātēna ॥ 24 ॥
svajanasamakṣaṁ dattāni yuṣmatkalaśēṣu mr̥ttikādikam । jātamapuṇyavaśataḥ kō dōṣastatra tātasya ? ||25|| -
tathāpi na muñcanti tatastēnāpi svajanēbhyaḥ kathitaṁ sarvam । svajanairvāritā api khalu tē śrīkaraṇē saṁprāptāḥ ॥
kathayanti nijavivādaṁ sacivāya, tataśca tēna bōdhitāḥ । yāvanna viramanti tatō narapatayē kathitaṁ prathamam ॥
sarvē savistaraṁ caramabandhunā svajanavargayuktēna । tatō bhaṇitaṁ bhūpatināṁ nānyathā karōti vaiśramaṇaḥ ||28||

supāsanāha cariśrammi-
ani buddhimmaṁ jaṁ sō kalasēsu maṭṭiyāīyaṁ । khiviḍaṁ khivēi khōṇīē akkhaē suyaṇamāīṇaṁ ||30|
tō paḍihārō bhaṇiō rannā āhavasu maṁtiṇō savvē । tēṇavi tē āhūyā bhaṇiyā rannā imāṇēmaṁ ||31||
kalasaviyāraṁ kuvvaha kaha tāēṇaṁ imāṇa kuṁbhēsu । khittaṁ maṭṭiyamāī rayaṇāṇi ya lahuyakalasamma ? ||32|
tēhipi parupparaō maṁtēūṇaṁ suniuṇabuddhīhi । kahiyaṁ rannō ēyaṁ na bujjhimō kiṁpi paramatthaṁ ||33||
tō rannā niyanayarē paḍahō dāvāviō jaha imāṇaṁ । kalasāṇaṁ paramatthaṁ nāuṁ jō vihaḍai vitrāyaṁ ॥ 34 ॥
tassāī maṁtipayaṁ savvāṇuvariṁ karēmi sacivāṇaṁ । tō buddhipayaḍaṇatthaṁ chittō paḍahō vaṇisuraṇa ||35||
nīō rāyasyāsaṁ kahiō kalasāṇa vaiyarō tassa । rannā tō pariyāṇiya kahēi sō kalasaparamatthaṁ || 36 |
jō jammi suō. kusalō jassa ya jaṁ dhāriaṁ diyaṁ hōhī । taṁ taṇayāṇaṁ tēṇa dinaṁ uvaēsagabbhaṁ tu ||37|
tathāhi;
1
jassa kalasamma puḍhavī khittaṁ khaladhannamāiyaṁ tassa । jēṇa kisikammakusalō nivvahihī sō imēṇēva ॥
ahīṇi jassa kuṁbhē dinaṁ sē tēṇa caupayaṁ savvaṁ । ēyāṇa pōsaṇaṁ ciya uvaidvaṁ tassa hiyajaṇayaṁ ॥ 39 ॥
jērasa kalasamma vahiyā khaṁḍāī tassa dhuradhaṇaṁ labhaṁ । puṇaravi dēuṁ dhurāṇaṁ iya nitthārōvi sē hōhī ||40|
jō puṇa kaṇitaṇaō kisikammāīṇa sō u asamatthō । rayaṇadhaṇēṇa ēsō kalaṁtarēṇāvi nivvahihī ॥
iya tumha jahājōgaṁ dinaṁ suyavacchalēṇa jaṇaēṇa । thaivavahutaṁpi imaṁ thaivavisēsaṁti mannēmi ॥42॥
1
yasmātsa jinadharmē suniścalaḥ pratyalaśca buddhayā । nō kapaṭakūṭakāryanyasya kathamapi tasmādētat ॥ 29॥
atinipuṇabuddhigamyaṁ yat sa kalaśēṣu mr̥ttikādikam । kṣitvā kṣipati kṣōṇyāmākhyāti svajanādibhyaḥ ||30
tataḥ pratihārō bhaṇitō rājñā''dvaya mantriṇaḥ sarvān । tēnāpi tē āhūtā bhaṇitā rājñaiṣāmimam ॥31॥
kalaśavicāraṁ kuruta kathaṁ tātēnaiṣāṁ kumbhēṣu । kṣiptaṁ mr̥ttikādikaṁ ratnāni ca laghukalaśē ? ॥32॥
tairapi parasparatō mantrayitvā sunipuṇabuddhibhiḥ । kathitaṁ rājña ētanna budhyāmahē kamapi paramārtham ॥33॥
tatō rājñā nijanagarē paṭahō dāpitō yathaiṣām । kalaśānāṁ paramārtha jñātvā yō vighaṭayati vivādam ||34||
tasyāhaṁ mantripadaṁ sarvēṣāmupari karōmi sacivānām । tatō buddhiprakaṭanārthaṁ spr̥ṣṭaḥ paṭahō vaṇiksutēna ॥35॥
nītō rājasakāśaṁ kathitaḥ kalaśānāṁ vyatikarastasya । rājñā, tataḥ parijñāya kathayati sa kalaśaparamārtham ॥
yō yasmin sutaḥ kuśalō yasya ca yaddhāritaṁ hitaṁ bhaviṣyati । tattanayēbhyastēna dattamupadēśagarbha tu ॥ 37॥
yasya kalaśē pr̥thivī kṣētraṁ khaladhānyādikaṁ tasya । yēna kr̥ṣikarmakuśalō nirvakṣyatē sō'nēnaiva ॥ 38 ॥
asthīni yasya kumbhē dattaṁ tasmai tēna catuṣpadaṁ sarvam । ētēṣāṁ pōṣaṇamēvōpadiṣṭaṁ tasya hitajanakam || 39॥
yasya kalaśē vahikākhaṇḍāni tasya r̥ṇidhanaṁ labhyam । punarapi dattvā r̥ṇibhya iti nistārō'pi tasya bhaviṣyati ॥
yaḥ punaḥ kaniṣṭhatanayaḥ kr̥ṣikarmādiṣu sa tvasamarthaḥ । ratnadhanēnaiṣa kalāntarēṇāpi nirvakṣyati ॥ 41 ॥
iti yuṣmabhyaṁ yathāyōgyaṁ dattaṁ sutavatsalēna janakēna । stōkaprabhūtamapīdaṁ stōkaviśēṣamiti manyē ॥ 42 ॥
1 ga. vahiyakhaṁḍāṇi kalasē tamsa ghurāṇaṁ dhaṇaṁ tu jaṁ labbhaṁ, ka. jassa kuḍayammi va° ।

tā tucchalacchikajjē mā ninnēhā parōpparaṁ hōha । jaṇayabhaṇiyāī sumaraha sahōyarā dullahā jēṇa ||43||
ailāliyāvi aipāliyāvi vihaḍaṁti sēsayā sayaṇā । huṁti sahijjā vihurē kuviyāvi sahōyarā cēva ||
tō rannā kaṇasaṁkhaṁ puṭṭhō paḍhamō kahēi jaha dēva ! । igamūḍalakkhasamahiyamavi dhannaṁ atthi tāyagihē ॥ 45 ॥
karikarahaturayamāīca uppayāṇaṁ tu dasa sahassāī । iya duiōvi kahēī, taiō puṭṭhō imaṁ kahaī ||46 ॥
maṁḍaliyāṇaṁ pāsē lahiyavvā saṁti pannarasa lakkhā । tō rayaṇāṇaṁ kuṁbhō rannā āṇāviō tatthaṁ ॥47॥
tataar mullaṁ taṁ caiva tāṇa tēhi kayaṁ । ēvaṁ karidhannāisa caunha puttāṇa pattēyaṁ ॥ 48 ॥
panarasa panarasa lakkhā jāyā tō vaṇiyaniuṇabuddhīē । satuṭṭā tē savvē nivōvitaṁ puccha ēvaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
kassa ō kināmō kō dhammō tujjha abhipaō kahasu । tēṇavi kahiyē jaha punabhavaṇiṇō suyā dōvi ।।
paḍhamōttha kōsalō haṁ duiō baṁdhū ya dēsalō majjha । jiṇadhammē paḍivannā bārasa vihasāvayavayāī || 51 ॥
tō bhaṇiō bhūvaiṇā giraghasu mudaṁ subuddhimayara hara ! | tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ na kappai kharakammaṁ jēṇimā bhaṇiyā ||
tō sō viṇāvi muddāē ṭhāviō sayalamaṁtisāmittē । maṁtijjai savvatthavi sōviya paḍhamaṁ naridēṇa ॥ 53 ॥
tō īsāē annē chalaṁ gavēsaṁti maṁtiṇō tassa । aha savvērhivi jugavaṁ maṁtiya bhaṇiō imaṁ rāyā ॥ 54 ॥
dēvagirinayavāsī rāyā riugaṁjaṇō na mannēi । tuha āṇaṁ niravikkhō tā tassa imō mahāmaṁtī || 55 ॥
pēsijjai jaṁ kusalō kicivi kōsalliyaṁ gaūṇaṁ । ghaḍaṇaṁ va vihaḍaṇaṁ vā tēṇa samaṁ kuṇai jēṇēsō ॥56॥
tō rannā sō bhaṇiō gaccha tumaṁ tattha pāhuḍaṁ gahiṁḍē । sacivāṇaṁ pāsāō jahajutaṁ tattha taṁ kuṇasu || 57॥
tasmātucchalakṣmīkāryē mā niḥsnēhāḥ parasparaṁ bhavata । janakabhaṇitāni smarata sahōdarā durlabhā yēna ॥ 43 ॥
atilālitā apyatipālitā api vighaṭantē śēṣāḥ svajanāḥ । bhavanti sahāyā vidhurē kupitā api sahōdarā ēva ॥
tatō rājñā kaṇasaṁkhyāṁ pr̥ṣṭaḥ prathamaḥ kathayati yathā dēva ! । ēkamūḍhakalakṣasamadhikamapi dhānyamasti tātagr̥hē ॥
karikarabhaturagādicatuṣpadānāṁ tu daśa sahasrāṇi । iti dvitīyō'pi kathayati, tr̥tīyaḥ pr̥ṣṭa idaṁ kathayati ॥ 46 ॥
maṇḍalikānāṁ pārśvē labdhavyāḥ santi pañcadaśa lakṣāḥ । tatō ratnānāṁ kumbhō rājñā''nāyitastatra ॥47॥
ratnaparīkṣakairmūlyaṁ tadēva tēṣāṁ taiḥ kr̥tam । ēvaṁ karidhānyādiṣu caturṇāṁ putrāṇāṁ pratyēkam ॥48॥
pañcadaśa pañcadaśa lakṣā jātāstatō vaṇignipuṇabuddhayā । saṁtuṣṭāstē sarvē nr̥pō'pi taṁ pr̥cchatyēvam ॥49॥
kasya sutaḥ kiṁnāmā kō dharmasvābhimataḥ kathaya ? । tēnāpi kathitaṁ yathā pūrṇabhadravaṇijaḥ sutau dvāvapi ॥ 10॥
prathamō'tra kōśalō'haṁ dvitīyō bandhuśca dēśalō mama । jinadharmē pratipannau dvādaśavidhaśrāvakatratāni ॥11॥
tatō bhaṇitō bhūpatinā gr̥hāṇa mudrāṁ subuddhimakaragr̥ha ! । tēna bhaṇitaṁ na kalpatē kharakarma yēnēyaṁ bhaṇitā॥52॥
tataḥ sa vināpi mudrā sthāpitaḥ sakalamantrisvāmitvē । mantrayatē sarvatrāpi sō'pi ca prathamaṁ narēndrēṇa ॥ 53 ॥
tata īrṣyayā'nyē chalaṁ gavēṣayanti mantriṇastasya । atha sarvairapi yugapad mantrayitvā bhaṇita idaṁ rājā || 54 ॥
dēvagirinagaravāsī rājā ripugajanō na manyatē । tavājñāṁ nirapēkṣastasmāttasyāyaṁ mahāmantrī ||15||
prēṣyatē yatkuśalaḥ kiñcidapi kauśalikāṁ gr̥hītvā । ghaṭanaṁ vā vighaṭanaṁ vā tēna samaṁ karōti yēnaiṣaḥ || 56॥

sugāsanāha-cariammi--
tērhivi tapacchannaṁ karaṁḍiyāē khivitta pāhuḍayaṁ । tālēvi dinnamuddā samapiyā tassa sā sigyaṁ ॥ 58 ॥
tō caliō sasahāō pattō rajjaṁtarammi taiyammi । girinayarē nivapāsē tattō paḍihārakahiō sō ।। 59 ।।
namiuṁ samappaē taṁ karaṁḍiyaṁ pāhuḍassa bhariya sō । vihaḍittu jāva muddē tō taṁ ughāḍaē rāyā ॥ 60 ॥
tā tattha niyai dhūli sasaharahara hāsa kāsasaṁkāsaṁ । tō bhūvālō bhūbhaṁgabhīsaṇō bhaṇai taṁ maṁti ॥ 61 ॥
rē rē tuha naranāhō jaṛa gayavivō naēṇa parihīṇō । maha pāhuḍammi dhūli pēsaha pēsēu, kiṁtu tumaṁ ॥ 62 ॥
kimihāgaō simaraṇassa kāraṇā vacca tāva taṁ turiyaṁ । jēṇa avajjhō ravvāriōtti gaṁtūṇa sāhēhi || 63 |
jaha ēi aituraṁtō rāyā riugaṁjaṇō jaṇiyakōvō | dhūlījavāyaṇēṇaṁ daṁsissai taphalaṁ tujjha ||64 ||
tō kōsalēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ māniva ! kō karē taṁ ēvaṁ । mihiyaṁtra viyāra tō rāyā pucchara tamēva ॥ 65
tō kahai tassa ēvaṁ maha pahuṇā caccarammi rayaṇīē । avalarillīnāmā pasāhiyā jōgiṇī vijjā ॥ 66
siddhāē tīi dinnā ēsā rēṇūbhimaṁtiu kahiyē । ēyāē ēgavāraṁ jō tilayaṁ viraihī tassa ||67॥
sāiṇiḍāiṇijō iṇikarālavēyāla jakkharakkhāṇaṁ । bhūyāī na bhayaṁ duḍḍāṇavi kahavi hōhitti ॥ 68 ॥
taṁ sōūṇa tadapiyarēṇū kuṇai naravaī tilayaṁ । thōvaṁ thōvaṁ adhivi aura maṁtimāīṇa ॥ 69 ॥
sēsā tumhāṇa uvāyaṇammi saṁpēsiyā imā rēṇū । iya sōuṁ naravaṇā tīē tilayaṁ sayaṁ vihiyaṁ ॥ 70 ॥
harisavasapulaiēṇa kōsalamaṁtī taō imaṁ puṭṭhō । annāvi kāvi sattī tuha pahuṇō asthi, sō āha ॥ 71
tatō rājñā sa bhaṇitō gaccha tvaṁ tatra prābhr̥taṁ gr̥hītvā । sacivānāṁ pārśvād yathāyuktaṁ tatra tvaṁ kuruṣva ॥57॥
tairapi tatpracchannaṁ karaṇḍikāyāṁ kṣiptvā prābhr̥tam । tālayitvā dattamudrā samarpitā tasya sā śīghram ॥ 58 ॥
tataścalitaḥ sasahāyaḥ prāptō rājyāntarē tr̥tīyē । girinagarē nr̥papārśvē tataḥ pratihārakathitaḥ saḥ ॥ 59 ॥
natvā samarpayati tāṁ karaṇḍikāṁ prābhr̥tēna bhr̥tāṁ saḥ । vighaṭaya yāvanmudrāṁ tatastāmudghāṭayati rājā ॥ 60 ॥
tāvattatra paśyati dhūliṁ śaśadharahararahāsakāśasaṁkāśām । tatō bhūpālō bhrūbhaṅgabhīṣaṇō bhaṇati taṁ mantriṇam ||
rē rē tava naranāthō yadi gatavibhavō nayēna parihīṇaḥ । mama prābhr̥tē dhūliṁ prēṣayati prēṣayatu, kintu tvam ॥ 62॥
kimihāgatō'si maraṇasya kāraṇād bhaja tāvattvaṁ tvaritam । yēnāvadhyō dūta iti gatvā kathaya ॥ 63 ॥
yathaityatitvaramāṇō rājā ripugañjanō janitakōpaḥ । dhūlyupāyanēna darśayiṣyati tatphalaṁ tava ॥ 64॥
tataḥ kōśalēna bhaṇitaṁ mā nr̥pa ! kōpaṁ kuruṣva tvamēvam । hitamahitaṁ vā vicāraya tatō rājā pr̥cchati tamēva ।
tataḥ kathayati tasyaivaṁ mama prabhuṇā catvarē rajanyām । anvayitrīnāmā prasādhitā yōginī vidyā ॥66॥
siddhayā tayā dattaiṣā rēṇurabhimantraya kathitam । ētasyā ēkavāraṁ yastilakaṁ viracayiṣyati tasya || 67॥
śākinīḍākinīyōginīkarālavētālayakṣarakṣasām । bhūtādīnāṁ na bhayaṁ duṣṭānāmapi kathamapi bhaviṣyatīti ॥ 6 ॥
tat śrutvā tadarpitarēṇvā karōti narapatistilakam । stōkaṁ stōkamarpayitvā'ntaḥ puramantryādibhyaḥ ॥ 69॥
śēṣā yuṣmākamupāyanē saṁprēṣitēyaṁ rēṇuḥ । iti śrutvā narapatinā tasyāstilakaṁ svayaṁ vihitam ||70 ||
1 ga. garuyā ।

savvāuvi sattīō maha pahuṇō saṁtinannasarisāō । āṇāsattīē puṇō nannā bhutraṇammi tarasarisō ||
tō bahudē samāgamahaṁta purisēhiṁ maccharagaēhiṁ । niyaniyapahuṇō āṇā pasaṁsiyā jāva tā nayarē || 73 ॥
ucchaliō tumulavō taṁ sōuṁ tassa jāṇaṇanimittaṁ । pucchēi naraṁ kaṁpi hu sōvi hu taṁ jāṇiuṁ kahai ||
dēva ! se after farrai sicchāē nayaramajjhammi । ummiṭṭhō cūraṁtō giṭṭāīṇi tō rannā ॥ 75 ॥
bhaṇiyaṁ bhō bhō giṇhaha mattakaritō na kōi paḍivayaṇaṁ । jā dēitā nivassābhimuhaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ aṇusaṇaṁ ॥ 76 ॥
dōvāriēṇa ēkkēṇa jaha imō dēva! niyanivāṇāē । kāhī vasamiha hatthitā ēvaṁ ciya samāisasu ॥77॥
ranā ata fare kōsalamaṁtī paḍicchiuṁ āṇaṁ । khaṇamēttēṇaṁ pattō hasthisamīvaṁ sanivalōō ॥78॥
kāū paṇihāṇaṁ savihāṇaṁ hatthikhaṁbhavijjāē । tō tēṇa karī bhaṇiōṁ tuha āṇā majjhatagayā ॥ 79 ॥
ja ittō ēkaṁpi hu payaṁ payacchēsi, tō imaṁ sōuṁ । cittalihiō thakkō avaṇamiyakarō karī tattō ॥
rāyā sapariyaṇōvi hu vimyicittō pasaṁsaē sacivaṁ । bhāi ya bhō bhō supurisa ! ālāṇagayaṁ gayaṁ kuṇasu ||
tō tēṇa sō bhaṇiō karivara ! gacchētu niyayakhabhammi । tēṇavi tahēva vihiyaṁ tā rannā taṁ ciya kariṁdaṁ ॥
dāūṇa pāhuḍē taha tappahuṇō sāsaṇaṁ paḍicchēuṁ । sammāṇiya sappaṇayaṁ visajjiō kōsalō maṁtī ॥83॥
pattō siddhapurammī tattō paḍhamaṁpi maṁtiṇō savvē । tassamagapahiyaniyacaramuhēṇa vinnāyattatā ||84||
rayapāhuḍapaṇēṇa saṁkaṁtā maraṇamattaṇō gaṁtuṁ । kōsalavāsē pāē laggiḍaṁ taṁ khamārciti ॥ 85 ॥

harpavaśapulakitēna kōśalamantrī tata idaṁ pr̥ṣṭaḥ । anyāpi kāpi śaktistava prabhōrasti sa āha || 71 ॥
sarvā api śaktayō mama prabhōḥ santyananyasadr̥śyaḥ । ājñāśaktyā punarnānyō bhuvanē tatsadr̥śaḥ ॥72॥
tatō bahudēśasamāgatamahāpuruṣairmatsaragataiḥ । nijanijaprabhōrājñā praśaṁsitā yāvattāvad nagarē ||73 ||
ucchalitastumularavastaṁ śrutvā tajjñānanimittam । pr̥cchati naraṁ kamapi khalu sōpi hi tajjñātvā kathayati ॥74॥
dēva ! iha hastirājō vicarati svēcchayā nagaramadhyē | unmuktaścūrṇayan gr̥hahaṭṭādīni, tatō rājñā ॥ 75 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ bhō bhō gr̥hṇīta mattakāriṇaṁ tatō na kō'pi prativacanam । yāvad dadāti tāvannr̥pasyābhimukhaṁ bhaṇitamanuśayēna ॥
dauvārikēṇaikēna yathāyaṁ dēva ! nijanr̥pājñayā । kariṣyati vaśamiha hastinaṁ tasmādēnamēva samādiśa || 77॥
rājñā tathaiva vihinē kōśalamantrī pratīṣyājñām । kṣaṇamātrēṇa prāptō hastisamīpaṁ sanr̥palōkaḥ ॥78॥
kr̥tvā praṇidhānaṁ savidhānaṁ hastistambhavidyāyāḥ । tatastēna karī bhaṇitastavājñā matprabhusaṁbandhinī ॥ 79 ॥
yati ēkamapi hi padaṁ prayacchāsa, tata idaṁ śrutvā । citralikhita iva sthitō'vanamitakaraḥ karī tataḥ ॥ 80 ॥
rājā saparijanō'pi hi vismitacittaḥ praśaṁsati sacivam । bhaṇati ca bhō bhōḥ supuruṣa ! ālānagataṁ gajaṁ kuru ॥
tatastēna sa. bhaṇitaḥ karivara । gaccha nijastambhē । tēnāpi tathaiva vihitaṁ tadā rājñā tamēva karīndram ॥82॥
dattvā prābhr̥tē tathā tatprabhōḥ śāsanaṁ pratīpya । sammānya sapraṇayaṁ visarjitaḥ kōśalō mantrī ॥83॥
prāptaḥ siddhapurē tataḥ prathamamapi mantriṇaḥ sarvē । tatsamaprahitanijacaramukhēna vijñātavr̥ttāntāḥ ॥ 84॥
rajaḥ prābhr̥tārpaṇēna śaṅkamānā maraṇamātmanō gatvā । kōśalapārśvē pādayōrlēgitvā taṁ kṣamayanti ॥ 89 ॥

supāsanāha - cariammi-
tassaṁ ya maimāhaṣpaṁ vannaṁtā jaṁti tēṇa samamēva । naravaipāsē sōvi hu siddhanaridaṁ paṇamiṇa || 86 ॥
sāhai savvaṁ jaṁ tattha sāhiyaṁ ahiyatōsaō rām̐yā । puṇaravi kuṇai pasāyaṁ giṇhasu dēsaṁ jamabhiruiyaṁ ||87||
tō sō bhaṇēi naravara ! tujjha pasāēṇa natthi maha khūṇaṁ । kiṁ kuṇimō dēsēṇaṁ viraivirāhaṇaparō jaṁ sō ॥
jai puṇa taṁ majjuvariṁ tuṭṭhō tā jiṇamayaṁ pabhāvēsu । rahajattāpamuhēṇaṁ mahēṇa mahanivbuikarēṇa ॥ 89 ॥
tō rannā sō bhaṇiō ivi nirīhō tumaṁ tahavi ginhaṁ । gēhavvayassa jōgaṁ kiṁcivi kaṇacōpaḍāīṁ ||
ēvaṁti tammi bhaṇiuṁ gayammi rannā niōgiṇō bhaṇiyā । jaha kaṇamūḍasahassaṁ ghayaghaḍasahassē ca maṁtigihē ॥
pēsaha, tēhi tahacciya aṇuṭṭiē kōsalēṇa lahubhāyā । bhaṇiō dēsalanāmā jaha amha niyamaō ahiyaṁ ॥
jaṁ kiṁci taṁ samapsu puṇōvi taṁ rājalammi, tēṇāvi । paḍivajjiūṇa tajhyā niyamāu samahiyaṁ savvaṁ ॥
appiya sayaṇāṇa taō bhaṇiyā ēvaṁ niēsa ṭhāṇēsu । gharaha niyamāvahīē paraō gihissamamēyaṁ || 94॥
tēhivi taha caiva kaē vinnāō kōsalēṇa vr̥ttaṁtō । ēsō kahavi hu tō tēṇa bhaṇiō dēsalō ēvaṁ ॥95॥
hā bhāya ! paṁcamatraē iya kuṇamāṇēṇa taiyaaiyārō । vihiō tumaē ajjavi tā ahiyē dēsu dhammammi ||
iya puṇaruttaṁ tēṇa bhaṇiōvi hu dēsalō akuvrvvatō । kālēṇaṁ mariūṇaṁ apaṭṭiyavaṁtarī jāō || 97 ॥
paṇasayamaṁtippavarō kō salamaṁtīvi maraṇasamayammi । gahiūṇaṁ pavvajjaṁ pattō mādikappammi ॥ 98 ॥
kiṁcahiyasattasāyaraāuṁ paripāliūṇa tattō ya । caiūṇaṁ sijjhissara mahāvidēhammi vāsammi ॥99॥
tasya ca matimāhātmyaṁ varṇayantō yānti tēna samamēva । narapatipārśvē sō'pi hi siddhanarēndra praṇamya ॥ 86 ॥
kathayati sarvaṁ yattatra sādhitamadhikatōṣatō rājā | punarapi karōti prasādaṁ gr̥hāṇa dēśaṁ yō'bhirucitaḥ ॥ 87॥
tataḥ sa bhaṇati naravara ! tava prasādēna nāsti mama kṣūṇam । kiṁ kurmō dēśēna virativirādhanaparō yat saḥ ॥ 88 ॥
yadi punastvaṁ mamīpōra tuṣṭastadā jinamataṁ prabhāvaya । rathayātrāpramukhēṇa mahēna mannivr̥tikarēṇa ॥ 89 ॥
tatō rājñā sa bhaṇitō yadyapi nirīhastvaṁ tathāpi gr̥hāṇa | gēhavyayasya yōgyaṁ kiñcidapi kaṇamrakṣaṇādikam ||10||
ēvamiti tasmin bhaṇitvā gatē rājñā niyōginō bhaṇitāḥ । yathā kaṇamūḍhakasahasraṁ ghr̥taghaṭasahasraṁ ca mantrigr̥hē ||
prēṣayata, taistathaivānuṣṭhitē kōśalēna laghubhrātā । bhaṇitō dēśalanāmā yathāssvayōrniyamatō'dhikam ॥92॥
yatkiñcidapi tatsamarpaya punarapi tvaṁ rājakulē, tēnāpi । pratipadya tadā niyamātsamadhikaṁ sarvam ॥93॥
arpayitvā svajanānāṁ tatō bhaṇitā ētad nijēṣu sthānēṣu । dharata niyamāvadhēḥ paratō grahīṣyē'hamētat ॥94॥
tairapi tathaiva kr̥tē vijñātaḥ kōśalēna vr̥ttāntaḥ । ēṣa kathamapi khalu tatastēna prabhaṇitō dēśala ēvam ॥95॥
hā bhrātaḥ ! pañcamavrata iti kurvāṇēna tr̥tīyāticāraḥ । vihitastvayā'dyāpi tasmādadhikaṁ dēhi dharmē ||96 ॥
iti bhr̥śaṁ tēna bhaṇitō'pi hi dēśalō'kurvan । kālēna mr̥tvā'lparddhikavyantarō jātaḥ ॥97॥
pañcaśatamantripravaraḥ kōśalamantryapi maraṇasamayē । gr̥hītvā pravajyāṁ prāptō māhēndrakalpē ॥98 ॥
kiñcidadhikasaptasāgarāyuḥ paripālya tataśca । cyutvā sētsyati mahāvidēhē varṣē ॥ 99 ॥

iya nikalaṁkavayapālaṇēṇa jaha kōsalō suhī jāō । duiō uṇa duhabhāgī tā hōya || hai || 100 ||
॥ iti pañcamāṇuvratatr̥tīyāticāravipākē dēśaladr̥ṣṭāntaḥ samāptaḥ ॥
iti niṣkalaṅkavratapālanēna yathā kōśalaḥ sukhī jātaḥ । dvitīyaḥ punarduḥkhabhāgī tasmād bhavitavyaṁ dr̥ḍhavrataiḥ ॥

niyamāvahīē paraō jaha pasavai capayaṁ tahā kuṇai । ailōhaggahaghatyō sa lahai dulahōvva uvahāsaṁ ॥ 1 ॥
tathāhi ;-
gurumahihararamaṇīyaṁ rayaṇāyarasarisaparihakayasōhaṁ । sōhaggapuraṁ nayaraṁ jaṁbuddīvaṁva suhavāsa ||2||
mahihara siraphuriyakarō aritamabharakhaṁḍaṇī tarhi asthi । sūruvva sūrasēṇō rāyā raṁbhā piyā tassa || 3 |
aha annayā niviṭṭō bhavaṇōvari pāsaē purapayāō । puvyamuhaṁ jaṁtīō tō rāyā pucchaē purisaṁ ||4||
iṁdamahō damahō nāgamahō vā kimajja iha nayarē । dīsa jaṇō vayaṁtō visēsaō vihiyasiṁgārō ? ॥ 5 ॥
tō tēṇaṁ purisēṇaṁ kahiyaṁ jaha ajja ittha caunāṇī | nāṇamahōyahī sūrī samōsaḍhō puvvajjāṇē ||6||
tavvaṁdaṇavaḍiyāē gacchacha lōutti iya nisāmē । savviḍḍhīē gaṁtuṁ baṁdai sūri naravariṁdō ||7||
nisuṇai jirṇidammaṁ sammaṁ muṇināhavayaṇaō jāva । tāva sahasā kaōvi hu pattaṁ surajuyalayaṁ tattha ॥ 8 ॥
ēgō ya accharāhiṁ picchaṁṇayachaṇaṁ payaṭṭaē tattha । vīō maṇaharasadēṇa vāyamāṇō kaṇayasiṁgaṁ ॥ 9 ॥
gōvāliṇīṇa viṁdaṁ nacāvara phāramuttiyāhāraṁ । unnamēyavāsa nivasaṇapīnnayathaṇaharābhōgaṁ ॥ 10 ॥
bahuhāvabhāvasabhāvasaṁgayaṁ garuyabhattisaṁjuttaṁ । uccārāvara chaṁdatarammi ēyaṁ ca thuikulayē ॥11॥
tathāhi :-
paṇamāmi jayattayatrasamaṇi maṇikaṁcaṇamukrakhapamukkaghaṇaṁ ।
dhaṇasāra suriṁdanariṁdanayē nayajuttasujuttisusuttakahaṁ ॥12॥
kaharaṁ jiyadēvanariṁdajaṇaṁ jaṇamāṇasāmāṇasa haṁsavaraṁ ।
niyamāvadhēḥ paratō yathā prasūtē catuṣpadaṁ tathā karōti । atilōbhagrahagrastaḥ sa labhatē durlabha ivōpahāsam ॥ 1 ॥
gurumahīdhararamaṇīyaṁ ratnākarasadr̥śa parikhākr̥taśōbham । saubhāgyapuraṁ nagaraṁ jambūdvīpavacchubhavāsa (varṣa) m ॥ 2 ॥
mahīdharāṁśiraḥsphuritakarō'ritamō bharakhaṇḍanastatrāsti । sūravacchūrasēnō rājā rambhā priyā tasya ॥ 2 ॥
athānyadā niviṣṭō bhavanōpari paśyati puraprajāḥ । pūrvamukhaṁ yāntīstatō rājā pr̥cchati puruṣam ॥4॥
indramahaḥ skandamahō nāgamahō vā kimahaṁ nagarē | dr̥śyatē janō vrajan viśēṣatō vihitaśr̥ṅgāraḥ 1 ॥5॥
tatastēna puruṣēṇa kathitaṁ yathā'dyātra caturjñānaḥ । jñānamahōdadhiḥ sūriḥ samavasr̥taḥ pūrvōdyānē ॥6॥
tadvandanavr̥ttitayā gacchati lōka iti niśamya । sarvaddhaya gatvā vandatē sūriṁ naravarēndraḥ ||7||
śr̥ṇōti jinēndradharma samyag munināthavacanatō yāvat । tāvatsahasā kutō'pi hi prāptaṁ surayugalaṁ tatra ॥ 8 ॥
ēkaścāpsarōbhiḥ prēkṣaṇakṣaṇaṁ pravartayati tatra । dvitīyō manōharaśabdēna vādayamānaḥ kanakāṅgam ॥9॥
gōpālinīnāṁ vr̥ndaṁ nartayati sphāramauktikahāram । unnamadvāsōnivasanapīnōnnatastanabharābhōgam ॥ 10 ॥
bahuhāvabhāvasadbhāvasaṁgataṁ gurubhaktisaṁyuktam । uccārayati cchandō'ntarē ētacca stutikulakam ॥11॥
praṇamāmi jagattrayavaṁśamaṇiṁ pramuktamaṇikāñcanamukhyadhanam ।
dhanasārasurēndranarēndranataṁ nayayuktasuyuktisusūtrakatham ॥ 12 ॥

supāsanāha cariammi-
dhammammi sayā tumbhēhiṁ ujjamō hōi ittha kāyavvō । namiūṇa taō tēhivi sappaṇayaṁ bhaṇiyamiya vayaṇaṁ ।
dhammujjamēṇa amhē migamāī māriūṇa nivvahimō । tō ammēdiṁ bhaṇiya nahu nahu ēyaṁ khamaṁ tumha || 26॥
jalalavacalammi jīē taḍitaralavilāsalacchivicchaḍḍē । paḍupavaṇapahayapaumiṇijalataralē sayaṇasaṁjōgē ||27||
mahumattakāmiṇīyaṇakaḍakkhavikkhēva caṁcalē pēmmē । vāmāṇa māṇasaṁ piva aicavalē jōvvaṇabharammi ||28||
jiṇadhammō aṇucariu juttō tumhāṇa tassa puṇa mūlaṁ । sammattaṁ nirdiṭṭhē tā taṁ gahiūṇa savisēsa | | 29॥
ujjamaha jiṇapaṇī dhammē iya jaṁpiyammi amhēhi । namiūṇa tēvi pabhaṇaṁti amha sāhēha jiṇadhammaṁ ||30||
tō duvihōvi kahiō dhammō aṁgīkaō puṇō tēhiṁ । paḍhamē asamatthēhiṁ gihidhammō vārasavihōvi ||31||
ittō annattha gayā amhē tāṇaṁ ca dhammanirayāṇaṁ । aha annayā ya paṁcamavayammi aikaḍaṁ jāyaṁ ||32||
jamhā cauppayāṇaṁ tēhiṁ dōhipi niyamakālammi । thōvā saṁkhā vihiyā, paivarisaṁ pasavamāṇāṇa ||33||
jāyai jayā samahiyā tayāiyārō vēi iya muṇiuṁ । mūlaparimāṇamajjhā vikaṇaē vallahō tāī ||34||
dulahēṇa puṇō punāē mūḷasaṁkhāē niyayagāvīṇaṁ । niyamāvahīē paraō jaha ganbhō hōi taha vihiyaṁ ॥
tō sō vallaharāēṇa paṇiō mūḍha ! iya kuṇaṁtēṇaṁ । paṁcamatrayaaiyārō vihiō tumaē ahiyaduhaō |
।
iya sōuṁ sa paṇa gurūṇa pāsammi jā maē gahiyā । sā caupayāṇa saṁkhā inhipi hu tattiyā caiva ॥
na maē kiṁcivi ahiṁya kiṇiyaṁ jēṇēha hōi aiyārō । sayamēva cauppayāī mēhuṇasannāē jāyaṁti || 38 ॥
। ||38||
1
vanditvā bhūpaviṣṭau, asmābhistayōḥ saṁmukhaṁ bhaṇitam । bhō bhō labdhvēdaṁ durlabhaṁ kathamapi manujatvam ||24||
dharmē sadā yuvābhyāmudyamō bhavatyatra kartavyaḥ । natvā tatastābhyāmapi sapraṇayaṁ bhaṇitamiti vacanam ||25||
dharmōdyamēnāvāṁ mr̥gādīnmārayitvā nirvahāvaḥ । tatō'smābhirbhaṇitaṁ nahi nahyētatsamaṁ yuvayōḥ ॥ 26 ॥
jalalavacapalē jīvitē taḍittaralavilāsalakṣmī vistārē । paṭupavanaprahatapadminījalataralē svajanasaṁyōgē ||27||
madhumattakāminījana kaṭākṣavikṣēpacañcalē prēmaṇi । vāmānāṁ mānasamivāticapalē mauvanabharē ||28||
।
jinadharmō'nucarituṁ yuktō yuvayōstasya punarmūlam । samyaktvaṁ nirdiṣṭaṁ tasmāttad gr̥hītvā saviśēṣam ॥ 29 ॥
udyacchataṁ jina praṇītē dharma iti jalpitē'smābhiḥ । natvā tāvapi prabhagata āvāṁ kathayata jinadharmam ||30||
tatō dvividhō'pi kāryaṁtō dharmō'ṅgīkr̥taḥ punastābhyām । prathamē'samarthābhyāṁ gr̥hidharmō dvādaśavidhō'pi ॥ 31 ॥
itō'nyatra gatā vayaṁ tayōśca dharmaniratayōḥ । athānyadā ca pañcamatratē'tisaṁkaṭaṁ jātam ॥ 32॥
yasmāccatuṣpadānāṁ tābhyāṁ dvābhyāmapi niyamakālē । stōkā saṁkhyā vihitā, prativarṣa prasūyamānānām ||33||
॥33॥
jāyēta yadā samadhikā 'tadāticārō bhavēditi jñātvā । mūlaparimāṇamadhyādvikrīṇītē vallabhastāni ||34||
durlabhēna punaḥ pūrṇāyāṁ mūlasaṁkhyāyāṁ nijagavīnām । niyamāvadhēḥ paratō yathā garbhō bhavēttathā vihitam ||35||
tataḥ sa vallabharājēna prabhaṇitō mūḍha ! iti kurvatā । pañcamavratāticārō vihitastvayā'dhikaduḥkhadaḥ ॥ 26 ॥
iti śrutvā sa prabhaṇati gurūṇāṁ pārśvē yā mayā gr̥hītā । sā catuṣpadānāṁ saṁkhyēdānīmapi tāvatyēva ||37||
na mayā kiñcidapyadhikaṁ krītaṁ yēnēha bhavatyavicāraḥ । svayamēva catuṣpadāni maithunasaṁjñayā jāyantē ||38||

kō tattha majjha dōsō iya bhāsatō hasijjaē lōē । iyarōṁ uṇa jaha bhaṇiyaṁ tahēva taṁ pālaē payaō ॥
ēvaṁ vaccatama kālē kālēṇa kavaliyāṁ kahani । vallahadullaharāyā dōvihu niyaāuyassaṁtē ||40|
paḍhamō paḍhanē kappē bīō gaṁdhavvisu uvatrannō । tō sumariyapuvvaṁbhavā pāunbhūyā maha samīvē ॥ 41 ॥
ēgō tumhā purō niyaniyamaphalaṁ payāsaē dēvō । accharasāhiṁ sahiō picchaṇayachaṇavihāṇēṇa ॥ 42 ॥
iyarō sakalaṁkavaō kivvisiyasurō sarēvi gōvaragaṁ । tumhapaḍivōhaṇatthaṁ gāyai gōtrīyaṇēṇa samaṁ ||43||
iya kahiuṁ taccariyaṁ sūrī jā uvaraō, sa gaṁdhavvō । paḍhai surō tō ēvaṁ pacchāyāvēṇa saṁtattō ॥ 44 ॥
ēkapahuṇō sayāsē gahiyā viraī maē imēṇāvi । hī hī pamāyabasaō sakalaṁkā sā maē vihiyā ॥ 45 ॥
hā hā ciṁtāmaṇisaṁnihāē viraīya kalaṁkamāṇēvi । nibbhaggasēharēṇa kōḍīē varāḍiyā kiṇiyā ||46 ॥
saṁtō sāmayapāṇaṁ kāuṁ uccakkiyaṁ hayāsēṇaṁ । jaṁ gahiūṇaṁ viraī kalaṁkiyā mōhamūḍhēṇa || 47||
taṁ viraipālaṇaphalaṁ jē kīlai ēsa accharāhiṁ samaṁ । maha puṇa palavaṁtassavi na diti ēyāō paḍivayaṇaṁ ।।
iya suṇiūṇa rāyā saṁvēgava succhalaṁta suhabhāvō । sammattāīdhammaṁ paḍivajjai sūripāsamma || 49||
dēvāvi sugurucaraṇē namiūṇaṁ paḍigayā niyadvāṇaṁ । kappasamattīē taō gurūvi annattha viharēi || 50 ॥
tā jaha vallaṁharāēṇa pāliyā nikalaṁkavayaviraī । taha ēvaṁ anēṇavi pāliyanvā payatē ॥ 51 ॥
॥ iti parigrahaparimāṇacaturthāticārē durlabharājakathānakaṁ samāptam ॥
1
kastatra mama dōṣa iti bhāṣamāṇō hasyatē lōkē । itaraḥ punaryathā bhaṇitaṁ tathaiva tatpālayati prayataḥ ॥ 39 ॥
ēvaṁ vrajati tu kālē kālēna kavalitau kathamapi । vallabhadurlabharājau dvāvapi nijāyuṣō'ntē ||40||
prathamaḥ prathamē kalpē dvitīyō gānvarvikēṣūpapannaḥ । tataḥ smr̥tapūrvabhavau prādurbhūtau mama samīpē ॥41॥
ēkō yuṣmākaṁ purō nijaniyamaphalaṁ prakāśayati dēvaḥ । apsarōbhiḥ sahitaḥ prēkṣaṇakṣaṇavidhānēna ॥ 42 ॥
itaraḥ sakalaṅkavr̥taḥ kilbiṣikasuraḥ sr̥tvā gōvargam । yuṣmatpratibōdhanārthaṁ gāyati gōpījanēna samam ॥ 43 ॥
iti kathayitvā taccaritaṁ suriryāvaduparataḥ, sa gandharvaḥ । paṭhati surastata ēvaṁ paścāttāpēna saṁtaptaḥ ॥ 44 ॥
ēkaprabhōḥ sakāśē gr̥hītā viratirmayā'nēnāpi । hī hī pramādavaśataḥ sakalaṅkā sā mayā vihitā ॥ 45 ॥
hā hā cintāmaṇisaṁnibhāyāṁ viratau kalaṁkamānīya । nirbhāgyaśēkharēṇa kōṭyā varāṭikā krītā ॥ 46 ॥
saṁtōṣāmr̥tapānaṁ kr̥tvā vamitaṁ hatāśēna । yad gr̥hītvā viratiḥ kalaṅkitā mōhamūḍhēna ॥ 47 ॥
tadū
viratipālanaphalaṁ yatkrīḍatyēṣō'psarōbhiḥ samam । mama punaḥ pralapatō'pi na dadatyētāḥ prativacanam ||48 ||
iti śrutvā rājā saṁvēgavaśōcchalacchubhabhāvaḥ । samyaktvādidharmaṁ pratipadyatē sūripārśva ॥ 49 ॥
dēvāpi sugurucaraṇau natvā pratigatauṁ nijasthānam । kalpasamāptyā tatō gururapyanyatra viharati ॥50॥
tasmādyathā vallabharājēna pālitā niṣkalaṅkataviratiḥ । tathaivamanyēnāpi pālayitavyā prayatnēna ॥ 51 ॥

mūlaniyamāhiyāī kacōlāīṇi bhaṁjiuṁ puṇavi । tassaṁkhaṁ kuṇamāṇō māṇuvva virāhaē viraī ||1||
tathāhi;
asthi iha sāligāmō gaṁdhiyahava surahidanvaḍḍhō । amiyakalasābhihāṇō sēṭṭhī tatyatthi vikkhāō ||2||
tabbhajjā jiṇadēvī puttō sē māṇadēvanāmōtti । savvakalākusalōvi hu dōguccuvvāiō bhai ||3||
aha jaṇaṇaṁ samayaṁ pattō sō sāhusaṁnihāṇampi । namiūṇaṁ muṇicaraṇē nisuṇai sadēsaṇaṁ payaō ||4|
tathāhi;
1
kāya rammī sōvihu saṁtōsaō havai parō । sō vaṁchāvicchēē tanvicchēō vivēgāō ||5||
sō uṇa guruvayaṇāō tavtrayaṇānnaṇē taō jattō । kāyavyō buddhimayā nicaṁ nibbhicca cittēṇa || 6 |
jamhā saṁtōsōcci paramō mōkkhassa sāhaṇōvāō । ihalōiyasōkkhassavi sōcciya mūlaṁ jaō bhaṇiyaṁ ।
"saṁtōṣaiśvarya sukhināṁ dūrē duḥkhasamucchrayāḥ । lōbhāśābaddhacittānāmapamānaḥ padē padē ॥"
kiṁ paramaṁ iha dukkhaṁ sajigīsaṁ māṇasaṁ manussāṇaṁ । sōkkhaṁpi hu kiṁ paramaṁ sunirīhattaṁ jamiha bhaṇiya |
“tandulamānakamēkaṁ kandarpaharāpi yuvatirēkaiva । pr̥thvīpatērapi phalaṁ śēṣaḥ klēśō'bhimānō vā ॥"
jaha jaha lōbhōvaramō jaha jaha appō pariggahāraṁbhō । taha taha suhaṁ dhavaḍi dhammassa ya hōi saṁsiddhī ||
iccāidēsaṇaṁ nisuṇiūṇa vaṇiēṇa taṇayasahiēṇa | sammadaṁsaṇaputraṁ paṁcamayamaṇuvvayaṁ gahiyaṁ ||10||
tabbhāvatthaṁ nāuṁ muṇiṇō pāsamma paramaviṇaēṇa । tō māṇūdēvasahiō siṭṭhī vaṁdēvi muṇinā || 11||
saṁpattō niyagēhē puttrēṇa samaṁ karēi jiṇadhammaṁ । dōgaccahakilatō bhamai sayā māṇadēvōvi || 12 ||
aha annayā diṁḍī jōgīsaranāmaō gurujjāṇē । diṭṭhō puṭṭhō ya taō namiūṇaṁ sāyaraṁ tēṇa || 13 |
mūlaniyamādhikāni pātrādīni bhaṅktvā punarapi । tatsaṁkhyaṁ kurvan māna iva virādhayati viratim ॥1
astīha śāligrāmō gāndhikahaṭṭamiva surabhidravyāḍhyaḥ । amr̥takalaśābhidhānaḥ śrēṣṭhī tatrāsti vikhyātaḥ ॥ 2॥
tadbhāryā jinadēvī putrastasya mānadēvanāmēti । sarvakalākuśalō'pi hi daurgatyakhinnō bhramati ॥3॥
atha janakēna samaṁ prāptaḥ sa sādhusaṁnidhānē । natvā municaraṇau śr̥ṇōti saddēśānāṁ prayataḥ || 4 ||
kartavyō varadharmaḥ sō'pi hi saṁtōṣatō bhavati pravaraḥ । sa vāñchāvicchēdē tadvicchēdō vivēkāt ॥5॥
sa punarguruvacanāt tadvacanākarṇanē tatō yatnaḥ । kartavyō buddhimatā nityaṁ nirmr̥tyācattēna ॥ 6 ॥
yasmāt saṁtōṣa ēva paramō mōkṣasya sādhanōpāyaḥ । aihalōkika saukhyasyāpi sa ēva mūlaṁ yatō bhaṇitam ॥7॥
kiṁ paramamiha duḥkhaṁ sajigīṣaṁ mānasaṁ manuṣyāṇām । saukhyamapi hi kiṁ paramaṁ sunirīhatvaṁ yadiha bhaṇitam |
yathā yathā lōbhōparamō yathā yathā'lpaḥ parigrahārambhaḥ । tathā tathā sukhaṁ pravardhatē dharmasya ca bhavati saṁsiddhiḥ
ityādidēśanāṁ śrutvā vaṇijā tanayasahitēna । samyagdarśanapūrva pañcamamaṇuvrataṁ gr̥hītam ॥ 10 ॥
tadbhāvārtha jñātvā munēḥ pārśvē paramavinayēna । tatō mānadēvasahitaḥ śrēṣṭhī vanditvā muninātham ॥ 11॥
saṁprāptō nijagēhē putrēṇa samaṁ karōti jinadharmam | daurgatyaduḥ khaklāntō bhramati sadā mānadēvō'pi ॥ 12 ॥

kahasu uvāyaṁ kiṁpi hu lacchīlāhō havēi maha jēṇa । ittiyadiṇāṇi savvē vihalā jāyā maha uvāyā ॥
tō āha diṁḍī ḍaḍavaṁ mā karēsu maha puraō | atucchalacchivicchaḍḍumicchasē vaccha ! nicchayaō ||
jatā, tō maha puṭṭimā maṁcasu kahavi jāva chammāsaṁ । nō bhōyaṇāicitā kāyavvā kāvi vaṇiya ! taē |
tō tēṇaṁ paḍibhaṇiya juttamiṇa kiṁtu majjha piyarāṇa । sō natthi kōi duiō bhōyaṇamēttaṁpi jō dāhī ॥
buḍḍhāī thaḍḍhāī vihuṇiyavihavāī vāhivihurāī । maha virahammi maraṁtī tā kaha tāī karēmihi ? || 18 ||
tō jaṁpēṛa tiṁdaṁḍī jai ēvaṁ vaccha ! gaccha niyagēhūṁ । gahiūṇa imaṁ vijjaṁ vajjakutanāmiyaṁ pavaraṁ ॥ 19 ॥
ēsā ya paidipi hu rūppasta palāī paṁca tuha dāhī । sumariyamittāvi lahuṁ tō jattō ittha kāyavvō ॥ 20 ॥
iya bhaṇiūṇamadaṁsaṇamaha pattē tammi sōvi niyagēhē । pattō rayaṇī taō vihipujvaṁ sumariyā vijjā |
taēva tassussī sē ruṣpassa palāī paṁca mukāī । sō picchiya paccūsē giṇhai tāī pahimaṇō ||22||
tō tāī vikiṇiuṁ gahiraṁ davvaṁ karēi tēṇāvi । gēhanvayāi savvaṁ taha kiṁci sa dēi dhammammi ||23||
kaccōlamāiyāṇivi kavi ghaḍāvē tēṇa ruppēṇa । tō piuṇā sō bhaṇiō rē saṁpai vacchaṁ ! tuha gēhē ॥
kaccālāī dīsaṁti kaha ṇu kaha mūladavyavirahēvi । kaha miyasaṁkhaṁ davtraṁ taē vittaṁ phuḍaṁ kahasu ? ||25||
kahiē jahaṭṭiē tēṇa jāva siṭṭī palōpaē tuṭṭō । kañcōlāī niyamāu samahiyāīpi tā niyai || 26॥
।
viraivirāhaṇabhīō tō sō jaṁpēi majjha tujjhavi ya । kaccōlāṇaṁ dasagaṁ niyamē mukalayamēyāī ||27|
athānyadāṁ tridaṇḍī- yōgīśvaranāmakō gurudyānē । dr̥ṣṭaḥ pr̥ṣṭaśca tatō natvā sādaraṁ tēna ॥ 13 ॥
kathayōpāyaṁ kamapi khalu lakṣmīlābhō bhavati mama yēna । iyaddināni sarvē viphalā jātā mamōpāyāḥ || 14 ||
tata āha tridaṇḍī tugaḍatāṇḍavaṁ mā kuru mama purataḥ | atucchalakṣmīvistāramicchasi vatsa ! niścayataḥ ||
yadi tāvat, tatō mama pr̥ṣṭhaṁ mā muñca kathamapi yāvatṣaṇmāsīm | nō bhōjanādicintā kartavyā kāpi vaṇik ! tvayā ॥
tatastēna pratibhaṇitaṁ yuktamidaṁ kintu mama pitrōḥ । sa nāsti kaścid dvitīyō bhōjanamātramapi yō dāsyati ॥
vr̥ddhau stabdhau vidhutavibhavau vyādhividhurau । mama virahē mriyētē tasmātkathaṁ tau karōmīdānīm ॥ 18 ॥
tatō jalpati tridaṇḍī yadyēvaṁ vatsa ! gaccha nijagēham । gr̥hītvēmāṁ vidyāṁ vajrāṅkuśānāmikāṁ pravarām ॥ 19॥
ēṣā ca pratidinamapi khalu rūpyasya palāni pañca tē dāsyati । smr̥tamātrāpi laghu tatō yatna iha kartavyaḥ ॥
iti bhaṇitvādarśanamatha prāptē tasmin sō'pi nijagēhē । prāptō rajanyāṁ tatō vidhipūrvaṁ smr̥tā vidyā ॥21॥
tayāpi tasyōcchīrṣē rūpyasya palāni pañca muktāni । sa dr̥ṣṭvā pratyūṣē gr̥hṇāti tāni prahr̥ṣṭamanāḥ ||22||
tatastāni vikrīya gr̥hītvā dravyaṁ karōti tēnāpi । gēhavyayādi sarva tathā kiñcitsa dadāti dharmē || 23॥
pātrādīnyapi kathamapi ghaṭayati tēna rūpyēṇa । tataḥ pitrā sa bhaṇitō rē saṁprati vatsa ! tava gēhē ॥ 24॥
pātrāṇi dr̥śyantē kathaṁ nu kathaṁ mūladravyavirahē'pi । kathamitisaṁkhyaṁ dravyaṁ tvayā'rjitaṁ sphuṭaṁ kathaya ? ।।25।।
kathitē yathāsthitē tēna yāvat śrēṣṭhī pralōkatē tuṣṭaḥ । pātrāṇi niyamātsamadhikānyapi tadā paśyati ।। 26 ।
virativirādhanabhītastataḥ sa jalpati mama tavāpi ca । pātrāṇāṁ daśaka niyamē mutphalamētāni ॥ 27॥

supāsanāha-cariśrammi-
dīsaṁti samahiyāī, iya suṇiuṁ tēṇa niyamaahiyāī । tāī ēgīkāuṁ dasakhāī karāvē ||28|
di fast foō kaccōlāī na tāya ! ahiyāī । jāyāī gahiyāē viraīē mā bhayaṁ kuṇasu ॥ 29 ॥
tulē puṇa paṁcaraṇāī tāī kārāviyāī aiyāī । siṭṭhī pabhaṇā ēvaṁpi vaccha ! sakalaṁkiyā viraī ||30||
avi agmimmi pavēsō paḍaṇaṁ avaḍammi saṁdabhīmammi । avi uggakhaggadhārāē rōhaṇaṁ jalahipaḍaṇaṁ vā ॥
avi ahiyasahiyavāsē vasiyavvaṁ avi visaṁpi asiyanvaṁ । pullīpaōharāō pāyavvaṁ pāyasaṁ vāvi ||32||
na uṇō niyaniyamadhurā kalaṁkiyavvā kayāvi dhīrēhiṁ । taḍicalamaḍappharāē lacchīi kaē visēsēṇa ||33||
tā parihara dhaṇamiṇamō dhammammi va dēsu samahiyaṁ jamiha । annaha bhavammi bhīmē biraī ladhuṁpi bhamiyavvaṁ ॥
tattō tēvi bhaṇiō siṭṭhī mā tāya ! ērisaṁ bhaṇatu । tai gahiyavatthusaṁkhā ēvaṁpi kaē na bhajjēi || 3 ||
tō sēṭṭhī bhaṇai suyaṁ mā mā kūttarāī maha puraō । jaṁpēsu hōsu bhinnō giṇhēvi niyadavvabhāyaṁ ca ॥ 36 ॥
tō tēvi paḍivanaṁ jāō bhinnō karēi vāṇijjaṁ । siṭṭīvi dhammaniraō pālai gihidhammamakalaṁkaṁ ||37||
ōvi aṇuvivō jāō kālēṇa lōhagahamūḍhō । mūḍhavisūiyavatthō mariḍaṁ narayammi saṁpattī ||38||
bhafmī bhavam ajjavi pāvēṇaṁ viraibhaṁgajaṇiēṇaṁ । paḍhamamaiyāramittaṁ pacchā bhaṁgōvi sē jāō ||39||
vōvi aiyārō paḍhamaṁ ciṁya nēya jujjaē kāuṁ । thēvēṇa avacchāsēvaṇēṇa rōguvva vaḍḍhēi ||40 ॥
amilō siṭṭhī avirāhiyavirairayaṇabhāvāō । vihivihiyadēhacāō jāō ya saṇakumārammi ।
hu
dr̥śyantē samadhikāni, iti śrutvā sa niyamādhikāni । tānyēkīkr̥tya daśasaṁkhyāni kārayati ॥ 28 ॥
tēna śrēṣṭhī bhaṇitaḥ pātrāṇi nē tāta ! adhikāni । jātāni gr̥hītāyā viratērmā bhayaṁ kuruṣva ॥ 29 ॥
taulyē punaḥ pañcānāni tāni kāritānyētāni । śrēṣṭhī prabhaṇatyēvamapi vatsa ! saṁkalaṅkitā viratiḥ ॥ 30 ॥
apyagnau pravēśaḥ patanamavaṭē viśālabhīmē । apyugrakhaḍgadhārāyāṁ rōhaṇaṁ jalādhipatanaṁ vā ॥ 31 ॥
abhyahitasahitavāsē vastavyamapi viṣamapyaśikyam । vyāghrīpayōdharātpātavyaṁ pāyasaṁ vāpi ॥ 32 ॥
na punarnija niyamadhurā kalaṅkayitavyā kadāpi dhīraiḥ । taḍiccalagavayā lakṣmyāḥ kr̥tē viśēṣēṇa ॥ 33 ॥
tasmātparihara dhanamidaṁ dharmē vā dēhi samadhikaṁ yadiha । anyathā bhavē bhīmē viratiṁ labdhvāpi bhramitavyam ॥
tatastēnāpi bhaṇitaḥ śrēṣṭhī mā tāta ! īdr̥śaṁ bhaṇa । tvayā gr̥hītavastusaṁkhyaivamapi kr̥tē na bhajyatē ॥ 35॥
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī bhaṇati sutaṁ mā mā kūṭōttarāṇi mama purataḥ । jalpa bhava bhinnō gr̥hītvā nijadravyabhāgaṁ ca ॥ 36 ॥
tatastēnāpi pratipannaṁ jātō bhinnaḥ karōti vāṇijyam । śrēṣṭhyapi dharmanirataḥ pālayati gr̥hidharmamakalaṅkam ॥
tanayō'pyatanuvibhavō jātaḥ kālēna lōbhagrahamūḍhaḥ । mūḍhavisūcikāgrastō mr̥tvā narakē saṁprāptaḥ ||38||
bhramiṣyati bhavē'dyāpi pāpēna viratibhaṅgajanitēna । prathamamaticāramātra paścād bhaṅgō'pi tasya jātaḥ ॥ 29 ॥
stōkō'pi khalvaticāraḥ prathamamēva naiva yujyata kartum । stōkēnāpathyāsēvanēna rōga iva vardhatē ॥ 40 ॥

iyabhavē bhavakō taō cuō hōhihī ya, tā bhavvā ! | thēvēōvi vayāvasasā pālēyavvō niraiyārō ||
tathā,
tanhāsusiyasarīśa saṁtōsarasāyaṇaṁ sayā piyaha। jēṇa jaramaraṇaharaṇaṁ bhaviyajaṇā ! nivvuī lahaha ||43||
tē ghaṇiṇa tē guṇiṇō tē samiṇō tē vivēiṇō vaiṇō । saṁtōsanaṁdaṇavaṇē ramaṁti jē pamuiyā niccaṁ ॥ 44 ॥
yataḥ,
ēgaṁ jassa kalattaṁ citāvi hu tassa thōviyā hōī । sā duguṇāikamēṇaṁ vaḍḍhai ēkkikaḍhī ||45 ||
ēvaṁ puttāīsuvi harikarirahabhavaṇadaviṇamāīsu । vatēsu vivaḍḍhai maṇasaṁtāvō maṇussā ||46 ||
apariggahāṇa jā hōi nibbuī pasamasuhiyahiyayāṇaṁ । vēyaṁti muṇivaracciya tīsē surasaṁ rasaṁ nanē ||47||
jēttiyamittō lōhō tēttiyamittaṁ jiyāṇa dāridaṁ । saṁtōsī suyai suhaṁ sirakayacaraṇō daridassa ||48॥
uvarimuvariṁ niyaṁtō vidāi dhaṇīvi aidaridōvva । rōrōvi īsarāyai saṁtōsarasāyanē pīē ॥ 49 ॥
॥ iti pañcamavratapañcamāticāravipākē mānadēvadr̥ṣṭāntaḥ samāptaḥ ॥
tr̥tīyabhavē bhavamuktastataścyutō bhaviṣyati ca tasmādbhavyāḥ ! । stōkō'pi vrataviśēṣaḥ pālayitavyō niraticāraḥ ॥
tr̥ṣṇāśuṣkaśarīrāḥ saṁtōṣarasāyanaṁ sadā pibata । yēna jarāmaraṇaharaṇaṁ bhavyajanāḥ ! nirvr̥tiṁ labhadhvam ॥43॥
tē ghaninastē guṇinastē śaminastē vivēkinō pratinaḥ । saṁtōṣanandanavanē ramantē yē pramuditā nityam ॥44॥
ēkaṁ yasya kalatraṁ cintāpi hi tasya stōkā bhavati । sā dviguṇādikramēṇa vardhata ēkaikavr̥ddhau ॥ 45 ॥
ēvaṁ putrādiṣvapi harikarirathabhavanadraviṇādiṣu । vardhamānēṣu vivardhatē manaḥsaṁtāpō. manuṣyāṇām ॥ 46 ॥
aparigrahāṇāṁ yā bhavati nirvr̥tiḥ praśamasukhitahr̥dayānām । vēdayanti munivarā ēva tasyāḥ surasaṁ rasaṁ nānyē ॥
yāvanmātrō lōbhastāvanmātraṁ jīvānāṁ dāridryam । saṁtōṣī svapiti sukhaṁ śiraḥ kr̥tacaraṇō dāridryasya ॥ 48 ॥
uparyupari paśyan vidrāti dhanyapyatidaridra iva । rōrō'pīśvarāyatē saṁtōṣarasāyanē pītē ॥49॥

iti śrutvā rājā gurucintāduḥkhasāgaranimagnaḥ । kārayitvā duhitaraṁ rahasi mantrayati yathā vatsē ! ||43||
kiṁ kartavyamēvamēta upakāriṇaḥ samagrā api । tasmātkasmai tvaṁ dēyā, sā prabhaṇati tāta ! śūrāya ॥ 44 ॥
yasmādatipracaṇḍa ēpa itarau hanyānna hi bhrāntiḥ । pratipannaśca mayā punaḥ pūrvaṁ vaiśyaḥ svacittēna ॥45॥
nahi cintitamapi labhyatē tasmānmāṁ dēhi tasmai śūrāya । itarāvapi bōdhyētāṁ yātāṁ svasthānamavilambam ||46 ॥
tasmāt saviśēṣaṁ satkārya dvāvapi hi visarjitau rājñā । śūrō vivāhya maṇḍalikapadē saṁsthāpitaḥ || 47 ||
rathakārō'pi trilakṣō jātō niścitaṁ duḥkhitaḥ kumārīvirahē । cintayatyahō anayā pratipannaṁ pālitaṁ naiva ॥48॥
tasmātkimanēna dhanajīvitēna mama svajanaparijanēna ca । vijñānēnāpyanēna vinā'nayā tatō jhaṭiti ॥ 49 ॥
āruhya giriśikhara ātmā kila mōkṣyatē maraṇacittaḥ । tāvattatra munirdr̥ṣṭō jñānī dhyānē vartamānaḥ ॥50॥
praṇataśca sa vinayēna munināpi khalu dharmalābhayitvā bhaṇitaḥ । nirmānuṣē'raṇyē kimāgatastvamāsa bhōḥ ! kathaya ||
tataḥ sa kathayati maraṇasya kāraṇāt munivarēṇa tatō bhaṇitam । yuṣmādr̥śānāṁ yuktaṁ na bālamaraṇamahō kartum ॥
yadētēna kr̥tēnāpi jīvasya punarapi karmavaśagasya । bhavanti maraṇāni nūnaṁ tasmātkarmakṣayaṁ kuru ॥53॥
sa punarbhavati ṣaṣṭhāṣṭamādivividhaistapōviśēṣaiḥ । tē punarbhavanti kr̥tārthāstrikaraṇaśuddhayā, sā ca punaḥ ॥ 54 ॥
samyag nirvahati yatīnāṁ tyaktasaṅgānāṁ tasmāttvamapi yatiḥ । bhavēdaṁ śrutvā tathā vihitaṁ tēna sa cāham ॥
iti śrutvā bhaṇitaṁ mēgharathēna munindra ! anudivasam | jīvānāṁ bhavanti śatacaivaṁvidhahētavaḥ kintu ॥ 56 ॥
kō'pi hi karōtyēvaṁ tasmātprasadya mamāpyādiśata । ucitaṁ dharmaṁ yēna samyak tamahaṁ prapadyē ||17||

marihakahā ।
445
sammattāī guruṇā gihidhammō sāhiō hiō tēsiṁ । tassavi savisēsaṁ samuciyaṁti tō disivayaṁ kahai ॥
tattāyagōlakappō pramattasattō'ṇivāriyappasarō । savvattha kiṁ na kujjā pāvaṁ avirāmapariṇāmō ! ॥59॥
disigamaṇaparīmāṇē gahiē jīvāṇa hōi niyamēṇa । jīvadayāpariṇāmō suvisuddhō niccakālaṁpi ॥ 60 ॥
।
tēṇa ya hōi ahiṁsā bhāvēṇa nicchiyā sayākālaṁ । tīē ya nijjarā niru tamhā ēvaṁ yavvaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
citēyavvaṁ ca namō sāhūṇaṁ jē sayā nirāraṁbhā । viharati vippamukkā nagarāgaramaṁḍiyaṁ vasu || 62 ||
tē dhannā tāṇa namō iriyāirayā riyaṁti vasuhāē । vihivihiyavaravihārā hārā iva bhuvaṇalacchīē ॥ 63॥
tēhivi sammatāī gahiō gihidhammasārajiṇadhammō । aisavisēsaṁ saṁkhēvaō ya sammaṁ disivayaṁ tu ॥ 64 ॥
namiūṇa maṇi puṇaravi pattā gēhammi tē payattēṇa । pāliti gahiyadhammaṁ sammaṁ sammattamāīyaṁ ॥ 65 ॥
tō annayā paṭṭā visahr̥kaṁdaṭṭakaliya sarayammi । ujjēṇiṁ paṛa gaṁtuṁ gahiūṇaṁ pavarabhaṁḍāī ॥ 66 ॥
aha tatthavi bhaṁḍāī gahiūṇaṁ tāī cētra anēvi । pattā bahavē vaṇiyā bahudēsāṇaṁ taō tattha ||67 ||
aisayasamayaṁ jāyaṁ bhaṁḍa tō niyavi bhaṁḍasālāē । khivamāṇō lahubhāyā mēharahēṇaṁ imō bhaṇiō || 68 ॥
baṁdhava ! gammau vāṇārasīē jaṁ tattha agghaē ēyaṁ । annaha uvakkhaēṇavi mūlā vaṭṭō ihaṁ hōhī || 69॥
tattō maṇōraṇaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ bhajjēi disivayaṁ ēvaṁ | lābhē uṇa saṁdēhō nissaṁdēhō niyamabhaṁgō || 70 ||
yataḥ ;
"yē'rthāḥ klēśēna mahatā dharmasyātikramēṇa vā । arēvī praṇipātēna mā sma tēṣu manaḥ kr̥thāḥ || ”
mēgharahēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ paḍhamaṁ vaṇijēṇa niggayā amhē । tō uvahāsa lahimō lōyāō, taha ya piyarāī ॥ 71 ॥
samyaktvādirguruṇā gr̥hidharmaḥ kathitō hitastayōḥ । tatrāpi saviśēṣaṁ samucitamiti tatō digvataṁ kathayati ॥
taptāyōgōlakalpaḥ pramattasattvō 'nivāritaprasaraḥ । sarvatra kiṁ na kuryātpāpamavirāmapariṇāmaḥ ? ||59॥
diggamanaparimāṇē gr̥hītē jīvānāṁ bhavati niyamēna । jīvadayāpariṇāmaḥ suviśuddha nityakālamapi ॥ 60॥
tēna ca bhavatyahiṁsā bhāvēna niścitā sadākālam | tayā ca nirjarā niścitaṁ tasmādētad grahītavyam ॥ 61 ॥
cintayitavyaṁ ca namaḥ sādhubhyō yē sadā nirārambhāḥ । viharanti vipramuktā nagarākaramaṇḍitāṁ vasudhām ॥62॥
tē dhanyāstēbhyō nama īryādiratā viharanti vasudhāyām । vidhivihitavaravihārā hārā iva bhuvanalakṣmyāḥ ॥
tābhyāmapi samyaktvādirgr̥hītō gr̥hidharmasārajinadharmaḥ । atisaviśēṣaṁ saṁkṣēpataśca samyag digvataṁ tu ॥ 64॥
natvā muniṁ punarapi prāptau gēhē tau prayatnēna । pālayatō gr̥hītadharmaṁ samyak samyaktvādikam ||65||
tatō'nyadā pravr̥ttau vikasitanīlōtpalakalitaśaradi । ujjayinīṁ prati gantuṁ gr̥hītvā pravarabhāṇḍāni ॥ 66 ॥
atha tatrāpi bhāṇḍāni gr̥hītvā tānyēvānyē'pi । prāptā bahavō vaṇijō bahudēśānāṁ tatastatra ॥ 67 ॥
atiśayasama jātaṁ bhāṇḍaṁ tatō dr̥ṣṭrā bhāṇḍaśālāyām । kṣipalaghubhrātā mēgharathēnāyaṁ bhaṇitaḥ ॥ 68 ॥
bāndhava ! gamyatāṁ vārāṇasyāṁ yattatrārghyata ētat । anyathōpakṣayēṇāpi mūlād hāniriha bhaviṣyati ॥69॥
tatō manōrathēna bhaṇitaṁ bhajyatē ditamēvam । lābhē punaḥ saṁdēhō niḥsaṁdēhō niyamabhaṅgaḥ ॥ 70 ॥

supāsanāha cariasmi -
nō puṇaravi vaṇijēṇaṁ nikhvaissaṁti taha ya dhammassa । hōhī buḍḍhī na jaō gihiṇō davvēṇa sā hōi ॥
tō tēṇaṁ paḍibhaṇiyaṁ kō uvahāsō nayaṁ pavannāṇa । paradavvāivahārē jēṇaṁ sō hōi vaṇiyāṇaṁ ॥73॥
vavaharamāṇāṇa puṇō hōi sulāhō kayāvalābhō vā । saṁgāmēvi hu suhaḍā hāraṁti jiṇaṁti kayāvi || 74 ॥
ēvaṁ tu na bhaṇiyavvaṁ paḍhamavaṇijjēṇa mūlahāṇīē । puṇaravi ya maē vaṇijjaṁ nahu kāyavvaṁti jaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥
jaivi guruvalligahaṇē bhaggakamō kahavi kēsarī jāō । tahavi ya mattagayāṇaṁ puṇōvi kuṁbhatthalaṁ dalai ||
jaṁ bhaṇasi puṇavi piyarō vaṇijatthaṁ nēya paṭṭavissaṁti | kā amhāṇaṁ hāṇī jai ēvaṁ tē karissaṁti ? ॥
jaṁ bhaṇasi dhammavuḍḍhī davvēṇaṁ hōi sāvayajaṇassa । taṁpi na juttaṁ kiṁ kōvi kuṇau tittaṁpi dhammatthaṁ ? ॥
yataḥ ;
"anyāyōpāttavittēna yō hitaṁ hi samīhatē । bhakṣaṇāt kālakūṭasya sō'bhivāñchati jīvitam " |
iccāisujuttīhi niruttarō sō kaōvi taṁ bhaṇai । jai ēvaṁ tō baṁdhava ! majjha vibhāgaṁ samapsu || 79 ॥
tō taṁ pai sō jaṁpai savrvvapi dhaṇaṁ dharēsu niyapāsē । iha gami kavi dinē piūṇa pāsē gamissāmi ||
tahavinaya niyamabhaṁga karēmi maṇasāvi nicchaō ēsa । ittō paraō jamhā disavvayaṁ samahiyē hō ||
tujjhavi na juttamēyaṁ maṁ mōttu taha vayaṁpi bhaṁjēuṁ । bāṇārasīē gamaṇaṁ davvapivāsāē naḍiyassa || 82 ॥
tō mēharahō jaṁvai mā pabhaṇasu kiṁpi ittha visayammi | gaṁtavvavamassaṁ ciya niyapunnaparikkhaṇakaraṇa ||
tō taṁ davvaṁ savvaṁ samapiyaṁ tassa, sōvi satthēṇa । saha patthiō kamēṇaṁ pattō vāṇārasiṁ nayariṁ ॥ 84 ॥
mēgharathēna bhaṇitaṁ prathamaṁ vāṇijyēna nirgatāvāvām । tata upahāsaṁ lapsyāvahē lōkāt, tathā ca pitarau ॥ 71 ॥
nō punarapi vāṇijyēna nirūpayiṣyatastathā ca dharmasya । bhaviṣyati vr̥ddhirna yatō gr̥hiṇō dravyēṇa sā bhavati ॥ 72 ॥
tatastēna pratibhaṇitaṁ ka upahāsō nayaṁ prapannānām ? । paradravyādyapahārē yēna sa bhavati vaṇijām ||73॥
vyavaharamāṇānāṁ punarbhavati sulābhaḥ kadāpyalābhō vā । saṁgrāmē'pi hi subhaṭā naśyanti jayantiṁ kadāpi ||74 ||
ēvaṁ tu na bhaṇitavyaṁ prathamavāṇijyēna mūlahānyām । punarapi ca mayā vāṇijyaṁ na hi kartavyamiti yad bhaṇitam ॥
yadyapi guruvalīgahanē bhagnakramaḥ kathamapi kēsarī jātaḥ । tathāpi ca mattagajānāṁ punarapi kumbhasthalaṁ dalayati ॥
yad bhaṇasi punarapi pitarau vāṇijyārthaṁ naiva prasthāpayiṣyataḥ । kā'smākaṁ hāniryadyēvaṁ tau kariṣyataḥ ? ||77||
yad bhaṇasi dharmavr̥ddhirdravyēṇa bhavati śrāvakajanasya । tadapi na yuktaṁ kiṁ kō'pi karōtu cintāmapi dharmārtham ? ॥
ityādisuyuktibhirniruttaraḥ sa kr̥tō'pi taṁ bhaṇati । yadyēvaṁ tatō bāndhava ! mama vibhāgaṁ samarpaya ॥ 79 ॥
tatastaṁ prati sa jalpati sarvamapi dhanaṁ ghara nijapārśvē । iha gamayitvā katyapi dinān pitrōḥ pārśvē gamiṣyāmi ॥
tathāpi na ca niyamabhaṅgaṁ karōmi manasāpi niścaya ēṣaḥ । itaḥ paratō yasmād digvataṁ samadhikaṁ bhavati ॥ 81 ॥
tavāpi na yuktamētada māṁ muktvā tathā vratamapi bhaktvā । vārāṇasyāṁ gamanaṁ dravyapipāsayā naṭitasya ॥ 82॥
tatō mēgharathō jalpati mā pramaṇa kimapyatra viṣayē । gantavyamavaśyamēva nijapuṇyaparīkṣaṇakr̥tē ॥ 83 ॥
tatastad dravyaṁ sarva samarpitaṁ tasmai, sō'pi sārthēna । saha prasthitaḥ kramēṇa prāptō vārāṇasīṁ nagarīm ||84॥

mōrahakahā ।

૪૪૭
sukaviyaṁ taṁ bhaṁḍa avalaviḍaṁ kiṁpi tassa majjhāō । taṁ sukapālaēhiṁ nāyaṁ gahiyaṁ ca sēsaṁpi ॥ 85 ॥
jāyaṁ samagyatarayaṁ samuṭṭhiyaṁ nēya mūlamullaṁpi । tō dhammāu pamattō ciṁtāsayasaṁkulattāō ॥ 86 ॥
vīō puṇa ujjēṇīvatthavvayavaṇimahiṁdasīhassa । gēhammi gamai diyahē saddhammaparāyaṇō dhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 87॥
aha annayā kayāvi hu nariṁdavaranaṁdaṇō udayapālō । bālavayaṁsasamēō kīlatō kāṇaṇē kammi ||
rat bhuyaṁgamēṇa pāyaguḍampi takkhaṇēṇēva । paḍiō dharaṇīi taō samuṭṭiō kalayalō jhati ॥ 89 ॥
tō kahiyē ēkēṇaṁ kumāramittēna rāulē gaṁtuṁ । naravaṇō jaha kumarō ḍakō ahiṇā vahi dēva ! ॥90॥
taṁ sōuṁ naravaṇā narē nirūvittu pavaragāruḍiyā । āhūyā tattha taō samagaṁ nīyā bahumāṇaṁ ॥ 91 ॥
visavasavisapipīḍaṁ kumaraṁ dadatuṁ nariṁdavidēṇa । bhaṇiyaṁ ēsō nijjau bhavaṇē jēṇujimō dēva ! || 92||
vihiyaṁ tahēva rannā tēhivi vihiṇā sa jiō payaō । niyayagurūuvaiṭuṁ agayaṁpi paraṁjiaṁ tattō ॥
jō jō kiṁpi pauṁja sō sō visadhāriōvva bhūvīḍhē । luṭai vihalaṁghalōcciya tō bhīō naravaī bhaṇaṛa ||
bhō bhō talāra ! viyaraha savvatō paḍahayaṁ tahā bhaṇaha । jō kumaraṁ jīvāvara tassaddhaṁ dēi rajjassa ॥95॥
ēvaṁ vi vihiyaṁ savvattō matavāiṇō iti । naya yēvōvi visēsō visēṇa puṇa ghāriyā savvē ॥ 96॥
tō khuhiō savvajaṇō hāhārāvō purē samucchaliō । paigēhaṁ parahaṭṭaṁ sōūṇa maṇōrahēṇa tayaṁ ॥ 97॥
bhaṇiō madisīhō jaṛa taṁ pabhaṇēsi tā ahaṁ kumaraṁ । takkhanamittēṇaṁ ciya pauṇasarīraṁ karēmi jaō ||
majjhavi gurūvasō iha visa kōvi vijjaē pavasē । iya sōūṇaṁ bhaṇiō mahiṁdasīhēṇa sō ēvaṁ ॥ 99 ॥
śulkitaṁ tadbhāṇḍamapalapitvā kimapi tasya madhyāt । tat śulkapālakairjñātaṁ gr̥hītaṁ ca śēṣamapi ॥85॥
jātaṁ samardhataraṁ samutthitaṁ naiva mūlamūlyamapi । tatō dharmāt pramattaścintāśatasaṁkulatvāt ॥86॥
dvitīyaḥ punarujjayinīvāstavya vaṇigmahēndrasiṁhasya । gēhē gamayati divasānsaddharmaparāyaṇō gāḍham ||87॥
athānyadā kadāpi hi narēndravaranandana udayapālaḥ । bālavayasyasamētaiḥ krīḍan kānanē kasmit ॥ 88 ॥
daṣṭō bhujaṁgamēna pādāṅguṣṭhē tatkṣaṇanaiva । patitō dharaṇyāṁ tataḥ samutthitaḥ kalakalō jhaṭiti ॥ 89 ॥
tataḥ kathitamēkēna kumāramittrēṇa rājakulē gatvā । narapatayē yathā kumārō dr̥ṣṭō'hinā bahidēva ! ॥90॥
tat śrutvā narapatinā narān nirūpya pravaragāruḍikāḥ । āhūtāstatra tataḥ samaṁ nītāḥ sabahumānam ॥91॥
viṣavaśavisarpipīḍaṁ kumāraṁ dr̥ṣṭvā narēndravr̥ndēna । bhaṇitamēṣa nīyatāṁ bhavanē yēna yuñjīmahi dēva ! ॥92॥
vihitaṁ tathaiva rājñā tairapi vidhinā sa yuktaḥ padataḥ । nijagurūpadiṣṭamagadamapi prayuktaṁ tataḥ ॥ 93 ॥
yaḥ yaḥ kimapi prayuktaṁ sa sa viṣaghātitavad bhūpīṭhē । luṭīta viddala ēva tatō bhītō narapatirbhaṇati ॥94॥
bhō bhōḥ purārakṣaka ! vitarata sarvataḥ paṭahaṁ tathā bhaṇata । yaḥ kumāraṁ jīvayati tasmai artha dadāti rājyasya ||
ēvaṁ tēnāpi vihitaṁ sarvatō mantravādina āyanti । naca stōkō'pi viśēṣō viṣēṇa punarghātitāḥ sarvē ॥96॥
tataḥ kṣubhitaḥ sarvajanō hāhārāva : purē samucchalitaḥ । pratigēhaṁ pratihaṭṭaṁ śrutvā manōrathēna tat ॥ 97 ॥
bhaṇitō mahēndrasiṁhō yadi tvaṁ prabhaṇasi tadāhaṁ kumāram । tatkṣaṇamātrēṇaiva praguṇaśarīraṁ karōmi yataḥ ||98||

448
supāsanāha-cariammi-
mā mā mammi ēvaṁ ciṁtasu taṁ vaccha ! jēṇa jō kōvi । tassa pauṁjai vijjaṁ mataṁ taṁtaṁ va sō sahasā ॥
visāriō lui mahīi ahiyaṁ nariṁdavidōvi । kā tattha tujjha gaṇaṇā guṇalavajuttassa vaṇiyassa 1 ॥
yataḥ,
"yasya vajramaṇērbhēdē bhidyantē lōhasūcayaḥ । karōtu tatra kiṁ nāma nārīnakhavilēkhanam ? ॥"
mā hu akaṁḍē khaṁḍa niyajīyaṁ vaccha ! vāriō virama । iya sōuṁ sō pabhaṇai ēvaṁ ciya natthi saṁdēhō ॥
kiṁtu karuṇāvarujjhai intiyalōyassa dukkhabhariyassa । paradukkhakkhayakajjē purisāṇaṁ tiṇasamaṁ jīyaṁ ॥
yataḥ,
jīyaṁ kāsu na ihaṁ lacchī kassa na vallahā hōi । avasarapattāī puṇō dunnivi tiṇayāu lahuyaṁti || 104 ||
navaraṁ pacchimarayaṇīē ajja jaṁ sumiṇayaṁ maē dihaṁ । lakkhēmi tayaṇusārēṇa savvamavi attaṇō kusalaṁ ॥
iya sōuṁ sō nīō mahiṁdasīhēṇa naravaisamīvaṁ । kahiyā ya tassa sattī, rannā tō daṁsiō kumarō ॥
tēvi tassa samī pavisaṁtēṇa nisīhiyā bhaṇiyā । paṁcapara miṭṭisaṁthavamiṇamō bhaṇiuṁ samādattō ॥
viḍiyōhē mahāpāḍihērakayasōhē । bhaviyakamalapaḍibōhē namimō jiṇanāhasaṁdōhē ||108॥
siddhisusamiddhāṇaṁ daṁsaṇavara nāṇatēyanidvāṇaṁ । tailōyapasiddhāṇaṁ namō namō savvasiddhāṇaṁ ॥ 109 ॥
kaṁdaṣpakariharīṇaṁ nimmalaguṇarayaṇarōhaṇagirīṇaṁ । paṇaō hē sūrīṇaṁ paṁcavihāyāradhārīṇaṁ ॥ 110 ॥
mayaṇānala vijjhāē aṇavarayavinnasāhusajjhāē । siddhivahūnijjhāē payaō paṇa prāmujjhāē | 111 ॥
paricattasavvasaṁgē duddharatavacaraṇaniccasusiyaṁgē । bahuvihasahiuvasaggē namimō bhattīē muviggē ॥ 112 ॥
mamāpi gurūpadēśa iha viṣayē kō'pi vidyatē pravaraḥ । iti śrutvā bhaṇitī mahēndrasiṁhēna sa ēvam ॥99॥
mā mā manasyēvaṁ cintaya tvaṁ vatsa ! yēna yaḥ kō'pi । tasya prayuṅktē vidyāṁ mantraṁ tantraṁ vā sa sahasā ॥
viṣaghātita iva luṭhati mahyāmadhikaṁ narēndravr̥ndamapi kā tatra tava gaṇanā guṇalavayuktasya vaṇijaḥ || 101 ॥
mā khalvakāṇḍē khaṇḍaya nijajīvitaṁ vatsa ! vāritō virama । iti śrutvā sa prabhavatyēvamēva nāsti saṁdēhaḥ ||
kintu karuṇōparuṇaddhi ētāvalōkasya duḥkhabhr̥tasya । paraduḥkhakṣaya kāryē puruṣāṇāṁ tr̥ṇasamaṁ jīvitam ॥102॥
jīvita kasya nēṣṭaṁ lakṣmīḥ kasya na vallabhā bhavati । avasaraprāptē punadvē api tr̥ṇād laghayantiḥ ॥ 104 ॥
navaraṁ paścimarajanyāmadya yaḥ svapnō mayā dr̥ṣṭaḥ । lakṣayāmi tadanusārēṇa sarvamapyātmanaḥ kuśalam ॥105॥
iti śrutvā sa nītō mahēndrasiṁhana narapatisamīpam । kathitā ca tasya śaktiḥ, rājñā tatō darśitaḥ
tēnāpi tasya samīpē praviśatā naiṣēdhikī bhāṇatā । pañcaparamēṣṭhisaṁstavamimaṁ bhaṇituṁ samārabdhaḥ || 107 ||
vighaṭitapracaṇḍa mōhānaṣṭamahāprātihāyakr̥taśōbhān । bhavikakamalapratibōdhān namāmō jinanāthasaṁdōhān ॥ 108 ॥
siddhisukhasamr̥ddhēbhyō darśanavarajñānatējōniṣṭhēbhyaḥ । trailōkyaprasiddhēbhyō namō namaḥ sarvasiddhēbhyaḥ ॥109॥
kandarpakāraharīn nirmalaguṇaratnarōhaṇāgirīn । praṇatō'haṁ sūrīn pañcavidhācāradhāriṇaḥ ॥ 110 ॥
vidhyātamadanānalāna'navaratavitīrṇasādhusvādhyāyān । siddhivadhūnidhyātān prayataḥ praṇamāmyupādhyāyān ॥ 111 ॥
ḥ kumāraḥ ॥

iti pañcaparamēṣṭhināṁ paramapadasthānāṁ niṣṭhitaduḥkhānām । atītānāgatasaṁpratikālagatānāṁ gatabhayānām ॥ 114 ॥
yaḥ karōti saṁstatraṁ nistaratyatidustaramapi duḥkhajaladhim । tallakṣamanāḥ śramaṇō gr̥hī vāsa śivasukhaṁ labhatē ।।
ētaṁ bhaṇitvā stavaṁ bhūtvā ca kumāra karṇamūlē । sapraṇidhānaṁ vidhinā trisaptakr̥tva idaṁ bhaṇati ॥ 116 ॥

paramēṣṭhiśravaṇatō mayā jñātō'vadhinā pūrvabhavadharmaḥ । gārlataṁ tathā mithyātvaṁ tama iva dinamaṇimayūkhaiḥ ॥ 118 ॥

kintu kumārēṇa kāryōṁ jinadharmō nr̥patināpi yēnaitaiau । tatra prasādēna sukhaṁ labhētē ladhvanyajanmanyapi ॥ 122 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ manōrathēna viṣaghātitamētallōkamapi nīrujam । kuru mahāyaśaḥ ! tatastēna sō'pi viṣavirahitō vihitaḥ ।।

sō bhai suṇē, āsī iha bharahē sivapurammi sivabhō । siṭṭī sammadiṭṭhī pithavaī bhāriyā tassa ||
tāṇaṁ ca paṁca putā parōpparaṁ nēhanivbharā savvē । varuṇaguṇacaṁda suṁdarajasaēvamahidanāmāṇō || 128 ||
dhammammi nirahilāsā dullaliyā taha aṇatthakulabhavaṇaṁ । aha siṭṭijāṇasālāē āgayā sūriṇō kēci ॥

pahu ! maha ēē puttā utpannā caiva sāvayakulammi | navaraṁ dēvagurūṇaṁ jāṇaṁti na nāmamittaṁpi ॥ 132॥

sa bhaṇati śr̥ṇu, āsīdiha bharatē śivapurē śivabhadraḥ । śrēṣṭhī samyagdr̥ṣṭiḥ priyaṁvadā bhāryā tasya ॥ 127 ॥

vihati niviḍaghaḍiyā purisatthā niyamaō pamāēṇa । ciravihaḍiyāvi lahu saṁghati suvidattadhammāṇaṁ ॥
iccāidēsaṇaṁ nisuṇiūṇa tē siṭṭhinaṁdaṇā sūriṁ । pabhaṇati jassa dhammassa jōggayā amha taṁ kahaha ।। 142॥
tō tēsi si sadēsaṇadaṁsaṇaṁ kayaṁ guruṇā । pāṇivahāīviraī paruviyā jāva disiviraī ॥ 143 ॥

tō siṭṭhī ahi vaṁditu bhaṇai ērisaṁ vayaṇaṁ । kēśava kēṇa na bhaṇiyā ēē saddhammaviyammi || 145 ॥
kiṁtu bahi luṭa jalaṁ jaha bharighassa taha imēsipi । ittiyadiṇāṇi vayaṇaṁ dhammāyariyāṇa vihivasaō ॥
iṇhiṁ puṇa ēēsi amayaṁ pitra pariṇaō tavāsō ! tō siṭṭisuyā bhaṇiyā guruṇā dhammē diḍhā hōha || 147 ॥
ēvaṁti pabhaṇiūṇaṁ gurupayapaumaṁ namitta sahāṇē । siṭṭhisamēyā pattā garmati kālaṁ samātā ॥ 148 ॥ .
savvatthaviṁ laddhajasā dhammiṭṭhā sacabāiṇō vaṇiṇō । dhaṇuvēyaṁ para kusalā riddhisamiddhā ya saṁjāyā ।। 149॥
1
aha tannayara nivēṇaṁ tāṇa pasiddhiṁ suṇittu vibhō । bhaṇiō paṇayapurassara mēgaṁtē sāyaraṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 150 ॥
siddhi ! maha natthi kōvi hu bhāyā jaṇaō ya sayaṇavaggō ya । tā ēē niyaputtā bhaṇasu jahā majjha sāhijjē ॥
va ṁti maē saddhiṁ bhamaṁti bhujaṁti jaṁti kajjēsu । annaha na havāi kaiyāvi majjha maṇanivvuī siṭṭi ! ||
tō siṭṭhī pabhaṇaṛa mē tujjhāyattaṁ khu jīviyavvaṁpi । kā taṇayāṇaṁ gaṇaṇā, paraṁ imē sāvayā savayā ।। 153 ॥
kharakampaniōgāṇaṁ virayā nirayāidukkhahēūṇa । cīnaṁdaṇāikiccaṁ kuvvaṁti vayaṁti muṇivāsē || 154 ||
vighaṭantē nibiḍaghaṭitāḥ puruṣārthōṁ niyamataḥ pramādēna । ciravighaṭitā api laghu saṁghaṭantē svarjitadharmaṇām ॥
ityādidēśanāṁ śrutvā tē śrēṣṭhinandanāḥ sūrim । prabhaṇanti yasya dharmasya yōgyatāsmākaṁ taṁ kathaya ॥ 142 ॥
tatastēbhyaḥ sarvēbhyaḥ saddarśanadarśanaṁ kr̥taṁ guruṇā । prāṇivadhādiviratiḥ prarūpitā yāvad digviratiḥ ॥ 143॥
iyanmātraṁ tairapi pratipannaṁ śēṣamapi śraddhitam । parityaktaṁ mithyātvaṁ yāvajjīvamapi trividhēna ॥ 144 ॥
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī atihr̥ṣṭō vanditvā bhaṇatīdr̥śaṁ vacanam । kēna vā kēna na bhaṇitā ētē saddharmaviṣayē ? ॥ 145॥
kintu bahirluṭhati jalaṁ yathā bhr̥taghaṭasya tathaiṣāmapi । iyaddināni vacanaṁ dharmācāryāṇāṁ vidhivaśataḥ ॥ 146 ॥
idānīṁ punarētēṣāmamr̥tamiva pariṇatastavādēśaḥ । tataḥ śrēṣṭhisutā bhaṇitā guruṇā dharmē dr̥ḍhā bhavata ॥ 147॥
ēvamiti prabhaṇya gurupadapadmaṁ natvā svasthānē । śrēṣṭhisamētāḥ prāptā gamayanti kālē samāyuktāḥ ॥ 148॥
sarvatrāpi labdhayaśasō dharmiṣṭhāḥ satyavādinō vaṇijaḥ । dhanurvēdaṁ prati kuśalā r̥ddhisamr̥ddhāśca saṁjātāḥ ॥ 149 ॥
atha tannagaranr̥pēṇa tēṣāṁ prasiddhiṁ śrutvā śivabhadraḥ । bhaṇitaḥ praṇayapurassaramēkāntē sādaramēvam ॥ 190॥
śrēṣṭhin ! mama nāsti kō'pi hi bhrātā janakaśca svajanavargaśca । tasmādētānnijaputrān bhaṇa yathā mama sāhāyyē |
vartantē mayā sārdhaṁ bhramanti bhuñjatē yānti kāryēṣu । anyathā na bhavati kadāpi mama manōnivr̥tiḥ śrēṣṭhin ! ॥
tataḥ śrēṣṭhī prabhaṇati mē tavāya khalu jīvitavyamapi । kā tanayānāṁ gaṇanā, paramimē śrāvakāḥ savratāḥ ॥ 153॥
kharakarmaniyōgēbhyō viratā nirayādiduḥkhahētubhyaḥ । caityavandanādikr̥tyaṁ kurvanti vrajanti munipārśvē ॥ 154॥

Fat guṇō vārēhi kammavasāō na uṇa iyarīē । tāṇa visēsaṁ jāṇai savvannū na uṇa chaumatthō |
tā avigappaṁ jattō kāyavvō āvayāē duvihāē । sōvakamāē viṁgamō iyarāi nicchiyaṁ maraṇaṁ ॥ 169 ॥
tasmātkathaṁ prabhusāhāyyē vartiṣyanta iha mama sutā ētē ? । tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā kharakarmādi na kārayiṣyē ॥
caityavandanādikr̥tyaṁ kurvataḥ kō'pi nō nivārayiṣyati । kintu rāma saṁnidhānaṁ mōktavyaṁ naivaitaiḥ ॥ 156॥
tataḥ pratipannaṁ tēnāpi nr̥pavacanaṁ sō'pi nijagr̥haṁ prāptaḥ । pratyūṣē tē tanayāḥ śikṣāṁ dattvā prēṣitāḥ ॥ 157 ॥
tēspi nr̥papādapārśvē tiṣṭhanti kurvanti nijamanuṣṭhānam । iti vrajati kālē kadāpi tē prabhaṇitā rājñā ॥ 118 ॥
yathā saṁprati mama kāryaṁ samutthitaṁ kimapi sidhyati yuṣmābhiḥ । tatastē bhaṇantyādiśa dēva !, sa jalpatyēvam ॥
catvārō mahānarapatayō vilōṭhitāścaturdikṣvapyaticalinaḥ । pañcamō malayācaladurgād vidravati mama dēśam ॥
tatō yūyaṁ buddhiyalēna saṁgatā gurugajaghaṭāsamētāḥ । pañcāpi pañcānāmupari yathāśakti yasya yō yōgyaḥ ॥
sa gacchatu tasyōpari, vayamiha dēśasyaṁ madhyē । sthāsyāmastasmāt saṁvahata jhaṭitīti bhaṇitē ॥ 162 ॥
tātasakāśaṁ prāptāḥ kathayanti nr̥pēṇa yadrahasi bhaṇitāḥ । tataḥ sa laghu gatvā nr̥pasya saṁmukhaṁ bhaṇatyēvam ॥ 163 ॥
śr̥ṇōtu mama vijñapti dēvaḥ prasadya gama laghuputram । atraiva dharatvanyatra kutrāpi mā nirūpayatu || 164 ॥
naimittikēna yasmādviṁśavarṣē tasya nirdiṣṭā । prāṇāntikāt prabhō ! viṁśavarṣamapi tadētat ॥ 165॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ narapatinā'traiva sthitasya kiṁ na sā bhaviṣyati ? | bhavitavyatāyā nāśō na bhavati kadāpi niścayataḥ ॥
ēvamēva sa prabhaṇati kintvihāpad bhavati dvividhā | sōpakramanirupakramabhēdēna tatra prathamāyām ॥ 167 ॥
bhavati guṇa upacāraiḥ karmavaśatō na punaritarasyām । tayōrviśēṣaṁ jānāti sarvajñō na punaśchāsthaḥ ॥ 168॥

āsi purā supasiddhō pōyaṇapurasāmiō miyaṁkamu hō । nīighaḍō tassacivō bhajjā sē rōhiṇī nāma ।।

jaṁ jārisammi laggē pasiṇō jammōvi tampi sē hōhī | tāṇuvariṁ puṇa kamasō kulavuṭṭhi sōvi kāhitti ||

niyasuyasusmr̥saṁ, tō iya jāva gayāī paṁca varisāī । tattō ya taṁ samappai lēhāyariyassa paḍhaṇatthaṁ । । 178 ॥

tō pabhaṇai mā pucchasu vacchē ! tucchāu jēṇa itthīō। airahasaṁpi hu kahiyaṁ payaḍī kuvvaṁti sahasēva ||
tō tī sahapucvaṁ savrvvapi hu pucchiūṇa vinnāē । niśyagharāu suraṁgā khaṇāviyā jāṁva bhūmiharaṁ ॥ 184 ॥
gaṁtūna suraṁgāē diṭṭhō sō sacivasaṁtiō puttō । tēvisā tō puṭṭhā kā si tumaṁ āgayā kimiha ? ||
sā bhai siṭṭitaṇayā hamāgayā tujjha daṁsaṇanimittaṁ । kattha vasasitti bhagiē tēṇaṁ, sā kahai tassa purō ॥
itthēva naramajjhē gharēdēulakūvavāviramaṇijjaṁ । tuvarapaccāsanē maha piuṇō varagharamatthi || 187 ||
puṭṭhā puṇōvi tēṇa gharapuramāīṇi kisaruvāṇi । jē kila caṁdāiccā nāmamālāē sē paḍhiyā || 188 ।।
tēsipi kiṁ sarūvaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ tō tīi kuṁmara ! maha saddhi । āgaccha jēṇa savvaṁ paccakkhaṁ tujjha payaḍēmi ।। 189॥
tō tī maggalaggō nīhariō sō purassa majjhami । jaṁjaṁ picchai taṁ taṁ pucchara tō tīē pāsammi ।।190॥
puṇaravi tīē nīō sahāṇē pabhaṇiyā ya sā ēvaṁ । niccapi daṁsiyavvaṁ ēēṇa kamēṇa maha savvaṁ ॥ 199 ॥
tō putrapaōgēṇaṁ paidiyahaṁ daṁsaē nayaramajjhē । gahatārāī savvaṁ tō bhaṇiyaṁ rāulē nēsu ॥ 192॥
dūraṭṭiyāē tīē pi hu sē daṁsiya, iya kamēṇa । pāyaṁ savvōvi hu tassa daṁsiō vatthuniurō ।।193।।
bhaṇiyaṁ nāhaṁ ētō tujjha sayāsammi āgamissāmi । jai kahavi hu tujjha piyā viyāṇaī tō ya maha piuṇō ।।
kuṇa aṇatthaṁ kiṁpi hu, tujjhavi kiṁ hiṁḍiēṇa bahuē । naimittiyassa vayapi sāhium̐ sā gayā, tahavi ।।
pairayaṇī bhamaṁtassa tassa kēṇavi tidaṁḍiṇā saddhi । jāō aīva nēhō, adēsīkāriṇī vijjā ।। 196 ॥
tataḥ prabhaṇati mā pr̥ccha vatlē ! tucchā yēna striyaḥ । atirahasyamapi hi kathitaṁ prakaṭīkuvanti sahasaiva ॥
tatastayā śapathapūrvaṁ sarvamapi pr̥ṣṭvā vijñātē । nijagr̥hāt suruṅgā khānitā yāvad bhūmigr̥ham ॥ 184 ॥
gatvā suruṅgayā dr̥ṣṭaḥ sa sacivasatkaḥ putraḥ । tēnāpi sā tataḥ pr̥ṣṭā kā'si tvamāgatā kimiha ? || 185 ॥
sā bhaṇati śrēṣṭhitanayā'hamāgatā tava darśananimittam । kutra vasasīti bhaṇitē tēna sā kathayati tasya puraḥ ॥
atraiva nagaramadhyē gr̥hadēvakulakūpa vāpīramaṇīyaṁ । tvadgr̥hapratyāsannē mama pituḥ pravaragr̥hamasti ॥ 187॥
pr̥ṣṭā punarapi tēna gr̥hapurādīni kiṁsvarūpāṇi ? | yau kila candrādityau nāmamālāyāṁ mayā paṣṭhitau ॥ 188 ॥
tayōrapi kiṁ svarūpaṁ, bhaṇitaṁ tatastayā kumāra ! mayā sārdham । āgaccha yēna sarvē pratyakṣaṁ tava prakaṭayāmi ||
tatastayā mārgalagnō niḥsr̥taḥ sa purasya madhyē । yadyat paśyati tattatpr̥cchati tatastasyāḥ pārśvē ॥ 190॥
punarapi tayā nītaḥ svasthānē prabhaṇitā ca saivam । nityamapi darśayitavyamētēna kramēṇa mama sarvam || 191 ||
tataḥ pūrvaprayōgēṇa pratidivasaṁ darśayati nagaramadhyē | grahatārādi sarvaṁ tatō bhaṇitaṁ rājakulē naya ॥ 192॥
dūrasthitayā tayā tadapi hi tasya darśitam, iti kramēṇa । prāyaḥ sarvō'pi khalu tasya darśitō vastunikurambaḥ ॥
bhaṇitaṁ nāhamitastava sakāśa āgamiṣyāmi । yadi kathamapi hi tava pitā vijānīyāttataśca mama pituḥ ॥
kuryādanarthaṁ kamapi khalu tatrāpi kiṁ hiṇḍitēna bahunā | naimittikasya vacanamapi kathayitvā sā gatā tathāpi ।।
pratirjani bhramatastasya kēnāpi tridaṇḍinā sārdham । jātō'tīva snēhaḥ, adr̥śyakāriṇī vidyā ॥ 196 ॥

supāsanāha-cariasmi-
iya nicchayaṁ vihē taiē paharammi niyagihaṁ pattō । maṁtī bhōyaṇakajjē paḍhamaṁ ciya puttavāsamma || 212 ॥
pahaē tajjaṇaṇi bhōyaṇakajjēṇa tēṇa sā puṭṭhā | ammō ! kimajja kajjaṁ jaṁ laggā ēttiyā vārā 1 ॥
tīvita kahiō puttō dappaṇāivuttatō । tā jā talabhatthaṁ kaō uvāō gihāīō || 214 ||
tuha piuṇā, tō sōvi hu ittiyavēlāē āgaō gēhē । tayaṇumayā saṁpattā tō laggā ittiyā vārā ||
iya sōūṇaṁ kāuṁ ca bhōyaṇaṁ sō visajjaē jaṇaṇi । aha cauhaṭṭayamajjhē rannā vihiyammi dhavalaharē ||
vāsavadattāē tarhi ṭiyāē rayaṇīi sōvi saṁpattō । adissō gahiūṇaṁ taṁ nivakhaggaṁ, taō tīē ॥ 217॥
'kō si tumaṁ' sō puṭṭhō kahē kō ittiyāē rayaṇīē । kuvvai paragihagamaṇaṁ, tō nāō tīi sō ēsō ॥
muṭṭhō jēṇa nariṁdō, iṁdō ki ēsa ahava khayariṁdō । rūvēṇa kāmadēvō dēvō vā dāṇavō vāvi ॥ 219 ॥
aha hōu jō va sōvā pariṇēyavvō maē imō niyamā । iya ciṁtivi tassa karāō tīē gahiūṇa karavālē ॥
bhaṇiō pariṇa hi mamaṁ mahābhāga ! niyayabhāgēhiṁ । pattaṁ, tō sō jaṁvai kaha taṁ annāyakulabhavaṇaṁ ॥
maṁ pariṇasi, sā pabhaṇai savvaṁ cciya sāhiyaṁ tuha guṇēhiṁ । kiṁtu nivadappaṇāivi samapiyavvaṁ tara majjha ॥
iya bhaṇiuṁ ubvūḍhō tīē saṁkhēvaō khaṇaṁ tattha । ṭhāuṁ sagihē pattō pairayaṇi jāi tapāsē ॥223॥
savrvvapi samappara dappaṇāī. sāvi hu nivassa pēsēi । tahavi na muṁcai rōsa rāyā cunnēṇa jaṁ jaṇiyaṁ ॥
bhaṇiō sacivō rannā vāsavadattaṁ bhaṇēsu gaṁtūṇaṁ । kēṇāvi uvāēṇaṁ jēṇa samappēī taṁ majjha || 225॥
,
yaḥ kō'pi darpaṇādīnarpayati tava praṇayinyā buddhyā । tallagnaṁ sumuhūrtaḥ supraśastaṁ tad dinamēva || 211||
iti niścayaṁ vidhāya tr̥tīyē praharē nijagr̥haṁ prāptaḥ । mantrī bhōjanakāryē prathamamēva putrapārśva ॥ 212 ॥
prasthāpayati tajjananīṁ bhōjanakāryēṇa tēna sā pr̥ṣṭā । amba ! kimadya kārya yalagna ētāvān vāraḥ ॥ 213 ॥
tathāpi tasmai kathitaḥ pūrvōktō darpaṇādivr̥ttāntaḥ । tāvadyāvattallābhārthaṁ kr̥ta upāyō gr̥hādikaḥ ॥ 214॥
tava pitrā, tataḥ sō'pi khalviyadvēlāyāmāgatō gēhē । tadanumatā saṁprāptā tatō lagna ētāvān vāraḥ ॥215॥
iti śrutvā kr̥tvā ca bhōjanaṁ sa visr̥jati jananīm । atha caturhr̥ṭṭamadhyē rājñā vihitē dhavalagr̥hē ॥ 216 ॥
vāsavadattāyāṁ tatra sthitāyāṁ rajanyāṁ sō'pi saṁprāptaḥ । adr̥śyō gr̥hītvā taṁ nr̥pakhaṅgaṁ, tatastayā ॥ 217 ||
' kō'si tvaṁ' sa pr̥ṣṭaḥ kathayati ka iyatyāṁ rajanyām । karōti paragr̥hagamanaṁ, tatō jñātastayā sa ēṣaḥ ॥ 298 ॥
muṣṭō yēna narēndraḥ indraḥ kimēṣō'thavā khacarēndraḥ । rūpēṇa kāmadēvō dēvō vā dānavō vāpi ॥ 219 ॥
atha bhavatu yō vāsa vā pariṇatavyō mayāyaṁ niyamāt । iti cintayitvā tasya karāttayā gr̥hītvā karavālam ॥
bhaṇitaḥ pariṇayēdānīṁ māṁ mahābhāga ! nijabhāgyaiḥ । prāptāṁ tataḥ sa jalpati kathaṁ tvamajñātakulabhavanam ॥
māṁ pariṇayasi, sā prabhaṇati sarvamēva kathitaṁ tava guṇaiḥ । kintu nr̥padarpaṇādyapi samarpayitavyaṁ tvayā mama ॥
iti bhaṇitvādanyūḍhastayā saṁkṣēpataḥ kṣaṇaṁ tatra । sthitvā svagr̥hē prāptaḥ pratirajani yāti tatpārśvē ॥ 223 ॥
sarvamapi samarpayati darpaṇādi sāpi khalu nr̥pāya prēṣayati । tathāpi na muñcati rōṣaṁ rājā cūrṇēna yō janitaḥ ॥
bhaṇitaḥ sacivō rājñā vāsavadattāṁ bhaṇa gatvā । kēnāpyupāyēna yēna samarpayati taṁ mama ||225 ||

mōrahakahā।

jaha mārēmi sayaṁ ciya tō maccō bhaṇai nāha ! kaha maccū । tassa havijja jahā sō duhiyādaiō, nivō bhraṇa ||
javi hu ēvaṁ ci tahavi hu rōsō niyattaē nō mē । tō bhaṇiyaṁ sacivēṇaṁ harisahāṇēvi na hu rōsō ||
kāyanvō buddhimayā jēṇiha tēṇēṇa apiyaṁ mōsaṁ । pariṇīyā tuha duhiyā pāṇanmahiyā visēsēṇa ॥ 228॥
ajjavi sō tuha uciō bahupasāyarasa, tā pasīūṇa | āṇāvijjau saṁpai pahu ! niyapāyāṇa pāsammi ||
iccāisujuttīhi nivassa uttāriūṇa taṁ rōsa । vāsavadattā ēvaṁ bhaṇāviyā niyapaī ittha || 230॥
āsu majjha samīvē jēṇa pasāyaṁ karēmi sē garuyaṁ । tīivi kahiyē paiṇō nivavayaṇa, sōvi paḍibhaṇa{} ||
paṁcavarimāṇamuvariṁ kāyavvaṁ dēvadaṁsaṇaṁ suyaṇu ! | tīivi bhūvaiṇō puṇa kahāviyaṁ tassa paḍivayaṇaṁ ॥ 232॥
iya kālē baccatē jāō puttō nivassa taṇayāē । tō sō adistamāṇō lōēṇaṁ ēi jaha tahavi || 233॥
khillāvivi niyataṇayaṁ jāi siṁhaṁ tāva jāva paṇa varisā । jāyā suyassa pacchā bhaṇiyā sā gaccha piupāsē ॥
ahamavi paḍō hōhimhi sattadiṇaṁtē na itya saṁdēhō । tīi taicciya vihiyaṁ niyaputtō daṁsiō rannō ।।
tēvitaṁ daṇaṁ ruvāiguṇōvalakkhaṇōvēyaṁ । niyaaṁkē kāūṇaṁ puṇō puṇō biu bhaṇiō || 236।।
tai diṭṭhē diḍōccaya tujha piyā tahavi maha maṇō vaccha ! । tadaṁsaṇaṁpi vaṁcha chaṇasasirvivaṁ cakōruvva ||
iya paidipi payaō saṁbhāsailaṁkarēi cuṁbē । niyaakasaṁṭhiyaṁ sō gharēi gurutēhanivbharaō || 238 ॥
aha gaccha sugapāsē samuhuttē bhajjasaṁgaō maṁtī | paḍipullē vīsaimē varisē, taṇaraṇa taṁ sahasā ॥ 239 ॥
• daṭṭhūṇaṁ niyajaṇaṇī puṭṭhā kō ēsa, tīi sē kahiyaṁ । tujjha piyā, tā ēyaṁ paṇamasu tēṇāvi taha vihiyaṁ ॥
yathā mārayāmi svayamēva tatō'mātyō bhaṇati nātha ! kathaṁ mr̥tyuḥ । tasya bhavēdyathā sa duhitr̥dayitaḥ, nr̥pō bhaṇati ||
yadyapi khalvēvaṁ tiṣṭhati tathāpi hi rōṣō nivartatē nō mē । tatō bhaṇitaṁ sacivēna harṣasthānē'pi na hi rōṣaḥ ॥
kartavyō buddhimatā yēnēha stēnēnārpitō mōṣaḥ । pariṇītā tava duhitā prāṇābhyadhikā viśēṣēṇa ॥ 228 ॥
adyāpi sa tavōcitō bahuprasādasya, tasmātprasadya । ānāyyatāṁ saṁprati prabhō ! nijapādayōḥ pārśvē ॥ 229॥
ityāddisuyuktibhirnr̥pasyōttārya taṁ rōṣam । vāsavadattaivaṁ bhāṇitā nijapatimatra ॥ 230॥
ānaya mama samīpē yēna prasādaṁ karōmi tasya gurum । tayāpi kathitē patyurnr̥pavacanaṁ, sō'pi pratibhaṇati ॥
pañcavarṣāṇāmupari kartavyaṁ dēvadarśanaṁ sutanu ! | tayāpi bhūpatēḥ punaḥ kathitaṁ tasya prativacanam ॥232॥
iti kālē vrajati jātaḥ putrō nr̥pasya tanayāyāḥ । tataḥ sō'dr̥śyamānō lōkēnaiti yathā tathāpi ॥ 233॥
ramayitvā nijatanayaṁ yāti gr̥haṁ tāvadyāvat pañca varṣāṇi । jātāni sutasya paścādbhaṇitā mā gaccha pitr̥pārśvē ॥
ahamapi prakaṭō bhaviṣyāmi saptadināntē nātra saṁdēhaḥ । tayā tathaiva vihitaṁ nijaputrō darśitō rājñē ॥ 235 ॥
tēnāpi taṁ dr̥ṣṭvā rūpādiguṇauvalakṣaṇōpētam । nijāṅkē kr̥tvā punaḥ punaścumbitvā bhaṇitaḥ ॥236॥
tvayi dr̥ṣṭē dr̥ṣṭa ēva tava pitā tathāpi mama manō vatsa ! । taddarśanamapi vāñchati kṣaṇaśaśibimbaṁ cakōra iva ॥
iti pratidinamapi prayataḥ saṁbhāṣatē'laṁkarōti cumbatē । nijāṅkasaṁsthitaṁ sa dharati gurusnēha nirbharataḥ || 238।।
atha gacchati sutapārśvē sumuhūrta bhāryāsaṁgatō mantrī । paripūrṇē viṁśē varṣē tanayēna taṁ sahasā ||239 ||

supāsanāha cariammi-
|
sacivēṇa samāligi kayi savvaṁ puvyanihiṁ । nēmittipassa vayaṇaṁ tattō gharauvari sō nīō |
majjaṇavāī kārāviūṇa sacivēṇa appaṇā saddhiṁ । sō nīō nivāsē taṁ namiu dōvi uviṭṭhā ||242||
tō puḍhō naravaṇā maṁtī, sō bhagai ēsa maha puttō । tō bhaṇai nivō na kayāvi nisuniō tujjha suyajammō ||
tō maṁtī kaes nivasa savaṇamūlammi nihuyasaṇa | nēmittiyassa bhaṇiyaṁ taha ya uvāyaṁ ca jahavihiyaṁ ॥
jāvēvaṁ sō sāhai tātra ya sō bālahāranarasahiō । maṁtisuyassavi puttō jaṇayaṁ daduṇa nēhēṇa || 245 ||
tāō tāuti payaṁpirō ya āliṁgiūṇa niru gāḍhaṁ । tassaṁkammi niviṭṭō diṭṭhō sanivēṇa lōēṇa || 246 ||
tō takkhaṇa khuddhō maṁtī jā kiṁci pihī tattha । tā bhūvaraṇā bhaṇiō kiṁ taṁ sō vīravarapurisō ? |
ēvaṁti tēṇa bhaṇiē āhūō naravarēṇa niyapāsē । āliṁgiūṇa saṁbhāsiuṁ ca uvavēsiō savihē || 248 ॥
tō paṁcagapasāyaṁ dāūṇaṁ taha ya turayakarikōsaṁ । ukkōsaṁ gurudēsaṁ āvāsa sayalariuvā || 249||
aha annayā ya puṭṭhō rannā maṁtissa naṁdaṇō ēvaṁ । ki bhō ! kuluggaēṇavi aṇajjakajjaṁ kayaṁ tumaē ? |
nēbhittiyassa vayaṇaṁ kahiyē savrvvapi tēṇa jaha nilayaṁ । jaṇayāō, tō rāyā bhagai saccō sa naimittī ॥
tēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ narēsara ! saccāī majjha ēttha kammāī । kammavasagēṇa jamhā dēva ! maēṇuḍiyē ēyaṁ ॥252॥
sumasu nakkhattarāsīdivasāī kammasaṁjaṇiyaṁ । jāēi jammamamaē samaēvi jaō imaṁ bhaṇiyaṁ ॥ 253 ॥
sabyō puṇyakāṇaṁ kammāṇaṁ pāvaē phalanivāyuṁ । gahanakkhattāī puṇō nimittamittaṁ ci havaṁti || 254 ||
dr̥ṣṭrā nijajananī pr̥ṣṭā ka ēṣaḥ, tathā tasya kathitam । tava pitā, tasmādētaṁ praṇama tēnāpi tathā vihitam ॥
sacivēna samāliṅgaya kathitaṁ sarvamapi pūrvanirdiṣṭam । naimittikasya vacanaṁ tatō gr̥hōpari sa nītaḥ ॥249॥
majjanādi kārayitvā sacivanātmanā sārdham । sa nītō nr̥papārśvē taṁ natvā dvāvapyupaviṣṭau ॥242॥
tataḥ pr̥ṣṭō narapatinā mantrī, sa bhaṇatyēṣa mama putraḥ । tatō bhaṇati nr̥pō na kadāpi śrutaṁ tava sutajanma || 243 ॥
tatō mantrī kathayati nr̥pasya śravaṇamūlē nibhr̥taśabdēna । naimittikasya bhaṇitaṁ tathā cōpāyaṁ ca yathāvihitam ॥
yāvadēvaṁ sa kathayati tāvacca sa bālaghāranarasahitaḥ । mantrisutasyāpi putrō janakaṁ dr̥ṣṭrā snēhēna || 245॥
tātastāta iti prajalpitā cāliṅgya niścitaṁ gāḍham । tasyāṅkē niviṣṭō dr̥ṣṭaḥ sanr̥pēṇa lōkēna || 246॥
tatastatkṣaṇē na kṣubdhō mantrī yāvatkiñcidapi jalpiṣyati tatra । tāvad bhūpatinā bhaṇitaḥ kiṁ tvaṁ sa vīravarapuruṣaḥ ? |
ēvamiti tēna bhaṇita āhūtō naravarēṇa nijapārśvē । āliṅgya saṁbhāṣya cōpavēśitaḥ savidhē ॥ 248 ॥
tataḥ pañcāṅgaprasādaṁ daravā tathā ca turagakarikōśam । utkr̥ṣṭaṁ gurudēśamāvāsaṁ sakalavāsam ॥ 249 ॥
athānyadā ca pr̥ṣṭō rājñā mantriṇō nandana ēvam । kiṁ bhōḥ ! kulōdgatēnāpyanāryakāryaṁ kr̥taṁ tvayā ? || 250 |
naimittikasya vacanaṁ kathitaṁ sarvamapi tēna yathā śrutam । janakāt, tatō rājā bhaṇati satyaḥ sa naimittikaḥ ॥
tēna bhaṇitaṁ narēśvara ! satyāni mamātra karmāṇi । karmavaśugēna yasmād dēva ! mayānuṣṭhitamētat ॥222॥
śubhamaśubhaṁ nakṣatrarāśidivasādi karmasaṁjanitam । jāyatē janmasamayē samayē'pi yata idaṁ bhaṇitam || 253 ||
sarvaḥ pūrvakr̥tānāṁ karmaṇāṁ prāpnōti phalavipākam । grahanakṣatrādayaḥ punarnimittamātramēva bhavanti ॥ 294॥

kiñca ।
maṇōrahakahā |
459
davvaṁ khittaṁ kālaṁ bhāvaṁ ca bhavēi kāraṇaṁ garuaṁ । asuhasuhakammabhavaṇē visēsaō sōvakamakammē || 255 ॥
iccāinisuṇiūṇaṁ sacivasuyāō nivō bhavuvviggō। taṁ ciya rajjē ṭhaviḍaṁ gihivi dikkhaṁ gaō mōkkhaṁ ॥
iya kahium̐ sō siṭṭī sivabhō bhāi naravaī ! ēvaṁ । duvihāē āvaīē tō jattō hōi kāyayō ॥ 257 ॥
tēṇa jaha maṁtiṇā niyamuyassa vihiō tahavihōvāō । taha vayamavi taṁ kuṇimō tujjhāṇāē niyamuyassa ॥
tō rannāṇunnāē dhariō sō niyagihammi jattēṇa । sēsā caurō taṇayā rāyā sē samāiṭṭā || 259॥
tō rannā tē savvē nirōviyā caudisāsu balakaliyā । jahajōggaṁ sattaṇaṁ pasāhaṇatthaṁ ca ittō ya॥ 260॥
malayācalamma caliō paḍhamō cauraṁgiṇīi sēṇāē । pattō kamēṇa āvāsiō ya duggassa talavaṭṭhē ॥ 261 ॥
tō mahiṁdasī varuṇasiṇēhēṇa taraliyavivēō । kahakahavi hu nīhariō gihāu, pattō ya tappāsē ॥
tatthēva tēṇa dhariō mahayā jattēṇa, siṭṭiṇō lēhō । paṭṭhaviḍaṁ jāṇāvā baṁdhusarūvaṁpi, ittō ya ॥ 263 ॥
āgaṁtūrṇa ikkēṇa thavirasavarēṇa tattha sō sahasā । bhaṇiō maha pasiūṇaṁ varuṇa ! payacchēsu ēgaṁtaṁ ॥ 264 ॥
tēvi tahatti vihiyaṁ kahiyaṁ tēṇāvi jaha guhāmajjhē । ciṭṭhai garuyasuraṁgā uḍḍhagamā māṇusapavēsā || 265॥
tā jāva duggamajjhaṁ tampi ya dhavalaharamajjhasijjāē । duggā hivaī ciṭṭhā, tappāsē nēmi jai majjha || 266॥
appēsi imaṁ duggaṁ, sōvi hu mannēvi tassa taṁ vayaṇaṁ । tēṇa samaṁ ciya caliō mōtuṁ lahu bhāyaraṁ sivirē ॥
saṁpattō dhavalaharē tassa ya majjhammi savararāōvi । bhajjāē saha suttō paryaṁsiō thērapurisēṇa ॥ 268 ॥
dravyaṁ kṣētra kālō bhāvaśca bhavati kāraṇaṁ guru । aśubhaśubhakarmabhavanē viśēṣataḥ sōpakramakarmaṇi ॥255॥
ityādi śrutvā sacivasutād nr̥pō bhavōdvignaḥ । tamēva rājyē sthāpayitvā gr̥hītvā dīkṣāṁ gatō mōkṣam ॥ 256 ॥
iti kathayitvā sa śrēṣṭhī śivabhadrō bhaṇati narapatē ! ēvam । dvividhāyāmāpadi tatō yatnō bhavati kartavyaḥ ||
tēna yathā mantriṇā nijasutasya vihitastathāvidhōpāyaḥ । tathā vayamapi taṁ kurmastavājñayā nijasutasya ॥ 298॥
talō rājñānujñātē dhr̥taḥ sa nijagr̥hē yatnēna । śēṣāścatvārastanayā rājādēśē samādiṣṭāḥ ॥ 259 ॥
tatō rājñā tē sarvē nirūpitāścaturdikṣu valakalitāḥ । yathāyōgyaṁ śatrūṇāṁ prasādhanārthaṁ ca itaśca ॥ 260॥
malayācalē calitaḥ prathamaścaturaṅgiṇyā sēnayā । prāptaḥ kramēṇāvāsitaśca durgasya talapr̥ṣṭhē ॥ 262 ॥
tō mahēndrasiṁha varuṇasnēhēna taralitavivēkaḥ । kathaṁkathamapi khalu niḥsr̥tō gr̥hāt prāptaśca tatpārśvē ॥262॥
tatraiva tēna dhr̥tō mahatā yatnēna śrēṣṭhinē lēkham । prasthāpya jñāpayati bandhusvarūpamapi, itaśca ॥ 263 ॥
āgatyaikēna sthaviraśabarēṇa tatra sa sahasā । bhaṇitō mama prasadya varuṇa ! prayacchēkāntam ॥ 264॥
tēnāpi tathēti vihitaṁ kathitaṁ tēnāpi yathā guhāmadhyē । tiṣṭhati gurusuruṅgōrdhvagamā mānuṣapravēśyā || 265 ||
tāvad yāvad durgamadhyaṁ tasmiṁśca dhavalagr̥ha madhyaśayyāyām । durgādhipatistiṣṭhati, tatpārśvē nayāmi yadi mama ||
arpayasīmaṁ durgē, sō'pi hi matvā tasya tad vacanam । tēna samamēva calitō muktvā laghubhrātaraṁ śibirē ॥
saṁprāptō dhavalagr̥hē tasya ca madhyē śabararājō'pi । bhāryayā saha suptaḥ pradarśitaḥ sthavirapuruṣēṇa ॥ 268 ॥
