supāsanāha cariasmi --
1
tō varuṇaniuttēhiṁ purisēhi baṁdhiūṇa sakalattō । niyaḍēhiṁ nigaḍiūṇaṁ samappiō daṁḍanāhasta || 269 ॥
tēviniyahupāsamma pēriō talavarassa appēḍaṁ । dāūṇaṁ saṁbalayaṁ taha sattaṁgapi tallacchi || 270 ।।
naravaivāyaṇatthaṁ, samapiḍaṁ taha jiṇidapa ḍimāō । phāliharayaṇamayāō piuṇōvi hu pūyaṇanimittaṁ ॥
thērasuyaṁ tanmaṇiṇa ṭhāva dugganāyagapayammi । varuṇō duggammi tahā niyapahuāṇaṁ ca dāvēī || 272 ||
tō mahiṁdasīhassa sāhiyaṁ duggagirisamīvammi | kēṇavi savaranarēṇaṁ vivaraṁ tēha kappamappēum̐ || 273 ||
tō parivāraṁ citrikarē karēūṇa kappaṭippaṇayaṁ । tambhaṇiyavihāṇēṇaṁ pavisaratō vivaramajjhammi|| 274 ||
tā jāva vaṁtarīē bhavaṇaṁ pāsēi tīēlaṁkariyē । paḍhamaguṇaṭhāṇaṭhiyāē tīē sō pabhaṇiō darda || 275 |
uvavisasu ramasu maṁ nāha! jēṇa vaṁtarapaṇaṁgaṇā ahahyaṁ । sō bhaṇai duvihativihaṁ dēvīṇa rayammi maha niyamō ॥
tō kuddhā sā paṇabhai kimihāgamaṇammi kāraṇaṁ kahasu । jai na samaṁ uvabhuṁjasi, bhaṇai sō kōugēṇēva || 277॥
pattō tātaṁ daṁsasu kiṁcivi maha kōuyaṁti, sā bhagai । maha ramaṇāu kimannaṁ jaṁ taṁ patthēsi rē mūḍha ! 1 ॥ 278 ॥ ॥
jai na mamaṁ ramasi tumaṁ saṁpayamavitā marēsi rē nūṇaṁ । sō bhagai havau saraṇaṁpi niyamanirayassa pasayacchi ! ॥
paraṁ maha sāhasa samabhūmibhāgaō kicciraṁ tuhāvāsō। tīē bhaṇiyaṁ bahujōyaṇāī, tō bhaṇai sō ēvaṁ ॥ 280 ॥
jai ēvaṁ tā majjhaṁ ahōdisaṁ jōyaṇammi gaṁtavvē । ahiyagamaṣēṇa jāō disivvaē duiaiyārō || 281॥
iya sōuṁ sā kuviyā pahipahārēṇa haṇihihī jāva । tā aṁtarammi paḍiō sammaṭṭhī surō kavi || 282 ॥
tatō varuṇaniyuktaiḥ puruṣairbaddhvā sakalatraḥ । nigaḍērnigaḍayitvā samarpitō daṇḍanāthāya || 269॥
tēnāpi nijaprabhupārśvē prēṣitaḥ purarakṣāyāpayitvā । dattvā śambalaṁ tathā saptāṅgāmapi tallakṣmīm ॥270॥
narapatyupāyanārthaṁ, samarpya tathā jinēndrapratimāḥ । sphaṭikaratnamayīḥ piturapi hi pūjananimittam ॥271॥
sthavirasutaṁ tadbhaṇitēna sthāpayati durganāyakapadē । varuṇō durgē tathā nijaprabhvājñāṁ ca dāpayati ॥ 272 ॥
itō mahēndrasiṁhasya kathitaṁ durgagirisamīpē । kēnāpi śabaranarēṇa vivaraṁ tathā kalpamarpayitvā ||273 ||
tataḥ parivāraṁ vañcayitvā karē kr̥tvā kalpaṭippanakam । tadbhaṇitavidhānēna praviśati tatō vivaramadhyē ||274 ||
tāvad yāvad vyantaryā bhavanaṁ paśyati tayā'laṁkr̥tam । prathamaguṇasthānasthitayā tayā sa prabhaṇitō dr̥ṣṭā || 275 ॥
upaviśa ramaya māṁ nātha ! yēna vyantarapaṇāṅganā'ham । sa bhaṇati dvividhatrividhaṁ dēvīnāṁ ratē mama niyamaḥ ॥ 276 ॥
tataḥ kruddhā sā prabhaṇati kimihāgamanē kāraṇaṁ kathaya । yadi na māmupabhuṅgē, bhaṇati sa kautukēnaiva ॥ 277॥
prāptastasmāt tvaṁ darśaya kiñcidapi mama kautukamiti, sā bhaṇati । mama ramaṇātkimanyadyattvaṁ prārthayasē rē mūḍha ! ||
yadi na māṁ ramayasi tvaṁ sāṁpratamapi tadā mriyasē rē nūnam । sa bhaṇati bhavatu maraṇamapi niyamaniratasya mr̥gākṣi ! |
paraṁ mama kathaya samabhūmibhāgāt kiyaddūraṁ tavāvāsaḥ । tathā bhaṇitaṁ bahuyōjanāni, tatō bhaṇati sa ēvam ।
yadyēvaṁ tadā mamādhōdiśi yōjanē gantavyē । adhikagamanēna jātō digvatē dvitīyāticāraḥ || 281 ॥
iti śrutvā sā kupitā pāṇiprahārēṇa hārniṣyati yāvat । tāvadantarē patitaḥ samyagdr̥ṣṭiḥ suraḥ kō'pi ॥
1, taṁ ।

tēkkhavirḍa sō jhatti āṇiō varuṇasiviramajjhami । dicvē ktthē dāum̐ sa gaō sadvāṇamaha varuṇō ॥ 283 ॥
kayauvaōgō jā uḍḍhadisivaē jōyaṇaṁ taō sarai । iya jōyaṇadugamāṇaṁ gamaṇaṁ nāūṇa jhūrēi ॥ 284 ॥
savvaviraī dharēu maha sattī dūraō gayā inhiṁ । ēgamugabharuvvahaṇē asamatthō kiṁ giriṁ vaha ? || 285||
kaha tē na baṁdaṇijjā kaha tē pūyārihā na hu havaṁti । muṇiṇō mahāṇubhāvā jāvajjīvaṁpi jē payayā ॥ 286 ॥
pāliti savyavira maṇavaikāraṇa tivihativihammi । hī hī ahamēṇa maē virāhiyā dēsaviraīvi ॥ 287॥
ēvamaṇusōiūṇaṁ varuṇō ōyarai dugganayarāō । saṁpattō āvāsē mahiṁdasīhassa tō kahai || 288 ॥
savvaṁ aiyārāī sōvi hu sāhēi appaṇō cariyē । aiyāramahōdisi saṁbhavaṁ ca tō tēṇa saṁjuttō ॥ 289 ॥
tāṇāō nayariṁ varuṇō pattō nasiō rāyā । kahiyaṁ savvaṁpi taō jahaṭṭhiyaṁ duggagahaṇāī || 290 ॥
niyaniyamasvavi bhaṁgō pasāhiō, naravarēṇa sō bhaṇiō । na hu tattha tujjha dōsō majjha niōgēṇa yēvōvi ॥
ittōpuvvadisā siḍiō āsi pēsiō putriṁ । jō guṇacaṁdabhihāṇō sō pattō dēśasaṁdhī ॥ 292 ॥
tō samaraḍāmarēṇaṁ puvvadisābhūsaṇēṇa bhūvaiṇā । guṇacaṁdassābhimuhaṁ bhaṇāviyaṁ niyayayāō || 293 ||
jaha majjha samajhē mā pavisasu jā na saṁmūhō ahayaṁ । saṁpattō vaṇiputtaya ! iha atthē asthi tuha āṇā ॥
dēvagurūṇaṁ niyasāmiṇō ya tā jāva paṁcamaṁ divasa tasmi puṇō haṁ sayamavi sīmāē samāgamissāmi ||
tattō guṇacaṁ dēṇaṁ bhaṇiya bhō dūya ! paṁcadiṇamajjhē । jai sīmamahaṁ laṁbēmi tā phuḍaṁ ēsa maha satrahō || 296 ||
jai puṇa kahiyadiṇāṇaṁ samahiyadivasaṁpi sō vilaṁbēhī । tā turiyaṁ gaṁtūṇaṁ uvavidvaṁ ciya gahissāmi ॥
tēnōtkṣipya sa jhaṭityānītō varuṇaśibiramadhyē | divyāni vastrāṇi dattvā sa gataḥ svasthānamatha varuṇaḥ ॥
kr̥tōpayōgō yāvadūrdhvadigvatē yōjanaṁ tataḥ smarati । iti yōjanādvikamānaṁ gamanaṁ jñātvā khidyatē ॥ 284 ॥
sarvaviratiṁ dhartu mama śaktirduratō gatēdānīm । ēkamuddramarōdvahanē'samarthaḥ kiṁ giriṁ vahati ? ॥ 285 ॥
kathaṁ tē na vandanīyāḥ kathaṁ tē pūjārhā na khalu bhavanti । munayō mahānubhāvā yāvajjīvamapi yē prayatāḥ ॥
pālayanti sarvaviratiṁ manōvacaḥ kāyēna trividhatrividhēna । hī hī ! adhamēna mayā virādhitā dēśaviratirapi ॥
ēvamanuśōcya varuṇō'vatarati durganagarāt । saṁprāpta āvāsē mahēndrasiṁhasya tataḥ kathayati ||288 ||
sarvamaticārādi sō'pi khalu kathayatyātmanaścaritam । aticāramadhōdiksaṁbhavaṁ ca tatastēna saṁyuktaḥ ॥ 289 ॥
tatsthānād nagarīṁ varuṇaḥ prāptō namasthitō rājā । kathitaṁ sarvamapi tatō yathāsthitaṁ durgagrahaṇādi ॥ 290 ॥
nijaniyamasyāpi bhaṅgaḥ prakathitō, naravarēṇa sa bhaṇitaḥ । na khalu tatra tava dōṣō mama niyōgēna stōkō'pi ॥
itaḥ pūrvadiśi śrēṣṭhasuta āsītprēṣitaḥ pūrvam । yō guṇacandrābhidhānaḥ sa prāptō dēśasaṁdhau ||292॥
tataḥ samaraḍāmarēṇa pūrvadigbhūṣaṇēna bhūpatinā । guṇacandrasyābhimukhaṁ bhāṇitaṁ nijadūtēna ॥293॥
,
yathā mama dēśamadhyē mā praviśa yāvad na saṁmukhō'ham । saṁprāptō vaṇikputraka ! ihārthē'sti tavājñā ॥ 294 ॥
dēvagurūṇāṁ nijasvāminaśca tāvadyāvatpañcamaṁ divasam । tasminpunarahaṁ svayamapi sīmni samāgamiṣyāmi ॥ 295 ॥
tatō guṇacandrēṇa bhaṇitaṁ bhō dūta ! pañcadinamadhyē । yadi samānamahaṁ laya yadā sphuṭamēṣa mama śapathaḥ ॥ 296 ॥

i bhaṇiṇaṁ dūō visajjiō sō gaō niyapurampi | sāhēi nivarasa tahā jaha bhaṇiyaṁ daṁḍanāhēṇa ||
tēvi puṭṭhō dūō kittipittā vaṇissa valasaṁkhā ? । tō tēṇavi sē kahiyaṁ tuha sinnāō phuḍaṁ duguṇā ||
kiṁca |
sapērakkamō ya kamasaṁgaō ya gurugabaghaḍāē ghaḍiō ya । sō guṇacaṁdō naravara ! tamhā taṁ rakkha appāṇaṁ ।।
niya saccāēṇaṁ daṁḍapayāṇēṇa vāvi chuṭṭēsi । annaha na havasi niva ! natthi saṁsaō iya suṇēuṁ sō ॥
bhīō saṁvahiūṇaṁ vahiūṇa ahanisaṁ gaō dūraṁ । taṁ paṇihīō nāuṁ guṇacaṁdō piṭṭhimaṇulaggō ॥ 302 ॥
।
puraō gaccha yā piṭṭhīē tassa jāi guṇacaṁdō। tō jāva jōyaṇasayaṁ ahiyaṁ tō disivayaṁ sariyē ।।
mui dasa jōyaṇāī ahiyāī samāgaō taō bhaṇai | saccaṁ jāō disivayakalaṁka daṁḍāhivō inhi ||
jaṁ maha ubbhāsēṇavi bhaggō ētti harisiō ahayaṁ । niyaniyamabhaṁgadaṁḍēṇa daṁḍiō ii na mē nāyaṁ ||
ratna niyamabhaṁgō jaṇēi aidāruṇaṁ mahādukkhaṁ । jaha visalavōvi mārai uvabhuttō pāṇiṇaṁ niyama ||
tā na khamaṁ maha gaṁtuṁ payapi ittō, taṁō ya tannayarē । muttūrṇa ahigāriṁ valiō sō niyapurāhutaṁ ॥
pattō ya vibhūīē guṇacaṁdō paṇamiyā naridāī । savrvvapi jahāvittaṁ nivēiyaṁ rāiṇō tēṇa ॥ 308 ॥
taiō suṁdaranāmā buddhīē baṁdhurōtti paṭṭaviō । uttaradisāē sirisamaravīrapāsammi sō jamhā ॥ 309 ॥
caiḍō na daṁḍasajjhō udaṁḍapathaṁḍa pabalabaḷakaliō । āīnīīgajjhō na jujjhasajjhō imō hōi ॥ 310 ॥
yadi punaḥ kathitadinēbhyaḥ samadhikadivasamapi sa vilambayiṣyati । tadā tvaritaṁ gatvōpaviṣṭamēva grahīṣyāmi ॥
iti bhaṇitvā dūtō visarjitaḥ sa gatō nijapurē । kathayati nr̥pāya tathā yathā bhaṇitaṁ daṇḍanāthēna ||298 ॥
tēnāpi pr̥ṣṭō dūtaḥ kiyanmātrā vaṇijō balasaṁkhyā ? । tatastēnāpi tasya kathitaṁ tava sainyātsphuṭaṁ dviguṇā ॥
saparākramaśca kramasaṁgataśca gurugajaghaṭayā ghaṭitaśca । sa guṇacandrō naravara ! tasmāttvaṁ rakṣātmānam ॥ 300॥
nijadēśatyāgēna daṇḍapradānēna vāpi chuṭyasē । anyathā na bhavasi nr̥pa ! nāsti saṁśaya iti śrutvā saḥ ॥
bhītaḥ samūdrā ūḍhā'harniśaṁ gatō dūram । tat praṇidharjñātvā guṇacandraḥ pr̥ṣṭhamanulagnaḥ ॥ 302 ॥
puratō gacchati rājā pr̥ṣṭhē tasya yāti guṇacandraḥ । tatō yāvadyēōjanaśatamadhikaṁ tatō digvataṁ smr̥tam ॥ 303 ॥
jānāti daśa yōjanānyadhikāni samāgatastatō bhaṇati । satyaṁ jātō digvatakalaṅkadaṇḍādhipa idānīm ॥
yanmamōdbhāsēnāpi bhagna ēṣa iti haṣitō'ham । nijaniyamabhaṅgadaṇḍēna daṇḍita iti na mayā jñātam ॥ 205 ॥
stōkō'pi niyamabhaṅgō janayatyatidāruṇaṁ mahāduḥkham । yathā viṣalavō'pi mārayatyupabhuktaḥ prāṇinaṁ niyamāt ॥
tasmānna kṣamaṁ mama gantuṁ padamapītaḥ, tataśca tannagarē | muktvādhikāriṇaṁ valitaḥ sa nijapurābhimukham ॥307॥
prāptaśca vibhūtyā guṇacandraḥ praṇatā narēndrādayaḥ । sarvamapi yathāvr̥ttaṁ nivēditaṁ rājñē tēna ॥ 308 ॥
tr̥tīyaḥ sundaranāmā buddhayā bandhura iti prasthāpitaḥ । uttaradiśi śrīsamaravīrapārśvē sa yasmāt ॥ 309 ॥
caṇḍō na daṇḍasādhya uddaṇḍapracaṇḍaprabalabalakalitaḥ । ādinītigrāhyō na yuddhasādhyō'yaṁ bhavati ॥ 310॥
.1 gaṁ. parikka' ।

aṇavarayapayāṇēhiṁ cauraṁgabalēṇa parigaō sōvi । jāva niya dēsasīmaṁ saṁpattō tāva ciṁtēi ॥ 311॥
ahaha maha jōyaṇasayaṁ ēkkaṁ ciya mukkalaṁ caudisaṁpi । taṁ tu sasīmāēvi hu saṁjāyaṁ tā kaha karimō ? ॥
ēgattō niyaniyamō annattō guruyaṇassa maha āṇā । jāō ya vagghadōttaḍināō iya ciṁtayaṁtassa ॥ 313॥
tassa maṇē viṣphuriyaṁ jaha tinha disāṇa majjhaō gahium̐ । dasa dasa ya jōyaṇāī khivēmi iha virairakkhaṭṭhā ।।
tīsahiyajōyaṇasayā puraō sirisamaravīranayaraṁpi । vijjai iya nicchauṁ caliō pattō ya tannayarē ||
bahupāhuḍaṁ bihēuṁ naranāhaṁ paṇamiūṇa tō bhaṇiyaṁ । vikkamavalēṇa ratnā paṭṭaviō haṁ tuha samīvē || 316 ||
kajjēṇamimēṇa nivēsa ! saṁpayaṁ tumha dēsasīmāē । jē saṁti amha gāmā haṇaṁti tē tujjha ṭhakkurayā || 317 !
tā kimuvakkhasi rakkha na khamaṁ tuha puṇtrapurisamajjāyaṁ । lōvēḍaṁ narapuṁgava ! samaggaguṇagāmaparidhāma ! |
annaṁ ca vikkamavalō tara samaṁ nēhanibharō bāḍhaṁ । tēṇa tuha duṭṭhaṭhakkura ciṭṭhiyamēyaṁ kahāvē || 319 ||
annaha nariṁda ! tāṇaṁ gaṇaṇāvi hu natthi majjha sāmissa । jassa agē riuṇō āṇaṁ sirasā paḍicchati ॥
taṁ niṇivi naranāhō jaṁpai ēvaṁ maē na vinnāyaṁ । annaha niyamittassavi gāmē kimuvaddavāvēmi 1 ॥321॥
tā ēsōcci daṁḍa tāṇaṁ hōuci duṭṭhacariyāṇa । sīmālaḍhakkurāṇaṁ jō dēsō sō maē dina || 322 ||
tumhāṇa, khamaha inhiṁ giṇhaha tadēsapattaliṁ jhati । annapi bhaṇaha jaṁ kiṁpi saṁpayaṁ samuciyaṁ amha || 323 ॥
iya bhaṇiūṇaṁ taha naravarassa niyapāhuḍaṁ samappēḍaṁ । sammāṇiuṁ ca bahuyaṁ visajjiō suṁdarī vaṇiō ||
saṁpattō ya kamēṇa niyanivapāsē samaggamavi vittaṁ । sāhēuṁ namiūṇa ya jaṇayāga hē jāi, tattō ya ॥ 325 ॥

anavarataprayāṇaiścaturaṅgabalēna parigataḥ sō'piṁ । yāvannijadēśasīmānaṁ saṁprāptastāvaccintayati ॥319॥
ahaha mama yōjanaśatamēkamēva mutkalaṁ caturdikṣvapi । tattu svasīmnyapi hi saṁjātaṁ tasmātkathaṁ kurmaḥ 1 ॥ 312 ॥
ēkatō nijaniyamō'nyatō gurujanasya mamājñā । jātaśca vyāghradvitaṭīnyāya iti cintayataḥ ॥313॥
tasya manasi visphuritaṁ yathā tisr̥ṇāṁ diśāṁ madhyatō gr̥hītvā । daśa daśa ca yōjanāni kṣipāmīha viratirakṣārtham ॥
triṁśadadhikayōjanaśatātpurataḥ śrīsamaravīranagaramapi । vidyata iti niścitya calitaḥ prāptaśca tannagarē ॥315॥
bahuprābhr̥taṁ vidhāya naranāthaṁ praṇamya tatō bhaṇitam । vikramabalēna rājñā prasthāpitō'haṁ tava samīpē || 316॥
kāryēṇānēna nr̥pēśa ! sāṁprataṁ tava dēśasīni । yē santyasmaddyāmā ghnanti tāṁstava ṭhakkurāḥ ||317॥
tasmātkimupēkṣasē rakṣa na kṣamaṁ tava pūrvapuruṣamaryādām । lōpayituṁ narapuṅgava ! samagraguṇagrāmaparidhāman ! ॥ 318॥
anyacca vikramabalastvayā samaṁ snēhanirbharō bāḍham । tēna tava duṣṭaṭhakkuracēṣṭitamētatkathayati ॥319॥
anyathā narēndra ! tēṣāṁ gaṇanāpi hi nāsti mama svāminaḥ । yasyānēkē ripava ājñāṁ śirasā pratīcchanti ||
tat śrutvā naranāthō jalpatyēvaṁ mayā na vijñātam । anyathā nijamittrasyāpi grāmānkimupadrāvayāmi ? ॥321॥
tasmādēṣa ēva daṇḍastēṣāṁ bhavatviti duṣṭacaritānām । samisthaṭhakkurāṇāṁ yō dēśaḥ sa mayā dattaḥ || 322॥
yuṣmabhyam, kṣamayatēdānīṁ gr̥hīta taddēśaprāptiṁ jhaṭiti । anyadapi bhaṇata yatkimapi sāṁprataṁ samucitaṁ mama ॥
iti bhaṇitvā tathā naravarāya nijaprābhr̥taṁ samayē । sammānya ca bahu visarjitaḥ sundarō vaṇik || 324 ॥

supāsanāha-variagmi-
jasacaṁdō jō turiō turiyaṁ sō pēsiō ya rāēṇa | siṁdhuvisayāhivaiṇō uvariṁ cauraṁgavalakaliō ||
pattō ya tamuddē tattō ciṁtēi disivayaṁ taiyā । kiṁrimāṇaṁ gahiyaṁ nē sumariyō sugurumūlammi || 327||
māō jāō nariṁdalacchīē ava ummāō । jaṁ suṁgurūṇutra ēsō pahuṭṭhō ahaha mujhē hai || 328 ||
iti tatta vittō hēriēhiṁ jaha rāyā । saṁpai palāiumaṇō saṁvahamāṇō ya ciṭṭhē || 329||
tō sigyaṁ ciya tubbhē jaṛa dēha payāṇagaṁ taō tassa । sataṁgaṁṣi hu lacchiṁ giṇhaha acirēṇa cirabhuttaṁ ॥
tō takkhaṇēṇa ḍhakkā davāviyā syaṇipaḍhamapaharapi । caliō sāravalēṇaṁ gaō ya vahiūṇa bahudēsaṁ ॥
tēvi āgacchaṁtō vinnāō tō palāṇiō dūraṁ । tō tēṇaṁ savvaṁpi hu gahiyaṁ tassaṁtiyaṁ davvaṁ ।। 332 ||
mōttūṇa tattha sinnaṁ saṁpattō niyapurampa nivapāsē । kayapaḍivattī savvaṁ sāhittā niyahiṁ pattōṁ ॥ 333 ॥
ēvaṁ kamēṇa ca pattā piupāyanaṁdaṇanimittaṁ । piuṇāvi taō puṭṭā kahēha niyaniyamanivvahaṇaṁ? ॥ 334॥
tēhivi savvaṁ kahiyam̐ savityaraṁ niyaniyāṇa niyamāṇa । jō jassa jaṁttha jāō uḍḍhadisāikamāiō ॥
aiyārō, tō sōuṁ siṭṭhī jaṁpēṛa ai ! niru ajutaṁ । vihiyaṁ vacchāpacchaṁ sutucchalacchīi kajjēṇa ॥ 336 ॥
parihariyā sivalacchī varasuhakucchī pasannamuhalacchī । rajjasirī u alacchī jā gahiyā viraivāhāē ||
tālō yaha duriyaṁ guruṇa pāsammi caraha pacchitaṁ । pariharaha rāyasēvaṁ jai dēvaṁ muṇaha savvannuṁ ||338||
tō tē bhōgahisaṁgā rāyasirīsāhilāsiṇō jāyā । pabhaṇaṁti jaṇayasamuhaṁ aviṇayavayaṇāī savvēṁvi ॥ 339॥
saṁprāptaśca kramēṇa nijanr̥papārśvē samagramapi vr̥ttam । kathayitvā natvā ca janakagr̥hē yāti, tataśca ॥ 329 ॥
yaśaścandrō yasturyastvaritaṁ sa prēṣitaśca rājñā । sindhuviṣayādhipatērupari caturaṅgabalakalitaḥ ॥ 326 ॥
prāptaśca tamuddēśaṁ tataścintayati digvataṁ tadā । kiṁparimāṇaṁ gr̥hītaṁ na smarāmaḥ sugurumūlē || 327 ||
ahaha pramādō jātō narēndralakṣmyā athavōnmādaḥ । yatsugurūṇāmupadēśō vismr̥tō'haha muṣṭō'ham ॥328॥
iti cintayaṁstatō vijñaptō hērikairyathā rājā । saṁprati palāpitumanāḥ saṁvahamānaśca tiṣṭhati ॥ 329॥
tataḥ śīghramēva yūyaṁ yadi datta prayāṇakaṁ tatastasya । saptāṅgāmapi hi lakṣmīṁ gr̥hṇītācirēṇa cirabhuktām ॥
tatastatkṣaṇēna ḍhakkā dāpitā rajaniprathamapraharē । calitaḥ sārabalēna gataścōduvā bahudēśam ||331||
tēnāpyāgacchan vijñātastataḥ palāyitō dūram । tatastēna sarvamapi khalu gr̥hītaṁ tatsaṁbandhi dravyam ||332 ||
muktvā tatra sainyaṁ saṁprāptō nijapurē nr̥papārśvē । kr̥tapratipattiḥ sarvē kathayitvā nijagr̥haṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 333॥
ēvaṁ kramēṇa catvāraḥ prāptāḥ pitr̥pādavandananimittam । pitrāpi tataḥ pr̥ṣṭāḥ kathayata nijaniyamanirvahaṇam ||
tairapi sarvaṁ kathitaṁ savistaraṁ nijanijānāṁ niyamānām । yō yasya yatra jāta ūrdhvadigādyatikramādikaḥ ॥
aticāraḥ, tataḥ śrutvā śrēṣṭhī jalpati ayi ! niścitamayuktam । vihitaṁ vatsāpathyaṁ sutuccha lakṣmyāḥ kāryēṇa ||
parihr̥tā śivalakṣmīrvaraśubhakukṣiḥ prasannamukhalakṣmīḥ | rājyaśrīstvalakṣmīryā gr̥hītā viratibādhayā ||337 ||
tasmādālōcayata duścaritaṁ gurūṇāṁ pārśvē carata prāyaścittam । pariharata rājasēvāṁ yadi dēva jānīta sarvajñam ॥ 338 ॥

tāya ! tacciya rannō samapiyā suppiyāvi kiṁ paḍhamaṁ ? । iha vaṇijjakajjē lajjāmō ujjamaṁḥ kāuṁ ।।
jiṇadhammaṁ puṇa karimō pabhāvaṇāī hiṁ tāya ! nipi । niccitō u tumapiṁ hu mā kassavi sēvamaṇurūrasu ।।
sarasu suguruṇa sēvaṁ kuṇasu payattēṇa dāṇavammāī | amhāṇaṁ puṇa tatti mā kuṇasa kayāvi masāvi ||
tōmō kāū siṭṭīvi ṭhiō samuṭṭiyā taṇayā । rāyakulē saṁpattā bharmati sicchāē riddhīē || 343 ॥
jaha jaha rāyasāō taha taha ōsarai dhammapariṇāmō । tēsiṁ pamāyavasaō siṭṭisyāṇaṁ samaggāṇaṁ ||
siddhīvi kālamāsē kālaṁ kāūṇa suravarō jāō । tē caurō sēṭṭhisuyā visayāsattā vigayadhammā ||
mariūṇa kamēṇa taō kugaigayā visahiūṇa dukkhāī । pāviyajiṇavaradhammā puṇōvi sugaī gamissāṁtē ॥
jō uṇa paḍhamō puttō varuṇō nāmēṇa sō ahaṁ jāō । mariuṁ mahōragēhum̐ disiniyamavirāhaṇāvasaō ॥
iya sōuṁ saṁbuddhō naravaikumarāiba huyajaṇanivahō । tō naravaiṇā bhaṇiō maṇōrahō lēsu maha rajjaṁ || 348 ॥
jēṇa taē maha puttō maō ya jīvāviō sudhammammi । uviō ahaṁpi tēṇaṁ paramuvayārī tumaṁ majjha || 349 ||
tō sō bhaṇēi naravara ! niyapunnaṁ caiva phalai jīvāṇa । tassudaē annōvi hu nimittamittaṁ puṇa havē | 1350 ॥
rajjēṇa maha na kajjaṁ nariṁda ! dhammammi ujjamō nicē । kiccō tē nibbhiccō subhiccajuttēṇa jattēṇa || 351॥
tō rannā dhavalaharē haraṁ bahubhūirēhiraṁ ruraṁ । gōṇaṁgaṇāgaṇēhiṁ nisēvaṇijjaṁ samappēḍaṁ || 352 ||
afas sēpi sō visidvadiṭṭhīpabhāvaṇāpuvaṁ । kubvaṁtō jiṇadhammaṁ gamēi diyahāī tatthēva || 353॥
tatastē bhōgābhiṣvaṅgādrājaśrīsābhilāṣiṇō jātāḥ । prabhaṇanti janakasaṁmukhamavinayavacanāni sarvē'pi ॥ 339 ॥
tāta ! tvayaiva rājñē samarpitāḥ supriyā api kiṁ prathamam ? । idānīṁ vāṇijyakāryē lajjñāmaha udyamaṁ kartum ॥
jinadharma punaḥ kurmaḥ prabhāvanādibhistāta ! nityamapi । niścintastu tvamapi hi mā kasyāpi sēvāmanusara ||
sara sugurūṇāṁ sēvāṁ kuru prayatnēna dānadharmādi । asmākaṁ punaścintāṁ mā kuru kadāpi manasāpi ॥ 342 ॥
tatō maunaṁ kr̥tvā śrēṣṭhapi sthitaḥ samutthitāstanayāḥ । rājakulē saṁprāptā bhramanti svēcchayā r̥ddhayā ॥ 343 ॥
yathā yathā rājaprasādastathā tathāpasarati dharmapariṇāmaḥ । tēṣāṁ pramādavaśataḥ śrēṣṭhisutānāṁ samagrāṇām ||344॥
śrēṣṭhyapi kālamāsē kālaṁ kr̥tvā suravarō jātaḥ । tē catvāraḥ śrēṣṭhitā viṣayāsaktā vigatadharmāṇaḥ || 34.5 ||
mr̥tvā kramēṇa tataḥ kuṁgatigatā viṣaya duḥkhāni । prāptajinavaradharmāḥ punarapi sugatiṁ gamiṣyanti ॥ 346 ॥
yaḥ punaḥ prathamaḥ putrō varuṇō nāmnā sō'haṁ jātaḥ । mr̥tvā mahōragēṣu digniyamavirādhanāvaśataḥ ॥ 347 ||
iti śrutvā saṁbuddhō narapatikumārādibahujananivahaḥ । tatō narapatinā bhaṇitō manōrathō lāhi mama rājyam ।।
yēna tvayā mama putrō mr̥taśca jīvitaḥ sudharmē । sthāpitō'hamapi tēna paramōpakārī tvaṁ mama ||349॥
tataḥ sa bhaṇati naravara ! nijapuṇyamēva phalati jīvānām । tasyōdayē'nyō'pi hi nimittamātraṁ punarbhavati ॥
rājyēna mama na kāryaṁ narēndra ! dharma udyamō nityam । kr̥tyastē nibhr̥tyaḥ subhr̥tyayuktēna yatnēna ||391 ॥
tatō rājñā dhavalagr̥haṁ gr̥hamiva bahubhūtirājitaṁ ruciram । gavāṅganāgaṇairniṣēvaṇīyaṁ samarpya ॥ 352 ॥
sthāpitaḥ śrēṣṭhipadēsa viśiṣṭadr̥ṣṭiprabhāvanāpūrvam । kurvana jinadharmaṁ gamayati divasāni tatraiva ॥ 353 ॥

tattō sō baṁdhū mēharahō muṇivi tassa vr̥ttaṁtaṁ । saṁpattō tannayarē kabaḍḍiyāēvi rahiō sō || 354 ||
saṁjhāē maṇōrahasiddhimaṁdirē dāravāliyanarēṇa । khaliō khalōvva puraō tattō sō sāhaē tassa || 355॥
mēharahō nāṇaṁ jēṭṭhō baṁdhū ya siṭṭiṇō ahayaṁ । vāṇārasīu pattō tā kahasu tumaṁ imaṁ tassa || 356 ||
takkahiē siddhī sasaṁbhramaṁ saṁmūhō samaṇupattō | tēṇavi namiṁu āliṁgiō ya gurugōravēṇa taō || 357॥

sandhyāyāṁ manōrathaśrēṣṭhimandirē dvārapālakanarēṇa । skhalitaḥ khala iva puratastataḥ sa kathayati tasya ॥ 395 ॥ .
mēgharathō nāmnā jyēṣṭhō vandhuśca śrēṣṭhinō'ham । vārāṇasītaḥ prāptastasmātkathaya tvabhidaṁ tasmai ॥ 356॥

nītō gr̥hē vihitā sakalā tatkālōcitapratipattiḥ । pratyūṣē jinabhavanē nītaḥ kr̥tasphāraśr̥ṅgāraḥ ॥ 358॥
aṣṭaprakārapūjāṁ kāritō vidhipurassaraṁ tataḥ । āhr̥taśca narēndrō mēgharathō darśitastasmai || 359 ||

tatō yathā manōrathēna dignataṁ pālitaṁ niraticāram । tathā'nyēnāpyēvaṁ pālayitavyaṁ prayatnēna ॥ 361 ॥
sarvajagajjīvahitamātmahitaṁ sa karōti yō'dhiṁkām । varjayati digyātrāṁ prayatnataḥ sūtrayuktitaḥ ॥ 362 ||

duvihaṁ bhōgavayaṁ iha bhōyaṇaō kammaō ya uvabhōgō | taṁbōlāhārāī paribhōgē vatthalalāī || 1 ||
bhōyaṇaō saḍḍhēṇaṁ bhōttavvaṁ phāsuēsaṇiyadavvaṁ । tayabhāvēṇēsaṇīyaṁ navaraṁ saccittaparivajjaṁ || 2 ||
tassaviya asatēṇatakāya bahuvīyavajjaṇaṁ tattha । asaṇammi aiyāī pāṇammi ya maṁsarasayāī || 3 ||
taha khāimammi uṁbarapaṁcagaparivajjaṇaṁ sayā kujjā । mahupabhiīṇaṁ puṇa sāimammi iya buḍḍha vasō ||4||
paribhōgammiya dhūlappallavatthāī parimiyaṁ sijjā sāsaṇapabhāvaṇaṭṭā varāī jā dēvasāī ||5||
navaraṁ tapparimāṇaṁ kujjā āharaṇamāiyāpi । kammayaō puṇa bhaṇṇai uvabhōgō, kuṇai jaṁ saḍḍhō ॥6॥
guttipālāikammaṁ igavāraṁ paharavavaharaṇa niyamā । jaṁ puṇa puṇō puṇōcciya kīrai sō hōi paribhōgō ||7||
annē uṇa āyariyā kammayaō jōyaṇaṁ na kuvvaṁti । uvabhōgaparībhōgāṇaṁ ēsa buḍḍhāṇa uvaēsō ॥8॥
jō vajjai saccittaṁ āhāraṁ sāvaō sayākālaṁ । sō vissasēṇakumaruvva lahai sivasaṁpayaṁ kamasō ॥9॥
tathāhi; —
"naṁdaṇavarṇava gurusālasaṁgayaṁ gayamuhaṁva rayaṇa । nāmēṇa bhōgapuraṁ paraṁ puraṁ asthi bharahammi || 10 ||
āsi samiddhakittī vibuhapiōṁ pavipattikarakamalō । rāyā puraṁdarō ina puraṁdarō dariyariudalaṇō ||
tassatthi piyā raivavibbhamā vigbhamāṇa kulabhavaṇaṁ । vigbhamavaībhihāṇā susīlaguṇasāliṇī saralā ||
tāṇaṁ ca suō suvaṇammi vissuō vissasēṇavarakumarō । kumarakarigaṁdha siṁdhurasamappahō dhariyadhavalaguṇō ॥
guṇacaṁda sōmacaṁdābhihāṇayā saṁti tassavi vayaṁsā । aha annam̐yā sa pattō tēhiṁ samaṁ malayagirisiharē ॥ 14 ॥
1
dvividhaṁ bhōgatratamiha bhōjanataḥ karmataśca upabhōgaḥ । tāmbūlāhārādiḥ paribhōgē vastralalanādiḥ ॥ 1 ॥
bhōjanataḥ śrāddhēna bhōktavyaṁ prāsukaiṣaṇīyadravyam । tadabhāvē'nēṣaṇīyaṁ kintu sacittaparivartam ॥2॥
tasyāpi cāsattvē'nantakāya bahubījavarjanaṁ tatra । aśanē ārdrakādi pānē ca māṁsarasādi || 3 ||
tathā khādimni udumbarapañcakaparivarjanaṁ sadā kuryāt । madhuprabhr̥tīnāṁ punaḥ svādimnīti vr̥ddhōpadēśaḥ ॥ 4 ॥
paribhōgē ca sthūlapramūlyavastrādi parimitaṁ śayyā । śāsanaprabhāvanārthaṁ varāṇi yāvad dēvadrūṣyāṇi ॥5॥
kintu tatparimāṇaṁ kuryādābharaṇādikānāmapi । karmataḥ punarbhaṇyata upabhōgaḥ, karōti yat śrāddhaḥ ||6||
guptipālādikamaikavāraṁ praharavyavaharaṇaniyamāta । yatpunaḥ punaḥ punarēva kriyatē sa bhavati paribhōgaḥ ॥ 7॥
anyē punarācāryā karmatō yōjanaṁ na kurvanti । upabhōgaparībhōgayēōrēṣa vr̥ddhānāmupadēśaḥ ||8||
yō barjayati sacittamāhāraṁ śrāvakaḥ sadākālam । sa viśvasēnakumāravallabhatē śivasaṁpadaṁ kramaśaḥ ||9 ॥
nandanavanamiva guruśālasaṁgataṁ gajamukhamiva ratnā ( racanā ) ḍhyam । nāmnā bhōgapuraṁ paraṁ puramasti bharatē ॥ 10 ॥
āsīcchaśiśuddha kīrttirvibudhapriyaḥ pavipavitrakarakamalaḥ । rājā purandara iva purandarō iptaripudalanaḥ ॥ 11॥
tasyāsti priyā ratirūpavibhramā vibhramāṇāṁ kulabhavanam । vibhramavatyabhidhānā suśīlaguṇaśālinī saralā ॥12॥
tayōśca sutō bhuvanē viśrutō viśvasēnavarakumāraḥ । kumārakarigandhasindhurasamaprabhō dhr̥tadhavalaguṇaḥ ॥13॥

picchara tattha mayacchi ēvaṁ pakkaṁbalaṁbiyā hatthē । itthiṁ vitthinnaniyaṁvahāriṇi punacaṁdamuhi ||15||
raṇaraṇayapabhāvulla sirapaṁcamuggāramaṇahara girāē । gāyaṁtiṁ virahasamubbhavāī gēyāī vihuraṁgī || 16 ||
gayasāraṁgā sāraṁgiyantra piyavirahiyā rahaṁgivva । duhadāhadīhanī sāsa susiyaaharā paḍhai ēvaṁ ||17||
cittaha māsaha cūyaha maṁjari, picchivi mayaṇamayallahi maṁjari ।
vissasēṇakumariṇuṁ harḍa rattī, duha aṇuhavau bahuya diṇaratī || 18 ||
kayasiṁgāraphāra tasurēsihi, ciṭṭhahu iha kisataṁṇu tasurēsihi ।
kira hauṁ hōsu kumaravaramāṇiṇi, tēṇa vihiya hayahiya hauṁ māṇiṇi ॥ 19 ॥
niyanāmasaṁkirēṇa puṭṭhāmā suyaṇu ! kō imō kumarōṁ । tai gijjai jai jujjai tō suṁdari ! majjha taṁ kahasu ।
sā sasaṁbhramaṁ ciya pulaiyadēhā palōyaē jāva । sakinnarasaṁ bālā tō takkhaṇamēvamaṇuhavai ॥21॥
tathāhi ;-
kimimō sōti saharasā kattō tassaṁbhavōti savisāyā । parapurisōtti ya sabhayā rūvēṇahiyatti sāsaṁkā ॥
nēmittiēṇa kahiyaṁ ajjaṁ piyamēlautti sarvisaṁbhā । vāmabhuyaacchiphuraṇē sunicchayā taha susauṇāō ||
ēmāirasaṁtara taralamāṇasā māṇasammi ciṁtēi । hōu iha jō va sō vā atihī viṇayārihō tāva || 24||
tō dēi pallavāṇamuva viṭṭō tammi bhaṇai tayabhimuṁhaṁ । jaivi na jujjai jaha taha maṇavallahanāma ullavaṇaṁ ॥
tahavi tannāmabhaṇaṇē amayarasāsāyaṇaṁ lahau rasaṇā । sappurisanāmagahaṇaṁ kuṇē jaṁ dukkhanimmahaṇaṁ ॥ 26 ॥
guṇacandrasōmacandrābhidhānau stastasyāpi vayasyau । athānyadā sa prāptastaiḥ samaṁ malayagiriśikharē ॥ 14 ॥
paśyati tatra mr̥gākṣīmēkāṁ pakvāmralumbikāhastām । striyaṁ vistīrṇanitambadhāriṇīṁ pūrṇacandramukhīm ॥15॥
bhautsukyaprabhā vōllasitr̥pañcamōdgāra manōhara girā । gāyantīṁ virahasamudbhavāni gēyāni vidhurāṅgī ॥ 16 ॥
gatasāraṅgā sāraṅgīva priyavirāhitā rathāṅgīva । duḥkhadāha darghiniḥśvāsaśuṣkāgharā paṭhatyēvam ॥ 17 ॥
caitrē māsē cr̥tasya mañjarīṁ, dr̥ṣṭrā madanalatāmañjarīm ।
viśvasēnakumāraṇāhaṁ raktā, duḥkhamanubhavāmi bahu dinarātrīḥ || 18 ||
kr̥taśr̥ṅgārasphārā tadarthaṁ, tiṣṭhāmīha kr̥śatanustadartham ।
kilāhaṁ bhaviṣyāmi kumāravaramāninī, tēna vihitā hr̥tahr̥dayā'haṁ māninī ॥ 19 ॥
nijanāmaśaṅkitrā pr̥ṣṭā sā sutanu ! kō'yaṁ kumāraḥ । tvayā gīyatē yadi yujyatē tadā sundari ! mama tatkathaya ॥20॥
tataḥ sā sasaṁbhramamēva pulakitadēhā pralōkatē yāvat । saṁkīrṇarasaṁ bālā tāvattatkṣaṇamēvamanubhavati ॥ 21 ॥
kimayaṁ sa iti saharṣā kutastatsaṁbhava iti saviṣādā । parapuruṣa iti ca sabhayā rūpēṇādhika iti sāyaṅkā ॥
naimittikēna kathitamadya priyamēla iti saviśrambhā । vāmabhujākṣisphuraṇē suniścayā tathā suśakunāt ॥23॥
ēvamādirasāntarataralamānasā mānasē cintayati । bhavatviha yō vā sa vā'tithirvinayārhastāvat ॥24॥
tatō dadāti pallavāsanamupaviṣṭastasminbhaṇati tadabhimukham । yadyapi na yujyatē yathā tathā manōvallabhanāmōllapanam ॥

bhōgapurāvitaṇaō nāmaṇaṁ vissasēṇavara kumarō । cāī kayannuō vacchalō ya paḍivannanivvahaṇō ||27||
iccāiguṇagaṇō māmahēhiṁ gahiō purā purō majjha । pōyaṇapuraujjāṇē jiṇabhavaṇagayāē garimāē ||28||
puṭṭhā na kiṁpi tē tattha kiṁtu sammāṇiyā maē bahuyaṁ । maha piuṇā naimittī majjha varaṭṭhā tayā puṭṭhō ॥ 29 ॥ ॥
dra kahiō sōcē piyayamō māgahēhiṁ jō paḍhiō । tō majjha tassa uvari jāō ya samaggalō rāō ॥
tō niyamahīmuhāō puṭṭhō nēmittiō jahā kaiyā । tēṇa samaṁ mēlāvō kumarīē kahasu katthavi ya 1 ॥
tēṇaṁ ca imaṁ kahiyē sattamadivasammi malayasēlampi । hōhī saṁgamasōkkhaṁ tēṇa sahātakiyaṁ kiṁtu ||32||
aidūrē sō sēlō satamadivasa tu āgayaṁ caiva । aiucchugō ya ahayaṁ kajjavasēṇaṁ gamissāmi ||33||
iharā taṁpi kahatō, tō sā tōsēṇa kahai taṁ gaṁtuṁ । kumarīē tō bhaṇiyaṁ halā ! diṇē satta, ittō ya ॥
sattasayajōyaṇēhiṁ kumarō ciṭṭhēi kaha ṇu tavtrayaṇaṁ । ghaḍai aidugghaḍamiṇaṁ ghaḍissaē navari vihivasaō ॥
ahavā sapacaōcciya naimittī avita ca tavvayaṇa । hōhī na ittha bhaṁtī paraṁtu kaha gammihī tattha ? |
iya saṁdēhaṁdōlayamārūḍhā rūḍhapēmapa-bhārā । aiukkaṁṭhavisaṁṭuladēhā bhūmīē lōhaṁtī ॥37॥
diṭṭhā adipuvēṇa kēvi vijjāharēṇa hariūṇa | āṇīyā iha anbhasthiyā ya jā satta divasāī ||
tathāhi :-
hē suṁdari ! maṁ mannasu bhattāraṁ kaṇayacūḍanāmāṇaṁ । uttarasēḍhīsāmissa naṁdaṇaṁ pavaṇavēyassa ॥ 39 ॥
tathāpi tannāmabhaṇanē'mr̥tarasāsvādanaṁ labhatāṁ rasanā । satpuruṣanāmagrahaṇaṁ karōti yad duḥkhanirmathanam ||26||
bhōgapurādhipatanayō nāmnā viśvasēnavarakumāraḥ । tyāgī kr̥tajñō vatsalaśca pratipannanirvahaṇaḥ ||27||
ityādiguṇagaṇō māgadhaigr̥hītaḥ purā purō mama । pōtanapurōdhānē jinabhavanagatāyā garim ||28||
pr̥ṣṭā na kimapi tē tatra kintu sammānitā mayā bahu । mama pitrā naimittikō mama varārtha tadā pr̥ṣṭaḥ ॥ 29 ॥
tēnāpi kathitaḥ sa ēva priyatamō māgadhairyaḥ paṭhitaḥ । tatō mama tasyōpari jātaśca samagalō rāgaḥ ||30||
tatō nijasakhīmukhātpr̥ṣṭō naimittikō yathā kadā । tēna samaṁ mēlaḥ kumāryāḥ kathaya kvāpi ca 1 ॥ 31 ॥
tēna cēdaṁ kathita saptamadivasē malayaśailē । bhaviṣyati saṁgamasaukhyaṁ tēna sahātarkitaṁ kintu ||32||
atidūrē sa śailaḥ saptamadivasaṁ tvāgatamēva । atyutsukaścāhaṁ kāryavaśēna gamiṣyāmi ॥33॥
itarathā tadapyakathayiṣyam, tataḥ sā tōṣēṇa kathayati tāṁ gatvā । kumāryā tatō bhaṇitaṁ halē dināḥ sapta, itaśca ॥
saptaśatayōjanēṣu kumārastiṣṭhati kathaṁ nu tadvacanam । ghaṭatē'tidurghaṭamidaṁ ghaṭiṣyatē kēvalaṁ vidhivaśataḥ ॥ 35॥
athavā sapratyaya ēva naimittikō'vitathaṁ ca tadvacanam । bhaviṣyati nātra bhrāntiḥ parantu kathaṁ gamiṣyatē tatra ? |
iti saṁdēhadōlāmārūḍhā rūḍhaprēmaprāgbhārā । atyutkaṇṭhavisaṁsthuladēhā bhūmyāṁ luṭhantī ||37||
dr̥ṣṭapūrvēkēnāpi vidyādharēṇa hr̥tvā । ānītēhābhyarthitā ca yāvatsapta divasāni || 38 ॥
hē sundari ! māṁ manyasva bhartāraṁ kanakacūḍanāmānam । uttaraśrēṇisvāminō nandanaṁ pavanavēgasya || 39॥
1 ga. kayalī harammi bhaṇiyā ya tēṇa imaṁ ।

supāsanāha-caritrmammi-
iccāi jāva jaṁpa tāvuttaraō surayaṇapuṁjōbba । tēṇa taraṇimaṁḍalamavi taralaṁtō muṇī pattō ॥ 40 ॥
ahiūṇa dōṇivi payaō paṇayāī sāhupayapamaṁ । cāraṇamuṇiṇā tō dhammalāhi sō imaṁ bhaṇiō ||
kiṁ kaṇayacūḍa ! ēvaṁ vicidviyaṁ siddhagarahiyaṁ kajjaṁ । maha bhāisuōvi tumaṁ na lajjasēṇajjakajjēṇa ॥ 42 ॥
naya tumha kulē kēṇaci kayāvi vihiyā kalaṁkasaṁkāvi । iṇhi puṇa tava cariyaṁ vivarīyaṁ dīsaē vaccha !।।
kiśca ।
visayapivāsānaḍiō ihēva ramasi paramahēlāō । taṁ nūṇa paramahēlāē paramahēlāē sahasi duhē ||44||
chāvijchēō ki kayāi saṁbhavai visayasēvāē ? । tanhā navariṁ ahiyā vaḍḍhai - lavaṇaṁbupāṇēṇa ॥ 45 ॥
kiñca ।
nāyāgayā visayā dusahadudaṁ dēti iya muṇēūṇa । cattā dhīrēhiṁ, tumaṁ tē vaṁchasi puṇa anāēṇaṁ ॥ 46 ॥
visataruphalaṁva visayā bhujjati surhēṇa mahurabhāvēṇa | duhadāyagadīharamōhasaṁgamō dūsahō puraō || 47||
jaha khalu jahannakammaṁ jūyaṁ viusāṇa garahaṇijjaṁ ca । jāṇiyajiṇatrayaṇāṇaṁ taha ēvaṁ visayasaṁgōvi ॥ 48 ॥
hārē khaṇēṇa jīō jūṇa cirajjiyaṁ jahā vihavaṁ । visayapasattō sattō taha caiva cirajjiyaṁ sukayaṁ ॥ 49 ॥
tāvaccha ! tujjha jaṁ kiṁci ruccaē - kuṇasuṁ taṁ viyārējaṁ । duccariyaṁ tuha hōhī puraō duhadāyagaṁ ēyaṁ ॥ 50 ॥
aha duccariyasamajjiyadukammasamutthabhāviduhabhīō । sō paṇivāyapurassaramēvaṁ vinavitō ||51 ||
bhayavaṁ । cirakālamahaṁ parvaciō visaya sukkharasarasiō । nipahiyakarēhiṁ karaṇēhiṁ dāruṇēhiṁ vinūhamaṇō ॥ 52॥
saṁsāraviyāragahīrasāyarē majjha majjaṇaṁ hutaṁ । jai maṁ na mūḍhahiyayaṁ samuddharaṁtō dayāē tumaṁ ॥ 53 ॥
ityādi yāvajjalpati tāvaduttarataḥ suratnapuñja iva । tējasā taraṇimaṇḍalamapi taralayanmuniḥ prāptaḥ ||40||
abhyutthāya dvāvapi padataḥ praṇatau sādhupādapadmam । cāraṇamuninā tatō dharmalābhayitvā sa idaṁ bhaṇitaḥ || 41 ॥
kiṁ kanakacūḍa ! ētad vicēṣṭitaṁ śiṣṭagarhitaṁ kāryam । mama bhrātr̥sutō'pi tvaṁ na lajjasē'nāryakāryēṇa ॥42॥
na ca tava kulē kēnāpi kadāpi vihitā kalaṅkaśaṅkāpi । idānīṁ punastava caritaṁ viparītaṁ dr̥śyatē vatsa ! ॥
viṣayapipāsānaṭita ihaiva yadramayasi paramahēlāḥ । tad nūnaṁ paramahēlayā paramahēlayā sahasē duḥkham ॥44॥
vāñchāvicchēdaḥ kiṁ kadācitsaṁbhavati viṣayasēvayā । tr̥ṣṇā kēvalamadhikā vardhatē lavaṇāmbupānēna ॥ 45 ॥
nyāyāgatā api viṣayā duḥsahaduḥkhaṁ dadatīti jñātvā । tyaktā dhīraiḥ, tvaṁ tānvāñchasi punaranyāyēna ॥ 46 ॥
viṣataruphalamiva viṣayā bhujyantē sukhēna madhurabhāvēna । duḥkhadāyaka dīrgha mōhasaṁgamō duḥsahaḥ purataḥ ॥ 47 ॥
yathā khalu jaghanyakarma dyūtaṁ viduṣāṁ garhaṇīyaṁ ca । jñātajinavacanānāṁ tathaivaṁ viṣayasaṅgō'pi ॥ 48 ॥
nāśayati kṣaṇēna jīvō dyūtēna cirārjitaṁ yathā vibhavam । viṣayaprasaktaḥ sattvastathaiva cirājitaṁ sukr̥tam ॥ 49 ॥
tasmād batsa ! tava yatkiñcidrōcatē kuru tadvicārya | duścaritaṁ tava bhaviṣyati puratō duḥkhadāyakamētat ॥50॥
atha duścaritasamarjitaduṣkarmasamutthabhāviduḥkhabhītaḥ । sa praṇipātapurassaramēvaṁ vijñapayitumārabdhaḥ ॥ 51 ॥
bhagavan ! cirakālamahaṁ pravañcitō viṣayasaukhyarasarasikaḥ । nijāhita karaiḥ karaṇairdāruṇairvimūḍhamanāḥ ॥52॥

tō kayaparadāravaō sō udvivi mēṁ khamāvi bhaṇai । maha bhaiṇī taṁ saṁpai tā ēsa naēmi sadvāṇaṁ ||54 ॥
tō jaṁpiyaṁ maē taṁ vacca ahaṁ puṇa ihēva ciṭṭhissaṁ । nēmittiēṇa kahiō jamhā piyasaṁgama ēttha ॥ 55 ॥
taṁ sōuṁ niyaṭhāṇaṁ saṁpattō saṁpayaṁ kaṇayacūḍō । cāraṇamuṇīvi malayaddikaṁdarē ciṭṭhaē inhi ॥ 56 ॥
iya savvaṁpi hu kahiyaṁ niyacariyaṁ saṁpayaṁ tumaṁ majjha । sāhasu kumāra ! kattō samāgaō ittha kōya tuma ? ||
ahaba nimittiyakaraṇēṇa iṁgiēhiṁ ca tumaṁ maē nāō । sō caiva vissasēṇō maha daiō pāṇaavamahiō ।।
tā tā inhiṁ niyakarakamalēṇa maha karaṁ gahijaṁ । sō ciya pasatthakālō ciṁtāmaṇiṇā jahiṁ jōgō |
takkālōciyavihiṇā kumarō taṁ pariṇaī tayaṇurōhā । parapatthaṇāē garuyā piēva pāṇē paricayati ॥ 64 ॥
tattō kumarī samaṁ gaṁtuṁ malayaddikaṁdarē vihiṇā । cāraṇamuṇimabhivaṁdēi sapariyaṇō paramaviṇaṇaṁ ॥ 61 ॥
muṇiṇāvi jahōcciyasaṁbhamēṇa sammāṇiō taō kumarō । uvavisai vasumaīē suṇīvi iya bhai tayabhimuhaṁ ||
aṇavarayamaraṇa raṇaraṇayarōya sōyāulammi saṁsārē | jīvāṇa natthi sōkkhaṁ kharṇapi kiṁ kumara ! na muṇēsi ? ।।
jaṁ vilasasi sicchāē niraggalaṁ samayanayagalōvva tumaṁ । asamaṁ jasaṁ samajjasu caēsa asamaṁjasaṁ taha ya ॥
asamaṁjasōvavajjaṇamiha jāyai savvasaṁgacāyāō । sō uṇa rāganirōhā rāganirōhō u saccaraṇā ॥ 65 ॥
saccaraṇaṁ puṇa kāuṁ pārijjai pauṇakaraṇagāmēṇa । karaṇāṇa puṇō jāya paṇattaṁ jōnvaṇē caiva ॥ 66 ॥
buṛaḍhattē jīvāṇa na pauṇabhāvō havēi kaiyāvi । duvvārajarāgamajajjarijjamāṇāṇa karaṇāṇaṁ ||67 ||
saṁsāravikāra gabhīrasāgarē mama majjanamabhaviṣyat । yadi māṁ na mūḍhahr̥dayaṁ samudadhariṣyō dayayā tvam ||13||
tataḥ kr̥taparadāravrataḥ sa utthāya māṁ kṣamayitvā bhaṇati । mama bhaginī tvaṁ saṁprati tasmādēhi nayāmi svasthānam ॥
tatō jalpitaṁ mayā tvaṁ vrajāhaṁ punarihaiva sthāsyāmi | naimittikēna kathitō yasmātpriyasaṁgamō'tra ||15||
tat śrutvā nijasthānaṁ saṁprāptaḥ sāṁprataṁ kanakacūḍaḥ । cāraṇamunirapi malayādrikandarē tiṣṭhatīdānīm ||16||
iti sarvamapihi kathitaṁ nijacaritaṁ sāṁprataṁ tvaṁ mama । kathaya kumāra ! kutaḥ samāgatō'tra kaśca tvam ! ||17||
athavā naimittikakathanēnēṅgitaiśca tvaṁ mayā jñātaḥ । sa ēva viśvasēnō mama dayitaḥ prāṇābhyadhikaḥ ॥ 58॥
tasmānmāṁ trāyasvēdānīṁ nijakarakamalēna mama karaṁ gr̥hatviā । sa ēva praśastakālaścintāmaṇinā yatra yōgaḥ ॥
tatkālōcitavidhinā kumārastāṁ pariṇayati tadanurōdhāt । paraprārthanayā guravaḥ priyānapi prāṇānparityajanti ॥
tataḥ kumāryā samaṁ gatvā malayādrikandarē vidhinā । cāraṇamunimabhivandatē saparijana : paramavinayēna ॥ 61 ॥
munināpi yathōcita saṁbhramēṇa sammānitastataḥ kumāraḥ । upaviśati vasumatyāṁ munirapīti bhaṇati tadabhimukham ||
anavaratamaraṇautsukyarōgaśōkākulē saṁsārē । jīvānāṁ nāsti saukhyaṁ kṣaṇamapi kiṁ kumāra ! na jānāti ॥ 63 ॥
yad vilapsasi svēcchayā nirargalaṁ samadamadakalavat tvam | asamaṁ yaśaḥ samarjaya tyajāsamañjasaṁ tathā ca ॥ 64 ॥
asamañjasōpavarjanamiha jāyatē sarvasaṅgatyāgāt । sa punā rāganirōdhād rāganirōdhastu saccaraṇāt ॥ 65॥
saccaraṇaṁ punaḥ kartuṁ śakyatē praguṇakaraṇagrāmēṇa । karaṇānāṁ punarjāyatē praguṇatvaṁ yauvana ēva ॥ 66 ॥
vr̥ddhatvē jīvānāṁ na praguṇabhāvō bhavati kadāpi । durvārajarāgamajarjaryamāṇānāṁ karaṇānām ||67 ||

supāsanāha caritryammi-
bālattē jīvāṇaṁ kajjākajjāināṇarahiyāṇaṁ । kaha saccaraṇavihāṇaṁ jāyara paḍaṇidiyāpi ? || 68॥
aparaṁ ca ।
jaha jōvvaṇammi ahamā marhati visayāmisaṁ jahā puritā । tai suyaṇā sivasukkhaṁ mahiti vimuhā visaya sukkhē ॥
imiṇā nibaṁdhaṇēṇaṁ kumāra ! niyakammaniṇakayacittō । sivasuhakaēṇa taruṇōvi ujjamaṁ kuṇasu saddhammē ॥
sō uṇa duvihō bhaṇiō jaigihibhēēṇa paḍhamaō tattha । kahiō savittharaṁ tō sammattāī ya gihidhammē ॥
nīsāmannaṁ sāmannamaggamāsēviuṁ acāryatō । tō gurumūlē sāvayavayāī giṇhēi sō kumarō ||72 ||
guṇacaṁda sōmacaṁdērhi saṁjuō taha vilāsavaiyāē । vārasavi vihāṇēṇaṁ nāūṇaṁ tāṇa bhāvatthaṁ ॥ 73 ॥
bīyaṁ guṇavvayaṁ puṇa kumarēṇaṁ kahavi saṁkaḍaṁ gahiyaṁ । mittakalattajuēṇavi pavamāṇāē saddhāē ||74 |
jalapattāī mōtuṁ sēsasacittassa bhōyaṇē niyamō । kammayaō puṇa jayaṇā kharakammāīṇa savvāṇa ॥75||
duppakkāpakāsārabhakkhaṇaṁ pariharēi parabhāgē । saccēyaṇaṁ ca tappaḍibaddhaṁ ca viśuddhapariṇāmō ||76 ||
iccāi pavajjēuṁ vaṁdēḍaṁ muṇivaraṁ ca jā caliō । tāva suramihuṇamēgaṁ samāgayaṁ munivaraṁ namiuṁ ॥ 77 ॥
bhaṇiō ya tēṇa kumarō picchaṇayachaṇaṁ niēsa khaṇamēgaṁ । iya suṇiūṇaṁ sō jāva ciṭṭhaē tattha tō tēṇa ॥
lahuuttaravēubviyadēvīdēvāṇa bahuyarūvēhiṁ । pāraddhaṁ picchaṇayaṁ picchai acchariyabhūyaṁva ॥ 79 ॥
bhūyaṁ paṇaccamāṇaṁ tāṇaṁ majjhammi saṁjhasamavannaṁ । kaṁṭhē vilaggiūṇaṁ vilāsavaiyaṁ imaṁ bhaṇai ||80||
sattamadiṇāu diṭṭhā vacchē ! taṁ tuha piyāmahī ahayaṁ । tujjha viōē ubbaṁdhēḍaṁ mayā vaṁtarī jāyā ॥ 81 ॥
bālatvē jīvānāṁ kāryākāryādijñānarahitānām । kathaṁ saccaraṇavidhānaṁ jāyatē praguṇēndriyāṇāmapi ? ॥ 38॥
yathā yauvanē'dhamāḥ kāṅkṣanti viṣayāmiṣaṁ yathā puruṣāḥ । tathā sujanāḥ śivasaukhyaṁ kāṅkṣanti vimukhā viṣayasaukhyē |
anēna nibandhanēna kumāra ! nijakarmanighātakr̥tacittaḥ । śivasaukhyakr̥tē taruṇō'pyudhamaṁ kuru saddharmē ॥70॥
sa punardvividhō bhaṇitō yatigr̥hibhēdēna prathamattastatra । kathitaḥ savistaraṁ tataḥ samyaktvādiśca gr̥hidharmaḥ ॥71॥
niḥsāmānyaṁ śrāmaṇyamārgamāsēvitumaśaknuvan । tatō gurumūlē śrāvakatrtāni gr̥hṇāti sa kumāraḥ ॥ 72 ॥
guṇacandrasōmacandrābhyāṁ saṁyutastathā vilāsavatyā । dvādaśadhāpi vidhānēnaṁ jñātvā tēṣāṁ bhāvārtham ॥73॥
dvitīyaṁ guṇavataṁ punaḥ kumārēṇa kathamapi saṁkaṭaṁ gr̥hītam । mitrakalatrayutēnāpi pravardhamānayā śraddhayā ||74 ||
jalapatrāṇi muktvā śēṣasacittasya bhōjanē niyamaḥ । karmataḥ punaryatanā kharakarmādīnāṁ sarvēṣām ॥75॥
duṣpakvāpakvāsārabhakṣaṇaṁ pariharati parabhāgē । saccētanaṁ ca tatpratibaddhaṁ ca viśuddhapariṇāmaḥ ॥ 76 ॥
ityādi prapadya vanditvā munivaraṁ ca yāvaccalitaḥ । tāvatsuramithunamēkaṁ samāgataṁ munivaraṁ natvā ॥ 77 ॥
bhaṇitaśca tēna kumāraḥ prēkṣaṇakṣaṇaṁ paśya kṣaṇamēkam । iti śrutvā sa yāvattiṣṭhati tatra tatastēna ॥ 78 ॥
laghūttara vikr̥tadēvīdēvānāṁ bahurūpaiḥ । prārabdhaṁ prēkṣaṇakaṁ paśyatyāścaryabhūtamiva ॥79॥
bhūtaṁ pranr̥tyat tēṣāṁ madhyē saṁdhyāsamavarṇam । kaṇṭhē vilagya vilāsavatamidaṁ bhaṇati ॥ 80 ॥
saptamadinād dr̥ṣṭā vatsa ! tvaṁ tava pitāmahī aham । tava viyōga udbadhya mr̥tā vyantarī jātā ॥ 81 ॥

vissasēkahā।
473
dahūṇa vibhaṁgēṇaṁ ihāgayā garuyanēhapaḍibaddhā । tā savvā piyāvi hu tuha marihī virahahahiyaō || 82||
divasāō taṁ avahiyā si samagaṁ tu pavasiyaṁ tassa । niddāchuhāiyaṁ taha suyā puṇō takkhaṇaṁ ahayaṁ || 83||
tammi dicciya savvattha niru gaviṭṭhāvi nōvaladdhā si । tā tumbhē savvēvi hu ciṭṭhaha itthēva khaṇamēgaṁ ॥ 84 ॥
jāva ahaṁ raṇamallaṁ tuha piyaraṁ putti ! ittha āṇēmi । tō takkhaṇēṇa gaṁtuṁ samāgayā taṁ gr̥hēūṇa || 85||
sō vaṁdēuṁ sāhuṁ ubaviṭṭhō tō kumāramāīhiṁ । abhivaṁdiō bhaī vilāsavaīsammuhaṁ ēvaṁ ॥ 86 ॥
savvōvi
sō manāō jaṇaṇīvayaṇā vaiyarō tujjha । aha nivapuraṁdarōvi hu kumaravasērīē saṁpattō ॥ 87॥
raṇamalāī taō abhuūṇa vaṁdiō rāyā । muṇiṇāvi samāraddhā puṇōvi sadēsaṇā tēsi ||88 ||
"dēśādanyasmādapi madhyādapi jalanidhērdiśō'pyantāt । ānīya jhaṭiti ghaṭayati vidhirabhimatamabhimukhībhūtaḥ ।। "
iccāidēsaṇaṁtē raṇamallēṇa puraṁdarō bhaṇiō । ēsā maha pāṇapiyā duhiyā pīīē davā ||89 ||
nivaraṇamakō nīō puraṁdarēṇaṁ niyammi nayarammi । guṇacaṁdāō nāuṁ savvaṁ saṁbaṁdhamāīyē ॥90॥
dēvamapi dāraṁ kumaravahūṇaṁ surayaṇamāharaṇaṁ । sahāṇē saṁpattaṁ muṇīvi viharēi vasuhāē ||91||
kaivayadiṇāī dhari sampāṇēuṁ visajjiō rannā । raṇamalō saṁpattō niyanayarē kuṇai saddhammaṁ ॥ 92||
vīguṇavara kutō kuṇai visayaparibhōgaṁ । sirivissa sēṇakumarō sumaraṁtō suguruguruāṇaṁ ॥ 93 ॥
guṇacaṁda sōmacaṁdā kālēṇa galiyasuguruuvaēsā । vīē guṇavvayammī aiyārē tē kuṇatēvaṁ ॥ 94 ||
uṁbīkaṇamāīṇa huraḍē bhuṁjēttu bhuṁjaē paḍhamō । apakē paribhōgaṁ bīōvi hu kuṇai kaiyāvi || 95||
dr̥ṣṭvā vibhaṅgēnēhāgatā gurusnēhapratibaddhā । tasmātsarvathā pitāpi hi tava mariṣyati virahahahr̥dayaḥ ॥ 82 ॥
yaddivasāttvamapahr̥tāsi samaṁ tu prōṣitaṁ tasya । nidrākṣudādikaṁ tathā mr̥tā punastatkṣaṇamaham ||83 ||
tasmindina ēva sarvatra niścitaṁ gavēṣitāpi nōpalabdhāsi । tasmād yūmaṁ sarvē'pi hi tiṣṭhatātraiva kṣaṇamakam ||84॥
yāvadahaṁ raṇamallaṁ tava pitaraṁ putri ! atrānayāmi । tatastatkṣaṇēna gatvā samāgatā taṁ gr̥hītvā ॥ 85 ॥
sa vanditvā sādhumupaviṣṭastataḥ kumārādibhiḥ । abhivanditō bhaṇati vilāsavatī saṁmukhamēvam ॥ 86 ॥
sarvō'pi mayā jñātō jananīvacanād vyatikarastava । atha nr̥papurandarō'pi hiṁ kumāragavēṣaṇayā saṁprāptaḥ ॥ 87 ॥
raṇamallādibhistatō'bhyutthāya vanditō rājā । munināpi samārabdhā punarapi sadēśanā tēṣām ॥ 88 ॥
ityādidēśanāntē raṇamallēna purandarō bhaṇitaḥ । ēṣā mama prāṇapriyā duhitā prītyā draṣṭavyā ॥ 89 ॥
nr̥paraṇamallō nītaḥ purandarēṇa nijē nagarē | guṇacandrājjñātvā sarva saṁbandhādikam ॥90॥
dēvamithunamapi dattvā kumāravadhūbhyāṁ suratnamābharaṇam । svasthānē saṁprāptaṁ munirapi viharati vasudhāyām ॥ 91 ॥
katipayadināni dhr̥tvā sammānya visarjitō rājñā । raṇamallaḥ saṁprāptō nijanagarē karōti saddharmam ||92||
dvitīyaguṇatratarakṣāṁ kurvan karōti viṣayaparibhōgam । śrīviśvasēnakumāraḥ smaran sugurugurvājñām ॥93॥
guṇacandrasōmacandrau kālēna galitasugurūpadēśau । dvitīyē guṇavatē'ticārāṁstau kuruta ēvam ॥94॥
umbīkaṇādīnāṁ samūhaṁ bhuktvā bhuṅgē prathamaḥ । apakvē paribhōgaṁ dvitīyō'pi hi karōti kadāpi ॥ 95||

supāsanāha- cariśrammi-
tō vismasēṇakumarō kōmalavāṇīē bhaṇai nāūṇa । bhō mittā ! nō juttaṁ guṇavvayaṁ iya kalaṁkēḍaṁ ॥96॥
avi uggagaralavisahara muhakuharē pakkhivaṁti niyapāṇi । hēlāē hālāhalakavalaṇapaṇā avi havaṁti ॥97॥
takkhaṇapasūyapullīpaōharēsuṁ suhaṁ piyati payaṁ । anukūlīkayapavaṇē davadahaṇamuhē suyaṁti varaṁ ॥ 98 ॥
pariōsēṇaṁ pavisaṁti nakkacakāulē mahājalahiṁ । rahasēṇaṁ pariraṁbhaṁti bhīsaṇaṁ tikkhakharanaharaṁ ||19||
na uṇō kharṇapi purisā pamāyalēsaṁpi kaṁiyavi kuṇaṁti । paijammajaṇiyadsa haduhadaṁdōlī mahābhīmaṁ ॥ 100 ॥
iya amayavidusaṁdōhadāya gaṁ nisuṇiūṇa kumara giraṁ । tē dōvi hu bāhuḍiyā aiyārāṇāṇakaraṇa mi ॥ 101 ॥
aha annā vasaṁtē vilāsavaīē sasaṁbhramaṁ kumarō । bhaṇiō piyayama ! kīlāparamhō jaivi taṁ tahavi ||
maha kōuyaṁ mahaṁta tā samagaṁ ēhi naṁdaṇujjāṇē । gaṁtūṇa kayalilavalīēlāivaṇēsu kīlēmō ।। 103 ।।
tō kumarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ payacchi ! na saṁgayaṁ imaṁ kāuṁ । tujjhuvarōhō- tahavi hu avarajjhai iya bhaṇēūṇa ||
tīi samaṁ saṁcaliō pattō sō naṁdaṇammi ujjāṇē । parisara jiṇabhavaṇatō bhuvaṇapahuṁ pūi thuṇi ॥ 105 ॥
nikkhatō sō tattō pattō gahirampri vaṇaniguṁjapi । gurjatamahura mahuyara para huya ravabhariyanahavivarē ।। 106 ।।
kusumabharabhāra bhāsurasuraviḍavimaraṭṭabha jaṇasamatthō । saccaviō tatthikkō mahātarū saralasāhālō || 107 ॥
aviralagurudalamāsaliyavahalacchāyāē channadēsampi । saha pāē kumarō javaviṭṭō jā palōēi ॥ 108 ॥
tassōhaṁ tō sahasā gayaṇāu samāgaō guruyavēgā । ēgō ra mahanvaiō rūmassī gahiyakhaḍuṁgō || 109॥
bhāsurajaḍākō ṭāṭaṁkāranēuraravaḍḍhō । sasisamakavālapāṇī pāṇīṇa palayakālōvva ॥ 110 ॥
tatō viśvasēnakumāraḥ kōmalavāṇyā bhaṇati jñānavā । bhō mitrē । nō yuktaṁ guṇavratamiti kalaṅkayitum ॥ 96 ॥
apyugragaralaviṣadharamukha kuharē prakṣipanti nijapāṇim । hēlayā hālāhalakavalanapraguṇā api bhavanti ॥ 97||
tatkṣaṇaprasūtavyāghrapiyōdharēṣu sukhaṁ pibanti payaḥ । anukūlīkr̥tapavanē davadahanamukhē svapanti varam ॥98॥
paritōṣēṇa praviśanti nacakrākulaṁ mahājaladhim । rabhasēna parirabhantē bhīṣaṇaṁ tīkṣṇakharanakharam ॥ 99 ॥
na punaḥ kṣaṇamapi puruṣāḥ pramādalēśamapi kadāpi kurvanti । pratijanmajanitaduḥ saha duḥkhadvandvālī mahābhīmam ॥
ityamr̥tabindusaṁdōhadāyikāṁ śrutvā kumāragiram । tau dvāvapi lajjitāvaticārājñānakaraṇē ॥101॥
athānyadā vasantē vilāsavattyā sasaṁbhramaṁ kumāraḥ । bhaṇitaḥ priyatama ! krīḍāparāṅmukhō yadyapi tvaṁ tathāpi ॥
mama kautukaṁ mahat tasmātsamamēhi nandanōdyānē । gatvā kadalīlavalyēlādivanēṣu krīḍāvaḥ ॥ 103 ॥
tataḥ kumārēṇa bhaṇitaṁ mr̥gākṣi ! na saṁgatamidaṁ kartum । tavōparōdhastathāpi hyaparādhyatīti bhaṇitvā ॥ 104॥
tayā samaṁ saṁcalitaḥ prāptaḥ sa nandana udyānē । praviśati jinabhavanāntō bhuvanaprabhuṁ pūjayitvā stutvā 105 ॥
niṣkrāntaḥ sa tataḥ prāptō gabhīrē vananikuñja । guñjanmadhuramadhukara paramr̥taravabhr̥tanabhōvivarē ॥ 106 ॥
kusumabharabhārabhāsurasuraviṭapigarvabhañjanasamarthaḥ । dr̥ṣṭastatraikō mahātaruḥ saralaśākhaḥ ॥ 107॥
avirala gurudala māṁsa litabahalacchāyayā channadēśē । saha priyatamayā kumāra upaviṣṭō yāvatpralōkatē ॥ 108॥
tacchōbhāṁ tataḥ sahamā gaganātsamāgatō guruvēgāt । ēkastu mahātratikō rūpadhān gr̥hītakhaṭāṅgaḥ ॥ 109॥

vissa sēṇakahā ।
૨૭
ḍamaḍamiyamarupārāvabhīsaṇō pēcchiūṇa sō kumaraṁ । aṇamisanayaṇōvva ṭhiō na jaṁpaē kiṁpi lihiubba ।।
ukkīliucca parithēbhiucca sunnuvva mukkajīucva । kumarēṇa piyā bhaṇiyā na hōi purisō imō, itthī ||
bhaṇiyaṁ vilāsavaīē kahamēyaṁ nāha ! purisarūtradharaṁ । jaṁpasi ramaṇīkaraṇīrahiyaṁpi hu itthiyaṁ ēyaṁ ? ।। 113 ||
tō bhaṇiyaṁ kumarēṇa mayacchi ! cihnaṁ niyasu ēyassa । tiricchīē niyaccha mēṁ picchivi sēyamuvvahai ||
unhai bahalapulayaṁ caraṇaguḍēṇa khaṇai khōṇiyalaṁ । iya cihnaṁ kuṇamāṇi māṇiṇi ! muṇa bhāmini ēyaṁ ॥
vijjāsiddhinimittaṁ gahiō vēsō imīē iha ēsō । jamhā kīivi kōvi hu vijjāē sāhaṇōvāō ।। 116 ॥
iya jā jaṁpara kumarō sā vijjā tīi takkhaṇaṁ siddhā । tō mōttuṁ kāvāliyavēsaṁ sā itthiyā jāyā ॥ 117 ॥
bhai ya tuha daṁsaṇaō siddhā vijjā kumāra ! sucirāō। kappadumaṁva sappurisadaṁsaṇamahavā na kiṁ kuṇai ? ||
tō maha dēhaṁ jīyaṁ savvaṁ tumhāṇa cēva āyattaṁ । gaṁtūṇaṁ vēgaḍḍhē piyarāī jāna āṇēmi ॥। 119 ।।
tāvakhaṇaṁ itthēva ya cisu pāṇēsa ! maha dayaṁ kāuṁ । tujjhuvayārakaraṇaṁ dēhaṁ jā dēmi tē vihiṇā ।। 120 ॥
iya bhaṇiūṇa gayā sā tattō pacchannabhamirarūpēṇa । vijjāharēṇa savvaṁ nisuyaṁ divaṁ ca taccariyaṁ ॥ 121 ॥
sō uṇa puvyarattō chammāsē tīi puṭṭima laggō । bhamiō jā tadivasa vijjāsiddhiṁ paḍicchatō ॥ 122॥
tō sō ucitō karirūvēṇaṁ kumāramukkhiviṁḍaṁ । uppaiō āgāsē picchaṁtassavi pariyaṇassa ॥ 123॥
tattō vilāsaaīē puriyaṁ viduravirahasadēṇa । tō guṇacaṁdaṣpamuhā pahāviyā gahiyasiyasatthā ॥ 124॥
bhāsurajaṭāsamūhō ghaṇṭāṭaṅkāranūpuraravāḍhyaḥ । śaśisamakapālapāṇiḥ prāṇinā pralayakāla iva ॥ 110 ॥
ḍamaḍamitaḍamarukā rāvabhīṣaṇō dr̥ṣṭā sa kumāram । animiṣanayanavat sthitō na jalpati kimapi likhitavat ॥
utkīlitavatparistambhitavacchranyavada muktajīvitavat । kumārēṇa priyā bhaṇitā na bhavati puruṣō'yaṁ, strī ॥ 112 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ vilāsavatyā kathamēnaṁ nātha ! puruṣarūpavaram | jalpasi ramaṇyākārarahitamapi hi striyamēnam ॥113॥
tatō bhaṇitaṁ kumārēṇa mr̥gākṣi ! cēṣṭāṁ paśyaitasya । tiryagakṣṇā paśyati māṁ dr̥ṣṭrā svēdamudvahati ॥ 114 ॥
udvahati bahulapulakaṁ caraṇāṅguṣṭēna khanati kṣōṇitalam । iti cēṣṭāṁ kurvāṇaṁ mānini ! jānīhi bhāminīmētam ॥
vidyāsiddhinimittaṁ gr̥hītō vēṣō'nayē haiṣaḥ । yasmātkasyā api kō'pi khalu vidyāyāḥ sādhanōpāyaḥ ॥ 116 ॥
iti yāvajjalpati kumāraḥ sā vidyā tasyāstatkṣaṇaṁ siddhā । tatō muktyā kāpālikavēṣaṁ sā strī jātā ॥ 117 ॥
bhaṇati ca tava darśanataḥ siddhā vidyā kumāra ! sucirāt । kalpadrumavat satpuruṣadarśanamathavā na kiṁ karōti ? |
tatō mama dēha jīvitaṁ sarvē yuṣmākamēvāyattam । gatvā vaitāḍhyē pitarau yāvadānayāmi ॥ 119 ॥
tāvatkṣaṇamatraiva ca tiṣṭha prāṇēśa ! mama dayāṁ kr̥tvā । tavōpakārakr̥tē dēhaṁ yāvaddadāmi tē vidhinā ॥ 120॥
iti bhaṇitvā gatā sā tataḥ pracchannabhramitr̥rūpēṇa । vidyādharēṇa sarva śrutaṁ dr̥ṁ ca taccaritam ॥ 121 ॥
sa punaḥ pūrvānuraktaḥ paṇmāsāṁstasyāḥ pr̥ṣṭhamanulagnaḥ । bhrāntō yāvattaddivasaṁ vidyāsiddhiṁ pratīcchan ॥ 122॥
tataḥ sa pradviṣṭacittaḥ karirūpēṇa kumāramutkṣipya । utpatita ākāśē paśyatyapi parijanē ॥ 123 ॥
tatō vilāsavatyā prakr̥taṁ vidhuravirahaśabdēna । tatō guṇacandrapramukhāḥ pradhāvitā gr̥hītaśitaśastrāḥ ॥124॥

૪૭૬
supāsamāha cariammi-
rāyāvi kahavi nāūṇa kumaravr̥ttaṁtamēi jā tattha । tā picchai mucchāē nimīliyacchiṁ vilāsavaī ॥ 125॥
tō bhai ya niyapurisē bhō bhō gaṁdhōdayaṁ samāṇēuṁ । turiyaṁ chaṁṭaha ēvaṁ taha vīyaha tālayaṁṭēṇa || 126 ॥
tō taha vihiē pauṇā sā jāyā tattha tā pattā | guṇacaṁdāī suhaḍā sāhaṁti nivassa jaha dēva ! |
kumarō kariṇā gayaṇē diṭṭhō amhēhiṁ nīyamāṇō tō। kiṁ kuṇimō sē jaṁ sō agōyarō amhabāṇāṇa ||
aha sā saha, pirēhi pattā vijjāharīvi pucchē । kattha gaō tumha suō, kahai nivō kēṇavi haḍōti ॥
tō tīē nāyamiṇaṁ hariō sō tēṇa pāvakhayarēṇa । kahiyē ca tassarūvaṁ piuṇō, sō bhai naranāhaṁ ||
jaha sattadiṇāṇatō tuha puttaṁ niccharaṇa āṇissaṁ । tā mā khaṇamavi khēyaṁ kuṇasa tumaṁ vaccasu sagēhaṁ ||
sōvi siṁha pas caliō guṇacaṁdāō vilāsavaidēviṁ । saṁdhīraṁtō pattō, khayarōvi kuḍhāvaē laggō ।। 132॥
sō duṭṭhō gayaṇacarō jalanihidīvammi vivi taṁ kumaraṁ । gaṁtūṇaṁ vēyaḍḍhē karēi sāmaggiyaṁ paṇaṁ ॥ 133 ॥
pariṇayaṇatthaṁ tattō kumarō dīvammi viyaraē jāva । vaṇadēvayavva tatthavi diṭṭhā tā bhāmiṇī ēgā ।। 134 ||
tō puṭṭhā kumarē kā si tumaṁ kiṁnimittamiha pattā ? । tō mukkadīha uṇhasāsa susiyāē tīēvi ।। 135 ।।
bhaṇiyaṁ puccha sudivvaṁ jēṇāhaṁ nimmiyā amiyadukkhā । bhuvaṇasiddhammi kulē jaṇiūṇa puṇō ihāṇīyā ॥
iya bhaṇiuṁ ruyamāṇī kumarēṇa nivāriḍaṁ imaṁ bhaṇiyā । mā kuṇasu maṇē khēyaṁ paribhāvasu divyapariṇāma ||
uccē nīē nīē ya unnaē vihaviṇō daridē ya । rōrē ya rāiṇōvi ya rāē kē kuṇai kammaṁ || 138 ॥
tamhā kammucchēē chēē ! taṁ āyaraṁ kuṇasu jēṇa । na puṇō puṇabbhavō bhavaduhāṇa tuha jāyai kayāī | | 139 ||
।
rājāpi kathamapi jñātvā kumāravr̥ttāntamēti yāvattatra । tāvatpaśyati mūrcchayā nimīlitākṣīṁ vilāsavatīm ॥
tatō bhaṇati ca nijapuruṣān bhō bhō gandhōdakaṁ samānīya । tvaritamukṣataitāṁ tathā vījayata tālavr̥ntēna ॥ 126॥
tatastathāvihitē praguṇā sā jātā tatra tāvatprāptāḥ । guṇacandrādayaḥ subhaṭāḥ kathayanti nr̥pasya yathā dēva ! |
kumāraḥ : kariṇā gaganē dr̥ṣṭō'smābhinayamānastataḥ । kiṁ kurmastasya yatsō'gōcarō'smadvāṇānām ॥128॥
atha sā saha pitr̥bhyāṁ prāptā vidyādharyapi pr̥cchati । kutra gatastava sutaḥ, kathayati nr̥paḥ kēnāpi hr̥ta iti ॥
tatastayā jñātamidaṁ hr̥taḥ sa tēna pāpakhacarēṇa । kathitaṁ ca tatsvarūpaṁ pituḥ, sa bhaṇati naranātham ॥ 130 ॥
yathā saptadinānāmantastava putraṁ niścayēnānēṣyāmi । tasmānmā kṣaṇamapi khēdaṁ kuruṣva tvaṁ vraja svagēham ॥ 131 ॥
sō'pi gr̥haṁ prati calitō guṇacandrād vilāsavatīdēvīm | saṁdhīrayan prāptaḥ khacarō'pi gavēṣayituṁ lagnaḥ ॥
sa duṣṭō gaganacarō jalanidhidvīpē kṣiptvā taṁ kumāram । gatvā vaitāḍhḍhayē karōti sāmagrīṁ praguṇām ॥133॥
pariṇayanārthaṁ, tataḥ kumārō dvīpē vicarati yāvat । vanadēvatēva tatrāpi dr̥ṣṭā tāvad bhāminyēkā ॥ 134 ॥
tataḥ pr̥ṣṭā kumārēṇa kā'si tvaṁ kiṁnimittamiha prāptā ? । tatō muktadīrghōṣṇaśvāsa śuṣkayā tayāpi ॥ 135 ॥
bhaṇitaṁ pr̥ccha daivaṁ yēnāhaṁ nirmitā'mitaduḥkhā । bhuvanaprasiddhē kulē janayitvā punarihānītā ॥ 136 ॥
iti bhaṇitvā rudatī kumārēṇa nivāryēdaṁ bhaṇitā । mā kuru manasi khēdaṁ paribhāvaya divyapariṇāmam ॥ 137॥
uccānnīcān nīcāṁścōnnatān vibhavinō daridrāṁśca । rōrāṁśca rājñō'pi ca rājñō raṅkānkarōti karma ॥ 138 ॥

iccāidēṇāra sōyaṁ mōyāviyā kumārēṇa । saṁṭhaviyā ṭhāṇavisaṁṭhulāvi gōvivya gōvēṇa || 140||
tō sāhiu pattā paraō cariyaṁ niyaṁ kumārassa । jaha sirinayara nivāsissa sēṭṭiṇō sōmadēvassa ||
taṇayā haṁ kaṇayasirī pariṇīyā sālibhaddanāmēṇaṁ । tannayaravāsiṇā sāyaraṁ ca nīyā ya niyagēhē ॥ 142 ॥
jhuṁja sō visayasu maē samaṁ samahiyāṇurāēṇa । bhaṇiyā haṁ tēṇa piē ! piugēhē nēya gaṁtavvaṁ ।। 143 ॥
ēvaṁti maē bhaṇiya navaraṁ kaiyāvi avatāyāṇa । āhavaṇē mōkalayaṁ aṇunāyāē tara nāha ! || 144 ॥
taṁpi huna bahu mayaṁ tassa, annayā rayaṇiaddharattampi | kōci maē gāyaṁtō nisuō niyaḍammi gēhammi ||
tō maṇiō niyamattā maē imaṁ nāha! gāyaṇō kōvi । gāyai paṇavīsavaō khattiyakulasaṁbhavō gōrō ॥
apāū asubhagō pīvaradēhō na ēttha saṁdēhō । gujjhammi masō asamō parissamō tassa dhaṇuvē ।। 147॥
iya jāva maē bhaṇiyaṁ nāūṇaṁ saravisēsasatthāō । tō tammaṇammi jaliō pabalō īsānalō sahasā ||
tō tadiṇā cattō saṁbhāsōvi hum̐ maē samaṁ tēṇa । tō ciṁtiyaṁ maē naṇu guṇōvi dōsattaṇaṁ pattō ॥ 149 ॥
taṇibhipi imō samujattāsamūsuō jāō । tattō piyaraṇunāō saṁcaliō sōhaṇadiṇammi || 150 ॥
ahamavi tassuvarōhaṁ viṇāvi saha tēṇa pōyamārūḍhā । rayaṇīē jalahimajjhammi uḍiyā vigayaniddāhaṁ ।। 151॥
jā dēhacitaṭhāṇaṁ pattā jalahimmi tēṇa tā khittā | saṁpattaphalahakhaṁḍā ihāgayā ajja chuhiyā haṁ ॥ 152 ॥
iya kahiūṇa samappara kumarasta phalāī sā sacittāī । tāī na bhuṁjai kumarō maṇammi niyamaṁ niyaṁ nāēṁ।
tasmātkarmōcchēdē chēkē ! tvamādaraṁ kuru yēna । na punaḥ punarbhavō bhavaduḥkhānāṁ tava jāyatē kadācit ॥139॥
ityādidēśanayā śōkaṁ mōcitā kumārēṇa । saṁsthāpitā sthānavisaṁsthalāpi gōpīva gōpēna ॥ 140॥
tataḥ kathayituṁ pravr̥ttā parataścaritaṁ nijaṁ kumārasya । yathā śrīnagaranivāsinaḥ śrēṣṭhinaḥ sōmadēvasya ॥ 141 ॥
'tanayā'haṁ kanakaśrīḥ pariṇītā śālibhadranāmnā । tannagaravāsinō sādaraṁ ca nītā ca nijagēhē ॥ 142 ॥
bhuṅgē sa viṣayasukhaṁ mayā samaṁ samadhikānurāgēṇa । bhaṇitā'haṁ tēna priyē ! pitr̥gēhē naiva gantavyam ॥ 143॥
ēvamiti mayā bhaṇitaṁ kintu kadāpyambātātayaḥ । āhvānē mutkalamanujñātāyāstava nātha ! || 144 ॥
tadapi hi na bahu mataṁ tasya, anyadā rajanyardharātrē । kō'pi mayā gāyan śrutō nikaṭē gēhē ॥145॥
tatō bhaṇitō nijabhartā mayēdaṁ nātha ! gāyanaḥ kō'pi । gāyati pañcaviṁśativayāḥ kṣatriyakulasaṁbhavō gauraḥ ॥
alpāyuratisubhaga: pīvaradēhō nātra saṁdēhaḥ । guhyē tilō'samaḥ pariśramastasya dhanurvēdē ॥ 147 ॥
iti yāvad mayā bhaṇitaṁ jñātvā svaraviśēṣaśāstrāt । tatastanmanasi jvalitaḥ prabala īṣyanilaḥ sahasā ॥ 148 ॥
tanastaddināt tyaktaḥ saṁbhāṣō'pi hi mayā samaṁ tēna । tataścintitaṁ mayā nanu guṇō'pi dōṣatyaṁ prāptaḥ ||
taddinaprabhr̥tyapyayaṁ samudrayātrāsamutsukō jātaḥ । tataḥ pitranujñātaḥ saṁcalitaḥ śōbhanadinē ॥ 190 ॥
ahamapi tasyōparōdhaṁ vināpi saha tēna pōtamārūḍhā । rajanyāṁ jaladhimadhya utthitā vigata nidrāham ॥ 111 ॥
yāvad dēhacintāsthānaṁ prāptā jaladhau tēna tāvat kṣiptā । saṁprāptaphalakakharāḍē hā gatā'dya kṣudhitāham ॥152॥

tō guruavarōhēṇa bhaṇiō sō tīē kahai jaṁha majjha । mōttūṇa pattasalilaṁ niyamō sacittadavvassa ॥ 154 ॥
ēvaṁ satta diṇēsō maṇasāvi ha vaṁchaē naya sacittaṁ । taha dēsaṇāē vihiyā vārasavayadhāriṇī sāvi ।। 155 ।।
hu
tō kayacittaniyamā sābuvavāsēhiṁ satta divasāī । ciṭṭhai tā puvvuttā pattā vijjāharī tattha ॥156॥
bahuparivārasamēyā pāsai kumaraṁ aīva kisakāyēṁ। puraō ya ṭhiāē khāmōyarīē saha kiṁpi japatē ।। 157 ॥
tō sirakayaṁkarakamalā sā japai taṁ pai imaṁ vayaṇaṁ । āruhaha vimāṇamiṇaṁ gacchāmō tuha purē jēṇa || 158।।
niō maha tāraṇaṁ sō tuha avayārakāraō khayarō | iya sumi sō jaṁpai ahaha viruddhaṁ kaha vihiyē ? ॥
kaṇavāsirī dhammōvalaṁbha hē uttaṇēṇa haṁ jāō । jaṁ tēṇa ihāṇīō sō uvayārī aō majjha || 160॥
ahavā tassa vikammaṁ kiṁcitri cirasaṁciyaṁ imaṁ phaliyaṁ । iya jaṁpiyāvasāṇē vaṇivahuyā kahai khayarī ||
jaha ajja sattamadiṇaṁ vaṭṭa uvavāsiyassa kumarassa | jamhā jaṁ vā taṁ vā na bhuṁjaē ēsa dhīrappā ॥ 162 ॥
tō khayarīparivārō āṇai phalapattakusumakaṁdāī | ḍhōēi kumarapuraō pubvaṁva na bhuṁjaē taṁpi ॥ 163 ॥
tō tapparivārēṇa tāī tāī, ghāriō sahaptā । sō savvō tō kumarō mammi ēvaṁ vicitē || 164||
sō jaya jaē dhammō jasta pabhāvēṇaṁ āvaisamudaṁ । laṁghēti bhavē bhaviṇō bhāvisubhā ya jāyati ॥ 165 ॥
kiñca ।
1
tē gurugō guṇaguruṇī suhaphalataruṇō tamōhadiṇamaṇiṇō । jīyaṁtu jaē jēhiṁ niyamapayāṇēṇa haṁ dhariō ||
nivaḍatā niviḍāvaigurutara aiviyaḍa ayaḍakhaḍḍāē । kakkhaḍabhavāḍavīē aḍapi hu vāriyē jēhiṁ ।। 167॥
I
iti kathayitvā samarpayati kumārāya phalāni sā sacittāni । tāni na bhuṅgē kumārō manasi niyamaṁ nijaṁ jñātvā ॥
tatō gurvavarōdhēna bhaṇitaḥ sa tayā kathayati yathā mama । muktvā patrasalilaṁ niyamaḥ sacittadravyasya ॥ 154॥
ēvaṁ sapta dināni sa manasāpi hi vāñchati na ca sacittam । tathā dēśanayā vihitā dvādaśatratadhāriṇī sāpi ॥
tataḥ kr̥tasacittaniyamā sāpyupavāsaiḥ sapta divasāni । tiṣṭhati tāvatpūrvōktā prāptā vidyādharī tatra ॥ 156 ॥
bahuparivārasamētā paśyati kumāramatīva kr̥śakāyam । purataśca sthitayā kṣāmōdaryā saha kimapi jalpantam ॥
tataḥ śiraḥkr̥takarakamalā sā jalpati taṁ pratīdaṁ vacanam। ārōhata vimānamidaṁ gacchāmastava purē yēna ॥ 158 ॥
nihatō mama tātēna sa tavāpakārakārakaḥ khacaraḥ । iti śrutvā sa jalpatyahaha viruddha kathaṁ vihitam ॥159॥
kanakaśriyā dharmōpalambhahētutvēnāhaṁ jātaḥ । yattēnēhānītaḥ sa upakārī atō mama ॥ 160 ॥
athavā tasya vikarma kiñcidapi cirasaṁcitamidaṁ phalitam । iti jalpitāvasānē vaṇigvadhūḥ kathayati khacaryāḥ ॥
yathā'dya saptamadinaṁ vartata upōṣitasya kumārasya । yasmād yadvā tadvā na bhuṅga ēṣa dhīrātmā ॥ 162॥
tataḥ khacararrāparivāra ānayati phalapatrakusumakandāni । ṭōkatē kumārapurataḥ pūrvamiva na bhuṅktē tadapi ॥ 163 ॥
tatastatparivārēṇa bhuktāni tāni, ghātitaḥ sahasā । sa sarvastataḥ kumārō manasyēvaṁ vicintayati ॥ 164 ॥
sa jayati jagati dharmōṁ yasya prabhāvaṇāpatsamudram । laṅghantē bhavē bhavinō bhāvasubhadrāśca jāyantē || 16
tē guravō guṇaguravaḥ śubhaphalataravastamaōghadinamaṇayaḥ । jīyāsurjagati yairniyamapradānēnāhaṁ dhr̥taḥ ॥166॥

vissa sēkahā ।
476
iya ciṁtaṁtē kumarē khayarī vijjāē muṇai jaha paḍhamaṁ । pucyuttavēyarēṇa visēṇa vāsitu ēyāī ॥ 168 ॥
ārōviyāī ihi tāṇaṁ pabhāvō viyabhiō ēsō । iya nicchiūṇa āṇē ōsahiṁ visavighāyakariṁ ॥
tō tīē nāsiōvaraṭaviyāē uḍiō imē sahasā । tō khayarīē kumarō kaṇayasirīē saha vimāṇē ॥
ārōviūṇa nīō bhōgapurē garuyavirahaduhiyāṇa | paṇaō piyarāṇa taō mahāvibhūīē vīvāha || 171 ||
pāraddhō khayarēhi tattōsā tēṇa pariṇīyā khayarī | surasuṁdarībhihāṇā sumuṇīṇavi mōhasaṁjaṇaṇī ॥ 172॥
kaṇaya sirīvi suniñcalacittā niñcapi sāvayavasu । nivasai tassēva gihē bhaiṇīē nivvisēsayarā ।। 173॥
tō samayaṁ nāūṇaṁ rāyā gii jiṇamaē dikkhaṁ । sirivissa sēṇakumaraṁ rajjē ṭhaviūṇa sulaggē || 174 ॥
sōvi kalattadugēṇaṁ saddhi muṁjēi rajjasirimaṇahaṁ । sāvayavaēsa niccaṁ aiyāraparyaṁpi rakkhatō ।। 175 ।।
tō kālēṇaṁ jāō vilāsavaīē suō jayāṇaṁdō । bāhattarikalakusalō kamēṇa sō jōvvaṇaṁ pattō ॥ 176 ॥
surasuṁdarīē jāyā duhiyā paḍipuñjalakkhaṇōkyā । ittiyamitta kuṭuṁbaṁ, niyamō sēsassa tēṇa kaō || 177 ||
rajjaṁ surajjubaṁdhō bhōgā rōgavva bhavaṇamabhibhavaṇaṁ । paṇaiṇīō sapiṇīō isa manatō gamai kāṁlaṁ ॥
jassa payāvō ārakkhiō ya maṁtīvi niyamaippasarō । āṇacciya cārayavaṁdhaṇāi dhaṇiyaṁ dhaṇaṁ puṇṇaṁ ॥
aha kahavi kammavasaō vilāsavaīē taṇummi gururōgō । saṁjāō vijjēhivi uvayariyā māuliṁgēṇa ॥
saṁjāyā nīrōgā tahāvi sā bhuṁjaē paidipi । abbhāsāu sacittaṁ tō rannā vāriyāṁ ēvaṁ || 181 ॥
nipatan niciḍāpadgurutarātivikaṭāvaṭagartē । karkaśabhavāṭavyāmaṭanamapi hi vāritaṁ yaiḥ ॥ 167 ॥
iti cintayati kumārē khacarī vidyayā jānāti yathā prathamam । pūrvōktakhēcarēṇa viṣēṇa vāsayitvaitāni ॥ 168 ॥
ārōpitānīdānīṁ tēṣāṁ prabhāvō vijr̥mbhita ēṣaḥ । iti niścityānayatyōṣadhīṁ viṣavighātakarīm ॥ 169 ॥
tatastayā nāsikōparisthāpitāyāmutthitā imē sahasā । tataḥ khacaryā kumāraḥ kanakaśriyā saha vimānē ॥ 170 ॥
ārōpya nītō bhōgapurē guruvirahaduḥkhitayōḥ । praṇataḥ pitrōstatō mahāvibhūtyā vīvāhaḥ ॥ 171 ॥
prārabdhaḥ khacaraistataḥ sā tēna pariṇītā khacarī । surasundaryabhidhānā sumunīnāmapi mōhasaṁjananī || 172।।
kanakaśrīrapi suniścalacittā nityamapi śrāvakatratēṣu । nivasati tasyaiva gr̥hē bhaginyā nirviśēṣatarā ॥ 173 ॥
tataḥ samayaṁ jñātvā rājā gr̥hṇāti jinamatē dīkṣām । śrīviśvasēnakumāraṁ rājyē sthāpayitvā śubhalagnē || 174 |
sō'pi kalatradvikēna sārdhaṁ bhuṅktē rājyaśriyamakṣatām । śrāvakatratēṣu nityamaticārapadamapi rakṣan ॥ 175 ॥
tataḥ kālēna jātō vilāsavatyāḥ sutō jagadānandaḥ । dvāsaptatikalākuśalaḥ kramēṇa sa yauvanaṁ prāptaḥ ॥ 176 ॥
surasundaryā jāṁtā duhitā paripūrṇalakṣaṇōpētā । ētāvanmātrakuṭumba, niyamaḥ śēṣasya tēna kr̥taḥ ॥ 977 ॥
rājyaṁ surajjubandhurbhōgā rōgā iva bhavanamabhibhavanam । praṇayinyaḥ sarpya iti manyamānō gamayati kālam || 178॥
yasya pratāpa ārakṣikaśca mantryapi nijamatiprasaraḥ । ājñēva cārakabandhanāni gāḍhaṁ dhanaṁ puṇyam ॥ 179॥
atha kathamapi karmavaśatō vilāsavatyāstanau gururōgaḥ । saṁjātō vaidyairapyupacaritā mātuliṅgēna ॥ 180 ॥
saṁjātā nīrōgā tathāpi sā mujhē pratidinamapi । abhyāsāt sacittaṁ tatō rājñā vāritaivam ॥ 1.81 ॥

bīyaguṇavvayamēvaṁ mā mā aiyaraha kāraṇēṇa viṇā । saṁjāyagāḍhagiddhī kuṇai imā uttaraṁ ēvaṁ || 182||
jai māuliṁgamahuṇā mahuṇā saha aha kahaṁ na muṁjēmi । tō rōgō maha dēhē karēi pīḍaṁ mahaṁtaṁpi ॥183॥
tō bhaṇiyā bhūvaṇā bhaddē ! sacittaōsahāīhiṁ । saṁjāyapaḍasarīrāṁ karēsi iya uttaramajuttaṁ ॥ 184 ॥
yataḥ,
।
"
11
ēgassa kaē niyajīviyassa bahuyāu jīvakōḍīō । jē kē ṭhavaṁti dukkhē tāṇaṁ kiṁ sāsaō appā ? ||
" kr̥mayō bhasma viṣṭhā vā niṣṭhā yasyēyamīdr̥śī । sa kāyaḥ parapīḍābhiḥ pōṣyatāmiti kō nayaḥ ॥
mahatā puṇyapaṇyēna krītēyaṁ kāyanaustvayā । pāraṁ duḥkhōdadhērgantuṁ tvara yāvanna bhidyatē
sugurumuhaniggayāṇaṁ vayaṇāṇaṁ niyamuhaṣpavannāṇa । jaṁ gaṁjaṇaṁ vihijjai taṁ mannē mōhamāha || 186 ॥
iha lōēva duhaṁ ci paralōē nittulaṁ tu taṁ hōhī । guruāṇābhaṁgāō bōhīvihu dullahā mannē || 187 ||
iccāidēsaṇāē vihiyāēvi huna tīi paḍivayaṇaṁ । dinaṁ gurukammāē ahaha ahō dāruṇō mōhō || 188॥
avahīriyā nivēṇa kaṁdāī sēvaē niraggalaē । rōgēṇavi abhibhūyā duhāvi gayadiṭṭiyā jāyā ॥ 189 ॥
aṇubhaviḍaṁ gurudukkhaṁ mariūṇaṁ vaṁtarēsu uvavannā । bhamiūṇa bhavē lahihī kamēṇa kammakkhayā mōkkhaṁ ॥
kaṇayasirī vaṇiduhiyā gahiyāṇuvvayaguṇavvayā taiyā । tassaṁsaggavasēṇaṁ siṭilēi guṇavvayaṁ bīyaṁ ॥
aipakka aṁbayāī accittāiti mannamāṇī sā । saccittappaḍibaddhaṁ bhuṁjai saccittakaya niyamā ।।192।।
tō naē naravaṇā bhaṇiyā karabhōru ! kiṁ na jāṇāsi । karayalakaliyajalaṁ piva galēi jaṁ āuyaṁ taha ya ।।
kiṁ na niyacchasi pasayacchi ! lacchilīlāsuhāīṁ virasāī । pariṇāmadāruṇāī anaṁtabhavabhamaṇahēūṇi ॥
dvitīyaguṇatratamēvaṁ mā māticarata kāraṇēna vinā । saṁjātagāḍhagr̥ddhiḥ karōtīyamuttaramēvam ॥ 182॥
yadi mātuliṅgamadhunā madhunā sahāhaṁ kathaṁ na muñjēya । tatō rōgō mama dēhē karōti pīḍāṁ mahatīmapi ॥ 183॥
tatō bhaṇitā bhūpatinā bhadrē ! sacittauṣadhādibhiḥ । saṁjātapaṭuśarīrā karōṣītyuttaramayuktam ॥ 184॥
ēkasya kr̥tē nijajīvitasya bahūrjīvakōṭīḥ । yē kē sthāpayanti duḥkhē tēṣāṁ kiṁ śāśvata ātmā ? ॥ 185 ॥
sugurumukhanirgatānāṁ vacanānāṁ nijamukhaprapannānām । yadavamānanaṁ vidhīyatē tanmanyē mōhamāhātmyam ॥186॥
ihalōkē'pi duḥkhamēva paralōkē nistulaṁ tu tad bhaviṣyati । gurvājñābhaṅgād bōdhirapi hi durlabhō manyē ॥ 187॥
ityādidēśanāyā vihitāyā api hi na tathā prativacanam । dattaṁ gurukarmayā'haha ahō dāruṇō mōhaḥ ॥ 188॥
avadhīritā nr̥pēṇa kandādīn sēvatē nirargalān । rōgēṇāpyabhibhūtā dvidhāpi gatadr̥ṣṭikā jātā ॥ 189॥
anubhūya guruduḥkhaṁ mr̥tvā vyantarēṣūpapannā । bhrāntvā bhavē lapsyatē kramēṇa karmakṣayād mōkṣam ॥ 190 ॥
kanakaśrīrvaṇigduhitā gr̥hītāṇuvrata guṇatratā tadā । tatsaṁsargavaśēna śithilayati guṇatrataṁ dvitīyam ॥191॥
atipakvāmlānyacittānīti manyamānā sā । sacittapratibaddhaṁ bhuṅktē kr̥tasacittaniyamā ॥ 192॥
tatō jñātē narapatinā bhaṇitā karabhōru ! kiṁ na jānāsi । karatalakalitajalamiva galati yadāyustathāca ॥ 193॥
kiṁ na paśyasi mr̥gākṣi ! lakṣmīlīlāsukhāni virasāni । pariṇāmadāruṇānyanantabhavabhramaṇa hētūn ॥ 194 ॥

kāyavvaṁ kiṁ avvō ! sāhaha nisurya vibhāviu cittē । tēhiṁ bhaṇiyaṁ narēsara ! bālōvi viyāṇaē ēyaṁ ॥
naihariyō suyahi vallahō niru pamattamuttōvi । kiṁ puṇa sapabuddhō taha ya sayaṁ nīharaṁtō vā ॥ 220 ॥
pajjaliyagihāhitō, iharā tē vallahāvi ya na huṁti । tō bhaṇiyaṁ bhūvaiṇā jai ēvaṁ tō nisāmēha ||221 ॥

iya jāva kiṁpi bhaṇiti tāva paḍihāramūiō pattō । ujjāṇapālapurisō vinnavai nivaṁ namivi ēvaṁ ॥
atha viśvasēnarājō dharmē samudyatō gamayati kālam । tataḥ kēnāpi niśīthē paṭhitā gāthēyaṁ tatra ॥ 209 ॥
mucyantē rajjubaddhāḥ śr̥ṅkhalabaddhāśca nigaḍabaddhāśca । snēhanigaḍairbaddhā bhavakōṭigatāḥ kliśyanti ॥210॥
avadhārya gāthārthamēṣa bhāvayati nijamanasyēvam । mā jīva ! kutrāpi tvaṁ pratibandhaṁ kuruṣvēti jñātvā ॥ 211॥
rē jīva ! lālasamanā rājyādiṣu mā bhavērīṣadapi । jānannētēpāmavasānaṁ dāruṇavipākam ॥ 212 ॥
ādimadhyāvasānaṁ yādr̥śaṁ tādr̥śamapi jīva ! tvam | paribhāvaya sūkṣmayā buddhacā dharma - rājyayōḥ ॥ 213॥
ēkamēkāntasukhaṁ dvitīyamēkāntaduḥkhataramēva । gururapi kila viśēṣō jñāyatē niścitaṁ vivēkibhiḥ ॥ 214 ॥

āhūtāḥ sacivādayaḥ kathitaṁ tēṣāṁ yathā jvalataḥ । gēhasya madhyē suptē ca vallabhē durlabhē ॥ 217 ||
nidrākṣayē viddhō yadi sa nissarati tasya madhyāt । tataḥ kiṁ dhārayitavyaḥ svajanairbalādapi bāhubhiḥ ॥218॥
kartavyaṁ kiṁ hanta ! kathayata nibhr̥taṁ vibhāvya cittē । tairbhaṇitaṁ narēśvara ! bālō'pi vijānātyētat ॥ 219 ॥
niḥsārayitavyaḥ svajanairvallabhō niściṁtaṁ pramattasuptō'pi । kiṁ punaḥ svayaṁ prabuddhastathā ca svayaṁ nissaran vā ॥
prajvalitagr̥hāta, itarathā tē vallabhā api ca na bhavanti । tatō bhaṇitaṁ bhūpatinā yadyēvaṁ tatō niśamayata ||
bhavagr̥hamadhyē pramādajvalanajvalitē mōhanidrayā । māṁ suptaṁ ya ihōtthāpayati na nivārayitavyaḥ saḥ ॥222॥

sirinēmicaṁdrasūrī subhadaē udaya sēharujjāṇē । caunāṇī saṁpatō supattamuṇisaṁgaō sugaō || 224 ||
tō tuṭṭaṇaṁ rannā niyaṁgalaggaṁ samaggamābharaṇaṁ । tassa vinaṁ sahasā samuḍiō sūrinamaṇatthaṁ ॥ 225 ॥
sūricaraṇāraviṁdaṁ vaṁdē dēsaṇaṁ ca suṇiūṇa । rajjammi jayānaṁda kumaraṁ ṭhāvē gihapattō ॥ 226 ॥
ucchapaṇāpurassara miha rāyā sūripāpāsamma । giors dikkhaṁ sikkhādurgaṁ ca tada jāi mōkkhēvi ||
bhajāu viharaṇaṁ bhavam bhīmammi jiṇamayaṁ papya । kaivayabhavāṇa majjhē sijjhissaṁtīha thukampā ||
tō jaha imiṇā nipuṁgavēṇa vīyaṁ gugavyayaṁ dhariyaṁ । asimakamiti akkhaliyē jāvajīvapi ॥
RE nē bhavyē bhāvimadēhi dēvanivēkvaṁ । pālēyō niyamō niyama kaṁṭhadvipajiēhiṁ ॥ 230 ॥
॥ iti bhōgaparibhōgatē viśvasēnakumārakathānakaṁ pañcāticāra kathāsamanvitaṁ samāptam ॥
iti yāvatkimapi bhaṇivyanti tāvatpratihārasūcitaḥ prāptaḥ । udyānapālapuruṣō vijñapayati nr̥paṁ natvaivam ॥223॥

utsarpaṇā purassara miha rājā sūripādapārśvē । gr̥hṇāti dīkṣāṁ śikṣādvikaṁ ca tathā yāti mōkṣē'pi ॥ 227 ॥
